Transcribed, Edited, Formatted, and Color-Coded by

 

**Patrick Olivelle**

 

Based on the edition:

 

Ganapati Sastri, T. _The Yājñavalkyasmṛti with the Commentary Bālakrīda of Visvarūpāchārya._ Two Parts. Trivandrum: Government Press, 1922–1924. Reprint. New Delhi: Munshiram Manoharlal, 1982.

### Formatting and Editorial Notes



*   YDh _mūla_ (root-text): **BOLD**
*   Names of authors and texts: RED
*   Citations from other texts: BLUE
*   Pūrvapakṣa and Uttarapakṣa: <span style="text-decoration:underline;">underlined</span>
*   Introductory comments that precede the _mūla _verses are given in _italics_.

## text

 **ācārādhyāyaḥ**

 

 

                    	yo bibharti namas tasmai candrasya kalayaḥ kalām |

                    	gaurīgaṇḍasthalajyotsnāniṣpandagalitām iva ||1||

                    	prasaktacintyadyutimaṇḍalātmasāmargyajurbhis tapanāt tapobhiḥ |

                    	jayaty asau yena vidhātṛdhāmno yajūṃṣi śuklāni samāhṛtāni ||2||

                    	suśliṣṭavedamūlaḥ pāvanaśākho mahādhvaraskandhaḥ |

                    	hāritrivargakusumo mokṣaphalo jayati vidhyarthaḥ ||3||

                    	māyābhir indraṃ pururūpam ekaṃ jāgarti yat suptam apīty avaiti |

                    	dūraṅgamaṃ dyotanavad dyutīnāṃ tan me manaḥ śivasaṅkalpam astu ||4||

                    	praṇamyārkaṃ mahānāgaṃ tilakasvāminaṃ tathā |

                    	vināyakaṃ sadgobhiḥ smṛtir uddyotyate mayā || 5 ||

 

 

yogīśvaram ityādi yājñavalkīyam idaṃ dharmaśāstraṃ vyācikhyāsayā prastūyate, abhyudayahetutvāt taddhetau ca vastuni mahāprayojanatvād vyākhyānādiprayāsasya | tathā cāmnāyaḥ: "priye svādhyāyapravacane bhavataḥ | yuktamanā bhavati | aparādhīno 'har ahar arthān sādhayate | sukhaṃ svapiti | paramacikitsakaś cātmano bhavati | indriyasaṃyamaś ca, ekāgratā, prajñāvṛddhiḥ, yaśo, lokapaktiḥ" ityādi (ŚB 11.5.7) | pravacanagrahaṇaṃ cātra granthakaraṇādāv apy upalakṣaṇārthaṃ draṣṭavyam | kathaṃ punar abhyudayaḥ śāstrasya ity ādita eva prapañcanīyaṃ, śāstraprayojanatvāt, sarvatraiva hi śāstrārambhe prayojanaṃ vācyam iti sthiteḥ | tathā cāha |

                    	sarvasyaiva hi śāstrasya karmaṇo vāpi kasyacit |

                    	yāvat prayojanaṃ noktaṃ tāvat tat kena gṛhyate || iti | (ŚVār 1.12)

yady api viṣayaprayojanasaṃbandhābhidhānam apeśalam iva manyante, alpaprayojanatvād durupapādatvāc ca | tathāpi kiṃcit sauhṛdād diṅmātraṃ pradarśyate | tatra ca,

                    	viṣayaḥ ślokanirdiṣṭo dharmākhyaś ca prayojanam |

                    	tadādikaś caturvargaḥ saṃbandho niyamātmakaḥ ||

viṣayas tāvac chlokanirdeśād "brūhi dharmān" iti, samākhyānāc ca dharmaḥ | prayojanaṃ tu dharmārthakāmāpavargāḥ | tathārthalakṣaṇatvād adharmo 'pi viṣayaḥ | tadanusāriṇaś cādharmānarthaduḥkhabandhāḥ prayojanam | so 'yaṃ heyopādeyalakṣaṇatvenābhyudayātmako 'ṣṭavargo 'smād eva śāstrād avagamyata iti niyamaḥ saṃbandhaḥ | yady api cārthakāmau pratyakṣāvaseyau, tathāpi na śāstrānapekṣāṇām āñjasyena tadavāptiḥ, āñjasyena ca prayojanatvam | tasmād anavadyam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kathaṃ</span> punar ekasyaiva dharmasya viṣayaprayojanatve bhavataḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">naiṣa</span> doṣaḥ, avagamyamānasya viṣayatvād avagatasya ca prayojanatvāt | na hi śāstraviṣayatām avagamyamānatayāpratipadyamānaḥ prayojanībhavati | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evaṃ saty arthakāmāpavargāḥ śāstrasyāviṣayatvāt prayojanaṃ na syuḥ | viṣayatvam api bhaviṣyatīti cen na, anirdeśāt | dharmapadasyopalakṣaṇārthatvān nirdiṣṭā eveti cen na, tasya śrautatvenaivopapatteḥ | arthādīnāṃ vā prayojanatvaṃ hātavyam, aviṣayate 'pi vā tad anumantavyam iti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">atrocyate</span> | dvividhaṃ hi kriyāṇāṃ prayojanaṃ kārakādhāram akārakādhāraṃ ca | tatra yat kārakādhāraṃ, na tad viṣayatām apratipadya prayojanībhavati | na ca tatra vairūpyād aviṣayateti śakyaṃ vaktum |

                    	yathā viklidyamānatve viklinnatve ca taṇḍulāḥ |

                    	dharmyabhedān an gacchanti nānārūpye 'pi bhinnatām ||

yady apy odanarūpatā viklidyamāneṣu taṇḍuleṣu nāsti, tathāpi taṇḍulatvānapāyād viṣayatvopapatter adoṣaḥ | akārakādhāraṃ punar viṣayatām apratipadyaiva prayojanībhavati | yathā svargo yāgasya, yathā ca vetanalābhādayaḥ pacyādīnām | odanavac ca dharmasya viṣayaprayojanatve, vetanalābhavac ca kevalaprayojanatvam arthādīnām | ato 'virodhaḥ | atha vā, asty arthādīnām api śāstraviṣayatvam | evaṃ hi vakṣyati:

                    	dharmam arthaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca yathāśakti na hāpayet | iti | (YDh 1.114)

                    	tasmāt striyaḥ sevyāḥ | (YDh 1.77)

                    	īśvaraṃ cādhigaccheta yogakṣemārthasiddhaye | iti | YDh 1.99)

tathā,

                    	paśyed ātmānam akṣayyam | (?)

ityādi | yat tv anirdiṣṭatvād iti, tad dharmapadasyopalakṣaṇārthatvena pratyuktam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kathaṃ</span> punaḥ śrautatve saṃbhavaty upalakṣaṇatvam | na hy upasaṃhārānusāry upakramo bhavati | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | naiva vayam upasaṃhārānusāriṇam upakramaṃ brūmaḥ | kiṃ tarhi | upakramād evaitad avagamyate, yogīśvaram iti viśeṣaṇāt | caturvargajñānāyaiva hi tadviśeṣaṇam yataḥ | mukhyatvāt tu dharmasya dharmān ity uktam | tasmāt siddham arthādīnām api viṣayaprayojanatvam | etenetaraś caturvargo vyākhyātaḥ |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">kathaṃ</span> punar asmād eva śāstrād ayam aṣṭavargo 'vagamyata iti niyamasyopapattiḥ | yadā hi vedād eva sarvam idam avagamyate | athāsmād apy avagamyata ity ucyeta, tathāpi niyamo 'nupapannaḥ | arthakāmayoḥ punaḥ pramāṇāntaragamyataiva | yat tv āñjasyaṃ śāstrād iti, tad apy ayuktam | na hi paradārābhigamajanitaḥ kāmo mithyeti śakyaṃ vaktum | duḥkhahetutayā vānandarūpaṃ kaivalkyam ālocayato bandhātmakatvād dharmo 'py apuruṣārthaḥ syāt |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">naitat sāram</span> | nāsmābhir anubhavanam aphnūyate | duḥkhanimittatvāt tv apuruṣārthatvam uktam | na hi duḥkhānubandhinam arthaṃ kṛtadhiyaḥ prārthayante | na cābuddhipūrvakṛd vyavahāro vicāryaḥ | tenocyate: "śāstrād ānandāvagateḥ śāstrīyāv arthakāmau" iti | śāstrānusāriṇaś ca dharmārthakāmāḥ prārthyamānatvād duḥkhānanubandhitvāc cāñjasyena puruṣārthāḥ | yathā ca nāpavargapratibandhikās tathāpavarganirūpaṇe vakṣyāmaḥ | na caivaṃ sati pramāṇāntarāvagatir virodhinī | yat tu vedād avagater niyamānupapattir iti, tad vedamūlatayaivāsya śāstrasya niyamyamānatvād acodyam | pramāṇāntarāpekṣayā hi vyāvṛttiḥ, na vedāpekṣayā, tadadhīnatvāt smṛtiśāstrasya | tathā ca svāyaṃbhuvam: 

                    	dharmaṃ jijñāsamānānāṃ pramāṇaṃ paramaṃ śrutiḥ | iti | (MDh 2.13)

dharmaśabdaś ca bhagavato 'pi caturvargopalakṣaṇārthaḥ | so 'yam veda eva pratyakṣaparokṣatayā śrutismṛtiśabdavācyaḥ | ataḥ suṣṭhūcyate 'smād eva śāstrād ayam aṣṭavargāvagateḥ samasto 'bhyudayaḥ prāpyata ity alaṃ prasaṅgena ||

 

_kasmāt punar vedasiddha evārthe bhagavataḥ śāstrārambhaprayatnaḥ | yasmāt,_

 

**              	yogīśvaraṃ yājñavalkyaṃ saṃpūjya munayo 'bruvan |**

**              	varṇāśrametareṣāṃ no brūhi dharmān aśeṣataḥ || 1.1 ||**

 

vedārthatattvavido 'pi munayo yasmāt saṃpūjyopetyārthitayābruvan, tatas tadanurodhād bhagavato 'yaṃ prayatna iti mantavyam | yuktaṃ caitat, tādṛśānām adhyāpyatvāt | tathā cāha manuḥ |

                    	ācāryaputraḥ śuśrūṣur jñānado dhārmikaḥ śuciḥ |

                    	śakto 'rthado 'rthī svaḥ sādhur adhyāpyā daśa dharmataḥ || iti | (MDh 2.109)

te tu punaḥ kasmād eva prayatnenābruvan | yogīśvaraṃ manyamānā yājñavalkyatayāpi ca mahābhijanatvād adhyāpanārham | tathā cāpastambaḥ: "tasmād vidyābhijanasamudetaṃ saṃskartāram īpset" iti (ĀpDh 1.1.2) | yuktaṃ ca guṇātiśayavati yājñavalkye munīnāṃ praśnakaraṇam, jñātasatattvānām api kadācit saṃśayotpatteḥ | tathā ca vyāsaḥ:

                    	jñātavedārthatattvena dharmān apy anutiṣṭhatā |

                    	asaṃśayāya kartavyaḥ kiyāṃś cid gurusaṃnidhiḥ || iti |

atha vā mandakhyātiyuktā jñānino 'py ativikhyātaṃ kañcic chiṣyabhāvenānugamyātmānaṃ prakhyāpayituṃ pṛcchanty eva | kinnimittā vāsyeyaṃ yogīśvaratvakhyātir iti jijñāsavaḥ | sarvathā ca praśnopapatter upasannānāṃ ca niyogato 'dhyāpyatvād anupālambhaḥ | tathā coktam: "upasannāya tu nirbrūyad" iti | kiṃ punar abruvan | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span>: arthakāmāpavargās tarhy apṛṣṭatvāc chāstrasyāviṣayāḥ | kiṃ ca ekatvād dharmasya dharmān iti bahuvacanam ayuktam eva | na ca dharmabhedopasaṃgrahārthaṃ tad iti yuktam, aśeṣata iti padāntarānarthakyaprasaṅgāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">naiṣa doṣaḥ</span>, dharmapadasyopalakṣaṇārthatvenoktatvāt | na hy anyathā yogīśvarapadopapattiḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">atha</span> stuthyarthaṃ tad ity ucyeta | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">tad apy asat</span> | na hi kāryānvayinaḥ stutimātratā yuktā | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">astu</span> nāma kāryānvayaḥ | tathāpy upalakṣaṇatvaṃ katham iti vaktavyam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">tad ucyate</span> | yogīśvaraṃ manyamānā dharmaṃ pṛcchantīty asaṃbaddham iva syāt | yasmād yogino hi dharmavidaḥ | teṣām ācāryatveneśvaro brahmavittamaḥ | sa ca brahmaiva praṣṭavyaḥ, na dharmam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca dharmajño 'pi paramārthato yogīśvara eva | arthakāmau vā sa kiṃ na jānāti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">na brūmo</span> na jānātīti | dharmajñavivakṣayātra yogīśvarābhidhānam | naitad yuktam | nopakramasya yogīśvarapadaṃ tadadhīnātmalābhopasaṃhārasthena dharmapadena virudhyamānaṃ viśeṣe 'vasthāpayituṃ śakyam | na caivaṃ sati kevalāpavargaviṣaya eva praśna ity avaseyaṃ, sarvajñatvād yogīśvarasya, dharmān iti ca bahuvacanopapatteḥ | kiṃ ca kevaladharmapraśne 'pavargamātrapraśne vā kṛtsnaṃ śāstram asamañjasaṃ syāt, caturṇām vakṣyamāṇatvāt | bhūyasāṃ caivam anugraho bhavati | mukhyāv api ca yogīśvaradharmaśabdāv anyonyāpāditavirodhavyāhatasāmarthyau durbalād eva | mahāviṣayatā caivaṃ śāstrasyety alaṃ prasaṅgena |

        	tam evaṃvidhaṃ yogīśvaraṃ manyamānā yājñavalkyam abruvan | yajñavalkyo brahmā iti paurāṇikāḥ | tadapatyaṃ yājñavalkyaḥ | kathaṃ kṛtvābruvan | saṃpūjya | pūjā cātropasadanādilakṣaṇā vijñeyā, sam ity upasargasya samyagarthatvāt | munayo vedārthatvavidaḥ | varṇāśrametareṣāṃ no brūhi dharmān aśeṣata ity abruvann iti saṃbandhaḥ | varṇā brāhmaṇādayaḥ | āśramā brahmacāryādayaḥ | varṇetarā antaraprabhavā anulomādayaḥ | āśrametarāḥ pāṣaṇḍādayaḥ | teṣāṃ varṇāśrametareṣām | samagrābhyudayātmakāṣṭavargapratipādakaṃ śāstraṃ no brūhīti ślokārthaḥ | dharmādīnāṃ vaktum aśakyatvād evam abhidhīyate | brūhīti cādhyeṣaṇeyam, ācāryatvād bhagavataḥ | aśeṣata iti | kārtsnyenety arthaḥ | vedād iti cādhyāhāryam | veda eva vānanyaśeṣatvād aśeṣa ity ucyate | tasmād aśeṣato 'nugrahārtham asmākaṃ dharmān brūhīti | anyaḥ pāṭhaḥ: "varṇānāṃ sāśramāṇām" iti | atrāpi sa evārthaḥ | antarajā apy anulomā varṇā eva | yathāha manuḥ |

                    	putrā ye 'nantarastrījāḥ krameṇoktā dvijanmanām |

                    	tān anantaranāmnas tu mātṛdoṣāt pracakṣate || iti |

anantaragrahaṇaṃ caikāntaradvyantarārtham api draṣṭavyam | kramānantaryavacanāc ca pratilomānām avarṇatvam | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "pratilomāt tu dharmahīnaḥ" (GDh 4.25) ity avarṇavivakṣayaivāha | jātūkarṇaś cāha: "pratilomās tv antāvasāyinaḥ" iti | yat tu kiṃcit tadgatadharmābhidhānaṃ, tad ānuṣaṅgikaviṣayam | prayojakaviṣayas tu praśnaḥ | pāṣaṇḍināṃ tv āśramapratipattyartho dharma ity āśramaśabdena grahaṇam | evaṃ ca pāṭhāntarāṇy api vyākhyeyāni | yad vā varṇāśrametareṣāṃ na iti saṃbandhaḥ | varṇāśrametarā eva hi tāvad vayaṃ, yāvad anirṇīto dharmaḥ | tenāsmākaṃ nirṇayāya brūhīti || 1 ||

 

_kim anabhigamyaiva munibhir yogīndraḥ pṛṣṭaḥ | nety ucyate |_

 

**              	mithilāsthaḥ sa yogīndraḥ samyag dhyātvābravīn munīn |**

**              	yasmin deśe mṛgaḥ kṛṣṇas tasmin dharmān nibodhata || 1.2 ||**

 

na hi mithilāsthaṃ yogīndram anabhigamyaiva munayaḥ praṣṭuṃ kṣamāḥ | mithilāsthatvavacanāc ca yogīndrasya munīnāṃ deśāntarasthatvaṃ siddham | anyathā viśeṣaṇam eva na syāt | yuktaś cābhigamaiva śreyasi praśnaḥ | tathā ca "abhigamya maharṣayaḥ" (MDh 1.1) iti mānavam | jātūkarṇo 'py āha: "nākasmāt samavāye guruṃ pṛcchet" iti | atha sa taiḥ pṛṣṭaḥ kim kṛtavān | "samyag dhyātvābravīn munīn" | praśnaviśeṣaṇaṃ vā samyag iti | dhyātvā nirūpya munīnāṃ yogyatādikam | anye "kṣaṇaṃ dhyātvā" iti paṭhanti | teṣāṃ kālavivakṣā | kṣaṇenaiveyān mahāgahanaḥ śāstrārtho 'nudhyātaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nūnam</span> ayaṃ yogīndraḥ syāt | vailakṣaṇyapradarśanārthaṃ vācāryasya | adhyāpanaprakāraniyamo vā | kiṃ punas tad abravīt | "yasmin deśe mṛgaḥ kṛṣṇas tasmin dharmān nibodhata" iti | bahuvacanam uktārtham | ye tu "dharmam" iti paṭhanti, teṣāṃ mukhyatvaṃ dharmasyety abhiprāyaḥ | nibodhateti śiṣyabuddhisamādhānārtham | prasaktasyāpi dharmasya punar vacanaṃ kṛṣṇopalakṣitadeśasaṃbandhārtham | kathaṃ yogīndra evaivaṃ brūyāt "yogīśvara yājñavalkya", "mithilāsthaḥ sa yogīndraḥ" iti ca | nāpy anyaḥ karteti śakyaṃ vaktum, "ślokatrayam api hy asmāt" (YDh 3.334) iti vakṣyamāṇatvād granthakartāpi bhagavān eveti gamyate | naivānyakṛtatvaṃ dharmaśāstrasyeti brūmaḥ | kim tu bhagavataiva parokṣīkṛtyātmā nirdiśyate, svapraśaṃsāniṣedhāt | yadi hi "māṃ yogīśvaram" "ahaṃ yogiśvaraḥ" iti brūyāt, tadātmastutir āpadyeta | vaktavyaṃ vaitad ātmapravṛttiprayojanakathanāya | ato vācyatvād ātmastavakarṇāyogāc ca parokṣatayābhidhānān nāyam upālambhaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> etad "yasmin deśe mṛgaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ" iti pradhānaṃ prayogam anabhidhāyaiva bāhyataradeśābhidhānam ayuktam | kiṃ ca brahmāvartāder aṅgatvam apy abhipretam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">athāyam</span> abhiprāyaḥ: ataḥ param ayajñiyo deśa iti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">tad apy asat</span> | "sūryasyodayanaṃ puraḥ" (BDh 1.2.12) ity anena kṛṣṇarahitadeśānām api prāśastyadarśanāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">mūrkha sādhv etat</span> | bahiraṅgatve 'pi deśasyādhikārāśrayatvena prādhānyād vakṣyamāṇākhilārthopayogitvāc ca sarvādāv adbhidhānam | anyathā hy ekakarmārthatāpi saṃnidher āśaṅkyeta | na ca naiyāmikaḥ kramādra iti cācāryābhiprāyaḥ | brahmāvartādyanabhidhānaṃ tu viśiṣṭaphalatvāt teṣām | na tu ta eva dharmyāḥ | ayaṃ tu nityatayā karmaṇām aṅgam, yajñiyatvenaiva dharmaniyamāt | tathā cāmnāyaḥ: "yajño hi kṛṣṇaḥ, sa kṛṣṇamṛgo bhūtvā pṛthivīm anvacarat | tam anu dharmaś cacāra" ityādi | śvetāśvatarāś ca: "sa kṛṣṇamṛgo 'bhavat | sa kṛṣṇamṛgo bhūtvā pṛthivīm anvacarat | tam anu dharmaś cacāra" ityādi | na ca tadrahitānāṃ dharmyatvam | evaṃ hi bhāllavināṃ gāthā: "yataḥ paścāt sindhur viharaṇī sūryasyodayaṃ puraḥ" iti (cf. VaDh 1.14–15) | vicchidyāyuḥ puṃsāṃ haratīti viharaṇo 'stamayakālaḥ | so 'sminn iti vaharaṇī | sindhuḥ samudraḥ parvato vā, ubhayatra syandanāviśeṣāt | ṛjv anyat | evam udayāstamayopalakṣitāyāṃ pṛthivyāṃ yāvat kṛṣṇo vicarati, tāvad brahmavarcasam iti | tāvad evety arthaḥ | yāvad vety api pāṭhe vāśabdo 'vadhāraṇārtho na vikalpārthaḥ | tathā ca śaṅkhaḥ: "deśa āryo guṇavān prāgastād arvāg udayāt" ity ārabhya "puṇyaḥ kṛṣṇo vā yāvad vicarati, tāvad ācāraḥ syāt" iti | ayam api vāśabdo 'vadhāraṇārtha eva | tathā cāha manuḥ:

                    	sa jñeyo yajñiyo deśo mlecchadeśas tv ataḥ paraḥ | iti | (MDh 2.23)

āmnāyaś ca: "taṃ devāḥ samājahruḥ | taṃ dharmo 'nvāgacchat | yajñaṃ hy any dharmaḥ" iti śvetāśvararīyaḥ kṛṣṇānuyāyitvaṃ hiśabdena dharmasyānuvadaṃs tadvān eva deśo dharmya iti darśayati | ataḥ sūktam: "yasmin deśe mṛgaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ" iti | utpadyata it cādhyāhāryaṃ, śrutismṛtyantarānusārāt | brahmāvartāder api dharma(mya)tvaṃ nityatayā śrutismṛtyanusārāt kṛṣṇopalakṣitatvenaiva, tādātmyena tu phalaviśeṣahetutvam ity alaṃ prasaṅgena || 2 ||

 

_yady api na munibhir vedād eva dharmān brūhīty uktaḥ, tathāpi na mantrabrāhmaṇalakṣaṇād vedād dharmāvagatiḥ, kiṃ tarhi |_

 

                    	**purāṇanyāyamīmāṃsādharmaśāstrāṅgamiśritāḥ |**

**              	vedāḥ sthānāni vidyānāṃ dharmasya tu caturdaśa || 1.3 ||**

 

purāṇādīnāṃ dharmopayogitvaṃ prasiddham | nyāyamīmāṃseti caikaṃ vidyāsthānam | purāṇam iti cetihāsapurāṇayor grahaṇam | dharmaśāśtraṃ smṛtiḥ | aṅgāni ṣaṭ śīkṣādīni | vedāś catvāraḥ | evaṃ caturdaśa | anye tu nyāyam ākṣapādādikaṃ varṇayanti | tanmatenetihāsapurāṇayor aikyam | miśraṇatvavacanāc ca vedopakaraṇatvena purāṇādīnāṃ vedasvātantryam abhihitam | vidyānāṃ dharmasyeti dve ṣaṣṭhyau vidyāśabdasya dharmaparyāyānvayakathanārthe | caturdaśeti śākyādigranthavyāvṛttyartham | tuśabdo 'vadhāraṇārthaḥ | caturdaśaiva, nābhyadhikānīty arthaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evaṃ saty aśeṣasmṛtyātmakam ekaṃ dharmaśāstram, anyathā saṅkhyāyogāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">naiṣa doṣaḥ</span>, pratismaraṇāvasāyitve 'pi dharmaśāstrasya samudāyālambanatvenaikavacanopapatteḥ, vanavat || 3 ||

 

_abheda eva siddha iti cet, nety āha |_

 

                    	**vaktāro dharmaśāstrāṇāṃ manur viṣṇur yamo 'ṅgirāḥ |**

**              	vasiṣṭhadakṣasaṃvartaśātātapaparāśarāḥ || 1.4 ||**

**              	āpastambośanovyāsāḥ kātyāyanabṛhaspatī |**

**              	gautamaḥ śaṅkhalikhitau hārīto 'trir ahaṃ tathā || 1.5 ||**

 

vaktāra iti pramāṇāntarapūrvakatābhiprāyam | vedād avagamya vaktāro vayaṃ, na svayaṃ draṣṭāra ity arthaḥ | dharmaśāstrāṇām iti bahuvacanaṃ bhedakathanārtham | "manur viṣṇur" iti khyātatamair nāmabhiḥ sāmarthyakathanārtham | "aham" ity antata ātmabhidhānam ācāraparipālanārtham | "tathā" iti cānuktopasaṃgrahārtham | tathā ca vṛddhayājñavalkyo dharmapravaktṝn uktvāha |

                    	bhūyāṃso dharmavaktāra utpannā bhāvinas tathā |

                    	nidhānaṃ sarvadharmāṇāṃ veda eva hi śāśvataḥ || iti |

punaś cāha |

                    	nāradaḥ pulaho gārgyaḥ pulastyaḥ śaunakaḥ kratuḥ |

                    	baudhāyano jātukarṇo viśvāmitraḥ pitāmahaḥ || iti |

mananān manuḥ | vividhajñānena snātaḥ śuddho veṣṭito vā viṣṇuḥ | yamanād dharmasya prajānāṃ vā yamaḥ | ityādi sarvatra yojyaṃ stutyatiśayārtham |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">kiṃ punar</span> asyāḥ smṛter mūlam | na tāvad āmnāyo dharmaśāstrabhedapratipādakaḥ | na ca tatprabhavo nyāyaḥ | api tu śrautānāṃ kṛtsnopasaṃhārāt tatpūrvakatvāc ca tathaivātrāpi prāpnoti | kārtsnyena caivaṃ dharmāvagatiḥ, na hy ekasmṛtyadhyayane sakaladharmāvāptir yataḥ | bhede ca dvayor apy adhyayanaṃ na syāt, śākhāntaravat | iṣyate ca tat, "smṛtidroṇapāṭhakaḥ" iti vacanāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">naitad evam</span> | na hi paraṃparāpekṣaṃ manvādīnāṃ dharmābhidhānam, sarvatra kārtsnyābhidhānāt | itarathā hi kvacid eva padārthābhidhānaṃ syāt, anyatra guṇavidhayaḥ | kvacic ca sāpekṣatvaṃ dṛśyate, vacanāt | tad yathā:

                    	āmnāyāt samyag uddhṛtya śaṅkhaś ca likhitas tathā | iti |

na cānumeyeṣv artheṣv aikyaṃ śakyate vaktum, liṅgānusāreṇa liṅgino 'pi bhedāvagateḥ | bhinnāni cāṣṭakādiliṅgāni pratiśākhaṃ, tathaivopalabdheḥ | tathā ca smaraṇaṃ bhedena | anyathā hy ekarūpa eva prayogaḥ smaryeta | yat tu śākhāntaravad upasaharaṇam uktaṃ, tac chrautakarmaṇāṃ pratyakṣatvena prakaraṇābhedād yuktam | iha tu pradhāne bhedo 'bhihito liṅgabhedāt | ato vaiṣamyam | yāni tu nāmato guṇavidhānāni tāny aviśeṣād atrāpi samuccīyanta eva | yathā śātātapaḥ śrāddham anuktvaiva tadgatān guṇān āha:

                    	vinā yajñopavītena gandhar yas tu samālabhet |

ityādi | sarvārthatā ca kathaṃ syād iti guṇārthasmṛtyārambhaḥ | yat tu smṛtidroṇādhyayanaṃ tan nānātve 'pi bahvaṅgaprayogakaraṇe phalabhūyastvalābhārtham adhikaguṇopasaṃhārārthaṃ ca | droṇavacanāt tu niyamādṛṣṭaṃ vratādhyayanavad bhūyastvavivakṣayā vā droṇaśabda ity avaseyam | yat tu "naikatra kārtsnyaṃ dharmasya" iti, tad vaitānikānekakarmakalāpānabhidhānāt~~ ~~kārtsnye 'pi naiva | akhilaparokṣārthāśrayitvena kārtsnyam iti cet, tad api karṇavedhādyanupasaṃhṛter asiddham | ācāraprāmāṇyābhidhānāt tadupasaṃhṛtam iti cet, vedo dharmamūlam ity anenaiva siddhatvān namaḥ śāstrāya | dharmapravaktṛsaṅkhyāniyamānavadhāraṇāc ca sāpekṣatvena sarvasmin dharmaśāstre samāptiḥ syāt | tataś cānanuṣṭhānam | na ca saṅkhyāvadhāraṇam asti, parigaṇanasya pradarśanārthatvāt, hetvantarasya cābhāvād ity eṣā dik |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca prayogabhede 'pi guṇārthasmṛtyantarāpekṣāṇāṃ tadavastham evānanuṣṭhānam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span> | yadi paripūrṇe 'pi prayoge 'bhyudayāya guṇāntaropasaṃhāraḥ, nityavat karaṇaṃ tv anupasaṃhṛtair apy upapannam ity avirodhaḥ | yad vāstu niyogatas tadupasaṃhāraḥ | sati tu jñāne jñātaguṇāntaratyāge naikasmṛtyavagataprayogānuṣṭhānad eva kṛtakṛtyatā | avagataś ca prayogo 'nuṣṭheyaḥ | guṇāntarāṇi cānveṣyāṇi | upalabdhaguṇānupasaṃhārāc ca pratyavāyaḥ | sāpekṣatve tu smṛtīnāṃ prāk prayogāvadhṛter anuṣṭhātum aśakyatvād avadhāraṇopāyāsaṃbhavāc cānanuṣṭhānam iti vaiṣamyam | paripūrṇe tu prayoge naimittikāṅgānvayo 'bhimataḥ | "bhinne juhoti" itivat | jñānagatam api ca guṇānāṃ naimittikatvam dṛṣṭam | tad yathā: vaiśvānaragrahagrahaṇe "sa yadi carakebhyo vā patato 'nubruvīta" iti (ŚB 4.2.4.1) | evam atrāpi | yady apramādyadbhir anviṣyamāṇaṃ guṇāntaram upalabhyeta, tata upasaṃhriyeta | anupalabdhau tv adoṣaḥ | yadā cānviṣyamāṇasya yasyopalabdhiḥ tadā tasyānupasaṃhāre pratyavāyād avyāhatam anuṣṭhānam | yatra tv aparipūṛṇaḥ prayogaḥ kartavyatopadeśamātraṃ ca yathopanayanādiṣu, tatrānumitaiva smṛtyantarāpekṣā | yathā ca mṛdbhir iti mṛdāṃ bahutve 'vagate tisraḥ pañca veti smṛtyantarāt | evaṃ sarvatronneyam | smaraṇavaicitryam evāsyāḥ kalpanāyāḥ pramāṇam iti na hetvantaraṃ mṛgyam | prayogaikye tūktānupapattiḥ | ataḥ sūktaṃ "vaktāro dharmaśāstrāṇām" iti smṛtibahutvam || 4–5 ||

 

_uktaṃ dharmādayaḥ śāstrasya viṣayā iti | teṣāṃ tu lakṣaṇaṃ vācyam ity ata āha |_

 

**              	deśe kāla upāyena dravyaṃ śraddhāsamanvitaiḥ |**

**              	pātre pradīyate yat tat sakalaṃ dharmalakṣaṇam || 1.6 ||**

 

deśaḥ sāmānyaviśeṣātmakatvena dvividhaḥ | sāmānyataḥ kṛṣṇopalakṣitaḥ | viśeṣataḥ śuddhādikaḥ | kālo 'py ahaḥpūrvāhṇādikaḥ | upāyas tv aṅgakalāpo dṛṣṭādṛṣṭārthaḥ | yathā: "abhigamyopaviśya hiraṇyaṃ dadyāt" iti | deśakālayos tūpāyatve 'py adhikārānvayād bhedenopanyāsaḥ | dravyasya ca prādhānyāt | dravyaṃ śuklaṃ hiraṇyam ityādi | śraddhā prasiddhaiva | saṃśabdaḥ samyagarthe | anvitair yuktair ity arthaḥ | pātraṃ jātisaṃskāravidyāvṛttatapobhiḥ saṃpannam | evaṃ yad dānaṃ, so 'navadyaḥ kṛtsno dharma iti | dānaśabdaś cāyaṃ yāgādyaśeṣavihitakṛtyopalakṣaṇārtho draṣṭavyaḥ | viparītaś cādharmaḥ | yat tu dānam evodāhṛtaṃ, tat sārvavarṇikādhikārapratipādanārtham | kurukṣetragrahoparāgādayas tu kāmyanaimittikatayāvaseyāḥ | tathā ca śaṅkhaḥ: "tatra dharmalakṣaṇāni | deśaḥ kāla upāyo dravyaṃ śraddhā pātraṃ tyāga iti samayaḥ | teṣu dharmodayaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ, anyathā viparītaḥ" iti | deśādyabhāve "viparītaḥ" iti vadan nityānīmānīti darśayati | na ca kurukṣetrādīnāṃ nityatvopapattiḥ, anyatra nivāsābhāvaprasaṅgāt | na caitad yuktam | ataḥ sūktaṃ kāmyanaimittikatvam evamādīnām iti || 6 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> iyaṃ dharmalakṣaṇāvadhṛtir nirmūleva lakṣyate | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">āmnāyānabhijña, maivam</span> |_

 

**              	vedaḥ smṛtiḥ sadācāraḥ svasya ca priyam ātmanaḥ |**

**              	samyaksaṅkalpajaḥ kāmo dharmamūlam idaṃ smṛtam || 1.7 ||**

 

yadi hi smṛtyādayo vedānapekṣā dharmamūlam ity ucyeran, tadā nirmūlatā syāt | yadā tv eṣām api vedāvinirbhāgaḥ, tadā nirmūlavacanaṃ pralāpaḥ | vedapūrvakatayā caiṣāṃ prāmāṇyam | ataḥ suṣṭhūcyate "dharmamūlam idaṃ smṛtam" iti | yathā cāha manuḥ: "smṛtiśīle ca tadvidām" iti | vedasmṛtī prasiddhe | akāmātmāno dambhādirahitā vedārthavido 'nuṣṭhātaraś ca santaḥ, teṣāṃ yad adṛṣṭāyācaraṇaṃ sa sadācāraḥ | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ: "śiṣṭaḥ punar akāmātmā, agṛhyamāṇakāraṇo dharmaḥ" iti | anupanibandhanāc ca smṛtito brāhmaṇaparivrājakavad bhedenopanyāsaḥ | anupanibandhaṃ tu smṛtyantarārthavat | vedāvirodhy asāhasaṃ svasyātmanaḥ priyaṃ, yathāvasīdati kuṭumbe saṃnyāsaḥ | vicikitsāśaṅkayā tu smṛtyācārayor bhedenopanyāsaḥ | yathaitad evaṃ tathā tadāśramanirūpaṇe vakṣyāmaḥ | anātmadruhā prītyutpādaḥ samyaksaṅkalpajaḥ kāmaḥ | yathā vaikalpikayor anyatarāvadhāraṇam | icchayā tu pravṛtteḥ pauruṣeyāśaṅkā mā bhūd iti bhedenopanyāsaḥ | ṛjv anyat |

        	pratyekaviśeṣaṇaṃ vā samyag iti | vedasya samyaktvaṃ vākyavivekāvadhṛtiḥ, tanmūlatvaniyamoparasmṛteḥ | yad vā svasya ceti kuladharmaḥ pitrādyācāro 'bhipretaḥ | satām a(dṛ?ri)ṣṭhāya cety atrāpi yojyam | tathā cāhuḥ |

                    	yenāsya pitaro yātā yena yātāḥ pitāmahāḥ |

                    	tena yāyāt satāṃ mārgaṃ tena gacchan na riṣyati || iti | (MDh 4.178)

priyaṃ tv ātmana ātmatuṣṭiḥ | tad api dharmamūlam | kiṃ punar ātmanaḥ priyaṃ, samyaksaṅkalpajaḥ kāmaḥ | kasyacit tv āptābhihitamātreṇa tatvāvadhṛtiḥ syād, anyasya mūlapramāṇapratipattyā | yāvad asya nirvicikitsaṃ samyaksaṅkalpajaḥ kāmaḥ syāt, tadā tasyātmanaḥ priyaṃ dharmamūlatayāvaseyam | vicitradhiyām api puṃsāṃ samyaksaṅkalpajatvenecchāniyamād anavadyam | samānam anyat |

        	atha vā svasya ca priyam ātmana ity apavargalakṣaṇam | samyagityādy arthakāmayoḥ | dharmasya tūktam | tad etat sarvaṃ smṛtiśāstreṇa pratipādyate | tac ca vedamūlatvād veda evety abhipretyocyate: "dharmamūlam idaṃ smṛtam" iti | nyāyamūlatvāc ca ślokasyānekārthatvam adoṣaḥ |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">kutaḥ</span> punar idam āmnāyamūlatvaṃ smṛter avagamitam | na tāvat sarvasmṛtīnāṃ mūlabhūtavedavākyopalabdhiḥ | katipayavākyadarśanaṃ tv asadāgameṣv apy aviśiṣṭam | na ca vedaḥ svayaṃ mūlatām alaṃ pratipādayitum | anumānādes tv asāmarthyam atiprasiddham | viparyaye vā tatpravṛttiḥ, sarvātmakavedamūlatvānupapatteḥ | na tāvad vidhirūpaḥ, adarśanāt smṛtyānarthakyāc ca | tathā hi |

                    	pratyakṣe vidhirūpe ca vede sati mudhā smṛtiḥ |

                    	kalpakārās tadā kuryur laghutāyai prakalpanam ||

                    	vākyānāṃ viprakīrṇānāṃ smṛtiḥ saṃgrahaṇāya cet |

                    	tad asat smārtatā mā bhūt tādrūpyāj jyotiṣo 'pi hi ||

                    	saṃhārād ekaśākhātve 'py ādimadhyāntavartinām |

                    	śākhāntaragatānāṃ ca samāhāraḥ pravargyavat ||

                    	maivaṃ na jyotiṣā tulyaṃ viprakīrṇatvam atra naḥ |

                    	itikartavyatā tadvat kḷptā na hy asti saṃnidhau ||

                    	ekaikaśaḥ prakīrṇāṅgapradhānaikadhyasaṃhṛteḥ |

                    	jyotiṣṭomāditulyatvaṃ smṛtīnām atidurbhaṇam ||

                    	śākhānāṃ viprakīrṇatvāt puruṣāṇāṃ pramādataḥ |

                    	nānāprakaraṇasthatvāt smṛtimūlaṃ na gṛhyate ||

                    	kāryo 'taś copasaṃhāraḥ puruṣānugrahātmakaḥ |

                    	tad vedādṛśyamānatvaṃ na doṣāyātra jāyate ||

                    	smṛtimūlā hi vidhayaḥ santi vede sahasraśaḥ |

                    	saṃpradāyavināśāt tu bhītaiḥ sākṣād asaṃhṛtiḥ ||

                    	utkraṣṭavyas tu khyāto 'yaṃ malavadvāsasā saha |

                    	na saṃvased iti vidhiḥ smṛtimūlatvasaṃmataḥ ||

                    	ātreyyā yoṣitainasvī bhaved ghātayitety api |

                    	vṛttaṃ tasmād anindyasya nāpakrāmed itīti ca ||

                    	anārabhya ca sauvarṇaṃ hiraṇyaṃ bhāryam ity ayam |

                    	rūpasaṃpattaye caivaṃ bhavitavyaṃ suvāsasā ||

                    	nanv evaṃ bhinnarūpatvaṃ smṛtīnāṃ nopapadyate |

                    	upasaṃharaṇīyānām aikyāt kṛcchrādikarmaṇām ||

                    	naitad asty eva bhinnatvaṃ pratyakṣādhyayane 'pi hi |

                    	karmaṇāṃ bhedakaiḥ saṅkhyāguṇaprakaraṇāntaraiḥ ||

                    	bhinnatvāc ca pradhānānām aṅgabhedas tadāśrayaḥ |

                    	bhinnāś cāto 'dṛṣṭakādīnāṃ prayogāḥ smārtakarmaṇām ||

                    	uddiśyaikyaṃ pradhānaṃ ca viśiṣṭaguṇalakṣitam |

                    	aṅgaṃ vidhīyamānaṃ hi na sarvārthaṃ prasajyate ||

                    	sādhāraṇaṃ hi nāmaikaṃ bhaviṣyaty akṣaśabdavat |

                    	smṛtīnāṃ bhinnarūpatvam ato bhinnārthasaṃgrahāt ||

                    	ekaikaṃ cāṣṭakākarma kṛtvaiva kṛtino narāḥ |

                    	phalasāmyād bhavanty asmān naikakartrākhilagrahaḥ ||

                    	sarveṣāṃ ye nṛṇāṃ dharmāḥ sarvais te tūpasaṃhṛtāḥ |

                    	manvādibhir yamāḥ prāyo niyamāś cāviśeṣataḥ ||

                    	evaṃ ca viprakīrṇaikaśākhāśākhāntarāśrayam |

                    	dṛśyamānaṃ smṛter mūlam apahātuṃ na śakyate ||

                    	samyagālocitaṃ naitad ācāryeṇeva lakṣyate |

                    	prakīrṇavidhivākyānāṃ mūlatvānupapattitaḥ ||

                    	jīvataḥ kāmino vā syād adhikāro 'ṣṭakādiṣu |

                    	jīvataś cet tataḥ sarvaṃ kartavyaṃ sarvakartṛbhiḥ ||

                    	kartavyatvāviśeṣāt syuḥ kṛtārthā naikakarmaṇā |

                    	akṛtveṣṭiṃ hi tulyatvāt kṛtino nāgnihotriṇaḥ ||

                    	tathāstv iti yadi brūyād atādrūpyopasaṃhṛteḥ |

                    	mānavādyapramāṇatvam anuṣṭhānaṃ ca durlabham ||

                    	smartṝṇāṃ jāyate doṣo nanv akartavyasaṃgrahāt |

                    	na punar nikhilatvena kartavyānupasaṃhṛtau ||

                    	anyonyanirapekṣatvaṃ smṛtīnāṃ yac ca varṇitam |

                    	ekakriyāprayoge hi taj jñeyaṃ nākhilagrahe ||

                    	maivam ekaprayoge 'pi na vedokto 'khilagrahaḥ |

                    	anuṣṭhānavirodhas tu tulyo bhede 'pi karmaṇām ||

                    	kartur ekasya yat kāryaṃ niyogenaikakālikam |

                    	tat smārthaṃ nairapekṣyārtham ekaikatrākhilātmanām ||

                    	sarvaṃ caitat prapañcena vakṣyāmaḥ śrāddhasaṃgrahe |

                    	yathāsmṛtyapramāṇatvam uktarūpānupagrahe ||

                    	kālaikyena viruddhatvād athaikakaraṇaṃ matam |

                    	tathāpi yāvatāṃ śaktiḥ kṛtir bhavati tāvatām ||

                    	pūrvāhṇānupasaṃhārād akriyā ced guṇatvataḥ |

                    	pradhānabādhanāt tasya na yukter upasaṃhṛtiḥ ||

                    	saṃskāratvād athaikena na kuryuḥ saṃskṛtāḥ param |

                    	saṃskāratvaṃ tathā vācyaṃ sarvasmṛtyuktakarmaṇām ||

                    	kṛtvaikāṃ cāṣṭakāṃ kuryur naikagṛhyoditām api |

                    	kāminām adhikāre tu yāthākāmyād anityatā ||

                    	nityavat smaraṇaṃ tatra smartṝṇāṃ syād amūlakam |

                    	na cānyathādhikāro 'sti tasmād iyam akalpanā ||

kiṃ ca |

                    	ekaikaśaḥ prakīrṇāṅgapradhānaikadhyasaṃhṛtau |

                    	smārtatvaṃ vaikṛtānāṃ syāt pauṣṇacarvādikarmaṇām (?) ||

                    	kḷptopakārasaṃbandhāt tatra ced aprakīrṇatā |

                    	paurṇamāsavikāratvāt tadvat syād aṣṭakādy api ||

                    	na cāsti paṭhyamānatve smārtānām avikāratā |

                    	darvihomeṣv apūrvatvam uktaṃ sādṛśyahānataḥ ||

                    	anvāruhyoktam etac ca vidhivākyaprakīrṇatām |

                    	śākhāsahasramadhye 'pi na tv ekā paṭhyate 'ṣṭakā ||

                    	prakīrṇā ye tu dṛśyante nṛdharmā vidhayaḥ kvacit |

                    	niyamānāṃ yamānāṃ ca te syur mūlaṃ na karmaṇām ||

                    	pratyakṣaṃ paṭhyamānānāṃ prakīrṇatvād dhi karmaṇām |

                    	kalpakārāś ca nindyāḥ syur asāmarthyād akalpane ||

                    	mantrārthavādamūlatvaṃ smartāraḥ kīrtayanti yat |

                    	tac cāsat syād vasiṣṭhādau kathaṃ lāṅgalam udvapet ||

                    	vyākhyānataḥ śunaḥśepha ity ukteś cārthavādajāḥ |

                    	śrutyā saha virodhe ca vikalpo vidhitulyataḥ ||

                    	tatra śaṅkhavaco dussthaṃ tayoś ca jyāyasī śrutiḥ |

                    	dvitīyas tadanuvyākhyā smārto baudhāyanasya ca ||

                    	anayāyaṃ diśā pakṣaḥ prapadyaiva vivekataḥ |

                    	sarvathā pariśodhyas tu smṛtyaprāmāṇyavādibhiḥ ||

 

evaṃ tāvad viprakīrṇavidhimūlatvam anupapannam | mantrārthavādayos tv anyaparatayaivāmūlatvam | kiṃ ca mantraḥ prakaraṇe vā syād aprakaraṇe vā | prākaraṇikas tāvat parārtha eva | itaro 'py upādānaśūnyaliṅgaviniyojakatvānabhyupagamād amūlam | svādhyāyādhyayanavidher api japayajñādyupayogitvena nairākaṅkṣyād audāsīnyam | arthavādās tu ye 'nārabhya paṭhyante, teṣāṃ prāg vidhikalpanād aparyavasanāt, kalpite ca tādarthyād akāraṇatvam | atha mantrārthavādānvitapadārthasatyatopapādanārthaṃ tadanusārikālpanikavidhyantaramūlatocyeta, yathā "pra te yakṣi" (RV 10.4.1) ity agnyabhidhānapare mantre "dhanvann iva prapā asi" (RV 10.4.1) ity etad dṛṣṭāntapadaṃ lokaprasiddhyānupapadyamānaṃ svasiddhyarthaṃ vidhyantaraṃ prapā kartavyeti kalpayati, tathārthavāde 'py aśvānugatau rāsabhasya "tasmāc chreyāṃsaṃ yantaṃ pāpīyān paścād anveti" (TS 5.1.2.3) iti hetvabhidhānāt tatsiddhyai śreyān anugantavya ityādyanumitavidhyarthamūlatocyeta | tad apy asāram | bhrāntijanito 'pi vyavahāraḥ padārthālambanahetutāṃ pratipadyate | bhrāntiḥ kim iti ced, asmād eva vākyārthaviparyayāt | satyatayā vā sālambanatve ko virodhaḥ | vijñānaghana ityāder api satyatā vacanīyā | tataś ca nairātmyāpatteś codanāvyavahāro duḥśliṣṭaḥ syāt | tathāstv iti cet, kaḥ khalv akalpanayaivopapadyamānaprāmāṇyaṃ vedaṃ kalpanām āropyāpramāṇī kuryāt | yathā ca kudṛṣṭīnāṃ bhrāntijanitānām eva pratiṣedhyatvena padārthālambanatvaṃ, tathaiteṣām apīty adoṣaḥ | kalpanāyām api phalavatprayogavacanāntargates tādarthyād apuruṣārthatvena smṛtyaviṣayatāprasaṅgaḥ | nāmnāṃ tu guṇaphalānvayamātropayogitvād dūrāpetaṃ mūlatvam |

        	etenotsannaśākhāmūlatvaṃ vyākhyātam | utsannā api hy evaṃrūpā eveti | kiṃ ca, utsādo 'pi pramāṇaśūnyaḥ kalpanīyaḥ syāt | na hi śākhotsādaḥ sambhavati, evaṃrūpaśākhāntarānupalabdheḥ | caturṇām api vedānāṃ kāścic chākhāḥ paṭhyante | na caikasyām api smṛtyabhihitadharmasādṛśyopalabdhir asti | na cātyantavilakṣaṇatvena śākhāntaratvopapattiḥ | na hi maitrāyaṇī śākhā kāṭhakasyātyantavilakṣaṇā | śākhaikadeśamūlatve vā mahaty adṛṣṭakalpanā syāt | utsannavedamūlatvaṃ tu vedacatuṣṭayaprasiddher nātīva peśalam | prāk cotsādāt smṛtyabhāvaprasaṅgaḥ | utsādāśaṅkayā vā smaraṇe 'gnihotrādīnām api smārtatvaṃ syāt | ato 'yam asāraḥ pakṣaḥ |

        	ye tu vedavat smṛtīnām api nityatayā prāmāṇyaṃ manyante pravacananimittā manvādisamākhyeti vadantaḥ, te khalu maunabhājo durnivārāḥ | abādhakatve 'pi hi puruṣāpraṇīter vedaḥ pramāṇam | sarvalokabāhyā cātra tadapraṇītiḥ | durnivāraṃ cāsadāgamāt tādrūpyam evaṃ sati syāt | tathāstv iti cet | alaṃ smṛtiśāstreṇa | idānīm adṛṣṭamātreṇoparatakartṛkāṇāṃ kūpārāmādīnām api tadakartṛtvaprasaṅgaḥ | manvādīnāṃ ca "sa sarvo 'bhihito vede" ityādyabhidhānaṃ mṛṣety āpadyeta | tadyaśaḥprotsāraṇena vā kathaṃcit kliṣṭakalpanayārthavādatvaṃ yojanīyam | kaṭhādicaraṇāni ca tāṃ tāṃ śākhāṃ bibhrati | na ca mānavādicaraṇopalabdhir asti | na ca chāndogyabrāhmaṇavat ta eva śākhino dhārakā iti śakyaṃ vaktum | anyatamavedaśākhānantargatatvāt | yad api śākhināṃ dhāraṇam upalabhyate, tad api smṛtitvenāvedatayā, aṅgavat | vratādhyayanānādaraś caivam upapadyate | tāś ca smṛtayo (a?)nityā iti vācyam | yadi tāvat katipayamanvādipraṇītā evety ucyeta, nāradāder aprāmāṇyaprasaṅgaḥ | tathāstv iti ced, viśeṣahetur vācyaḥ | idānīṃ praṇītabaudhāyanādismṛteś ca manvādivad ādaro na syāt | yat tv aprayatnapūrvakaṃ sarvā brahmaṇo mukhān nissṛtā iti tac chākyamunideśanevātisthūlam | api ca nityatve smṛtīnām adhyayanavidhyabhāvāt saṃpradāyavicchittiḥ syāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> asti,

                    	viduṣā brāhmaṇenedam adhyetavyaṃ prayatnataḥ | iti | (MDh 1.103)

na tenākhilasmṛtyadhyayanavidhānam, idam iti ca prakṛtaparatvāt | prakṛte ca virodhād asamarthatvam | yadi cādhyetavyam ity asya vidher arthāvagamyatocyeta tadānupanītasya śūdrasamatvād vedārthatvena copanītasya tadadhyayanāt saṃdhyopāsanādikatipayārthaśikṣaṇavacanāc ca smṛtyanadhyayanam | adhītavedasya ca gurukulanivartanam ityādi prapañcanīyam | pāṭhamātraparyavasāyitve tv asyāpy adṛṣṭārthatvāt smṛtisaṃpradāyo durghaṭaḥ syāt | vedamūlatve tu svādhyāyādhyayanavidhivijṛmbhaṇāt kathaṃcid upapadyetāpi | tad eva durupapādam ity uktaṃ purastāt | naivaṃ truṭitavikalpajālena parāvṛtticaturaprajñāsahāyā gṛhyante | ko vā vedamūlatayā smṛtīnāṃ prāmāṇyaṃ brūyāt | saṃpradāyāvicchedād vedavat smṛtayo 'pi svatantrā yataḥ | na ca pūrvābhihitadoṣaprapañcanam | granthanityatvānabhyupagamāt | granthena ca nātīva prayojanaṃ, smārtakriyānuṣṭhānarahitakālābhāvāt | yathaiva hi kṛṣyādayo viśiṣṭaphalopāyānvitatvena lokata upalabhyante, tathāṣṭakādayo 'pi yataḥ | iyāṃs tu viśeṣaḥ: saṃnikṛṣṭaphalāḥ kṛṣyādayaḥ | aniyataphalāś cāṣṭakādayaḥ | na caitāvatā laukikatvaṃ śakyaṃ vaktum | asmād eva vivekāvadhāraṇāt | pramāṇāntarataḥ sa viveko bhrāntyāpīti cet, na | pramāṇāntarasya nirākṛtatvād dṛḍhatvāvagateś cābhrāntiḥ | bhrāntikalpane cāveda eva vedatayā gṛhīta ity apy āśaṅkyeta | yathaiva vedo 'yam iti buddhir laukikatve 'pi vācakatvasmaraṇān na bhrāntir ity ucyate tathāṣṭakādyupāyaphale svarūpaniyamo 'pīty avagantavyam | na ca parokṣatvāt phalasādhanaśakter alaukikatvābhidhānaṃ, śabdaśaktivat | pratipattyanyathānupapattyā seti cet, tad atrāpi samānaṃ dṛḍhatvāt pratyayasya | yathaiva hi śabdāḥ pratyāyakatvena śaktikalpanānimittaṃ, tathā nirūḍhapratipattihetavo 'rthā apīty adoṣaḥ | kasya vātra parokṣatā | aṣṭakādayas tāvat puruṣāntarair anuṣṭhīyamānāḥ pratyakṣatvenāśeṣāṅgā upalabhyante | tatra ca vedaśabdavad aṣṭakādiśabdavyutpattiḥ | viśiṣṭakāryanimittaṃ ca tadanuṣṭhānam iti svarūpavad anuṣṭhātṛbhya evāvagamyate | tatprasiddhyanupapattikalpite ca saṃbandhini bodhakaśaktivat pravṛtter avyāghātaḥ | tasmāt svātantryaṃ smṛtīnām ity uktam | tathā cāha |

                    	agranthakānāṃ arthānāṃ cakāropanibandhanam |[^1] iti |

āmnāyaś ca: "yady ukto bhūr" ityādyupakramya, "yajuṣṭas sāmataḥ" ity uktvā, "yady avijñātam" ity[^2] āha | smārtaṃ cāvijñātam iti saṃpradāyaḥ | tac ca vedamūlatve saty anupapannam, sarvathāvijñānāsambhavāt | na hi vidyamānamūlaṃ nirūpyamāṇe 'vijñātam iti śakyaṃ vaktum | puruṣāntarāpekṣayā tv avijñāne 'tiprasaṅgaḥ | svātantryapakṣe tv avirodhaḥ |

        	sāhasika, maivam | rājanvān janapadaḥ | na khalu sadbhiḥ parigṛhītā nāryaḥ svatantrā bhavanti | na hi laukikam anuṣṭhānaṃ pramāṇarahitaṃ smṛtyarthasatattvāyālaṃ bhavitum arhati | mā bhūc caityavandanādikriyāsv api tathātvam | avedavidāṃ tadanuṣṭhānād vaiṣamyam iti cet, kiṃ vā svātantryavādināṃ vedavidbhiḥ prayojanam | na khalu vedo vedavitparigrahāt pramāṇam | nāpi lokanibandhanāḥ kṛṣyādayo vedavidapekṣāḥ | sāṃdṛṣṭikaphalās ta iti cet, anyathā vā kathaṃ lokanibandhanatvam | na hy asāṃdṛṣṭikam artham āgamānapekṣo lokaḥ pratipattuṃ kṣamaḥ | atha vācakaśabdaval lokavyavahārādhīnatocyeta, tad asat | tatrārthapratyayānupapattiḥ kalpanāmūlam | iha tu kiṃ nopapadyate | vyavahārasya caityavandanādiṣv api darśanāt | na cābhiyuktamanvādismaraṇād viśeṣopapattiḥ, vyavahāramūlatve 'sadāgamair aviśeṣāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca vedas tāvat pramāṇam ity uktam | tadvihitadarśapūrṇamāsādyanuṣṭhātāraś ca dharmaṃ praty abhiyuktāḥ | te cāṣṭakādinām anuṣṭhātāraḥ | tenetaravyavahārād vaiṣamyam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span>, viparyayeṇa sutarām asyopapatteḥ | vedavidāṃ hi tenaiva nirākāṅkṣatvān na vyāvahārikadharmādaraḥ | parityaktavedamūlavyavahārāṇāṃ tv ananyagatikatvād vyavahāre sulagnatā | astu, teṣām api kāryateti cet, suśliṣṭam evaṃ sati prāmāṇyam |

        	evaṃ tarhi codanārthānuṣṭhātṛvyavahārasāmānyād eva tatpravṛttisamarthaṃ kāraṇam anumīyatām | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> tad eva nāstīty uktam | ata evānumīyate | kim asad apy anumīyate | na hy anumāpakaliṅgasaṃbhave saty asad iti śakyaṃ vaktum | kiṃ punas talliṅgam | traivarṇikānām asāṃdṛṣṭiko vyavahāraś codanāmūlo dṛṣṭaḥ | tathāvidhaś cāyam | tasmād atrāpy asti codanā mūlabhūteti | nāpi tadvad upalabdhiprasaṅga ity evaṃ viśeṣaṇaviruddhatvam, adarśanasyābādhakatvāt | itaravyavahāre tu vyāptyabhāvād vaiṣamyam | kim anupalabhyamānaiva codanā vyavahāraṃ pravartayati | kim anayānupayujyamānavicāraṇayā, sarvathā pravartayati | na cānupalabdhiḥ sāmānyato viśeṣataś cānumānāt | niyatakāraṇāni hi kāryāṇi tathaiva svakāraṇāny apy avagamayanti | evaṃ ca vidhyarthānuṣṭhānam upapadyate | svātantrye tu kriyānuṣṭhānam | tatra ca phalābhāvaprasaṅgo 'nantarotpādanānanvayaphalānām | na ca saṃskārotpattidvāreṇa kālāntare phalotpādakatvam iti śakyaṃ vaktum, laukikābhidhānavyāghātāt, kalpanāhetvabhāvāc ca | ato 'yam eva pakṣa śreyān | darśanāni cātrāpy upapadyanta eva |

        	nāyaṃ pakṣo nirvahaṇīyaḥ | na khalu prameyagamyāni pramāṇāni bhavanti | anuṣṭhānānupapattyā hi kāraṇaṃ kalpayataḥ kuto 'nuṣṭhānam | na hi prāk kāraṇakalpanāto 'nuṣṭhānasiddhiḥ | tatsiddhau mudhā kāraṇakalpanā | athocyeta puruṣāntarastham anuṣṭhānaṃ dṛṣṭvā tadanupapattyā kāraṇam anumāya tato 'nuṣṭhānapravṛtter adoṣa iti | tad ayuktam | na hi puruṣāntarānuṣṭhānānupapattiḥ, tasya siddhatvāt | yad apy anumānam uktaṃ kartṛsāmānyād iti, tatrāpi hetor aprayojakatvam | na hi darśapūrṇamāsādīnāṃ traivarṇikānuṣṭhānād dharmyatvam, api tu vedavihitatvāt | na caiṣāṃ tad asti | athāsāṃdṛṣṭikaṃ tadanuṣṭhānaṃ dharma iti | tad api vyabhicāri | avaidikatve 'pi viguṇadharmānuṣṭhānadharśanāt | bhrāntes tad iti cet | evaṃ saty atrāpi bhrāntyupaplavād vyabhicāraḥ | athābādhībhāvād abhrāntir ity ucyeta, tad apy asiddham | vedaviruddhe hi smṛtyarthe 'bādhādarśanāt | atha yatra tadabhāvas tat pramāṇam ity ucyeta, tad api duradhigamam | sarvaṃ cāvedavihitṃ tadviruddham evānuṣṭhānam asāṃdṛṣṭikam | ato 'yam apy asāraḥ pakṣaḥ | "sa sarvo 'bhihito vede" (MDh 2.7) ityady asaṃbaddhaṃ syāt | pramāṇarahitakāraṇakalpanāyāṃ tv andhaparamparā | nyāyokte tu darśanānām ātmalābhaḥ | "vacanāni tv apūrvatvāt" (PMS 3.5.21) ity asyāyam aviṣayaḥ | anayā diśā paricodanīyaṃ prapañcanīyam | sarvathā tu smṛtīnām aprāmāṇyaṃ mūlakāraṇānupalabdhau smṛtitvād vandhyādauhitrasmaraṇavat |

        	atrābhidhīyate | naivaṃ svotprekṣitavikalpajālaiḥ smṛtīnām aprāmāṇyāropaṇaṃ yuktam | svayaṃ hi manvādibhir uktaṃ "sa sarvo 'bhihito vede" (MDh 2.7), "vedo dharmamūlam" (GDh 1.1) "āmnāyaprāmāṇyād ācāraḥ," "dvitīyas tadanuvyākhyā smārtaḥ" (cf. BDh 1.1.1–3), vedaḥ smṛtiḥ sadācāraḥ" (MDh 2.12) ityādi | na caivaṃrūpābhyupagamātikrameṇa mūlāntarānveṣaṇaṃ yuktam | yuktaś cāyam abhyupagamo 'sminn arthe pramāṇāntarābhāvāt, "codanālakṣaṇa eva dharmaḥ" iti (cf. PMS 1.1.2) niyamo yataḥ | na ca bhrāntyādikalpanopapattiḥ, vedavitparigrahavirodhāt | nāpy anyamūlatve tatparigrahopapattiḥ caityavandanādivat | bhrāntyādikalpane vā vede 'py avedatāprasaṅgaḥ | na cāsaṃbhāvyaṃ vedamūlatvaṃ, "vedavido hi manvādayaḥ" iti smaraṇāt | na caitad bhrānteḥ, smartṛtvasmaraṇavat | ataḥ sūktaṃ vedamūlatvam | āha ca |

                    	bhrānter anubhavāc cāpi puṃvākyād vipralambhanāt |

                    	dṛṣṭānuguṇyasādhyatvāc codanaiva laghīyasī || iti | (TV II: 74)

<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> tad eva vedamūlatvaṃ durupapādam ity uktam | uktā hi sarvathā vedasya mūlatvānupapattiḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">na tat</span> samyag uktaṃ pramāṇato hi mūlatvopapatteḥ | upalabhyate hi smṛtīnāṃ tanmūlatvam | vidhyarthānyathānupapattilabhyatvāt | tathā hi "svādhyāyo 'dhyeyaḥ" ity ukte, "vidyāṃ cādhyāpayet" iti dvayasyānupapattyānyo vidhis tatra praklapyate | "vidyām adhyāpayet" iti hi vidhir ātmopapādanāyādhyayanaṃ prayuṅkte | adhyayanvidhir api tatprayuktyaivopapannānuṣṭhāno 'dhikārāntarakalpanām antareṇaudāsīnyaṃ pratipadyate | na cādhyāpayitādhyetāram anupanīyādhyāpayituṃ kamaḥ | tatra vidhidvayopapattyarthaṃ vidhyantarānumityā "brāhmaṇādīn upanayīta" iti | evaṃ vedārthāvagatyuttarakālaṃ vidhidvaye caritārthe saty anantaraṃ prajotpādanavidhyapekṣāyā patnyabhāve tadanupapatteḥ kāmaikasādhanatvāc ca "lakṣaṇyāṃ striyam udvahet" iti (YDh 1.52) vidhyantarotthānam | agnihotrādyanuṣṭhānasya ca patnyapekṣatvāt tatsaṃnidhānāc ca "tayā saha yajeta" ity anatikramaṇavidhyudayaḥ | tathā "ṛtāv upeyat" (GDh 5.1) ityādi | tatra tatra pradhānopapādakā vidhayaḥ sādhikārā anayaiva diśā kalpanīyā | tathāṅgasaṃbandhaḥ pratyakṣair ānumanikaiś ca śrutyādibhir adhyavaseyaḥ | nipuṇatas tu granthavyākhyāyām eva pradarśayiṣyāmaḥ | na caivaṃ sati duḥśliṣṭatā smṛtiprāmāṇyasya |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evaṃ saty arthagamyā smārthā vidhayaḥ prasajyante | tad yatha | "juhuyāt sarpiṣā" ity ukte "sruveṇāvadyati" iti ca "ājyaṃ sruveṇa gṛhṇīyāt" iti vidhyantarodayaḥ | yathā hi caturavattaviśiṣṭaḥ saripiṣā homo 'vadānasamarthadravyaviśeṣāpekṣaḥ sruvādyākāṅkṣati, tathā "sruveṇāvadyati" iti sruvavidhiḥ svaśaktyanusārād dravadravyaviṣayatayopaplavamānas tadviśeṣābhimukhatā cālocya vidhyantaram āvir bhāvayati "sruveṇājyaṃ gṛhṇīyat" iti | evañjātīyakāḥ sarve vidhayaḥ smārtāḥ prasajyeran |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span>, eśā viniyogamātrāvasāyitvāt | yo hy utpādakḥ padārthasyānuṣṭhāpako vā syāt, sa evopadeśakāraṇam | na tūtpannaidamarthyamātraniyāmako 'pīty avirodhaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">evaṃ</span> tarhi smṛtiviniyuktānām apy asmārtatvaprasaṅgaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">na</span>, smṛteḥ padārthotpādakatvena vaiṣamyāt | kā vārtāṣṭakādiṣu | na tadabhāve kasyacid vider anupapatiḥ | svādhyāyādhyayanavidher mantrāṇāṃ copapannatvāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | atrāpy aṣṭakādisamākhyātamantravān svādhyāyādhyayanavidhir nopapadyate | na hi japayajñādyanvaye sati samākhyānopapattiḥ | na ca spaṣṭataraviniyogopalabdhiḥ, yadbalenākhyāyā bādhaḥ | śakyate ca mantrair dravyadevatāsaṃyogo 'dhikārahetutvaṃ ca pratipādayitum | tadyuktādhyayanavidhyanupapattitaś ca kāryatāvamagaḥ | aṅgānvayaprakāras tūkta eva | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evaṃ samākhyānābhedād aśeṣair mantrair ekam evāṣṭakākarmānumīyeta | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span>, sāmarthyabhedāt | svaśaktyā hi mantrāḥ karma pratipādayanti | na caikakarmapratipādanaśaktir asti | ataḥ siddho 'ṣṭakādikarmaṇāṃ bhedaḥ | na caivaṃ saty aśeṣaśākhādhigatāṣṭakādyanuṣṭhānam ekasyaiva syāt | na khalv ekaśākhādhigatakriyānuṣṭhāne tadakaraṇanimittapratyavāyo na parihṛtaḥ syāt | paṭhyamānatve hi karmaṇāṃ bhinnānāṃ samānanāmnām apy ekakriyāyām akṛtī syāt, kartavyatāvagateḥ samānatvāt, prayojanaikyānavagamāc ca | anumeyatve tad anupapannam, aṣṭakādyabhinnakālasaṃbandhinas tadanusāreṇa prayojanasyābhedāt | avagatakālādisaṃbandhāvirodhena hi prayojanaṃ kalpanīyam | tac cānekakarmānuṣṭhāne 'nupapannam | na hy ekasmin kāle 'nekakarmānuṣṭhānopapattiḥ | na cānumeyatve pūrvāhṇādikālasyāṅgatvakṛtaḥ kaścid viśeṣo 'sti, paṭhyamānavat | kiṃ ca paṭhyamānaṃ karmātmānaṃ kārayitum akriyāyāṃ pratyavāyaṃ kalpayati | kālpanikaṃ punaḥ paṭhyamānany athānupapattyā kalpyeta | tac ca kalpyakarmānanuṣṭhānanimittadoṣakalpanām antareṇaivopapannam iti na kalpanāvasaro 'sti | atha kḷptakarmānuṣṭhānāvagamānupapattyā kalpyeta, tadaivaṃrūpā kalpanā syad: yo hy asmin kāle 'ṣṭakākhyaṃ karma na kuryāt sa pratyaveyād iti | evaṃ sati tadākhyaikakarmakaraṇe 'pi kṛtī syāt | na caikaikatra kalpanāhetusadbhāvād anekakalpanāprasaṅga iti śakyaṃ vaktum | tasyaikakalpanāyām apy avirodhāt | athāgṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatvād anekakalpanam ity ucyate | tad ekaśākhāpaṭhyamānaviṣayatvād ekaikaśākhādhigatatve 'nupapannam | na hi bhinnaśākhādhigatatve 'py agṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatāsti | paṭhyamāne 'py etat samānam iti cet | na, tasya svamahimnaivānuṣṭhāpakatvāt | iha tu svarūpasyānyato 'dhigater vaiṣamyam | kiṃ ca, anuṣṭhānopapattyarthā kalpanā | na caikakartṛviṣayatayā sarvakarmānuṣṭhānābhyupagame tadupapattiḥ | na hi svahetuvirodhinyaḥ kalpanāḥ saṃbhavanti | pratyakṣādhyayane tv aprādhānyāt kālasya prasaktāv api virodhaḥ parihriyeta, na tv anumeyatve 'pi | ataḥ sūktam ekakaraṇe 'pi kṛtī syād iti | virodhādarśanāt tu catasro 'ṣṭakāḥ kriyanta ity anavadyam | evaṃ ca sāmānyataḥ kāryāvagamaḥ | kvacic ca pratyakṣato 'pi paṭhyamānatvena sāmānyataḥ kāryāvagatau mantrārthavādā viśeṣasamarpakā bhavanti | tāny api smṛtimūlāni | yathā, "etad u khalv addhā tapaḥ yad ahiṃsā yad damo yad dānaṃ yad atithisaparyā | atha paramaṃ tapo bhūtānām yad anujighṛkṣā tasmād evaṃvit sarveṣāṃ bhūtānām addhaivopakuryād" iti brāhmaṇam | addhopakāraś ca dṛṣṭakāraṇarahita upakāraḥ | tadapekṣitaprakāraviśeṣo mantrārthavādair anyaparair api pratipādyamāno nāpeśalaḥ | yathā, "sthalayodakaṃ parigṛhṇanti" iti taṭākādikaraṇam | "dhanvann iva" (RV 10.4.1) iti ca prapākaraṇam | yat tu phalavat prayogāntargateḥ kalpyamānasyāpi tādarthyam iti | talliṅgena prakaraṇasya bādhyamānatvād acodyam | yamaniyamās tu prāyaśaḥ pratyakṣamūlā eva | yatra punaḥ pratyakṣaṃ tadanupapattau kḷptaṃ vā na sāmānyakaraṇam asti, tatrāpy anyaparatvān mṛṣārthatvena copapannatvān na mantrārthavādāḥ svānvitapadārthasatyatābhājo bhavanti | tenāsadāgamair vaiṣamyam | smṛtayo 'pi ca tadrūpā eva bādhyante | na caitāvatā samūlatve 'pi tanmithyātvakalpanety alaṃ prasaṅgena | sarvathā vedamūlatvaṃ smṛtinām upapannam | śakyate caiva sati smṛtīnām avijñātatvaṃ vaktuṃ, kālpanikatvāt | kalpanānimittam evargvedādayaḥ, na vyapadeśakāraṇam | tathā ca manuḥ: "sa sarvo 'bhihito vede" (MDh 2.7) ityādyabhidhānamantraṃ bruvan kalpyatvād vidher vedavyapadeśo nāstīti darśayati, āpastambaś ca "brāhmaṇoktā vidhayas teṣām utsannāḥ pāṭhāḥ prayogād anumīyante" (ĀpDh 1.12.10) iti vadaṃs teṣāṃ mūlasatyatām | utsannā iva prayogād anumīyanta ity arthaḥ | smārtavyapadeśānāditā caivam upapadyata ity eṣā dik | virodhe caiva bādha upapannataro bhavati | anyathā tu virodhe vikalpaḥ syāt | na ca bhavatv iti sakyaṃ vaktuṃ, śiṣṭānabhyupagamāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> viparītaḥ śiṣṭābhyupagamaḥ | na khalu smṛtiviruddhaṃ śrutyuktam apy ādriyamāṇā dṛśyante | tathā hi |

                    	govadhaṃ nānumanyante śrutyuktam api tadvidaḥ |

                    	tasyopapātakaśraiṣṭhyaṃ smṛtau yasmād udāhṛtam ||

                    	karaṇaṃ ca śruter jñātaṃ jyotiṣṭomādikarmaṇām |

                    	steyādyarthārjanenāpi na tat smṛtivirodhataḥ ||

                    	maivaṃ na khalu śiṣṭānāṃ kvacit smṛtivirodhataḥ |

                    	śrutyuktārthānanuṣṭhānaṃ dṛḍham alpīyasām api ||

                    	na hi cchāgavadhaṃ tajjñā na kurvanti nivāritam |

                    	avāritaḥ sa cet smṛtyā govadho 'pi hi tatsamaḥ ||

                    	smārtā hi vidhayaḥ sarve śrutyuktavyatirekiṇaḥ |

                    	tena smṛtiviruddhatvaṃ nānanuṣṭhānakāraṇam ||

                    	smārto 'pi govadho 'sty arghyam arhayet prathamaṃ gavā |

                    	nityāni cāṣṭakādīni hetus tadakṛtau ca yaḥ ||

                    	vedamūlabalaṃ vāpi bhrāntir vā vaidike ca saḥ |

                    	na tu smṛtibalāc chiṣṭā na kuryuḥ karma vaidikam ||

                    	ardhāstamita āditye prārabhyārkṣavibhāvanāt |

                    	japaḥ smṛtyuditas tyakto virodhād agnihotribhiḥ ||

                    	anuṣṭhānānanuṣṭhāne kāraṇaṃ na balābale |

                    	mā bhūd dharmaḥ kharārūḍhāvastrasañchādanady api ||

                    	vedam eva tv adṛṣṭārthe pramāṇaṃ manyate manuḥ |

                    	pramāṇaṃ paramaṃ dharme śrutir ityadibhāṣaṇāt ||

                    	manyante cātidaurbalyaṃ smartāraḥ śrutitaḥ smṛteḥ |

                    	dharmamūlatayā vedaṃ vadantas tadvidām iti ||

                    	tena vedaviruddhāyāḥ smṛter bādha iti sthitiḥ |

                    	śrūyamāṇaviruddhatvāt kalpanānupapattitaḥ ||

                    	pratyakṣo 'py upakārādividhiḥ sāmānyagocaraḥ |

                    	yāyād ālocya daurbalyaṃ viśeṣaviṣayāṃ smṛtim ||

                    	vidhyarthān anyathābhāvakḷptyaiḥ prāyo vidhāyakaiḥ |

                    	dṛṣibhir bahudhā bhinnaiḥ smṛtayaḥ saṃpravartitāḥ ||

              	pratyakṣataḥ kalpanayā ca samyak siddhasya sāmānyavidhāyakasya |

              	mantrārthavādair vidhibhiś ca kuryād dṛśyānumeyaiḥ paripūraṇāni ||

              	itthaṃ ca gāḍhaṃ nṛkṛtatvapaṅkaṃ vidhūya darmākhyahiraṇyamālā |

              	āmnāyasūryāṃśuvikāsitāni bibharti vidhyarthasaroruhāṇi ||

                    	evaṃ prāmāṇyam ālocya vedamūlatayā smṛteḥ |

                    	te sarvārtheṣv amīmāṃsye ity āha bhavān manuḥ || 7 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evaṃ sati "dharmamūlam idaṃ smṛtam" iti vacanād arthāder mūlaṃ_[^3]_ na prāpnoti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span> | dharmapadasya pradarśanārthatvāt | athāpi dharmamātra eva dharmapadaṃ syāt | tathāpy arthakāmau tāvac chāstraniyatau dharmyāv eva | apavargasyānyatvam iti cet | tad apy asat |_

 

**              	ijyācāradamāhiṃsādānasvādhyāyakarmaṇām |**

**              	ayaṃ tu paramo dharmo yad yogenātmadarśanam || 1.8 ||**

 

ijyeti yāgādīnāṃ vaidikānām upalakṣaṇam | ācāra iti smārtānāṃ sopanibandhānām anupanibaddhānāṃ ca | dama indriyasaṃyamaḥ | ahiṃsā yajñādyātatāyivyatirekeṇa | dānaṃ prasiddham | svādhyāyo brahmayajñaḥ | eṣāṃ karmaṇāṃ dharmyatvaṃ yady api prasiddhaṃ, tathāpy alpadharmo 'yaṃ, dhāraṇālpatvena yogasyāpauṣkalyāt | ayam eva paramo dharmaḥ yad yogenātmadarśanam | manovṛttisaṃnirodho yogaḥ | tena yad āñjasyenātmadarśanaṃ tad evātyantikadhāraṇatvena paramo dharmaḥ | tasmāt siddham arthādīnāṃ śāstrāvaseyatvam | kasmāt punaḥ śrutismṛtyantargatatve 'pi damādīnāṃ pṛthag upanyāsaḥ | smārtatvapradarśanārthaḥ | ācāraḥ smārtānāṃ grāhakaḥ, tāni punar damādīny api | ata eva brahmayajño 'py atraivodāhṛtaḥ | pratyakṣaśrutipāṭhe 'pi smārtatvād gāthādilakṣaṇaḥ śūdrasyāpi kathaṃ syād iti | sarvādhikārārthaṃ vā damādīnāṃ pṛthag vidhānam | ācāraśabdena tv aṣṭakādīnāṃ traivarṇikārthānām grahaṇam | tathā cāhuḥ |

                    	ahiṃsā satyam akrodhaḥ śaucam indriyanigrahaḥ |

                    	eṣa sādhāraṇo dharmaś cāturvarṇye prakīrtitaḥ || iti | (MDh 10.63)

satyam iti cātra vyāhṛtyupalakṣito brahmayajñaḥ parigṛhyate | satyavacanasyendriyanigrahād eva labdhatvāt | tathā ca vakṣyaty etat | "pañcayajñān na hāpayet" iti (YDh 1.120) | atha vā ijyeti saṃskāropalakṣaṇam | ācāra ity ātmaguṇānām | damādayas tūdāharaṇārthāḥ | samānam anyat | apavarganirūpaṇārthaś cāyaṃ ślokaḥ | tad etad ṛcāpy uktam: "tam evaṃ viditvā mṛtyum atyeti" iti (cf. VS 31.18) | smṛtiś cātmajñānaṃ prakṛtyāha:

                    	tad dhy agryaṃ sarvavidyānāṃ prāpyate hy amṛtaṃ tataḥ | iti | (MDh 12.85)

sarvaṃ caitat śrutismṛtyavaseyam iti tayoḥ sūktaṃ dharmamūlatvam || 8 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca śrutismṛtyor abodhakatve 'pi puruṣasāmarthyāpekṣayā pratibhānato 'rthaniyamaḥ | tathā khalv ekasmād eva vākyād anyathā cānyathā ca pratipannā dṛśyante | kathaṃ caivaṃ sati dharmanirṇayaḥ | tad uktam: "dharmasya tattvaṃ nihitaṃ guhāyām" iti _(MBh 3. App. 32.67) _| <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> evaṃ, yadi nirṇayopāyo na syāt | asti hy upāyaḥ |_

 

**              	catvāro vedadharmajñāḥ parṣat traividyam eva vā |**

**              	sā brūte yaṃ sa dharmaḥ syād eko vādhyātmavittamaḥ || 1.9 ||**

 

catvāra iti niyamaḥ pañcādivyāvṛttyarthaḥ, mahāsamavāye niścayakleśāt | vedavido dharmaśāstravidaś ca vedadharmajñāḥ | pārārthyāc ca jñānasya na tanmātrāvasāyinaḥ | kiṃ tarhi, jñānino 'nuṣṭhātāraś ca te savivekāḥ pariṣat | traividyaṃ vā | trayī vidyā ṛgyajuḥsāmalakṣaṇā yasmin, tat traividyam | traya ṛgyajuḥsāmapāragā ity arthaḥ | puruṣasaṃkhyāniyamāc cārthavavedādhyayanam aviruddham | asmiṃś ca pakṣe ye prativākyaṃ śrutismṛtyor mūlamūlibhāvaṃ jānanti, te gṛhyante | evakāras tv apyarthaḥ | sa ca saṃbhāvanāyām | vāśabdo 'bhyarhitatvena vikalpadyotanārthaḥ | trayo 'pi yadi bhavanti dvau vā yadi syātām eko 'pi vādhyātmavittamaḥ | sa hi samyag vettānanyathāvaktā ca | tathā coktam |

                    	eko 'pi vedavid dharmaṃ yaṃ vyavasyed dvijottamaḥ | iti | (MDh 12.113)

ātmayājino 'pi gṛhasthā brahmavido naiṣṭhikāś ca brahmacāriṇaḥ vanasthāś ca | tadartham adhyātmavittama ity uktaṃ parāśramābhiprāyam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> etad ayuktaṃ, sa khalu "hiṃsānugrahayor anārambhī" iti (GDh 3.24–5) | ko vā tam ārambhiṇam āha | abhigamya tu saṃśaye pṛṣṭaḥ so 'pi brūyad ity uktam asmābhiḥ | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

                    	sarvabhūtagaṇādrohī cared avyaharann api |

                    	pṛṣṭo 'nyaiḥ sādhubhir brūyāt pṛcched anyāṃś ca saṃśaye || iti |

yat tu "prāg uttamāt traya āśramiṇaḥ" iti (GDh 28.49), vaikhānasābhiprāyaṃ tad bhikṣoḥ samavāyapratiṣedhād daśāvarādiviṣayaṃ draṣṭavyam | tatrāpi tu yadi kaścit svaniyamātilaṅghanena samaveyāt tataḥ pariṣat saguṇaiva | tathā cāṅgirāḥ |

                    	brahmacāryāśramād ūrdhvaṃ traya āśramiṇaḥ smṛtāḥ |

ity āha | vāśabdadvayāc ca dvau vety uktam | pūrvāpekṣayā ca tau prakṛṣṭaguṇau draṣṭavyau | tathā cāhuḥ |

                    	catvāras tu trayo dvau vā yad vaikaḥ syād aninditaḥ |

                    	yatīnām (?) agryavidyānām eko 'pi pariṣad bhavet || iti |

sā pariṣad anyonyaṃ vimṛśya samyag avadhārya yad brūte sa dharmaḥ syāt | sa nirvicikitsyo dharma ity avagantavyam | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "yac cātmavanto vṛddhāḥ samyagvinītā ḍambhalobhamohaviyuktā vedavida ācakṣate tat samācaret" iti (GDh 9.62) | śaṅkho 'py āha: "śrutivirodhe traividyasamavāyeṣu nirṇayaḥ" iti, "yathāvalepaṃ śāstratas te 'nubrūyuḥ" iti ca | yat tu pañcāvarā daśāvarā vā pariṣad dharmapravaktṛbhir uktā, sā mahāpātakādiprāyaścittaviṣayā draṣṭavyā, śuddhyaśuddhyos tatra prakāśyatvāt | yā tv ekaviṃśatyā śatena aṅgirasābhihitā, sā kila bhūyāṃso brāhmaṇāḥ, te yat brūyus tat tathaiva bhavatīti śraddhāmātreṇeti mantavyā, gāyatrīmātrasāraiś cīrṇavratair api dharmasya nirṇetum aśakyatvāt | pūrvoktapariṣatpraśaṃsārthaṃ vā, aviduṣāṃ nindārtham | tathā coktam, "netare tu sahasraśaḥ" iti (BDh 1.1.9) | guṇavidviṣayatve vā kāryagauravajñāpanārtham | yat tu,

                    	rājñāṃ (tu) saiva dviguṇā vaiśyānāṃ triguṇā smṛtā |

iti, tat kṣatriyavaiśyayoḥ prāyaścittadāne yatnātirekārtham, āpadviṣayaṃ vā, prāyaścittasya vāvaśyakāryatājñāpanārtham, pariṣadi vācāvedananiyamārthaṃ vā | yat tu kṣatriyādiprāyaścittadāne purohitādyadhikāraḥ, anyeṣāṃ ca prāyaścittam iti, tat prāyaścittaprakaraṇe vakṣyāmaḥ | sarvathā pariṣadi dharmanirṇayaḥ | alpāpi ca prakṛṣṭaguṇā pariṣat praśastety ācāryābhiprāyaḥ | nyāyamūlatvāt pariṣannirṇayārthasmṛter anekārthatvam aviruddham | anayaiva diśā vivekaḥ kāryaḥ || 9 ||

 

**iti upodghātaprakaraṇam |**

 

**atha brahmacāriprakaraṇam |**

 

_uktaṃ dharmādīnāṃ svarūpaṃ pramāṇaṃ ca | idānīṃ tatsādhanāni vācyāni | tatra ca kriyāmātrasādhāraṇyāt kartuḥ pūrvam abhidhānaṃ yuktam ity ata āha |_

 

**              	brahmakṣatriyaviṭśūdrā varṇās tv ādyās trayo dvijāḥ |**

**              	niṣekādyāḥ śmaśānāntās teṣāṃ vai mantrataḥ kriyāḥ || 1.10 ||**

 

brāhmaṇakṣatriyavaiśyaśūdrāś catvāro varṇā iti vyavahārārthā paribhāṣeyam | tu śabdo 'pakṛṣyāvadhāraṇārtho vyākhyeyaḥ | ādyās trayo dvijā itīyam api saṃjñā pūrvavat | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> cādyā dvijā ity etāvad vācyaṃ, bahuvacanāt tritvāvagateḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> evaṃ | rathakāravyāvṛttyarthas triśabdaḥ | yat tu smṛtyantare rathakārasyopanayanasmaranaṃ, tad ādhānādhikṛtatvād bhrānter ity avaseyam | vikalpo vāstu | nety ācāryaḥ | teṣāṃ dvijātīnāṃ niṣekād ārabhyāsthisaṃcayanād mantrataḥ kriyā bhavanti | śāstrataḥ ity arthaḥ | tṛtīyārthe pañcamī draṣṭavyā | vaiśabdo hetvarthaḥ | yasmān mantrārhaṃ teṣām upanayanākhyaṃ janma, tasmān mantravatyaḥ kriyā bhavantīti || 10 ||

 

_kāḥ punas tāḥ kriyāḥ, kasmin kāle kartavyā ity ata āha |_

 

                    	**garbhādānam ṛtau puṃsas savanaṃ spandnāt purā |**

**              	ṣaṣṭhe 'ṣṭame vā sīmanto māse 'to jātakarma ca || 1.11 ||**

 

garbhādhānākhyaḥ prathamaḥ saṃskāro niṣekalakṣaṇaḥ | sa cartau kāryaḥ | sāmarthyād ṛtur vakṣyamāṇo na vasantādikaḥ | puṃsavanākhyo dvitīyaḥ saṃskāraḥ | sa ca prāg garbhaspandanāt | tathā ca pāraskaraḥ: "atha puṃsavanaṃ purā spandanāt" iti (PārGṛ 1.14.1) prathamakalpam āha | ṣaṣṭhe garbhamāse 'ṣṭame vā sīmantonnayanākhyas tṛtīyaḥ | ataḥ paraṃ nāmnaivāgatakālaṃ jātakarma bhavati | caśabdāt soṣyantīkarma ca | tathā cāha: "soṣyantīm adbhirabhyukṣati," "jātasya kumārasya ca" iti (PārGṛ 1.16.1, 3) | ete ca saṃskārāḥ kārtsnyena gṛhyād avagantavyāḥ | pratigarbhaṃ cāpasīmantonnayanāḥ pravartante,[^4] tasya strīsaṃskāratvāt | tatsaṃskāratvaṃ ca "sīmantam ūrdhvaṃ vinayanti" iti (PārGṛ 1.15.4) vacanāt | mantravarṇāc ca "ājīvaṃ phalinī bhava" iti (PārGṛ 1.15.6), sīmantinīti samākhyānāc ca | anyā ca smṛtiḥ: "sīmantonnayanaṃ puṃsavanavat prathame garbhe māse ṣaṣṭhe 'ṣṭame vā" iti (PārGṛ 1.15.1–2) | na ca tad evaṃ neyaṃ prathame garbhe māsaniyamārtham iti, śrutibādhaprasaṅgāt | na ca strīsaṃskāratve 'pi garbhanimittatvād āvṛttir iti śayaṃ vaktum, prathamagarbhasyaiva nimittabhāvāt | kāryaśūnyatvāc cānāvṛttiḥ | garbhādhānaṃ tv arthād evāvartate | liṅgāc ca puṃsavanam | soṣyantīkarma tu sukhaprasavārthatvāt | ato 'vaiṣamyam | ataḥ sūktam apasīmantonnayanā pravartanta iti | evaṃ ca samācarānugrahaḥ || 11 ||

 

_kiṃ cānyat |_

 

**              	ahany ekādaśe nāma caturthe māsi niṣkramaḥ |**

**              	ṣaṣṭhe 'nnaprāśanaṃ māse cūḍā kāryā yathākulam || 1.12 ||**

 

ekādaśe 'hani nāma kartavyam | evaṃ niṣkramaṇady api | tathā cāha: "caturthe māsi niṣkramaṃ karoti" iti (PārGṛ 1.17.5) | yat tu "daśamyām utthāpya brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā pitā nāma karoti" iti (PārGṛ 1.17.1), daśamyāṃ vyuṣṭāyām iti tatrārthaḥ | tathā cāha manuḥ |

                    	nāmadheyaṃ daśamyāṃ tu dvādaśyāṃ cāsya kārayet | iti | (MDh 2.30)

ānantaryārthaś cakāraḥ | daśamyāṃ vyuṣṭāyāṃ dvādaśyāṃ veti draṣṭavyam | aṃśajātatvenaikādaśyām iti noktam | tuśabdāc cāyam evādyaḥ kalpa iti dyotitam | atha tu daśamyām eveti tasyārthaḥ, tadā yasya prāg daśarātrāc chuddhis tadviṣayatvena draṣṭavyaṃ, sūtakavākyoparodhāt | ekādaśe tv aviśeṣeṇa prāthamakalpikaḥ | yathākulam iti cūḍābhiprāyam | yathā, "pañcacūḍā bharadvājāḥ" iti | kālas tv aṅgam | gurulāghavaṃ gṛhyād avagantavyam | atha vā kālābhiprāyam evaitaj jātakarmādiviṣayatvenāpi yojyam | yathā, janmāntaraṃ daśarātre vā jātakarma | ekādaśe dvādaśe vāhni, śatarātre puṇye nakṣatre vā nāmakaraṇam | daśarātre caturthe māse vā niṣkramaṇam | ṣaṣṭe māse saṃvatsare vānnaprāśanam | saṃvatsare sārdhe tṛtīye va cūḍākaraṇam | tat sarvaṃ yathākulaṃ vā kāryam, uktakālaṃ vā | dvirmāsagrahaṇaṃ tu chandaḥsamādhānārtham | ṛjv anyat || 12 ||

 

 

_kasmāt punar eṣāṃ saṃskārakarmaṇāṃ prayatnenaiva niyogato 'nuṣṭhānam | ucyate | yasmāt,_

 

                    	**evam enaḥ śamaṃ yāti bījagarbhasamudbhavam |**

 

mātāpitror janyasya vā niyatanimittatvād enasaś ca nirākāryatvāt prayatnenaivaṃ niyogataḥ karaṇam | garbhārthatve 'pi cākaraṇe mātāpitror eva prathyavāyaḥ | tathā cāha manuḥ |

                    	baijikaṃ gārbhikaṃ caino dvijānām apamṛjyate | iti | (MDh 2.27)

 

_kiṃ punar etāḥ kriyāḥ puṃviṣayā eva | nety āha |_

 

                    	**tūṣṇīm etāḥ kriyāḥ strīṇāṃ**

 

api kāryā iti śeṣaḥ, saṃskāryatvāviśeṣāt | etā iti sarvanāmno 'taśśabdāvacchinnajātakarmādiviṣayatvaṃ draṣṭavyam | garbhādhānādau tv aviśeṣaḥ | sukhaprasavārthatvāt tu soṣyantīkarmaṇaś caśabdāvagatasyāpi grahaṇam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evaṃ sati strīṇāṃ mantrahānāt tadyuktakarmādhikāro duḥśliṣṭaḥ syāt | vacanagamyatvād adhikārasyaitad acodyam |

 

_na ca strīṇām ātyantiko mantrābhāvaḥ | yadi nāma jātakarmādi tūṣṇīm |_

 

                                            	**vivāhas tu samantrakaḥ || 1.13 ||**

 

samantraka eva | tasmād avirodhaḥ | kāryābhāvāt tu napuṃsake saṃskāranivṛttiḥ | arthalakṣaṇās tu nāmakaraṇādayaḥ śūdrasyāpi pravartante | tathā ca manuḥ: "śūdrasya preṣyasaṃyutam" iti (MDh 2.32), avihitāpratiṣiddhatvāt | "mantravarjaṃ śūdrasya" iti śaṅkhaḥ | niḥśeṣato vā strīsamatvavacanād iti kecit | tat tu sāmānyatodṛṣṭatvāc chabdalakṣaṇe vyavahāre nādaraṇīyam | ete ca saṃskārāḥ strīṇām api brāhmaṇādīnām eteṣv eva kāleṣu bhavanti || 13 ||

 

_ataḥ paraṃ tu |_

 

                    	**garbhāṣṭame 'ṣṭame vābde brāhmaṇasyopanāyanam |**

**              	rājñām edādaśe saike viśām eke yathākulam || 1.14 ||**

 

<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> etat pāriśeṣyād brāhmaṇasyaivopanayanam uktam "ādyās trayo dvijāḥ" iti | ayuktaṃ brāhmaṇagrahaṇam | atha brāhmaṇasya sata upanayanam, nopanayanād brāhmaṇyam iti jñāpanārtham ity ucyeta, tad api varṇaparibhāṣayaiva siddher asāram | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | hetvartham idam | garbhādhānāj janmano vāṣṭame varṣe brāhmaṇam upanayet | kasmāt | brāhmaṇatvād eva | evaṃ hy āmnāyaḥ: "gāyatro vai brāhmaṇaḥ, aṣṭākṣarā vai gāyatrī, tasmād aṣṭavarṣaṃ brāhmaṇam upanayīta" ityādi | evaṃ kṣatriyavaiśyaśabdāv api yojyau | hetvabhidhānaṃ tu śloke vasantādikālaprāptyartham | tathā cāmnāyaḥ: "brahma hi vasantaḥ, kṣatraṃ grīṣmo, viḍ varṣāḥ" iti (ŚB 2.1.3.5) | vasantādisaṃbandhaṃ ca brāhmanādīnām anyataḥ siddhaṃ hi śabdenānuvadan vasante brāhmaṇopanayanaṃ kāryam iti darśayati | yady apy etāny ādhānādau vākyāni, tathāpi hetvarthopapattyartham upanayanāpekṣitakālasamarpaṇam aviruddham | mantravarṇaś ca: "gāyatrī vāsantīti gāyatrīchando vasantād ṛtor niramimīta" iti | ayam eva tasyāpy arthaḥ | carakās tu spaṣṭatarāṇy upanayana eva paṭhanti | tathā ca āpastambas tāny evānukaroti: "vasante brāhmaṇam upanayīta" ityādi (ĀpDh 1.1.19) | śaṅkhaś ca: "vasanto grīṣmaḥ śarad iti kālāḥ" ity āha | vaiśyasya tu vikalpaḥ | vedādhyayanāyācāryasamīpe nayanam upanayanam | tad evopanāyanam ity uktaṃ chando'nurodhāt | tadarthaṃ vā karma | rājñām iti kṣatriyarājaśabdayor ekārthatvajñāpanārtham | ekādaśe 'bda upanayanaṃ kāryam iti śeṣaḥ | saike viśām iti | dvādaśa ity arthaḥ | eke yathākulam iti punarvacanāt paramatopanyāsaḥ | eke yathākulam icchanti, na vasantādau | vayaṃ tv aṣṭavarṣaṃ vasante brāhmaṇam upanayīteti | anulomānantarajānām apy eta eva kālāḥ mātṛjātīyavyapadeśāt "putrā ye 'nantarastrījāḥ" iti (MDh 10.14) manuvacanād draṣṭavyaḥ | liṅgasya ca vivakṣitatvāt strīṣv aprasaṅgaḥ | pratilomās tv anadhikṛtā eva | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "pratilomāt tu dharmahīnaḥ" iti (GDh 4.25) || 14 ||

 

_atha kim upanīyānantaraṃ veda evādhyāpayitavyaḥ, tādarthyād upanayanasya | evaṃ khalu prāpnotīty ata āha |_

 

**              	upanīya guruḥ śiṣyaṃ mahāvyāhṛtipūrvakam |**

**              	vedam adhyāpayet paścāc chaucācārāṃś ca śikṣayet || 1.15 ||**

 

tuśabdārthaś caśabdaḥ | upanayanānantaram eva na vedam adhyāpayet | kiṃ tarhi, paścāt | śaucācārāṃś cānantaram eva śikṣayed ity abhiprāyaḥ | tathā ca manuḥ |

                    	upanīya guruḥ śiṣyaṃ śikṣayec chaucam āditaḥ |

                    	ācāram agnikāryaṃ ca saṃdhyopāsanam eva ca || iti | (MDh 2.69)

yadā tv adhyāpayet, tadā mahāvyāhṛtipūrvakam | mahāvyāhṛtiśabdena tv oṃkāro vyāhṛtayaḥ sāvitrī ceti pratyetavyaṃ, smṛtyantarāt | yathāha manuḥ |

                    	oṃkārapūrvikās tisro mahāvyāhṛtayo 'vyayāḥ |

                    	tripadā caiva gāyatrī vijñeyā brahmaṇo mukham || iti | (MDh 2.81)

gautamīyaṃ tu sāmavedaviṣayam "oṃpūrvā vyāhṛtayaḥ pañca satyāntāḥ" iti (GDh 1.51) draṣṭavyaṃ, tatra hi "puruṣaḥ satyam" iti pañcānāṃ pāṭhāt | atha vā mahāvyāhṛtaya eva pūrvaṃ yasya vedasya sa mahāvyāhṛtipūrvakaḥ | sāpekṣatve samāsānupapatteḥ sāvitryabhāvaḥ | oṃkāras tv ādyantayor avirodhāt kartavya eva | "sravaty ānoṃkṛtaṃ pūrvam" (MDh 2.74) iti vacanāt | mānavaṃ tu vikalpena vyākhyeyam | oṃkārapūrvā vyāhṛtayo brahmaṇo mukhaṃ tatpūrvā vā sāvitrīti | tathā ca samācāraḥ | gurugrahaṇaṃ tu mukhyaṃ pitur upanetṛtvam iti | tathā ca śrutiḥ: "tasmāt putram anuśiṣṭaṃ lokyam āhuḥ" iti  (BāU 1.5.17) | śiṣyagrahaṇaṃ tu putratve 'py akhilaśuśrūṣāniyamārtham | kṣatriyavaiśyayor apy āpatkāle putropanetṛtvād gurutvam aviruddham | ācāryopanayanaṃ tu brāhamaṇasyānukalpaḥ | śaucam ācārāś ca śaucācārāḥ | śaucaṃ manovākkāyalakṣaṇaṃ trividham | apratirūpāsaṅkalpanaṃ manasaḥ śuddhiḥ, pāpmanetarasya viruddhatvāt | sādhuśabdaprayogaḥ satyavacanaṃ ca vācaḥ | tathā ca bhāradvājaḥ: "na mlecchabhāṣāṃ śikṣeta | mleccho ha vā eṣa yad apaśabda iti hi vijñāyate | tasmāc chiṣyam upanīya sādhuśabdāñ chikṣayet saṃdhyopāsanāgnīndhanāni" ityādi (cf. VaDh 6.41) | kāyikaṃ tu mṛdvārilakṣaṇaṃ prasiddham | anye tu pañca śaucāny ācakṣate | tathā hi |

                    	satyaṃ śaucaṃ manaḥśaucaṃ śaucam indriyanigrahaḥ |

                    	sarvabhūtadayā śaucaṃ jalaśaucaṃ tu pañcamam || iti |

ācārāś cāgnīndhanādyā āśramasaṃbandhinaḥ | varṇasaṃbandhino 'steyādyāḥ | śikṣayed iti copadeśāt prāg upanayanād apravṛttiḥ | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "prāg upanayāt kāmacāravādabhakṣaḥ" iti (GDh 2.1) | yady api kaścit prājñaḥ svayaṃ jānīyāt, tasyāpy anupanītasyānadhikāro gautamavacanād eva | kālalakṣaṇārthaṃ copanayagrahaṇam, na saṃskārārtham, kālasyāpekṣitatvāt | varṇadharmā hi janmānantaram aśaktyā bādhyamānās tasyāś ca pratipuruṣam aniyatatvād avadhyarthaniyatakālāpekṣiṇas tatparatvenopanayanaśrutiṃ parigṛhṇanti | tathā cātharvaṇānāṃ vitānakalpaḥ "anenasaḥ puro 'ṣṭamād vasantāt kumārakāḥ kāmaṃ caranti samrāḍdharmaṇaḥ pañcatvayājinaḥ" iti kālaparatā darśayati | strīṇām apy ā vivāhāt kāmacāritvam, tasyaiva vaidikatvavacanāt | yathāha manuḥ |

                    	vaivāhiko vidhiḥ strīṇāṃ saṃskāro vaidikaḥ smṛtaḥ | iti | (MDh 2.67)

yadā ca niścitaṃ vaidikatvenopanayanaṃ vivāho vā pravartate, tatsāmānyāt tadaivānye 'pi varṇadharmā ity avaseyam | tathā nyāyavidho yājñikāḥ paṭhanti: "api vā vedatulyatvād upanayanena pravarteran" iti (PMS 6.2.22) | śūdrasya tv avadhyarthakālānupadeśāt sāmarthyaṃ niyāmakaṃ, ṣoḍaśābdaṃ vā prāg bālatvasmṛteh "bālo vāpy ūnaṣoḍaśaḥ" iti (ViDh 54.33) | brāhmaṇānām api paramopanayanakālāt prāg anupanītānāṃ kāmacāritvaṃ kecit strīṇāṃ cartutrayāt, sa hi paramo vivāhakāla iti | tat tu pramāṇaśūnyatvān nātīvānumanyate, prāthamakalpikakālalakṣaṇāyaivopanayanaṃ yataḥ | tathā cānenasaḥ puro'ṣṭamād ity uktam evety alaṃ prasaṅgena || 15 ||

 

_idānīṃ śaucābhidhitsayā tannimittatvān mūtrapurīṣotsarge vidhim āha |_

 

**              	divāsaṃdhyāsu karṇasthabrahmasūtra udaṅmukhaḥ |**

**              	kuryān mūtrapurīṣe tu rātrau ced dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ || 1.16 ||**

 

divā saṃdhyayoś ca karṇāropitayajñopavīta udaṅmukho mūtrapurīṣe kuryāt | rātrāv apy evam | dakṣiṇāmukhatvaṃ tu viśeṣaḥ | cecchabdād yadā kuryāt tadaivam iti gamyate | tuśabdo 'vadhāraṇārthaḥ | mūtrapurīṣe evaivaṃ kuryāt, nānyad api reta-utsargādi | yad vā caśabdārthe smṛtyantaropasaṅgrahaṇāya | yathāha śaṅkhaḥ: "vagyato 'vaguṇṭhitaśirā bhūmim anatardhāya mehet" iti | upaviṣṭaś ca, utthānavacanāt || 16 ||

 

_kiṃ punas tasminn eva deśe śaucaṃ kartavyam | nety āha |_

 

**              	gṛhītaśiśnaś cotthāya mṛdbhir abhyuddhṛtair jalaiḥ |**

**              	gandhalepakṣayakaraṃ śaucaṃ kuryād atandritaḥ || 1.17 ||**

 

caśabdāt pūrvam api gṛhītaśiśnaḥ kuryāt | utthāya tasmād deśāt | mṛdbhir abhyuddhṛtair jalaiḥ śaucaṃ kuryāt | mṛdbhir iti bahuvacanaṃ smṛtyantaroktaparimāṇaprāptyartham | yathāha manuḥ |

                    	ekā liṅge gude tisras tathaikatra kare daśa | iti | (MDh 5136)

yat tu smṛtyantaroktaṃ "pañcāpāne" (DkSm 5.5) iti, tad agnihotriviṣayaṃ draṣṭavyaṃ, pulastyavacanāt:

                    	snātakasya trayo 'pāne pañcāpāne 'gnihotriṇaḥ |

                    	sarvān eva gṛhastheṣu śaucakalpān niyojayet || iti |

etad eva dviguṇaṃ naiṣṭhikasya triguṇam apatnīkavanasthasya caturguṇaṃ jñānabhikṣoḥ | mānavāt tu dviguṇādyupakurvāṇādīnām (MDh 5.137) | yathāha vyāsaḥ |

                    	śuklaṃ dhautaṃ yathā vastraṃ malinaṃ tad bhavet punaḥ |

                    	nirmalaṃ tu bhavet kleśāt strīpuṃvargāśramās tathā ||

                    	prāyaścittaṃ ca daṇḍaṃ ca śaucaṃ cāto yathākramam |

                    	kalpyam utkṛṣṭam utkṛṣṭe madhaṃ madhye 'dhame 'dhamam || iti |

yat tu mṛdviśeṣaparimānaṃ dakṣoktam,

                    	ardhaprasṛtimātrā tu prathamā mṛd udāhṛtā | (DkSm 5.7)

iti, tat tritve sati gandhalepāpakarṣaṇe ca virodhāt pūrvā pūrvā bhūyasī parā parā mṛd alpety evam upalakṣaṇārthaṃ vijñeyam | yat tu tatraiva mūtraśaucam,

                    	ekā liṅge tu dātavyā tathaikatra kare trayaḥ |

iti, tat kevalamūtraviṣayam, anyatra karaśaucasya tāntrikatvāt | sarvāśramāṇāṃ caitad eva mūtraśaucaṃ, viśeṣānabhidhānāt | gṛhasthasya caitad iti na dviguṇakalpanā | tathā mṛllakṣaṇam apy anveṣyam,

                    	valmīkākhūtkaro (tke?) vā jalāt pathi kṛtā ca yā |

                    	kṛtaśaucāvaśiṣṭā ca ṣaḍbhiḥ śaucaṃ na vidyate ||

ityādi | abhyuddhṛtair jalaiḥ, jalāśayāt pāṇyādinā | gandhalepakṣyakaram iti | tathā mṛd grahītavyā, yathā tisṛbhir eva gandhalepakṣayo bhaviṣyatīty arthaḥ | śleṣmādiviṣyaṃ vaitad draṣṭavyam, anyatra gandhāpakarṣaṇād eva lepāpakarṣaṇsiddheḥ | atandritaḥ analasaḥ | yathāvidhiṃ śaucaṃ kuryād iti vidhiḥ, na yadetyarthaḥ (?) | yad vā mṛdbhir adhiś ca yathāvihitaṃ śaucaṃ kuryuḥ | vihitaparimāṇābhir yathāśramaṃ śaucaṃ kuryāt | yasya tu viśeṣaparimāṇaṃ nāmnātaṃ sa mṛjjalair gandhalepakṣayakaraṃ śaucaṃ kuryāc chūdrādiḥ | tathā ca pitāmahaḥ |

                    	triṣu ye nopanīyante śūdrāḥ saudhanvanā striyaḥ |

                    	gandhalepāpaka(rṣaṇaṃ?) teṣāṃ śaucaṃ mṛdambhasā || iti | || 17 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvan mṛdvārilakṣaṇam śaucaṃ nirvartya tasmād deśād apakramya pādau prakṣālya tataḥ,_

 

**              	antarjānu śucau deśa upaviṣṭa udaṅmukhaḥ |**

**              	prāg vā brāhmeṇa tīrthena dvijo nityam upaspṛśet || 1.18 ||**

 

prāg vā praṅmukho vety arthaḥ | smṛtyantarāc ca baddhaśikho baddhakakṣya ā maṇibandhanāt pāṇī prakṣālya brāhmeṇa tīrthena dvijo nityam upaspṛśet | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "prāṅmukha udaṅmukho vā śaucam ārabheta | śucau deśa āsīno dakṣiṇaṃ bāhuṃ jānvantarā kṛtvā yajñopavīty ā maṇibandhanāt pāṇī prakṣālya vāgyataḥ" ityādi (GDh 1.36) | dvijagrahaṇaṃ stryādivyāvṛttyartham | nityaśabdāt sarvāśrameṣv ayam evācamanakalpaḥ | sūtakādāv py anivṛttir ity anye || 18 ||

 

_brāhmeṇa tīrthenety uktam | tasya cālaukikatvāl lakṣaṇam āha |_

 

**              	kaniṣṭhādeśinyaṅguṣṭhamūlāny agraṃ karasya ca |**

**              	prajāpatipitṛbrahmadaivatīrthāny anukramāt || 1.19 ||**

 

brāhmaprasaṅgād anyany api tīrthāni kāryaupayikatvād ucyante | tīrtham iti ca dakṣiṇahaste 'vatārapradeśanāmadheyam | loke 'py udakādyavatāre tīrthaśabdaḥ prasiddhaḥ | tāni ca viśeṣakāryaupayikatvāt stutyarthaṃ devatābhir ākhyāyante | arthataś caturṇām avagatānāṃ[^5]<sup>[5]</sup> vyavahārarthaṃ viśeṣasaṃjñāḥ kathyante | kaniṣṭhāmūle prājāpatyam | deśinīmūle pitryam | deśiny aṅguṣṭhānantarāṅguliḥ | tasyāṅguṣṭhasya cāntarāla ityarthaḥ | brāhmaṃ tv aṅguṣṭhamūle | karāgre daivam | tatra brāhmeṇopaspṛśed iti prakṛtasaṃbandhaḥ | tathā ca śāṭyāyanakaḥ kalpaḥ: "dakṣiṇe brāhmaṇahaste pañca tīrthāni bhavanti | prāṅmukhaś cet purastād daivaṃ, dakiṇataḥ pitryaṃ, paścād brāhmam, uttarataḥ prājāpatyaṃ, madhye pārameṣṭhyam" ityādi | vṛddhavāsiṣṭhe 'py evam eva | madhye saumyam iti tu viśeṣaḥ | ācāryasya pañcatīrthānabhidhānaṃ tasya kamaṇḍalūpasparśanādiviniyogenālpaprayojanatvāt | brāhmaṇagrahaṇaṃ codāharaṇopalakṣaṇārtham anyaparatvāt | savye pāṇau virodhāt tīrthābhāva eva | ataś ca brāhmopadeśād eva dakṣiṇenācamanam iti jñāyate | tathā coktaṃ "dakṣiṇenācamanam" iti |

 

_upaspṛśed ity uktam | sādhāraṇaś cālambhanasnāneṣūpasparśanaśabdaḥ | tasya guṇavidhānato vākyaśeṣān nirṇayaḥ | kāni puns tāni guṇavidhānānīty ata āha |_

 

**              	triḥ prāśyāpo dvir unmṛjyāt khāni cordhvam upaspṛśet |**

 

trir apaḥ pītvā dvir unmṛjet | ucchabdaḥ parer arthe, dṛṣṭārthatvāt | ata eva parimārjanaṃ mukhasya, khāni cordhvam upaspṛśed iti vacanāt | ūrdhvam iti khāni śīrṣaṇyāni cakṣurādīny ucyante | caśabdād adhaś ca, "pādāv ukṣen mūrdhani ca dadyān nābhiṃ copaspṛśet" iti smṛtyantarānusārāt | pūrvaṃ ca pādābhyukṣaṇaṃ tata indriyālambhaḥ | upaśabdaprayogāc ca bahiḥ sparśaṇaṃ, nākṣṇoḥ | atra prakṛtatvād adbhiḥ | dakṣādyuktaś cāṅgulīniyamo 'nuroddhavyaḥ | aviśeṣāc caśabdasāmarthāc cācamanaprayogabhedo 'pi | yatha: "saṃhatābhis tisṛbhiḥ pūrvam āsyam evam upaspṛśet" ityādi |

 

_kiṃlakṣaṇāḥ punar āpa ācamanayogyāḥ | tad āha |_

**              	adbhis tu prakṛtisthābhir hīnābhiḥ phenabudbudaiḥ || 1.20 ||**

 

adbhir iti punaḥ śrutir guṇārthā | tuśabdo vivekārthaḥ | adbhir eva nānyasaṃsṛṣṭābhiḥ | tathā ca śaṅkhaḥ: "uddhṛtya paripūtābhiḥ" iti | prakṛtisthāḥ svabhāvataḥ sthitāḥ akṣārā aśṛtāś cety arthaḥ | tathā ca āpastambaḥ: "na taptābhiś cākāraṇāt" (ĀpDh 1.15.6) iti | ātapāditaptāś tu jalāśaye na duṣyanti | mānavaṃ ca "anuṣṇābhiḥ" (MDh 2.16) iti | śaṅkhavacanād aśṛtābhir iti vyākhyeyam | tathā cāturāpavādaḥ |

                    	anāpadi dvijātīnām aśṛtena yathāmbhasā |

                    	tadvad eva bhavec chuddhiḥ śṛtena śṛtapāyinām || iti |

"na taptābhiś cākāraṇād" ity asyāpy ayam evārthaḥ | ṛjv anyat || 20 ||

 

_kiṃ punas tāsāṃ parimāṇam | ucyate |_

 

**              	hṛtkaṇṭhatālugābhis tu yathāsaṃkhyaṃ dvijātayaḥ |**

**              	śudhyeran strī ca śūdraś ca sakṛt spṛṣṭābhir antataḥ || 1.21 ||**

 

tuśabdāt prāgghṛdayaprāpter aśuddhiḥ, na parato gamane | "strī ca śūdraś ca sakṛt spṛṣṭhābhir antataḥ" | pūrvaś cakāra utkṛṣyaivakārārtho vyākhyeyaḥ | spṛṣṭābhir evety arthaḥ | tataś cānyaparisaṃkhyānād indriyālambhanādinivṛttiḥ | parimārjanaṃ tu dṛṣṭārthatvāt pravartate | tathā ca baudhāyanaḥ: "na budbudābhir na phenābhir na kaluṣābhir na hasan na jalpan na tiṣṭhan na vilokayan na prahvo na praṇato na muktaśikho nābaddhakakṣyo na bahirjānuḥ śabdam akurvan trir apo hṛdayaṅgamāḥ pibed dviḥ parimṛjyāt | trir ity eke | sakṛd ubhayaṃ śūdrasya striyāś ca" (BDh 1.8.17–22) iti sakṛt parimārjanaṃ darśayati | antato jihvyety arthaḥ | tṛtīyārthe pañcamī || 21 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvad ācamanavidhim uktvānantaraṃ snānādividhim āha |_

 

**              	snānam abdaivatair mantrair mārjanaṃ prāṇasaṃyamaḥ |**

**              	sūryasya cāpy upasthānaṃ gāyatryāḥ pratyahaṃ japaḥ || 1.22 ||**

 

kārya iti śeṣaḥ | snānaṃ pratyahaṃ kuryāt | tasya ca vidhir ācāryeṇaivānyatrābhihitaḥ |

                    	vidyamāne prabhūte hi nālpe snānaṃ smācaret | iti |

ubhayātmakaṃ hi snānaṃ śaucam ācāraś ca | tatra kecit pañcavidham āhuḥ "āgneyaṃ vāruṇam"[^6] ityādi | tat punar gṛhasthsyāpadviṣayaṃ draṣṭavyam | iha tv ambhasaiva snānam daṇḍavad āplavavacanād brahmacāriṇaḥ | saṃdhyopāsanādayas tv ācārāḥ | tatrāyaṃ saṃdhyopāsanavidhiḥ "abdaivatair mantrair mārjanam," "āpohi ṣṭhā" ityevamādibhiḥ | prāṇasaṃyamaś ca vakṣyamāṇaḥ | "sūryasya cāpy upasthānam," caśabdād drupadāyāś ca | tathā ca saṃdhyopāsanavidhau hārītaḥ |

                    	yataḥ prāṇān samādhāya trir japed drupadām ṛcam |

                    	trisaṃdhyam enaso mukto dīpikeva virājate || iti |

sūryopasthānaṃ ca saurībhyām ṛgbhyām | yathoktam |

                    	āpohiṣṭhātṛcenādbhir mārjayitvā śucir naraḥ |

                    	athod u tyam iti dvābhyām upatiṣṭheta bhāskaram || iti |

sāvitrīṃ ca gāyatrīṃ "tat savitur" ity oṃkāravyāhṛtipūrvikāṃ pratyahaṃ japet | tathā ca manuḥ |

                    	etad akṣaram etāṃ ca japan vyāhṛtipūrvikām |

                    	saṃdhyayor ubhayor vipro vedapuṇyena yujyate || iti | (MDh 2.78)

apiśabdāt snānādy api nityam | snānaṃ ca daṇḍavad āplavanaṃ brahmacāriṇo 'viruddham | gautamīyaṃ tu sukhārthasya pratiṣedhaḥ (cf. GDh 1.13) | tathā ca āpastambaḥ "nāpsu ślāghamānaḥ snāyāt" (ĀpDh 1.2.30) ity adṛṣṭārtham aniṣiddham iti darśayati | evaṃ manuḥ |

                    	nityaṃ snātvā śuciḥ kuryād devarṣipitṛtarpaṇam | iti | (MDh 2.176)

devatarpaṇādiprāptyartho vāpiśabdo vyākhyeyaḥ, asmād eva manuvacanāt (?) || 22 ||

 

_prāṇāyāmaḥ kartavya ity uktam | tatsvarūpam āha |_

 

**              	gāyatrīṃ śirasā sārdhaṃ japed vyāhṛtipūrvikām |**

**              	pratipraṇavasaṃyuktāṃ trir ayaṃ prāṇasaṃyamaḥ || 1.23 ||**

 

"mahar janas tapaḥ satyaṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ suvas tat savitur vareṇyam" ity ṛcam |

                    	sāvitryāś ca śiraḥ puṇyam āpo jyotī raso 'mṛtam | iti |

ayaṃ ca prāṇasaṃyamas triḥ kārya iti yojanīyam | anye tv evaṃrūpāṃ sāvitrīṃ trir japed ayaṃ ca prāṇasaṃyama ity varṇayanti | saṃyatocchvāsena cāyaṃ japaḥ kāryaḥ, samākhyānāt | tathā ca manuḥ |

                    	trir japed āyataprāṇaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ sa ucyate | iti | (MDh 2.83 addition)

 

_pāṭhakramāc ca mārjanāt parataḥ prāṇāyāmaprāptāv āha |_

 

**              	prāṇān āyamya saṃśuddhas tṛcenābdaivatena tu |**

**              	japann āsīta sāvitrīṃ pratyag ā tārakodayam || 1.24 ||**
