yad vā, ayaṃ sāyaṃsaṃdhyaviṣaya eva kramaḥ | pūrvaṃ prāṇān āyamya saṃśodhanaṃ kāryam | saṃśabdāc cādbhir mārjanaṃ darbhaiḥ | tṛcenety adhikanivṛttyartham | punarvacanam atraiva | ataś ca madhyaṃdina ādhikyam aviruddham | tuśabdaś caśabdārthe drupadāprāptyarthaḥ | ardhāstamita āditye prāṇān āyamya "āpo hi ṣṭhā" iti tṛcena mārjayitvā drupadāṃ ca japtvā sūryam upasthāya japann āsīta sāvitrīm oṃkāramahāvyāhṛtipūrvikāṃ pratyaṅmukha ā nakṣatrodayāt | yad api "ā jyotiṣo darśanāt" ity uktam, tad apy udayopalakṣaṇārtham eva, darśanasyāniyatatvāt | dvayaṃ cānena ślokena vidhīyate: prāṇāyāmasya pūrvakālatā sāyaṃ ca saṃdhyāvidhānam, ā nakṣatradarśanād iti liṅgāt | kālaviśiṣṭasaṃdhyopāsanavidhir vā syāt | evaṃ ca "tṛcenābdaivatena" ity adhikanivṛttyarthaṃ punarvacam arthavat | tathā ca snānavidhau spaṣṭīkariṣyate || 24 ||

 

_kiṃ sāyam eva saṃdhyopāsanam uta prātar api | yadā ca prātaḥ, tadā kim evam eva | ucyate |_

 

**              	saṃdhyāṃ prāṅ prātar evaṃ hi tiṣṭhed ā sūryadarśanāt |**

**              	agnikāryaṃ tataḥ kuryāt saṃdhyayor ubhayor api || 1.25 ||**

 

evam eva prātaḥ saṃdhyopāsanaṃ kuryāt | ayaṃ tu viśeṣaḥ: prāṅmukhas tiṣṭhan nakṣatradarśanād ārabhya ā sūryadharśanāj japaṃ kuryāt | madhyaṃdine tu viśeṣānabhidhānāt prāṅmukha udaṅmukho vāsīnaḥ śaktyā sāvitrīṃ japet | anye tv ādityābhimukhas tiṣṭhan sahasrādisaṃkhyātāñ japed ity āhuḥn, hārītavacanāt |

                    	devī sahasraśīrṣā tu śatamadhyā daśāvarā |

                    	japed ataḥ sahasrāntāṃ śatamadhyāṃ daśāvarām || iti |

tat tu kāryoparodhād agnihotriviṣayaṃ draṣṭavyam | prāk sūryodayād upasthānānupapatter utkarṣa iti kecit | na tv evaṃ samācāraḥ | abhividhāvāṅ draṣṭavyaḥ,

                    	ṛṣayo dīrghasaṃdhyatvād dīrgham āyur avāpnuyuḥ | (MDh 4.94)

ity smṛtyantaradarśanāt | saṃdhyeti copasthānakarmaṇo nāmadheyaṃ, kālasya cānyataḥ prāptatvāt | yathāha gārgyaḥ |

                    	pūrvāṃ saṃdhyāṃ sanakṣatrāṃ prātar ā bhāskarodayāt |

                    	ā tārakodayāt sāyaṃ paścimāṃ sadivākarām || iti |

"ardhāstamitabhāskarām" iti saṃvartaḥ | mārjanaṃ tv ātmasaṃskārārthaṃ saṃdhyāṅgaṃ ca | anye tu japakarmaprādhānyaṃ manyante | yathāha manuḥ |

                    	pūrvāṃ saṃdhyāṃ japaṃs tiṣṭhet sāvitrīm ārkadarśanāt | iti | (MDh 4.93)

tiṣṭhañ japed iti vibhaktivyatyayas tathā syāt | evaṃ ca saṃdhyām upāsyāgnikāryaṃ kuryāt | tasya vidhir gṛhyād avagantavyaḥ | "saṃdhyayor ubhayoḥ" saṃdhyāśabdaś cāyam anantarakālopalakṣaṇārthaḥ, virodhāt | ubhayagrahaṇaṃ cādarārtham | "kṛtāgnikāryo bhuñjīta" (YDh 1.35) ity agnikāryam anyat kartavyam ity āśaṅkā mā bhūd ity ādaraḥ | anye tu saṃdhyayor ity aṅgāṅgibhāvaṃ manyante | tat punar nātīva peśalam, "tataḥ" iti kramābhidhānāt saptamīnirdeśāc ca | apiśabdo nityatvajñāpanārthaḥ | ahar ahar ity anukarṣaṇāt || 25 ||

 

_evam agnikāryaṃ nirvartya,_

 

**              	tato 'bhivādayed vṛddhān asāv aham iti bruvan |**

**              	guruṃ caivāpy upāsīta svādhyāyārthaṃ samāhitaḥ || 1.26 ||**

 

tata iti kramārtham | "abhivādayed vṛddhān" vidyābhijanavṛttavayodhanādibhiḥ | asāv iti nāmādeśaḥ | itikaraṇaḥ prakārārthaḥ | yathāha baudhāyanaḥ: "kāmam anyasmai sādhuvṛttāya guruṇānujñātaḥ asāv ahaṃ bho iti śrotre saṃspṛśya manasaḥ samādhānārtham adhastāj jānvor ā padbhām" ityādi (BDh 1.3.26–28) | śrotrasaṃsparśaś ca samācārād deśaniyata iti kecit | yad āpastambenoktam: "dakṣiṇaṃ bāhuṃ śrotrasamaṃ prasārya brāhmaṇo 'bhivādayet" ityādi (ĀpDh 1.5.16) | tad dṛṣṭārthatvād dūrasthaviṣayaṃ draṣṭavyam | abhivādyānabhivādyaviveko 'nveṣṭavyaḥ | yathā: "nāprayato nāprayatāya" ityādi (BDh 1.3.29) | yathā: "saminmṛdudakumbhahasto nābhivādayet" (BDh 1.3.31) | anyad apy evaṃsaṃyuktaṃ "na samavāye 'bhivādanam atyantaśo bhrātṛpatnīnāṃ jātavīryaś ced" ityādi (BDh 1.3.32–33) | "nāmno 'nte ye na plutiṃ vidur" ityādi | "guruṃ caivāpy upāsīta" iti tuśabdārthaś caśabdaḥ | evaśabdaś ca makārāntaḥ | guruṃ tv evam upasaṃgṛhṇīyāt, nābhivādayed ity arthaḥ | yathāha manuḥ |

                    	vyatyastapāṇinā kāryam upasaṃgrahaṇaṃ guroḥ |

                    	savyena savyaḥ spraṣṭavyo dakṣiṇena tu dakṣiṇaḥ || (MDh 2.72)

iti vacanāt | yat tv āpastamboktaṃ, "dakṣiṇaṃ pādaṃ pāṇibhyāṃ parimṛjya hastaṃ gṛhṇīyāt" (ĀpDh 1.5.21) iti, tat prasādaviśeṣārthatvān naimittikam | pūrvaṃ guror upasaṃgrahaṇam, "guruṇānujñātaḥ" iti vacanāt | na kevalam upasaṃgṛhṇīyāt, apy upāsīta svādhyāyārthaṃ samāhitaḥ praṇihitamanāḥ | yad vā, antareṇāpi svādhyāyārtham upāsītety evam apiśabdārthaḥ || 26 ||

 

_ayaṃ cānyas taddharmaḥ |_

 

**              	āhūtaś cāpy adhīyīta labdhaṃ cāsmai nivedayet |**

**              	hitaṃ cāsyācaren nityaṃ manovākkāyakarmabhiḥ || 1.27 ||**

 

āhūto 'vicārayan guruṇā gacchet | caśabdād anāhūtaś ca | kiṃ cānyat | apy adhīyīta guruṇānujñātaḥ, apiśabdāt | prakārārtho vāpiśabdaḥ, "arthanityaḥ parīkṣeta" (Nirukta 2.1) iti śabdajñā yataḥ | prakāraṃ cāha gautamaḥ: "pāṇinā savyam upasaṃgṛhya" ityādi (GDh 1.46) | labdhaṃ ca baikṣam asmai nivedayet, lābhāntarābhāvāt | yad vā, anyad apy ayācitam apratyākhyeyaṃ, brāhmaṇādyāhṛtam asmād eva vacanād gṛhṇīyāt | gurvarthaṃ vā tadanujñayā bhikṣeteti | tatha ca āpastambaḥ: "sarvaṃ lābham āharan gurave" (ĀpDh 1.3.25) iti sarvagrahaṇād bhaikṣasya pṛthaṅnivedanād etad eva jñāpayati | yat tu "pakvānnasvāmino bhikṣavaḥ" iti, tad ātmavṛttyarthaṃ draṣṭavyam | "hitaṃ tasyācaren nityam", caśabdāt priyaṃ ca | tathāha gautamaḥ: "yuktaḥ priyahitayoḥ" iti (GDh 2.30) | apriyam api ca tadātve hitaṃ bhavaty evauṣadhādi | ato bhedenābhidhānam | nityaśabdāc ca samāvṛtto 'pīti gamyate | manovākkāyakarmabhir iti sarvathety arthaḥ | yathāhāmnāyaḥ: "yas te na druhyet katamac canāhaṃ ye guruṃ nādriyante viprā manasā vācā karmaṇā vā" iti (cf. VaDh 2.9, 11) | hitaprakāraviśeṣaś ca lokataḥ śāstrāntarataś cāvagamayitavyaḥ | ete brahmacāriṇo niyamāḥ || 27 ||

 

_guroḥ punaḥ |_

 

**              	kṛtajño 'drohī medhāvī śuciḥ kulyo 'nasūyakāḥ |**

**              	adhyāpyāḥ sādhuśaktāptasvārthdā dharmatas tv ime || 1.28 ||**

 

kṛtajñaḥ prasiddha eva | adrohī sarvabhūtānām, ācāryādrohasya hitavacanād eva siddhatvāt | śucir vyākhyātaḥ | kulyaḥ kulīnaḥ | anasūyakāḥ asūyārahitāḥ | asūyā paramarmasūcanam abhinayādinā, parivādo vā | uktavakṣyamāṇaviśeṣaṇaṃ vaitad, bahuvacanasāmarthyāt | ekavacanapāṭhe 'py ayam adhyāpyāntaropanyāsaḥ | sādhuḥ sadbhir vyākhyātaḥ | śakto 'bhiyogagrahaṇasamartha ūhāpohakṣamo vā | āpto mitram | svaḥ putravyatirekeṇa bhrātrādiḥ | arthado dravyadaḥ, vidyāprado vā | "vidyā manuṣyāś ca vihitāḥ parivartakena" (VaDh 2.39) iti smṛtyantarāt | dravyadaś cāpaṇena, dharmata it vacanād bhṛtakādhyāpanapratiṣeḍhac ca | ete dharmato 'dhyāpyāḥ | tuśabdāc ca vṛttyartham anyo 'pi | yathāha manuḥ |

                    	ācāryaputraḥ śuśrūṣur jñānado dhārmikaḥ śuciḥ |

                    	śakto 'rthado 'rthī svaḥ sādhur adhyāpyā daśa dharmataḥ || iti | (MDh 2.109)

ācāryacchalena śiṣyasyāmī dharmā vidhīyante | evaṃguṇo 'dhyāpyaḥ | tena caivaṃ bhavitavyam ity arthaḥ | amī ca brahmacāriṇa eva || 28 ||

 

**              	daṇḍājinopavītāni mekhalām caiva dhārayet |**

**              	brāhmaṇeṣu cared bhaikṣam anindyeṣv ātmavṛttaye || 1.29 ||**

 

evaśabdo makārānto draṣṭavyaḥ, smṛtyantaroktaprakārārthaḥ | caśabdo 'nuktasamuccayārthaḥ | yathāha gautamaḥ: "vāsāṃsi śāṇakṣaumacīrakutapāḥ sarveṣām" ityādi (GDh 1.17) | daṇḍaprakāraś ca: "bailvapālāśau brāhmaṇadaṇḍau" ityādi (GDh 1.22) | "kṛṣṇarurubastājināni" (GDh 1.16) ity ajinaprakāraḥ | tāni cottarīyāṇi | yathāha āpastambaḥ: "ajinam evottarīyaṃ dhārayeyuḥ" iti (ĀpDh 1.3.10) | upavītaṃ ca | yathāha baudhāyanaḥ: "kauśaṃ sautraṃ vā tris trivṛd yajñōpavītam | ā nābher dakṣiṇaṃ bāhum avadhāya śiro 'vadadhyāt" iti (BDh 1.8.5–7) | mānavaṃ tu: "uddhṛte dakṣiṇe pāṇau" (MDh 2.63) ityādi vinyāsārtham | yat tu varṇaviśeṣeṇa "kārpāsam upavītaṃ syād viprasya" ityādi (MDh 2.44), taj jātukarṇivacanāt "dīkṣitau ced rājanyavaiśyau śāṇāvike kuryātām" iti dīkṣitaviṣayam | mekhalāprakāraś ca: "mauñjī trivṛt samā ślakṣṇā" ityādi (MDh 2.42) | etāni ca daṇḍādīny aviruddheṣu kāleṣu nityaṃ dhāryāṇi | yat tu manunoktam: "pratigṛhyepsitaṃ daṇḍam" iti (MDh 2.48), tad āpdy anyadaṇḍagrahaṇārthaṃ draṣṭavyam | "brāhmaṇeṣu cared baikṣam anindyeṣv ātmavṛttaye," na sarvārtham | brāhamaṇakuleṣv iti cāyaṃ prathamaḥ kalpaḥ | kṣatriyavaiśyakuleṣv iti cāyam anukalpaḥ | śūdrakuleṣv apīty āpatkalpaḥ | tathā cāha manuḥ |

                    	vedayajñair ahīnānāṃ praśastānāṃ svakarmasu |

                    	brahmacāry āhared bhaikṣaṃ gṛhebhyaḥ prayato 'nvaham ||

                    	sarvaṃ vā vicared grāmaṃ pūrvoktānām asambhave | iti | (MDh 2.183, 185)

"sārvavarṇikaṃ bhaikṣacaraṇam" (GDh 2.35) iti ca gautamaḥ | brāhmaṇavacane 'pi brāhmaṇstrībhyo bhaikṣacaraṇam | yathāha āpastambaḥ: "apratyācakṣāṇām" iti (ĀpDh 1.3.26) | āmnāyaś ca: "yasyā ācārabhūyiṣṭhaṃ ślakṣṇatā ca tāṃ bhikṣed ity āhus tallokyam iti | atha yady anyāṃ bhikṣitavyāṃ na vindetāpi svām evācāryānīṃ bhikṣeta" iti striyaṃ bhikṣitavyāṃ darśayati | "svasti vācya bhikṣādānam appūrvam"[^7] (GDh 5.18) ity etad api strīviṣayam eva | dātur vaitad ity adoṣaḥ || 29 ||

 

_brāhmaṇaviṣayaiveyaṃ baikṣavṛttiḥ | itarayoḥ pratigrahānadhikārād ityāśaṅkāṃ nirākariṣṇur guṇopadeśadvāreṇa prāptim āha |_

 

**              	ādimadhyāvasāneṣu bhavacchabdopalakṣitā |**

**              	brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśāṃ bhaikṣacaryā yathākramam || 1.30 ||**

 

nigadavyākhyānaḥ ślokaḥ || 30 ||

 

_vṛttyarthatvād avidyamānadhanasyaiva prāptāv āha |_

 

**              	brahmacarye sthito naikam annam adyād anāpadi |**

**              	brāhmaṇaḥ kāmam aśnīyāc chrāddhe vratam apīḍayan || 1.31 ||**

 

sthitavacanād anyathā vṛttāv abrahmacārī syāt | "naikasmin gṛhe buñjītānāpadi" iti bruvann āpadi pratiprasavād vidyamānadhanasyāpi baikṣeṇa vṛttiniyamaṃ darśayati | "brāhmaṇaḥ kāmam aśnīyāt," bhikṣārtham āgato 'nindyair āmantritaś ca | na rājanyavaiśyau |  vratam apīḍayan, madhumāṃsādivarjam ity arthaḥ| tathā ca manuḥ |

                    	vratavad daivadevatye pitrye karmaṇy upasthite |

                    	kāmam abhyarthito 'śnīyād vratam asya na lupyate || iti | (MDh 2.189)

anantaraṃ ca brāhmaṇastutyā rājanyavaiśyayor anadhikāraṃ darśayati | yat tu brahmacāriṇaḥ śrāddhabhojane prāyaścittm āmnātaṃ, tat pūrvedyur āmantritasyeti draṣṭavyam || 31 ||

 

_uktāś ca brahmacāriṇo niyamāḥ | yamā ucyante |_

 

**              	madhumāṃsāñjanocchiṣṭaśuktastrīprāṇihiṃsanam |**

**              	bhāskarālokanāślīlaparivādāṃś ca varjayet || 1.32 ||**

 

yady api madhvaśanam āmnāye 'numatam, "tat svādukāram evāśnīyāt" iti, tathāpy ācāryasya na brahmacārī san madhv aśnīyad ity ayam eva pakṣo 'bhimataḥ, anujñānasyāpadviṣyayatvāt | ṛgyajuḥsāmādibhir vyavahāravān vidvān kartavyam ity āpadi madv aśnīyād ity arthaḥ, nānyasmin | tathā ca carakāḥ paṭhanti: "śvetaketuṃ hāruṇeyaṃ brahmacaryaṃ carantaṃ kilāso jagrāha | tam aśvināv ūcatuḥ: 'madhumāṃsau kila te bhaiṣajyam' iti | sa hovāca: 'brahmacaryamānī kathaṃ madv aśnīyām' iti | tau hocatuḥ: 'yadā cātmanā puruṣo jīvati, athānyat sukṛtaṃ karomi' iti | ātmānaṃ hy eva sarvato gopāyet" | atha khalv āhur vājasaneyinaḥ: "ācāryāya madhumāṃse pradāsyāmas taducchiṣṭaṃ bhokṣyāmaḥ | tathā na duṣyāmahe, tad yathāgnihotrocchiṣṭam eva nas tad bhaviṣyati" ityādinā āpadviṣayatā vājasaneyivākyasyeti vijñāyate | tataś cānāpady anyathābhakṣaṇe ca prāyaścittam | añjanagrahaṇaṃ tv alaṅkāralakṣaṇārtham | ucchiṣṭaṃ cāguroḥ | tathā cāhuḥ: "ucchiṣṭam aguror abhojyam" iti | śuktaṃ paryuṣitaṃ bhakṣādi | striyaś ca saṃbhāṣaṇādāv api, anyatrāvaśyakāryāt | tathā ca āpastambaḥ: "strībhir yāvadarthaṃ saṃbhāṣeta" iti (ĀpDh 1.3.16) | prāṇihiṃsanaṃ manasāpi | tathā ca bharadvājaḥ: "manasā prāṇihiṃsāyāṃ trir drupadām āvartayet" iti | bhāskarālokanam udayāstamayādau | yathāhuḥ |

                    	nekṣetodyantam ādityaṃ nāstaṃ yantaṃ kadācana | iti | (MDh 4.37)

aślīlaṃ saṅkalpanam api, "yadi vedam apratirūpaṃ saṃkalpayati" iti śruteḥ | yat tu "śuktā vācaḥ" (GDh 2.19) iti, tat prāyaścittaviśeṣārtham | parivādaṃ dviṣadbhyo 'pi | caśabdaḥ smṛtyantaroktayamaprāptyarthaḥ | yathokam "upānacchatrakāmakrodha" ityādi (GDh 2.13) | auṣadharthaṃ cānalaṅkāratvād añjanādy apratiṣiddham | tathā cāmnāyaḥ: "ātmānaṃ hy eva sarvato gopāyet" iti darśita eva | evam udāharaṇārthaṃ katicid yamaniyamā uktāḥ | sarvathā yān eva gurur ācāryo vā brūyāt, ta eva brahmacāriṇo yamaniyamā ity avaseyam | tathā ca śaunakaḥ: "yad eva vidvān ācāryo vā brūyāt tad evāvicikitsann ācaret | upadeśata eva brahmacāriṇo dharma iti hi vijñāyate" ity āha || 32 ||

 

_kiṃlakṣaṇaḥ punar guruḥ kiṃlakṣaṇo vācārya iti | ucyate |_

 

**              	sa gurur yaḥ kriyāḥ kṛtvā vedam asmai prayacchati |**

**              	upanīya dadad vedam ācāryaḥ sa udāhṛtaḥ || 1.33 ||**

 

niṣekādyāḥ kriyāḥ kṛtvā vedam asmai prayacchati yaḥ, sa gurur ucyate | "niṣekādīni karmāṇi" iti (MDh 2.142) smṛtyantarāt pitety arthaḥ | upanayanam eva kevalaṃ kṛtvā vedaṃ dadad ācāryaḥ sa udāhṛto manvādibhiḥ | tathā cāha manuḥ |

                    	upanīya tu yaḥ śiṣyaṃ vedam adhyāpayed dvijaḥ |

                    	sakalpaṃ sarahasyaṃ ca tam ācāryaṃ pracakṣate || iti (MDh 2.140) || 33 ||

 

_mānyatvajñāpanārthaṃ prasaṅgād ṛtvigupādhyāyāv ucyete |_

 

**              	ekadeśam upādhyāya ṛtvig yajñakṛd ucyate |**

**              	ete mānyā yathāpūrvam ebhyo mātā garīyasī || 1.34 ||**

 

prakṛtasya vedasyaikadeśaṃ dadad upādhyāya ucyate, sarvāṇi vā vedāṅgāni | yathāha manuḥ |

                    	ekadeśaṃ tu vedasya vedāṅgāny api vā punaḥ |

                    	yo 'dhyāpayati vṛttyartham upādhyāyaḥ sa ucyate || iti | (MDh 2.141)

atra ca śloke vṛttyartham apīti yojanīyam | parārthaṃ tu yajñakṛd ṛtvig ucyate | sa ca trividhaḥ | yathāha nāradaḥ |

                    	ṛtvik tu trividhaḥ proktaḥ pūrvair juṣṭaḥ svayaṃ vṛtaḥ |

                    	yadṛcchayā ca yaḥ kuryād ārtvijyaṃ vidhipūrvakam || iti | (NSm 3.10)

yat tu mānavam |

                    	agnyādheyaṃ pākayajñam agniṣṭomādikān makhān |

                    	yaḥ karoti vṛto yajñe sa tasartvig ihocyate || iti | (MDh 2.143)

tad iheti vacanān mānātiśayajñāpanārthaṃ, na tv anyavyāvṛttyartham | eṣāṃ pūrvaḥ pūrvo 'tiśayena mānyaḥ | mātā tu sarvebhyo garīyasīti draṣṭavyam | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "mātety eke" iti (GDh 2.51) | manur apy evaṃvidhād eva pitur mātaraṃ garīyasīm āha |

                    	sahasraṃ tu pitur mātā gauraveṇātiricyate | iti | (MDh 2.145)

anyādṛśas tu pitāpy ācāryād ūnaḥ | tathā ca āpastambaḥ: "tac chreṣṭhaṃ janma śarīram eva mātāpitarau janayataḥ" iti (ĀpDh 1.1.18) | utpādakamātratve 'pi mātaiva pitur garīyasī | yas tu pitā prāg upanayanān niṣekādīni vidhivat kuryāt kārayed vā, annena ca saṃbhāvayet, sa ācāryeṇa tulyaḥ | yathāha manuḥ |

                    	niṣekādīni karmāṇi yaḥ karoti yathāvidhi |

                    	sambhāvayati cānnena sa vipro gurur ucyate || iti | (MDh 2.142)

vipragrahaṇaṃ copalakṣaṇārtham anupanetṛtvāt | mātāpi hi pitrādyapekṣayā saguṇanirguṇatvenālocya mānanīyā | ye tv anye vittādibhir mānyās teṣām atrānupanyāsaḥ, yasmāt tanmānane 'bhyudayo na tv anyathā pratyavāyaḥ | mātṛgrahaṇāc cānyā api striyo mānyā iti jñāyate | yathāha manuḥ |

                    	pitur bhaginyāṃ mātuś ca jyāyasyāṃ ca svasary api |

                    	mātṛvad vṛttim ātiṣṭhen mātā tv ābhyo garīyasī || iti | (MDh 2.133)

pitṛmātṛsaṃbaddhāś ca sarve mānyāḥ smṛtyantarāt samācārāc ca | mānyāś caivaṃ mānitā bhavanti, yadi tatsaṃbaddhā api mānyante | tasmān mānyasaṃbandhino mānyā eva | tebhyaś cānyonyaṃ vittādibhir mānaviśeṣaḥ | amānyasaṃbaddhānām api vittādibhir mānyatvm uktaṃ kāmataḥ | vittādivakyāni ca svāvasare vakṣyāmaḥ | sarvathā "śrutaṃ tu sarvebhyo garīyaḥ" (GDh 6.21) ity ayam eva samastavākyālocanāyām api rāddhāntaḥ | "tanmūlatvād dharmasya" (GDh 6.22) iti hetvabhidhānād vittādīnām api mānakāraṇatvam || 34 ||

 

_bhūyaś ca guror mānyatvaṃ darśayitum āha |_

 

**              	kṛtāgnikāryo bhuñjīta vāgyato gurvanuñayā |**

**              	apośanakriyāpūrvaṃ satkṛtyānnam akutsayan || 1.35 ||**

 

gurvanujñayā satkṛtyānnaṃ bhuñjīteti saṃbandhaḥ | itthaṃ gurur mānyaḥ, yena kṛtāgnikāryasyāpi tadanujñayā bhojanam annasaṃskāraś ca bhavati | agnikāryaṃ tu prātaḥkālīnam evānūdyate gurupraśaṃsārtham | yad vā bhaikṣād agnau homo 'gnikāryaṃ prakaraṇāt, na samidādhānaṃ, tasya "sāyaṃ prātar" iti (ĀpDh 1.4.16) niyamāt | tathā ca āpastambo "bhaikṣād agnau kṛtvā" (ĀpDh 1.3.42) ityādinaitad evāgnikāryam iti darśayati | evaṃ ca bhaikād agnau hutvā gurave nivedya tadanujñayā satkṛtyāpoṣanakriyāpūrvaṃ vāgyato 'śnīyāt | gurunivedaṃ ca bhaikṣasaṃskāro 'dṛṣṭārthaḥ, ātmavṛttaya iti vacanāt | akutsayan annadoṣān anudbhāvayann ity arthaḥ || 35 ||

 

_kiyān punaḥ kāla evaṃ vratacaryāyāḥ | ucyate |_

 

**              	prativedaṃ brahmacaryaṃ dvādaśābdāni pañca vā |**

**              	grahaṇāntikam ity eke keśāntaś caiva ṣoḍaśe || 1.36 ||**

 

parisamāpyaikaṃ vedaṃ vedāntarārambhaḥ | sa cec chāto na naiyamikaḥ | yathāha manuḥ |

                    	vedān adhītya vedau vā vedaṃ vāpi yathākramam | iti | (MDh 3.2)

"grahaṇāntikam ity eke" iti | atretikaraṇo hetvarthaḥ | vedārthatvād brahmacaryasya tad grahaṇāntam eva yuktam ity eke manyante | keśāntas tu sarvapakṣeṣu ṣoḍaśa evābde kartavyaḥ | caśabdas tuśabdasyārthe | evakārasyotkarṣaḥ | keśāntākhyaś ca saṃskāraś cūḍākaraṇād īṣadbhinnaḥ | sa gṛhyād avagantavyaḥ | yadā punaḥ prāk ṣoḍaśābdāt kathaṃcin nopanītas tadā kālaprāptāv anupanītasya tadabhāvaḥ, tadā cāsamāvṛttasyāpi keśāntapravṛttiḥ | tasmiṃs tu kāla upanayanaṃ kāryaṃ prādhānyāt | keśāntasya guṇatvāt kālabādhaḥ | kiṃ punar garbhāṣṭamādikālād ūrdhvam apy upanayanaṃ pravarteta | bāḍhaṃ pravartate | guṇatvāt kālasya yathoktābhāve 'pi pradhānasya pravṛttir aviruddhā || 36 ||

 

_evaṃ tarhi yāvajjīvam upanayanaṃ syāt | nety āha |_

 

**              	ā ṣoḍaśād dvāviṃśāc ca caturviṃśāc ca vatsarāt |**

**              	brahmakṣatraviṣāṃ kāla aupanāyanikaḥ paraḥ || 1.37 ||**

 

ā ṣoḍaśād ity abhividhāv āṅ draṣṭavyaḥ, "dviguṇāṃ gāyatrīm atikramya brāhmaṇō vrātyaḥ syat" iti jātukarṇivacanāt | gautamaś ca "dvyadhikāyā vaiśyasya" (GDh 1.14) ity adhikagrahaṇād etad eva jñāpayati | dvāviṃśāc caturviṃśāc cety atrāpy āṅanuṣaṅgeṇa draṣṭavyaḥ | guṇatve 'pi kālasyātaḥ paraṃ nopanayanam iti || 37 ||

 

_etad eva nindārthavādena spaṣṭīkaroti |_

 

**              	ata ūrdhvaṃ patanty ete sarvadharmabahiṣkṛtāḥ |**

**              	sāvitrīpatitā vrātyā vrātyastomād ṛte kratoḥ || 1.38 ||**

 

ataḥ paraṃ ṣoḍaśād dvāviṃśāc caturviṃśāc ca varṣāt | patanty ete brāhmaṇādayo dvijātikarmabhyaḥ, prāg etasmāt kālād āpady apy anupanayane adhyāpanasāmarthye tu prāthamakalpikāt kālād ūrdhvaṃ patanam eva | yathāha manuḥ |

                    	prabhuḥ prathamakalpasya yo 'nukalpena vartate | (MDh 11.30)

ityādi | tataś ca dvijātikarmahānāt sarvadharmabahiṣkṛtā asaṃvyavahāryā bhavanti | yathā ca āpastambaḥ: "te brahmahasaṃstutās teṣām abhyāgamanaṃ bhojanaṃ vivāha iti ca varjayet" (ĀpDh 1.1.33–34) ityādinā asaṃvyavahāryatāṃ darśayati | kasmāt punar asaṃvyavahāryā bhavanti | yasmāt sāvitrīpatitā vrātyāḥ | sāvitrīśabdaś copanayanakālopalakṣaṇārthaḥ | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ: "ata ūrdhvaṃ patitasāvitrīkā bhavanti | naitān upanayeyuḥ" (VaDh 11.74–75) ityādi | ākhyākaraṇaṃ ca nindāvyavahārārtham | atha kim ete vrātyā eva | na | "vrātyastomād ṛte kratoḥ" | kratugrahaṇaṃ gauravārtham | stomamātravyāvṛttyarthaṃ vā | tathā ca yājñikāḥ "vrātyastomeneṣṭvā vrātyabhāvād virameyur vyavahāryā bhavanti" (KātŚr 22.4.27–28) ity āhuḥ | kāryagauravārthaṃ vā | aprakaraṇe prāyaścittābhidhānam anantarānuṣṭhānārthaṃ, lāghavārthaṃ vā | smṛtyantaroktānāṃ vrātyaprāyaścittānāṃ svāvasare vivekaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ | kāmaṃ patitasāvitrīkatvād upanayanam adhyayanaṃ vā mā bhūd, dvijātikarmahānaṃ tu kutas tv ity uktam advijātitvād ity ucyate || 38 ||

 

_kasmāt punar advijātitvam | yasmāt,_

 

**              	mātur agre 'dhijāyante dvitīyaṃ mauñjibandhane |**

**              	brāhamaṇakṣattriyaviśas tasmad ete dvijātayaḥ || 1.39 ||**

 

"tad dvitīyaṃ janma" (GDh 1.8) iti smṛtyantaram | na cānupanītānāṃ tad asti | ata eva śūdro 'py advijātiḥ | advijātitvād eva dvijātikarmabhyaḥ patanam | varṇadharmās tu pravartanta ity uktam | ataḥ sūktaṃ "patanty ete sarvadharmabahiṣkṛtāḥ" iti || 39 ||

 

_asyaiva dārḍhyārtham iyam anyā vrātyanindā dvijātistutir vā |_

 

**              	yajñānāṃ tapasāṃ caiva śubhānāṃ caiva karmaṇām |**

**              	veda eva dvijātīnāṃ niḥśreyasakaraḥ paraḥ || 1.40 ||**

 

caśabdaivaśabdau chandaḥsamādhānārthau | yajñānāṃ jyotiṣṭomādīnām | tapasāṃ cāndrāyaṇādīnām | mūlaṃ param | paraś naiḥśreyasakaraḥ, apavargamūlatvāt | sarvakarmaṇāṃ ca kāraṇādhīnatvāt paratvābhidhānam aviruddham | sa ca dvijātīnām eveti stutiḥ | advijātīnāṃ vā sa eva nāstīti nindā | brahmayajñasya cāyam upodghātaḥ | evaṃ ca vakṣyamāṇaślokānām api prakṛtasaṃbandho vācyaḥ | brahmayajñavidhānaparatve 'pi vrātyanindeyaṃ, teśām anadhikārāt | dvijātistutir vā, teṣām adhikārāt || 40 ||

 

_tathā cāha |_

 

**              	madhunā payasā caiva sa devāṃs tarpayed dvijaḥ |**

**              	pitṝn madhughṛtābhyāṃ ca ṛco 'dhīte hi yo 'nvaham || 1.41 ||**

 

dvijagrahaṇaṃ stutyartham | anvaham iti nityādhikārajñāpanārtham, adhikārāviśeṣatvāt kāmapadānanubandhitvāc ca | devāditarpaṇam arthavādaḥ | stutyā ca vidhikalpanam | caśabdasyāpakarṣaviṣayatvam | pitṝṃś ceti yojanā | evaṃ vakṣyamāṇaviṣayā api ślokā vyākhyeyāḥ | ṛgādiśabdā ṛgvedadivacanā evety upakramasāmarthyād avaseyam | ṛjv anyat ||41||

 

**              	yajūṃṣi śaktito 'dhīte yo 'nvahaṃ sa ghṛtāmṛtaiḥ |**

**              	prīṇāti devān ājyena madhunā ca pitṝṃs tathā || 1.42 ||**

 

prīṇātīty anuṣaṅgaḥ | ghṛtāny amṛtāni vā ghṛtāmṛtāni | ghṛtabahutvaṃ cāhutibhedāt | amṛtaṃ tv amaraṇadharmakatvāt suvarṇam | tena śatakṛṣṇalādau tarpaṇam | dugdhābdhiprabhavaṃ vā | tad aitihāsikānāṃ prasiddham || 42 ||

 

**              	sa tu somaghṛtair devāṃs tarpayed yo 'nvahaṃ paṭhet |**

**              	sāmāni tṛptiṃ kuryāc ca pitṝṇāṃ madhusarpiṣā || 1.43 ||**

 

caśabdasyotkṛṣya pitṝṇāṃ ceti yojanā || 43 ||

 

**              	medasā tarpayed devān atharvāṅgirasaḥ paṭhan |**

**              	pitṝṃś ca madhusarpirbhyām anvahaṃ śaktito dvijaḥ || 1.44 ||**

 

punaḥ punar anvaham ity ādarārtham uktam | ṛgādīnāṃ nairapekṣyakathanārthaṃ vā | dvijagrahaṇaṃ cātra vākovākyādāv advijātiprāptyartham | ṛjv anyat || 44 ||

 

**              	vākovākyaṃ purāṇaṃ ca nārāśaṃsīś ca gāthikāḥ |**

**              	itihāsāṃs tathā vidyā yo 'dhīte śaktito 'nvaham || 1.45 ||**

 

vākovākyaṃ trayyanugatāni vādaprakaraṇāni | nārāśaṃsyaḥ paureṣeyyo yajñagāthāḥ, devastotrāṇi puruṣakṛtāny evety anye | gāthā ātmavādaślokāḥ | puruṣakṛtā eva yajñagāthā ity anye | vidyā mīmāṃsādayaḥ | yo 'nvahaṃ śaktito dvijātir advijātir vādhikṛtaḥ sann adhīte || 45 ||

 

**              	māṃsakṣīraudanamadhutarpaṇaṃ sa divaukasām |**

**              	karoti tṛptiṃ ca tathā pitṝṇāṃ madhusarpiṣā || 1.46 ||**

 

māṃsaudanakṣīraudanābhyāṃ madhunā ca tarpaṇam | divi oko nivāso yeṣāṃ te divaukasaḥ | devā ity arthaḥ | tathā pitṝṇāṃ ca madhusarpiṣā tṛptiṃ karotīti yojanā || 46 ||

 

_kiṃ punas tais tṛptaiḥ prayojanam |_

 

                    	**te tṛptās tarpayanty enaṃ sarvakāmaphalaiḥ śubhaiḥ |**

**              	yaṃ yaṃ kratum adhīte ca tasya tasyāpnuyāt phalam || 1.47 ||**

 

te devā pitaraś ca | tṛptāḥ, enaṃ svādhyāyinam | tarpayanti, sarvakāmaphalaiḥ sarve kāmā phalāni yeṣāṃ te sarvakāmaphalāḥ kratavaḥ | tais tarpayanti, tṛptiṃ kurvantīty arthaḥ | śubhair iti śyenādivyāvṛttyartham | samānam etad dvijātīnām advijātīnāṃ ca | yad vā, evaṃ brahmayajñābhyastā ṛgādayo mantrā kratvaṅgaṃ bhavanti, brāhmaṇāni ca vidhānakṣamāṇi | ataś ca yo yo yaṃ yaṃ kratum adhīte, sa sa tatra tatrādhikāralābhāt tasya tasyāpnuyāt phalaṃ, nānyaḥ | advijāteś cānadhyayanān mahāphalakratvanadhikārān nindā | kratvabhidhānāc cāyam ṛgvedādyadhayanaśeṣaḥ ślokaḥ | uttarārdho vā | na vākovākyādyadhyayanaśeṣaḥ || 47 ||

 

_iyam anyā brahayajñasyātistutiḥ |_

 

**              	trir vittapūrṇapṛthivīdānasya phalam aśnute |**

**              	tapasaś ca parasyeha nityasvādhyāyavān dvijaḥ || 1.48 ||**

 

tathā cāmnāyaḥ: "yāvantaṃ ha vā imāṃ vittena pūrṇāṃ dadat svargaṃ lokaṃ jayati tris tāvantaṃ lokaṃ jayati bhūyāṃsaṃ cākṣayyam" ityādi (ŚB 11.5.6.3) | tapasaś ca parasya phalam aśnute | caturthāśramagatasyety arthaḥ | ihaiva brahmacarye sthitaḥ | nityasvādhyāyavān niṣkāma ity arthaḥ | dvijagrahaṇam uktārtham | yad vā ihety asyānyo 'rthaḥ | iha grāmye dharme sthito 'laṅkṛtaḥ sukhitaḥ sukhe śayane śayānaḥ parasya tapasaḥ phalaṃ prāpnuyāt | dvijagrahaṇaṃ dvijātīnāṃ yāvajjīviko 'yaṃ brahmayajña iti jñāpanārtham | tathā cāha manuḥ |

                    	ā haiva sa nakhāgrebhyaḥ paramaṃ tapyate tapaḥ |

                    	yaḥ sragvy api dvijo 'dhīte svādhyāyaṃ śaktito 'nvaham || iti | (MDh 2.167)

upalakṣaṇārthaṃ caitat tṛtīyaṃ dvijagrahaṇam | dvijo 'dvijo vā yathāvihitasvādhyāyavān idaṃ nāma prāpnuyād iti | evaṃ ca sarvaśeṣo 'yaṃ ślokaḥ | kratuprāptyādayaś ca phalārthavādā iti prapañcanīyam | tadālambanāni ca kāraṇe kāryavad upacārāt sādṛśyādibhir vā kathaṃcid upapādanīyāni || 48 ||

 

_evam uktakālaṃ brahmacarye samāpyānantaraṃ gurukulāt samāvartitavyaṃ gṛhasthadharmānuṣṭhānāya | naiṣṭhikaṃ vā brahmacaryam anantaraṃ pratipattavyam | yathāha vasiṣṭhaḥ: "avaśīrṇabrahmacaryo yam icchet tam āvaset" iti_ (VaDh 7.3)_ | gautamaś ca "tasyāśramavikalpam eke bruvate" _(GDh 3.1) _ity etad eva darśayati | tasya cāvaśīrṇavratasyety arthaḥ | tatrānantaryād brahmacāriṇa evānyaḥ prakāro naiṣṭhikatvaṃ tāvad ucyate |_

 

**              	naiṣṭhiko brahmacārī tu vased ācāryasaṃnidhau |**

**              	tadabhāve 'sya tanaye patnyāṃ vaiśvānare 'pi vā || 1.49 ||**

 

tuśabdasyāpakarṣaḥ | naiṣṭhikas tv ācāryasaṃnidhau vaset | saṃnidhivacanād adṛṣṭārtho vāsaḥ | samākhyānāc ca tacchuśrūṣaṇaparas tatraiva niṣṭhāṃ gamayet | tadabhave tv asyaiva putre guṇānvite patnyāṃ vā guṇānvitāyām | vāśabdāpiśabdāt sapiṇḍe vācāryasyātmano vā sabrahmacāriṇi vā | tathā cāha manuḥ |

                    	ācārye tu khalu prete guruputre guṇānvite |

                    	gurudāre sapiṇḍe vā kāṅkṣan gatim anuttamām || iti | (MDh 2.247)

gautamaś ca: "gurvabhāve tadapatye vṛttiḥ | tadabhāve vṛddhe sabrahmacāriṇi" ityādi (GDh 3.7–8) | "vaiśvānare 'pi vā", nityadhāraṇabhaikṣahomasamidindhanopalepanādibhiḥ śuśrūṣāviśeṣair dehaṃ kṣapayet | ācāryāgnyor icchāvikalpaḥ | doṣavati cācārye 'gniḥ | itareṣāṃ tv abhāvato guṇato vā grahaṇam, sarvatra sādguṇyābhāvāt || 49 ||

 

_tataś ca |_

 

**              	anena vidhinā dehaṃ sādhayan vijitendriyaḥ |**

**              	brahmalokam avāpnoti na cehājāyate punaḥ || 1.50 ||**

 

sādhanaṃ kṣapaṇam | anena vidhinā pūrvoktenāgnīndhanādinā ācāryādisaṃnidhau dehaṃ samāpayan brahmalokam avāpnoti | na ca punar ihājāyate | yad vā, anena vidhineti smṛtyantaroktavidhisaṃbandhaḥ, asya ca prakaraṇād eva siddheḥ, "caturthaṣaṣṭhāṣtamakālabhojī bhaikṣam" (VaDh 7.8–9) ityādinā smṛtyantroketena vidhinā | vijitendriyatvaṃ cātmopāsanam abhipretaṃ, brahmalokaprāptivacanāt punarājananapratiṣedhāc ca | tathāha manuḥ |

                    	ā nipātāc charīrasya yas tu śuśrūṣate gurum |

                    	sa gacchaty añjasā vipro brahmaṇaḥ sadma śāśvatam || iti | (MDh 2.244)

añjasā ātmajñānenety arthaḥ | "guroḥ karmaśeṣeṇa japet" (GDh 3.6) iti gautamaḥ | evaṃbhūto brahmalokam avāpnoti jitendriya iti | evaṃbhūto jitendriya ātmavid ity arthaḥ | bahyendriyajayas tu pūrvam uktaḥ |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> iyaṃ naiṣṭhikatvavidhānasmṛtir āmnāyaviruddhā | kathaṃ, "yāvajjīvam agnihotraṃ juhuyāt", "yāvajjīvaṃ darśapūrṇamāsābhyām yajeta" (cf. Śab on PMS 2.4.1) ity evamādyāmnāyaḥ pratyakṣaḥ | sa naiṣṭhikatve saty uparudhyeta | tadvirodhinyaś ca smṛtayo na pramāṇam ity uktam | na caivam avirodhasaṃbhavaḥ, kṛtadārāṇām evāgnihotrādividhaya iti | prāg api jīvanānvayāt tadvataś cādhikāraḥ | kāmam adhikṛtānām evāstu dārasaṃgrahaḥ | na caivaṃ sati prāg upanayanād upanītamātrasya vā prasaṅga iti śakyaṃ vaktum, aviduṣo 'nadhikārāt | na ca niṣādavad vācaniko 'dhikāraḥ saṃbhavati, anadhyayanaprasaṅgāt | yadi hy aviduṣām adhikāraḥ syāt, ko 'dhyayanādikleśaṃ kuryāt | na cādhyayanāt phalāntaram iti śakyaṃ vaktum, aśravaṇāt | phalavatkarmāvabodhanena ca prayojanavattvād ghṛtakulyādīnām arthavādatvam | na cāstv adhyayanam iti śakyaṃ vaktuṃ, saṃpradāyocchedaprasaṅgāc ca | ataś ca yuktaṃ vaktum aviduṣām anadhikārakalpanam | na ca prāg adhyayanād aviduṣāṃ paratas tu viduṣām iti yuktaṃ, vairūpyaprasaṅgāt | tenāviduṣām nirāsaḥ | viduṣāṃ punar adhikārahetuḥ patnyabhāva ity cet, kriyatāṃ tarhi patnīsaṃgrahaḥ | na ca kevalakāmaprayuktā seti śakyaṃ vaktum "anyatarāpāye dārān kurvīta" iti vacanāt | kiṃ ca "jāyamāno vai brāhmaṇas tribhir ṛṇavā jāyate" ity upakramya, "atha tarhy anṛṇo bhavati yadi hi yajvā brahmacārī prajām utpādayet" (TS 6.3.10.5) ityādinā prajotpādananiyamaṃ darśayati | na cākṛtadāratve tadupapattiḥ | ato 'pi niyogataḥ kāryo dārasaṃgrahaḥ | api ca smṛtivirodho 'pi syāt, tannaiyamikasaṃskārahanāt | tathā ca manuḥ |

                    	mahāyajñaiś ca yajñaiś ca brāhmīyaṃ kriyate tanuḥ | iti | (MDh 2.28)

"catvāriṃśat saṃskāraiḥ saṃskṛtaḥ" (GDh 8.8) iti gautamaḥ | na caitad agṛhasthasya saṃbhavati | na ca yo gṛhasthas tasya tad iti yuktam, aviśeṣaśruteḥ | tathā ca gautamaḥ "tasyāśramavikalpam eke bruvate" (GDh 3.1) ity upakramyāśramān abhidhāyānantaram "aikāśramayaṃ tv ācāryāḥ pratyakṣavidhānād gārhasthyasya" (GDh 3.36) ity upasaṃharann etad eva spaṣṭīkroti, yad upavarṇitam asmābhiḥ | ato naiṣṭhikatvasmṛtir asārā | tatrānye 'gnihotrādyanadhikṛtānām atryārṣeyāṇām (?) andhapaṅgvādīnāṃ naiṣṭhikādismṛtaya iti varṇayanti | teṣām apy āśramasamuccayo duḥśliṣṭa eva | svābhiprāyeṇa ca viṣayakalpanā "yam icchet tam āvaset" (VaDh 7.3) iti | ato 'śabdārthakalpanātas tu varam aprāmāṇyam eva | tathā cāṅgirāḥ |

                    	svābhiprāyakṛtaṃ karma yat tu dharmavivarjitam |

                    	krīḍākarmeva bālānāṃ tat sarvaṃ niṣprayojanam || iti |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">atrābhidhīyate</span>: neyam apasmṛtiḥ, vedamūlatvāviśeṣāt | virodhād atanmūlatvam iti cet, kaḥ khalv atra virodhaḥ | yadi hi na kṛtadārāḥ kāmataḥ syus tadāgnihotrādividhayaḥ prayojakā iti kalpyeta | kāmānāṃ tu prayojakatve na tatkalpanāvasaraḥ | na ca kratvarthatve pramāṇam asti | nāpi dravyārjanavad dārā iti śakyaṃ vaktuṃ, dravyābhāve hi jīvanānupapatteḥ | sarveṇa hi dravyam arthyate yataḥ, ataś cādravyatvaṃ niruṇaddhi | tathā ca nyāyavido yājñikā: "jīviṣyanti hi vidhānenety anpupannam" ity āhuḥ | na caivaṃ dārasaṃgrahe pravṛttir iti vaiṣamyam | na hi dārābhāve jīvanānupapattiḥ | yā tu "anyatarāpāye dārān kurvīta" iti kratoḥ prayojakatvāśaṅkā, sā kṛtadārasyādhikṛtatvāt kevalānaupayikadārasadbhāve ca dravyārjanenāviśiṣṭā | yathaiva hy ātmārtham ārjane pravṛtta ātmārthatvāviśeṣāt kratvartham apy ārjayati, nāham adravyatvād anadhikṛta iti manyate, tathaiva kṛtadāreṇākṛtadāro 'ham iti ca nāvamantavyam | vītarāgasya tv ātmārtham api pravṛttyabhāvān nādhikṛtatvam | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ "gṛhastho 'vinītakrodhaharṣaḥ" (VaDh 8.1) ity etad eva darśayati | avinītakrodhaharṣasyaiva gārhasthyaṃ, vinītakrodhaharṣas tu "yam icchet tam āvaset" (VaDh 7.3) ity asyārtho yataḥ | yat tu gautamīyam "aikāśramyam" (GDh 3.36) iti, tad vanasthāśramanirūpaṇe nirṇeṣyāmaḥ | yat tu "brāhmīyaṃ kriyate tanuḥ" (MDh 2.28) iti, saṃskāratvaṃ yajñādīnām iti tasyārthaḥ, na tu tadrahitānām abrāhmī tanur iti | gautamīyaṃ tv ātmaguṇapraśaṃsārtham ity uktam evety anavadyam | evam ṛṇavākyam api gṛhasthaviṣayatayaiva vyākhyeyam | yathaivāviduṣo na prajotpādanāya dārasaṃgrahaḥ, tathaiva viduṣo 'y arāgiṇaḥ |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> etat kāmaprayuktve pi samānam, asamāvṛttasyāpi kāmasaṃbhavāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">naivam</span> | kāmaprayuktatve brahmacāriṇo dārādhigamaḥ smṛtyā nirākriyate, prajotpādanavidhiprayuktatve 'gnihotrādividhiprayuktatve ca smṛter daurbalyāt kena vāryate | ataḥ kāmaprayuktatve vaiṣamyam | āmnāyaś ca "ye cāmī araṇye śraddhā satyam upāsate" (ChU 5.10.1) ity agnihotrādyanapekṣām apavargaprāptiṃ darśayati | evaṃ chāndogye 'pi "trayo dharmaskandhāḥ | yajño 'dhyayanaṃ dānam iti prathamaḥ | tapa eva dvitīyaḥ | brahmacāry ācāryakule vāsīti tṛtīyaḥ | atyantam ātmānam ācāryakule 'vāsādayan" (ChU 2.231) iti naiṣṭhikatvaṃ darśayati | ata sūktaṃ "naiṣṭhiko brahmacārī" ityādi || 50 ||

 

**iti brahmacāriprakaraṇam**

** **

**atha vivāhaprakaraṇam**

 

_ukto brahmacārī, anantaraṃ gṛhastho vaktavyaḥ | tadabhidhānāyāha |_

 

                    	**gurave tu varaṃ dattvā snāyīta tadanujñayā |**

**              	vedaṃ vratāni vā pāraṃ nītvāpy ubhayam eva vā || 1.51 ||**

 

apīty asyāpakṛṣya yojanā, smṛtyantaraikavākyatvād arthavattvāc ca | vedam adhītya naiṣṭhikādyāśrame vaset | api vā gārhasthyaṃ kartuṃ snāyīta | snānam iti ca saṃskārakarmaṇo nāmadheyam | tac ca gṛhyād avagantavyam | gṛhasthatāṃ ca pratipadyamānasyaiva snānasaṃskāro nāśramāntaram api, tatparatvavidhānāt | yathāha gautamaḥ: "sa vidhipūrvaṃ snātvā" iti (GDh 9.1) | "sa" ity anena gṛhastho 'bhidhīyate | tathā vāsiṣṭho 'pi "gṛhastho 'vinītakrodhaharṣaḥ" iti prakṛtya snānavidhānaṃ "guruṇānujñātaḥ snātvā" iti (VaDh 8.1) | yadā snāyāt tadā gurave varaṃ dattvā | varadānaṃ ca gavādeḥ śreṣṭhadravyasya dānam | yathāha pāraskaraḥ: "gaur brāhmaṇasya varo grāmo rājanyasyāśvo vaiśyasya" iti PārG 1.8.15–17) | anujñātaś ca guruṇā na varadānamātreṇa kṛtī syāt | yad vā, varaṃ vā dattvā snāyīta | tadanujñayā vā varam adattvā snāyīta | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "kṛtvānujñātasya vā snānam" iti (GDh 2.49) | tuśabdo 'vadhāraṇārthaḥ | gurav eva varaṃ dadyād, nānyasmai | anujñānaṃ cānyato 'pīti kecit | evaṃ tv adṛṣṭārthatvam asāmañjasyaṃ ca syāt | tasmāt pitur varadānābhāvāśaṅkānivṛttyarthas tuśabdaḥ | "vedaṃ vratāni vā pāraṃ nītvā" | vedasya pāranayanam arthato granthataś ca svīkaraṇaṃ, na granthata eva | tathā ca vaktāro bhavanti: vedādhyāyy ayaṃ na vedapāraga iti | vratānāṃ pāranayanaṃ dvādaśa varṣāṇi prayatnato 'nuṣṭhānam | ubhayam eva vā pāraṃ nītvā, vedaṃ vratāni ca | ayaṃ prathamaḥ kalpaḥ, ubhayānugrahād, evakārāc ca | vedam iti cānukalpaḥ | prādhānye 'pi vedasya vratānupasaṃhārāt | vratāny evety āpatkalpaḥ, vedārthatvād brahmcaryasya, tasya cānirvṛtter ityādi prapañcanīyam | vedam iti caikavacanaṃ śākhāntarādhyayanavyāvṛttyartham, brahmatve trivedasaṃyogavacanāt | tathā cāha manuḥ |

                    	vedān adhītya vedau vā vedaṃ vāpi yathākramam | iti | (MDh 3.2)

pāṭhāntare 'py ayam evārthaḥ: "vedavratāni vā pāraṃ nītvā hy ubhayam eva vā" iti | vedaṃ vratāni ca vedavratānīty evaṃ vigrahaḥ | hiśabdaś ca hetvarthaḥ | yadeti cādhyāhāryam | yadā snāyāt, tadaivam iti | samānam anyat || 51 ||

 

_brahmacāriṇo brahmacaryavidhānāt samāvṛttasya nivṛttiḥ prāpnotīty ata āha |_

 

**              	aviplutabrahmacaryo lakṣaṇyāṃ striyam udvahet |**

**              	ananyapūrvikāṃ kāntām asapiṇḍāṃ yavīyasīm || 1.52 ||**

 

samāvṛtto 'pi sann aviplutabrahmacarya evodvāhaṃ kuryāt | brahmacaryavacanāc ca madhvaśanādau viplavaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">katham</span> punaḥ prāg vivāhād viplavāśaṅkā | paradārābhigamanaṃ hi niṣiddham eva | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> evam | vakṣyati tu: "yatnāt parīkṣitaḥ puṃstve" iti (YDh 1.55) | parīkṣaṇopāyatvena viplavāśaṅkāsty eva | anye tu niyogapakṣeṇa viplavam āhuḥ | lakṣaṇyāṃ lakṣaṇopetām | yathāha manuḥ: "savarṇāṃ lakṣaṇānvitām" iti (MDh 3.4) | tathā ca |

                    	avyaṅgāṅgīṃ saumyanāmnīṃ haṃsavāraṇagāminīm | iti | (MDh 3.10)

strīgrahaṇam anuvādaḥ, guṇārthaṃ vā | apatrapaṇaśīlām ity arthaḥ | evam apy ananyapūrvikām iti | anyenānupabhuktām ity arthaḥ | kāntāṃ ca kamanīyām | asapiṇḍāṃ ca mātṛtaḥ pitṛtaś ca | yavīyasīm ātmano hīnavayasam | tām evaṃvidhoktalakṣaṇām udvahed iti saṃbandhaḥ || 52 ||

 

_kiṃ cānyat |_

 

**              	arogiṇīṃ brātṛmatīm asamānarṣigotrajām |**

**              	pañcamīṃ saptamīṃ caiva mātṛtaḥ pitṛtas tathā || 1.53 ||**

 

arogiṇīṃ kuṣṭhādirogarahitām | dṛṣṭamūlatvāc ca smṛteḥ samādheyarogitvam adoṣaḥ | bhrātṛmatīṃ ca, putrikāśaṅkānivṛttyartham | "nābhrātrīm upayacchet tat tokaṃ hy asya bhavati" iti bhāllavināṃ śruteḥ | yadā punar ayaṃ hetuvan nigadaḥ, tadā "nābhrātrīm upayacchet" ity evaṃ manyante | asamānarṣigotrajām asamānārṣeyagotraprabhavām | asamānapravarām ity arthaḥ | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "asamānapravarair vivāhaḥ" iti (GDh 4.2) | yad api "asagotrām" (MDh 3.5) iti mānavaṃ, tad apy evam eva vyākhyeyam | tataś ca samānagotrāṇām apy asamānapravarāṇām aniṣiddho vivāhaḥ | yathā pañcārṣeyāṇāṃ tryārṣeyāṇāṃ bharadvājānām | tathedam aparaṃ: pañcamīṃ mātṛtaḥ, saptamīṃ pitṛtaḥ | mātṛpitṛśabdau ca jñātilakṣaṇārthau, "mātṛbandhubhyaḥ pitṛbandhubhyaś ca" iti smṛtyantarāt | asapiṇḍām ity anenaiva siddhe vivekārthaḥ punar ārambhaḥ | mā bhūt

                    	sapiṇḍatā puruṣe saptame vinivartate | (MDh 5.60)

ity aviśeṣavacanān mātṛto 'pi saptapuruṣī sapiṇḍatā | tathā cāha gautamaḥ: "piṇḍanivṛttiḥ saptame pañcame vā" iti (GDh 14.13) | ayaṃ ca tasyārthaḥ: saptame pitṛtaḥ pañcame mātṛta iti, mātṛbandhubhyaḥ pañcamād ity ārambhāt | tatheti bījigrahaṇārtham | tathā cāha gautamaḥ: "ūrdhaṃ saptamāt pitṛbandubhyo bījinaś ca mātṛbandhubhyaḥ pañcamād" iti (GDh 4.3–5) | caśabdaivaśabdau chandaḥsamādhānārthau | yad vā vikalpārthaś caśabdaḥ | pañcamīṃ saptamīṃ vā mātṛtaḥ pitṛtaś cōdvahet, sapiṇḍatāyās tadavadhikatvāt | tathā ca gautamīyaṃ sūtraṃ aviśeṣābhidhānāt samarthitaṃ bhavati | evaṃ cobhayatra pañcame vivāhaḥ syāt | yat tu "ūrdhvaṃ saptamāt pitṛbandhubhyo mātṛbandhubhyaḥ pañcamāt" (GDh 4.3–5) iti, tan mātṛtaḥ pañcamād evety avadhāraṇārtham | pitṛtas tu saptamāt pañcamād veti vikalpaḥ | pañcamād ity anukalpo 'yam, anyānarthakyāt | prathamakalpe ca nyūnatvadarśanād anukalpaḥ | mātṛtaś caturthe 'pīti kecit | tat punaḥ sāmānyatodṛṣṭam | tenobhayatra samatvam evānukalpaḥ | tathā ca śaṅkhaḥ: "pañcamīṃ vobhataḥ" iti | yat tv āmnāyavacanaṃ: "tasmad u samānād eva puruṣād attā cādyaṃ ca jāyate | idaṃ hi caturthe tṛtīye vā puruṣe saṃgacchāvahe iti his videvaṃ dīvyamānayā jānyā sahāsata" iti | tan mantravikārastutimātrārthatvād anādṛtyam iti kecit | athāpi jānyā ityādipadārthopapattyarthaṃ kartavyatocyeta | tathāpi deśopasaṃhṛtasyety āhuḥ | tat punar nyāyasmṛtiviruddham | yathāha baudhāyanaḥ: "pañcadhā vipratipattir dakṣiṇatas tathottarataḥ" ity upakramya, "itarad itarasmin kurvan duṣyatītarad itarasmin" iti coktvā, "ubhayaṃ tv eva nādriyeta" ityādi (BDh 1.2.1–8) | nyāyavidaś ca yājñikāḥ: "api vā sarvadharmaḥ syāt tannyāyatvād vidhānasya" iti (PMS 1.3.16) | ataḥ kāryatve sati sarvadharmatvam | ayaṃ cātra vākyārthaḥ: samānād ekasmāt puruṣād attā ca bhoktā, ādyaṃ ca bhogyaṃ, dvāv apy utpadyete | tatrotpannamātraḥ pariṇetā krīḍan saṃkalpayati: idaṃ bhogyam caturthe puruṣe tṛtīye vā bhokṣyāmīti | tatrotpattipuruṣāt pañcamaḥ saṃbhavati, tṛtīyapakṣe caturthaḥ | te cāmī śrutismṛtyanusārāc catvāraḥ kalpāḥ: ūrdhvaṃ saptamāt pañcamād vety ekaḥ, pañcame mātṛtaḥ saptame pitṛta iti dvitīyaḥ, ubhayataḥ pañcama iti tṛtīyaḥ, caturthe 'pīti caturthaḥ | pūrvaḥ pūrvaḥ śreyān | strīviṣayaś cāntyaḥ kalpaḥ, idam iti sarvanāmno bhogyaparatvāt | evaṃ ca varacaturthe na vivāhaḥ | mantravarṇo 'py evam eva vyākhyeyaḥ, "kḷptāṃ mātulasyeva yoṣām" iti, vyavadhāne 'pi ṣaṣṭhyupapatteḥ vājapeyasya yūpa itivat, "paitṛṣvaseyī vapām iva" (RVKh 7.55.8) iti ca, apatyāpatye 'pi taddhitāvirodhāt | śrutismṛtyanusārāc caivaṃ kalpanety eṣā dik | bhūtapūrvagatyā ca mātṛtaḥ sapiṇḍatvam iti sūtakādyaprasaṅgaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evaṃ sati strītas tṛtīye 'pi prāpnoti, "aprattānām tu strīṇāṃ tripuruṣī sapiṇḍatā vijñāyate" iti vasiṣṭhavacanāt (VaDh 4.18) | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">naivam</span> tasyāśaucamātraviṣayatvāt | aprattānāṃ tu pāribhāṣikaṃ tad uktam | tathā ca vivāhe pañcamīty upapannaṃ bhavati | anyathā tad asamañjasaṃ syāt | kṣatriyādīnāṃ tu brāhmaṇādiprabhavānām ubhayataś caturthe 'py aviruddho vivāhaḥ | kṣatriyādiprabhavānāṃ tu viśeṣābhāvāt pūrvoka eva kalpaḥ | tathā ca śaṅkhaḥ |

                    	yady ekajātā bahavaḥ pṛthakkṣetrāḥ pṛthagjanāḥ|

                    	ekapiṇḍāḥ pṛthakcchaucāḥ piṇḍas tv āvartate triṣu || iti |

evam anyāny apy anayaiva diśā vākyāni yojanīyāni || 53 ||

 

_kiṃ cānyat |_

 

**              	daśpūruṣavikhyātāc chrotriyāṇāṃ mahākulāt |**

**              	sphītād api na saṃcārirogadoṣasamanvitāt || 1.54 ||**

 

śrotriyatvenaiva khyātir garīyasī, na rājasatkārādibhiḥ | tathā cāha manuḥ |

                    	mantratas tu samṛddhāni kulāny alpadhanāny api |

                    	kulasaṃkhyāṃ ca gacchanti prāpnuvanti mahad yaśaḥ || iti || (MDh 3.66)

tenālpadhanād api śrotriyakulāt kanyām udvahet, na tu dhanādisamṛddhād api saṃcārirogasaṃyuktād doṣasaṃyuktād vā | maukhyādayo 'pi hi mātulādisaṃparkāt saṃcāriṇa eva, rogāś ca śvitrakuṣṭhādayaḥ | na tu saṃcāriṇo 'pi śiraḥśūlādayaḥ, dṛṣṭamūlatvāt smṛteḥ | tathā cāha manuḥ |

                    	mahānty api samṛddhāni go'jāvidhanadhānyataḥ |

                    	strīsaṃbandhe daśaitāni kulāni parivarjayet ||

                    	hīnakriyaṃ niṣpuruṣaṃ niśchandoromaśārśasam |

                    	kṣayyāmayāvyapasmāriśvitrikuṣṭhikulāni ca || iti | (MDh 3.6–7)

kulagrahaṇāc ca siddhe yad arogiṇīm ity uktaṃ, tad ādarārtham | evam anye 'pi guṇadoṣāḥ smṛtyantarāl lokataś cānveṣyāḥ, pramāṇāntaramūlatvāt smaraṇasya || 54 ||

 

_uktāḥ kanyāgunāḥ | varasyedānīm ucyante |_

 

                    	**etair eva guṇair yuktaḥ savarṇaḥ śrotriyo varaḥ |**

**              	yatnāt parīkṣitaḥ puṃstve yuvā dhīmāñ janapriyaḥ || 1.55 ||**

 

etair eva guṇair yukto varo 'pi syāt | ayaṃ tu viśeṣaḥ, yaḥ savarṇaḥ śrotriyaś ca | savarṇagrahaṇaṃ ca hīnavarṇavyāvṛttyartham | yad vā, utkṛṣṭavedanasyānukalpatvajñāpanārtham | anukalpatvaṃ cādhikāraviprakarṣāl lokapaktyanusārāc ca puṃsāṃ tu "śrotriyāṇāṃ mahākulād" iti vacanāt tisra ity eva prathamaḥ kalpaḥ | smṛtyantarād vā svarṇetarodvahanam anukalpaḥ | tathā cāha manuḥ |

                    	savarṇāgre dvijātīnāṃ praśastā dārakarmaṇi |

                    	kāmatas tu pravṛttānām imāḥ syuḥ kramaśo varāḥ || iti | (MDh 3.12)

evaṃguṇatve 'pi brahmacaryāviplavena yatnāt parīkṣitaḥ puṃstve, vītabījādivyudāsadvāreṇa | evaṃ striyo 'pi strītve parīkṣaṇīyāḥ, puṃstva ity upalakṣaṇārthatvāt | striyam udvahed iti vā strīgrahaṇasyaitad eva prayojanam iti vyākhyeyam | ādarārthaṃ vā | puṃsaḥ parīkṣaṇābhidhānam aparityāgajñāpanārtham | ananyapūrvatvaṃ strīviṣayam eva | puṃviṣayatve 'pi prathamaḥ kalpaḥ | evaṃbhūto yaḥ, sa varaḥ syāt | sa varayitavyaḥ | tādṛśo vā kanyāṃ varayed iti vyākhyeyam | ṛjv anyat || 55 ||

 

_"śrotriyāṇāṃ mahākulād" iti vacanāc chūdrāvivāho na prāpnoti | iṣyate ca kaiś cit tatrācāryaḥ svamatam upanyasyati sma |_

 

                    	**yad ucyate dvijātīnāṃ śūdrād dāropasaṃgrahaḥ |**

**              	na tan mama mataṃ yasmāt tatrāyaṃ jāyate svayam || 1.56 ||**

 

"kṛṣṇavarṇīyā rāmā ramaṇāyaivopeyata" iti brāhmanavādaḥ | na ca viduṣāṃ kāmārthe pravṛttir yuktā | ataḥ śūdrāvivāho na kartavya ity etad eva spaṣṭīkaroti hetunā: "yasmāt tatrāyaṃ jāyate svayam" iti | tathā bahvṛcāḥ paṭhanti |

                    	patir jāyā praviśati garbho bhūtvā sa mātaram |

                    	tasyā punar navo bhūtvā daśame māsi jāyate || iti | (AitB 7.13)

ato naitan mamābhipretam || 56 ||

 

_idaṃ punar asmābhir apy abhipretam |_

 

                    	**tisro varṇānupūrvyeṇa dve tathaikā yathākramam |**

**              	brāhmaṇakṣattriyaviṣāṃ bhāryā svā śūdrajanmanaḥ || 1.57 ||**

 

śūdrasyeti vaktavye śūdrajanmana ity uktaṃ, sāpi hi brāhmaṇādijātā śūdrajanmanā na vivāhyeti jñāpanārtham | evaṃ kṣattriyādīnām antaraprabhavānāṃ cānulomapratilomānāṃ yathāyathaṃ yojyam | sarvathā manāg apy utkṛṣṭajā nikṛṣṭajanmanā na vivāhyā | nikṛṣṭāpi yathāsaṃnikarṣaṃ kramād vivāhyeti ślokārthaḥ | ṛjv anyat || 57 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ayaṃ vivāhākhyaḥ saṃskāraḥ na nityam upasaṃhartuṃ śakyaḥ, parādhānatvāt kanyālābhasya | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | syād ayaṃ doṣo dātrabhāvād yady aprārthitā kanyā na pradīyate, dadato vā pratyavāyaḥ syāt | adya tu khalu dātur abhyudayaḥ | yathāha |_

 

**              	brāhmo vivāha āhūya dīyate śaktyalaṃkṛtā |**

**              	tajjaḥ punāty ubhayataḥ puruṣān ekaviṃśatim || 1.58 ||**

 

brāhmaṇa evainam arhatīti brāhmaḥ | tatra cayaṃ vidhiḥ | yathāśakty alaṃkṛtya uktalakṣaṇaṃ varam āhūya gṛhyoktena vidhinā kanyāpradāṃ (yadā), tadā noktadoṣaprasaṅgaḥ | na caivaṃ brāhme lokānusāribhir bhavitavyam, katham aprārthitā kanyā dīyata iti | ayam eva satāṃ dharma yataḥ | tasyāṃ tathoḍhāyāṃ jātaḥ putraḥ ubhataḥ pitṛto mātṛtaś caikaviṃśatiṃ kulāni punāti śodhayatīty arthaḥ | yad vā daśātītāni daśotpatsyamānāni ātmānaṃ cety evaṃ yojanā | tathā cāha gautamaḥ: "daśa pūrvān daśāvarān ātmānaṃ ca brāhmīputraḥ" iti (GDh 4.33) | stutimātram etad, bhūtānāṃ bhāvināṃ pāvanānupapatteḥ | upapattau vā kṛtanāśākṛtāgamaprasaṅgāt | yad vāstu phalavidhiḥ, vivāhaviśeṣasya phalaviśeṣāpekṣatvāt | na cāgamānusāriṇyarthe 'nupapattir iti śakyaṃ vaktum | tathā ca naiyāyikā "na hi vacanasyātibhāro 'sti" (Śab on PMS 5.3.10) ity āhuḥ | ayaṃ ca brāhmaṇasya prāthamakalpiko vivāhaḥ || 58 ||

 

_ime tv anukalpāḥ |_

 

**              	yajñastha ṛtvije daiva ādāyārṣas tu godvayam |**

**              	caturdaśa prathamajaḥ punāty uttarajaś ca ṣaṭ || 1.59 ||**

 

yajñasthavacanaṃ pūrvajuṣṭādivyāvṛttyartham | devā ṛtvijas ta enam arhantīti daivaḥ | ataś ca brāhmaṇsyaivāyam, itarayor ārtvijyānadhikārāt | mahartvigbhyaś ca | yathāha vyāsaḥ |

                    	steyaṃ kuryāṃ yady ahaṃ vo bisānāṃ mahartvijāṃ vitate yajñatantre |

                    	adhvaryave duhitaraṃ saṃpradadyām udgātre vā brahmaṇe vātha hotre || iti |

udgātṛvacanāc ca somartvikpratyayaḥ | dakṣiṇātiriktaṃ caitad dānaṃ, phalaśravaṇāt | ārṣas tu varād godvayam ādāya | tac ca mithunaṃ, smṛtyantarāt | (mantra)draṣṭāro brāhmaṇā ṛṣayaḥ, ta enam arhantīty ārṣaḥ | tuśabdaḥ parikrayāśaṅkānivṛttyarthaḥ | tathā cāha manuḥ |

                    	ekaṃ gomithunaṃ dve vā varād ādāya dharmataḥ | iti | (MDh 3.29)

kasmāt punar imāv anukalpau, pūrvasmād ūnaphalatvāt | tathā cāha: prathamajaś caturdaśa punāti | prathamo daivaḥ, tatra jātaḥ prathamajaḥ | tathottarajaḥ ṣaṭ | uttara ārṣaḥ, tatra jāta uttarajaḥ | pravibhajya paurvāparyeṇa yojanā | tathā cāha manuḥ |

                    	daivoḍhāyāḥ sutaś caiva sapta sapta parāvarān |

                    	ārṣoḍhāyāḥ sutas trīṃs trīn ṣaṭ ṣaṭ kāyoḍhajaḥ sutaḥ || iti | (MDh 3.38)

| nyūnaphalatvāc cāsya daivān nikṛṣṭatvam | daivasahapāṭhāc cāyam api brāhmaṇasyaiva | prājāpatyān nyūnaphalatve 'pi cāsyāta eva pūrvapāṭha iti mantavyam || 59 ||

 

_ayaṃ tu sārvavarṇikaḥ |_

 

**              	saha dharmaś caryatām ity uktvā yā dīyate 'rthine |**

**              	sa kāyaḥ pāvayaty ādyaḥ ṣaṭ ṣaḍ vaṃśyān sahātmanā || 1.60 ||**

 

"dharmaś caryatām" ity etāvad evoktvārthine yat kanyādānaṃ, sa prājāpatyaḥ | uktveti vacanān nābhyupagamād eva | yathāha gautamaḥ: "saṃyogamantraḥ prājāpatye" ityādi (GDh 4.7) | prajotpādanecchāsāmānyāt prajāpatiḥ snātakaḥ | sa enam arhatīti prājāpatyaḥ | evaṃ cārthina ity anuvādo mantravidhānārthaḥ | sārvavarṇikatve 'pi śūdranivṛttiḥ mantraprayogāt | so 'yaṃ prājāpatyaḥ ādyaḥ ārṣāt pūrva ity arthaḥ | kuta etat, phalabhūyastvāt | atra hi jātaḥ ṣaṭ ṣaḍ vaṃśyān punāti, ātmānaṃ ca | ārṣajas tu trīṃs trīn | sahātmanety etat pūrvatrāpi yojyam || 60 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evaṃ saty āhūya yadi kaścid ārtvijyādibhir vā na kanyāṃ dadyāt, tathāpi gṛhasthāśramo duḥśliṣṭa eva | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | yady eta eva vivāhā syuḥ | anye 'pi tu vivāhāḥ paṭhyante | ato neyam asatkalpanā | ke punas ta ity ata āha |_

 

                    	**āsuro draviṇādānād gāndharvaḥ samayān mithaḥ |**

**              	rākṣaso yuddhaharaṇāt paiśācaḥ kanyakācchalāt || 1.61 ||**

 

samayaḥ saṅketaḥ | mithaḥ sahety arthaḥ | āsuraḥ, ātmārthaṃ kanyārthaṃ ca dhanādānam | yathāha manuḥ |

                    	jñātibhyo draviṇaṃ dattvā kanyāyāś caiva śaktitaḥ|

                    	kanyādānaṃ tu svācchandyād āsuro dharma ucyate ||

                    	icchayānyonyasaṃyogaḥ kanyāyāś ca varasya ca |

                    	gāndharvaḥ sa vidhir jñeyo maithunyaḥ kāmasaṃbhavaḥ ||

                    	hatvā chittvā ca bhittvā ca krośantīṃ rudatīṃ gṛhāt |

                    	prasahya kanyāharaṇaṃ rākṣaso vidhir ucyate ||

                    	suptāṃ mattāṃ pramattāṃ vā raho yatropagacchati |

                    	sa pāpiṣṭho vivāhānāṃ paiśācaḥ prathito 'ṣṭamaḥ || iti | (MDh 3.31–34)

upagamanaśabda āliṅganādiṣv iti kecit | tat tv aśabdārthatvād anādṛtyam | pāpiṣṭhatā caivam upapannatarā bhavati, upapātakayogāc ca | anyathā tad asamañjasaṃ syāt | tathā ca "kevalaṃ mantrasaṃskṛtā " ity uktvā "sā ced akṣatayoniḥ syāt" (VaDh 17.74) iti vasiṣṭho 'py etad eva jñāpayati | ataḥ śrautārthagrahaṇaṃ yuktam iti | asurā dhanavantaḥ | strīsaktā gandharvāḥ | tenānayoḥ sārvavarṇikatvam | dāruṇatvasāmānyād rakṣaḥ kṣatriyāḥ | ta enam arhantīti rākṣasaḥ | kṣātra ity arthaḥ | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ: "bhittvā chittvā" ity upakraya "sa kṣātraḥ" (VaDh 1.33) ity āha | chalavṛttayaḥ piśācāḥ, tadarhaḥ paiśācaḥ | sarvavarṇānāṃ cāyam evāpatkalpaḥ | āsurādīnāṃ tu yathābhidhānaṃ kṣatriyādiviśeṣāpekṣayā ca stutinindākalpanam || 61 ||

 

_kim ekarūpa eva savarṇāsavarṇayor vivāhaḥ | nety ucyate |_

 

                    	**pāṇir grāhyaḥ savarṇāsu gṛhṇīta kṣatriyā śaram |**

**              	vaiśyā pratodam ādadyād vedane tv agrajanmanaḥ|| 1.62 ||**

 

brāhmaṇapāṇigṛhītaṃ dhanuḥśaram kṣatriyā gṛhṇīyāt | pratodaṃ ca vaiśyā | pratodo vrājanikaḥ | striyāś ca grahaṇe kartṛtvān mantranivṛttiḥ | ūhane vā prayoga ity anye | kṣatriyavedane 'pi vaiśyā pratodam eva gṛhṇīyād iti kecit, "utkṛṣṭavedane" iti manuvacanāt (MDh 3.44) | tat punaḥ sāmānyasya viśeṣopasaṃhṛter ayuktam || 62 ||

 

_kasya punar ayaṃ kanyāpradānopadeśaḥ | yadi tāvat pituḥ tadabhāve duḥśliṣataiva | atha tadabhāve 'py anyasya | sa kim iti parakīyāṃ dadyāt | tena kaḥ kanyāṃ dadyād iti | ucyate |_

 

**              	pitā mātāmaho bhrātā svakulyo jananī tathā |**

**              	kanyāpradaḥ pūrvanāśe prakṛtisthaḥ paraḥ paraḥ || 1.63 ||**

 

svakulya iti bhrātṛviśeṣaṇaṃ pitṛvyaputrādivyāvṛttyartham | pūrvasya pūrvasyābhāve paraḥ paraḥ kanyāpradaḥ | prakṛtisthaś ca svabhāvasthaḥ | unmādādyanabhibhūta ity arthaḥ | kanyāprada iti vacanād akṣatāyā eva naiyamikaṃ dānam | pitā tv akanyām api dadyād iti kecit | chandonurodhāc ca mātāmahasya pūrvapāṭhaḥ | arthatas tu bhrātaiva pūrvaḥ | sarveṣāṃ ca svatvasaṃbandhāc codanāto vā pravṛtter avirodhaḥ | pāṭhāntaraṃ vā: "pitā pitāmaho bhrātā sakulyo jananī tathā" iti | tatra pāṭhakrameṇaiva niyamaḥ | sakulya iti ca mātulādiparigrahārthaḥ | tathānye 'pi yonisaṃbaddhā ity adhyāhāraḥ | samānam anyat || 63 ||

 

_yat tu parakīyāṃ kim iti dadyād iti, tatrāha | yasmād,_

 

                    	**aprayacchan samāpnoti bhrūṇahatyām ṛtāv ṛtau |**

 

nindārthavādo 'yaṃ pravṛttyarthaḥ | pratyavāyavidhir vā || 63ab ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> etad apy uktam | dātrabhave gṛhasthāśramo duḥśliṣṭa eva | tatra pumāṃsa āśramāntarāśrayaṇenāpi kṛtinaḥ syuḥ | strīṇāṃ tu kā gatir iti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | syād ayaṃ doṣaḥ, yadi parādhīnataiva strīṇām ātyantikī syāt | dātṛsadbhāva eva tu tāsāṃ parādhīnatā | tadabhāve tu kim | ucyate |_

                    	**gamyaṃ tv abhāve dātṝṇāṃ kanyā kuryāt svayaṃ varam || 1.64 ||**

 

gamyaṃ gamanārham uktalakṣaṇam | svayam evartumatī varṣatrayād ūrdhvaṃ varaṃ kuryād dātrabhāve | vidyamāno 'pi ca dātā yadi na dadyāt, tato 'tyām ('syām ?) avasthāyāṃ tadīyam alaṃkāram utsṛjya svayam eva varaṃ varayet, smṛtyantarāt | yadāpy uktalakṣaṇas tāṃ necchet, tadāpi savarṇamātrāśrayaṇam aviruddham | yathāha baudhāyanaḥ |

                    	trīṇi varṣāṇy ṛtumatī kāṅkṣeta pitṛśāsanam |

                    	tataś caturthe varṣe tu vindeta sadṛśaṃ patim ||

                    	alabhamāne sadṛśe guṇahīnaṃ samāśrayet || iti | (BDh 4.1.14)

guṇavacanāc ca jātiniyamaḥ | sarvathā bhāryāyā bhartṛprāptiḥ, bhartuś ca bhāryāprāptiḥ, ity anavadyo gṛhasthāśramaḥ | tathā cāmnāyaḥ: "uta vai yācan dātāraṃ labhata eva | ato bhartā bhāryām" ityādi || 64 ||

 

_kasmāt punar adbhir vācā kanyāṃ dattvā pūrvadātari prete paraḥ svātantryād anyasmai na dadyāt | yasmāt,_

 

**              	sakṛt pradīyate kanyā haraṃs tāṃ coradaṇḍabhāk |**

 

tasmād anyasmai na dadyāt | tenaiva vivāhaṃ kārayet || 64ab ||

 

_kim eṣa evotsargaḥ | nety āha |_

 

                    	**dattām api harat pūrvaṃ śreyāṃś ced vara āvrajet || 1.65 ||**

 

pūrvavacanād adbhir vācā ca dattām api haret | na tu śreyāṃsam api varaṃ prāpya mantropanītām ity abhiprāyaḥ || 65 ||

 

_yaḥ punar duṣṭāṃ kanyām aduṣṭeyam iti prayacchet, tasya kā katheti | ucyate | sa tādṛśaḥ,_

 

**              	anākhyāya dadad doṣaṃ daṇḍya uttamasāhasam |**

 

yad vaivaṃ yojanā: pūrvavare spaṣṭaṃ doṣam anākhyāya nyāyato 'nubhāvyānyasmai śreyān iti matvā yaḥ prayacchati, sa daṇḍyaḥ ||

 

_na kevalaṃ dātā, varo'pi ca,_

 

                    	**aduṣṭāṃ yas tyajet kanyāṃ dūṣayaṃs tu mṛṣā śatam || 1.66 ||**

 

yas tu doṣarahitāṃ tyajet kanyāṃ, so 'py evaṃ daṇḍyaḥ | mṛṣaiva tu dūṣayan kārṣāpaṇaśataṃ daṇḍyaḥ, mṛṣety abhidhanāt | aduṣṭavacanāc ca duṣṭāṃ tyajato na doṣaḥ || 66 ||

 

_kasmāt punar mṛte bhartari na pāṇimātradūṣitānyasmai punar dīyate | yasmāt,_

 

                    	**akṣatā vā kṣatā vāpi punarbhūḥ saṃskṛtā punaḥ |**

 

yathaiva kṣatayoniḥ punar bhartṛsaṃyogāt punarbhūr bhavati, evam akṣatayonir api, aviśeṣāt | kasmāt punar dānam | smṛtyantarāt | yathāha manuḥ |

                    	sā ced akṣatayoniḥ syāt . . . . . punaḥ saṃskāram arhati || iti | (MDh 9.176)

tat kāmataḥ pravṛttau viśeṣavidhānam, na kartavyatayopadeśaḥ | tathā cāha manuḥ |

                    	na vivāhavidhāv uktaṃ vidhavāvedanaṃ kvacit || iti | (MDh 9.65)

                    	na dvitīyaś ca sādhvīnāṃ kvacid bhartopadiśyate || iti ca | (MDh 5.162)

tasmān na punaḥsaṃskāra ity ācāryābhiprāyaḥ ||

 

_yadā punaḥ svayam evānyaṃ savarṇam utkṛṣṭaṃ va samāśrayet, tadā ko doṣa iti, ucyate |_

 

**              	svairiṇī yā patiṃ hitvā savarṇaṃ kāmataḥ śrayet || 1.67 ||**

 

punarbhūḥ svairiṇīti ca saṃjñā dauṣṭyajñāpanārthā | jīvantaṃ mṛtaṃ vā yā bhartāraṃ tyaktvā svātantryāt savarṇam utkṛṣṭavarṇaṃ vā samāśrayet, sāpi svairiṇī | ataḥ svayam api nānya āśrayitavyaḥ | yat punaḥ śaṅkhenoktam, "tisraḥ punarbhvaś catasraḥ svairiṇyaḥ" iti, tad anayor dauṣṭyaprapañcanārthaṃ prāyaścittavivekārthaṃ vety etan nātīvopu(pa?)yujyate | evaṃ vāsiṣṭham api punarbhūlakṣaṇaṃ draṣṭavyam (VaDh 17.19–20) | sarvathā bhogye apy ete nirṇītatvād upekṣaṇīye iti ślokārthaḥ | tathā ca vakṣyati: "mṛte jīvati vā patyau" iti (YDh 1.75) || 67 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evaṃ saty aputrasya maraṇāt saṃtatyucchedaprasaṅgaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">astu</span> | kā naḥ pīḍā | atha vā_:

 

                    	**aputrāṃ gurvanujñānād devaraḥ putrakāmyayā |**

**              	sapiṇḍo vā sagotro vā ghṛtābhyakta ṛtāv iyāt || 1.68 ||**

 

ghṛtābhyañjanavacanaṃ kāmapravṛttinirodhārtham | tataś cāliṅganādi vaikārikatvād dūrāpetam | ṛtugrahaṇaṃ tv anyadā darśanādy api kathaṃ na syād ity evam artham || 68 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">kiṃ</span> sakṛd eva gamanam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">na</span>, adṛṣṭārthatvaprasaṅgāt | apatyārthaṃ hy etad gamanam | atas tu,_

 

                    	**ā garbhasaṃbhavād gacchet patitas tv anyathā bhavet |**

 

prāg garbhasaṃbhūteḥ parityāgāt | tuśabdaś caivakārārthaḥ ||

 

_yad vaivaṃ yojanā | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ayaṃ niyogapakṣo duḥśliṣṭaḥ, pātakaprasaṅgāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">na</span> |_

 

                    	**anena vidhinā jātaḥ kṣetriṇaḥ sa bhavet sutaḥ || 1.69 ||**

anena niyogavidhinā jātaḥ kṣetriṇo bhrātrāder aurasavat putro bhavatīty ayam vidhiḥ | nātra vicikitsā kāryety arthaḥ | na caivaṃvṛttaḥ patito bhavati | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kathaṃ</span> tarhi "patitas tv anyathā bhavet" iti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">tadaniyukter</span> vikārād vā gacchann ity abhiprāyaḥ | ayaṃ punaḥ paropakārāya pravṛtter abhyudayabhāg ity anavadyo niyogaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">atra codayanti</span> | nāyaṃ niyogapakṣaḥ śreyān, smṛtyācāravirodhāt | tathā cāha manuḥ |

                    	nānyasmin vidhavā nārī niyoktavyā dvijātibhiḥ |

                    	anyasmin hi niyuñjānā dharmaṃ hanyuḥ sanātanam || iti | (MDh 9.64)

purākalpaṃ copanyasyopasaṃhṛtam |

                    	tadāprabhṛti yo mohāt pramītapatikāṃ striyam |

                    	niyojayaty apatyārthe taṃ vigarhanti sādhavaḥ || iti | (MDh 9.68)

ato nāsti niyogaḥ | tathā ca śiṣṭasamācāraḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> iyam api smṛtir eva "aputrāṃ gurvanujñānāt" (YDh 1.68) ityādi | mānave 'pi |

                    	devarād vā sapiṇḍād vā striyā samyaṅ niyuktayā | (MDh 9.59)

ityādi | na ceyaṃ lobhādimūleti śakyaṃ vaktum, sarvathā vikārapratiṣedhāt | tad uktaṃ "ghṛtābhyaktaḥ" iti (YDh 1.68) | manunāpi ca:

                    	vidhavāyāṃ niyuktas tu ghṛtākto vāgyato niśi | iti | (MDh 9.60)

ato neyam apasmṛtiḥ | atha śvaśuradhanādīcchayā lobha āśaṅkyeta, tad api

                    	prajepsitādhigantavyā santānasya parikṣaye | (MDh 9.59)

ity anenaiva nirastam | tathā coktam |

                    	patitau bhavato gatvā niyuktāv apy anāpadi | iti | (MDh 9.58)

vasiṣṭhenāpi: "dhanalobhān nāsti niyogaḥ" iti (VaDh 17.65) | ato nirdoṣaḥ | śāstrāviśeṣāt tu pratiṣedho vikalpāya bhavati | ato na virodhaḥ | anye tu prāg vivāhād uparate bhartari niyogādhikāraṃ varṇayanti, sāmānyaviśeṣopasaṃhṛtinyāyāt | yathāha manuḥ |

                    	yasyā mriyeta kanyāyā vācā satye kṛte patiḥ |

                    	tām anena vidhānena nijo vindeta devaraḥ || iti | (MDh 9.69)

tat tu vidhavāyāṃ niyuktas tv ity anenaiva nirastam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca sāpi vidhaveti śakyaṃ vaktum | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">na</span> smṛtyantaravirodhāt | yathāha vasiṣṭhaḥ: "pretapatnī ṣaṇmāsaṃ vratacāriṇī" ity upakramya, "pitrā bhrātrā vā niyogaṃ kārayet" ityādi (VaDh 17.55–56) | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> anūḍhāpi prete patyau pretapatny eva | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span> | na hi prāg vivāhāt patnīśabdapravṛttir iti | evaṃ hi bhagavataḥ pāṇineḥ smaraṇam: "patur no yajñasaṃyoge" iti (Pāṇ 4.1.33) | ato 'satkalpanam, upakramopasaṃhārāt | kathaṃ tarhi "yasyā mriyeta" (MDh 9.69) ity ayaṃ ślokaḥ | āsuravivāhaviṣayatayā vyākhyeyaḥ | yasyāḥ kanyāyāḥ śulkaṃ dattvā śulkado mriyeta, sā yadīcchet, tato devarāya pūrvavat pradātavyā | na ced, niyogaṃ devareṇaiva kārayet | yad vā "nijo vindeta" (MDh 6.69) iti nijagrahaṇāt sodaryo devaraḥ anena vidhinā naiyogikena vaivāhikena vā vindetaiva | sāpatnas tu kanyānumataḥ | tathā cāha |

                    	kanyāyāṃ dattaśulkāyāṃ mriyeta yadi śulkadaḥ |

                    	devarāya pradātavyā yadi kanyānumanyate || iti | (MDh 9.97)

yadā tv adattaśulka eva mriyeta, tadā tasmin prete kumāry eva satīcchayānyasmai pitrā vidhivad deyā | yathāha vasiṣṭhaḥ |

                    	adbhir vācā ca dattā yā mriyetādau varo yadi |

                    	na ca mantropanītā syāt kumārī pitur eva sā || iti | (VaDh 17.72)

ādāv iti vacanād vivāhasaṃnidhau vāgdattāpy akanyaketi jñayate | "balāc cet prahṛtā kanyā" (VaDh 17.73) ity asya punar ayam arthaḥ | prahṛtā dūṣitā, praśabdasāmarthyāt | kṣātrāc ca vidher anyatraiva draṣṭavyam, tatra dūṣaṇāsaṃbhavāt | yadi mantrair na saṃskṛtā tato 'nyasmai vidhivat prāyaścittaṃ kārayitvā deyā | kṛtaprāyaścittā ca "yathā kanyā tathaiva sā" (VaDh 17.73) iti mantavyam | idaṃ tu kalpāntaram |

                    	pāṇigrāhe mṛte kanyā kevalaṃ mantrasaṃskṛtā | iti | (VaDh 17.74)

asyārthaḥ: grāmadharmeṇa pūrvam api vivāhāt pāṇigrahaṇam | tasmin pāṇigrāhe | mṛte kanyāhuter vā prāk paṇigrahaṇād yady akṣatayoniḥ | tathāpy anyena bhartrā punar vivāhasaṃskāram arhatīti | sarvathā pariṇītāyāḥ punaḥ pariṇayanābhāvaḥ | tad uktam:

                    	na vivāhavidhāv uktaṃ vidhavāvedanaṃ kvacit | iti | (MDh 9.65)

tathā ca baudhāyanaḥ |

                    	nisṛṣṭāyāṃ hute vāpi yasyai bhartā mriyeta saḥ | iti | (BDh 4.1.16)

api nisṛṣṭāyām, api hute, na pariṇītāyām ity arthaḥ | "sā ced akṣatayoniḥ syāt" (BDh 4.1.16) ity etad eva spaṣṭīkaroti, yad upavarṇitam asmābhiḥ | ato na kanyāviṣayā niyogasmṛtiḥ | kas tarhi viṣayaḥ | prete patyau santānaparikṣaye ca | pratiṣedhasāmarthyāc ca vikalpaḥ | tathā cāmnāyaḥ: "tasmād ekasya bahvyo jāyā bhavanti, naikasyai bahavaḥ sahapatayaḥ" iti (AitB 3.23) | sahapratiṣedhāc ca krameṇa bhavantīti jñāyate | tathā "yasmai māṃ pitā dadyād naivāhaṃ taṃ jīvantaṃ hāsyāmi" iti (ŚB 4.1.5.9) jīvannahānavacanāc ca mṛte bhartari niyogo 'stīti jñāyate |

                    	ko vāṃ śayutrā vidhaveva devaraṃ

                                	maryaṃ na yoṣā kṛṇute sadhastha ā | (RV 10.40.2)

ity asmāt punar mantravarṇāt spaṣṭataro niyogaḥ | evaṃ hīndreṇa cirād dṛṣṭāv aśvināv uktau durdarśau yuvāṃ kva punar vidhaveva yoṣā devaraṃ maryaṃ manuṣyabhāvaṃ śayane harṣasthāne āpādayantī kaccid ā kurute vām upacaratīty arthaḥ | anena niyogaṃ spaṣṭīkaroti | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ: " prājāpatye muhūrte pāṇigrāhavad upacaret" iti (VaDh 17.61) | ato 'navadyo niyogaḥ |

        	 <span style="text-decoration:underline;">atrocyate</span> | naivaṃ niyogasmṛtir vyākhyeyā, samācāravirodhāt, vikalpasya cānyāyyatvāt | kathaṃ tarhi | śūdrāviṣayā niyogasmṛtiḥ | kuta etad, manuvacanāt |

                    	nānyasmin vidhavā nārī niyoktavyā dvijātibhiḥ | (MDh 9.64)

iti dvijātisaṃbaddhaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ | sāmānyataḥ śūdrasaṃbandhitayā vidhiḥ | tasmād avikalpaḥ | tathā coktam |

                    	ayaṃ dvijair hi vidvadbhiḥ paśudharmo vigarhitaḥ |

                    	manuṣyāṇām api prokto vene rājyaṃ praśāsati || iti | (MDh 9.66)

manuṣyāṇām api śūdrāṇām apīty arthaḥ | tathā ca samācāraḥ | yat punar vyāsena vicitravīryabhāryāsv apatyotpādanam, tad draupadīvivāhavad anādṛtyam | atha vā kṣatriyāṇām apy anvayakṣaye rājyaparipālanāya niyogo 'bhyanujñāyate | sa ca rājñām eva | kāryānurodhād vyāsavacanāc ca | rājñāṃ brāhmaṇenaiva kārayitavyam | evaṃ ca saty āmnāyā api kṣatriyaviṣayā eva "naivāhaṃ taṃ jīvantaṃ hāsyāmi" (ŚB 4.1.5.9) ityādi | jīvan samartho na hātavya ity āmnāyārthaḥ | "naikasyai bahavaḥ sahapatayaḥ" (AitB 3.23) iti tu punaḥsaṃskāraviṣayam | tatra mukhyaḥ patiśabdaḥ | mantravarṇas tu śūdraviṣaya eva vyākhyeyaḥ | evaṃ devarādivākyāny anyāny api vyākhyeyāni | tathā ca vṛddhamanuḥ |

                    	śūdrāṇām eva dharmo 'yaṃ patyau prete 'nyasaṃśrayaḥ |

                    	lobhān mūḍhair avidvadbhiḥ kṣatriyair api caryate ||

ity uktvāha |

                    	vāyuproktāṃ tathā gāthāṃ paṭhanty atra manīṣiṇaḥ |

                    	viprāṇāṃ na niyogo 'sti prete patyau na vedanam ||

iyaṃ sā gāthā |

                    	akāryam etad viprāṇāṃ vidhavā yan niyujyate |

                    	uhyate vā mṛte patyau devareṇa viśeṣataḥ || iti |

<span style="text-decoration:underline;">katham</span> idānīm etad vasiṣṭhavacanam |

                    	bhrātary avyapadeśena nādhyetavyaṃ kadācana | iti | (not in VaDh)

anena hy adhyāpanasaṃbandhād brāhmaṇānām api niyogādhikāro 'stīti gamyate | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | naitad yuktam, uktatvān nyāyasya | bhūyasām ananyaparāṇāṃ cānarthakyād varam ekasyānyaparasya ca bādhakalpanā | kṣatriyaviṣayaṃ caitad vākyam | teṣāṃ hy āpadi niyogādhikārāt | sa ca brāhmaṇenaivety uktam | tenaivaṃ yojanā: bhrātary adhyāpayaty api nādhyetavyam | kena | avyapadeśena | na vyapadiśyate 'nenety avyapadeśaḥ | anyajātīya ity arthaḥ | kimartham | boddhavyam “gurutalpasya nimittam”, bhrātuḥ śiṣyabhāryāgamanāt, “bhartā hy āpatsu devaraḥ” |[^8] bharteti bharaṇayogāc chraiṣṭhyāc ca brāhmaṇaḥ sa yasmād āpatsu devaro bhavati, niyojyata ity arthaḥ | tasmāt tato nādhyetavyam | āpatsv iti caikasyām evāpadi | bahuvacanaṃ gauravārtham | santānaparikṣayalakṣaṇaivāpad yathā syāt | nādhyāpayitavya iti ca vaktavye nādhyetavyam ity uktaṃ kṣetriṇaḥ putra iti jñāpanārtham | kathaṃ vāsya brāhmaṇaviṣayatvopapattiḥ | na hi sodaryayor ni(r?)yogasaṃbhavaḥ | kathaṃ kṛtvā | yadi tāvan niyojyo 'py aputraḥ, tadātmana evotpādayet | atha tasya putro 'sti, tadā

                    	bhrātṝṇām ekajātānāṃ yady ekaḥ putravān bhavet |

                    	sarve te tena putreṇa putriṇo manur abravīt || (MDh 9.182)

iti vacanād akṣīṇatvāt santānasya kuto niyogaḥ | kṣatriyaviṣayatve tu naiṣa virodhaḥ | atha sāpatnaviṣayatocyeta | tat kṣatriye 'pi samānam | yadā tv ekajātānām ity asyaikavarṇajātānām ity arthaḥ, tadā spaṣṭaiva kṣatriyaviṣayatā | yat tu brāhmaṇyāḥ proṣite bhartari kālapratīkṣaṇavacanaṃ, tad bhartur antikagamanārthaṃ na niyogārtham iti vivicya vacanīyam | tasmāt sūktā niyogavākyānāṃ viṣayakalpanā | evaṃ tāvac chūdrāṇāṃ niyogādhikāra uktaḥ || 69 ||

 

_yadā punar brāhmaṇy apy evaṃ kuryāt tadā tāṃ tadrakṣaṇādhikṛtaḥ |_

 

                    	**hṛtādhikārāṃ malināṃ piṇḍamātropajīvinīm |**

**              	paribhūtām adhaḥśayyāṃ vāsayed vyabhicāriṇīm || 1.70 ||**

 

evaṃ tāvat saṃtānaparikṣaye 'pi niyogānadhikārāt pravartamānā vyabhicāriṇy eva | tām evam apanītagṛhādhipatyāṃ kucelāṃ varopanītasaṃskārarahitāṃ grāsamātrabhaktāṃ sarvathā paribhūtāṃ sthaṇḍilaśāyinīṃ vāsayet | etad eva prāyaścittaṃ na vakṣyāmāṇaṃ, śāstravyāmohāt pravṛtter alpadoṣatā yataḥ | smṛtyantarāc caitat saṃvatsaraprāyaścittam || 70 ||

 

_atha vā, yadi striyaḥ svātantryād anyam āśrayeyus tato doṣabhāginyaḥ syuḥ | yadā punar dhanalobhād vyāmohād vā bandhubhir niyujyante, tadā teṣām eva doṣaḥ prāyaścittaṃ ca, na tu strīṇām | ataḥ striyo nirdoṣāḥ | kiṃ tu |_

 

**              	somaḥ śaucaṃ dadau strīṇāṃ gandharvaś ca śubhāṃ giram |**

**              	pāvakaḥ sarvabhakṣatvaṃ medhyā vai yoṣito matāḥ || 1.71 ||**

 

vaiśabdo 'vadhāraṇārthaḥ | yasmāt somādibhir āsāṃ śaucaṃ manovākkāyalakṣaṇaṃ dattam, tasmān nirdōṣā evaitāḥ | puṃsām eva niyogakartṝṇām doṣa ity abhiprāyaḥ | anena niyogakartṝṇām api prāyaścittam astīty uktam, na tu strīṇāṃ niṣiddham, pūrvaślokānarthakyaprasaṅgāt | svātantryād vyabhicāre vā tad draṣṭavyam | niyoge tu pāratantryāt striyo nirdoṣāḥ || 71 ||

 

_kva punaḥ strīṇāṃ doṣaḥ | kva vā tyāgaḥ | ucyate |_

 

                    	**vyabhicāra ṛtau śuddhir garbhe tyāgo vidhīyate |**

**              	garbhabhartṛvadhe cāsāṃ tathā mahati pātake || 1.72 ||**

 

strīṇāṃ doṣo vyabhicārād bhartuḥ | tatra coktaṃ prāyaścittaṃ hṛtādhikārām ityādi | evam ṛtāv api vyabhicāre na ced garbhasaṃbhavaḥ śuddhir asty evety abhiprāyaḥ | garbhotpattau tyāga eva | vidhīyata iti vicikitsānivṛttyartham | tathā garbhavadhe bhartṛvadhe mahāpātakasaṃbaddhe ca brahmahatyādau | tyāga ity anuṣaṅgaḥ | garbhavadhaś ca saubhāgyadarpādinā ṛtuskandanam | tathā ca baudhāyanaḥ |

                    	bhartuḥ pratiniveśena yā bhāryā skandayed ṛtum |

                    	tāṃ grāmamadhye vikhyāpya bhrūṇaghnīṃ nirdhamed gṛhāt || iti | (BDh 4.1.20)

bhartṛvadhaś ca vācanikaḥ, anyatra mahāpātakavacanād eva siddhatvāt | tathā cāha gārgyaḥ: "patitāḥ striyas tyājyāḥ bhartṛvadhapratijñāyāṃ ca" iti | kṣatriyādiviṣayo vāyaṃ garbhabhartṛvadho yojyaḥ | ato 'nyatra mahaty api doṣe na tyājyāḥ || 72 ||

 

_kiṃ tarhi |_

 

**              	surāpī vyādhitā dhūrtī vandhyārthaghny apriyaṃvadā |**

**              	strīprasūś cādhivettavyā puruṣadveṣiṇī tathā || 1.73 ||**

 

evamādibhir doṣair adhivettavyā | na tyājyety arthaḥ | surāśabdena cātra gaulīmādhvyor grahaṇaṃ, mahāpātake tyāgopadeśāt | kṣatriyādibhir api niṣiddhāṃ pibantyas tyājyāḥ | vyādhitā asamādheyakuṣṭhādirogagrastā | dhūrtī vañcanaśīlā | vandhyā prasiddhā | arthaśabdas tu dharmakāmayor api grāhakaḥ | puruṣārthaghnīty arthaḥ | apriyaṃvadā prasiddhaiva | strīprasūḥ kevalastrīprajananī | puruṣadveṣiṇī ratiparāṅmukhī | adhivedanam uparipariṇayanam | tad āsām anubhāṣya doṣaṃ kartavyaṃ, smṛtyantarāt: "duṣṭāṃ bhāryāṃ jāyāṃ paribhāṣyādhivedayet" iti || 73 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> adhivedanam api tyāga eva, anyopādāne tayā kāryābhāvāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span> |_

 

**              	adhivinnā tu bhartavyā mahad eno 'nyathā bhavet |**

**              	yatrānukūlyaṃ dampatyos trivargas tatra vardhate || 1.74 ||**

 

tuśabdo 'piśabdārthaḥ | adhivinnāpīty arthaḥ | yad votkṣyāvadhāraṇārthaḥ | bhartavyaiva nopagantavyety arthaḥ | doṣāparityāge ca tat | anyathā mahad enaḥ syāt | mahāpātakam ity arthaḥ | kasmāt punar evam adhivedanādyupadeśaḥ | yasmāt, yatrānukūlyam aikamatyaṃ jāyāpatyoḥ, trivargo dharmārthakāmalakṣaṇas tatra vṛddhim upaiti | anyathā tu viparyayaḥ syāt | tasmāt sūktam adhivedanādyanuṣṭhānam || 74 ||

 

_kasmāt punar adhivinnā bhartāraṃ parityajyānyaṃ na samāśrayet | yasmāt,_

 

**              	mṛte jīvati vā patyau yā nānyam upagacchati |**

**              	seha kīrtim avāpnoti modate comayā saha || 1.75 ||**

 

sahety upamārthe | anupagame ca stutidarśanād upagame doṣānumānam | aihikaphalaṃ ca kīrtiḥ, āmuṣmikaṃ svargāvāptiḥ | anyathā tu dvayaviparyayaḥ | tasmād adhivinnayāpi na bhartā tyājyaḥ || 75 ||

 

_bhartā tu doṣavān madhye tyājyaḥ, tādṛṣasyaiva cājñānanyaparābhir anuṣṭheyā, yasmāt,_

 

**              	strībhir bhartṛvacaḥ kāryam eṣa dharmaḥ paraḥ striyāḥ |**

**              	ā śuddheḥ saṃpratīkṣyo 'pi mahāpātakadūṣitaḥ || 1.76 ||**

 

doṣavato 'pi bhartuḥ strībhir vacanam avikalpamānābhiḥ kāryam | eṣa strīṇāṃ paro dharmaḥ | avadhāraṇārtho vā paraśabdaḥ | eṣa eva dharmaḥ | nānyo dharma ity arthaḥ | tathā ca manuḥ |

                    	viśīlaḥ kāmavṛtto vā guṇair vā parivarjitaḥ |

                    	upacaryaḥ striyā sādhvyā satataṃ devavat patiḥ || iti | (MDh 5.154)

yadā punar mahāpātakadoṣād vyavahārāyogyo bhartā syāt, tadā kim | tadāpy ā śuddheḥ saṃpratīkṣyaḥ | abhividhāv āṅ draṣṭavyaḥ | apeś cotkṛṣya yojanā | mahāpātakadūṣito 'pīty arthaḥ | tataś ca tatsamādau prāg api śuddher na tyājyaḥ | saṃśabdāc ca brahmacāriṇyā tatparayā ca pratīkṣitavyaḥ | sarvathā strībhir bhartā jīvan mṛto vā na tyājya iti prakaraṇārthaḥ | tathā ca vyāsaḥ: "bhartrekadevatā  nāryaḥ" iti || 76 ||

 

_yāś caivaṃ bhartāram ananyaparatayaivopacaranti, tāḥ prayatnato bhartṛbhir api |_

 

                    	**lokānantyadivaprāptiḥ putrapautraprapautrikā |**

_strītaḥ |_

                    	**yasmāt tasmāt striyaḥ sevyāḥ**

 

_kiṃ ca,_

                                                                    	**bhartavyāś ca surakṣitāḥ || 1.77 ||**

 

lokaprāptir ānantyaprāptir divaprāptiś ca krameṇa putrapautraprapautrikā yasmāt, tasmāt striyaḥ sevyāḥ | tathā cāhuḥ |

                    	putreṇa lokāñ jayati pautreṇānantyam aśnute |

                    	atha putrasya pautreṇa bradhnasyāpnoti viṣṭapam || iti | (MDh 9.137)

lokaḥ pṛthivī | ānantyam antarikṣam | divaḥ svargaḥ | pāṭhāntaram: lokānantyaṃ divaprāptir iti | tasyārthaḥ: divaprāptis tv agnihotrādyanuṣṭhānāt | lokānantyaṃ ca tadabhyāsāt | tathā ca carakāḥ: "na sa tasmāl lokāt pracyavate, yas trir ījānaḥ" iti | kiṃ ca putrapautraprapautrikā ca saṃtatir ata eva | yasmāc caivaṃ tasmāt striyaḥ sevyā ityādi samānam || 77 ||

 

_striyaḥ sevyā ity uktam | tatrāniyamaprāptāv āha |_

 

**              	ṣoḍaśartur niśāḥ strīṇāṃ tasmin yugmāsu saṃviśet |**

**              	brahmacāry eva parvāṇy ādyāś catasraś ca varjayet || 1.78 ||**

 

rajodarśanādiḥ ṣoḍaśa rātraya ṛtusajñakaḥ kālaḥ | tatra nāryo garbhagrahaṇasamarthā bhavantīti tāsu yugmāsu rātriṣūpagacchet | kim evaṃ syāt, brahmacāry eva, evaṃ gacchan nityenoparitanaślokenāsya saṃbandhaḥ | brahmacaryaśabdaś cāyaṃ virodhāt tatphale vartate | brahmacaryaphalaṃ brahmalokaprāptir asyety arthaḥ | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ |

                    	ṛtau ca gacchan vidhivac ca juhvan

                                	na brāhmaṇaś cyavate brahmalokāt || iti | (VaDh 8.17)

yad vā kāraṇāntarād brahmacarye sthito 'pi gacchet | yato gacchann api brahmacāry eva, vratān na hīyata ity arthaḥ | evaṃ cātiprasaktāv āha: parvāṇy amāvāsyādīni | ādyāś cartau catasro rātrīr varjayed iti || 78 ||

 

_kiṃ cānyat |_

 

                    	**evaṃ gacchan striyaṃ kṣāmāṃ maghāmūlaṃ ca varjayet |**

**              	sustha indau sakṛt putraṃ lakṣaṇyaṃ janayet pumān || 1.79 ||**

 

kṣāmā durbalā rogiṇī vā | vandhyety anye, yathāha bhṛguḥ |

                    	adhivinnāṃ tu yo bhāryām upeyād apy ṛtau dvijaḥ|

                    	rakṣaṇārtham akāmaś cet prājāpatyena śudhyati || iti

tat punaḥ putrārthatvād adhigamanasyātrāprasaktam eva | maghāpauṣṇaṃ cety ante paṭhanti | tathā ca gaṇitajñāḥ |

                    	prasavas tu niṣekarkṣāt daśame yoṣitāmuḍau |

                    	yasmāt taṃ varjayet tasmād revatīṣu maghāsu ca || iti |

tat punaś caśabdād eva revatyavāpter akiṃcit | mūlam apy aśvinyāder gaṇḍāntatvād varjanīyam eva | upalakṣaṇārthatvāc ca mūlaśruter anyad apīdṛk pariharaṇīyam, pramāṇāntaramūlatvāc cāsya punar varjanavacanasya | kiṃ ca, "sustha indau sakṛt putraṃ lakṣaṇyaṃ janayet pumān" | sakṛd ity asya pūrvaślokagatena saṃbandhaḥ saṃviśed ity anena | tathā cāha manuḥ |

                    	nindyāsv aṣṭāsu cānyāsu striyo rātriṣu varjayet |

                    	brahmacāry eva bhavati yatra tatrāśrame vasan || iti || (MDh 3.50)

ṣaḍ nindyāḥ ādyāś catasraḥ ekādaśī trayodaśī ca | aṣṭāv anyā anindyāḥ | evaṃ caturdaś varjyāḥ | śiṣṭaṃ rātridvayam | tatraikā stryartheti manvabhiprāyaḥ | ācāryas tu putrotpādanam eva naiyogikaṃ manyamānaḥ sakṛd ity āha | ata eva catasraś cety ayam api cakāro na rātryantarārthaḥ | catasra iti pratiṣedho 'nyadāvarjanārthaḥ | astu vaivaṃ rātryantaragrahaṇārthaś cakāro 'pi, arthātirekāt | evaṃ gacchan lakṣaṇyaṃ janayet pumān strīto 'tiriktaśuklaḥ | tathā cāha manuḥ: "pumān puṃso 'dhike śuklaḥ" iti (MDh 3.49) | sarvathā śāstrābādhena bhiṣagdaivajñādyupadeśānusārāt tathābhigamanakriyā, yathā ca lakṣaṇyaputrotpādaḥ syād iti ślokadvayasyārthaḥ | putram iti coddeśyatvād atantraṃ saṃkhyā | tathā ca śaṅkhaḥ |

                    	putrapautrapratiṣṭhasya bahvapatyasya jīvataḥ | iti |

mantravarṇaś ca "aśūnyopasthā jīvatam astu mātā" (ĀpMP 1.4.8) iti bahuputratāṃ darśayati, "daśāsyāṃ putrāṇ ā dhehi patim ekādaśaṃ kṛdhi" (ĀpMP 1.4.6) iti ca | yugmarātryādivacanaṃ tu liṅgavivakṣayety adoṣaḥ | pūrvaślokaḍ eva ca putrārthaṃ striyaḥ sevyā ity ṛtāv eva gamanaprāpteḥ sakṛdgamananiyamaparatayaitac chlokadvayam ṛtugatarātryantaranivṛttiphalaṃ draṣṭavyam | mānavaṃ tu "ṛtukālābhigāmī syāt" (MDh 3.45) iti vrate 'rthe smaryamāṇaṇinipratyayāntatvān niyamaparatayaiva vyākhyeyam | ślokāntarānusārāt tu putrārthinaḥ sakṛdgamananiyama it vyākhyātam | etenaiva vāsiṣṭhaṃ vyākhyātam (VaDh 8.17) | "ṛtukālābhigāmī syāt" iti phalaśruteś ca "ṛtau gacchann" (VaDh 8.17) iti smṛtyantarānusārāc ca yugmāyāṃ rātrau sakṛd iti vyākhyeyam | gautamīyaṃ tv anṛtuparisaṃkhyārtham "ṛtāv upeyad" iti kecit (GDh 5.1) | ṛtāv anṛtau vārthād eva gamanprāpteḥ, sūtrāntarārambhāc ca "sarvatra vā pratiṣiddhavarjam" iti (GDh 5.2) | tathā sūtradvayam apy anarthakaṃ syād, arthād eva vikalpaprāpteḥ | tasmāt tad api niyamārtham eva vyākhyeyam | uttarasūtraṃ tv arthaprāptam evānṛtau gamanavikalpam anūdya pratiṣiddhavarjam ity evam artham | ayaṃ tv atra saṃpradāyaḥ: ṛtāv ajātaputraḥ sakṛd agacchan pratyavaiti, jātaputrasya tv agamane 'py adoṣaḥ | tathā cāhuḥ |

                    	jyeṣṭha eva tu putraḥ syāt kāmajān itarān viduḥ | iti | (cf. MDh 9.107)

yāvadbhāryaṃ caikaikaputrānutpādane pratyavāyaḥ, tadapekṣayaiva putrotpādanavidhānāt | asavarṇāsu tu jātaputrasya yāthākāmyam, smṛtyantarāt |

                    	kṛtadāro 'varān dārān bhikṣitvā yo 'dhigacchati |

                    	ratimātraṃ phalaṃ tasya dravyadātus tu saṃtatiḥ || iti | (MDh 11.5)

avaraśabdo 'yam asavarṇābhiprāyaḥ, savarṇayaiva kṛtadāratvāt | yathā caitad evaṃ tathokaṃ prāk | jātūkarṇaś cāha: "savarṇayā kṛtadāro nānyām icchet saṃtānasyānyagāmitvād" iti | nāryutpādane tu vikalpaḥ, rātridvayasya manunoktatvāt, atra ca sakṛcchruteḥ | anṛtau tu strīkāmād eva gamanaṃ, "sarvatra vā" (GDh 5.2) iti sūtrārambhāt | ṛtāv apy uktakālātirekeṇānṛtutulyatvāt stryanurodhenaiva gamanam iti sthitiḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ṛtāv api strīkāmād eva gamanaṃ yuktaṃ, kāmātmatāniṣedhāt, mantravarṇāc ca: "uto tv asmai tanvaṃ vi sasre jāyeva patya uśatī suvāsāḥ" iti (RV 10.71.4) | apy ekasmai vāgvisrabdham ātmanam arpayati jāyeva patye uśatī kāmayamānā suvāsāḥ ṛtukāleṣv iti strīkāmād eva gamanapravṛttiṃ darśayati | naivam | ubhayaniyamadyotanārtho 'yaṃ mantravarṇa iti | viśeṣeṇa putrotpādanacodanā strīpuṃsayor yataḥ, tathā ca dvayor apy agamane pratyavāyāmnānam | tathā cāha baudhāyanaḥ |

                    	ṛtumatīṃ tu yo bhāryāṃ saṃnidhau nopagacchati |

                    	tasyā rajasi taṃ māsaṃ pitaras tasya śerate || iti | (BDh 4.1.18)

striyo 'pi |

                    	bhartuḥ pratiniveśena yā bhāryā skandayed ṛtum |

                    	tāṃ grāmamadhye vikhyāpya bhrūṇaghnīṃ nirdhamed gṛhāt || iti | (BDh 4.1.20)

tasmād ṛtau na strīkāmād eva gamanaṃ yuktam ity eṣā dik || 79 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvad ṛtau gamanavidhim uktvāthedānīm arthaprāptatvād gamanasyāniyame prāpta āha |_

 

**              	yāthākāmī bhaved vāpi strīṇāṃ varam anusmaran |**

**              	svadāranirataś caiva striyo rakṣyā yataḥ smṛtāḥ || 1.80 ||**

 

apiśabdasya kramabhedena yojanā: yāthākāmy api bhavet | strīvat kāmo yasya sa yāthākāmī, vacanābhāve 'pi yadṛcchayā gamanasya prāptatvāt | yad vā yāthākāmy api vā yāthākāmy eva syād ity avadhāraṇārtho vāśabdaḥ | kasmāt | strīṇāṃ varam anusmaran | "api naḥ śvo vijaniṣyamāṇāḥ patibhiḥ saha śayīran" (VaDh 12.24; 5.8) ityādivākyaṃ sūcayati | strīkāmād anṛtāv api gacched iti ślokārthaḥ | kiṃ ca svadāranirataś caiva syāt | kutaḥ | striyo rakṣyā yataḥ smṛtāḥ | uktam etat: "bhartavyāś ca surakṣitāḥ" (YDh 1.77) iti | rakṣā ca strīṇāṃ svadāraniratatvam eva paramārthatvena | na tu tāḍanādikā | tayā tāsām anartho 'pi saṃbhāvyeta | tathā ca laukikāḥ "pāñcālastrīṣu mārdavam" iti paṭhanti | cakāra evakāraś ca pādapūraṇārthau | yad votkṛṣya striyo rakṣyā eva yataḥ smṛtā iti yojyam | rakṣaṇavidhinaiva svadāraniratatvaniyamān na vidhyantarāpekṣety abhiprāyaḥ | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ |

                    	yā syād anaticāreṇa ratiḥ sā dharmasaṃśritā | iti | (VaDh 12.23)

manur apy āha |

                    	svāṃ prasūtiṃ caritraṃ ca kulam ātmānam eva ca |

                    	svaṃ ca dharmaṃ prayatnena jāyāṃ rakṣan hi rakṣati || iti | (MDh 9.7)

"prasūtirakṣaṇam asaṃkaro dharmaḥ" (GDh 8.3) iti ca gautamaḥ | tena rakṣaṇārthaṃ varaśruter anṛtāv api strīkāmād agacchato doṣa ity anavadyam || 80 ||

 

_yasmāc ca lokānantyadivaprāptiḥ putrapautraprapautrakāḥ strītaḥ, striyaḥ sevyā iti ca sthitam | tasmād eva kāraṇāt,_

 

**              	bhartṛbhrātṛpitṛjñātiśvaśrūśvaśuradevaraiḥ |**

**              	bandhubhiś ca striyaḥ pūjyā bhūṣaṇācchādanāśanaiḥ || 1.81 ||**

 

sarvopakārakatvāt saṃtānasya strīṇāṃ ca tatkāraṇatvāt sarvaiḥ pūjyā iti | na mūlāntarāpekṣā | jñātiśabdo mātulādyarthaḥ | caśabdaḥ sakhyādyarthaḥ || 81 ||

 

_evaṃ sarvaiḥ paripūjyamānā na garvitā vyayaśīlā ca syāt | kiṃ tarhi |_

 

**              	saṃyatopaskarā dakṣā hṛṣṭā vyayaparāṅmukhī |**

**              	kuryāc chvaśurayoḥ pādavandanaṃ bhartṛtatparā || 1.82 ||**

 

ca syād iti śeṣaḥ || 82 ||

 

_idaṃ cānyat |_

 

                    	**krīḍāśarīrasaṃskārasamājotsavadarśanam |**

**              	hāsaṃ paragṛhaṃ yānaṃ tyajet proṣitabhartṛkā || 1.83 ||**

 

tathā cāha manuḥ |

                    	pānaṃ durjanasaṃsargaḥ patyā ca viraho 'ṭanam |

                    	svapno 'nyagehavāsaś ca nārīsaṃdūṣaṇāni ṣaṭ || iti (MDh 9.13) || 83 ||

 

_yadā punar etāny aniyamāt strīsvābhāvyāt sarvajñātipūjyatvād vā svayaṃ nānutiṣṭhet tadā ka enām anuṣṭhāpayet | yadā vā proṣito bhartā vipanno 'nutpanno vā tadā kāsyāḥ pālaka ity ata āha |_

 

**              	rakṣet kanyāṃ pitā vinnāṃ patiḥ putras tu vārdhake |**

**              	abhāve jñatyas tv eṣāṃ svātantryaṃ na kvacit striyāḥ || 1.84 ||**

 

kāle karmaṇi vā | tathā cāha manuḥ |

                    	nāsti strīṇāṃ pṛthag yajño na vrataṃ nāpy upoṣitam |

                    	patiṃ śuśrūṣate yena tena svarge mahīyate || (MDh 5.155)

iti karmaṇy api pāratantryaṃ darśayati || 84 ||
