_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evaṃ sati strīṇām adoṣaḥ, pitrādīnāṃ rakṣaṇopadeśāt | yad vānyarakṣakāsaṃnidhāne yady utpannarakṣakavipāttiḥ, tadā kāmacāritāpi strīṇāṃ prasajyeta | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">manda, maivaṃ</span> |_

 

                    	**pitṛmātṛsutabhrātṛśvaśrūśvaśuramātulaiḥ|**

**              	hīnā na syād vinā bhartrā garhaṇīyānyathā bhavet || 1.85 ||**

 

bhartṛśabdo 'yaṃ rakṣakamātre vartate | mātrādivacanād anyām api striyaṃ vṛddhāṃ kāṃcid upāsīta | na tu svatantrā syāt | yatra vā kaścit pālayitā, tatra yāyāt | garhaṇīyānyathā bhavet | asmin loke | pretya ca narakapātaḥ, asmād eva garhānumānāt || 85 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evaṃ sati bhartṛtantratvāt strīṇāṃ tasya ca svatantratvāt yāvatyo jāyās tāḥ sarvās tulyavat karmaṇi viniyuñjīta | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">naivam</span> |_

 

                    	**satyām anyāṃ savarṇāyāṃ dharmakāryaṃ na kārayet |**

**              	savarṇāsu vidhau dharmye jyeṣṭhayā na vinetarām || 1.86 ||**

 

satyāṃ savarṇāyām anyāṃ dharmakāryaṃ na kārayed iti saṃbandhaḥ | savarṇāsv api jyeṣṭhayā vinā netarāṃ kaniṣṭhām | tāsām api yathājyaiṣṭhyam | vidhau agnihotrādikarmaṇi | dharmye ājyāvekṣaṇādau, kratvartha iti yāvat | kanīyasīm api tu savarṇām evaṃ kārayet | asavarṇāsv apy ekāntaratvajyaiṣṭhyādikrameṇa vyākhyeyam || 86 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evaṃ sati jyeṣṭhāyāṃ dhriyamānāyāṃ yadi kaniṣṭhā pramīyeta, tasyā agnihotrādyarthenāgninā dāho na prāpnoti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> |_

 

                    	**dāhayitvāgnihotreṇa striyaṃ vṛttavatīṃ patiḥ |**

**              	āhared vidhivad dārān agnīṃś caivāvilambitaḥ || 1.87 ||**

 

kratvartheṣu hi jyeṣṭhāyā niyamo na puruṣārtheṣu | puruṣārthaś ca dāhaḥ, śarīrasaṃskāratvāt | ataś ca vṛttavatī cet saṃskartavyaiva | vṛttavaty adhikāriṇīti yāvat | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> puruṣārtheṣv api varakartṛkeṣu jyeṣṭhaivāgre saṃskartavyā | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">tathā</span> nāmāstu | ko doṣaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">dvayor</span> yugapanmaraṇe kaniṣṭhāyāḥ saṃskāralopaḥ syāt, pātrāṇām agnīnāṃ ca jyeṣṭhāyām upakṣīṇatvāt | pratipādyatvāc ca na pātrāntarotpattiḥ | agnīnāṃ tv aśakyataiva | ekacitikaraṇe 'pi yathoktāyā dāhāghṛto (?) 'nupapattir eva | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | ayājñikacodyam etat | saṃtāpajatvād agnīnām anekasminn apy āhavanīyasaṃtāpaje tacchabdalābhāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ekasmin saṃtāpena rūḍhe śiṣṭo 'gnir anāhavanīya eva, laukikatvāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kenākhyātam</span> āyuṣmataḥ | apavṛktakarmā hi laukiko bhavati | dāhārthaṃ coddhṛto dāhyānusāreṇaivāpavṛjyeteti viśeṣāgrahaṇāc coddharaṇasya sarvadāhyārthatvam aviruddham | pātracayas tu jyeṣṭhāyā eva, mukhyatvāt | śarīrasaṃskāratve 'pi ca pātrāṇām aprayojyatvaṃ sviṣṭakṛty uttarārdhasyeva | tenaiva ca kanīyasī nindyate | yad vā, agnīnām eva saṃskāratvam | pātracayas tu tatpratipattiḥ | tathā ca pātreṣu dvitīyayaiva dṛśyate: "juhūṃ ghṛtena pūrṇāṃ dakṣiṇe pāṇau sādayati" iti | "agnibhir ādīpayanti" ity agniṣu tṛtīyāpratipādyatvaṃ tu karmāntarānusārāt | "yātv agnibhir dahantī yajñapātraiś ca" iti tṛtīyā arthaprāptatvād anuvādaḥ | yajñāyudhivākyaṃ tv arthavādatvād akiṃcit | tasmād yāvatyaḥ patnyaḥ sarvā evāgnihotrādyarthenāgninā dagdhavyā iti sthitam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecit</span> tv adāham eva patnyā icchanti | yat punaḥ "āhitāgnim agnibhir dahanti" (Śab PMS 4.1.9) iti liṅgasyāvivakṣitatvāt prātipadikārthasaṃbhavāc ca śrutiviruddham | tathā ca kāṭhake śrutau "śavāgnayo vā ete bhavanti, ye patnyāṃ pramītāyāṃ dhāryante" ity upakramya, "tasmāt patnīm agnibhir dahet" iti vispaṣṭo viśeṣavidhiḥ | sūtrakārādivacanāni śrutiviruddhatvād anādṛtyāni | evam arthavādādyunneyā vidhayaḥ pratyākhyeyā ity alaṃ prasaṅgena | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> asavarṇāgnihotreṇa na dagdhavyā | yathāha manuḥ |

                    	evaṃvṛttāṃ savarṇāṃ strīṃ dvijātiḥ pūrvamāriṇīm |

                    	dāhayed agnihotreṇa yajñapātraiś ca dharmavit || iti | (MDh 5.167)

<span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam,</span> āhitāgnitvāviśeṣāt | mānavaṃ tu savarṇāgrahaṇam adhikāropalakṣaṇārtham | yajñaprāptyā hi sarvasya brāhmaṇatvāt sāvarṇyaṃ yataḥ | tathā cāmnāyaḥ: "brāhmaṇo hi jāyate yo yajñāñ jāyate" iti | api ca dāhayed agnihotreṇa savarṇāṃ ceti vākyabhedaḥ syāt | tasmād aviśeṣeṇaiva dāhaḥ | "āhared vidhivad dārān agnīṃś caivāvilambitaḥ" | śīgram | yad vāvilambitaśabdaḥ svahetāv aparābhaṅge vijñeyaḥ | na cet parābhaṅgo gārhasthyād dārān āharet | bhaṅgaś ced āśramāntaraṃ pratipadyeta | avidyamānadārasya ca dārakriyā dṛṣṭārthatvāt | vidhivad ity asyāpy ayam evārthaḥ | na ced yogyā patny asti, anyām udyacched iti | āharaṇādhikāraś ced āharet, dharmaprajāsaṃpanne 'nyānadhikārāt | yat tu "anyatarāpāye dārān kurvīta" iti, tasyāpy ayam evāvasaraḥ samarthaḥ, kṛtādhānasyodvāhāsaṃbhavāt | tathā ca smaranti: "yady udvahet prāg agnyādheyāt" iti | nyāyavidhaś ca yājñikāḥ "savīryatvāt putrārthe na prayojayet" ity āhuḥ | yat punaḥ "āhṛtoḍhāyāṃ bhāryāyāṃ punar ādadhīta" iti, tad āvasathyaviṣayam ity alaṃ prasaṅgena vistareṇa || 87 ||

 

_vṛttavatyā agnihotreṇa dāha ity uktam | kiṃ punas tallakṣaṇam ity ata āha |_

 

                    	**patipriyahite yuktā svācārā saṃyatendriyā |**

**              	seha kīrtim avāpnoti pretya cānuttamāṃ gatim || 1.88 ||**

 

etad vṛttavatyā lakṣaṇam | priyahite yuktā na rāmaṇīyakapradhānā | sādhvācārā kāmādyanabhibhūtā ca yā, saivehāsmaddarśane kīrtiṃ yajñādhikāraṃ prāpnoti prākāśyāt kīrtanād vā | prakaraṇānugrahāc ca kīrtir adhikāraḥ, yajño vā | pretya cānuttamāṃ gatim iti | nāsyā uttamā anyā gatir astīty anuttamā jñānakarmasamuccayagamyā bhartṛsāyujyalakṣaṇā, tāṃ prāpnotīti vyākhyeyam || 88 ||

 

**iti vivāhaprakaraṇam**

** **

**atha varṇajātivivekaprakaraṇam**

*** prakaraṇa division only in later edition

 

_putrārthaṃ "striyaḥ sevyā bhartavyāś ca surakṣitā" _(YDh 1.77)_ ity uktam | savarṇāyāś cotkṛṣṭatvaṃ vivāhaniyamaś ca | asyaiva dārḍhyārthe jātinirūpaṇāyāha |_

 

**              	savarṇebhyaḥ savarṇāsu jāyante hi sajātayaḥ |**

**              	anindyeṣu vivāheṣu putrāḥ saṃtānavardhanāḥ || 1.89 ||**

 

yasmāt savarṇāsv eva savarṇebhyaḥ sajātayaḥ putrā jāyante, yasmāc cānindyabrāhmādivivāhoḍhāsv evaite utpannāḥ putrāḥ saṃtānavṛddhyā pitṛbhya ānṛṇyaṃ kurvanti, yasmāc cānyathā jātināśād viparyayaḥ, tasmāt pūrvoktaṃ sarvaṃ vivāhādi prayatnato 'nuṣṭheyam iti ślokārthaḥ prakaraṇārthaś ca samāsataḥ || 89 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvat savarṇāyā avyabhicāre jātiniyama uktaḥ | vyabhicāre 'py utkṛṣṭavarṇaviṣaya eva śreyān | yataḥ |_

 

**              	viprān mūrdhāvasiktaṃ strī rājño 'mbaṣṭhaṃ viśo 'ṅganā |**

**              	śūdrāṅganā niṣādākhyaṃ sūte pāraśavaṃ tathā || 1.90 ||**

 

viprāc chūdrāyām utpannasyaikasyaiva saṃjñādvayaṃ niṣādaḥ pāraśava iti ca draṣṭavyam | kimarthaṃ tarhi dvijīyā pāraśavasaṃjñā | asavarṇāvyabhicāranindārtham | brāhmaṇabījodbhavo 'pi tatsaṃskārahānāt pārayann eva jīvann eva śava ity arthaḥ | tathā cāha manuḥ |

                    	sa pārayann eva śavas tasmāt pāraśavaḥ smṛtaḥ | iti | (MDh 9.178)

utkṛṣṭavyabhicārastutyarthaṃ tu vipān mūrdhāvasiktam abhiṣekayogyaṃ rājñaḥ kṣatriyasyāpi strī janitavatī | evaṃ sarvatra yojyam || 90 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

**              	māhiṣyograu prajāyete viṭchūdrāṅganayor nṛpāt |**

**              	śūdrāyāṃ karaṇo vaiśyād vinnāsv eṣa vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ || 1.91 ||**

 

vaiśyāyāṃ māhiṣyaḥ śūdrāyām ugraḥ kṣatriyāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca śūdrāpariṇayanapratiṣedhād "vinnasv eṣa vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ" iti viruddham | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">anabhijñaḥ</span> ślokārthasyāyuṣmān | vinnāsu hīnavarṇāsu | vinnāsv eṣa vidhiḥ, yad uta svajātināśaḥ, tasmān na hīnavarṇām udvahed ity asyārthaḥ | ata eva cāvinnasv api saṃjñāntarālābhaḥ | itarathā tatra saṃjñāntarakriyāprasaṅgaḥ | utkṛṣṭavedane tadvyabhicāre vā varṇotkarṣa iti stutiparatayaiva vidhiśabdayojanā || 91 ||

 

_utkṛṣṭavarṇasaṃbandhenotkarṣadarśanāt prātilomye 'pi tathātvāśaṅkā mā bhūd ity ata āha |_

 

                    	**brāhmaṇyāṃ kṣatriyāt sūto vaiśyād vaidehakas tathā |**

**              	śūdrāj jātaś ca caṇḍālaḥ sarvadharmavigarhitaḥ || 1.92 ||**

**              	kṣatriyā māgadhaṃ vaiśyāj chūdrāt kṣattāram eva ca |**

**              	śūdrād āyogavaṃ vaiśyā janayāmāsa vai sutam || 1.93 ||**

 

bhūtārthapratyayayogaḥ prayogānāditvajñāpanārthaḥ| ata eva smṛtyantareṣv ekasyaivārthasyānekasaṃjñādarśane 'pi deśabhedena tathāvidhaprayogasattānumānam | na punaḥ pāribhāṣikatvakalpanā, vedeṣv apy anekavidhasaṃjñopalabdheḥ || 92, 93 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvat prātilomyenotkṛṣṭasaṃbandhe sati caṇḍālatvādiprāptiḥ | ānulomyena punaḥ |_

 

                    	**māhiṣyeṇa karaṇyām tu rathakāraḥ prajāyate |**

**              	asatsantas tu vijñeyāḥ pratilomānulomataḥ || 1.94 ||**

 

kṣatriyeṇa vaiśyāyāṃ jāto māhiṣyaḥ vaiśyena śūdrāyāṃ karaṇī | tasyām karaṇyām māhiṣyād rathakāro jāyate | sa cādhānādhikṛto yasmāt tasmād ānulomyena yugāntareṣūtkarṣaḥ, pradarśanārthatvāt prātilomyenāpakarṣa iti draṣṭavyam | tathā ca spaṣṭīkaroti "asatsantas tu vijñeyāḥ" iti | yathākrameṇāsantaḥ pratilomāḥ santaś cānulomāḥ | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "pratilomāt tu dharmahīnaḥ" iti (GDh 4.25) || 94 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**jātyutkarṣo yuge jñeyaḥ pañcame saptame 'pi vā |**

**              	vyatyaye karmaṇāṃ sāmyaṃ pūrvavac cādharottaram || 1.95 ||**

 

jātyutkarṣo varṇotkarṣaḥ, kṣatriyasyāpi brāhmaṇyaprāptiḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ko 'yaṃ</span> kūśmāṇḍapātaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span> | uktavarṇāntaravihitadharmavyavacchedena brāhmaṇādiśabdapravṛttir ity arthaḥ | pañcame saptame vā parivarte | kṣatriyasya pañcame vaiśyasya saptame brāhmaṇyam | kṣatriyajatve tu tasyāpi pañcama eva | pūrvajātivihitakarmavyavacchedād jātyantaroktakarmaprāptitaś ca tacchabdalābhād anavadyam | kutaḥ prāptivyavacchedāv iti ced, asmād evotkarṣavacanād, amīmāṃsyatvāc c śāstrasya | tad eva draḍhayann āha "vyatyaye karmaṇāṃ sāmyam" | uktotkarṣavyatyaye yugaparivartābhāve prakṛtivihitāny eva karmāṇi bhavantīty arthaḥ | yadi mūrdhāvasiktāṃ brāhmaṇaḥ pariṇayet, tatsutāṃ tatsutāṃ ca, tataḥ pañcame parivarte brāhmaṇakarmādhikāraḥ | yadi mūrdhāvasikta eva tāṃ tatsutāṃ tatsutāṃ ca, tataḥ kṣatriyakarmaiva bhavati | kiṃ ca teṣām apy antaraprabhavānāṃ pūrveṇaiva nyāyenānulomyaprātilomyenauttarādharyaṃ, yojyam iti śeṣaḥ | granthagauravabhayāt tu tatsaṃjñānabhidhānam | sarvathotkṛṣṭavarṇasaṃkare strīṇām utkarṣaḥ | anyathā tu viparyayaḥ | puruṣāṇāṃ tu dvidhāpy apakarṣa iti prapañcanīyaṃ vyākhyātṛbhiḥ | ayaṃ ca mārgaḥ | ānulomyaprātilomye mūrdhavasiktādīnāṃ varṇacatuṣṭaye caturviṃśatir eva varṇābhāsā jāyante | svayaṃ ca ṣaṭ | evaṃ triṃśat | prātilomye 'py evam eva sūtādīnām ity evaṃ ṣaṣṭir varṇābhāsāḥ | tathā ca smaranti |

                    	prātilomyānulomyena varṇais tajjaiś ca varṇataḥ |

                    	ṣaṣṭyevānye prajāyante tatprasūtes tv anantatā || iti || 95 ||

 

**iti varṇajātivivekaprakaraṇam |**

** **

**atha gṛhasthadharmaprakaraṇam |**

** **

_evaṃ tāvad gṛhasthadharmam uktvā, idānīṃ gṛhasthasyānvāhikaṃ vivakṣus tanmūlabhūtāgniniyamāyāha |_

 

                    	**karma smārtaṃ vivāhāgnau kurvīta pratyahaṃ gṛhī |**

**              	dāyakālāhṛte vāpi śrautaṃ vaitānikāgniṣu || 1.96 ||**

 

dṛṣṭāntārthaṃ śrautavacanam | yathaiva śrautam agnyantare kriyamāṇam akarmaiva syād, evaṃ smārtam akṣatahomānnapākādi | vaivāhikaś cāgniś caturthyuttarakālam, tenaiva patnyarthāvāpteḥ, patnīvataś cādhikārāt | dāyavibhāgakālāhṛte vā | apiśabdāt kālāntarāhṛte 'pi | yathā vidyamānapatnīkasya patnyantaramaraṇe | patnyantarotpāde tu vaivāhikavacanād eva siddhiḥ | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "bhāryādir agnir dāyādir vā" iti (GDh 5.7) | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ādhānādhikṛtasyāyaṃ kālavidhiḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">na</span>, vidyamānāgneḥ patnyantarotpādamātreṇādhikāraḥ | tasyā evādhikāra iti cet, na, sahatvāsaṃbhavāt | tadanurodhāt sahatvāpattir iti cet, na, agnimattvāt, tattyāgāsaṃbhavāc ca | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evam api madhyakaṃ dravyaṃ katham ivaikas tyaktuṃ kṣamaḥ syat | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span> | yathaiva rajasvalāyāṃ patnyām ekāky eva yajamānas tyajed vacanāt tadanujñāmātreṇa, evam atrāpīty adoṣaḥ | tathaiva cāsau kārayitavyā, yathātmīyasaṃbandhaṃ na virodhāya kuryāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">yad vā</span> dravyābhāva evāsyāḥ, kutaḥ | asmād evānadhikārāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span> | na hi kratvarthaṃ dravyārjanaṃ, puruṣārtham eva | tac cānadhikāre 'py avyāhatam eva | "bhasadāhavā etāḥ paragṛhāṇām aiśvaryam avarundhate" iti śruteḥ | adhikārānapekṣo hi dravyasaṃbandhaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | sa tu pūrvatarajyeṣṭhāyā eva | tadatikramāc ca pariṇītāpy asvāminy eva, veśyāvat | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> adhivedananimitte saty ūḍhā katham itvāsvāminī syāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | dvividhaṃ hy adhivedanam, dharmaprajāpāyarūpatvāt | tatra dharmāpāye paraiva syāt, na pūrvā | prajāpāye tu kuto dharmādhikāraḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">atrocyate</span> | aho sūkṣamadarśitvam ācāryavataḥ | dharmaprajāpāyāvadhivedanaṃ prayuñjāte | na tv adhivinnāyās tādarthyam āpādayataḥ, pramāṇābhāvād, anyad dhi tādarthyam anyā ca prayuktir yataḥ | tatra "anyatarāpāye dārān kurvīta" iti smṛter arthaḥ | dāratvāc ca taduddeśavihitaṃ dravyādi katham iva na syāt | ato nāsvāmitvam | yat tūktaṃ tadanujñayaiva karaṇam iti | tad apy asat, pūrvāgnivināśāt | kuto vināśa iti cet, kārakatvāpāyāt | patnīyajamānayor hi kārakaikyaṃ vā syāt, bhedo vā | dvidhāpi ca dravyāntaropādānād vināśaḥ, agnīṣomavat | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ayaṃ doṣaḥ kārakānupraveśe sati syāt | vayaṃ tv anupraveśam eva vārayāmaḥ | apāyas tu siddhe kārakatva iti vaiṣamyam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span> | na śakyaḥ svecchāmātreṇānupraveśaḥ phalotsāhāviśeṣāt prasajyamāno vārayitum | yadi hi kartṛtvapūrvo 'dhikāraḥ syāt, tatas tadanupapattyā vāryetāpi | adhikārapūrvake tu kartṛtve durnivāro 'nupraveśaḥ | tataś ca pūrvakārakavināśāt tadāhitāgnivināśaḥ | tataś ca siddho nimittāntarābhāvād vivāha eva punar agnyutpādaḥ | tathā ca nyāyamūlaiva smṛtiḥ: "āhṛtoḍhāyāṃ punar ādadhīta" ity alam atyabhidhānena | ataś cāpiśabdaḥ kālāntarārthaḥ | yathoktam asmābhiḥ || 96 ||

 

_ayaṃ cānyas taddharmaḥ |_

 

                    	**śarīracintāṃ nirvartya kṛtaśaucavidhir dvijaḥ |**

**              	prātaḥ saṃdhyām upāsīta dantadhāvanapūrvikām || 1.97 ||**

 

dantadhāvanavidhyartha evāyaṃ ślokaḥ, anyasya brahmacāryuktasyaivānuvādāt, tatprakaraṇoktasyāniṣiddhasya sarvāśramasādhāraṇyāt | ślokākṣarāṇy ṛjvarthāny eva | yat tu "rajasvalo jaṭilaḥ paṅkadanta uṣṇīṣī śikhī vadati satyam eva" iti (cf. ĀpDh 1.7.11), tad amāvāsyādiviṣayam, tatraiva satyavacananiyamāt | tathā ca śrutiḥ: "paṅkadanto yajati" iti | evaṃ vyāsaḥ |

                    	dantakāṣṭham amāvāsyāṃ maithunaṃ ca caturdaśīm |

                    	hanti saptakulaṃ tāta tailagrahaṇam aṣṭamīm || iti |

dvitīyā cātra saptamyarthe draṣṭavyā || 97 ||

 

_kiṃ cānyat |_

 

                    	**hutvāgnīn sūryadevatyāñ japen mantrān samāhitaḥ |**

**              	vedārthān adhigaccheta śāstrāṇi vividhāni ca || 1.98 ||**

 

japakarmaṇo dīrghakālatvād dhomasya kālabādho mā bhūd ity ārambhaḥ | vedārthān mantrabrāhmaṇavyākhyānāni | śāstrāṇi vyākaraṇādīni | caśabdo vidyāntarārthaḥ | anena cānirvṛttākhiladharmajñānasyāpi gārhasthyādhikāra iti jñāpitaṃ bhavati | yad vā, jñātavedaśāstrasyaivāyaṃ dhāraṇārtho vidhiḥ | tathā ca vyāsaḥ: "jñātavedārthatatvena" iti || 98 ||

 

_idaṃ cānyat |_

 

                    	**upeyād īśvaraṃ caiva yogakṣemārthasiddhaye |**

**              	snātvā devān pitṝṃś caiva tarpayed arcayet tathā || 1.99 ||**

 

yogo 'labdhalābhaḥ | labdhaparipālanaṃ tu kṣemaḥ | tadartham īśvaram upeyād iti | anenaitad darśayati: na paryāptadhanasyaiva karmapravṛttiḥ | kiṃ tarhi pravṛttakarmaṇo 'py anvahaṃ dravyārjanam iti | ata eva ca sarvādāv (?) agnyāharaṇopadeśaḥ | yogādyarthavacanāc cādravyasyaivāyaṃ vidhir jñeyaḥ | kiṃ ca | snātvā devān pitṝṃś ca tarpayed udakena | arcayet puṣpādyupahāraiḥ | caśabdād ṛṣīṃś ca | snātvaiveti sukhārthasyāpy ayam eva kāla ity evakārārthaḥ | tatheti dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ pitṛtīrthena bhūmāv asau tṛpyatv ity evamādiprakārārthaḥ || 99 ||

 

_kiṃ cānyat |_

 

                    	**vedātharvapurāṇāni setihāsāni śaktitaḥ |**

**              	japayajñārthasiddhyarthaṃ vidyāṃ cādhyātmikīṃ japet || 1.100 ||**

 

vedādyarcanānantaryapradarśanārthaṃ pūrvam evāyaṃ japayajña uktaḥ | bhedenātharvagrahaṇaṃ chandaḥsamādhānārthaṃ vedatve 'pi | kiṃ ca vidyāṃ cādhyātmikīṃ brahmavidyām upaniṣallakṣaṇām japet | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "upaniṣado vedāntā iti pāpakṣapaṇāya" ity āha (cf. GDh 19.12) | ṛjv anyat || 100 ||

 

_idānīṃ gṛhasthasyāsādhāraṇān mahāyajñān āha |_

 

**              	balikarmasvadhāhomasvādhyāyātithisatkriyāḥ |**

**              	bhūtapitramarabrahmamanuṣyāṇāṃ mahāmakhāḥ || 1.101 ||**

 

makho yajñaḥ | balikarmādayo bhūtādīnāṃ krameṇa pañca mahāyajñāḥ | kāryā iti śeṣaḥ | tathā cāmnāyaḥ: "pañcamahāyajñās tany eva mahāsatrāṇi bhūtayajño manuṣyayajñaḥ pitṛyajño devayajño brahmayajñaḥ" iti (cf. BDh 2.11.1) | "ahar ahar bhūtebhyo baliṃ haret" ityādipratyakṣaśrutyuktānām api smārtatvaprasiddhyartho 'sya vidhiḥ, "karma smārtaṃ vivāhāgnāu" iti vacanāt (YDh 1.96) || 101 ||

 

_agnyanapekṣatvāt tu brahmayajñaḥ kāmaṃ pravarteta | bhūtapitṛyajñayor apy agnyanapekṣatvāt pravṛttiprāptāv āha |_

 

                    	**devebhyaś ca hutād annāc cheṣād bhūtabaliṃ haret |**

**              	annaṃ bhūmau śvacaṇḍālavayobhyaś caiva nikṣipet || 1.102 ||**

 

yasmād devebhyo hutaśeṣād balikarma tadantargataś ca pitṛyajñaḥ svadhākāropadeśāt | tasmād agnyabhāve tayor apravṛttiḥ | sarvaṃ caitad gṛhyād viśeṣato 'vagantavyam | annaṃ cāsminn eva kāle śvacaṇḍālādibhyo bahir bhūmau nikṣipet | kramavidhānārthaś cakāraḥ | evakāro 'tithidānād api pūrvakaraṇād vicikitsānivṛttyarthaḥ | vaiśvadevārthapākasaṃbandhāc cānagnikasyāpravṛttiḥ | kecit tu tasmād eva pātrasthād annād devebhyo hutvā śeṣāc ca balikarma kṛtvā yacchiṣṭam annaṃ tad bahir nikṣipanti | tat tu balikarmaṇi pātraprakṣālanopadeśād anādṛtyam | atrāpi ca punarannavacanam anyopādānārtham || 102 ||

 

_evaṃ vāyasādidānāntaṃ karma kṛtvā tataḥ |_

 

**              	annaṃ pitṛmanuṣyebhyo deyam apy anvahaṃ jalam |**

**              	svādhyāyaṃ cānvahaṃ kuryān na paced annam ātmanaḥ || 1.103 ||**

 

"annaṃ pitṛmanuṣyebhyo deyam" ity anena hantakārasyobhayārthasya vidhānam | svadhākārātithisatkārayor mahāyajñatvena pūrvatraiva vihitatvād dhantakārākhyam annadānāntaram eva pitṛmanuṣyārthaṃ vidhīyate | tathā ca pāraskaraḥ: "uddhṛtyānnaṃ brāhmaṇāyāvanejya dadyāt" (PārG 2.9.11) ity ubhayārthatvam evāvanejyeti liṅgād darśayati | kiṃ ca | apy anvahaṃ dadyāj jalaṃ, pitṛmanuṣyayajñanirvṛttyartham | na tu hāpayed iti śeṣaḥ | tathā cāmnāyaḥ: "ahar ahar dadyād odapātrāt" ityādi | yad vā | apiśabdaḥ samuccayārthaḥ | jalam apy anvahaṃ dadyāt | kiṃ ca svādhyāyaṃ ca brahmayajñam anvahaṃ kuryāt | caśabdād bhūtayajñādīṃś ceti yojyam | brahmayajñādipunaḥśrutiś cānvahaṃ kuryād ity evamartham | tena cābhyarhitatvāt karmāntarāśaktāv apy eṣām anuṣṭhānam | kiṃ ca | na cātmārtham annaṃ paced ity anena vaiśvadevārthataiva pākasyeti jñāpyate | tataś ca smārtatvād aupāsana eva bhavati | tathā ca manuḥ: "paktiṃ cānvāhikīṃ gṛhī" (MDh 3.67) ity atraiva paktim āha | āmnāyaś ca: "sa yatra surān yajate tena manuṣyā bhuñjate" iti paktyarthatāṃ darśayati | pratiṣedhamātraṃ tv aprakṛtam eva syāt | tataś cānagnikasyātmārtham api pacato na doṣa iti sthitam || 103 ||

 

_evaṃ pitṛmanuṣyebhyo hantakāraṃ nirvartya, tataḥ |_

 

                    	**bālasvavāsinīvṛddhagarbhiṇyāturakanyakāḥ |**

**              	saṃbhojyātithibhṛtyāṃś ca dampatyoḥ śeṣabhojanam || 1.104 ||**

 

saṃśabdo yathārhabhojanārthaḥ | yathāha pāraskaraḥ: "bālajyeṣṭhā gṛhyā yathārham aśnīyuḥ" iti (PārG 2.9.13) | ūḍhā duhitaraḥ svavāsinyaḥ | tadvacanād eva daṇḍāpūpavad bālavacanād vā kanyakāprāptau punarvacanaṃ svavāsinīnāṃ tatrāniyamajñāpanārtham | garbhiṇīvacanaṃ patnyartham | āturagrahaṇaṃ tu svayam apy āturaḥ pūrvam aśnīyād ity evamartham | atithivacanaṃ dṛṣṭārtham | caśabdo 'bhyāgatārthaḥ | evaṃ sarvān bhojayitvā dampatyoḥ paścāc cheṣabhojanam | yad vā | sarvopayoge punaḥpākaprayuktinivṛttyartham | tathā ca smaraṇam: "sarvopabhoge na punaḥpākaḥ" iti | anyonyaṃ tu dampatyoḥ kramāniyamaḥ | patnī vā paścāt | tathā ca pāraskaraḥ: "paścād gṛhapatiḥ patnī ca | pūrvo vā gṛhapatiḥ" (PārG 2.9.14) iti || 104 ||

 

_idānīṃ bhojanaprāptau niyamāyāha |_

 

                    	**apośānenopariṣṭhād adhastād aśnatā tathā |**

**              	anagnam amṛtaṃ caiva kāryam annaṃ dvijanmanā || 1.105 ||**

 

prāptasyaivāpośānasya tathāśabdaḥ prakārārthaḥ bhojanāṅgam ācamanāntaraṃ vidadhāti | ata eva cānagnavacanena śrutim anukaroti: "tasyo me kim annaṃ kiṃ vāsaḥ" iti prakṛtya "tadvidvāṃsaḥ śrotriyā aśiṣyanta ācāmanti | aśitvā cācāmanti | amṛtam eva tad annam anagnaṃ kurvanto manyante | tasmād evaṃvid aśiṣyann ācāmed aśitvā cācāmet" (cf. BāU 6.1.14) ity ubhayatrācamanam eva darśayati | ācamanamātrāṅgatayā ca guṇavidhānāt sāṅgam eva tat syāt | laukikās tu nityatvāt pradhānamātrakriyāta eva kṛtitvaṃ manyamānāḥ sakṛd abbhakṣaṇamātraṃ kurvantīty avaseyam || 105 ||

 

_atithisatkāra uktaḥ | kaḥ punar atithitve 'dhikriyata ity ata āha |_

 

                    	**atithitve 'pi varṇebhyo deyaṃ śaktyānupūrvaśaḥ |**

**              	apraṇōdyo 'tithiḥ sāyam api vāgbhūtṛṇodakaiḥ || 1.106 ||**

 

ātithyanimitte yad dānaṃ, tad varṇebhya eva nāpaśadebhya ity arthaḥ | tatrāpi varṇato guṇataś cānupūrvyeṇeti vyākhyeyam | prasaṅgāt tu sāyaṃkālīnopadeśaḥ || 106 ||

 

_hantakāradānānantaram eva ca |_

 

                    	**satkṛtya bhikṣave bhikṣā dātavyā suvratāya ca |**

**              	bhojayec cāgatān kāle sakhisaṃbandhibāndhavān || 1.107 ||**

 

bhikṣuśabdo 'yaṃ bhikṣukāśramivacanaḥ suvrataśabdas tu niścitavratatvāt paramahaṃsābhiprāyaḥ | tasya caikabhaikṣatvād bhedenopanyāsaḥ | caśabdaś cādarātiśayadyotanārthaḥ, anyabhikṣukagrahaṇārtho vā syāt | ānṛśaṃsyārthaṃ sakhyādīṃś ca svabhojanakālāgatān bhojayet, satkṛtyaiva | caśabdād akāle 'pi tadarthaḥ pākārambhaḥ | samānagrāme ca kālāgatānām eveti vyavasthā || 107 ||

 

_evaṃ sakhyādibhyo nityam eva satkāravad bhojanaṃ deyam | śrotriyāgamane punaḥ |_

 

                    	**mahokṣaṃ vā mahājaṃ vā śrotriyāyopakalpayet |**

**              	satkriyā sevanaṃ svādu bhojanaṃ sūnṛtaṃ vacaḥ || 1.108 ||**

 

kāryam iti śeṣaḥ | upakalpanavacanāt tadanujñāpekṣo mahokṣādivadhaḥ | satkriyām atithisaparyām | sevanam upāsanam | tac ca kuryāt | svādu ca mṛṣṭaṃ bhojanaṃ dadyāt | sūnṛtaṃ ca priyaṃ brūyād iti | etac cātithiviśeṣāpekṣayā vyastasamastatvena yojyam || 108 ||

 

_asaṃbandhaśrotriyāgamana uktam | saṃbandhe tu |_

 

                    	**pratisaṃvatsaraṃ tv arghyāḥ snātakācāryapārthivāḥ |**

**              	priyo vivāhyaś ca tathā yajñaṃ praty ṛtvijaḥ punaḥ || 1.109 ||**

 

snātakācāryaśabdau saṃbandhivacanau, anyathātiprasaṅgāt | yo hi yasyopanetā sa tasyācāryaḥ | yaś ca tataḥ samāvṛttaḥ sa tasya snātakaḥ | pārthivo 'pi svadeśabhokteti na kṣatriyaḥ | pratiśabdo vīpsārthaḥ | tuśabdo 'vadhāraṇārthaḥ | arghyā eva madhuparkādibhiḥ | "priyo vivāhyaś ca" | tathā tattulyaguṇa ity arthaḥ | ṛtvijas tu yajñam eva praty arghyāḥ prāg api ca saṃvatsarāt | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "yajñavivāhayor arvāk" iti (GDh 5.29) | yajñaśabdaś ca somayāge, "yady asakṛt saṃvatsarasya somena yajeta" iti vacanāt || 109 ||

 

_atithiśrotriyayoḥ satkāra uktaḥ | adhunā tallakṣaṇam āha |_

 

                    	**adhvanīno 'tithir jñeyaḥ śrotriyo vedapāragaḥ |**

**              	mānyāv etau gṛhasthasya brahmalokam abhīpsataḥ || 1.110 ||**

 

varṇānupūrvyeṇātithitvaṃ guṇānusārād uktam | tatraivāyaṃ viśeṣo 'dhvanīna iti | tathā ca nigamaḥ |

                    	anityaṃ hi sthito yasmāt tasmād atithir ucyate | iti | (MDh 3.102)

śrotriyopanyāsaḥ sārthatvārthaḥ | ṛjv anyat || 110 ||

 

_evaṃ ca saty atithitvena mṛṣṭānnāsvādanalagno 'dhvanīna eva nityaṃ mā bhūd iti vivakṣayāha |_

 

**              	parapākarucir na syād anindyāmantraṇād ṛte |**

**              	vākpāṇipādacāpalyaṃ varjayec cātibhojanam || 1.111 ||**

 

anindyair āmantryamāṇo 'pi cātibhojanaṃ varjayet | ekāntatas tadanurodhād aprahṛṣyan gacched ity arthaḥ | ataś cādhvany api svapākāśaktāv evātithitvenopatiṣṭhet | naikagrāme tv āpady apy evaṃ syād iti || 111 ||

 

_yaḥ punaḥ svavidhyanurodhenātithitvaṃ pratipannaḥ, tathāvidham |_

 

                    	**atithiṃ śrotriyaṃ tṛptam ā sīmāntād anuvrajet |**

**              	ahaḥśeṣaṃ samāsīta śiṣṭair iṣṭaiś ca bandhubhiḥ || 1.112 ||**

 

saheti śeṣaḥ | atithiṃ śrotiryam iti sāmānādhikaraṇyam | na ca śabdakalpanā | anyasyāpy atither yathārhaṃ pūjā kalpanīyā | tathā ca pāraskaraḥ: "yathārhaṃ bhikṣukān atithīṃś ca saṃbhajeran" iti (PārG 2.9.12) | samāsīteti vacanād āgnyuddharaṇakālād āsanam || 112 ||

 

_uddhṛtāgnis tu |_

 

**              	upāsya paścimāṃ saṃdhyāṃ hutvāgnīṃs tān upāsya ca |**

**              	bhṛtyaiḥ parivṛto bhuktvā nātitṛptyātha saṃviśet || 1.113 ||**

 

dvitīyabhojanakālārthaḥ ślokaḥ | pūrvabhojanavidhikārtsnye prāpte bhṛtyaiḥ sahaivāśnīyād, na paurvāparyeṇety arthaḥ | ataś ca nāntarā bhojanam | tathācāmnyāyaḥ: "tasmād āhuḥ sāyaṃprātar āśyeva syāt" ity antrāniṣedhāyaivāha || 113 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evam anyaparatvād vākyasyātitṛptyā bhojane na doṣaḥ syāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> evam | kiṃ tu |_

 

**              	dharmam arthaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca yathāśakti na hāpayet |**

**              	brāhme muhūrta utthāya cintayed ātmano hitam || 1.114 ||**

 

<span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | śāstrato naiṣa niṣedhaḥ | kiṃ tu arthakāmāv apy ahāpanīyāv eva, na ced dharmavirodhinau | tadatikrame 'pi śāstrabādha eva | dharmo 'py ekāntatas tadviruddho na dharmatām upeyāt | tathā ca manuḥ: "parityajed arthakāmau" iti (MDh 4.176) | yad vā prakaraṇāt saṃveśanāṅgakāmānujñāpanārtham evaitat | kiṃ ca | brāhme muhūrte paścime yāma utthāyātmano hitaṃ paramātmānaṃ cintayet, tasyaiva paramārthato hitatvāt, kālāntarānupadeśāc ca, asya ca kālasya yogyatvāt | utthānavacanaṃ cārthavyāpāranivṛttyā manaḥsamādhānārtham | ata eva ca tatsamākhyayā muhūrtopadeśaḥ | manuvacanāt tv avirodhenārthādicintāpi "dharmārthāv anucintayet" iti (MDh 492) | kasmāt punaḥ prādhānyena paramātmacintā na dharmārthayoḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca tāv eva cintyau prādhānyena, apavargasyāpi kāraṇabhūtatvāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span> | uktaṃ hi paramārthato hitatvāt samākhyānopadeśāc ceti || 114 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

**              	vidyākarmavayobandhuvittair mānyā yathākramam |**

**              	etaiḥ prabhūtaiḥ śūdro 'pi vārdhakye mānam arhati || 1.115 ||**

 

vidyeti brahmavidyaivocyate | anyathā hi tadrahitasya karmānadhikārāt karmaṇo 'dhikatvaṃ niryuktikam iva syāt | tathā ca gautamo vidyāṃ ca vayaso nikṛṣṭām abhidhāya "śrutaṃ tu sarvebhyo garīyas tanmūlatvād dharmasya" iti bhedam evāha (GDh 6.21–22) | kathaṃ tarhi vayaso 'dhikatvam | caturthāśramavacanaḥ sa vayaḥśabdaḥ, na vārdhakyavacanaḥ | tathā hi, daśamīsthasya patho dānena mānyatvam uktvā snātakam eva sarvebhyo mānyatvenāha | atra tu vayaḥśabdo vārdhakya eva | tasyāpi mānyatvaṃ "yo vā śataṃ varṣāṇi jīvati sa ihaivāmṛtatvaṃ prāpnoti" ity āmnāyāt (ŚB 10.2.6.8) | yat punar vasiṣṭhena "vidyāvittavayaḥsaṃbandhāḥ karma ca mānyaṃ pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ balīyaḥ" iti vayaso 'pi mānyam uktam (VaDh 13.56–57) | tad brāhmaṇaśrutalakṣaṇavittābhiprāyaṃ,

                    	pṛthivīm api caivemāṃ kṛtsnām eko 'pi so 'rhati | (MDh 1.105)

iti bāhyavittakāraṇatvāt, "śrutaṃ tu sarvebhyo garīyaḥ" iti gautamānusārāc ca (GDh 6.21) | tad api nanu karmaṇo nātiriktam | atiriktaṃ hi, brāhmaṇagatasyaiva śrutasya taddhetutvāt, "prabrūyad itarebhyaś ca" (MDh 10.2) iti ca sarvopakārakatvāt | karma tv abrāhmaṇāśritam eva, āmnāyānusārāt "tasmād brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyam adhastād upāste rājasūye" iti (BāU 1.4.11) | saṃbandho 'pi ca brāhma eva vasiṣṭhokto na yaunaḥ, svāmitvasaṃbandhasyartvijāṃ kṣatryāder api mānyatvāt | ācāryābhiprāyas tu laukikam eva vittaṃ dvividho 'pi ca bandhur iti | evaṃ manuḥ: "vittaṃ bandhuḥ" ityādi (MDh 2.136) | kim etāni brāhmaṇasthāny eva mānakāraṇāni | nety ucyate | "etaiḥ prabhūtaiḥ śūdro 'pi vārdhakye mānam arhati" iti, yadi bhavanti | yatra daivān na bhavanti, tatra kiṃ kurmaḥ | kṣatriyavaiśyayos tv avyāhataṃ mānyatvam ity abhiprāyaḥ | tathā ca manuḥ: "pañcānāṃ triṣu varṇeṣu" iti (MDh 2.137) | yad vā etaiḥ prabhūtair adhikataraṃ mānyatvam iti yojyam | kiṃ ca, śūdro 'pi vārdhakye mānam arhatīty eṣā dik || 115 ||

 

**              	vṛddhabhārinṛpasnātastrīrogivaracakriṇām |**

**              	panthā deyo nṛpas teṣāṃ mānyaḥ snātaś ca bhūpateḥ || 1.116 ||**

 

vṛddhādisamavāye 'lpe ca pathy anevaṃlakṣaṇair mārgād apasartavyam | teṣāṃ tv anyonyaṃ smṛtyantarāt kramāvagatiḥ | yathāha vasiṣṭhaḥ: "sthavirabālāturabhārikastrīcakrīvatāṃ samāgame parasmai parasmai panthā deyaḥ" iti (VaDh 13.58) | nṛpas teṣāṃ mānya iti kartari ṣaṣṭhī | tais tu vṛddhādibhiḥ sarvair eva rājā mānyaḥ | nṛpeṇapi snātako brāhmaṇaḥ | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "rājñā tu śrotriyāya" iti (GDh 6.25) | "sarvaiś ca vadhvā uhyamānāyāḥ" (VaDh 13.60) iti vasiṣṭhavacanād varas tato 'pi mānyataraḥ | striyaṃ tu garbhiṇīm evecchanti | anugrāhyagautamavacanād (cf. GDh 6.24), atra ca rogisaṃnidhānāt tat punar vicāraṇīyam | cakri cakravad yānam | ṛjv anyat | yatra tu śrotriyo 'pi sarvair mānyaḥ, tatra kim iva brahmavido vaktavyam iti prakṛtayojanā | prakaraṇayojanaṃ caitat | ślokas tv avagataviṣaya eva, anyatrāpy evam eva draṣṭavyam || 116 ||

 

_kasmāt punar brāhmaṇa eva snātakaḥ parigṛhyate | kṣatriyavaiśyayor yāgādayo 'pi santy eva | satyam |_

 

**              	ijyādhyayanadānāni vaiśyasya katriyasya ca |**

**              	pratigraho 'dhiko vipre yājanādhyāpane tathā || 1.117 ||**

 

vṛttyarthāny apy etāni mānakāraṇaṃ bhavanty eva | yad vā, uktaṃ śaktito dharmādyahāpanam | tatrejyādayaḥ sarveṣāṃ dharmasādhanam | pratigrahādayaś ca yathādhikāram arthasādhanam | kāmasya tūktam evety evaṃ yojanā || 117 ||

 

**              	pradhānaṃ kṣatriye karma prajānāṃ paripālanam |**

**              	kusīdakṛṣivāṇijyaṃ pāśupālyaṃ viśaḥ smṛtam || 1.118 ||**

 

pūrvatra tathāśabdasyārthāntarāpekṣatvāt, kṣatriyakarmaṇi prādhānyavacanāt, "kusīdakṛṣivāṇijyam" iti ca samāsakaraṇāt, "pāśupālyaṃ viśaḥ smṛtam" iti ca smṛtyantarārthopakṣepāt, kusīdādīnām anukalpatayā sādhāraṇatvam | vaiśyasya tu svayaṃkartṛkāṇy apy etāni svakalpa eva, smṛtyantarāt || 118 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvad dvijātīnām uktam | ekajāteḥ punaḥ |_

 

**              	śūdrasya dvijaśuśrūṣā tayājīvan vaṇig bhavet |**

**              	śilpair vā vividhair jīved dvijātihitam ācaran || 1.119 ||**

 

śūdrasya dvijaśuśrūṣaiva dharmasādhanaṃ, na yāgādayaḥ, adhyayanavidhyabhāvāt | arthasādhanam api saiva | kiṃ tu tayā yadā na jīvet, tadā vāṇijyaṃ krītavikrītaṃ kuryāt | nānāprakārair vā śilpair jīvet | sarvathā tu dvijātihitam ācaret | tad eva hi tasya dharmasādhanaṃ yataḥ || 119 ||

 

_ayaṃ cānyaḥ śūdrasyaiva dharmaḥ |_

 

**              	bhāryāratiḥ śucir bhṛtyabhartā śrāddhakriyārataḥ |**

**              	namaskāreṇa mantreṇa pañca yajñān na hāpayet || 1.120 ||**

 

pāradāryāprasakteḥ svadāra eva yathākāmī syāt | śuciḥ snānādyanuṣṭhātā | bhṛtyamātrabhartā | śrāddhakarma cāmantrakaṃ yathākālaṃ kuryād, anvahaṃ pañca mahāyajñān | iyāṃs tu viśeṣaḥ: namaskāramātram eva prayuñjīta, na devatābhidhānāni | mantratayā ca pratiṣedhād devatoddeśena tyāgaḥ kartavya eva | śrāddhe tu devatāpadāny api mantramātrāniṣedhāt pravartante || 120 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvad dvijātīnāṃ śūdrasya ca dharmasādhanam uktam | idaṃ punaḥ |_

 

                    	**ahiṃsā satyam asteyaṃ śaucam indriyasaṃyamaḥ |**

**              	damaḥ kṣamārjavaṃ dānaṃ sarveṣāṃ dharmasādhanam || 1.121 ||**

 

caturṇām api varṇānām ity arthaḥ | tathā coktam: "ahiṃsā satyam asteyam" iti | yad vā pratilomārthaḥ sarvaśabdaḥ | pūrveṣāṃ tu daṇḍāpūpikayaiva syāt | evaṃ ca sati dānavacanam apy apunaruktaṃ syāt | śūdramātraparatve tu sarvaśabdānupapattiḥ | ubhayārthatve 'virodhaḥ || 121 ||

 

_idaṃ cānyad yathāyogaṃ sarvasādhāraṇam uttarādhikārārtham āha |_

 

**              	vayobuddhyarthavāgveṣaśrutābhijanakarmaṇām |**

**              	ācaret sadṛśīṃ vṛttim ajihmām aśaṭhāṃ tathā || 1.122 ||**

 

ajihmām akuṭilām | aśaṭhāṃ parānupadravakāriṇīm || 122 ||

 

_tad evādhunā sādṛśyaṃ prapañcayitum āha |_

 

                    	**traivārṣikādhikānno yaḥ sa somaṃ hi pibed dvijaḥ |**

**              	prāksaumikāḥ kriyāḥ kuryād yasyānnaṃ vārṣikaṃ bhavet || 1.123 ||**

 

kāmyakarmārthaḥ ślokaḥ, anyatra śrutivirodhāt || 123 ||

 

_akāmyaviṣaye punaḥ |_

 

                    	**pratisaṃvatsaraṃ somaḥ paśuḥ pratyayanaṃ tathā |**

**              	kartavyāgrayaṇeṣṭiś ca cāturmāsyāni caiva hi || 1.124 ||**

 

kāmyanityavivekārthaḥ ślokaḥ | cādayo nipātāḥ śrautavidhānadyotanārthāḥ | tathāśabdo 'pi śrutyuktaparāmarśārthaḥ | nityatvāc caiṣāṃ yathāsaṃbhavaṃ kriyā || 124 ||

 

_yasya tv ātyantikyevāśaktiḥ, tadā,_

 

                    	**eṣām asaṃbhave kuryad iṣṭiṃ vaiśvānarīṃ dvijaḥ |**

**              	hīnakalpaṃ na kurvīta sati dravye phalapradam || 1.125 ||**

 

kāmyaṃ karma hīnopakaraṇaṃ na kuryāt, yasmāt saty eva dravye tat phalapradaṃ, sarvāṅgopasaṃhāraniyamāt | somādyabhāve ceṣṭivacanaṃ niyogataḥ kartavyatākhyāpanārtham || 125 ||

 

_evaṃ ca sati naiyamikatvāt kutaścid dravyāharaṇaprasaktāv āha |_

 

**              	caṇḍālo jāyate yajñakaraṇāc chūdrabhikṣitā |**

**              	yajñārthaṃ labdham adadad bhāsaḥ kāko 'pi jāyate || 1.126 ||**

 

<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca puruṣārthaṃ dravyaṃ na kratvartham | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | puruṣa eva yat kratunimittam ārjayati, tat kratvartham ity adoṣaḥ | vananīyavananārtho vāyam upadeśaḥ | puruṣārthatve 'pi śūdrabhikṣaṇanindā | śūdrabhiṣukasya kratavo 'pi pratyavāyāya, kim utānyat | tādarthyavacanam uktaviṣayam evety adoṣaḥ | paryavasite 'pi kratau sadasyebhya eva dadyād, na svayam upayuñjītety arthaḥ || 126 ||

 

_idānīm adhikṛtānām eva svārthavṛttiniyamāyāha |_

 

                    	**kusūlakumbhīdhānyo vā traihiko 'śvastano 'pi vā |**

**              	jīved vāpi siloñchena śreyān eṣāṃ paraḥ paraḥ || 1.127 ||**

 

ādyo 'piśabdo 'yācitārthaḥ | dvitīyas tu siloñchayor bhedakathanārthaḥ | kusūlaṃ koṣṭhako viṃśatidroṇamānam | tadardhaṃ kumbhī,

                    	daśa droṇāḥ smṛtā kumbhī kusūlo dviguṇas tataḥ |

ity abhiyuktopadeśāt | traihiko dinatrayopayogidhānyaḥ | aśvastanaḥ sadyaḥprakṣālakaḥ | silaḥ saśūkoccayanam | kaṇoccayanam uñchaḥ |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca somādyanuṣṭhānavirodhāc chrutiviruddheyaṃ smṛtiḥ | na ca vṛttyapekṣo 'dhikāraḥ | adravyatvasyādhikārāpratibandhakatvāt |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | jīved iti vacanāj jīvanārtho vṛttisaṃkocaḥ | ṛtvarthaṃ pratigrahādibhir apy aniṣiddham evārjanam ity avirodhaḥ | yad vā etan naiṣṭhikādivad eva draṣṭavyam | na hi rāgitayaiva pravṛttadravyārjanān utsṛjya vṛttisaṃkocasmṛtibādhenāgnihotrādividhayaḥ pravartante | yataḥ pravṛttau vā ṛtvarthataiva dravyārjanasya syāt | tathā ca sarvatantraparilopaḥ | tasmāt pratigrahādivṛttiviṣayā evāgnihotrādividhaya ity avirodhaḥ | nipuṇatas tv etad vanasthāśramanirūpaṇe vakṣyāmaḥ | pravṛttāśramāntarasya caitā vṛttayaḥ | tathā ca śaṅkhaḥ: "ata ūrdhvaṃ putrān utpādya" ity upakramya "kratuprasthānaliṅgo vṛttiviśeṣānukramaḥ śreyān yāyāvarāṇāṃ vārtām upāsya vanam āśrayet" ity āha | ato 'py avirodhaḥ || 127 ||

 

**iti gṛhasthadharmaprakaraṇam**

** **

**atha snātakadharmaprakaraṇam**

 

_evaṃ tāvad uttarottarajyāyastvena vṛttisaṃyamo 'bhihito jñānātiśayenocchinnarāgāṇām | ye tu rāgiṇo bahutaradravyakāmāḥ pūrvoktapratigrahādibhir aniyataṃ dravyam ārjayituṃ pravṛttāḥ, tān praty āha |_

 

                    	**na svādhyāyavirodhyartham īheta na yatas tataḥ |**

**              	na viruddhaprasaṅgena saṃtoṣī ca bhavet sadā || 1.128 ||**

 

nārdhakṛtaṃ svādhyāyam utsṛjyārthārtham īśvaram upeyāt | na ca yatas tataḥ śūdrād apraśastād vārtham īheta | na ca dharmārthayor yugapatprasaṅge dharmavirodhinam arthaṃ parigṛhṇīyāt | tathā ca āpastambena brahmahatyāprāyaścittaṃ viruddhaprasaṅge 'bhyadhāyi: "dharmārthasaṃnipāte 'rthagrāhiṇa etad eva" iti (ĀpDh 1.24.23) | sarvathā saṃtoṣy eva sadā bhaved, na lubdhaḥ syād ity upasaṃhāraḥ kāmātmatāniṣedhārthaḥ || 128 ||

 

_nisargajananānusāriṇo yājanādyāḥ siloñchāntāḥ prathame kalpe tv ete | naite 'nukalpāḥ | ayaṃ tu sarveṣām āpatkalpaḥ |_

** **

**              	rājāntevāsiyājyebhyaḥ sīdann icched dhanaṃ kṣudhā |**

 

sīdann iti vacanād āpatkalpatvam | rājā kṣatriyaḥ, śāstravartī ca rājyakartā | antevāsī śiṣyaḥ | ṛjv anyat ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**ḍambhihaitukapāṣaṇḍibakavṛttīṃś ca nārcayet || 1.129 ||**

 

caśabdo vikarmasthādyarthaḥ | yathāha manuḥ: "pāṣaṇḍino vikarmasthān" iti (MDh 4.30) | etāṃś ca sarvathā nārcayet | tathā ca manuḥ: "vāṅmātreṇāpi nārcayet" iti (MDh 4.30) | ḍambhī dharmavyājajīvī | haitukāḥ kutārkikāḥ | pāṣaṇḍinaḥ kṣapaṇakādayaḥ | bakavṛttir atisaṃdhāyakaḥ, svārthaniṣṭhaś ca | yathāha manuḥ: "adhodṛṣṭir naikṛtikaḥ" ityādi (MDh 4.196) || 129 ||

 

_adhunānyān apy asyaiva vistareṇa yamaniyamān āha |_

 

                    	**śuklāmbaradharo nīcakeśaśmaśrunakhaḥ śuciḥ |**

**              	na bhāryādarśane 'śnīyān naikavāsā na saṃsthitaḥ || 1.130 ||**

 

yat tu "aniyatakeśaveṣā" iti, tad āśritaśūdraviṣayaṃ draṣṭavyam | na ca bhāryādarśane 'śnīyāt, tathā ca kuryād yathā bhāryāsya darśane na bhuñjīta | yathāha manuḥ:

                    	nāśnīyād bhāryayā sārdhaṃ nainām īkṣeta cāśnatīm | iti | (MDh 4.43)

āmnāye 'py evam eva: "tasmād imā manuṣyāḥ striyas tira iva puṃso jaghatsanti" iti | yat tu tatraiva "tasmāj jāyāyā ante nāśnīyāt" iti | abhigamanātirekeṇaikaśayyāśayanapratiṣedhārthaṃ tat, prakramānusārāt | tathā ca samācāraḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 130 ||

 

                    	**na saṃśayaṃ prapadyeta nākasmād apriyaṃ vadet |**

**              	nāhitaṃ nānṛtaṃ caiva na stenaḥ syān na vārdhuṣī || 1.131 ||**

 

stenapunarvacanaṃ nākasmād ity anena saṃbandhārtham | yad vā varjanārtham idam | pūrvatra dharmasādhanam iti || 131 ||

 

 

                    	**dākṣāyaṇī brahmasūtrī yaṣṭimān sakamaṇḍaluḥ |**

**              	kuryāt pradakṣiṇaṃ devamṛdgovipravanaspatīn || 1.132 ||**

 

dākṣāyaṇaṃ hiraṇyaṃ tadvān syāt | tathā ca mantravarṇaḥ:

                    	na tad rakṣāṃsi na piśācās taranti |

                                	devānām ojaḥ prathamajaṃ hy etad,

                    	yo bibharti dākṣāyaṇaṃ hiraṇyam || iti | (RVKh 4.6.7a-b)

brahmasūtrapunaḥśrutir mekhalādinivṛttyarthā | yaṣṭis tu daṇḍakārye | tataś ca tatpramāṇaiva syāt | sakamaṇḍalur iti sahatvamātravacanān na niyogataḥ svayam eva dhāryaḥ | matvarthīyayogāt tu svayam eva yaṣṭyādayo dhāryāḥ | na gṛhasthitayānyagṛhītayā vā yaṣṭyā yaṣṭimān ity ucyate, sahayogas tv anyasaṃsthe 'pi dṛṣṭaḥ | sodakaṃ caitad, dṛṣṭārthatvāt | tathā ca manuḥ |

                    	vaiṇavīṃ dhārayed yaṣṭiṃ sodakaṃ ca kamaṇḍalum |

                    	yajñopavītaṃ vedaṃ ca śubhe raukme ca kuṇḍale || iti | (MDh 4.36)

dhārayed iti ca prayojakatvenāpy upapatter anyadhāraṇe 'pi kamaṇḍalor avirodhaḥ | devādīnāṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kuryāt | devaśabdaś cārcanāśritāyāṃ tatpratikṛtau draṣṭavyaḥ | mṛdādīnāṃ cābhimukhāgamane pradakṣiṇaṃ gacchet | vanaspatiśabdaś ca prajñātayajñiyāśvatthādivanaspatyarthaḥ || 132 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**na meheta nadīcchāyāvartmagoṣṭhāmbubhasmasu |**

**              	na pratyagnyarkagosomasaṃdhyāmbustrīdvijanmanaḥ || 1.133 ||**

 

ambūpādānenaiva siddhatvān nadīvacanaṃ tacchabdavācyakṣetrādyartham | chāyā copajīvyacchāyā, "nopajīvyacchāyāsu" iti vasiṣṭhavacanāt (VaDh 6.12) | tathā ca manuḥ |

                    	chāyāyām andhakāre vā rātrāv ahani vā sadā |

                    	yathāsukhamukhaḥ kuryāt prāṇābādhabhayeṣu ca || (MDh 4.51)

iti chāyāmātrasyāniṣedhaṃ darśayati | saṃdhyāśabdaś codayāstamayānvitadikpratiṣedhārthaḥ, kāle hi mehanānujñānāt | mehanaśabdaś cobhayatrāpi mūtrapurīṣotsarge draṣṭavyaḥ | brahmacāriprakaraṇe ca prasaktasyāpy anabhidhānaṃ sarvāśramavihitam aviruddhaṃ sarvāśrameṣu pravartata iti jñāpanārtham | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "uttareṣāṃ caitad avirodhi" iti (GDh 3.10) | caśabdād āśramāntaroktaṃ ca brahmacāriṇa ity etad evāha |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evaṃ kasmān na bhavati: brahmacāriprakaraṇoktam anyasya mā bhūd iti tatrānārambhaḥ | tathā ca brahmacāriṇo diṅniyama ukte snātakasyārkādyabhimukhapratiṣedhopapattiḥ | anyathā tūdaṅmukhasya katham ādityābhimukhyaṃ, yena pratiṣidhyeta |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | uktaṃ tu smṛtyantaraikavākyatvād iti | tathā ca manunā snātakasyaiva diṅniyama uktaḥ | kathaṃ tarhi pratyarkapratiṣedhaḥ | diṅmohādiviṣayam etad draṣṭavyam | digaparijñāne 'py aniyama eva sāmarthyāt prasaktaḥ | tatredam ucyate: na pratyagnyarketi || 133 ||

 

_idaṃ cānyat |_

 

                    	**nekṣetārkaṃ na nagnāṃ strīṃ na ca saṃspṛṣṭamaithunām |**

**              	na ca mūtraṃ purīṣaṃ vā nāśucī rāhutārakāḥ || 1.134 ||**

 

nityam evākasmād arkadarśanapratiṣedhaḥ | na ca saṃspṛṣṭamaithunām iti | caśabdo 'vasthāntarārthaḥ | yathā "kṣuvantīṃ jṛmbhamāṇāṃ vā" ityādi (MDh 4.43) | sāmarthyāc cāyaṃ parakīyāyā niṣedhaḥ | na nagnām iti tu svakīyāyā api | anyatrāviruddhaḥ | asmād eva ca strīṇāṃ nagnodvartanādy abhyanujñātam | aśuceś ca rāhunakṣatradarśananiṣedhān nānyadā doṣaḥ | rāhuvacanaṃ copaspṛṣṭasomādyartham || 134 ||

 

**              	ayaṃ me vajra ity enaṃ sarvaṃ mantram udīrayet |**

**              	varṣaty aprāvṛto gacchet svapet pratyakchirā na ca || 1.135 ||**

 

tathā cāmnāyaḥ: "tasmād varṣaty aprāvṛto na vrajet" | "ayaṃ me vajraḥ pāpmānam ahatād" (PārG 2.7.7) ity etad eva mantrasya kārtsnyam | yadā varṣati gacchet, tadaivam iti vyākhyeyam || 135 ||

 

_idaṃ cānyat |_

 

                    	**ṣṭhīvanāsṛkchakṛnmūtraviṣāṇy apsu na saṃkṣipet |**

**              	pādau pratāpayen nāgnau na cainam atilaṅghayet || 1.136 ||**

 

praśabdo 'bhiprāyeṇa naitat kuryād ity evamarthaḥ | caśabdo 'gnāv api ṣṭhīvanādyasaṃkṣepārthaḥ, smṛtyantaroktāny acodanārthaś ca | asṛg lohitam | śakṛt purīṣam | spaṣṭam anyat || 136 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                 	**jalaṃ piben nāñjalinā na śayānaṃ prabodhayet |**

**            	nākṣaiḥ krīḍen na dharmaghnair vyādhitair vā na saṃvaset || 1.137 ||**

 

jalagrahaṇāt kṣīrādyapratiṣedhaḥ | upalakṣaṇārthaṃ jalagrahaṇam ity anye | śayānaṃ cābhighnan kāmakāreṇa vā na bodhayet | tathā cāmnāyaḥ: "tasmād u ha svapantaṃ dhūr iva na bodhayet" iti | dhūr hiṃsā, tayā na bodhayet | abhighnann ivety arthaḥ | sarvatra cāsmin yamaprakaraṇe pūrvoktaṃ nākasmāt kuryād iti yojanīyam | tathā cāmnāyaḥ kāraṇāntarāt kartavyatām darśayati: "tam etair namabhir āmantrayāṃ cakara" ity upakramya "sa nottasthau" ity uktvotthāpanavidhim āha "taṃ pāṇinā peṣaṃ prabodhayām cakāra" iti || 137 ||

 

_idaṃ cānyat |_

 

                    	**viruddhaṃ varjayet karma pretadhūmaṃ nadītaram |**

**              	keśabhasmatuṣāṅgārakapāleṣu ca saṃsthitim || 1.138 ||**

 

viruddhaṃ karmābhicārādikaṃ varjayet | vidhānāśaṅkā mā bhūd iti pratiṣedhaḥ | nadītaraṇaṃ bāhubhyām, "na bāhubhyām nadīṃ taret" iti manuvacanāt (MDh 4.77) | nadīgrahaṇaṃ copalakṣaṇartham | bhasmāṅgārayor gomayakāṣṭhajanyatvād bhedenopanyāso 'nyatrāpi bhedāvabodhanārthaḥ | ṛjv anyat || 138 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**nācakṣīta dhayantīṃ gāṃ nādvāreṇāviśet kvacit |**

**              	na rājñaḥ pratigṛhṇīyāl lubdhasyocchāstravartinaḥ || 1.139 ||**

 

gā parakīyāṃ nācakṣīta | "gā dhayantīṃ parasmai nācakṣīta" (GDh 9.23) iti smṛtyantarāt | goś ca kartṛtvāt tadanicchayā staneṣu tudyamāneṣv ācakṣītaiva | "īheta na yatas tataḥ" (YDh 1.128) iti pūrvaniṣiddhasyāpi rājñaḥ punar upanyāsas tatprapañcārthaḥ, atiśayanindāpradarśanopodghātārthaś ca || 139 ||

 

_idānīṃ tam eva nindātiśayam āha |_

 

                    	**pratigrahe sūnicakridhajiveśyānarādhipāḥ |**

**              	duṣṭā daśaguṇaṃ pūrvāt pūrvād ete yathottaram || 1.140 ||**

 

sūnā prāṇivadhārthaṃ kāṣṭhaṃ, tadvān sūnī | cakraṃ vāgurā | dhvajaḥ śauṇḍikacihnam,

                    	dhvajaṃ ca kuryāc cihnārthaṃ samayā grāmaṃ ca saṃvaset |

                    	na caivāntāvasāyibhyaḥ surāṃ dadyād anāpadi ||

iti smṛtyantarāt | veśo rūpaṃ maithunaṃ vā, tena jīvantī veśyā | tathā ca manuḥ: "veśenaiva ca jīvatām" iti (MDh 4.84) | tātparyaṃ tūktam eva || 140 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvad arthapravṛttyāśritān yamaniyamān abhidhāyādhunādhyayanāśritān vivakṣus tadupodghātārtham āha |_

 

                    	**adhyāyānām upākarma śrāvaṇyāṃ śravaṇena tu |**

**              	haste vauṣadhibhāve vā pañcamyāṃ śrāvaṇasya vā || 1.141 ||**

 

_evaṃ chandāṃsy upākṛtyārdhapañcamān māsān ardhaṣaṣṭhān vādhītya tataḥ |_

 

                    	**pauṣamāsasya rohiṇyām aṣṭakāyām athāpi vā |**

**              	jalānte chandasāṃ kuryād utsargaṃ vidhivad dvijaḥ || 1.142 ||**

 

aṣṭakā cātra māghasya gṛhyate | tathā ca pāraskaraḥ: "pauṣamāsasya rohiṇyāṃ madhyamāyāṃ vāṣṭakāyām adhyāyān utsṛjeran" iti (PārG 2.12.1) | ete copākarmotsargakarmaṇī ācāryasyaiva, "yāvantaṃ śiṣyagaṇam icchet" (cf. PārG 2.10.17) ity upākarmaṇi pāraskarābhidhānāt | dvijagrahaṇaṃ tu śiṣyābhiprāyeṇānuvādaḥ | gṛhyaśāstrāpekṣa eva cāyam upadeśaḥ, vidhivad iti vacanāt | vidhivac copākṛtyotsṛjya cādhīyānasyābhyāsārthaṃ vā vedākhyaṃ brahmārthato granthato vā dvijātimātrasya || 142 ||

 

                    	**tryahaṃ preteṣv anadhyāyaḥ śiṣyartviggurubandhuṣu |**

**              	upākarmaṇi cotsarge svaśākhe śrotriye tathā || 1.143 ||**

 

gurur atropādhyāyo nācāryaḥ | yathāha pāraskaraḥ: "gurau prete 'po 'bhyaveyāt | daśarātraṃ coparamet | satānūnaptriṇi sabrahmacāriṇi trirartram | ekarātram asabrahmacāriṇi" iti (PārG 2.11.7–9) | etad apitary ācārye draṣṭavyam | anayaiva diśānyatrāpi viṣayakalpanā, na tu yadṛcchātaḥ | ṛtviksamaye tu satānūnaptravacanād yajamānavad ṛtvigantarāṇām api syāt | ata eva cāsomartvijy ekarātram eva | sabrahmacārī caikācāryopanītaḥ | "svaśākhe śrotriye tathā" iti | śrotriyo mantrabrāhmaṇādhyāyī | yad vā svaśākhādhyāyini śrotriye ceti bhedaḥ | srotriyaśabdaś ca vedapāragādyarthaḥ | anyatra tu ekarātram eva | tathāśabdaś ca smṛtyantaroktānadhyāyaprakārasaṃgrahārthaḥ | yathāha gautamaḥ: "antarā gamane śvādīnāṃ tryaham upavāso vipravāsaś ca" ityādi (GDh 1.58–59) | spaṣṭam anyat || 143 ||

 

_tathā |_

 

                    	**saṃdhyāgarjitanirghātabhūkampolkānipātane |**

**              	samāpya vedaṃ dyuniśam āraṇyakam adhītya ca || 1.144 ||**

 

dyuniśam ahorātram | tac ca vyavasthayā | sāyaṃ saṃdhyāgarjite niśāyām eva, "pratar divaiva varṣāsu anyadā tu samuccayaḥ, saṃdhyāgarjite cāpartāv ahorātram" iti smṛtyantarāt | atra copariṣṭād dyuniśam iti prakṛte 'py ahorātram iti vacanāt || 144 ||

 

_tathā ca |_

 

**              	pañcadaśyāṃ caturdaśyām aṣṭamyāṃ rāhusūtake |**

**              	ṛtusaṃdhiṣu bhuktvā vā śrāddhikaṃ pratigṛhya vā || 1.145 ||**

 

dyuniśam iti vartate | pañcadaśī ca pakṣāpekṣayāmāvāsyāpi gṛhyate | tathā ca "vāte 'māvāsyāyāṃ sarvānadhyāyaḥ" iti pāraskaraḥ (PārG 2.11.1) | śrāddhārtham āmantraṇaṃ śrāddhikaṃ, tad ālabhyāpy anadhyāyaḥ | āmaśrāddhārtho vāyam ārambhaḥ, "pāṇyāsyo hi dvijaḥ smṛtaḥ" (MDh 4.177) iti vacanāt | tathā ca vāśabaś caśabdārthe, bhuktābhuktvā ceti | yat tu rāhusūtake trirātraṃ, tad grahanārthe 'dhyayane na dhāraṇārthe | anye 'pi cātra guravaḥ kalpasvaparaśākhāgranthārthabhedena grahaṇārthatayaiva kalpyāḥ | tathā ca dhāraṇābhiprāyeṇaivāha manuḥ:

                    	dvāv eva varjayen nityam anadhyāyau prayatnataḥ |

                    	svādhyāyabhūmiṃ cāśuddhām ātmānaṃ cāsuciṃ dvijaḥ || iti | (MDh 4.127)

āmnāyaś ca "tasmād eva vidvān vidyotamāne stanayaty avasphūrjaty adhīyītaiva" (ŚB 11.5.6.9) iti dhāraṇārtha eva, brahmayajñe 'nadhyāyāsaṃbhavāt || 145 ||

 

                    	**paśumaṇḍūkanakulaśvāhimārjārasūkaraiḥ |**

**              	kṛte 'ntare tv ahorātraṃ śakrapāte tathocchraye || 1.146 ||**

 

tuśabdo 'vadhāraṇārthaḥ | ahorātram eva, na pūrvavad vyavasthā | paśuḥ chāgaḥ, "meṣakas te paśuḥ" iti mantravarnāt, smṛtyantare ca meṣakopadeśāt | spaṣṭam anyat | anyaḥ pāṭhaḥ: "mahotsave" iti | evaṃ ca mahānavamyādāv ahorātram | yat tūktam: "bhojanād ūrdhvam utsavaḥ" iti, utsavamātraviṣayaṃ tat | śakrocchraye tu smṛtyantarāt || 146 ||

 

                    	**śvakroṣṭugardabholūkasāmabāṇārtaniḥsvane |**

**              	amedhyaśavaśūdrāntyaśmaśānapatitāntike || 1.147 ||**

 

kroṣṭā sṛgālaḥ | bāṇo vīṇā | antyo 'paśadaḥ | śūdravacanād eva daṇḍāpūpavad antyaprāptau tadvacanam āśritaśūdranivṛttyartham | medhyadeśasthasyāpy amedhyasamīpe śmaśānasamīpe vānadhyāyaḥ | amedhyavacanāt siddhe śmaśānavacanaṃ dūrataravarjanārtham | tathā ca āpastambaḥ: "śmaśāne sarvataḥ śamyāprāsān nādhīyīta" iti (ĀpDh 1.9.6) || 147 ||

 

_tathā |_

 

                    	**deśe śucāv ātmani ca vidyutstanitasaṃplave |**

**              	bhuktvārdrapāṇir ambho'ntar ardharātre 'timārute || 1.148 ||**

**              	pāṃsuvarṣe diśāṃ dāhe saṃdhyānīhārabhītiṣu |**

**              	dhāvataḥ pūtigandhe ca śiṣṭe ca gṛham āgate || 1.149 ||**

 

nīhāro dhūmikā || 148, 149 ||

 

                    	**kharoṣṭrayānahastyaśvanauvṛkṣeriṇarohaṇe |**

**              	saptatriṃśad anadhyāyān etāṃs tātkālikān viduḥ || 1.150 ||**

 

saṅkhyāvacanaṃ vidyutsaṃplave stanitasaṃplave bhuktvaivārdrapāṇiḥ kharārohaṇe uṣṭrārohaṇe yānārohaṇe nāvārohaṇa ity evamādivivekārtham | śvanādād ārabhya iriṇarohaṇāntās tātkālikāḥ, yāvad ārūḍhas tāvad eva bhavatīti | iriṇam ūṣaram | etān vidur iti paramatopanyāsārtham | tataś ca smṛtyantaroktān apy anadhyāyān anviṣya vidhivat kuryād ity abhiprāyaḥ || 150 ||

 

_śiṣṭāgamane 'nadhyāya uktaḥ | tatra sūdrādimadhyapāṭhād anyaḥ kaścic chiṣṭo 'py alaukiko 'śrāvya ity āśaṅkānivṛttyartham āha |_

 

                    	**devartviksnātakācāryarājñāṃ chayāṃ parasya ca |**

**              	nākrāmed raktaviṇmūtraṣṭhīvanodvartanāni ca || 1.151 ||**

 

chāyāśabdo hi khyātivacanaḥ | yathā: mahatī chāyā devadattasyeti | ato devādīnāṃ chāyām nākrāmet | tatra yathaivartvigādyāgamane snehān madhuparkādyākulatvāc cānadhyāyaḥ, evaṃ parasminn api prakṛṣṭaguṇe 'nadhyāya ity arthaḥ | tathā cāmnāyaḥ: "ya u haivaṃvit sveṣu pratibubhūṣati, sa haivālaṃ bhāryebhyo bhavati" ityādi (BāU 1.3.18) | "ya u haivamvidā spardhate, so 'nuśuṣyehaivāntato mriyate" iti (BāU 1.5.21) | devavacanam atistutyartham | raktādīnāṃ tv abhibhavābhāvād adhiṣṭhānapratiṣedhaḥ | raktaṃ rudhiram | viṭ purīṣam | spaṣṭam anyat | anadhyāyasaṃnidheś caitad vyatirekeṇaiva deśasyāmedhyatvaṃ padopaghātādinā | tataś copaliptādāv adhyayanasiddhiḥ | anye tu devādīnām api śarīracchāyānadhiṣṭhānam evecchanti | tat punar vicāryam || 151 |

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evaṃ saty aprakṛṣṭe 'py āgate 'nādhyāyaḥ pūjā vā prasajyeta, "sarvasyābhyāgato guruḥ" iti vacanāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span> |_

 

                    	**viprāhikṣatriyātmāno nāvajñeyāḥ kadācana |**

**              	ā mṛtyoḥ śriyam ākāṅkṣen na kaṃcin marmaṇi spṛśet || 1.152 ||**

 

viprakṣatriyaśabdau pūrvaślokānuvādāc chiṣṭapārthivavacanau | ahiśabdo dṛṣṭāntārthaḥ | yathaivāhir nāvajñeya utkṛṣṭabrāhmaṇarājānau ca, tathaivātmāpi | ato na yaṃ kaṃcid apekṣyātmābhyutthānānadhyāyādinā nyak kartavyaḥ | śrotriyasyaiva tat kartavyam ity arthaḥ | tathā cāha manuḥ |

                    	vidvadbhojyāny avidvāṃso yeṣu rāṣṭreṣu bhuñjate |

                    	tāny anāvṛṣṭim icchanti mahad vā jāyate bhayam || iti | (MDh ?)

ātmalāghavākaraṇa eva hetum āha "āmṛtyoḥ śriyam ākāṅkṣet" iti | idaṃ tv aviśeṣeṇaiva kuryāt "na kaṃcin marmaṇi spṛśet" iti | anyā vyākhyā "viprādimātrasyaivāvajñā na kāryā" iti | tathā ca bhagavān vāsudevaḥ |

                    	vidvān avidvān aśuciṃ śuciṃ vā

                                	yo brāhmaṇaṃ na praṇamed yathārham |

                    	sa pāpakṛd brahmadavāgnidagdho

                                	daṇḍyaś ca vadhyaś ca na cāsmadīyaḥ || iti |

tat punar vakṣyamāṇatvād akiṃcit || 152 ||

 

_idānīṃ mānaprasaṅgād gṛhadevatānāṃ mānārtham āha |_

 

                    	**dūrād ucchiṣṭaviṇmūtrapādāmbhāṃsi samutsṛjet |**

 

gṛhadevatānāṃ mānārtham | gṛhād iti śeṣaḥ ||

 

                    	**śrutismṛtyuditaṃ samyaṅ nityam ācāram ācaret || 1.153 ||**

 

"pradarśanārtham idaṃ mayoktam" (cf. YDh 3.217), anyad api śrutismṛtyantarebhyaś cānveṣyam ity abhiprāyaḥ || 153 ||

 

_idaṃ cānyan mānaprasaṅgād eva |_

 

                    	**gobrāhmaṇānalānnāni nocchiṣṭo na pada spṛśet |**

 

analo 'gniḥ | annaṃ bhujyamānaṃ pakvam āmaṃ vā |

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**na nindātāḍane kuryāt**

 

prakṛtebhyo gavādibhyaḥ|

 

_asyāpavādaḥ |_

 

                                                        	**sutaṃ śiṣyaṃ ca tāḍayet || 1.154 ||**

 

caśabdān nindec ca | patnyādyartho vā caśabdaḥ | saṃnidhānān nindyatvāvagateḥ || 154 ||

 

_ayaṃ tv atropadeśasaṃkṣepaḥ |_

 

                    	**karmaṇā manasā vācā yatnād dharmaṃ samācaret |**

 

nārthakāmāv iti śeṣaḥ |

 

_asyāpavādaḥ |_

 

                    	**asvattaṃ lokavidviṣṭaṃ dharmam apy ācaren na tu || 1.155 ||**

 

anekārthatvād dhātūnām ader gatyarthatvam | asvattam asugatam | asupariniścitam ity arthaḥ | anyaḥ pāṭhaḥ: avantam iti | tasyāpy ayam evārthaḥ | asvantam aśobhanāntam | ante na śobhanam, aniścitatvād iti | tasyaiva nigamanaṃ: lokavidviṣṭam ityādi | tuśabdo 'vadhāraṇārthaḥ | anye tv asvantaṃ rūḍhyaiva dharmāntaravirodhinam ācakṣate | yathā svādhyāyātiśaya iti | tat tv anveṣyam | lokavidviṣṭaṃ sarvajanānabhyupagataṃ govadhādīti kecit | tat tv ayuktaṃ, vidhānānarthakyāt | ato lokaṃ karmasādhyaṃ ye jānanti, te lokavido manvādayaḥ, tair dviṣṭaṃ nācaret | u(tpa ? papa)nne 'py ayaṃ dharma iti svayam abhimānena manvādibhir nindite na pravartetety arthaḥ | adviṣṭe tv aviruddhā pravṛttiḥ || 155 ||

 

_mānyaprasaṅgād anyad apy āha |_

 

                    	**mātṛpitratithibhrātṛjñātisaṃbandhimātulaiḥ |**

**              	vṛddhabālāturācāryavaidyasaṃśritabāndhavaiḥ || 1.156 ||**

**              	ṛtvikpurohitāmātyabhāryādāsasanābhibhiḥ |**

**              	vivādaṃ varjayitvā tu sarvāṃl lokāñ jayed gṛhī || 1.157 ||**

 

tasmād etair vivādaṃ na kuryād iti śeṣaḥ | eṣāṃ ca pratyekaṃ vivādakaraṇanimittabhedād daṇḍāpūpavad gatārthatvaprasaṅgaparihāraḥ || 156, 157 ||

 

_idaṃ cānyat paribhavākaraṇaprasaṅgād ucyate |_

 

                    	**pañca piṇḍān anuddhṛtya na snāyāt paravāriṣu |**

**              	snāyān nadīdevakhātahradeṣu ca sarassu ca || 1.158 ||**

 

yadi parakhāteṣv anuddhṛtyaiva kardamaṃ snāyāt, tatas tatkartā paribhūtaḥ syāt | atas tadanurodhād api tāvat kardamoddharaṇaṃ yuktam ity abhiprāyaḥ | ayaṃ ca nadyādyabhāve snānakalpaḥ | caśabdaḥ prasravaṇādyarthaḥ || 158 ||

 

_mānyaprasaṅgād anyad apy āha |_

 

                    	**paraśayyāsanodyānagṛhayānāni varjayet |**

**              	adattāni**

 

adattānīti cchedaḥ | paraśabdaḥ prakṛṣṭārthaḥ | tadīyāny asādhāraṇāni śayyāsanakrīḍodyānavāsagṛhādīni nādhitiṣṭhet | adattānīti vacanād anujñāto 'dhitiṣṭhed iti gamyate ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	                    	**agnihīnasya na cāśnīyād anāpadi || 1.159 ||**

 

prakṛṣṭasyāpy anaupāsanasya cānnaṃ na cāśnīyāt | caśabdād vakṣyamāṇadoṣayuktasya ca | anye tv anyamātravacanaṃ paraśabdaṃ varṇayanti, adattāni na cāśnīyād ity anena ca yojayanti | tat punar vicāryam || 159 ||

 

_idānīm anyān api prasaṅgād abhojyānnān āha |_

 

                    	**kadaryabaddhacorāṇāṃ klībaraṅgāvatāriṇām |**

**              	venābhiśastavārdhuṣigaṇikāgaṇadīkṣiṇām || 1.160 ||**

 

eṣām annaṃ nāśnīyād iti śeṣaḥ | kadaryas tṛṣṇāluḥ | baddho nigalādiyantritaḥ | coraḥ prasiddhaḥ | raṅgāvatārī mallaḥ | veno naṭaḥ | abhiśasto mahāpātakādivyājadūṣitaḥ |vārdhuṣī samarghadhanam ādāya mahārghadhanavikretā | gaṇikā dāsī | gaṇaḥ pariṣat | dīkṣitaḥ prāg agnīṣomīyāt | dvijātayo 'py evamādikarmadūṣitā na bhojyānnāḥ || 160 ||

 

_tathā |_

 

**              	cikitsakāturakruddhapuṃścalīmattavidviṣām |**

**              	krūrograpatitavrātyaḍāmbhikocchiṣṭabhojinām || 1.161 ||**

 

cikitsako vaidyaḥ | āturo 'samādheyarogī | kruddho nityakrodhanaḥ | puṃścalī prajananendriyapradhānā | matto dhanamadādyabhibhūtaḥ | vidviṭ śatruḥ | krūro 'ntarāśayakaṭhinaḥ | ugraḥ prasahyakārī | patito mahāpātakī, abhiśatavacanāt siddhasyāpy abhidhānaṃ prāyaścittagauravārtham | anyatrāpy evaṃ draṣṭavyam | vrātyaḥ patitasāvitrīkaḥ | ḍāmbhika uktaḥ | ucchiṣṭabhojī śūdraḥ || 161 ||

 

**              	avīrastrīsvarṇakārastrījitagrāmayājinām |**

**              	śastravikrayikarmāratunnavāyaśvavṛttinām || 1.162 ||**

 

aputrapatikāvirastrī | svarṇakārastrījitau prasiddhau | gramayājako vaiśvadevika iti mālavānāṃ prasiddhaḥ | karmāro bhastrerimakaḥ (?) | tunnavāyaḥ sīvanavṛttiḥ | śvavṛttiḥ pādaprakṣālanādihīna(kayā? kriyā)sevakaḥ śvakaṇṭhako vā || 162 ||

 

                    	**nṛśaṃsarājarajakakṛtaghnavadhajīvinām |**

**              	celadhāvasudhājīvasahopapativeśmanām || 1.163 ||**

 

nṛśaṃso 'nudārapāṭhakaḥ (?) rājaviśeṣaṇaṃ vā | rājā pārthivaḥ | rajakaś cimpakaḥ | kṛtaghnaḥ prasiddhaḥ | vadhajīvī mārakaś cāṭaḥ | celadhāvo vastranirṇejakaḥ | sudhā devakulādīnāṃ saṃskāradravyaṃ, tayā jīvati yaḥ sa sudhājīvaḥ | saha upapatinā veśma yasya sa sahopapativeśmā | upapatir bhāryājāraḥ | veśmasaṃbandhitayā snuṣājāro 'pi gṛhyate || 163 ||

 

_ya ete uktāḥ kadaryādayaḥ |_

 

                    	**eṣām annaṃ na bhoktavyaṃ somavikrayiṇas tathā |**

**              	piśunānṛtinoś caiva tathā cākrikavandinām || 1.164 ||**

 

eṣāṃ kadaryādīnām | na kevalaṃ gṛhe nāśnīyāt, tadīyam annam apy āhṛtaṃ na bhuñjīta, na ca pratigṛhṇīyād iti, ārambhasāmarthyāt | eṣām iti vacanād anagnikasyānnaṃ gṛhānītaṃ prokṣaṇādibhiḥ saṃskṛtya bhoktavyam | yathā ca kadaryādīnāṃ somavikrayyādīnām api tathā | somavikrayī latāsomasya vikretā yajñaphalavikretā vā | somaśabdaś ca karmamātropalakṣaṇārthaḥ | piśunaḥ khalo marmasūcakaḥ | anṛtī paropadravaprasaṅge 'nṛtavaktā | cākrikaḥ pāṭahikaḥ | vandī nagnācāryaḥ | tathāśabdaḥ smṛtyantaroktābhojyānnaparigrahārthaḥ | yad vā, eṣāṃ annaṃ na bhoktavyaṃ, na tv aprigrāhyā apy eta iti mantavyam | annapratiṣedhāt phalamūlāder āhṛtasyābhyanujñā | tathāha vasiṣṭhaḥ: "edhodakayavasamūlaphala-madhvabhayābhyudyatayānāvasathaśapharīpriyaṅgusraggandhamāṃsany eṣām api pratigṛhṇīyāt" iti (VaDh 14.12) | nindārtho vāyam ārambhaḥ | naiṣām annaṃ na bhoktavyam eva | kiṃ tarhi bhuktam api bhoktāram eva bhakṣayatīty arthaḥ | sarvavyākhyāvikalpāś cānyatrāpi śāstrāntarāpekṣayā vivicya vyastasamastatvenālocyopādeyā hātavyā vā iti | evaṃ caśabdādayo 'pi kramabhedānarthakatva(tvādi)śabdāntarārthatvapādapūraṇārthatvena vā yathāsthānaṃ yojanīyāḥ || 164 ||

 

**iti snātakadharmaprakaraṇam**

** **

**atha bhakṣyābhakṣyaprakaraṇam**

 

_evaṃ tāvad anaupāsanādyāśrayato 'nnasyābhojyatvam abhidhāyādhunā bhojyaparigṛhītasyāpi nimittāntarād abhojyatvam āha |_

 

                    	**anarcitaṃ vṛthāmāṃsaṃ keśakīṭasamanvitam |**

**              	śuktaṃ paryuṣitocchiṣṭaṃ śvaspṛṣṭaṃ patitekṣitam || 1.165 ||**

 

vṛthāmāṃsaṃ pakvam anagikagṛhāgatam | keśkīṭasamanvitaṃ tadbahulam | saṃśabdād alpāṃs tūddhṛtya saṃskṛtya ca bhakṣaṇam eva | śuktam avasvinnaṃ tadahar api | spaṣṭam anyat || 165 ||

 

                    	**udakyāspṛṣṭasaṃghuṣṭaṃ paryācāntaṃ ca varjayet |**

**              	goghrātaṃ śakunocchiṣṭaṃ pādaspṛṣṭaṃ ca kāmataḥ || 1.166 ||**

 

tuśabdārthaś caśabdaḥ | pūrvokteṣu pratīkāro 'pi kvacid asti, etāni tu varjayed evety abhiprāyaḥ | udakyā rajasvalā | saṃghuṣṭaṃ, yathāha vasiṣṭhaḥ: "ko bhokṣyata iti cābhikruṣṭam" iti (VaDh 14.9) | udakyāspṛṣṭam ity evaṃ vā saṃghuṣṭam | paryācāntam ekapaṅktyām abhitas tv ācāntam, ācāntasya vā svam ucchiṣṭam | spaṣṭam anyat | kāmat iti vacanād akāmād brāhmaṇapādaspṛṣṭṃ bhojyam eva || 166 ||

 

_kiṃ cānyat |_

 

                    	**śūdreṣu dāsagopālakulamitrārdhasīriṇaḥ |**

**              	bhojyānnā nāpitaś caiva yaś cātmānaṃ nivedayet || 1.167 ||**

 

bhojyā iti vaktavye bhojyānnā iti vacanāt prakaraṇāc cānnam evaiṣāṃ bhojyam | śūdrāntarāṇāṃ tu tatpratiṣedho 'pi | dāsādayaś ca svakīyā eva, anyathātiprasaṅgāt || 167 ||

 

                    	**annaṃ paryuṣitaṃ bhojyaṃ snehāktaṃ cirasaṃsthitam |**

**              	asnehā api godhūmayavagorasavikriyāḥ || 1.168 ||**

 

annavacanaṃ māṃsādivyāvṛttyartham | māṃsaṃ hi paryuṣitam abhojyam eva | annaṃ tu śuktam eva paryuṣitam abhojyam | anyat tu dvitrirātrādiparyuṣitam, cirasaṃsthitaṃ, tad api snehāktaṃ bhojyam eva, na ced rasādivikṛtam | pūrvatrāpi paryuṣitam etad apekṣayaiva vyākhyeyam | pariśabdāc cāhorātroṣitaṃ gṛhyate | tataś cāpararātre siddhaṃ bhojyam eva | spaṣṭam anyat || 168 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvan nimittatvena dauṣṭyam uktvādhunā svabhāvato vaktum āha |_

 

                    	**saṃdhinyanirdaśāvatsagopayaḥ parivarjayet |**

**              	auṣṭram aikaśaphaṃ straiṇam āraṇyakam athāvikam || 1.169 ||**

 

saṃdhinī paravatsasaṃyuktā, garbhasahitā vā | ekakālikety anye | anirdaśā prasavād ārabhya ā daśarātrāt | anye tu "gavyaṃ pīyūṣam" (MDh 5.6) iti pratiṣedhāt, tatkālād ūrdhvaṃ daśarātram ity āhuḥ | tad asad, viśeṣābhāvāt | anirdaśeti copādhyapekṣaṇāt, kṣīrasattaivopādhir yataḥ | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "goś ca kṣīram anirdaśāyāḥ sūtake" (GDh 17.22) iti prasavm evāvadhitvenāha | pīyūṣaniṣedhas tu prāyaścittātirekārthaḥ | tathā cāha: "prayatnena vivarjayet" iti (MDh 5.6) | avatsā mṛtavatsā pranaṣṭavatsā vā | vatsaśabdo hi bālagovacanaḥ | tataś ca siddhe govacanaṃ payomātrapratiṣedhārtham | ato dadhyāder adoṣaḥ | pariśabdāt tv auṣṭrādīnāṃ savikārāṇāṃ pratiṣedhaḥ | yadi tv anirdaśāyā vikārapratiṣedho 'pi kvacid asti, tato varjane 'bhyudayaḥ | anyatrāpy evam evaitad draṣṭavyam | spaṣṭam anyat || 169 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

** **

**              	devatārthaṃ haviḥ śigruṃ lohitāvraścanāni ca |**

**              	anupākṛtamāṃsāni viḍjāni kavakāni ca || 1.170 ||**

 

devatārthaṃ haviḥ puroḍāśādi | balir ity anye | śigruḥ saubhāñjanakaḥ | lohitāḥ lohitavarṇāḥ vṛkṣaniryāsāḥ | āvraścanaṃ sthāṇuḥ | sa cādanīyo yadi syāt tato varjyaḥ | caśabdāt tatprarohaś ca | tathā ca manuḥ:

                    	lohitān vṛkṣaniryāsān vraścanaprabhavāṃs tathā | iti | (MDh 5.6)

anupākṛtam apaśubandhaprabhavam | viḍjāni māṣādīni | kavakāny avikasitasarpacchatrāṇi | caśabdād itarāṇi smṛtyantaroktābhakṣyāṇi ca | devatārthahavirvacanaṃ ca svabhāvaduṣṭaprakaraṇopalakṣaṇād ahaviṣo 'pi prasiddhadevatārthasvabhāvasya pratiṣedhārtham | anupākṛtamāṃsavacanam api māṃsasya svabhāvadauṣṭyajñāpanārtham || 170 ||

 

_evaṃ sati māṃsasya svabhāvād abhakṣyatve prāpte viśeṣopasaṃhārārtham āha |_

 

                    	**kravyādapakṣidātyūhaśukapratudaṭiṭṭibhān |**

**              	sārasaikaśaphān haṃsān sarvāṃś ca grāmavāsinaḥ || 1.171 ||**

 

kravyādā māṃsādāḥ pakṣiṇo gṛdhrādayaḥ | pakṣiśabdo 'nyatrāpy amedhyapakṣiprasaṅga eṣāṃ eva pratipattyarthaḥ, ekaśaphopādānavad vā kevalapakṣyarthaḥ | dātyūhaḥ saṃpātakaḥ | pratudya bhakṣakāḥ pratudāḥ sūcīmukhādayaḥ | ekaśaphā ekakhurā aśvādayaḥ | pakṣimadhya eṣām abhidhānaṃ paśavo 'pi grāmavāsinaḥ śvādayo yathā syur iti | spaṣṭam anyat || 171 ||

 

                    	**koyaṣṭiplavacakrāhvabalākabakaviṣkirān |**

**              	vṛthākṛsarasaṃyāvapāyasāpūpaśaṣkulīḥ || 1.172 ||**

 

koyaṣṭiko meḍhrakaḥ | plavaḥ śakaṭibalaḥ | cakravākādayaḥ prasiddhāḥ | viṣkirāḥ pādena vikīrya bhakṣakāḥ kukkuṭādayaḥ | grāmavāsivacanād grāmakukkuṭapratiṣedhe siddha āraṇyārtho 'yam ārambhaḥ | tatrāpi "kukktuṭā nakhaviṣkirāṇām" ity (not in ĀpDh) āpastambavacanāḷ lābakādyapratiṣedhaḥ | kṛsarādayaḥ prasiddhāḥ | atrābhidhānaṃ māṃsavat prāyaścittajñāpanārtham | svabhāvaduṣṭatvaṃ ca | tataś cānagner apy ātmārthatve doṣaḥ | tathā ca śaṅkhaḥ: "vṛthākṛsarasaṃyāvapāyasāpūpamāṃsāśanam āhitāgniḥ kṛtvā prājāpatyaṃ caret | trirātram itareṣam" iti |

 

_tathā |_

 

                    	**kalaviṅkaṃ sakākolaṃ kuraraṃ rajjudālakam |**

**              	jālapādān khañjarīṭān ajñātāṃś ca mṛgadvijān || 1.173 ||**

 

kalaviṅko grāmacaṭakaḥ | tasya varṣāsv araṇyavāsāśaṅkayā punarvacanam iti kecit | tat punar grāmacaṭakavyapadeśād evāyuktam, ataḥ svabhāvadauṣṭyātirekārtham | tataś ca strīśūdrayor apy abhakṣyatvasiddhiḥ | grāmavāsimātropalakṣaṇaṃ caitat | tathā ca samācāraḥ | asmin prakaraṇe 'nyāny api punarvacanāny evam eva vyākhyeyāni | kākolaḥ śyenaḥ | kuraraḥ śabdānukārī karañjakaḥ | rajjudālo 'raṇyakapotaḥ | khañjarīṭākhyo dīrghapucchaḥ pūrvadeśaprasiddhaḥ | śleṣmātaka ity anye | māṃsatulyadoṣārthaṃ caitad vacanam | jālapādā haṃsādayaḥ | punarvacanaṃ tūktārtham | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evaṃ cakravākādivacanam ayuktam | sarvajālopalakṣaṇatvaṃ kalaviṅkavan mā bhūd ity <span style="text-decoration:underline;">evamartham</span> | ata eva cāṭyā(?)dayaḥ strīśūdrayor apratiṣiddhāḥ | khañjarīṭān iti bahuvacanaṃ strīśūdrayor apy abhyakṣatvārtham | haṃśān iti tu siddhe 'pi dauṣṭye 'nyatrāpi bahuvacanasyāyam evārtho yathā syād ity uktam | ajñātavacanaṃ dṛṣṭāntārtham | yathaiva māṃsāśanābhiyuktair bhaikṣyatvenājñātāḥ paśavaḥ pakṣiṇaś ca maraṇādibhayān na bhakṣyante, tathā śāstroktasvabhāvaduṣṭā apīty abhiprāyaḥ || 173 ||

 

_tathā |_

 

                    	**cāṣāṃś ca raktapādāṃś ca saunaṃ vallūram eva ca |**

**              	matsyāṃś cākāmato jagdhvā sopavāsas tryahaṃ bhavet || 1.174 ||**

 

bahuvacanaṃ tūktārtham | saunaṃ sūnārūḍhaduṣṭam | vallūraṃ prasiddham | śuktamāṃsam iti kecit | etān matsyāṃś ca vakṣyamāṇātirekeṇākāmato bhakṣayitvā sahopavāsena tryahaṃ syāt | caturaham evety arthaḥ | saha vā tena trirātram || 174 ||

 

_tathā kāmata eva |_

 

                    	**palaṇḍuṃ viḍvarāhaṃ tu chatrākaṃ grāmakukkuṭam |**

**              	laśunaṃ gṛñjanaṃ caiva jagdhvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret || 1.175 ||**

 

gṛñjanaṃ palaṇḍusadṛśam udīcyadeśaprasiddham | laśunagṛñjanapalaṇḍūnāṃ prāyaścittavidhānāt pratiṣedhakalpanā | viḍvarāhādīnāṃ tu prāyaścittārtham vacanam | viḍvarāho grāmasūkaraḥ | chatrākaṃ sarpacchatrakam | caśabdo viḍvarāhatulyagrāmavāsipaśupratiśedhārthaḥ | tathā cāmnāyaḥ: "trayo hatvā paśavo 'medhyā viḍvarāha elakaś ca" iti | pāṭhasiddhe traya ity amedhyatvaprakārārtham: evaṃjātīyakā evāmedhyā na tv ajādaya iti | tuśabdaḥ sarvathā sarvavarṇāṇāṃ cety dytotanārthaḥ | aprakaraṇe prāyaścittābhidhānaṃ sarvatrānantarānuṣṭhānārtham | yaticāndrāyaṇam caitat |

                    	amatyaitāni ṣaḍ jagdhvā kṛcchraṃ sāntapanaṃ caret |

                    	yaticāndrāyaṇaṃ vāpi śeṣeṣūpavased ahaḥ || iti | (MDh 5.20)

ayaṃ tv atra saṃpradāyaḥ: anagnikādyāśrayaduṣṭabhojane trirātram akāmāt, kāmatas tu prājāpatyam | yathāha manuḥ |

                    	bhuktvāto 'nyatamasyānnam amatyā (tu) tryahaṃ kṣapet |

                    	matyā bhuktvā caret kṛcchraṃ retoviṇmūtram eva ca || iti | (MDh 4.222)

naimittikābhojye 'py etad eva, prakaraṇābhedāt | svabhāvaduṣṭe tv amatyehoktaṃ catūrātram | matyā kṛcchra eva japādyupabṛṃhitaḥ | palaṇḍvādīnāṃ cāmatyā yaticāndrāyaṇam | matyā tu patitavacanād bhakṣaṇasāmānyāc ca surāpānaprāyaścittam | tatra "surāyāś cājñāne" (VaDh 20.19) ity etad vasiṣṭhoktaṃ kṛcchrātikṛcchraṃ punaḥ saṃskāraś ceti, na tu kāmakṛtasurāpānaprāyaścittaṃ, patitatvopacārāt | evam āhitāgner dvijanmanaḥ | itarasya tu "śeṣeṣūpavased ahaḥ" (MDh 5.20) ity akāmād upavāsaḥ | kāmatas trirātraṃ, "trirātram itareṣām" iti śaṅkhavacanāt | palaṇḍvādāv amatyā sāntapanaṃ, matyā tv atikṛcchra eva, "palaṇḍvādibhojaneṣv atikṛcchraḥ" iti vasiṣṭhavacanāt (VaDh 14.33) | yady api kākādyavalīḍhabhojane 'tikṛcchra uktaḥ, tathāpy evam eva, smṛtyantaraikavākyatvāt | prāyaścittaprakaraṇe tu viṣayakalpanānyāyaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ || 175 ||

 

_kiṃ sarvāny abhakṣyāny eva māṃsāni | nety ucyate |_

 

                    	**bhakṣyāḥ pañcanakhāḥ sedhāgodhākacchapaśalyakāḥ |**

**              	śaśaś ca matsyeṣv api hi siṃhatuṇḍakarohitāḥ || 1.176 ||**

 

bhakṣaṇārhā bhakṣyāḥ | pañcanakhāḥ sedhādayaḥ śaśāntāḥ | caśabdaḥ khaḍgādyarthaḥ | yat tu vāsiṣṭhaṃ: "khaḍge tu vivadanty agrāmyasūkare ca" (VaDh 14.47) iti, vividhaṃ śrāddhādau praśaṃsārthaṃ vadantīty asyārthaḥ | tathā ca "ānantyaṃ khaḍgamāṃsena" ity ātreyaḥ | pañcanakhagrahaṇaṃ hastyādiparisaṃkhyārtham | matsyeṣv api siṃhatuṇḍādayo bhakṣyāḥ, na sarpaśīrṣādayaḥ | siṃho dīrghamukho dīrghaḥ | tuṇḍaḥ sthūlaḥ sthūlamukhaḥ | rohito lohitavarṇaḥ | hiśabdo hetvarthaḥ | yasmān matsyādimāṃsair māsavṛddhyā pitṛtṛptir abhidhāsyate, tasmān matsyā bhakṣyā iti | hetvabhidhānaprayojanaṃ tu śrāddha eva bhakṣyatvajñāpanārtham | tathā ca manuḥ: "pāṭhīnarohitāv ādyau" iti (MDh 5.16) | apiśabdas tu matsyasaṃbaddhaṃ pañcanakheṣv api prāyaścittaṃ yathā syāt: "sopavāsaṃ tryahaṃ bhavet" (YDh 1.174) iti, śrāddhe sedhādiprāptyarthaṃ ca || 176 ||

 

                    	**tathā pāṭhīnarājīvau saśalkāś ca dvijātibhiḥ |**

**              	ataḥ śṛṇudhvaṃ māṃsasya vidhiṃ bhakṣaṇavarjane || 1.177 ||**

 

pāṭhīnādayaḥ prasiddhāḥ | tathāśabdāt pāṭhīnarājīvāv api śrāddha eva | saśalkās tv aviśeṣeṇaiva | tuśabdārthaś caśabdaḥ | dvijātivacanāc coktaṃ vakṣyamāṇaṃ ca dvijātyartham eva, dvijātibhir apy etat kartavaṃ kim utānyair iti | yasmāc ca sedhādimāṃsaṃ na svabhāvaduṣṭaṃ śrāddhaupayikam vā, tasmāc "chṛṇudhvaṃ māṃsasya vidhiṃ bhakṣaṇavarjane" | bhakṣaṇe varjanaṃ bhakṣaṇavarjanam | nirdoṣaṃ bhakṣaṇam ity arthaḥ | bhakṣaṇasya vā prāptasya varjanam | vidhiśabdaḥ prakārārthaḥ | māṃsavarjane saṃbhodhanaṃ tv ādarārtham || 177 ||

 

_kaḥ punar asau vidhir ity ata āha |_

 

                 	**prāṇātyaye tathā śrāddhe prokṣitaṃ dvijakāmyayā |**

**            	devān pitṝṃs tathābhyarcya khādan māṃsaṃ na doṣabhāk || 1.178 ||**

 

_yas tv ato 'nyathā |_

 

                    	**vaset sa narake ghore dināni paśuromabhiḥ |**

**              	saṃmitāni durācāro yo hanty avidhinā paśūn || 1.179 ||**

 

pūrvaśloke tathāśabdadvayāt prakāradvayam | prāṇātyaye tathā śrāddhe prokṣitam ity ekaḥ prakāraḥ | dvijakāmyayā devān pitṝṃs tathābhyarcyety aparaḥ | tatra yathaiva prāṇātyaye kratau ca maraṇapratyavāyabhītyā nigoyato bhakṣyaṃ, tathā śrāddhe niyuktenāpīty arthaḥ | tathā cāha manuḥ: "niyuktas tu yathānyāyam" iti (MDh 5.35) | yathānyāyavacanāt tu prītivyāvṛttiḥ | prāṇātyayopādānaṃ ca dṛṣṭāntārthatve 'py asiddhasyādṛṣṭāntatvāc chāstrataś cāsiddhatvād vidhīyata eva | prokṣitam api vyāmohāpanuttaye prāṇātyaye cābhakṣayatā paśūn ātmāvidhinaiva hataḥ syāt, prokṣitābhakṣaṇe kratuvaiguṇyāt | tasmāt prāṇātyayāder anyatra ca lobhādinā yo hanty avidhinā paśūn, vaset sa narake ghora iti yojyam | vadhaś cāṣṭavidhaḥ | yathāha manuḥ: "anumantā viśasitā" ityādi (MDh 5.51) | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ayaṃ prokṣitaśabdaḥ prakṛṣṭasecanam āha | tat kuto viśiṣṭārthāvagatiḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | ayam eva tv asau prakarṣaḥ | yadvidhānalakṣaṇatvaṃ kratāv eva ca tat | dvayaṃ cānyatra kāryaṃ: prokṣaṇaṃ ca kuryāt, prokṣitaṃ ca bhakṣayed iti | kratau tu tasya siddhatvāt parārthopādānam aviruddham | tathā cāmnāyaḥ: "jīryanti ha vai juhvato yajamānasyāgnayaḥ" ity upakramya "athaiteṣāṃ nāto 'nyā māṃsāśā vidyate yasya caite bhavanti" (ŚB 11.7.1.1–2) iti kratāv eva māṃsaprāptim anyatra cāprāptiṃ darśayan prokṣitaśabdasya kratvarthatām eva dyotayati | yas tv aparaḥ prakāro dvijakāmyayetyādiḥ, tenāśnan na doṣabhāk || 179 ||

 

_yadi tu varjayet tadā |_

 

                    	**sarvān kāmān avāpnoti hayamedhaphalaṃ tathā |**

**              	gṛhe 'pi nivasan vipro munir māṃsasya varjanāt || 1.180 ||**

 

dvijaiḥ kāmyamānatvād dvijakāmyā atithipūjā | tayopanītaṃ mahokṣādi bhakṣayato na doṣaḥ | tathā devapitrarcanaṃ śrāddhakarma | tat kṛtvā śiṣṭaṃ māṃsam aśnataḥ | yadi tv etad api varjayet, tataḥ sarvān kāmān avāpnoti hayamedhaphalaṃ tathā ityādi yojyam | vicitrāṃ caiva māṃsāśanakriyām ālocyāha manuḥ: "na māṃsabhakṣaṇe doṣaḥ" iti (MDh 5.56) || 180 ||

 

**iti bhakṣābhakṣyaprakaraṇam**

** **

**atha dravyaśuddhiprakaraṇam**

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evaṃ māṃsabhakṣaṇavidhānam ayuktam, nimittadauṣṭyasyāsamādheyatvāt | śvacaṇḍālādibhir hi māṃsam utpādyate yataḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyaṃ</span> śvacaṇḍālādyutpādyaṃ, tathāpy aduṣṭam evety etat pratipipādayiṣayaiva prasaṅgāt dravyāntarāṇām api nimittāntarato 'medhyānāṃ medhyatvavidhānāyāha | yad vā sarvadravyāṇāṃ śaucam asti, na tu svabhāvaduṣṭānāṃ viḍvarāhādīnām iti dravyaśuddhyārambhaḥ | viḍvarāhādyaśucisaṃpṛktaṃ vā dravyaṃ kathaṃ śudhyed ity ākāṅkṣita āha |_

 

                    	**sauvarṇarājatābjānām ūrdhvapātragrahāśmanām**

**              	śakarajjumūlaphalavāsovidalacarmaṇām || 1.181 ||**

**              	pātrāṇāṃ camasānāṃ ca vāriṇā śuddhir iṣyate |**

 

śuddhir iṣyata ity etad evāsmin prakaraṇe kriyāpadaṃ yathayathaṃ yojyam | sauvarṇānāṃ ca nirlepānām aśucisparśanamātre 'śuddhiḥ | yathāha manuḥ |

                    	nirlepaṃ kāñcanaṃ bhāṇḍam adbhir eva viśudhyati |

                    	abjam aśmamayaṃ caiva rājataṃ cānupaskṛtam || iti | (MDh 5.112)

rājataṃ raupyam | abjaṃ śaṅkhaśuktyādi | ūrdhapātrāṇi ṣoḍaśipātrādīni | grahā aindravāyavādipātrāṇi | grahatvād evordhvapātre siddhe bhedābhidhānaṃ kṛtsnapātrārtham | tataś ca droṇakalaśādy apy uktaṃ bhavati | aśma dṛṣadādi | śākādīni spaṣṭāni | vidalo veṇvādi | sarvatra cāsmin prakaraṇe prakṛtivikṛtyor anyataragrahaṇe 'py ubhayalābhaḥ | tathā ca vasiṣṭho dāravāṇāṃ takṣaṇam uktvā prakṛtyātidiśati: "dāruvad asthnām" iti (VaDh 3.52) | ācāryo 'pi rājatānām aśmanām iti pātraviśeṣaṇatvenopadiśann etad eva spaṣṭayati || 181–2b ||

 

_evam eṣāṃ someṣṭilaukikānāṃ pātrāṇāṃ svalpopaghāte nirlepānāṃ vāriṇā śuddhir iṣyate | salepānāṃ tu |_

 

                    	**carusruksruvasasnehapātrāṇy uṣṇena vāriṇā || 1.182 ||**

 

punar vārigrahaṇaṃ tasyaivauṣṇyaguṇatvajñāpanārtham | tataś ca yasya yac chuddisādhanaṃ, tad eva guṇavikṛtaṃ doṣavikṛtasyety etat siddham | tathā ca yat śaṅkhenoktam, "celānām utsvedanaṃ tanmātrcchedo vā" ity etad api siddhaṃ bhavati | padārthāniruktaṃ ca spaṣṭam anyat || 182 ||

 

_sparśanamātropaghāte nirlepānām eva |_

 

                    	**sphyaśūrpājinadhānyānāṃ musalolūkhalānasām |**

**              	prokṣaṇaṃ saṃhatānāṃ ca bahūnāṃ caiva vāsasām || 1.183 ||**

 

sphyādīni yajñasādhanāni yathā karmaṇi prokṣaṇamātrān naimittikam upaghātaṃ nighnanti, evam evaṃrūpāṇi puruṣārthāny api saṃhatāni śayyādīni, asaṃhatāni ca puruṣavāhyāni vāsāṃsi | caśabdo dhānādyarthaḥ | tathā cāmnāyaḥ: "yad yad evaiṣāṃ mantrāśuddhaś takṣā vāmedhyaḥ kaścit parāhanti, tad tad evaiṣām eva tad adbhir medhyaṃ karoti" iti nimittāntarād amedhyatvaprasaktau medhyatā prokṣaṇena darśayati || 183 ||

 

_alpopaghāta uktam | mahati punaḥ |_

 

                    	**takṣaṇam dāruśṛṅgāsthnāṃ govālaiḥ phalasaṃbhuvām |**

**              	mārjanaṃ yajñapātrāṇāṃ pāṇinā yajñakarmaṇi || 1.184 ||**

 

carvādīnāṃ dāravādīnāṃ caivaṃ śaucam | kecid dīrṇavṛkṣāṇāṃ dārutvasāmānyāt sarjarasādīny api dāravāṇīcchanti | tat punar vicāryam | saṃpūrvād bhavateḥ kvibantāt ṣaṣṭhībahuvacana āmyuvaṅādeśe ca kṛte saṃbhuvām iti rūpam | tāni punar alābupātrādīni | teṣāṃ govālair avagharṣaṇam | salepānāṃ mārjanam | yajñapātrāṇāṃ kṛtaśaucānām eva | pāṇinā yajñakarmaṇīty anyārtham etad: udakavad brāhmaṇapāṇer api śuddhikāraṇatvaṃ yathā syād iti | tataś ca kamaṇḍalvādes tanmārjanāc chuddhiḥ | bhojanakāle ca medhyānām api pātrāṇāṃ parimārjanam | tathā cāmnāyaḥ: "tasmād yadā manuṣyāṇāṃ pariveṣaṇam upakḷptaṃ bhavati | atha pātrāṇi nirṇenijati" iti | athaśabdena śuddhānām eveti dyotayati || 184 ||

 

_upaghātātireka evam |_

 

                    	**soṣair udakagomūtraiḥ śudhyaty āvikasautrikam |**

**              	saśrīphalair aṃśupaṭṭaṃ sāriṣṭaiḥ kutapaṃ tathā || 1.185 ||**

 

āvikaṃ sautrikam ūrṇāmayaṃ, kārpāsaṃ ca | sūtraśabdasya sādhāraṇyāt kauśeyādisaṃgrahaḥ | yat tu "ādityenorṇāmayānām" iti (cf. BDh 1.8.40), tat prāyogikopaghātaviṣayam | yat tu bhāradvājam: "na śaucaṃ śayanāsanakaṭaprastarayānaprastaragaṇḍopadhānakaśipukambhala-kugṛhadhānyamaniphalakaśilāsahasraromṇām anikhātānāṃ ca kāṣṭhānāṃ tṛṇapalāladāmnāṃ kumārāṇām anyatra prokṣaṇād antyasparśane snānaṃ kumārāṇām eke" iti, tat sparśaviṣayam, antyasparśanavacanāt | mūtrādisaṃsarge tu doṣāpekṣayā soṣair udakagomūtrair yathārhaṃ śaucakalpanā | tair evodakagomūtraiḥ sabilvakalkair aṃśupaṭṭānām | aṃśupaṭṭo netrapaṭṭaḥ | kutapaḥ kambaviśeṣaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 185 ||

 

_udakagomūtrair eva |_

 

**              	sagaurasarṣapaiḥ kṣaumaṃ punaḥpākān mahīmayam |**

 

udakagomūtrādhikāre mārttikasyopdeśāt tad api tasyālpopaghāte śuddhisādhanaṃ draṣṭavyam | punaḥśabdāc ca pakvasyaitat | āmaṃ tu pākyaṃ pākāt, apākyaṃ tu bhūśuddhyaiva | doṣātiśaye ca tyāgaḥ | yathāha vasiṣṭhaḥ |

                    	madyamūtrapurīṣaiś ca śleṣmapūyāśruśoṇitaiḥ |

                    	saṃspṛṣṭaṃ naiva śudhyeta punaḥpāken mṛnmayam || iti | (VaDh 3.59)

saṃśabdāc ca madyādiklinnaṃ tyājyam, na vipruṇmātrasparśanāt | punaḥpākena cāśuddhivacanād ādyapākāc śudyaty eva ||

 

_sarvadaivopahataprāyatve 'pi |_

 

                    	**kāruhastaḥ śuciḥ paṇyaṃ bhaikṣaṃ yoṣinmukhaṃ tathā || 1.186 ||**

 

kāruḥ kumbhakārādiḥ | bhaikṣaṃ brahmacāryādigatam | yoṣinmukham asavarṇāyā api | guṇārthaś ca yoṣicchabdaḥ | yathāha śaṅkhaḥ: "kāruhastaḥ śucis tathākarāḥ | taddravyāṇi prokṣitābhyukṣitāni śucīni | ākarajānām abhyavaharaṇīyānāṃ ghṛtenābhighāritānāṃ punaḥpacanam | evaṃ snehānāṃ snehavad dravāṇām" iti | prokṣaṇaṃ prakṣālanam | abhyukṣaṇam uparisecanamātram | punaḥ śucigrahaṇam ākarajatvān nātra duṣṭatvam iti jñāpanārtham | punar ākarajavacanaṃ yāni prāyeṇākarajāny eva kilāṭādīni, tany eva, na tv apūpavyañjanādīnīty evam artham | abhighāritānāṃ pakvānāṃ punaḥpākaḥ | abhighāraṇam evetareṣām | snehānāṃ tu pākamātram | snehavad dravāṇāṃ pākayogyānāṃ madhvādīnām ityādi yojyam || 186 ||

 

_yathāsthānaṃ tu doṣaviśeṣāt |_

 

**              	bhūśuddhir mārjanād dāhāt kālād gokramaṇāt tathā |**

**              	sekād ullekhanāl lepād gṛhaṃ mārjanalepanāt || 1.187 ||**

 

tathāśabdān mṛdantarāvapanāc ca | "āvapanaṃ ca bhūmeḥ" iti gautamaḥ (GDh 1.32) | mārjanaṃ śodhanaṃ, bahūddharaṇam iti yāvat | kālād varṣādibhiḥ, rajasvalādiparigṛhītāv ā tacchudhikālāt | aparigrahe tv āha bhṛguḥ |

                    	upaliptaṃ tu yat sārdhaṃ parikrāntam udakyayā |

                    	śuddhaṃ tac chudhyate yad vā suvarṇasalilokṣitam || iti \

sekaḥ prokṣaṇam | tathā cāha yamaḥ |

                    	gokarṇamātram abbinduḥ punati patataḥ kṣitau |

                    	samūḍham asmūḍḥaṃ vā yatra lepo na dṛśyate || iti |

gṛhaṃ mārjanalepanād anvaham | kuḍyavacano vā gṛhaśabdaḥ, anyatra bhūśuddhyaivoktatvāt || 187 ||

 

_anabhyavahārya uktam | abhyavahārye tu |_

 

                    	**goghrāte 'nne tathā keśamakṣikākīṭadūṣite |**

**              	salilaṃ bhasma mṛd vāpi prakṣeptavyaṃ viśuddhaye || 1.188 ||**

 

_annādhikārāt taducchiṣṭalepopahatānām |_

 

                    	**trapusīsakatāmrāṇāṃ kṣārāmlodakavāribhiḥ |**

**              	bhasmanā kāṃsyalohānāṃ śuddhiḥ plāvo dravasya tu || 1.189 ||**

 

tuśabdād anyatrāpy alpopaghāte dravyasyāyaṃ śaucavidhiḥ || 189 ||

 

_mūtrapurīṣādibhis tu |_

 

                    	**amedhyāktasya mṛttoyaiḥ śuddhir gandhāpakarṣaṇam |**

**              	vākśastam ambunirṇiktam ajñātaṃ ca sadā śuci || 1.190 ||**

 

sarvadravyāṇām ayaṃ śaucakalpaḥ | gandhavacanān nirgandhaśleṣmādyupaghāte 'dbhir eva lepāpakarṣaṇam iti kecit | tat punar vācyam | yathāha manuḥ |

                    	yāvan nāpaity amedhyāktād gandho lepaś ca tatkṛtaḥ |

                    	tāvan mṛd vāri cādeyaṃ sarvāsu dravyaśuddhiṣu || iti | (MDh 5.126)
