yat punaḥ śaṅkhenoktam: "taijasānāṃ kuṇaparetomūtrapurīṣopahatānām āvartanam ullekhanaṃ bhasmanā vā triḥsaptakṛtvaḥ parimārjanam" iti, tad gandhādyapakarṣaṇāśaktau draṣṭavyam | bhasmanāpy apakṛṣṭagandhānām evāvirodhāt, parimārjanaṃ śuṣkāmedhyopaghāta eva | iyaṃ tu sarvasādhāraṇadravyaśuddhiviṣayakalpanā: yad viśiṣṭapramāṇena duṣṭam ity ajñātaṃ, yac ca hṛdvilekhe sati śobhanam evaitad iti vākśastam udakena vā prakṣālitaṃ prokṣitaṃ vā, tat sadā nirvicikitsaṃ śuddham evety avaseyam || 190 ||

 

_evam āpaḥ śuddhikāraṇatvenoktāḥ | tāsāṃ punar iyaṃ śuddhiḥ |_

** **

**              	śuci gotṛptikṛt toyaṃ prakṛtisthaṃ mahīgatam |**

**              	tathā māṃsaṃ śvacaṇḍālakravyādādinipātitam || 1.191 ||**

 

avagāhanādikṣamaṃ gotṛptikṛt kecid icchanti | tat tv ayuktam, "pradarād api yā gos tarpaṇāḥ śyuḥ" iti vasiṣṭhavacanāt (VaDh 3.35) | prakṛtisthaṃ gandhavarṇarasāgamādyaduṣṭam | sarvathā bhūmigatatve 'pi medhyam | tathā cāmnāyaḥ: "vāg vai devebhyo 'pākrāmat | sā āpaḥ prāviśat | te devā adbhyo vācam aicchan | tān āpo 'bruvan: 'yad asmākaṃ prajābhyo yad anyajebhyo 'śubhaṃ tat pāvayadhvaṃ, tato vācaṃ dāsyāma' iti | tatheti devāḥ prāhuḥ" ity upakramya, "yo hy ādityaḥ sa brahmayajñaḥ sarvā devatāḥ savitā anvahaṃ brahmayajñapūtābhī raśmibhiḥ pāvayet | tasmād evāhani śuddhāḥ śuddhyai kalpyante | tasmād yad yan mīmāṃsyaṃ syāt, tat tad adbhiḥ spṛśet, śucy eva bhavati | rātrau varuṇaṃ prāviśat | tasmān na rātrau gṛhṇīyāt | dhāmno dhāmna iti vāgniṃ vopariṣṭād gṛhṇīyāt" iti | na ca karpūrādivikāre 'pi doṣaḥ, "gandhādiduṣṭābhiḥ" (cf. VaDh 3.36) iti duṣṭatvavacanāt | tathāśabdān māṃsam api prakṛtistham eva medhyam | ataś ca caṇḍālādyupaghāte nipātitasya doṣa evety avaseyam || 191 ||

 

_yathā copaghātāśaṅkāyām apy udakaṃ medhyaṃ, tathaitāny api |_

 

**              	raśmir agnī rajaś chāyā gaur aśvo vasudhānilaḥ |**

**              	vipruṣo makṣikāḥ sparśe vatsaḥ prasnāvane śuciḥ || 1.192 ||**

 

ādityaraśmayo 'gnir vātodbhūtaṃ rajaś caṇḍālādiśarīracchāyā gāvo 'śvā bhūmir vāyus tadīritāś cāspṣṭāḥ sarvato vipruṣo makṣikāś cāśucisevinyaḥ sparśe medhyāḥ | prasnāvane ca mātur vatsamukhaṃ medhyam | vatsagrahaṇaṃ ca sarvaprasnāvakopalakṣaṇārthaṃ, nyāyasāmyāt | sarvathā śāstram amīmāṃsyaṃ yataḥ || 192 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> gavāśvayor medhyatvavacān mahiṣyādāv aśuddhatvaprasaṅgaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span> | guṇārtham etad na parisaṅkhyārtham | ko guṇa iti, ucyate |_

 

                    	**ajāśvaṃ mukhato medhyaṃ na gaur na nakhajā malāḥ |**

**              	panthānaś ca viśudhyanti somasūryāṃśumārutaiḥ || 1.193 ||**

 

caśabdād anyad apy evaṃrūpaṃ somādisparśanāc chudhyaty eva | tathā ca mantravarṇaḥ: "agniḥ pavitraṃ sa mā punātu vāyuḥ somaḥ sūrya indraḥ" iti (ĀpŚr 12.20.6) | ataś ca yasyaivānyac chaucaṃ noktaṃ, tasyaivaitad iti śāstrasaṃkṣepaḥ || 193 ||

 

_amedhyatvaśaṅkāyām api hi |_

 

**              	mukhajā vipruṣo medhyāḥ parācamanabindavaḥ |**

**              	śmaśru cāsyagataṃ dantasaktaṃ tyaktvā tataḥ śuciḥ || 1.194 ||**

 

vipruṣāṃ punarvacanaṃ sākṣātkāreṇa dauṣṭyāvagatāv anyatrāmedhyā eveti jñāpanārtham | gautamīyaṃ ca "na ced aṅge nipatanti" (GDh 1.41) iti parakīyaviṣayam | idaṃ cātmīyārtham iti bhedaḥ | spaṣṭopalabdhau tv ātmīyeṣv api doṣa eva | parācamabindavaś ca medhyāḥ | tathāha vasiṣṭha |

                    	parān athācāyayataḥ pādau yā vipruṣo gatāḥ |

                    	bhūmisthais tu samā jñeyāḥ | iti | (VaDh 3.42)

etasmād eva cānyāvarjitenāpy ācamanasiddhiḥ | tathā ca āpastambaḥ: "yaṃ vā prayatas tv ācāmayati" iti (ĀpDh 1.15.3) | śmaśru cāsyagataṃ medhyam | caśabdāt śmaśrugataś ca lepaḥ, "na śmaśrugato lepaḥ" iti vasiṣṭhavacanāt (VaDh 3.40) | śmaśrugatatvaśruteś cāpakarṣaṇāśaktāv eva | dantaśliṣṭaṃ tyaktvā tataḥ śuciḥ nigiraṃś ca | yasyācamanakāle prayatnato 'nupalambhaḥ, tataḥ paścān nigīrya tyaktvā vā tenaivācamanena śuddha ity avaseyam | atraiva pradeśe kecid imaṃ śokaṃ paṭhanti |

                    	rathyākardamatoyāni spṛṣṭāny antyaśvavāyasaiḥ

                    	mārutenaiva śudhyanti pakveṣṭakācitāni ca || iti | (= YDh 1.195 in cr. ed.)

tat punaḥ pūrveṇaiva gatatvād akiṃcit || 194 ||

 

_pūrvasmād evācamanāc chiddir uktā | na ca tad anyatrācamanam upadiṣṭam ity adhunaivopadeṣṭum āha |_

 

                    	**snātvā pītvā kṣute supte bhuktvā rathyāprasarpaṇe |**

**              	ācāntaḥ punar ācāmed vāso viparidhāya ca || 1.195 ||**

 

ācānta ity upadeśāt snānādinimitteṣv anyeṣu cocchiṣṭasparśanādiṣu smṛtyantarānusārād anyad ācamanavidhāyakaṃ kalpanīyam | tadvaśāc cācāntaḥ snānādiṣu punar ācāmed ity eṣa ślokaviṣayaḥ | ataś cānyatra sakṛdācamanam eva | rathyāprasarpaṇa iti praśabdād anupāntkasyaivācamanaṃ, na sarvatra | vāsasaś ca viparivarta evācamanaṃ, na ślathitasamādhāne | kecit tv ādyantayor ācamanam icchanti | tat punar vicāryam | spaṣṭam anyat | ayaṃ tv atra saṃpradāyaḥ: kātyasyācamanavidher vicitraprakāratvam, ācamanasya śaucāśubhakṣapaṇādyarthatvāt | tathā hi |

                    	mūtradyutsarjane śaucaṃ yajñādau karmasādhanam |

                    	kṣute naimittikaṃ śuktabhāṣaṇe pāpanāśanam ||

                    	jāhnavyādau ca dharmāya prasthānādau ca siddhaye |

                    	krūradṛṣyekṣaṇe kṣuṇṇalakṣaṇadyapanuttaye ||

                    	smṛtyantarāt samācārād āmnāyāc caivamādibhiḥ |

                    	prakārais tad vivektavyaṃ sadā tattvabubhutsubhiḥ ||

tatra śaucārthācamanārhaspṛṣṭitatspṛṣṭinor apy ācamanam eva śaucam | parasya tv adoṣaḥ | tathā ca smaranti |

                    	ucchiṣṭena tu saṃspṛṣṭa eka eva sa duṣyati |

                    	taṃ spṛṣṭvānyo na duṣyeta sarvadravyeṣv ayaṃ vidhiḥ || iti |

acetanasya tu dravyasya prokṣaṇam | yathāha śaṅkhaḥ: "dravyahasta ucchiṣṭo nidhāyācāmet | adbhir abhyukṣya dravyaṃ śudhyati" iti | śrutiś coktaiva: "yad yan mīmāṃsyaṃ syāt tat tad adbhiḥ spṛśet" iti | ucchiṣṭācetanadravyaspṛṣṭisparśe tv adoṣaḥ, "sarvadravyeṣv ayaṃ vidhiḥ" iti vacanāt | apuruṣaprāṇināṃ tu nirdoṣataiva | etenaiva snānavaicitryaṃ prapañcanīyam | iyāṃs tu viśeṣaḥ: śaucārthatve 'pi dvaividhyam, maithunyudakyādibhedāt | udakyādispṛṣṭitatspṛṣṭinor api snānaṃ dravyasya ca prakṣālanam | maithunyādau tv ācamanaprokṣaṇe | yac ca dravyaṃ mānuṣaṃ vā snānakṣālanakṣamaṃ, tasyaivaitat | tadvināśinas tv ācamanaprokṣaṇe evāturapustakādeḥ | yathāha baudhāyanaḥ |

                    	deśaṃ kālaṃ tathātmānaṃ dravyaṃ dravyaprayojanam |

                    	upapattim avasthāṃ ca jñātvā śaucaṃ prakalpayet || iti || (BDh 1.8.53)

ayaṃ cātra paramārthaḥ | asyaiva smṛtyantareṣu prapañcanamātram | yathāha manuḥ: "śaucaṃ yathārhaṃ kāryam" iti (MDh 5.114) | taijasaviśeṣaśaucārthatve 'pi sarvārtham evaitat | evaṃ caṇḍālādisaṃkare sarvadravyaprakṣālanaprāptau viśeṣaḥ: taijasānāṃ bhasmanā triḥsaptakṛtvaḥ parimārjanam | sakṛdbhuktānām ullekhanaṃ, cirabhuktānām āvartanam | evaṃ mūtralaśunaśūdrabhogādiṣv api yojyam | mārttikānāṃ tu caṇḍālalaśunādisparśane punaḥpākaḥ | mūtrādyupaghāte caṇḍālādibhoge ca tyāgaḥ | kākādibhir layane paryagnikaraṇam | tatpurīṣādyupaghāte punaḥpākaḥ | evaṃ dāravāṇāṃ prakṣālanaprokṣaṇaparigharṣaṇollekhanatakṣaṇatyāgādi yojyam | tāntavānāṃ tu caṇḍālādisaṃkare 'lpānāṃ prakṣālanaṃ, sakṛdbhuktānāṃ tuṣādibhir yathārhaṃ mṛdbhir adbhiś ca | laśunādyupahatānāṃ mūtrādivyāptānāṃ tv apanayanāśaktau tanmātrachedaḥ | paiṣṭyādivyāptau caṇḍālādicirabhuktānāṃ ca tyāga eva | vaivarṇye tūtsvedanam | sarvadravyāṇāṃ tu svaṃ svaṃ varṇam utpādya mṛdbir adbhiś ca kṣālanam | abjopalāsthidantamaṇimayānāṃ skṛcchūdrādibhuktānāṃ laśunādisparśe vā parimārjitānām udakagomūtrābhyāṃ kṣālanaṃ, cirabhuktānāṃ tu tyāgaḥ | mahārhaṃ tu atyājyam eva, "amedhyād api kāñcanam" (MDh 2.239) ity upanyāsāt | uktaṃ ca "deśaṃ kālam" (BDh 1.8.53) iti, "mṛttoyaiḥ śodhyate śodhyam" (MDh 5.108) iti ca mānavam | sarvatrānādiṣṭaśauce lepasadasadbhāvāpekṣayā yathārhaṃ kalpanīyam | bahūnāṃ tu dhānyavāsasāṃ śayanādīnāṃ ca caṇḍālādisaṃkare prokṣaṇam | yasya ca snānārhasparśane prokṣaṇaṃ, tasya cocchiṣṭasparśane na kiṃcit | caṇḍālādyāhṛtānāṃ tṛṇakāṣṭhaśuṣkagomayamūlaphalādīnāṃ prokṣaṇam | aprokṣitasprśane tu snānam eva | ārdragomayādes tu śuṣkasya suvarṇodakaprokṣitasya vā śuddhiḥ | mūtrādyupaghāte tu dhānyānāṃ tatsaṃspṛṣṭaṃ tyaktvā paryagnikaraṇādibhiḥ śeṣaśuddhiḥ | śuṣkapurīṣādyaniyatasaṃsarge cāpastamboktaṃ vrīhīṇāṃ prakṣālyāvaśoṣaṇaṃ taṇḍulānām tu tyāgaḥ iti | rasānāṃ tu pātradoṣe pātrāntaropanayanotpavane | laśunādisaṃsarge tūddhṛtya plāvanam abhakṣyānupapatanīyarasasaṃsargāśaṅkāyāṃ pākyasya kvāthanam, āplāvyānyasmin suvarṇādiprakṣepaḥ | tailasarpṣī ucchiṣṭasamanvārabdhe udake 'vadhāyopayojayed iti | etac chvakākādyupghāte 'pi droṣāḍhakāvasecanasamarthānāṃ vijñeyam | kūpādīnām uddhṛtadoṣāṇāṃ hiraṇyādiprakṣepaḥ | pulkasādyutpāditalavaṇāṇāṃ madhunaś ca bhūnikṣepaṇāt | tattyāgenaiva śuddhiḥ sarvadravyāṇāṃ ca,

                    	amedhyatāṃ gataṃ dravyaṃ yad amedhyaparigrahāt |

                    	ātyantikaprahāṇena tat tasmāc chiddhim āpnuyāt ||

iti smṛtyantarāt | sarvasya ca dravyasyātyalpasya tyāg eva | pakvānnānāṃ tūcchiṣṭasparśe 'lpānām api prokṣaṇaṃ, "pracarann abhyavahāryeṣu" iti vasiṣṭhavacanāt (VaDh 3.43) | śūdrocchiṣṭasparśe 'pi, udakyāspṛṣṭasyābhakṣyatvopadeśāt | laśunādisparśe tu svalpam uddhṛtyānyasya dhānyavat saṃskāraḥ, alpasya tu tyāga eva | śvakākādyavalīḍhe tu prāg droṇāḍhakāt tyāgaḥ | tadākrameṇa tu sākṣāt spṛṣṭam uddhṛtya śiṣṭasya dhānyavat saṃskāraḥ | gṛhītānnasya mūtrādikaraṇe pūrvavat saṃskāraḥ | śūdraś ced gṛhītānna ucchiṣṭaḥ syāt, saṃskṛtya kūśmāṇḍībhiḥ prokṣaṇam | sarvānnadoṣeṣu ca sāvitryāṣṭaśatenābhimantrya saṃskṛtyopayogaḥ | sarvatra "deśaṃ kālam" ity ālocyam | yatra ca hṛdvilekhaḥ syāt tat tyājyam eva, ātmatuṣṭer api śaucakāraṇatvāt | śuṣkavaṭakādīnāṃ tu tanmātratyāgaḥ | atyantāśucisaṃpṛktānāṃ tyāgaḥ | pātropaghāte tv annasyāpi, rasavat | caṇḍālādisaṃkare tu pakvānnasya tyāga eva | celavad rajjuvidalacarmaṇāṃ tanmātracchedādi | kukuṇṭhādicarmaṇāṃ tu rañjanaṃ mūtrādisaṃsarge | sarvatrāsmād eva cārañjitair na vyavahāraḥ | upānacchaucaṃ tu mṛttoyenaiva yathārham | etad api śaṅkhoktaṃ draṣṭavyaṃ "mṛdbhasmagomūtrakṣārodakaiś celānāṃ celavad dhānyānāṃ pakṣmacāmaracarmatṛṇavālavetravalkalādīnām" ityādi | ādigrahaṇaṃ kutapādyartham | tṛṇaśabdena ca tālapatrasyāpi grahaṇaṃ, tṛṇarājatvāt tatrāpi tṛṇaśabdo yataḥ | caṇḍālādyanvārabdhanikhātakāṣṭhasparśe ca na kiṃcit | yathāha āpastambaḥ: "mūḍhaprastare ca saṃspṛśaṇn anyān aprayatān prayato manyeta | tathā tṛṇakāṣṭheṣu nikhāteṣu" iti (ĀpDh 1.15.13–14) | "anekoddhārye kāṣṭhśile bhūmisame" iti ca vṛddhagārgyaḥ | gṛhasaṃlagnakavāṭakaṭaniḥśreṇyādīni ca, tathāśabdāt | kecit tu niḥśreṇyāḥ prokṣaṇam icchanti | tac ca vṛddhagārgyavacanād ayuktam | mṛdiṣṭakākardamāṇāṃ sarvayantrāṇāṃ cādityadarśanād ity eṣā dik | sarvatra "yad evānūcānā vidvāṃso brāhmaṇā brūhuḥ, tac chaucam ādriyeta" iti smṛtyantarāc chaucaṃ brāhmaṇavacanam evety alam abhidhānena | sarvatra cātra mūlabhūtavākyānupanyāso granthātirekabhītyā | pradarśanārthaṃ tu katipayāny upanyasyante | yathāha hārītaḥ: "yathārthaṃ śaucam adbhiḥ kāñcanarajataśaṅkhaśuktyādīnāṃ tadguṇavarṇayogāt snehato varṇopahatānāṃ yavagodhūmamāṣakalāyamasūracūrṇair mārjanam adbhiḥ prakṣālanaṃ ca | amlalavaṇābhyāṃ tāmrāṇāṃ, bhasmanā kāṃsyānāṃ, śailatailāvagharṣaṇaiḥ kārṣṇāyasānāṃ, śailāvagharṣaṇamārjanair maṇimayānāṃ, sikatāvagharṣaṇaiḥ śailānāṃ salepānāṃ, nirlekhanam dārumayānāṃ, niṣṭapanam eva mārttikānāṃ, govālarajjvā sodakayā phalamayānāṃ, kṣāroṣṇodakābhyāṃ kārpāsaśaṇamayānāṃ, putrañjīvāriṣṭakaiḥ kṣaumadukūlānāṃ, putrañjīvodaśvidbhyāṃ cājinānāṃ, śrīphalaśvetasarṣapakalkaiḥ kauśeyānām, udaśvidvalmīkamṛdā sarṣapaiś corṇāmayānāṃ, snehasaktukulmāṣonmardanair gurūṇām ūrṇāmayānām atyantopahatānāṃ sarvataijasānām agninā śaucam | mṛddārucarmaṇāṃ tyāgaḥ | tanmātracchedanam eke vāsasām | na vā sādhāraṇatvāt | "sādhāraṇaṃ hi vāsa" ity ācāryāḥ | tasmāt sarvavāsasām upaghātāpanodanād eva śuddhiḥ | celavac carmaṇāṃ śuddhiḥ | dṛtīnāṃ rañjanaṃ, payasā dāntānāṃ, krītānāṃ paryagnikaraṇaprokṣaṇaiḥ payaādīnāṃ, dadhyādīnām prokṣaṇaṃ, paryagnikaraṇāvahananair vrīheḥ, yavagodhūmānāṃ prokṣaṇaṃ, phalīkṛtānāṃ vimarśanam, avagharṣaṇadalanapeṣaṇaiḥ śamīdhānyānāṃ, vimarśanaprakṣālanaiḥ śākamūlaphalānāṃ bhūsthānāṃ, grahaṇād abhūsthānāṃ, takṣaṇaprakṣālanair ikṣukāṇḍānāṃ, svavidhānād yajñadravahaviṣām, uṣṇena vāriṇā sruvāṇāṃ, carūṇāṃ ca śrapaṇam eva | snehānāṃ kṛtalavaṇānāṃ pulkasādispṛṣṭānāṃ bhūsthānāṃ tṛṇakāṣṭhānām ādityadarśanāt | evam iṣṭakānāṃ ca śakalīkṛtānāṃ sparśanāniṣṭagandhopaghrāṇaśravaṇadarśanodāharaṇeṣu ca | keśapipīlikādibhir annopaghāte kāñcanarajatabhasmatāmravajravaiḍūryagovālājinadarbhāṇām anyatamenādbhiḥ saṃspṛṣṭena śuddhaṃ bhavati | mantraprokṣaṇaparyagnikaraṇādityadarśanaiḥ śaucaṃ bahvannopaghāte, brāhmaṇānumatād vā, tanmātram apanīyājenopaghrāpya śuddhaṃ bhavati | atyantopahatānāṃ tyāgaḥ, rasamayānāṃ ca | bhūsthā āpaḥ puṇyā aśubhāgamavarjam | tathāpi ca brāhmaṇaṃ bhavati: "devānāṃ vāg apākrāmat" ityādi | athāpy atrodāharanti |

                    	śodhitānāṃ tu pātrāṇaṃ yady ekam upahanyate |

                    	tasya pātrasya tac chaucaṃ netareṣāṃ kathaṃcana || iti |

                    	vatsaḥ prasnāvane medhyaḥ śvā mṛgagrahaṇe śuciḥ |

                    	ākarāḥ śucayaḥ sarve śakuniḥ phalaśātane || (MDh 5.130)

tathā |

                    	gobhir ākramaṇād dāhāt khananād abhivarṣaṇāt |

                    	mārjanāḷ lepanāt kālād bhūmir etair viśudhyati || iti |

na caṇḍālopahatā bhūḥ snānārhāprāyatyaṃ janayati | yasmād āha |

                    	makṣikā vipruṣo nāryo bhūmis toyaṃ hutāśanaḥ |

                    	mārjāraś caiva darvī ca mārutaś ca sadā śuciḥ |

                    	yathāśubhaugho nadisaṃśrito (?) vahan

                                	nadīguṇais tadguṇabhāvayuktaḥ |

                    	tathānnapānaṃ vidhipūrvam āgataṃ

                                	dvijātipātrāntaritaṃ na duṣyati || iti |

smṛtyantarāṇy evam udāhāryāṇi vivektavyāni cety alaṃ prasaṅgena |

                    	mayā nirukātra padārthaśuddhiḥ

                                	prāyeṇa lokasya hitaiṣiṇeyam |

                    	śraddheyamārgaiva yatas tataś ca

                                	prapañcanīyā bahubhiḥ sudhībhiḥ || 195 ||

 

**iti dravyaśuddhiprakaraṇam**

** **

**atha dānaprakaraṇam**

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> iyaṃ katipayadravyāśritaiva śuddhir uktā | anantas tu tadviṣayaḥ | sa katham ivānukto vijñeyaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">uktam</span> evaitat pariṣacchloke: yad vādhyātmavid eko 'pi brāhmaṇo brūyāt, sa nirvicikitsaḥ sarvathā dharma iti _(cf. YDh 1.9) _| api ca |_

 

                    	**tapas taptvāsṛjad brahmā brāhmaṇān vedaguptaye |**

**              	tṛptyarthaṃ pitṛdevānāṃ dharmasaṃrakṣaṇāya ca || 1.196 ||**

 

evaṃ ca vedaguptir dharmasaṃrakṣaṇaṃ ca bhavati, yadi sarvathā sa vedārtham adhigacchet | sṛṣṭyādivacanaṃ ca kāraṇānusārāt kāryasya sāmarthyātirekaprāptyartham || 196 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evam api jñātaiva brāhmaṇaḥ sa kadācin na brūyad apīty ata āha |_

 

                    	**sarvasya prabhavo viprāḥ śrutādhyayanaśīlinaḥ |**

**              	tebhyaḥ kriyāparā śreṣṭhās tebhyo hy adhyātmacintakāḥ || 1.197 ||**

 

sarvasyaiva jagataḥ svāmino viprāḥ | te ca dharmopadeśadvāreṇaiva svāmino nānyathā | tathā cāha manuḥ |

                    	sarveṣāṃ brāhmaṇo vidyād vṛttyupāyān yathāvidhi |

                    	prabrūyād itarebhyaś ca svayaṃ caiva tathā bhavet || iti | (MDh 10.2)

kiṃ jāter evāitan (?) māhātmyam | nety ucyate, śrutādhyayanaśīlina eveti anyeṣām anupadeṣṭṛtvāt | tebhyaḥ kriyāparā ityādi mānyaśloke vyākhyātam eva || 117 ||

 

_kasmāc caivam uttarottaraśraiṣṭhyam | yasmāt |_

 

**              	na vidyayā kevalayā tapasā vāpi pātratā |**

**              	yatra vṛttam ime cobhe tad dhi pātraṃ prakīrtitam || 1.198 ||**

 

tapaḥśabdena cātra sṛṣṭyanusārāj jātir evocyate, anyathā kṣatriyāder api mānyatvaprasaṅgāt | ato yatra vidyātapasī vṛttaṃ cānuṣṭhānaṃ, tat pātraṃ dānādisādhanam | yasmāc ca tat sarvaṃ brahmavidi, vairāgyādiguṇātirekaś ca, tasmāt tasyaiva sarvaśraiṣṭhyam | yad vā svārtha eva tapaḥśabdaḥ | caśabdād upakramāc ca jātyupādānam || 198 ||

 

_yasmāc caivaṃrūpo brāhmaṇaḥ pātṛtvāj jagataḥ pātraṃ, tasmāt |_

 

**              	gobhūtilahiraṇyādi pātre dātavyam arcitam |**

**              	nāpātre viduṣā kiṃcid ātmanaḥ śreya icchatā || 1.199 ||**

 

pātre pātari | arcitaṃ sarvam eva dadyāt | āha ca: "yo 'rcitaṃ pratigṛhṇīyāt" iti (MDh 4.235) | apātari tv ātmanaḥ śreya icchan na kiṃcit dadyāt | ādigrahaṇād bhojanādy api | bhojanādi cādhyātmavido 'pi gṛhṇanty eva | ataś ca teṣāṃ ca saṃpradānatvasiddhiḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca brāhmaṇo na parīkṣitavyaḥ, parīkṣāyāṃ vedavikrayaśravaṇāt | anyathā ca jñānānupapatteḥ kathaṃ pātrāvagatiḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | laukika evātrābhyupāyaḥ || 199 ||

 

_kiṃ ca, yady asau pratigṛhṇīyāt taddoṣāyāpekṣāpi prasajyeta | tasya tv anadhikāra eva | yataḥ |_

 

**              	vidyātapobhyāṃ hīnena na tu grāhyāḥ pratigrahaḥ |**

 

_yasmāt |_

 

**              	gṛhṇan pradātāram adho nayaty ātmānam eva ca || 1.200 ||**

 

tuśabdo 'vadhāraṇārthaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 200 ||

 

_yasmāc caivaiṃ, tasmāt |_

 

**              	dātavyaṃ pratyahaṃ pātre nimitteṣu viśeṣataḥ |**

**              	yācitenāpi dātavyaṃ śraddhāpūtaṃ tu śaktitaḥ || 1.201 ||**

 

pratyaham evāyācitam upanīya pātre dadyāt | tathā cāmnāyaḥ: "ahar ahar dadyād odapātrādi" ityādi (ŚB 11.5.6.2) | tathā "hiraṇyam ādāyāgnīdhram abhyeti" ity upanīya dānaṃ darśayati | tathā "yo vai jñāto jñātakulīnaḥ sa pitṛmān paitṛmatyaḥ" ity upakrama "yo vai jñātāyāpi katipayīr dakṣiṇā dadāti, tābhir mahar jayati" iti pātra eva dānaṃ darśayati | nimitteṣu grahoparāgādiṣu | viśeṣato bahutaram | deyam ayācitenaiva | kiṃ ca, yācitenāpi dātavyaṃ sāṃtānikādibhyo daśabhyaḥ śnātakebhyaḥ | na ca yācitatvād evāvajñā kāryā | kiṃ tarhi śraddhāpūtam evādareṇa deyaṃ, śaktitaś ca, ātmavittānusārāt tadguṇānusārāc ca | tathā cāha manuḥ: "daśaitān snātakān vidyāt" iti (MDh 11.2) || 201 ||

 

_gavādīnāṃ deyatvam uktam | tatprakārapapañcāyāha |_

 

                    	**svarṇaśṛṅgī śaphai raupyaiḥ suśīlā vastrasaṃyutā |**

**              	sakāṃsyadohā dātavyā kṣīriṇī gauḥ sadakṣiṇā || 1.202 ||**

 

satkṛtā dakṣiṇā sadakṣiṇā | dakṣiṇāśabdāc ca hiraṇyabāhulyaṃ kāryam || 202 ||

 

_na cāyaṃ nityadānaprakāra eva | kiṃ tarhi |_

 

**              	dātāsyāḥ svargam āpnoti vatsarān romasaṃmitān |**

**              	kapilā cet tārayati bhūyaś cāsaptamaṃ kulam || 1.203 ||**

 

anenaiva vidhinā dīyamānā viśeṣataḥ | nitye 'pi cāyam eva prakāraḥ, anyānupadeśād apekṣitatvāc ca | evam anyatrāpi yojyam | yad vā nimitteṣu viśeṣataḥ iti yad uktam, ayaṃ sa viśeṣo 'bhihitaḥ | nityaṃ tu yathārhaṃ satkṛtya dadyād ity avaseyam || 203 ||

 

_akapilā vā |_

 

**              	savatsāromatulyāni yugāny ubhayatomukhīm |**

**              	dātā svargam avāpnoti pūrveṇa vidhinā dadat || 1.204 ||**

 

saha vatsena yāvanti romāṇi, tāvanti yugāni varṣāṇi | ubhayatomukhīṃ soṣyantīṃ nirgatavatsamukhīm | pūrveṇa hemaśṛṅgādividhinā (YDh 1.202) | dadad dātā svargam āpnotīti yojyam | tathā ca "aditir asy ubhayataḥ śīrṣṇī" (TS 1.2.4.2) iti mantravarṇaḥ || 204 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvad uktaḥ prakāraḥ | tad asambhave 'pi |_


    **yathākathaṃcid dattvā gāṃ dhenuṃ vādhenum eva vā |**


    **arogām aparikliṣṭāṃ dātā svargam avāpnuyāt || 1.205 ||**

spaṣṭārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 205 ||

_yasya tu gomātram api nāsti tasyāpi_ |

                    	**śrāntasaṃvāhanaṃ rogiparicaryā surārcanam |**

**              	pādaśaucaṃ dvijocchiṣṭamārjanaṃ gopradānavat || 1.206 ||**

 

nigadoktaḥ ślokaḥ || 206 ||

 

_yathāsambhavam eva ca |_

 

**              	bhūmipaśvannavastrāmbhastilasarpiḥpratiśrayam |**

**              	naiveśikaṃ svarṇadhuryaṃ dattvā svarge mahīyate || 1.207 ||**

 

naiveśikaṃ vivāhārthaṃ dhanaṃ, kanyā vā | dhuryo 'naḍvān | ṛjv anyat || 207 ||

 

_vittānusārād eva ca |_

 

**              	gṛhadhānyābhayopānacchatramālyānulepanam |**

**              	yānaṃ vṛkṣajalaṃ śayyāṃ dattvātyantaṃ sukhī bhavet || 1.208 ||**

 

yānaṃ gantryādi | vṛkṣasekārhaṃ jalaṃ vṛkṣajalam | spaṣṭam anyat | sarvatra cāsmin prakaraṇe dātur vittānusārāt phalaviśeṣakalpanā | yathā coktam: "nāyaṃ yajñaḥ saktuprasthatulyaḥ" iti | āmnāyaś cokta eva: "yo vai jñātāyāpi katipayīḥ" ityādiḥ (cf. YDh 1.201 com.) | bāhyavittānusārī cātireko brāhmaṇādyarthe svaprāṇapaṇenābhayapradānādeḥ | āmnyāyaś ca: "tasmād yady api sarvajyānīma jīyeta ātmanā cec jīvati pravināśād ity āhuḥ" (?) ity aprādhānyaṃ vittasya darśayati | evaṃ sarvatra vivekakalpanā || 208 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvad vibhavavataḥ sarvasādhāraṇo dānadharma uktaḥ | yas tu khalu vidvān brāhmaṇaḥ, tasya |_

 

**              	sarvadharmamayaṃ brahma pradānebhyo 'dhikaṃ tataḥ |**

**              	pradadat tat samāpnoti brahmalokam avicyutaḥ || 1.209 ||**

 

spaṣṭārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 209 ||

 

_evaṃ ca sati |_

 

**              	pratigrahasamartho 'pi nādatte yaḥ pratigraham |**

**              	ye lokā dānaśīlānāṃ sa tān āpnoti puṣkalān || 1.210 ||**

 

brahmapradānenaivety arthaḥ | tasmān na dāsyāmīti pratigṛhṇīyāt | tathā ca laukikāḥ |

                    	prakṣālanād dhi paṅkasya dūrād asparśanaṃ varam | iti |

ataś ca pratigrahanivṛttir eva jyāyasīty avaseyam || 210 ||

 

_nivṛttenāpi ca |_

 

**              	kuśāḥ śākaṃ payo matsyā gandhāḥ puṣpaṃ dadhi kṣitiḥ |**

**              	māṃsaṃ śayyāsanaṃ dhānyaṃ pratyākhyeyaṃ na vāri ca || 1.211 ||**

 

nigadoktaḥ ślokaḥ || 211 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvac chākādyapraṇodyam iti sthitam | hiraṇyādy api |_

 

**              	ayācitāhṛtaṃ grāhyam api duṣkṛtakarmaṇaḥ |**

**              	anyatra kulaṭāṣaṇḍapatitebhyas tathā dviṣaḥ || 1.212 ||**

 

kulāny aṭatīti kulaṭā duṣāriṇī | tathāśabdād dveṣyaś ca, apratigrāhyaprakārārtho vā | tathānye 'pi ṣaṇḍasadṛśā anadhikṛtāḥ śūdrādayaḥ | yat tu gautamīyam: "tena cottaras tadartho 'sya nicayaḥ" (GDh 10.62–63) iti, tad āśritaśūdraviṣayaṃ draṣṭavyam | dānāyaivaiṣāṃ sthityatiriktavittasaṃgrahādhikāro 'pi | tadartho 'sya nicaya ity anenāpy etad evokam ity avaseyam || 212 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvad ayācitāhṛtagrahaṇam uktam | yācitvāpi tu |_

 

**              	surātithyarcanakṛte gurubhṛtyārtham eva ca |**

**              	sarvataḥ pratigṛhṇīyād ātmavṛttyartham eva ca || 1.213 ||**

 

sarvaśabdaḥ pūrvaślokānusārād evāyam akulaṭādiṣu draṣṭavyaḥ | yat punar vāsiṣṭhaḥ |

                    	gurvarthe dāram ujjihīrṣann arciṣyan devatātithīn |

                    	sarvataḥ pratigṛhṇīyān na tu tṛpyet svayaṃ tataḥ || (VaDh 14.13)

iti, tat kulaṭādiṣu pratiprasavārtham | tathā ca tatraiva "udakādy eṣām api pratigṛhṇīyāt" iti (VaDh 14.12) | anena sarvanāmnaita eva parāmṛśyante | prāṇasaṃrakṣaṇārthaṃ caitad, na punarbhogārtham ityādivivekaḥ prapañcanīyaḥ || 213 ||

 

**iti dānaprakaraṇam**

** **

**atha śrāddhaprakaraṇam**

 

nimitteṣu viśeṣato dānam uktam | kāni punas tāni nimittānīty ata āha |

 

**              	amāvāsyāṣṭakā vṛddhiḥ kṛṣṇapakṣo 'yanadvayam |**

**              	dravyabrāhmaṇasaṃpattir viṣuvat sūryasaṃkramaḥ || 1.214 ||**

**              	vyatīpāto gajacchāyā grahaṇaṃ candrasūryayoḥ |**

**              	śrāddhaṃ prati ruciś caiva śrāddhakālāḥ prakīrtitāḥ || 1.215 ||**

 

amāvāsyāṣṭakayoḥ kṛṣṇapakṣāntargatatve 'pi bhedenopādānam ādarātirekārtham | evaṃ sūryasaṃkramaviṣuvāyanādīnāṃ vacanāni yojyāni | dravyaṃ vārdhrāṇasādi śrāddhārtham, ubhatomukhyādi dānārtham | brāhmaṇasaṃpad uktā vakṣyamāṇā ca | gajacchāyā tv anyaiva, vyatīpātasaṃnidhānāt,

                    	yadi syāc candramāḥ pitrye kare caiva divākaraḥ|

                    	varṣāsu ca trayodaśyāṃ sā chāyā kuñjarasya tu ||

iti ca smaraṇāt | ete śrāddhakālāḥ prakīrtitāḥ | śrāddhavacanaṃ dānāder api pradarśanārthaṃ, prakramāviśeṣāt | tathā cāhuḥ: "śatam indukṣaye dānam" iti | etāni vyastāny api nimittāni | yad vā, śrāddhaśabdaḥ svārtha eva | tasya cāyaṃ kālavidhiḥ | saṃnidhānāc ca dānasyāpy ayam evāpekṣitatvāt smṛtyantarānusārāc cāviruddhaḥ kāla ity avaseyam | kṛṣṇapakṣe 'viśeṣata eva śrāddham uktam | yathāha jātūkarṇiḥ: "atha śrāddham aparapakṣe sarvatrāviśeṣāt | nabhasya eva vā sāmarthyopapattibhyām" iti | āmnāyaś ca "atha yatra dakṣiṇā vartate sūryaḥ, pitṛṣu tarhi bhavati" ityādinaitam evārthaṃ sphuṭayati | atha vā praśastataratvaṃ tasya | aviśeṣeṇaivātra nimittatvam, "māsi māsi cāśanam" ity āmnāyāt | jātūkarṇam py evam eva neyam || 214, 215 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvat kālasaṃpadam uktvā pātrasaṃpadam āha |_

 

**              	agryaḥ sarveṣu vedeṣu śrotriyo vedavid yuvā |**

**              	vedārthavij jyeṣṭhasāmā trimadhus trisuparṇakaḥ || 1.216 ||**

**              	svasrīyaṛtvigjāmātṛyājyaśvaśuramātulāḥ |**

**              	trināciketadauhitraśiṣyasaṃbandhibāndhavāḥ || 1.217 ||**

**              	karmaniṣṭhataponiṣṭhapañcāgnibrahmacāriṇaḥ |**

**              	pitṛmātṛparāś caiva brāhmaṇāḥ śrāddhasaṃpadaḥ || 1.218 ||**

 

agryo 'gragāmī, sarveṣu vedeṣv ṛgvedādiṣu | śrotriyo jñātā vedapāraga ity arthaḥ | vedavid ekaśākhāpāragaḥ | yuvā taruṇaḥ | vedārthavin mīmāṃsādiśāstrajñaḥ | jyeṣṭhasāmākhyaṃ chāndogyaṃ vrataṃ, tat cīrṇaṃ yena sa jyeṣṭhasāmā | evam uttaratrāpi yojyam | trimadhur ātharvaṇam | trisuparṇakaṃ bāhvṛcyam | svasrīyo bhāgineyaḥ | ṛtvigādayaḥ prasiddhāḥ | trināciketam ādhvaryavaṃ vrataṃ, triragnicayanaṃ vā | śiṣyo 'nuśiṣṭaḥ snātakaḥ | saṃbandhī sthālādiḥ | bāndhavā mātṛśvasīyādayaḥ | karmaniṣṭhā yāvajjīvāgnihotriṇaḥ | taponiṣṭhā naiṣṭhikaparivrājakādayaḥ | pañcāgnir agnihotrī, vanastho vā | brahmacāry upakurvāṇakaḥ | pitṛmātṛparās tadbhaktāḥ | caśabdaḥ smṛtyantaroktasmṛtidroṇapāṭhakādyarthaḥ | svasrīyādīnāṃ saṃbandhanimittatvāt, kṣatriyādeś ca śrāddhādhikārāt, tajjātīyaprasaktāv āha: "brāhmaṇāḥ śrāddhasaṃpadaḥ" iti | śrāddhaṃ saṃpādayantīti śrāddhasaṃpadaḥ | bahucavanād vyatyastā api | abhraṣṭasaṃskārāś ca svasrīyādayo 'lpaguṇā apīty avaseyam | punaḥ śrāddhavacanaṃ dāne guṇātirekāt pātrateti jñāpanārtham || 216–218 ||

 

_kim aviśeṣeṇaivaite brāhmaṇāḥ śrāddhabhojinaḥ | neti brūmaḥ yataḥ |_

 

**              	rogī hīnātiriktāṅgaḥ kāṇaḥ paunarbhavas tathā |**

**              	avakīrṇī kuṇḍagolau kunakhī śyāvadantakaḥ || 1.219 ||**

**              	bhṛtakādhyāpakaḥ krūraḥ kanyādūṣy abhiśastakaḥ |**

**              	mitradhruk piśunaḥ somavikrayī parivindakaḥ || 1.220 ||**

**              	mātāpitṛsutatyāgī kuṇḍāśī vṛṣalātmajaḥ |**

**              	parapūrvāpatiḥ stenaḥ karmaduṣṭaś ca ninditāḥ || 1.221 ||**

 

rogī asamādheyavyādhyabhibhūtaḥ | avakīrṇī ādiṣṭaprāyaścittaḥ, anyasya karmadauṣṭyenaiva ninditatvāt | kuṇḍagolakau, yathāha manuḥ |

                    	paradāreṣu jāyete dvau sutau kuṇḍagolakau |

                    	patyau jīvati kuṇḍas tu mṛte bhartari golakaḥ || iti | (MDh 3.174)

parivindako jyeṣṭhabhrātari sthite dārāginotrāhartā | mātṛtyāgī sarvathā, pitṛsutatyāgī akāraṇāt | kuṇḍāśī kuṇḍagolakādyannabhoktā | vṛṣala ātmajo yasya sa vṛṣalātmajaḥ śūdrāpatyaḥ | parapūrvā punarbhūḥ, tadbhartā parapūrvāpatiḥ | stenaś coraḥ | karmadauṣṭyavacanāt siddhe prakārārthaṃ vacanam | spaṣṭam anyat || 219–221 ||

 

_evam aninditān śrāddhabhojane |_

 

**              	nimantrayīta pūrvedyur brāhmaṇān ātmavāñ chuciḥ |**

**              	nimantritaiś ca tair bhāvyaṃ manovākkāyasaṃyataiḥ || 1.222 ||**

 

brāhmanagrahaṇaṃ guṇārtham | tataś ca dṛṣṭārthatayaiva guṇavataḥ pūrvedur āmantraṇam | anyeṣāṃ tu tadahar apy avirodhaḥ || 222 ||

 

_atha śrāddhāhani |_

 

                    	**aparāhṇe samabhyarcya svāgatenāgatāṃs tu tān |**

**              	pavitrapāṇir ācāntān āsaneṣūpaveśayet || 1.223 ||**

 

saṃśabdāt svayam abhyutthānādinābhyarcyaitān | āgatavacanāc ca nimantraṇasyānyakartṛkatve 'py adoṣaḥ | pavitraṃ darbhāstaraṇādi | ācāntavacanāc ca na svayaṃ pādaprakṣālanakriyā | svayam eva tv āsaneṣu paṅktipāvanādyapekṣayā yathārham upaveśayet | āsanavacanaṃ pūrvam āsanopakḷptyartham | tathā cāha |

                    	āsaneṣūpakḷpteṣu barhiṣmatsu vidhānataḥ | iti (cf. MDh 3.208) || 223 ||

 

_kaḥ punar upaveśanaprakāraḥ | ucyate |_

 

**              	daive yugmān yathāśakti pitrye 'yugmāṃs tathaiva ca**

**              	pariśrite śucau deśe dakṣiṇāpravaṇe tathā || 1.224 ||**

** **

tathāśabdaḥ prāṅmukhatvādiprakārārthaḥ | śaktiś cāvaiguṇyalakṣaṇā draṣṭavyā || 224 ||

 

_manovākkāyasaṃyataiḥ avaiguṇyaśaktyapekṣayaiva ca |_

 

**              	dvau daive prāg udak pitrye traya ekaikam eva vā |**

**              	mātāmahānām apy evaṃ tantraṃ vā vaiśvadevikam || 1.225 ||**

 

tathā cāha manuḥ |

                    	dvau daive pitṛkārye trīn ekaikam ubhayatra vā |

                    	bhojayet susamṛddho 'pi na prasajyeta vistare ||

                    	satkriyāṃ deśakālau ca śaucaṃ brāhmaṇasaṃpadam |

                    	pañcaitān vistaro hanti tasmāt taṃ parivarjayet || iti | (MDh 3.125–26)

evam upaveśanāntaṃ pitrye vidhāyātidiśati: matāmahānām py evaṃ sarvaṃ kālādi saṃpādyam | tataś ca sarvathākaraṇe prasakte śaktyapekṣayaivāpavādaḥ: tantraṃ vā vaiśvadevikaṃ karma kuryād iti | vāśabdaḥ kalpāntarārtho 'pi, smṛtyantarāt:

                    	eka eva yadā vipro dvitīyo nopalabhyate |

                    	taṃ niyujya hi pitrarthe daive tv agniṃ niyojayet ||

dvitīyam |

                    	yady ekaṃ bhojayec chrāddhe daivaṃ tatra kathaṃ bhavet |

                    	annaṃ pātre samuddhṛtya sarvasya prakṛtasya tu ||

                    	devatāyatane sthāpya tataḥ śrāddhaṃ prakalpayet |

                    	prāsyed agnau tad annādyaṃ dadyād vā brahmacāriṇe || iti |

        	iha cādhunā vicāryate: kim idaṃ śrāddhaṃ nāma, kasya vātrādhikāra iti | atrāyaṃ śrāddhaśabdo yaugikatve 'pi na guṇavidhiḥ | "śraddhāpūtaṃ tu śaktitaḥ" (YDh 1.202) iti śraddāyā anyataḥ prāptatvāt | prayuktasya ca yogānumānān nātiprasaṅgaḥ | tenāgnihotrādivan nāmaivaitad iti sthitam | tac ca piṇḍadānasyaiva, na brāhmaṇabhojanādeḥ, "yat pitṛbhyo nipṛṇāti" (BāU 1.4.16) ity āmnāyāt | niparaṇaṃ ca piṇḍadānam eva, na brāhmaṇabhojanādi, "sarvebhya eva nipṛṇīyāt" ityādiprayogadarśanānusārāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca śrāddhabhug devadatta ityādy api prayogo dṛṣṭa eva | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | aupacārikas tu saḥ | kuto 'yaṃ viveka iti cet, "śāstrasthā vā tannimittatvāt" (PMS 1.3.9) iti nyāyāt, piṇḍapitṛyajñe ca prayogadarśanāt | yathāha jaiminiḥ: "śrāddhavad iti cet" (PMS 6.8.16), apiṇḍake cānvāhikapitṛbrāhmaṇabhojane 'nupalambhāt, "dadyāt piṇḍaṃ hared dhanam" iti ca piṇḍadānasyaiva pitṛsaṃbhandhadarśanāt | "yady ekaṃ bhojayec chrāddhe" ityādayas tu prayogās tādarthyanimittatvenaivāvaseyāḥ | vyāsaś ca piṇḍadāna eva pitṛhastotthānābhidhānāt tatpradhānatām eva dyotayati | evam āmnāyāt smṛtyantarānusārāc ca piṇḍadānasyaiva śrāddhatvasiddhiḥ | cintāprayojanaṃ tu tathoktabrāhmaṇālābe piṇḍamātrapravṛttir yathā syād iti | kva punar etat piṇḍadānaṃ yāgādimadhye 'ntarbhāvyam | naikatrāpīti kecit | anya evāyaṃ niparaṇākhyo vyāpāra utsargalakṣaṇa iti | sakyaṃ caitad dānam iti vaktum, parasvatvāpattiparyantatvāt | pitṝṇāṃ hi saṃpradānataivotpattivākye | yataḥ pitṛbhyo dadyāt piṇḍaṃ dadyād iti ca | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> atra dānārthānupapattiḥ pitṛgatasvatvasaṃbandhānupapatteḥ, pretapitṛkasya cādhikārāt | yathāha kātyāyanaḥ: "pretebhyo dadāti" iti (KātŚr 4.1.23) | manur api |

                    	pitā yasya tu vṛttaḥ syāj jīved vāpi pitāmahaḥ | (MDh 3.221)

ityādinā pretebhya eva dānaṃ darśayati | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> evam | pretānām api yathā saṃpradānatvaṃ tathopariṣṭād vakṣyāmaḥ | etāny eva tu kathaṃ vacanāni |

                    	dhriyamāṇe tu pitari pūrveṣām eva nirvapet |

                    	vipravad vāpi taṃ śrāddhe svakaṃ pitaram āśayet ||

                    	pitā yasya tu vṛttaḥ syāj jīved vāpi pitāmahaḥ |

                    	pituḥ sa nāma saṃkīrtya kīrtayet prapitāmaham || iti | (MDh 3.220–221)

tathedam anyat: "pitāputrau ced āhitāgnī syātām, yebhya eva pitā dadyāt tebhyaḥ putro 'pi" iti | virodhād anādṛtyāny eveti <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecit</span> | evaṃ hy āmnāyaḥ: "asāv etat te" iti (ŚB 2.4.2.19) | evaṃ "yajamānasya pitre" ityādi (ŚB 2.4.2.19) | kātyāyanaś caitad evālocya "pitṛprabhṛti tu nityāḥ" ity āha | vacanāc ca parānadhikāraḥ | jīvapitrādyapekṣayā ca "na jīvantam ati dadāti" ity āmnāyopanyāsaḥ (KātŚr 4.1.27) | jīvapitṛkasya vā samāvartanārthaśrāddhaviṣayāny etāni | tasyāpi

                    	aniṣṭvā tu pitṝñ chrāddhe na kuryāt karma vaidikam |

ity anagnikasyaiva sāmarthyāc chrāddhādhikāro 'sty eva | kuto 'yaṃ viśeṣa iti cet, sāgnikasya jīvapitṛkasya piṇḍapitṛyajñānadhikārāt śrāddhānadhikāraḥ,

                    	piṇḍānvāhāryakaṃ śrāddhaṃ kuryān māsānumādikam | (MDh 3.122)

ity aṅgatvavacanāt | evaṃ tarhy aparapakṣādiśrāddhaviṣayatāpy astu | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">na</span>, pārvaṇavikāratvāt, tasya ca pretaviṣayatvāt, prakṛtivac ca vikṛtyanuṣṭhānāt | samāvartane 'pi tarhy ayam eva nyāyaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">stayam</span>, ānarthakyaparijihīrṣayā tadviṣayatvābhidhānam | tāvataivānarthakyaparihārān nātiprasaṅgaḥ | kiṃ ca, agnyabhāve 'pi hi sāmarthyāt tasyaivāgnaukaraṇakalpaḥ,

                    	agnyabhāve tu viprasya pāṇāv evopapādayet | iti | (MDh 3.212)

tatsāmānyād anyo 'py evaṃjātīyakas tasyaiva yuktaḥ | evaṃ tāvad viṣayopakḷptir uktā | pūrvapakṣatayaiva tv ayaṃ bhagavato 'pi lakṣyate | kathaṃ hi bhagavatā pratyakṣāḥ śrutayo na nirūpitāḥ syuḥ | tathā cāha |

                    	pitāmaho vā tacchrāddhaṃ bhuñjītety abravīn manuḥ |

                    	kāmaṃ vā tadanujñātaḥ svayam eva samācaret || iti | (MDh 3.222)

ayam asyārthaḥ: "dhriyamāṇe tu pitari" (MDh 3.220) ityādītikaraṇāntam (cf. MDh 3.286) uktavān manuḥ, na tv anuṣṭhitavān | kāmam eva tu tenaiva pitāmahena viduṣā śāstrārtham ālokyānujñāto yad yuktaṃ tat svayam eva samācared iti | tathā cāmnāyo 'py uktam apy ananuṣṭhitam akartavyatayaiva darśayati: "tad vai santo mīmāṃsām eva cakre na tu cakāra tatkṛtam eva" ity anuṣṭhānakṛtam eva prāmāṇyaṃ nābhidhānamātrakṛtam ity abhiprāyaḥ | yat tu "pitāputrau ced āhitāgnī syātām" iti, tad āhitāgnivacanāt kratugatapiṇḍadānārthaṃ draṣṭavyam | tathā ca tādarthyenaiva "yebhya eva pitā dadyāt, tebhyaḥ putro 'pi" iti yājñikasmaraṇam cf. (Haradatta on ĀpG 8.21.4) | ataś ca jīvapitṛkasyāvasathyādy api śrāddharahitam evety alaṃ prasaktyā | snānavivāhayos tu jīvapitṛkasyāpi pitṛvac chrāddhakriyeti saṃpradāyaḥ |

        	sthitam etat piṇḍadānaṃ srāddham iti | adhikāras tu vaktavyaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> uktaḥ pretapitṛko 'gnimāñ chrāddhādhikṛta iti | yady evam ātmatyāgipitṛkasyāpi prasajyeta | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">tac cāyuktam</span> | yathāha manuḥ |

                    	vṛthāsaṃkarajātānāṃ pravrajyāsu ca tiṣṭhatām |

                    	ātmanas tyāgināṃ caiva nivartetodakakriyā || iti | (MDh 5.89)

evaṃ sarvasmṛtiṣv evaṃjātīyakānām udakakriyāniṣedhād ekoddiṣṭanivṛttiḥ | tadanusārāt sapiṇḍīkaraṇābhāvāc chrāddhānadhikāraḥ | atrocyate | na sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ śrāddhanimittaṃ, kiṃ tarhi, amāvāsyādīni | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> amāvāsyādhikṛtasya kālaḥ | sapiṇḍīkṛtapitṛkasyaiva tu śrāddhādhikāraḥ | anyathā hi prāg api sapiṇḍīparaṇāt prasajyeta | prasajyatām iti ced, na, pratiṣedhāt | yathāha manuḥ |

                    	asapiṇḍakriyākarma dvijāteḥ saṃsthitasya tu |

                    	adaivaṃ bhojayec chrāddhaṃ piṇḍam ekaṃ ca nirvapet || iti | (MDh 3.247)

<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ekoddiṣṭam api śrāddham eva | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | pārvaṇānadhikāras tv asmābhir uktaḥ | tathā cetarad anāhitāgner api bhavati | ābhyudayikaṃ vā kiṃ tasya na bhavati | bhavati, na tv asapiṇḍīkṛtapitṛkasya | ekoddiṣṭaṃ tu tasyāpi bhavatīti viśeṣaḥ | tasmān na sapiṇḍīkaraṇābhāve śrāddhādhikāraḥ | anye tu kutaścid āgamayyemaṃ ślokaṃ paṭhanti |

                    	niṣiddhodakakalpānāṃ patitādidvijanmanām |

                    	ūrdhavaṃ saṃvatsarāt kuryāt sarvam evaurdhvadehikam || iti |

ayaṃ tv aspaṣṭamūlatvād vicāryaḥ | atra brūmaḥ | pretakriyaiva manvādibhir niṣiddhāḥ | na tu śrāddhādhikāraḥ | sapiṇḍīkaraṇābhāvān neti ced, na, atiprasaṅgāt | yadā hi daivān na sapiṇḍīkṛtaḥ, tadāpy anadhikāraḥ syāt | saṃvatsarāc cordhvaṃ sapiṇḍikaraṇānupapattiḥ, anupadeśāt | tatraitat syāt | akāle vā tat kartavyam, tadabhāve vādhikāro vaktavyaḥ | tatra yady atikrāntakālasyāpi kriyā śrāddhaprayuktatvāt sarvair aviśeṣāt kartavyaṃ, brāhmaṇāmantraṇādivat | anadhikārahetutvaṃ tūpapannam eva, tadabhāve 'pi darśanāt | na tāvan mātāmahān dauhitraḥ sapiṇḍīkaroti, karoti tu śrāddham | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca mātur mātāmahenaiva saha sapiṇḍīkaraṇam iṣyate, tat katham ucyate dauhitraḥ sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ na karotīti | "sapiṇḍīkaraṇavidhāne catvāri pātrāṇi" ity upakramya "trīṇi pitṝṇām ekaṃ pretasya" ity uktam | pretasya ca pitṝṇāṃ trīṇīti tatrābhisaṃbandhaḥ, nādhikṛtasya pitṝṇām iti samañjasaṃ syāt | mātuś ca mātāmahā eva pitaraḥ | tasmāt tair eva saha sapiṇḍīkaranaṃ yuktam iti |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">atrocyate</span> | syād etad yadi pretasyeti pitṛviśeṣaṇaṃ syāt | pātrasaṃbandhitayā tu pretasyeti śrutaṃ na pitṛviśeṣaṇatvaṃ pratipattuṃ kṣamam | ato 'dhikṛtāpekṣam eva pitṝṇām iti yojyam | kiṃ ca, mātāmahaiḥ saha sapiṇḍakriyāyām ānarthakyam eva syāt | na tāvan mātāmahasantāninas tasyāḥ piṇḍaṃ dadyuḥ, anupadeśāt | na cādhikṛtasaṃtāninaḥ, teṣām atyantam adhikṛtamātāmahaiḥ sahāsaṃbandhāt | ataḥ siddhaṃ dauhitro mātāmahān na sapiṇḍīkarotīti | na cānyena sapiṇḍīkṛtāḥ sapiṇḍīkṛtā bhavanti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ pretasaṃskāratvād yena kenacit kṛtaṃ sarveṣām upakarotīti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span> | pretopakārakaṃ hy etan na saṃskārakam, tatkalpane hy adṛṣṭakalpanāprasaṅgāt | upakārakatvaṃ tu śrāddhāntaravat siddhaṃ, saṃskāramadhye cāparigaṇanād vispaṣṭaśrutyabhāvāc ca | evaṃ sati yāvantaḥ putrāḥ, sarveṣām adhikāraḥ syāt, tasya tasyāviśeṣāt | putramātrāśrita upadeśo na saṅkocitaḥ syāt | tasmān nānyakṛtenānyasyādhikārasiddhiḥ | atas tadabhāve 'py adhikāra iti jyāyasī kalpanā | kiṃ ca putrābhāve sapiṇḍādīnāṃ piṇḍadānaṃ śrūyate | tac ca sapiṇḍakriyāpūrvakatve 'nupapannam eva | tasmāt tad api te na kurvanti, aputrasyāsaṃbhavāt | yathāha pāraskaraḥ: "piṇḍakaraṇe prathamaḥ pitṝṇāṃ pretaḥ syāt putravāṃś cet" iti (PārG 3.10.50) | śārāddhamātracodanaiva teṣāṃ na sapiṇḍakriyācodanāpi | api ca mātre mātāmahaiḥ saha piṇḍadānam | na ca tatra sapiṇḍīkaraṇopapattiḥ | tasmān na tadapāye 'py adhikāravyāvṛttir iti siddham | manvādivacanāny apy ekoddiṣṭapratiṣedhārthatayaiva caritārthatvān na śrāddhapratipakṣatām upayāntīty avaseyam | pratyakṣāpi ca piṇḍapitṛyajñaśrutir evam anuparuddhā syāt | anyathā tu smṛtyuparodhāt sā bādhyeta | tad apeśalaṃ syāt | tasmād apy uktasiddhiḥ | yadā tu "niṣiddhodakakalpānām" ity ayaṃ ślokaḥ pramāṇam | tatas tadanusārād api karaṇam astu | sarvathā śrāddhāstitvaniyamaḥ | yat tūktam "asapiṇḍakriyākarma" iti (MDh 3.247), tad arvāk saṃvatsarād draṣṭavyam | paratas tv asapiṇḍīkṛtasyāpi śrāddhapravṛttiḥ | kuta etat | "yadā vā vṛddhir āpadyeta" iti prāg eva saṃvatsarād ayam upadeśo yataḥ, na śrāddhāṅgaṃ sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ, pramāṇābhāvāt | kathaṃ punaḥ prāg evāyaṃ vidhiḥ na parato 'pīty avagamaḥ, smṛtyantarānusārāt | yathāha pāraskaraḥ: "saṃvatsaraṃ pṛthag eka" iti (PārG 3.10.52) | yatra ca saṃvatsaraprāptir api saṃdigdhā, kutas tatrātiprasaṅgaḥ | kātyāyano 'pi ca "saṃvatsare pūrṇe" iti pūrṇavacanāt parato nety etad eva jñāpayati | anyathā saṃvatsara ity eva siddhe tad anarthakaṃ syāt | tasmāt saṃvatsarād ūrdhvaṃ sapiṇḍīkaraṇānupapatteḥ prāg eva saṃvatsarāc chrāddhaniṣedhārtham "asapiṇḍakriyākarma" (MDh 3.247) ity etad ity anavadyam |

        	idaṃ tu cintyam | kim anagniko 'pi sapiṇḍakriyāṃ kuryād, uta sāgnika eveti | sāgnika iti yuktam, itarasya sarvāṅgopasaṃhārānupapatteḥ | na hy agnaukaraṇam tasyāsti,

                    	na paitṛyājñiko homo laukike 'gnau vidhīyate | (MDh 3.282)

iti vacanāt | ata eva ca jñayate agnaukaraṇarahitatvād ekoddiṣṭam anagniko 'pi kuryād iti | evaṃ prāpte bhrūmaḥ | aviśeṣeṇaivādhikāraḥ | anyathā hi saṃvatsaropadeśo 'narthaka eva syāt | yas tāvad agnimān, prāg evāsau karoti | anagnikas tu yady agnim ādhāya kuryāt, tadā pūrvataraṃ śrāddhānadhikārāt sapiṇḍīkaraṇam eva kartavyam | atha vaiguṇyāśaṅkayā tadakṛtiḥ, tataḥ prāg varṣād asapiṇḍīkṛtapitṛkasya śrāddhānadhikārāt tatpūrvakatvāc cāvasathyasyādhikarato vidhiḥ | tasmad anagnikasyāpi sapiṇḍakriyādhikāraḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evaṃ brahmacāry api kasmān na sapiṇḍīkaroti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">anupadeśāt</span> | ekoddiṣṭam eva hi tasyopadiṣṭaṃ na tu sapiṇḍakriyādy api, śavakarmaṇa evānujñānāt | ato 'virodhaḥ | kasmāt punaḥ pitari prete ekādaśe 'hny āvasathyaṃ kurvataḥ sapiṇḍakriyāpūrvakataiva na bhavati | vacanāntareṇāpavādāt | yathāha yamaḥ |

                    	mṛtāhni tu kartavyaṃ pratimāsaṃ tu vatsaram |

                    	pratisaṃvatsaraṃ caivam ādyam ekādaśe 'hani || iti |

etad evādyavacanasya prayojanam | ataś ca jīvapitṛkavac chrāddharahitam eva tasyāpy āvasathyādhānam iti sthitam | idam adhunā cintyam: kim idaṃ mātāmahaśrāddhaṃ yadā kuryāt tadaivam, athaitad apy evaṃ nityam eva kuryād iti | ubhayathātideśopapatteḥ saṃśaye, yadā kuryāt tadaivam iti prāpta ucyate | codanāntarābhāvād asyāś cāviśeṣān nityam iti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evaṃ putrapraśaṃsānupapannaiva syād, yadi hi putravad dauhitro 'pi śrāddaṃ kuryāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">naivam</span> | duhitaram apekṣya praśaṃsā, na dauhitram api, tasyāḥ svayaṃ pitṛśrāddhānadhikṛtatvāt | bhartrā ca saha śvaśuraśrāddhakaraṇāt | dauhitrapautrayos tv aviśeṣaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evaṃ rikthagrāhy asau kasmān na bhavati | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">rikthavibhāge</span> viśeṣaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ | dattakādibhis tu putrair mukhyatvāj janayitur eva sapiṇḍīkaraṇādi kartavyam, ekoddiṣṭamātram itarasyāpi | atha kim ekam evaitac chrāddhaṃ dvidevatyam uta dve ity aniyame prāpte dve iti brūmaḥ | pṛthak pitṝṇāṃ mātāmahaśrāddhaṃ, mātāmahānāṃ caivam itīyam eva hi taccodanā yataḥ | tatra mātāmahānām api śrāddhaṃ kuryād ity ayam evārtho bhavati, na punaḥ śrāddhābheda iti | api ca "tantraṃ vā vaiśvadevikam" (YDh 1.227) iti bhedaprasaktāv upapadyeta | anyathā tu svābhāviky eva tantratā syāt | tatropadeśānarthakyam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> caikaśrāddhatāpi dṛśyate:

                    	mātāmahānām apy evaṃ dadyād ācamanaṃ tataḥ | iti | (YDh 1.240)

<span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyaṃ</span> dṛśyate | arthaprāptā tu sā, deśakālādyabhedāt | na cārthataḥ prāptau śabdavyāpārakalpanaṃ yuktam | tasmāc chrāddābhedaḥ prayogatantratā ceti siddham | prayojanaṃ tu jīvapitṛkasyājivamātṛkasya cādhikārāvyāghātaḥ |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">atha</span> kim etan mātāmahaśrāddhaṃ mātṛmātāmahapramātāhahebhya eva | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">bāḍhaṃ</span>, mātāmahaśabdasya bahuvacanāntasyaivam evopapatteḥ, mātā ca mātāmahau ca mātāmahā iti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca mātāmahaś ca pramātāmahau cety evam apy upapadyata eva | kiṃ ca,

                    	ekatvaṃ sā gatā bhartuḥ piṇḍe gotre 'tha sūtake |

ity anyagotratvān mātur mātāmahena sahāyuktam eva dānam | strībhiś ca saha tasyāḥ sapiṇḍīkaraṇam āmnātam |

                    	bhartṛgotreṇa nāmnā ca mātuḥ kuryāt sapiṇḍatām |

                    	tūṣṇīṃ daṃpatipiṇḍābhyāṃ kuśenāntarathet (?) pitṝn || iti |

ato 'pi mātāmahena sa dānāyogaḥ | anyac ca |

                    	mātuḥ prathamataḥ piṇḍaṃ nivapet putrikāsutaḥ |

                    	dvitīyaṃ tu pitus tasyās tṛtīyaṃ tu pituḥ pituḥ ||

ity evaṃ piṇḍadānopadeśo 'rthavān syāt | anyathā tv evam eva prāpter ānarthakyam | strīpuṃsayoś caikatra dānam ayuktam | vairūpyaṃ ca pitaraṃ duhitaraṃ ca lakṣayato mātāmahaśabdasya syāt | tasmān mātāmahādy eva yuktam iti |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">atrocyate</span> | mātṛdvāreṇaiva hi mātāmahe pratyayaḥ, na tadanapekṣaḥ, mātṛprātipadikād eva pratyayavidhānāt | tatra mātāmahaśabda uccāryamāṇaḥ pūrvaṃ mātaram eva pratyāyayati | pratītasya ca bādhahetur vaktavyaḥ | na ca duhitrādyanusārāt pratītabādho yuktaḥ, śabdapramāṇakatvāt | yathā ca,

                    	māsavṛddhyā hi tuṣyanti dattair hi pitāmahāḥ | (YDh 1.255)

iti pitāmahaśabdaḥ pitṛprapitāmahayor api grāhakaḥ, tathā mātāmahaśabdo 'pi tadanusārād avaseyaḥ | yat tu strībhiḥ saha sapiṇḍīkaraṇam āmnātam iti, ānvaṣṭakyadānaprayojanārthaṃ tad an śrāddhārthaṃ, tvayānabhyupagatatvāt | yaś cobhayoḥ samo doṣo nāsāv ekaṃ prati codyaḥ | kiṃ ca mātāpitroḥ samāna eva putratve mātuḥ śrāddaṃ na kuryād ity anucitam eva syāt | tatsaṃbandhapratītasya ca mātāmahādes tadatilaṅghanenāyuktam evopādānaṃ, prathamātilaṅghane hetvabhāvāt | yat tu,

                    	mātuḥ prathamataḥ piṇḍaṃ nivapet putrikāsutaḥ | (MDh 9.140)

iti, tat putrikāputrasya pautratvajñāpanārthaṃ draṣṭavyam | tathā coktam |

                    	pautrī mātamahas tena dadyāt piṇḍaṃ hared dhanam | iti | (MDh 9.136)

rikthavibhāge nipuṇataraṃ vakṣyāmaḥ | tasmān mātṛprabhṛty eva mātāmahaśrāddham iti siddham || 225 ||

 

_evaṃ śrāddhadvaye 'pi tantreṇāvṛttyā vā brāhmaṇān upaveśya |_

 

                    	**pāṇiprakṣālanaṃ dattvā viṣṭarārthān kuśān api |**

**              	āvāhayed anujñāto viśvedevāsa ity ṛcā || 1.226 ||**

 

viṣṭarārthān āsanārthān ity arthaḥ | "viśvān devān āvāhayiṣye" iti paṅktimūrdhanyaṃ sarvān vā pṛṣṭvā tadanujñāto "viśve devāsa āgatā" (RV 1.3.7) itīmām ṛcaṃ japet | etad evāvāhanaṃ nānyat || 226 ||

 

_tataḥ_ |

 

                    	**yavair anvavakīryātha bhājane sapavitrake |**

**              	śaṃ no devyā payaḥ kṣiptvā yavo 'sīti yavān kṣipet || 1.227 ||**

**              	yā divyā iti mantreṇa hasteṣv arghyaṃ vinikṣipet |**

 

yavair anvavakiraṇaṃ pradakṣiṇena vikiraṇam | athaśabdasāmarthyāt smṛtyantaroktaṃ draṣṭavyam | "viśve devāḥ śṛṇutemam" iti mantraṃ japtvā yathālābhopapanne bhājane smṛtyantrānusārād yajñīyavṛkṣapātrādau pavitre nidhāya "śaṃ no devīḥ" (RV 10.9.4) ity anayarcodakaṃ prakṣipya "yavo 'si yavaya" (TS 1.3.1.1) ity anena yavān opya brāhmaṇahaste pavitre nidhāya "yā divyā" (TB 2.7.15.4) ity anenārghyaṃ ninayet | hastagrahaṇaṃ smṛtyantare pātrāntaritaśravaṇāt tannivṛttyartham | arghyavacanāt puṣpāṇy api prakṣeptavyāni | hasteṣv iti bahuvacanaṃ brāhmaṇāpekṣam | arghyas tv eka eva || 228 ||

 

_evam arghyaṃ pradāya_ |

 

**              	dattvodakaṃ gandhadhūpamālyadānam sadīpakam || 1.228 ||**

**              	apasavyaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā pitṝṇām apradakṣiṇam |**

**              	dviguṇāṃs tu kuśān dattvā uśantas tv ity ṛcā pitṝn || 1.229 ||**

**              	āvāhya tadanujñāto japed āyantu nas tataḥ |**

**              	yavārthāṃs tu tilaiḥ kuryāc cheṣaṃ tv arghyādi pūrvavat || 1.230 ||**

 

dhūpamālyayoḥ (?) kramabhedaś chando'nurodhārthaḥ | apasavyāpradakṣiṇavacanāc ca vaiśvadeve viparyaya iti jñāyate | tataḥśabdo hetvarthaḥ | tato hetoḥ śrutyupanyāsalakṣaṇāt, "prācīnāvītaṃ pitṝṇām | pitṝṇāṃ vā eṣā dik yā dakṣiṇā | parāñcaḥ pitaraḥ" ityādeḥ pitrarthe 'pasavyādiprayoga ity arthaḥ | tataś cādita eva sarvam etat pitṛkārye siddhaṃ bhavati | pitṝṇām iti ca tadarthabrāhmaṇārthā ṣaṣṭhīty avaseyam | yady api ca kāṇḍānusamayo lāghavārtham ācāryeṇa darbhāsanādipradīpānta uktaḥ, tathāpi pradhānāsattyanurodhāt padārthānusamaya eva yuktaḥ | tena vaiśvadeve darbhāsanaṃ, tataḥ pitrye | evam arghyādy api yojyam | devatādisaṅkhyayā tv arghyādikalpanaṃ, na brāhmaṇasaṅkhyayā | "trīṇy arghyapātrāṇi pitṛbhyaḥ kuryāt" iti smṛtyantarāt | tenaikasyāpi brāhmaṇasyārghyatrayaṃ kāryam | brāhmaṇabahutve caika evārghyaḥ sarvebhyo deyaḥ, sarvabrāhmaṇānāṃ pitṛtrayārthatvāt | spaṣṭam anyat || 227–230 ||

 

_pitṛbhya eva tu |_

 

**              	dattvārghyaṃ saṃsravān eṣāṃ pātre kṛtvā vidhānataḥ |**

**              	pitṛbhyaḥ sthānam āsīti nyubjaṃ pātraṃ karoty adhaḥ || 1.231 ||**

 

eṣām arghyāṇāṃ śeṣān ekasmin pātre 'vadhāya tat pātraṃ "pitṛbhyaḥ sthānam asi" ity anena mantreṇādhomukhaṃ bhūmau kuryāt | "sthānam āsi" iti dīrghapāṭhaś chando'nurogārthaḥ || 231 ||

 

_tataḥ_ |

 

                    	**agnau kariṣyann ādāya pṛcchaty annaṃ ghṛtāplutam |**

**              	kuruṣvety abhyanujñāto hutvāgnau pitṛyajñavat || 1.232 ||**

**              	hutaśeṣaṃ pradadyāc ca bhājaneṣu samāhitaḥ |**

**              	yathālābhopapanneṣu raupyeṣu tu viśeṣataḥ || 1.233 ||**

 

ghṛtāplutam annam ādāya "agnau kariṣye" iti pṛṣṭvā pitṛyajñavan mekṣaṇena "agnaye kavyavāhanāya" ity āhutidvayaṃ juhuyāt | agnivacanam āhitāgner apy aupāsane yathā syād, na tu anvāhāryapacana ity evamartham | hutaśeṣaṃ cānnaṃ brāhmaṇabhājaneṣv ācārataḥ prakṣāliteṣu nivaped raupyeṣu, alābhe tadanviteṣu, alābhe 'nyeṣv api | anye tu katipayaraupyasaṃbhave paṅktipāvanebhyas tānīti varṇayanti, viśeṣata iti vacanāt | tathāpy adoṣaḥ | pitrarthebhyaś cāgnaukaraṇaśeṣadānaṃ na vaiśvadevikebhyaḥ, agnaukaraṇasya pitrarthasaṃbandhāt | tuśabdo 'vadhāraṇārthaḥ | tataś ca niyogataḥ śeṣanīyaṃ, na śeṣasya sato dānam ity avaseyam | hutaśeṣavacanāt tu homābhāve nivṛttiḥ || 232–233 ||

 

_daivapūrvakam eva tv anyat |_

 

**              	dattvānnaṃ pṛthivī pātram iti pātrābhimantraṇam |**

**              	kṛtvedaṃ viṣṇur ity anne dvijāṅguṣṭhān niveśayet || 1.234 ||**

 

punar annavacanam agnaukaraṇaśeṣa evāṅguṣṭhaniveśanārtham | tatsaṃyogāc ca pātrālambho 'pi tatraivavaseyaḥ | dānapadārthasya cābhedāt sarvebhyo 'nnaṃ dattvā tataḥ pātrālambanam | "pṛthivī te pātram" iti vaktavye "pṛthivī pātram" ity uktaṃ chando'nurodhāt || 234 ||

 

_evam annaṃ pariveṣyāpośanaṃ ca parikalpya tataḥ |_

 

                    	**savyāhṛtikāṃ sāvitrīṃ madhu vātā iti tryṛcam |**

**              	japtvā yathāsukhaṃ vācya bhuñjīraṃs te 'pi vāgyatāḥ || 1.235 ||**

 

apiśabdāt svayaṃ ca vāgyataḥ syāt | yathāsukhaṃ tu bhojanaviṣayam | yad rocate yena ca krameṇa, te tathaiva bhuñjīrann ity arthaḥ || 135 ||

 

_atha kim annam aniyatam eva bhoktavyam | nety ucyate |_

 

**              	annam iṣṭaṃ haviṣyaṃ ca dadyād akrodhano 'tvaraḥ |**

**              	ā tṛptes tu pavitrāṇi japtvā pūrvajapaṃ tathā || 1.236 ||**

 

tuśabdāj japa eva svayaṃ kāryaḥ | pariveṣaṇaṃ tv anyakartṛkam eva | evaṃ ca patnīvyāpāro 'pi śrāddhe saṃpāditaḥ syāt | annavacanaṃ pakvānnārtham | caśabdo mūlaphalādyarthaḥ | iṣṭaṃ brāhmaṇābhipretaṃ śāstracoditaṃ vā kālaśākādi | haviṣyavacanaṃ vidalādinivṛttyartham | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

                    	ajānānas tu yaḥ śrāddhaṃ vidalaiḥ pariveṣayet |

                    	rakṣāṃsi tad vilumpanti śrutir eṣā purātanī || iti |

"māṣāḍhakīmudgavarjaṃ vidalāni na dadyāt" iti bhāradvājaḥ | tathāśabdaḥ smṛtyantaroktapariveṣaṇabhojanajapaprakārārthaḥ | tathā ca śaṅkhaḥ: "darbhair dakṣiṇāgrair agniṃ paristīrya juhuyāt" ity upakramya, "jānū niṣadya bhūmau pitṝn dhyāyan manasā tatas tilair māṃsaiḥ śākair yūṣaiḥ kṛsarapāyasāpūpair lājair madhunā ghṛtena dadhnā payasā ca prabhūtam iṣṭato 'nnaṃ dadyād anasūyuḥ | brāhmanāś cāśnantaḥ na guṇadoṣān abhidadhyuḥ, nānyonyaṃ saṃspṛśeyuḥ, nānyonyaṃ praśaṃseyuḥ | annapānām prabhūtam iti na brūhuḥ| na vikṛtaṃ brūyuḥ, anyatra hastasaṃjñānāt | yāvat soṣmānnaṃ tāvad aśnanti pitaraḥ, anyatra mūlaphalapānebhyaḥ | pavitrapāṇir darbheṣv āsīno madhvātīyaṃ japet | pavitraṃ dharmaśāstram" ityādi | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

                    	yādvad ūṣmānnam aśnanti yāvad aśnanti vāgyatāḥ |

                    	tāvad aśnanti pitaro yāvan noktā havirguṇāḥ|| iti |

tathānyatra "rākṣoghṇīḥ pāvamānyaḥ puruṣasūktam" ity evamādi | etat sarvaṃ tathāśabdākṣiptaprakāraparipūraṇārthaṃ draṣṭavyam || 236 ||

 

_evaṃ tṛptāñ jñātvā tataḥ pūrvajapaṃ savyāhṛtikasāvitryādilakṣaṇaṃ japtvā svayam eva |_

 

**              	annam ādāya tṛptāḥ stha śeṣaṃ caivānumānya ha |**

**              	tad annaṃ prakired bhūmau dadyāc cāpaḥ sakṛt sakṛt || 1.237 ||**

 

annaṃ gṛhītvā "tṛptāḥ stha" iti brāhmaṇān pṛṣṭvā taiś ca "tṛptāḥ sma" ity ukte śeṣam annaṃ tebhya eva nivedya tair yatheṣṭaṃ viniyujyatām ity evam anumānya, anujñāpyety arthaḥ | haśabdo 'vadhāraṇārthaḥ, smṛtyantare "yathā brūyus tatā kuryāt" (MDh 3.253) iti śravaṇāt | evaṃ śeṣam anujñāpya yad gṛhītaṃ tad annaṃ prakired bhūmau, na darbheṣu | tataś cāpo brāhmaṇebhyaḥ sakṛt sakṛd dadyād, na pūrvaṃ tṛptipraśnād ity arthaḥ || 237 ||

 

_evam evodakaṃ dattvā yat prakṛtaṃ tat |_

 

                    	**sarvam annam upādāya satilaṃ dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ |**

**              	ucchiṣṭasaṃnidhau piṇḍān pradadyāt pitṛyajñavat || 1.238 ||**

 

upaśabdo 'vayavopādānārthaḥ, sarvasmād annād avayavaśa ādāyety arthaḥ | piṇḍapitṛyajñavad iti sakṛdācchinnāvanejanādiprāptyartham | ayaṃ tu viśeṣaḥ: satilam ucchiṣṭhasaṃnidhau ceti | piṇḍavacanaṃ sūtradānādinivṛttyartham | praśabdo madhyamapiṇḍabhakṣaṇapratiṣedhārthaḥ || 238 ||

 

_yathā caitat pitṛbhyaḥ piṇḍadānam |_

 

**              	mātāmahānām apy evaṃ dadyād ācamanaṃ tataḥ|**

**              	svasti vācya tato dadyād akṣayyodakam eva ca || 1.239 ||**

 

pūrvasmād evātideśe siddhe punarvacanaṃ yathārtham ūhasiddhyartham | kramasiddhis tu pāṭhād eva | ācamanāṃ ca sarvebhyo dattvā tataḥ svastivācanaṃ kuryāt: svastīti brūhīty evaṃ pratyekaṃ vācayet | vidhānāc ca kṣatriyādayo 'pi vācanaṃ kuryur ity evaśabdaḥ | kiṃ ca, akṣayyodakaṃ dadyāt tilavyāmiśritam | akṣayyam astv iti ca vācayet || 239 ||

 

_kiṃ svastivācyānantaram evākṣayyodakam | nety ucyate | pūrvam akṣayyodaokam pradāya, tataḥ |_

 

**              	dattvā tu dakṣiṇāṃ śaktyā svadhākāram udāharet |**

**              	vācyatām ity anujñātaḥ prakṛtebhyaḥ svadhocyatām || 1.240 ||**

 

svadhākārodāharaṇaṃ "svadhāṃ vācayiṣye" iti | taiś ca "vācyatām" ity anujñātaḥ prakṛtebhyaḥ pitṛbhyo mātāmahebhyaś ca svadhocyatām iti brūyāt || 240 ||

 

_tatas te 'pi |_

 

                    	**brūyur astu svadhety ukte bhūmau siñcet tato jalam |**

**              	prīyantām iti cāhaivaṃ viśvedevā jalaṃ dadat || 1.241 ||**

 

bhūmivacanāt kuśavyāvṛttiḥ | tataḥśabdas tu piṇḍapitṛyajñād ālocyety evamarthaḥ | tataś ca "ūrjaṃ vahantī" (VS 2.34) ity aneneti labhyate | vaiśvadevikebhyaś ca brāhmaṇebhyo jalaṃ dadat svayam evāha: "viśvedevāḥ prīyantām" iti | na vācayed, āheti vacanāt || 241 ||

 

_idaṃ cānyat |_

 

                    	**dātāro no vivardhantāṃ vedasaṃtatir eva ca |**

**              	śraddhā ca no mā vyagamad bahu deyaṃ ca no 'stv iti || 1.242 ||**

**                    	uktvoktvā ca priyā vācaḥ praṇipatya visarjayet |**

**              	vāje vāja iti prītaḥ pitṛpūrvaṃ visarjanam || 1.243 ||**

 

visarjanam eva pitṛpūrvam, anyat sarvaṃ devapūrvam ity abhiprāyaḥ || 242–243 ||

 

_idaṃ ca kuryāt |_

 

                    	**yasmiṃs te saṃsravāḥ pūrvam arghyapātre niveśitāḥ |**

**              	pitṛpātraṃ taduttānaṃ kṛtvā viprān visarjayet || 1.244 ||**

 

pitṛpātravacanaṃ mātāmahapātranivṛttyartham || 244 ||

 

_evaṃ brāhmaṇān utthāpya |_

 

**              	pradakṣiṇam anuvrajya bhuñjīta pitṛsevitam |**

**              	brahmacārī niśāṃ tāṃ tu niyatātmā saha dvijaiḥ || 1.245 ||**

 

syād iti śeṣaḥ | pitrarthatvād apradakṣiṇanivṛttyarthaṃ pradakṣiṇavacanam | bhuñjīta pitṛsevitam ity anyatrābhojanārthaṃ, punaḥ pākanivṛttyarthaṃ vā | tataś ca pūrvam eva hantakārādyānvahikaṃ karma kṛtvā tataḥ śrādddhanityāvaseyam | niyatātmā tāṃ rātriṃ brāhmaṇaiḥ saha brahmacārī syāt | tām iti ca prayatnātirekaḥ ṛtāv api brahmacaryārtham | tuśabdo vicikitsāpanodārthaḥ | niyatātmavacanaṃ ca brāhmaṇabrahmacaryākaraṇe 'py avaiguṇyajñāpanārtham, anadhyāyārthaṃ vā | yat tu purastād "ātmavāñ chuciḥ" ity uktaṃ, tan niścitaparalokasyaivādhikārajñāpanārtham | sarvārthaṃ vāviśeṣāt tad draṣṭavyam | śucivacanṃ ca tatra tatra bāhyaśaucārtham | samāhitavacanaṃ caikāgryārtham | "akrodhano 'tvaraḥ" ity anaśnataḥ kṣutpīḍitasya svabhāvaprāptakrodhādipratiṣedhārtham | evam anyāny api yathārthaṃ vivektavyāni | smṛtyantarāṇi ca sarvatra vyākhyānākṣiptāni jñapakatvenodāhartavyāni,

                    	śrāddhaṃ kṛtvā paraśrāddhe yastu bhuñjīta vihvalaḥ |

ityevamādīni | granthātirekabhītes tv anupanyāsaḥ || 245 ||

 

_sarvaprakṛtibhūtaṃ śrāddham upanyasya vikāropadeśam idānīm āha |_

 

**              	evaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā vṛddhau nāndīmukhān pitṝn |**

**              	yajanti dadhikarkandhūmiśrāḥ piṇḍā yavaiḥ kriyāḥ || 1.246 ||**

 

yathā ca śrāddham uktam amāvāsyādau, evam eva vṛddhāv api | ayaṃ tu viśeṣaḥ: ādita eva pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā sarvaṃ śrāddhaṃ kuryāt | pradakṣiṇavacanaṃ cāpasavyādinivṛttyartham api | kuta etat | yata āha yajantīti | asyāyam arthaḥ | devatātvenātra pitaro na saṃpradānatvena | tataś ca pitṝṇām api devatātvāt taddharmā eva yajñopavītādayaḥ pravartante, na pitṛdharmāḥ prācīnāvitādayaḥ | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

                    	pitṝṇāṃ rūpam āsthāya devā annam adanti hi | iti |

ayaṃ viśeṣaḥ: pitṝn āvāhayiṣya ity evamādiṣu nāndīmukhaśabdaḥ prayoktavyaḥ | piṇḍadānaṃ tu nāmagotreṇaiva | dadhikarkandhūmiśrāś ca piṇḍāḥ kāryāḥ | karkandhūr badaram | miśravacanāc cānnenaiva piṇḍāḥ, yavais tilārthāḥ kāryāḥ | devatvād eva yavaprāptau tadvacanād vaiśvadeve 'pi tilaprāptir astīti jñāpayati | tataś ca prakṛtau vaiśvadevike vaikalpikās tilā ity avaseyam | devatvād eva ca svadhāvacananivṛttiḥ | prayogas tu prapañcanīyaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca pūrvaṃ śrāddham api vṛddhāv upadiṣṭam: "amāvāsyāṣṭakā vṛddhiḥ" iti (YDh 1.214) | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | vṛddhau tu nimitte pūrvaṃ tu yac chrāddham ābhyudayikākhyaṃ, tasyāyaṃ vidhiḥ yathā samāvartanādyārambhe | yat tūtpannāyāṃ vṛddhau putrajanmādilakṣaṇāyāṃ, tat pūrvavad eveti vyavasthā | yad vā nimittamātratayaiva tatra tatra vṛddhyupādānam | iha tu prakāropadeśa iti vyākhyeyam || 246 ||

 

_athānyad api vikārabhūtaṃ śrāddham āha |_

 

                    	**ekoddiṣṭaṃ daivahīnam ekārghyaikapavitrakam |**

**              	āvāhanāgnaukaraṇarahitaṃ hy apasavyavat || 1.247 ||**

 

ekaṃ pretam uddiśya yat kriyate tad ekoddiṣṭam | tac ca pūrvavad eva | ayaṃ tu viśeṣaḥ: vaiśvadevikakarmahīnam ekaś cārghyaḥ | tatrāpy ekaṃ pavitram | asmād eva ca jñāyate 'nyatra pavitradvayam iti | ekadevatātvād evārghyaikatvasiddhau tadvacanaṃ pavitrasaṃkhyāvidhānārtham | asmād eva caitad api jñāyate: devatāsaṃkhyayaivārghyakaraṇaṃ na brāhmaṇasaṃkhyayā, nāniyamo vety āśaṅkanīyam | ayaṃ cānyo viśeṣaḥ: āvāhanāgnaukaraṇarahitaṃ syāt | kutaḥ prāptir iti cet | yato 'pasavyavad etad bhavati | apasavyasādhanatvād apasavyaṃ pārvaṇaṃ, tadvad etat syāt | na saṃnihitābhyudayikavad ity arthaḥ || 247 ||

 

_ayaṃ cānyo viśeṣaḥ |_

 

**              	upatiṣṭhatām ity akṣayyasthāne vipravisarjane |**

**              	abhiramyatām iti vaded brūyus te 'bhiratāḥ sma ha || 1.248 ||**

 

upatiṣṭhatām ity akṣayyam astv ity asya sthāne brūyāt | vipravisarjane ca vāje vāja ity asmin vaktavye 'bhiramyatām ity etat | ayaṃ cātra viśeṣaḥ: abhiratāḥ smeti brāhmaṇā brūyuḥ | haśabdo 'vadhāraṇārthaḥ | etad eva syān na vāje vāja ity arthaḥ | anyatra pratyāmnānād bādha iti jñāpitaṃ bhavati || 248 ||

 

_idaṃ cānyad vaikṛtaṃ śrāddhaṃ pretasya mṛtāhād vā saṃvatsare pūrṇe prāg api vā kāraṇāntarāt |_

 

**              	gandhodakatilair yuktaṃ kuryāt pātracatuṣṭayam |**

**              	arghyārthaṃ pitṛpātreṣu pretapātraṃ prasecayet || 1.249 ||**

 

gandhodakatilair yuktaṃ pātracatuṣṭayaṃ kuryāt | trīṇi pitṝṇām ekaṃ pretasya | kim artham | arghyārtham | tataś ca pratyāmnānāt prākṛtārghyanivṛttiḥ | tac ca pretapātraṃ pitṛpātreṣu tridhā vibhajyāvasecayet | pretaśabdena ca kecid vṛddhaprapitāmahaṃ vyācakṣate, prakarṣeṇetaḥ preta iti vyutpādayanti, tadīyaṃ ca pātraṃ pitrādiprātreṣv āsecayanti | tat punar na yuktaṃ, smṛtyantaravirodhāt | "piṇḍakaraṇe prathamaḥ pitṝṇāṃ pretaḥ syāt putravāṃś cet" iti pāraskaraḥ (PārG 3.10.50) | na ca vṛddhasyāputratvāśaṅkopapattiḥ | na cārvācīna āseko yuktaḥ, sakṛd ūhya iva "parāñcaḥ pitaraḥ" ity āmnāyavirodhāt | rūḍhyā ca pretaśabdaḥ prathama eva vartate, sarvatra prayogadarśanāt | yogo 'pi ca tadgata evānugantavyaḥ, na tu tatsaṃbhavamātrād rūḍhyatikramo yukta ity anayā diśā bhrāntyapanodaḥ kāryaḥ || 249 ||

 

_kiṃ tūṣṇīm eva secayet | nety ucyate |_

 

                    	**ye samānā iti dvābhyāṃ śeṣaṃ tv arghyādi pūrvavat |**

**              	etat sapiṇḍīkaraṇam ekoddiṣṭaṃ striyā api || 1.250 ||**

 

"ye samānāḥ" (VS 19.45) iti dvābhyām ṛgbhyāṃ pitṛpātreṣv āsekaḥ | śeṣaṃ pūrvavat pārvaṇavat | ācared ity arthaḥ | kuta etat | pātratrayaliṅgāt | pradarśanārthaṃ cārghyavacanam | tataś ca piṇḍadānam apy evam eva | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ: "etenaiva piṇḍo vyākhyātaḥ" iti | etac caikoddiṣṭapārvaṇayor vilakṣaṇaṃ sapiṇḍīkaraṇākhyaṃ śrāddhaṃ pratyetavyam | saṃjñākaraṇam ataḥ paraṃ sahaiva piṇḍadānaniyamārtham | "ekoddiṣṭaṃ striyā api" mātur api bhavati | sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ tu pitur evety arthaḥ | ayaṃ ca mātāmahaiḥ saha sapiṇḍīkaraṇapratiṣedhaḥ, taiḥ saha piṇḍadānāt | strībhis tu saha sapiṇḍīkaraṇam asty eva, smṛtyantarāt | yad vā etat sapiṇḍīkaraṇam ekoddiṣṭaṃ striyā api ity asyāyam arthaḥ: eka ācāryā updiśantīty ekoddiṣṭaṃ, striyā apy etat sapiṇḍīkaraṇam astīti | sarvathā strībhiḥ saha sapiṇḍīkaranāniṣedhaḥ || 250 ||

 

_smṛtyantaroktaṃ sapiṇḍīkaraṇasya kāladvayam abhipretyāha |_

 

**              	arvāk sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ yasya saṃvatsarād bhavet |**

**              	tasyāpy annaṃ sodakumbhaṃ dadyāt saṃvatsaraṃ dvije || 1.251 ||**

 

sapiṇḍīkaraṇāt pṛthagdānaniṣedhe prāpte 'pavādārthaḥ ślokaḥ | dvijagrahaṇaṃ dānasaṃbandhād brāhmaṇārtham eva | caturthyarthe saptamī chando'nurodhāt || 251 ||

 

_kiṃ punaḥ sapiṇḍīkṛtasya pṛthagpiṇḍatā nāsty eva | samākhyānād evaṃ khalu prāptam | asyāpavādaḥ |_

 

                    	**mṛtāhani ca kartavyaṃ pratimāsaṃ tu vatsaram |**

**              	pratisaṃvatsaraṃ caiva śrāddhaṃ vai māsikārthavat || 1.252 ||**

 

mṛto yasminn ahani, tasminn eva śrāddaṃ kurvīta | ahaḥśabdas tithyarthaḥ | tataś ca pratipadādau yasyām eva mṛtaḥ, tasyām eva kuryāt | caśabdāt saṃskārāhani ca | "tataḥ saṃvatsare pretāyānnaṃ dadyād, yasminn ahani pretaḥ syāt" iti saṃskārāhani ca sraddhaṃ darśayati, pretaśabdasya saṃskāryavacanatvāt | kuta etat | mṛtāyeti vaktavye pretāyeti vacanāt | smṛtita āmnāyāc ca | tathā ca pāraskaraḥ: "pretaspṛśo grāmaṃ na praviśeyur ā nakṣatradarśanāt" iti (PārG 3.10.35) pretaśabdaṃ saṃskāryavacana darśayati | manur api |

                    	ahnā caikena rātryā ca trirātrair eva ca tribhiḥ |

                    	pretaspṛśo viśudhyanti | iti | (MDh 5.64)

tathā śavasparśane snānam evoktam |

                    	śavaṃ tatspṛṣinaṃ caiva spṛṣṭvā snānena śudhyati | iti | (MDh 5.85)

āmnāyaś ca: "etad vai paramaṃ tapo yat pretam araṇyaṃ nayanti, yat pretam agnāv abhyādadhati" iti saṃskārapravṛttāv eva pretaśabdaṃ darśayati | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> etad viparītaṃ, pretasya sato 'raṇyanayanopadeśāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span>, anyatrābhidhānād "yo vai kaścin mriyate sa śavaḥ" iti | ato mṛtamātravacanaḥ śavaśabdaḥ, saṃskāryavacanaś ca pretaśabdaḥ | ataś ca yasminn ahani pretaḥ syāt saṃskṛtaḥ syād ity ayam evāsyārthaḥ | tatrāsaṃskṛtasya śrāddhalopo mā bhūd ity ācāryasya mṛtāhargrahaṇam | iyaṃ cātra vyavasthā: yo na saṃskṛtaḥ, tasya mṛtāhani | anyasya saṃskārāhany eva | yasya tūbhayam api na jñātaṃ, tasya yadādhikṛtānāṃ tattvato maraṇāvagatiḥ, tad ahar eva sāmarthyāt kuryāt | anyathā hy aviśeṣeṇaiva vihitaikoddiṣṭalopaḥ syāt | kim etad antardaśāha eva srāddhaṃ kuryāt | neti brūmaḥ | pratimāsam eva nāntardaśāha ity avadhāraṇārthas tuśabdaḥ | kiyantaṃ kālam | yāvad vatsaram | paratas tu pratisaṃvatsaram eva | caśabdaḥ śastrahatādeḥ kṛṣṇacaturdaśyarthaḥ, tripakṣādyarthaś ca | sapiṇḍīkṛtasya pṛthakpiṇḍābāvaprasaktāv āha: "śrāddaṃ vai māsikārthavat" kuryāt | vaiśabdaḥ samākhyābādhanārthaḥ | arthaśabdo vidhānārthaḥ | yathā vihitaṃ māsikaṃ, tathety arthaḥ | tataś ca māsikavidhānavat sapiṇḍīkṛtasyāpy ekoddiṣṭam asty eveti ślokārthaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca māsikaṃ pārvaṇam evocyate,

                    	piṇḍānāṃ māsikaṃ śrāddam anvāhāryaṃ vidur budhāḥ | (MDh 3.122)

iti māsikavacanāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">naitad evam</span> | evaṃ sati sapiṇḍīkaraṇāt prāg api pārvaṇavat syāt | tatraitad virudhyeta,

                    	asapiṇḍakriyākarma dvijāteḥ saṃsthitasya tu | (MDh 3.247)

iti, saṃvatsare vā sapiṇḍīkaraṇavidhir anarthakaḥ syāt | samākhyayaiva siddhe ślokānarthakyam eva syāt | tasmāt smṛtyantaroktam ekoddiṣṭam eva māsikaśabdena pratyetavyam | tathā ca yamaḥ:

                    	sapiṇḍīkaraṇād ūrdhvam ṛte kṛṣṇacaturdaśīm |

                    	pratisaṃvatsarād anyad ekoddiṣṭaṃ na kārayet ||

tathā |

                    	varṣe varṣe tu kartavyā mātāpitros tu saṃnatiḥ |

                    	adaivaṃ bhojayec chrāddhaṃ piṇḍam ekaṃ ca nirvapet || iti |

yat punar manoḥ "asapiṇḍakriyākarma" ity upakramya,

                    	saha piṇḍakriyāyāṃ tu kṛtāyām asya dharmataḥ |

                    	anayaivāvṛtā kāryaṃ piṇḍanirvapaṇaṃ sutaiḥ || iti | (MDh 3.248)

anayaiveti saṃnihitapārvaṇāvṛdupadeśaḥ, tad anyatra pratisaṃvatsarād avaseyam | tathedam api,

                    	pradānaṃ yatra yatraiṣāṃ sapiṇḍīkaraṇāt param |

                    	tat syāt pārvaṇavat sarvam anyatrābhyudayāt pitṝn ||

iti, tad api pratisaṃvatsarād anyatraiva | atha vā, mānavam apy ekoddiṣṭavidhānāyaiva | anayaiveti saṃnihitataratvād edoddiṣṭāvṛd eva gṛhyate | na pārvaṇāvṛd, vyavahitatvāt, ekoddiṣṭe 'pi tv āvṛtsaṃbhavāt | kim arthaṃ tarhi vacanaṃ, sapiṇḍīkaraṇam iti samākyānāt sahapiṇḍadānāśaṅkā mā bhūd iti | itaratā pūrvaślokāt samākhyānāc ca tatsiddher ārambho vyartha eva syāt | tasmāt sahapiṇḍakriyāyāṃ tv ityapiśabdārthas tuśabdaḥ, saṃśayavyāvṛttyartho vā, na samākhyānamātrād vyāmohaḥ kārya iti sapiṇḍīkṛtasyāpy anayaivaikoddiṣṭāvṛtā kāryam ity arthaḥ | evaṃ ca sati sarvadaivaikoddiṣṭaprasaṅge pārvaṇaśrāddhavidhānasāmarthyād ācāryavacanāc ca mṛtāhanītyādeḥ pratisaṃvatsarādāv evaikoddiṣṭam, anyatra pārvaṇavad eveti vyavasthā | yat tu "pradānaṃ yatra yatraiṣām" iti, tat prācīnāvītādyarthaṃ na piṇḍatritvārtham, "anyatrābhyudayāt" ity apavādāt | kiṃ ca, eṣām iti bahuvacanād yatra yatra bahūnāṃ dānaṃ pitṝn uddiśya prāptaṃ tatra tatraivam iti gamyate, na tu yatra pradānaṃ tatra bahava iti | pitṛvacanaṃ ca pretavyāvṛttyartham eva | tathā ca bhṛguḥ |

                    	varṣe varṣe tu kartavyā mātāpitros tu saṃnatiḥ |

                    	adaivaṃ bhojayec chrāddaṃ piṇḍam ekaṃ ca nirvapet || iti |

tataḥ saṃvatsare saṃvatsare pretāyānnaṃ dadyād iti coditam eva | anye tu kutaścid āgamayyemaṃ ślokaṃ paṭhanti:

                    	yaḥ sapiṇḍīkṛtaṃ pretaṃ pṛthak piṇḍena yojayet |

                    	vidhighnas tena bhavati pitṛhā copajāyate || iti |

ayaṃ tv aspaṣṭamūlatvād akiṃcitkaraḥ | kiṃ ca, asyāpy uktaviṣayataiva, uktatvān nyāyasya | atha vā ayam apy ekoddiṣṭadyotanārtha eva | ayam asyārthaḥ: yaḥ sapiṇḍīkṛtam iti vyāmohāt pretadharmaikapiṇḍārhaṃ pretaṃ pratisaṃvatsarādau naiva pṛthak piṇḍe yojayet, sa tena vyāmohenaikoddiṣṭavidhighno bhavatītyādi | yad vā pṛthagbhāvaḥ piṇḍānāṃ yasmiṃs tat pṛthakpiṇḍaṃ pārvaṇam eva, tatraiva ca yojanaṃ saṃbhavati, naikoḍḍiṣṭe, dvitīyāpekṣatvād yogasya iti | kiṃ ca sahapiṇḍadānprasaktau yukta ārambhaḥ, anyathā tu nirnimitta eva syāt, prāptyabhāvad ity alaṃ prasaṅgena || 252 ||

 

_sarvaśrāddheṣu prātisviko bheda uktaḥ piṇḍadānāntaḥ | sādhāraṇaṃ tv idānīm āha |_

 

                    	**piṇḍāṃs tu go'javiprebhyo dadyād agnau jale 'pi vā |**

**              	prakṣipet satsu vipreṣu dvijocchiṣṭaṃ na mārjayet || 1.253 ||**

 

viprādibhyaḥ piṇḍaṃ dadyat, agnāv udake vā prakṣiped na svecchayā viniyuñjīta | brāhmaṇeṣu cānutthiteṣu pitrarthabrāhmaṇocchiṣṭaṃ na mārjayet | dvitīyaṃ dvijagrahaṇaṃ pitrarthabrāhmaṇārtham | ayaṃ cāntyaḥ kalpaḥ | śaktiviṣaye tu vāsiṣṭham |

                    	ucchiṣṭaṃ na pramṛjyāt tu yāvan nāstam ito raviḥ | iti | (VaDh 11.22)

<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> etad vaikṛtaśrāddhābhidhānāt prāg eva vaktavyam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | pratipattīnāṃ tv apravṛttyartho 'yam ārambhaḥ | tataḥ saṃsravādhānāder apravṛttisiddhiḥ | vakṣyamāṇasya caivaṃ sādhāraṇyāt pāyasādidravyam api sarvārthaṃ syāt | anyathā pitṛtuṣṭyarthopadeśād ābhyudayikādāv abhāvaśaṅkāpi syāt | kāmasaṃyogāc caivaṃ tithyādyāśrayāḥ sarvārthāḥ bhavanti, anyathā prakṛtāv eva syuḥ, phalasyānatideśād ityādikramabhedaprayojanam avaseyam || 253 ||

 

_kāni punaḥ pitṛtuṣṭyarthāny annāni | imānīty ucyate |_

 

**              	haviṣyānnena vai māsaṃ pāyasena tu vatsaram |**

**              	mātsyahāriṇaaurabhraśākunacchāgapārṣataiḥ || 1.254 ||**

**              	aiṇarauravavārāhaśāśair māṃsair yathākramam |**

**              	māsavṛddhyā hi tuṣyanti dattair iha pitāmaḥāḥ || 1.255 ||**

 

haviṣyānnena vrīhyādinā māsikī tṛptiḥ, matsyādibhiḥ śaśāntair dvitrimāsādyekādaśamāsāntā | pāyasena tu gavyena saṃvatsaram | tathā ca manuḥ |

                    	saṃvatsaraṃ tu gavyena payasā pāyasena vā | iti | (MDh 3.271)

pitāmahagrahaṇaṃ ca mātāmahādyupalakṣaṇam api prakaraṇāviśeṣād draṣṭavyam | matsyahāriṇau prasiddhau | aurabhram āvikam | śākunaṃ śakunihatabhakṣyaprāṇiṣu bhavam | pārṣataṃ pṛṣanmāṃsam | eṇaḥ śiśuḥ kṛṣṇamṛga eva | jātyantaram ity anye | rurur bṛhacchṛṅgo mṛga eva | varāhaḥ sūkaraḥ | śaśaḥ prasiddhaḥ | tuṣṭivacanānusārāc ca yathārthavādaṃ dānavidhikalpanā, na tu pāyasadānāt saṃvatsaṃ tṛptā eva pitara iti śrāddhākaraṇam || 254–255 ||

 

_imāni tv atituṣṭyarthāni |_

 

                    	**khaḍgāmiṣaṃ mahāśalkaṃ madhu munyannam eva ca |**

**              	lohāmiṣaṃ kālaśākaṃ māṃsaṃ vārdhrāṇasasya ca || 1.256 ||**

**              	yad dadāti gayāsthaś ca sarvam ānantyam aśnute |**

**              	tathā varṣe trayodaśyāṃ maghāsu ca na saṃśayaḥ || 1.257 ||**

 

khaḍgāmiṣaṃ gandhakamāṃsam | mahāśalkaḥ śarabha iti kecit | tat tv amedhyaśruter ayuktam | ato matsyaviśeṣa eva kaścin mahāśalkaḥ pratyetavyaḥ | munyannaṃ śyāmākādi | loho lohitacchāgaḥ | āmiṣavacanaṃ paśvālambhāśaṅkānivṛttyartham | vārdhrāṇaso vṛddhacchāgaḥ | kaṅkaṇāhir ity anye | punar māṃsavacanaṃ stutyartham | tathā cāmnāyaḥ: "etad vai paramam annādyaṃ yan māṃsam" iti | gayāsthaś ceti caśabdo maghādikālasamuccayārthaḥ | uttaratra tu samastālābhe pratyekam api dadyād iti vikalpārthaḥ | sarvaśabdād anyad api yad vātra dadāti, tad evākṣayaṃ pitṝn prāpnotīty arthaḥ | asaṃśayavacanād arthavādād eva phalakalpanā na stutimātrāvasāyitvam iti mantavyam || 256–257 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvad deśakālāśrayaṃ naiyogikaṃ śrāddham uktvedānīṃ kāmasaṃyogenāha |_

 

**              	kanyāṃ kanyāvedinaś ca paśūn mukhyān sutān api |**

**              	dyūtaṃ kṛṣivaṇijyaṃ ca dviśaphaikaśaphaṃ tathā || 1.258 ||**

**              	brahmavarcasvinaḥ putrān svarṇarūpye sakupyake |**

**              	jñātiśraiṣṭhyaṃ sarvakāmān āpnoti śrāddhadaḥ sadā || 1.259 ||**

**              	pratipatprabhṛti hy etā varjayitvā caturdaśīm |**

**              	śastreṇa tu hatā ye vai teṣāṃ tatra pradīyate || 1.260 ||**

 

ślokatrayasyāpy ayam arthaḥ: sārvakālam eva pratipatprabhṛtyamāvāsyāntāsu tithiṣu caturdaśīvyatirekeṇa pratyekaṃ yathākrameṇa kanyālābhādīni caturdaṣa phalāny avaseyāni | pratipadi śrāddhakaraṇāt kanyāṃ duhitṛkāmāḥ kanyāvedinaś ca pariṇayanakāmās tāṃ prāpnuvantīti | evam uttaratrāpi yojyam | paśavaś chāgādayaḥ | mukhyāḥ sutā brāhmīputrādayaḥ | dyūtakṛṣivāṇijyeṣu lābhātirekaḥ | dviśphaṃ gavādi | ekaśapam aśvādi | brahmavarcasvinaḥ śrutādhyayanasaṃpannāḥ | svarṇarūpye prasiddhe | kupyaṃ tāmropaskarādi | sarvakāmāḥ prakṛtā eva | spaṣṭam anyat || 258–260 ||

 

_tathedam api kāmasaṃyogenaiva |_

 

**          	svargaṃ hy apatyam ojaś ca śauryaṃ kṣetraṃ balaṃ tathā |**

**          	putrān śraiṣṭhyaṃ sasaubhāgyam apatyaṃ mukhyatāṃ sutān || 1.261 ||**

**          	pravṛttacakratāṃ putrāñ jñatibhyaḥ prabhutāṃ tathā |**

**          	arogitvaṃ yaśo vītaśokatāṃ paramāṃ gatim || 1.262 ||**

**          	dhanaṃ vidyāṃ bhiṣaksiddhiṃ kupyaṃ gāvo hy ajāvikam |**

**          	aśvān āyuś ca vidhivad yaḥ śrāddhaṃ pariveṣayet || 1.263 ||**

**          	kṛttikādibharṇyantaṃ sa kāmān āpnuyād imān |**

**          	āstikaḥ śraddadhānaś ca vyapetamadamatsaraḥ || 1.264 ||**

 

idam api ślokacatuṣṭayaṃ pūrvavad vyākhyeyam | kṛttikādibharaṇyantāni saptaviṃśatir eva nakṣatrāṇi | tāvanty eva svargādīny api phalāni pratyekaṃ yathākramaṃ yojyāni | kṛttikāsu sarvakālaṃ śrāddhakaraṇāt svargaprāptiḥ | evaṃ rohiṇyādāv apatyādiprāptiyojanā | hiśabdādayaś ca pādapūraṇārthāḥ | evaṃ pūrvatrāpi vyākhyeyam | na cātra phalatayopanyāsād dyūtādikartavyatāpratiṣedhātikrameṇa tu pravṛttānām abhyupāya iti mantavyam | spaṣṭam anyat || 261–264 ||

 

_atha kim etac chrāddhaṃ kartur eva phalapradam uta pitṝṇām apy upakārakam iti | ubhayārtham iti brūmaḥ, tathaivāvagamāt | uktā hi pitṛtṛptiḥ kartuś ca kāmāvāptiḥ | satyam uktā | anupapannā (?) tu sā | kathaṃ hi svakarmānusārād anekavidhayonigatapitṛtuṣṭyupapattiḥ | śāstrapramāṇakatvād asyārthasyācodyam etat | kiṃ ca |_

 

**              	vasurudrāditisutāḥ pitaraḥ śrāddhadevatāḥ |**

**              	prīṇayanti manuṣyāṇāṃ pitṝñ chrāddhena tarpitāḥ || 1.265 ||**

 

agnyādayo nakṣatrāntā vasavaḥ | prāṇādyātmaikādaś rudrāḥ | dvādaśa māsā ādityāḥ | ete nityā evārthāḥ pitaraḥ | eta eva śrāddhadevatāḥ pratyetavyāḥ | tasmād avirodhaḥ | evaṃ sati manuṣyapitṝṇāṃ kim āyātam | ucyate | ete devā vasvādayaḥ prītāḥ prīṇayanti yatratatrasthān manuṣyāṇāṃ pitṝn śrāddhāttarasānupradānenety (?) arthaḥ | sarvaprāṇigatatvāc caiṣāṃ sarvāvasthitapitṛtarpaṇasāmarthyam aviruddham | agnyādīnāṃ ca sarveṣām antarvartinyo devatā iṣyanta evety avirodhaḥ | pūrvam apy anenaivābhiprāyeṇa pitṝṇāṃ saṃpradānatvam uktam | pitṛbhyo dadyād iti coditatvāt tadupapattyapekṣām upapādayanto 'rthavādā api hi pramāṇam evety avadhārya nātīva kutārkikoktakusṛtyālīkacodyābhiniveśaḥ kāryaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> cācoditā eva vasvādayo devatāḥ | iyam eva hi taccodanety ucyamāne pūrvacoditapitṛdevatātvahāniḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">atrocyate</span> | vasvādīnāṃ ca devatātvābhidhānāt pitṝṇāṃ ca saṃpradānatvād avirodhaḥ | devā iti vaktavye devatā iti pādapūraṇārthaḥ | anarthaka eva vā talprayogaḥ | devo dānād iti ca vyutpādanād dātāro vasvādaya iti gamyate | tataś cāyam artho bhavati: yat kartrā pitṛbhyo dātum iṣṭaṃ tad vasvādayo yatratatrasthebhyaḥ sarvagatatvena samarthā dātum iti | ato 'navadyam | vasvādibhyo 'pi ca pradātṛvacanāt tṛptir asty evety avaseyam | yad vā pitṝṇāṃ rūpadvayam | saṃsārirūpatā vasvādirūpatā ca | tatra ye vasvādirūpatā prāptās te 'nyebhyaḥ saṃsaribhyo vibhutvāt tṛptiṃ kurvantīty arthaḥ | yatra cābhyudayādau devatātvenaiva pitṝṇāṃ saṃbandhaḥ, tatra vasvādirūpatayaiva devatātvam | codanānusārāt tu nāmagotreṇaiva | evaṃ ca jānato 'dhikāra ity avaseyam | atha vā anyārtha evāyaṃ ślokaḥ | vasvādayo 'pi śrāddhadevatā eva | tatreyaṃ viṣayakḷptiḥ | yaḥ pitṛnāmānabhijñaḥ sa vasvādibhyas tribhyo dadyāt | jīvapitṛko vābhyudaye, anyas tu pitṛbhyas tribhya eveti | tathā cāśvalāyanaḥ: "nāmāny avidvāṃs tatapitāmahaprapitāmaheti" (ĀśŚr 2.6.24) nāmānabhijñasyādhikāraṃ darśayati | smṛtidvayāc ca vikalpaḥ, vasvādipadair vādeśas tatādipadair veti | evaṃ ca saty arthavādaprāptasaṃpradānānusārād dadyād ity utpatticodanopapattiḥ | evaṃ ca vidvadbhiḥ putraiḥ śrāddhenāpyāyyamānāḥ pitaraḥ svayam apuṇyakṛto 'pi vasvādipadaṃ labhante ity avaseyam || 265 ||

 

_tac ca prāpya tataḥ |_

 

**              	āyuḥ prajñāṃ dhanaṃ vidyāṃ svargaṃ mokṣaṃ sukhāni ca |**

**              	prayacchanti tathā rājyaṃ prītā nṝṇāṃ pitāmahāḥ || 1.266 ||**

 

apaṣṭārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 266 ||

 

 

        	evam etac chrāddham ācāryamatenāmāvāsyādiṣu tithiṣu pitṛdveṣibhir api codanānusārāc chaktiviṣaye niyogataḥ kartavyam | aśaktau tu māvavaṃ pratyetavyam |

                    	anena vidhinā śrāddhaṃ trirabdasyeha virvapet |

                    	hemantagrīṣmavarṣāsu pāñcayajñikam anvaham || iti | (MDh 3.281)

pāñcayajñikavacanaṃ dṛṣṭāntārtham | yathaiva pratyakṣaśrutyanusārād aśaktāv api "ahar ahar dadyād odapātrādi" (ŚB 11.5.6.2) ity anvahaṃ pāñcayajñikakaraṇaṃ, tathānenāpi smārtavidhinoktaṃ: nirvicikitsam iha gṛhāśame vasatā trirvarṣasyātyantam aśaktenāpi kāryam iti | agnihotriṇaś cāyaṃ kalpaḥ | suṣṭhv apy aśaktau,

                    	na darśena vinā śrāddham āhitāgner dvijanmanaḥ | iti | (MDh 3.282)

"na śrāddhena vinā darśe" iti vibhaktivyatyayaḥ | anyathā hy asāmañjasyaṃ syāt | yasya tv aupāsanam api nāsti, tasya śrāddhānadhikara eva | yataḥ,

                    	na paitṛyajñiko homo laukike 'gnau vidhīyate | iti | (MDh 3.282)

tadabhāve ca śrāddhavaiguṇyam | sarvasyaiva tv atyantāśaktāv ayaṃ kalpaḥ |

                    	yad eva tarpayaty adbhiḥ pitṝn snātvā samāhitaḥ |

                    	tenaiva sarvam āpnoti pitṛyajñakriyāphalam || (MDh 3.283)

ity eva tāvan manuḥ | "śākenāpi nāparapakṣam atikrāmed māsi māsi cāśanam iti śrutiḥ" (PārG śrāddhasūtra 1) iti ca kātyāyanaḥ | tac cāparapakṣikārtham iti saṃpradāyaḥ | sarvathā śaktyanusārād aśāṭhyena śrāddhakaraṇam iti paramārthaḥ |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">kasmāt</span> punar mānavo 'pi śrāddhakalpa ācāryeṇa nopanibaddhaḥ | samānārthatvāt, anenaiva ca prayojanāvāpteḥ | na ca sarvaṃ sarvasmartṛbhir vaktavyaṃ, smṛtibahutvasyānarthakyaprasaṅgāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span> | ekakālīnaṃ yat puṃso naiyogikaṃ karyaṃ, tat sarvaiḥ smartavyam, anyathā sāpekṣatvaprasaṅgāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca yad yenopalabdhaṃ, sa tad eva smartuṃ kṣamaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">smartṛsvarūpānibhijña! maivam</span> | yena hy aśeṣato vedārtho nāvagataḥ, sa katham ivopadiśet | upadiśan vā kathaṃ vidvadbhir grāhyavacanaḥ syāt | ādṛtāś ca manvādayaḥ, tasmād akhilavedārthābhijñāḥ, tadupadeśāc cānyasyāvagater anuṣṭhānāvirodhaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evaṃ sati sarvaṃ sarvasmartṛbhir upadeṣṭavyam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">bāḍham</span> | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kathaṃ</span> tarhy anupadeśaḥ | kāraṇāntarāt | yathaiva śraddhaṃ samānārthatvān mānavam ācāryeṇa noktaṃ, tathā manunāpi mātāmahaśrāddhaṃ, vaikalpikatvāt | kuto vaikalpikatvam iti ced, asmād eva manvanabhidhānāt | yat tu nityatvam uktaṃ, tad ācāryābhiprāyeṇa | evaṃrūpāś ca vikalpāḥ draṣṭavyāḥ | tenaiva caśabdādihiḥ smṛtyantaroktārthāntarbhāvaḥ | yatra tv antarbhāvāsaṃbhavaḥ, tatra prayogārthāyāṃ smṛtāv anucyamānaṃ vaikalpikatvena draṣṭavyam | guṇārthāyāṃ tv anyaparatvāt svarūpābhidhānam atantram ity uktam evaitad "vaktāro dharmaśāstrāṇām" ity atra | sarvathā smṛtiracanāviśeṣān nirvicikitsāṃ pramāṇatām ālocya sarvam evamādi yathāyogaṃ vivicya vyākhyeyam | ata eva smṛtibahutvānarthakyacodyam apy acodyam eveti sthitam |

                    	iti viracita eṣa śrāddhakalpaḥ purāṇaḥ

                                	sphuṭavikaṭaviviktanyāyasandarbhagarbhaḥ |

                    	imam iti ca vivasvān yājñavalkyāya sākṣāt

                                	pitṛsamayavidhijñaḥ proktavāñ chrāddhadevaḥ ||

 

 

**iti śrāddhaprakaraṇam**

** **

**atha vināyakādikalpaprakaraṇam**

 

_evaṃ tāvac chrāddham upadiṣṭam, nimittasaṃyogau ca | idaṃ tv atra vaktavyam | kasmāt punar etāny anantaram eva svargādīni phalāni karmaṇo notpadyante | viśiṣṭaśarīropabhogyatvāt svargasyeti cet, putrādīnāṃ tarhy anantarotpādaprasaṅgaḥ | kasya caitad aniṣṭam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> adarśanād bhavataḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span> | nimittāntarāt tadadarśanaṃ, na tu karmaṇām anutpādakatvāt | kiṃ tannimittāntaram iti | ucyate |_

** **

**              	vināyakaḥ karmavighnasiddhyarthaṃ viniyojitaḥ |**

**              	gaṇānām ādhipatyāya rudreṇa brahmaṇā purā || 1.267 ||**

 

vināyakaśabdenātra vyāmoha ucyate | sa hi bhāvābhāvābhyāṃ karmavighnārthaṃ siddhyarthaṃ ca viruddhāsu kriyāsu puruṣanayanād vināyakaśabdavācyaḥ krodhādiṣv ārambhakatvenāpakarṣahetor gaṇasyādhipatye viniyukto rudreṇa | brahmaṇā śarīrasraṣṭrety arthaḥ | yad vā prākṛtāśubhakarmanicayo vināyakaśabdavācyaḥ | so 'pi svaphalotpādapravṛttau vividhaṃ manuṣyān nayan vināyaka eva | sa ca sāṃprataṃ karmaṇaḥ phalapradānapravṛttasya vighnārthaṃ rudrabrahmaśabdavācyāpūrvaśaktyā viniyojitaḥ prāṇigaṇānāṃ balavattvenādhipatyāyaiva pravṛttaḥ sarvathā svecchāpravṛttiṃ niruṇaddhīty arthaḥ | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |
