                    	yat tat pūrvakṛtaṃ karma na smarantīha mānavāḥ |

                    	tad idaṃ pāṇḍavaśreṣṭha daivam ity abhidhīyate || iti |

devair iva sṛṣṭaṃ daivam | rudreṇa brahmaṇā cety atrāpi yojyam | krodho vā rudraḥ | brahma śāstrīyaṃ vidhānam | tatra krodhopahatena yad brahma nādṛtaṃ tena brahmaṇā prākkṛtāśubhenaiva rūpeṇāyam idānīṃ krodhākhyo vināyako viniyukta ityādi yojyam | astu vā devataiva vināyako 'rthavādānusārāt | adhikāratas tu nityatvāvyāghātaḥ || 267 ||

 

_kathaṃ punaḥ prāktanāśubhasaṃyogaḥ puruṣasyāvagamyata ity āha |_

 

**              	tenopasṛṣṭo yas tasya lakṣaṇāni nibodhata |**

**              	svapne 'vagāhate 'tyarthaṃ jalaṃ muṇḍāṃś ca paśyati || 1.268 ||**

**              	kāṣāyavāsasaś caiva kravyādāṃś cādhirohati |**

**              	antyajair gardabhair uṣṭraiḥ sahaikatrāvatiṣṭhate || 1.269 ||**

**              	vrajamānas tathātmānaṃ manyate 'nugataṃ paraiḥ |**

**              	vimanā viphalārambhaḥ saṃsīdaty animittataḥ || 1.270 ||**

 

jāgradavasthāyām apy etāni kaunakhyādivat purākṛtāśubhakarmanimittāni draṣṭavyāni || 268–270 ||

 

_idaṃ tv atrātispaṣṭaṃ prāktanāśubhasaṃyoganimittam |_

 

**              	tenopasṛṣṭo labhate na rājyaṃ rājanandanaḥ |**

**              	kumārī na ca bhartaram apatyam garbham eva ca || 1.271 ||**

 

garbhiṇy apatyam ṛtumaty api na garbham iti ca yojyam || 271 ||

 

                    	**ācāryatvaṃ śrotriyaḥ san na śiṣyo 'dhyayanaṃ tathā |**

**              	vaṇig lābhaṃ na cāpnoti kṛṣiṃ caiva kṛṣīvalaḥ || 1.272 ||**

 

śrotriyaḥ śrutasaṃpanno 'py ācāryatvaṃ na labhate | śiṣyaś ca śuciḥ śobhano 'pramattaḥ śiṣyaguṇayukto 'py adhyāpakam adhyayanaṃ vā na labhata iti vyākhyeyam | udāharaṇārthaṃ caitat | sarvathā yo yad yogya iti śāstrato lokato vāvagataḥ sa tad alabhamānaḥ prāktanāśubhakarmopasṛṣṭa ity avaseyam || 272 ||

 

_ayaṃ tv atra pratisamādhiḥ |_

 

                    	**snapanaṃ tasya kartavyaṃ puṇye 'hni vidhipūrvakam |**

**              	gaurasarṣapakalkena sādyenocchāditasya tu || 1.273 ||**

**              	sarvauṣadhaiḥ sarvagandhair viliptaśirasas tathā |**

**              	bhadrāsanopaviṣṭasya svasti vācya dvijāñ chubhān || 1.274 ||**

 

tathā snapanaṃ kartavyam iti saṃbandhaḥ | puṇyāhaś candrabalādiyogaḥ | ucchādanam udvartanam | tac ca sadyaḥpiṣṭena gaurasarṣapakalkena | tuśabdāt tenaiva śiraso vilepanam | tathāśabdāc ca sarvauṣadhigandhair udvartanam | apratiṣiddhauṣadhagandhāpekṣaḥ sarvaśabdaḥ | bhadrāsanaṃ śobhanam āsanam | svastivācanaṃ brāhmaṇebhyo hiraṇyādidānam || 273–274 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

**              	aśvasthānād gajasthānād valmīkāt saṃgamād dhradāt |**

**              	mṛttikāṃ rocanāṃ gandhān gulguluṃ cāpsu saṃkṣipet || 1.275 ||**

**              	yā āhṛtā ekavarṇaiś caturbhiḥ kalaśair hradāt |**

**              	carmaṇy ānaḍuhe rakte sthāpyaṃ bhadrāsanaṃ tathā || 1.276 ||**

 

yathāyogaṃ kalpanā || 275–276 ||

 

_amī tu snapanamantrāḥ |_

 

                    	**sahasrākṣaṃ śatadhāram ṛṣibhiḥ pāvanaṃ kṛtam |**

**              	tena tvām abhiṣiñcāmi pāvamānīḥ punantu te || 1.277 ||**

**              	bhagaṃ te varuṇo rājā bhagaṃ sūryo bṛhaspatiḥ |**

**              	bhagam indraś ca vāyuś ca bhagaṃ saptarṣayo daduḥ || 1.278 ||**

**              	yat te keśeṣu daurbhāgyaṃ sīmante yac ca mūrdhani |**

**              	lalāṭe karṇayor akṣṇor āpas tad ghnantu te sadā || 1.279 ||**

 

tribhir mantraiḥ pratimantraṃ kalaśatrayeṇa snāpanam | caturthena tv aviśeṣāt sarvamantrair eva | mantrārthās tu vyākhyātṛbhyo 'vaseyāḥ || 277–279 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvat kalaśacatuṣṭayenāpi |_

 

**              	snātasya sārṣapaṃ tailaṃ sruveṇaudumbareṇa tu |**

**              	juhuyān mūrdhani kuśān savyena parigṛhya ca || 1.280 ||**

 

caśabdo dakṣiṇajānvañcanādiprakārārthaḥ || 280 ||

 

_amī tu homamantrāḥ |_

 

                    	**mitaś ca saṃmitaś caiva tathā sālakaṭaṅkaṭaḥ |**

**              	kūśmāṇḍarājaputraś ca japet svāhāsamanvitān || 1.281 ||**

 

catvāro vināyakamantrāḥ | etāny eva caturṇāṃ nāmāni | tatra svāhākārāntair japabalikarmaṇī, svarūpeṇaiva vā balikarmeti | ayaṃ ca prayogaprakāraḥ: mitāya svāhā, saṃmitāya svāhā, sālakaṭaṅkaṭāya svāhā, kūśmāṇḍarājaputrāya svāheti | caśabdadvayena mitasaṃitayor bhedaṃ darśayann itarayos tadabhāvāt samāsakaraṇāc cābhedaṃ darśayati | ataś catvāra eva mantrā iti || 281 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvad gṛha eva karma | ataḥ paraṃ tu |_

 

                    	**nāmabhir balimantraiś ca namaskārasamanvitaiḥ|**

**              	dadyāc catuṣpathe śūrpe kuśān āstīrya sarvataḥ|| 1.282 ||**

 

nāmāni mitādīni | balimantrā balidānavihitāḥ namaskriyā ityevamādayaḥ | atra hi baliliṅgayogo 'sti namo 'stu balim ebhyo harāmīti | upasthāne cāmbikādarśanāt strīmantratvād eta eva yuktāḥ | catuṣpathe kuśāstaraṇaṃ, na śūrpe | spaṣṭam anyat || 282 ||

 

_kiṃ punas tac chūrpe deyam |_

 

**              	kṛtākṛtāṃs taṇḍulāṃś ca palalaudanam eva ca |**

**              	matsyān pakvāṃs tathaivāmān māṃsam etāvad eva tu || 1.283 ||**

 

kṛtāḥ phalīkṛtāḥ | akṛtā aphalīkṛtāḥ | caśabdād odanam api dvirūpam eva | māṃsam apy etāvad eva pakvam āmaṃ cety arthaḥ || 283 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

**              	puṣpaṃ citraṃ sugandhaṃ ca surāṃ ca trividhām api |**

**              	mūlakaṃ pūrikāpūpāṃs tathaivaoḍḍerakasrajam || 1.284 ||**

 

etat sarvaṃ nāmabhir balimantraiś ca dattvā || 284 ||

 

_anantaram |_

 

**              	dūrvāsasarṣapakalkena dattvārghyaṃ pūrṇam añjalim |**

 

pūrvamantrair eva |

 

**              	vināyakasya jananīm upatiṣṭhet tato 'mbikām || 1.285 ||**

 

ambikā cātra buddhir ucyate | sā hy aśubhanimittaṃ lobhādiṃ janayati | yad vā, devy evāmbikā rudrapatnī, adhikāranityatvenety ubhayathāpy adoṣaḥ || 285 ||

 

_ayaṃ tūpasthānamantraḥ |_

 

**              	rūpaṃ dehi yaśo dehi bhagaṃ bhavati dehi me |**

**              	putrān dehi śriyaṃ puṇyān sarvakāmāṃś ca dehi me || 1.286 ||**

 

_evam upasthāya tataḥ |_

 

**              	śuklāmbaradharaḥ śuklamālyagandhānulepanaḥ |**

**              	brāhmaṇān bhojayed dadyād vastrayugmaṃ guror api || 1.287 ||**

 

guruḥ snāpakaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 287 ||

 

**              	evaṃ vināyakaṃ pūjya grahāṃś caivaṃ vidhānataḥ |**

**              	karmaṇāṃ phalam āpnoti śriyaṃ cāpnoty anuttamām || 1.288 ||**

 

aśubhakṣapaṇārthatvād asya karmaṇaḥ kṣīṇāśubhasaya karmaphalāvāptir anavadyā | yas tu puṇyakṛd ivopalabhyate, so 'py etat kṛtvā śriyam anuttamāṃ prāpnoti | atas tenāpi kartavyam eva, "ā mṛtyoḥ śriyam ākāṅkṣet" (YDh 1.152) iti vacanāt | grahapūjāvidhānaṃ ca vakṣyamāṇaṃ draṣṭavyam || 288 ||

 

_yas tv evam api karmaphalaṃ na prāpnuyāt, tasyāyam aparo 'bhyupāyaḥ |_

 

**              	ādityasya sadā pūjāṃ tilakasvāminas tathā |**

**              	mahāgaṇapateś caiva kurvan siddhim avāpnuyāt || 1.289 ||**

 

aviśeṣeṇa ceyaṃ smṛtiḥ | sarvapuṃsāṃ siddhyarthaṃ pūjāvidhir avaseyaḥ, sadāśabdasāmarthyāt | spaṣṭam anyat || 289 ||

 

**iti vināyakādikalpaprakaraṇam**

** **

**atha grahaśāntiprakaraṇam**

 

_grahānāṃ karmāvighnasiddhyarthaṃ pūjyatvaṃ vidhānata uktam | tadvidhānam adhunā vivakṣuḥ svātantryeṇāpi prayogasiddhyarthaṃ kāmasaṃyogenādhikārāntaram āha |_

 

                    	**śrīkāmaḥ śāntikāmo vā grahayajñaṃ samārabhet |**

**              	vṛṣṭyāyuḥpuṣṭikāmo vā tathaivābhicaran punaḥ || 1.290 ||**

 

punaḥśabdād avighnārthaṃ kṛtvā punaḥ kāmārthaṃ karaṇam || 290 ||

 

_ke punar amī grahā nāma |_

 

**              	sūryaḥ somo mahīputraḥ somaputro bṛhaspatiḥ |**

**              	śukraḥ śanaiścaro rāhuḥ ketuś ceti grahāḥ smṛtāḥ || 1.291 ||**

 

_kim ete gaganasthāḥ pūjyante | nety ucyate |_

 

**              	tāmrikāt sphaṭikād raktacandanāt svarṇakād ubhau |**

**              	rajatād ayasaḥ sīsād grahāḥ kāryāḥ kramād ime || 1.292 ||**

 

ubhau budhabṛhaspatī sauvarṇakau kāryau | ketus tu saṃnidhānāt sīsakād eva | ima iti vacanāt puruṣavigraheṇeti gamyate | arthavādotthād vetihāsād vigrahāvagatiḥ || 292 ||

 

_śaktyapekṣayā tu tāmrādyabhāve |_

 

**              	svarṇair vā paṭe lekhyā gandhamaṇḍalakeṣu vā |**

 

_sarvakalpeṣv eva |_

 

**              	yathāvarṇaṃ pradeyāni vāsāṃsi kusumāni ca || 1.293 ||**

**              	gandhāś ca balayaś caiva dhūpo deyaḥ sagulguluḥ |**

 

yathāvarṇaṃ tāmrādipratikṛtivarṇa evaiṣā varṇa ity avaseyam ||

 

_sarveṣāṃ cādityādīnāṃ grahāṇāṃ |_

 

**              	kartavyās tantravantaś ca caravaḥ pratidaivatam || 1.294 ||**

 

tantravantaḥ ekatantrā ity arthaḥ | caśabdāt pratyekaṃ pūjāvidhir avaseyaḥ || 294 ||

 

_amī tu sarvārthā pradhānamantrāḥ |_

 

**              	ākṛṣṇena imaṃ devā agnir mūrdhā divaḥ kakut |**

**              	udbudhyasveti ca ṛco yathāsaṃkhyaṃ prakīrtitāḥ || 1.295 ||**

**              	bṛhaspate ati yad aryas tathaivānnāt parisrutaḥ|**

**              	śaṃ no devīs tathā kāṇḍāt ketuṃ kṛṇvann imā api || 1.296 ||**

 

_pākayajñasāmānyena ca yajñavṛkṣamātrāt samitprasaktāv apavādam āha |_

 

**              	arkaḥ palāśakhadirāv apāmārgo 'tha pippalaḥ|**

**              	udumbaraḥ śamī dūrvā kuśāś ca samidhaḥ kramāt || 1.297 ||**

 

_idānīṃ saṃkhyāviśeṣārtham āha |_

 

**              	ekaikasyātrāṣṭaśatam aṣṭāviṃśatir eva vā |**

**              	hotavyā madhusarpirbhyāṃ dadhnā caiva samanvitāḥ || 1.298 ||**

 

yad vā, ayam apūrvaḥ samiddhomo 'ṅgatvena vidhīyate | tataś ca prāśanānte pūrvamantrair eva kartavyaḥ | vaikalpikaś cāyaṃ carubhiḥ saha samddhomavidhir iti saṃpradāyaḥ || 298 ||

 

_pakṣadvaye 'pi tu |_

 

                    	**gulaudanaṃ pāyasaṃ ca haviṣyaṃ kṣīraṣāṣṭikam |**

**              	dadhyodanaṃ haviḥ pūpān māṃsaṃ citrānnam eva ca || 1.299 ||**

**              	dadyād grahakramād etad dvijebhyo bhojanaṃ budhaḥ |**

**              	śaktito vā yathālābhaṃ satkṛtya vidhipūrvakam || 1.300 ||**

 

spaṣṭārthau ślokau || 299–300 ||

 

_evaṃ brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā tebhya eva |_

 

**            	dhenuṃ śaṅkham anaḍvāhaṃ kāñcanaṃ vasanaṃ hayam |**

**            	kṛṣṇāṃ gām āyasām chāgaṃ pradadyād daikṣiṇāḥ kramāt || 1.301 ||**

 

śaktyapekṣaṃ caiṣāṃ parimāṇam || 301 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvat samastagrahapūjā vighnopaśamanāya kāmasaṃyogena coktā | jyotiḥśāstrānusāreṇa tv ekaikam api |_

 

**              	yaś ca yasya yadā duḥsthaḥ sa taṃ yatnena pūjayet |**

 

_kasmāt |_

 

**              	brahmaṇaiṣāṃ varo dattaḥ pūjitāḥ pūjayiṣyatha || 1.302 ||**

 

pūjā ca pratyekam apy uktavidhilakṣanaiva || 302 ||

 

_bhūyaś ca grahāṇāṃ pratyekaṃ saṃhatānāṃ ca pūjyatve hetum āha |_

 

**              	grahādhīnā narendrāṇām ucchrayāḥ patanāni ca |**

**              	bāvābhāvau ca jagatas tasmāt pūjyatamā grahāḥ || 1.303 ||**

 

spaṣṭārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 303 ||

 

**iti grahaśāntiprakaraṇam**

** **

**atha rājadharmaprakaraṇam**

 

_kaḥ punar ayaṃ narendro nāma, yasya grahādhīnau pātocchrāyau | nanu ca prasiddho rājani narendraśabdaḥ | kiṃ kṣatriye | bāḍham | tathā coktam |_

_                    	pradhānaṃ kṣatriye karma prajānāṃ paripālanam | iti | _(YDh 1.118)

_uktaṃ ca svayaṃbhuvā |_

_                    	brāhmaṃ prāptena saṃskāraṃ kṣatriyeṇa yathāvidhi |_

_                    	sarvasyāsya yathānyāyaṃ kartavyaṃ parirakṣaṇam || iti |_ (MDh 7.2)

_ayaṃ tu viśeṣaḥ | abhiṣekādiguṇayuktasyaiva rājyādhikāro na kṣatriyamātrasya, "samūrdhno rājānam asṛjata sa mūrdhany abhiṣikto rājā bhavet" ity āmnāyāt | na caivaṃ sati grahādhīnatvāt pātocchrāyayor daivatantra eva rājā syāt | kiṃ tarhi |_

 

**              	mahotsāhaḥ sthūlalakṣaḥ kṛtajño vṛddhasevitā |**

**              	vinītaḥ sattvasaṃpannaḥ kulīnaḥ satyavāk chuciḥ || 1.304 ||**

**              	adīrghasūtraḥ smṛtimān akṣudrapariṣat tathā |**

**              	dhārmiko dṛḍhabhaktiś ca prājñaḥ śūro rahasyavit || 1.305 ||**

                    	**svarandhragoptānvīkṣikyāṃ daṇḍanītyāṃ tathaiva ca |**

**              	vinītas tv atha vārtāyāṃ trayyaṃ caiva narādhipaḥ || 1.306 ||**

 

syād iti śeṣaḥ | mahotsāho vijigīṣuḥ | sthūlalakṣaḥ prabhūtadātā | kṛtajña upakārajñaḥ, na svārthaikaniṣṭhaḥ | vṛddhasevitā jñānavayovṛddhasevī | vinīto 'nuddhataḥ, viviktanayatayā vā yena kenacid aneyaḥ | sattvasaṃpannaḥ sarvathāviṣādī | kulīno mahākulaprasūtaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> etad aśakyaṃ, daivādhīnatvāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | kulīnanṛpatyanukārī syād ity asyārthaḥ | satyavāk satyasaṃdhaḥ | śuciḥ sarvopadhāśuddhaḥ | adīrghasūtraḥ sarvathā kṣiprakārī | smṛtimān ālocanako 'vismaraṇaśīlaś ca | akṣudrapariṣatko haṃsaparivāraḥ | tathā ca śaṅkhaḥ: "na haṃso gṛdhraparivāraḥ kāmaṃ tu gṛdhro haṃsaparvāraḥ syāt" iti | tathāśabdāt prakṛtyantaragrahaṇam | dhārmiko yathāvihitadharmānuṣṭhātā | dṛḍhabhaktir bhaktigrāhyaḥ, yatra vā samāśritaḥ tatrāvicalitabhaktiḥ, devabrāhmaṇagurvādau ca | prājñaḥ sarvatra sārāsāravivekajñaḥ | śūraḥ prasahya sakalārātimaṇḍalavikṣobhitā tadabhubhūtaś cāviṣaṇṇaḥ | rahasyavid mitrāryudāsīnavijigīṣumadhyamākhilaguptiprayuktipracārajñaḥ, amātyādiprakṛtiparīkṣāprakārajñaś ca, nigūḍhāvyabhicāricāracakṣuḥ | adhyātmaṃ rahasyaṃ tajjñaḥ, prasaṃkhyānavān ity arthaḥ | svarandhragoptā akhilanijavyasanagopanaḥ paracchidrodbhāvakaś ca | ānvīkṣikyāṃ daṇḍanītyāṃ vividhavārtāyāṃ trayyāṃ ca vinītaḥ | ānvīkṣikī samastāsāṃdṛṣṭikanirūpaṇakṣamā hetuvidyā | nijānyapratāponnatihānihetur nijadaṇḍodyogātmikā yathārhaṃ daṇḍanītiḥ, daṇḍyeṣu vā yathārhaṃ daṇḍapātanena yojyā | anye tu tarkaviśeṣaṃ daṇḍanītim āhuḥ | trayī ṛgyajuḥsāmalakṣaṇā | evaṃ mahotsāhādiguṇayuktaḥ syād, na daivanikṣiptabharaḥ, puṇyābhimānāt | mahotsāhādiguṇavān anyo vārir api kaṣṭatvāc cintyaḥ, viparītaś cārabhya iti nayasaṃkṣepaḥ | tad yathā: arājabījī lubdhaḥ kṣudraparṣatko viraktaprakṛtir anyāyavṛttir ayukto vyasanī nirutsāho yatkiṃcanakāryagatir ananubandho nityāpakārī cetyādi | sarvathā ca tathā ca kuryād yathākilakṛtyavargo mahotsāhādiguṇasaṃpadvaiparītyād ārabhyaḥ syāt, svayaṃ ca yathākhilamahīmaṇḍalasvīkaraṇakṣamo vijigīṣur ananyārabhyo yātā paramaṇḍalocchittisamarthaḥ syād iti | anvayavyatirekamūlatvāc ca smṛter anuktam uktaṃ vākhilaṃ vivicya yathārhaṃ vyākhyeyam | yataś ca narādhipa evaṃguṇaḥ syāt tataś ca pratiṣṭhitarājyasyāpi guṇārjanam aviruddham || 304–306 ||

 

_evaṃguṇo 'pi kim amātyeneti naivam atimānī syāt, kiṃ tarhi | evaṃguṇa eva yaḥ |_

 

**              	sa mantriṇaḥ prakurvīta prājñān maulān sthirāñ chucīn |**

**              	taiḥ sārdhaṃ cintayet kāryaṃ vipreṇātha tataḥ svayam || 1.307 ||**

 

tathā ca manuḥ |

                    	api yat sukaraṃ karma tad apy ekena duṣkaram |

                    	viśeṣato 'sahāyena kim u rājyaṃ mahodayam || iti | (MDh 7.55)

mantrivacanaṃ ca sarvasacivopalakṣaṇārtham | tathā cāha |

                    	nirvartetāsya yāvadbhir itikartavyatā nṛbhiḥ |

                    	tāvato 'tandritān dakṣān prakurvīta vicakṣaṇān || iti | (MDh 7.61)

pradhānamantryarthaṃ caitad vacanam | kāryatas tv anyakaraṇāvirodhaḥ | dṛṣṭārthatvāc cānyamantryabhāva eva karaṇam | yas tu paitṛkādikam anyadīyaṃ vā rājyam avāpnuyāt, sa yadi tadrājyayogyaṃ pūrvāmātyānām ātmaviśiṣṭam adhikaṃ vānyaṃ manyeta tataḥ prakṛtyakopakrameṇa sarvān evaivaṃguṇān anyān mantriṇaḥ kuryāt | praśabdaś coktanyāyena prakarṣālocanārthaḥ | te ca prājñā vivekino maulāś ca | mūlaṃ rājyaṃ tadarhāḥ maulāḥ, rājyavistārakṣamā ity arthaḥ | mūlato vā jñātā mahākulīnāḥ | mūlakramāgatā vā te hy adhikārāt pracyāvitā api saty eva sāmarthye 'nurāgātirekāt kulāṅkuśopagrahād vā virodhānārambhakāḥ | sthirāḥ sarvāpatsahiṣṇavo 'nanyagāminaḥ sādhvārambhakāś ca | śucayo dharmārthakāmabhayopadhāśuddhāḥ | pradarśanārthaṃ caitat | sarvathā lokataḥ śāstrataś cālocya yathārhaṃ svādhikārānusāreṇa sacivasaṃniveśaḥ kāryaḥ | yathāha bṛhaspatiḥ:


    svadharmavid anuraktaḥ śucir anuddhata udyukto deśakālavin nītinigametihāsakuśalo 'vyasanī mṛdur arthaśāstrakṛtayogyo hastyaśvapuruṣācārāhorātrayāmanirgamaviniścitamatiś ca svaparabalabalābalajño balādhikṛtaḥ senāpatiḥ syāt | kulāḍhya udyukto mṛdur udāttaḥ samaracittaḥ śūro 'nurakto 'bhedyaḥ pattiviśeṣajña iṅgitākārakuśalaḥ pratihāraḥ syāt | vanakulakālajātisātmyaguṇavayaḥśīlāyurādānagamanakalpanāvān vyapagatabhayo vijayorjitamanā hastyadhyakṣaḥ syāt | kṣetrajātisātmyaguṇalakṣaṇavāhanāstrajño 'tyarthasamarthaḥ śucir anuddhato 'nurūpo 'śvādhyakṣaḥ syāt | saṃdhibhedasaṃdhānasthānajño 'nuraktaḥ śucir dakṣaḥ smṛtimān deśakālajño darśanīyo nītigatijñaḥ prājño vāgmī dūtaḥ syāt | ubhayata uttamavaṃśaprabhavaḥ śuddho manubṛhaspatyuśanaḥśāstravid daṇḍanītyādikuśalo 'śaṭho 'jihmaḥ saṃmānāsaṃmānāvikṛto vigatabhīḥ kāryākaryaviniścitamatir ahāryaḥ sarvopadhāśuddho gūḍhamantro mantrī syāt | avikāryo 'vikalendriyaḥ pratāpavān subhagaḥ sumukho 'kṛpaṇo 'pramādī dakṣo dākṣiṇyacāritrarakṣaṇārtham adhikaraṇasaṃdigdhavivekakṛd uparikaḥ syāt | iti |

evaṃ ca bhāṇḍāgārāntaḥpuramahānasaśayyāgṛhādyadhikṛtā yathārhaṃ vivicya vyākaraṇīyāḥ | evaṃ bṛhaspatyuśanaḥśāstramatena sarvasacivān yathārthaṃ rajā kṛtvā taiḥ sārdhaṃ yathārhaṃ sāmānyaṃ ca mantrayitvā vyastasamastābhiprāyaṃ ca vivicya paścāt paramarahasyagāminā mahāmantrisaṃpadyuktena viduṣā brāhmaṇena saha ṣāḍguṇyayuktaṃ mahodayaṃ citraphalaṃ nayabījaṃ mantrayet | tatas tadviśvāsāt svayaṃ ca tad eva nipuṇato 'pararātrotthitaḥ samyag vivicyādīrghasūtry eva kṣipram anutiṣṭhet | evam akhilonnatibījaṃ samāsato 'bhihitaṃ vivicya vistareṇa vyākhyeyam | ity alaṃ prasaṅgena || 307 ||

 

_pūrvoktanyāyenaiva |_

 

                    	**purohitaṃ ca kurvīta daivajñam uditoditam |**

**              	daṇḍanītyāṃ ca kuśalam atharvāṅgirase tathā || 1.308 ||**

 

tathāśabdād pūrvaguṇayogaś ca | daivajño jyotiḥśāstravit | prāktanakarmaphalasaṃbandhajño vā | idam asmāt karmaṇo 'dya phalam upabhujyate paścāt tu pratisamādhir ity uditoditaḥ | daṇḍanītyāṃ ca pravīṇaḥ | caśabdāt trayyām ānvīkṣikyāṃ vividhavārtāyāṃ ca | etac ca mantriṇām api samānam | ayaṃ tv asya viśeṣaḥ: atharvāṅgirase śāntikapauṣṭikābhicārādyarthaṃ pravīṇaḥ syāt | etenāpi saha yathārthaṃ mantraṇīyam | sarvāmātyāś cānenaiva dharmopadhāśuddhatvena parīkṣyāḥ | evam anyair api yathāsthānam upadhāviśeṣaiḥ sarvāmātyaparīkṣā kartavyeti nītisaṃkṣepaḥ || 309 ||

 

_ayaṃ ca rājño 'abhyadhiko vaiśeṣiko dharmaḥ |_

 

                    	**śrautasmārtakriyāhetor vṛṇuyad ṛtvijas tathā |**

**              	yajñāṃś caiva prakurvīta vidhivad bhūridakṣiṇān || 1.309 ||**

 

tathāśabdāt purohito 'pi śrautasmārtakriyāhetor eva | ṛtvigvaraṇaṃ caitat karmaprayogād bahir ādita eva draṣṭavyam | yajñāṃś ca vidhivat kuryāt, na tu yathā kathaṃcanety arthaḥ | bhūridakṣiṇā bahusuvarṇakādayaḥ | prasarpakadānāpekṣayā vā bhūridakṣiṇatvaṃ yojyam || 309 ||

 

_yajñavyatirekeṇāpi |_

 

                    	**bhogāṃś ca dadyād viprebhyo vasūni vividhāni ca |**

 

_kasmāt | yasmāt |_

 

                    	**akṣayo 'yaṃ nidhī rājñāṃ yad vipreṣūpapāditam || 1.310 ||**

 

bhogā annapānādayaḥ | caśabdo 'bhayasatkārādyarthaḥ | vasūni hiraṇyādīny anekavidhāni | caśabdaḥ saṃpradānagatavaicitryārthaḥ | tathā ca manuḥ: "samam abrāhmaṇe dānam" ityādi (MDh 7.85) | spaṣṭam anyat || 310 ||

 

_bhūyaś ca dānavidhiprarocanāyāha |_

 

                    	**askannam avyathaṃ caiva prāyaścittair adūṣitam |**

 

_yasmāt, tasmāt |_

 

                    	**agneḥ sakāśād viprāgnau hutaṃ śreṣṭam ihocyate || 1.311 ||**

 

_kiṃ pūrvārjitam āpadarthaṃ sthitaṃ bhāṇḍāgārād eva dātavyam | nety ucyate |_

 

                    	**dharmeṇa labdhum īheta labdhaṃ yatnena pālayet |**

**              	pālitaṃ vardhayen nityaṃ vṛddhaṃ pātreṣu nikṣipet || 1.312 ||**

 

spaṣṭārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 312 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvad dhiraṇyādiṣu pradānāntataiva | bhūminibandhadānayos tv ayaṃ viśeṣaḥ |_

 

                    	**dattvā bhūmiṃ nibandhaṃ vā kṛtvā lekhyaṃ tu kārayet |**

 

_kasmāt |_

 

                    	**āgāmikṣudranṛpatiparijñānāya pārthivaḥ || 1.313 ||**

 

nibandho 'kṣayanidhiḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 313 ||

 

_kiṃ punar vakṣyamāṇalekhyalakṣaṇavat kāryam | nety ucyate | kiṃ tarhi |_

 

                    	**paṭe vā tāmrapaṭṭe vā svamudrāparicihnitam |**

**              	abhilekhyātmano vaṃśyān ātmānaṃ ca mahīmatiḥ || 1.314 ||**

**              	pratigrahaparīmāṇaṃ dānācchedopavarṇanam |**

**              	svahastakālasaṃpannaṃ śāsanaṃ kārayet sthiram || 1.315 ||**

 

paṭavacanaṃ bhūrjanivṛttyartham | pariśabdāt prajñādūtakasvahastamudrāskandhāvārasamāvāsanāmadeśādicihnitam | ādāv evābhilekhanīyāḥ pūrvapuruṣās trayaḥ | vaṃśyatvavacanāc ca striyo 'pi | anantaram ātmānam | tataḥ pratigrahaparīmāṇam | asmin deśe 'mukanāmeyān grāma ityādi | tato dānācchedam upavarṇya | etad dānaphalam, etad ācchedanaphalaṃ,

                    	ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣasahasrāṇi svarge niṣṭhati bhūmidaḥ |

                    	ācchettā cānumantā ca tany eva narake vaset ||

ityādi | lekhakanāmāṅkitaṃ svahastasaṃyuktam āgāmikṣudranṛpatyaśocanaṃ sthiraṃ bhūmeś chidranyāsenācandrāt sthitisaṃsthānaṃ kārayet | sarvathā yathāgāmino 'py asmād eva śāsanān na vikuryuḥ, tathā kāryam iti || 314–315 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca rāṣṭrasaṃkocaprasaṅgāt bhūmidānam ayuktam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">rājavṛttāntānabhijña, maivam</span> | nityam eva hi trivargavṛddhicaturo rājā |_

 

                    	**ramyaṃ paśavyaṃ svājīvyaṃ jāṅgalaṃ deśam āśrayet |**

**              	tatra durgāṇi kurvīta janakośātmavṛddhaye || 1.316 ||**

 

durgāṇīti bahuvacanaṃ durgabhedaprakārārtham | yathāha manuḥ |

                    	dhanvadurgaṃ mahīdurgam abdurgaṃ vārkṣam eva ca |

                    	nṛdurgaṃ giridurgaṃ ca samāśritya vaset puram ||

                    	sarveṇa tu prayatnena giridurgaṃ samāśrayet |

                    	eteṣāṃ bāhuguṇyena giridurgaṃ praśasyate || (MDh 7.70–71)

ityādi || 316 ||

 

_evaṃ durgāṇi kṛtvā taṃ deśam adhyāsya tataḥ |_

 

                    	**tatra tatra ca niṣṇātān adhyakṣān kuśalāñ chucīn |**

**              	prakuryād āyakarmāntavyayakarmasu codyatān || 1.317 ||**

 

nātra tirohitam ivāsti || 317 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvat svarāṣṭra evārjananiyama uktaḥ | idānīṃ parasvānapaharaṇaprasaktāv apavādam āha |_

 

                    	**nātaḥ parato dharmo nṛpāṇāṃ yad raṇārjitam |**

**              	viprebhyo dīyate dravyaṃ prajābhyaś cābhayaṃ sadā || 1.318 ||**

 

raṇārjitād ity abhiprāyaḥ || 318 ||

 

_idānīṃ "na saṃśayaṃ prapadyeta" _(YDh 1.132) _"na hiṃsyāt sarvabhūtānī" iti pratiṣedhadvayāt saṃgrāmāprāptiprasaktāv āha |_

 

                    	**ya āhaveṣu vadhyante bhūmyartham aparāṅmukhāḥ |**

**              	akūṭair āyudhair yānti te svargaṃ yāgino yathā || 1.319 ||**

 

āhavaḥ saṃgrāmaḥ | bhūmyarthavacanaṃ daṇḍakośāder apy upalakṣaṇārtham | akūṭair āyudhair yudhyamānā iti yojyam | kūṭāni viṣadigdhakarṇikādīni | āyudhavacanaṃ sarvāyudhopalakṣaṇārtham | spaṣṭam anyat || 319 ||

 

_bhūyaś ca saṃgrāmavidhiprarocanāṃ yuddhākṛtiprakāraṃ cāha |_

 

                    	**padāni kratutulyāni bhagneṣu vinivartatām |**

**              	rājā sukṛtam ādatte hatānāṃ vipalāyatām || 1.320 ||**

 

yuddhārtham eva hi tatsaṃgrahād yuktam evaitat || 320 ||

 

_evaṃ ca sati sarvathā saṃgrāme hiṃsāyāṃ prāptāyām apavādārtham āha |_

 

                    	**tavāhaṃvādinaṃ klībaṃ nirhetiṃ parasaṃgatam |**

**              	na hanyād vinivṛttaṃ ca yuddhaprekṣakam eva ca || 1.321 ||**

 

caśabda āyudhādivyasanāpannādyarthaḥ | nirhetir ayudhyamānaḥ | parasaṃgato 'nyena yudhyamānaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 321 ||

 

_evām tāvat sāmāsiko rājanayaḥ | idānīm ānvahikaṃ rājñaḥ karma |_

 

                    	**kṛtarakṣaḥ samutthāya paśyed āyavyayau svayam |**

**              	vyavahārāṃs tato dṛṣṭvā snātvā bhuñjīta kāmataḥ || 1.322 ||**

** **

rakṣā divyā mānuṣī ca dvividhā | devabrāhmaṇapūjādilakṣaṇā maṅgalātmikā ca divyā, suparīkṣitodyatāyudhayuddhapuruṣaiḥ pariveṣṭhanaṃ mānuṣī | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ: "brahmaśaṅkhastutipuṇyāhaśabdair vibudhyotthāya saṃdhyām upāsya devapitṛbrāhmaṇān manasā vā namaskṛtya dharmārthakāmabhayopadhāśuddhāvañcakagṛhītāyudhāyātayāmaviśvāsotpannāsannaparivṛtaḥ" ityādi | gurutarātyayikakāryānurodhena svayam evāyavyayaṃ paśyed vyavahārāṃś ca vakṣyamāṇavidhinā | tataḥ snātvā devapitrādyarcanaṃ kṛtvāntaḥpuraṃ praviśya kāmataḥ suparīkṣitam annam aśnīyāt || 322 ||

 

_evaṃ svapararāṣṭravyavasthayā dravyārjanavidhir uktaḥ | tat punar dravyaṃ kim utpannam eva pātre samarpaṇīyaṃ tadarthatvād utpādanasya | evam iti prāpta āha |_

 

                    	**hiraṇyaṃ vyāpṛtānītaṃ bhāṇḍāgāre nyaset tataḥ |**

**              	paśyec cārāṃs tato dūtān preṣayen mantrisaṃgataḥ || 1.323 ||**

 

sarvādhikāravyāpṛtair āhṛtamātraṃ bhāṇḍāgāra eva nyaset, na dadyāt | tata eva hetor "vṛddhaṃ pātreṣu nikṣipet" iti (YDh 1.312) | nityaṃ ca bhuktvā vyapetaklamo viśvastacittaḥ paśyec cārān avasthitānekavidhacāraprahitān prahetavyāṃś ca | ayaṃ hi nītisaṃkṣepaḥ: nityaṃ hy anekavidhāḥ sarvāśramasarvapāṣaṇḍino liṅgino 'nekavidyāvyājakapaṭaiḥ pararāṣṭrasvarāṣṭravinyastās tatprahitāndhamūkajalabadhironmattādiprakārakapaṭapracchannāḥ prakhyāpitakutūhalapradhānatayā sarvasattvānujighṛkṣāparatvaprasiddhyā vā rājñā prayatnato gūḍhasaṅketanipuṇenānvaham apramattena draṣṭavyāḥ | yad vā, ekaṃ kaṃcid vāmanakubjādikam ātmano 'tiśayavāllabhyaprakhyātaṃ suparīkṣitam āptaṃ cāravyāpare niyojayet | sa cākhilāṃ rājño nityayuktacāraprahitāṃ muhur muhur vārtāṃ saṃpādayet | evaṃ cārān dṛṣṭvā tadarthaniścayānusāreṇa sarvārtheṣu yathārthaṃ dūtān preṣayet pradhānāmātyasaṃgataḥ | ṣāḍguṇyanayānusāriṇā tv etac citrasaṃcāram ābhyudayikabījam apramattenānvahaṃ vaptavyam || 323 ||

 

_yataś ca gūḍhamantratvam ābhyudayikabījam |_

 

                    	**tataḥ svairavihārī syān mantribhir vā samāgataḥ |**

**              	balānāṃ darśanaṃ kṛtvā senānyā saha cintayet || 1.324 ||**

 

svairavihāritā pradhānamantriṇy apy aprakaṭitamantratā | yad vā mantribhir utpannaviśvāsaiḥ sahaivaitac cārādidarśanaṃ kuryād iti | agūḍhamantratāpy anabhyudayāyaivety abhiprāyaḥ | nayāvirodhena caitayor vyavasthā | bhūyo bhūyaḥ sarvasacivāḥ suparīkṣitā api parīkṣyāḥ | parīkṣitaiś ca saha yathārhaṃ kāryapravṛttir iti | kiṃ ca, balānāṃ hastyaśvarathapādātāyudhasaṃnāhādisaretaravivekena nipuṇato mahābalādhikṛtasenāpatisamakṣaṃ darśanaṃ kṛtvā tataḥ ṣāḍguṇyaṃ nipuṇataḥ pūrvoktakrameṇaiva cintayet | daṇḍakośādyanusāreṇaiva saṃdhivigrahādiniyama ity abhiprāyaḥ || 324 ||

 

_na caikāntato 'rthaniṣṭhatayaivetarapuruṣārthahāpanam | kiṃ tarhi |_

 

                    	**saṃdhyām upāsya śṛṇuyāc cārāṇāṃ gūḍhabhāṣitam |**

**              	gītanṛttaiś ca bhuñjīta paṭhet svādhyāyam eva ca || 1.325 ||**

 

gītanṛttaiś ca bhuñjīta, kāmam apy anurundhyāt | paṭhec ca svādhyāyam | dharmān na hāpayed ity arthaḥ | yad vā, etatparam etacchlokārdharam: mahatyām apy āpady aviṣādinam ātmānaṃ darśayituṃ sthitakṛtyacintāpravaṇa eva svavyasanagopanāya paraprasvāpanāya vānākulatayaiva, gītanṛttaiś ca bhuñjīta paṭhet svādhyāyam eva ca | caśabdān mṛgayām apy anutiṣṭhet || 325 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**saṃviśet tūryaghoṣeṇa suptvā budhyet tathaiva ca |**

**              	śāstrāṇi cintayed buddhvā sarvakartavyatās tathā || 1.326 ||**

 

apasvapnāyato mantrasrutir mā bhūd iti yāvatsvāpaṃ yathāsthānaṃ tauryatriko nṛttagītavāditralakṣaṇaḥ prayojyaḥ | caśabdo vandyādighoṣaṇārthaḥ | kāmo 'pi caivam utpannaḥ saṃvṛto bhavati, arthaś ca | suptvā vibudhya vyapetaklamo nipuṇayā prajñayā trivargacāturyeṇa sarvārthaṃ viniścinuyāt || 326 ||

 

_evaṃ ca nipuṇataś citrodayāṃ nītiṃ niyamya |_

 

**              	preṣayet tataś cārān sveṣv anyeṣu ca sādaram |**

**              	ṛtvikpurohitācāryair āśīrbhir abhinanditaḥ || 1.327 ||**

 

paścimayāma eva cārān preṣayet, sveṣu sthitacāramaṇḍaleṣu | ye tu pararāṣṭrasacivā nīticāturyād bheditāḥ, teṣu ca sabahumānaṃ cārān preṣayet | caśabdād āṭavikasvamaṇḍalagateṣu ca | evaṃ ca viśālākṣaḥ |

                    	vanyān vanagatair nityaṃ maṇḍalasthāṃs tathāvidhaiḥ |

                    	cārair ālocya satkuryāj jigīṣur dīrghadūradṛk || 327 ||

 

_evaṃ cārān preṣyāgnīn hutvartvigādyāśīrbhir abhinanditaḥ sabhāṃ praviśya tataḥ |_

 

**              	dṛṣṭvā jyotirvido vaidyān dadyād gāṃ kanakaṃ mahīm |**

**              	naiveśikāni ca tathā śrotriyāṇāṃ gṛhāṇi ca || 1.328 ||**

 

jyotirvido vaidyāṃś ca dṛṣṭvātmīyaśarīrasaṃsthāṃ grahagocaraṃ cālocya nimittaviśeṣaṃ ca buddhvā tadanusāreṇaiva śrotriyebhyo yathārhaṃ gāṃ kanakam ityādi dadyāt | gatārtham anyat || 328 ||

 

_ayaṃ cānyo rājyaprāptisthitikaraḥ sāranayasaṃkṣepaḥ |_

 

                    	**brāhmaṇeṣu kṣamī snigdheṣv ajihmaḥ krodhano 'riṣu |**

**              	syād rājā bhṛtyavargeṣu prajābhyaś ca yathā pitā || 1.329 ||**

 

snigdho nirabhisaṃdhisnehaikanibandhanatayā mitram | ajihmo 'kuṭilaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 329 ||

 

_kasmāt punar etad evam | yasmāt |_

 

**              	puṇyāt ṣaḍbhāgam ādatte nyāyena paripālayan |**

 

_kasmāt |_

 

**              	sarvadānādhikaṃ yasmān nyāyena paripālanam || 1.330 ||**

 

_kena punaḥ prajāḥ pīḍyante, yenāyaṃ prayatnaḥ | ucyate |_

 

                    	**cāṭataskaradurvṛttamahāsāhasikādibhiḥ |**

**              	pīḍyamānāḥ prajā rakṣyāḥ kāyasthaiś ca viśeṣataḥ || 1.331 ||**

 

kāyasthā rāgādayaḥ | lekhakā ity anye || 331 ||

_ _

_yadi tv evamādibhyo rājā rakṣāṃ na kuryāt tataḥ|_

 

**              	arakṣyamāṇāḥ kurvanti yat kiṃcit kilbiṣaṃ prajāḥ|**

**              	tasmāt tu nṛpater arthaṃ**

 

syād iti śeṣaḥ |

 

_kasmāt |_

 

**                                         	yasmād gṛhṇāty asau karān || 1.332 ||**

 

_kathaṃ punaḥ pīḍāḥ prajābhyo vijānīyād rājā | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> uktaṃ _"_tatra tatra ca niṣṇātān adhyakṣān_"_ kuryād iti _(YDh 1.317)_ | eta eva yadā vikuryus tadā katham iti cet | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> |_

 

                    	**ye rāṣṭrādhikṛtās teṣāṃ cārair jñātvā viceṣṭitam |**

**              	sādhūn saṃmānayen nityaṃ viparītāṃs tu ghātayet || 1.333 ||**

 

_yadā tu duṣṭajanāḥ sahādhyakṣair ekībhūya lubdhāḥ sādhujanaṃ khalīkuryuḥ, tatas tān api |_

 

**              	utkocajīvino dravyahīnān kṛtvā vivāsayet |**

 

_ye tu sādhavas tān |_

 

                    	**sadānamānasatkāraiḥ śrotriyān vāsayet sadā || 1.334 ||**

 

śrotriyavacanaṃ dṛṣṭāntārtham | yad vā dānādibhir api śrotriyān eva vāsayed, na karadān apy avinītān ity arthaḥ || 334 ||

 

_yataś caitad evam, ataḥ |_

 

**              	anyāyena nṛpo rāṣṭrāt svakośaṃ yo 'bhivardhayet |**

**              	so 'cirād vigataśrīko nāśam eti sabāndhavaḥ || 1.335 ||**

 

_kasmāt punar etad eva, yasmāt |_

 

**              	prajāpīḍanasaṃtāpasamudbhūto hutāśanaḥ |**

**              	rājñaḥ kulaṃ śriyaṃ prāṇān nādagdhvā vinivartate || 1.336 ||**

 

atyaparādhād ekaloṣṭavadhenāpy enaṃ hanyur ity abhiprāyaḥ | daṇḍakośādyucchittis tu tanmūlatvān niyataiva || 336 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evaṃ pararāṣṭre 'pi pīḍanād ayam eva doṣaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">dharmetarānabhijña, maivam</span> |_

 

                    	**ya eva dharmo nṛpateḥ svarāṣṭraparipālane |**

**              	tam eva kṛtsnam āpnoti pararāṣṭraṃ vaśaṃ nayan || 1.337 ||**

 

iyaṃ tāvad dharmagatiḥ | doṣāntaraṃ tv atra nāsaṅkanīyam evety abhiprāyaḥ || 337 ||

 

_kiṃ tu |_

 

                    	**yasmin yasmin ya ācāro vyavahāraḥ kule shitiḥ |**

**              	tathaiva paripālyo 'sau yadā vaśam upāgataḥ || 1.338 ||**

 

dharmāvirodheneti śeṣaḥ | ātmīyatvād eva pālane prāpte guṇārthaṃ vacanam || 338 ||

 

_kathaṃ punaḥ pararāṣṭrasiddhiḥ | mantrata iti brūmaḥ | tadadhīnā hi kośadaṇḍādayaḥ | ataś ca |_

                    	**mantramūlaṃ yato rājyam ato mantraṃ surakṣitam |**

**              	kuryād yathāsya na viduḥ karmanām ā phalodayāt || 1.339 ||**

 

svapararāṣṭraprāptisthitivṛddhihetur mantra eva sunirṇītaḥ sugupto yasmāt, tasmān nirṇayaguptibhyāṃ surakṣitaḥ kāryaḥ, viparyaye sarvocchedaprasaṅgāt | na ca phalodaye 'pi mantraḥ prakāśyaḥ, punar api tathākaraṇāt | phaladarśanāt tu kāraṇam anumimānā na viśeṣanirdhāraṇaṃ kuryuḥ kutūhalenātra samutpannena | ataḥ kṛtyetaravargayoḥ sarvathā mantrapracchādanaṃ niyogataḥ kartavyam | mantraśaktyadhīne eva hy utsāhaprabhuśaktī, tadapāye 'pi hi mantraśaktyaiva siddhidarśanāt atas tadguptau yatnaḥ kārya iti || 339 ||

 

_kiṃ punas tan mantraṇīyam | uktaṃ ca dikpracāradūtasaṃpreṣaṇakāpaṭikodāsthitagṛhapatika-vaidehakatāpasavyañjanāvasthitacāraprapañcaparinirūpaṇaparaprayuktakāpaṭikādyuccheda-durgādikaraṇakanyāsaṃpradānakumāracintāntaḥpurapracārādyanekavidhaṃ ca | idaṃ cāparam |_

 

**              	arir mitram udāsīno 'nantaras tatparaḥ paraḥ |**

**              	kramaśo maṇḍalaṃ cintyaṃ sāmādibhir upakramaiḥ || 1.340 ||**

 

vijigīṣor avasthitasya bhūmyantaraḥ śatruḥ | tasmāt paro mitram | tatparas tūdāsīnaḥ | evam idaṃ maṇḍalam avasthitaṃ sāmopapradānabhedadaṇḍair yathārhaṃ cintyam || 340 ||

 

_kasmāt punar yathārhaṃ sāmādiyojanā | yasmāt |_

 

**              	upāyāḥ sāma dānaṃ ca bhedo daṇḍas tathaiva ca |**

 

_upāyatvād eva ca |_

 

                    	**samyak prayuktāḥ sidhyeyur daṇḍas tv agatikā gatiḥ || 1.341 ||**

 

sāma vācikaṃ kāyikaṃ ca | dānaṃ dīyamānasyākopena grahaṇaṃ, svakīyasya ca dānam | bhedaḥ saṃhatayor upajapyaviśleṣaṇam | daṇḍo haṭhāt prasādhanam | te 'mī vyastāḥ samastāś ca yathārhaṃ yojyāḥ | ādyopayatrayakṣaye daṇḍaḥ | tatrāris trividhaḥ sahajaḥ kṛtrimo bhūmyanantaraś ca | anantaro daṇḍasādhya eva | tathā mitraṃ sahajakṛtrimānantaraparatvena | anantaraparaḥ sāmopapradānagocaraḥ | sāmaivodāsīneṣu | aripakṣyāḥ sarvadā bhedyā eva | ityevamādiprakāro bahudhā prayogānusārād dravyaśuddhivad "deśaṃ kālaṃ tathātmānam" (BDh 1.8.53) ity avekṣya sāmādiprayuktiniyamaḥ || 341 ||

 

_yāś caitā rājyaprakṛtayaḥ svāmyādyāḥ, tāsu yathārham ālocya surakṣitamantro vijigīṣuḥ |_

 

                    	**saṃdhiṃ savigrahaṃ yānam āsanaṃ saṃśrayaṃ tathā |**

**              	dvaidhībhāvaṃ guṇān etān yathāvat parikalpayet || 1.342 ||**

 

hiraṇyādipaṇanibandhenobhayānugrahārthaḥ saṃdhiḥ | sa kadācid dvayor api tādātvikaphalaḥ | kadācid ekasya tadātve 'nyasyāyatyām | tathā ca manuḥ |

                    	samānayānakarmā vā viparītas tathaiva ca |

                    	tadātvāyatisaṃyuktaḥ saṃdhir jñeyo dvilakṣaṇaḥ || iti | (MDh 7.163)

evaṃ vigrahādidvaividhyam apy udāhāryam | saṃdhiviparīto vigrahaḥ | abhyuccayātireke ripūn prati gamanaṃ yānam | anārambhatvam āsanam | saṃdhivigrahadvayabījopādānaṃ dvaidhībhāvaḥ | kṣīṇasyānyāśrayaṇaṃ saṃśrayaḥ | tadātve parikṣīṇasya bhāviny abhyuccaye saṃdhikaraṇam, viparyaye vigrahaḥ | mitroparodhāc cobhayam | mitrānurodhād bhāvibalāpekṣayā ca prakṣīṇaḥ śanakaiḥ parān sāntvayan āsanena vṛddhim ātiṣṭhet | prakṣīṇa eva cāvaṣṭabdho dvidhā balaṃ vyuhya dvayabījam upādadyāt | sarvaparikṣaye tu svabalavyasanena vā kulīnaṃ balavantam alubdhaṃ dhārmikaṃ pūrvapuruṣāśritaṃ mitravargabhūyiṣṭhaṃ rājānaṃ kṣipram āśrayet | sarvathā ca sāmopapradānābhyāṃ tam evārādhayet | tathā cāha |

                    	nigrahaṃ prakṛtīnāṃ ca kuryād yo 'ribalasya ca |

                    	upseveta taṃ nityaṃ sarvayatnair guruṃ tathā || iti | (MDh 7.175)

yadā tu mantrotsāhaprabhuśaktiyuktaḥ, tadā yātavyaṃ pratividhāyāmitraṃ prati gacchet | tathā cāhuḥ: "sāmantayor vyasanasādhye na yātavyaṃ tam amitram eva yāyāt" iti || 342 ||

 

_mitrānurodhena svecchayā vā gacchan sāṃparāyikena vidhinā |_

 

                    	**yadāsamyagguṇopetaṃ pararāṣṭraṃ tadā vrajet |**

**              	paraś ca hīna ātmā ca hṛṣṭavāhanapūruṣaḥ || 1.343 ||**

 

gatārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 343 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evaṃ sakala evārambho 'narthakaḥ, susamṛddhānām api viparyayadarśanāt | tathā ca suyodhanasya virāṭaṃ prati ghoṣayātrāyāṃ ca dṛṣṭam eva | uktaṃ ca: "grahādhīnā narendrāṇām ucchrayāḥ patanāni ca" iti _(YDh 1.303)_ | ato daivatantratvāt rājyasyāpabhraṣṭamūlām ivemāṃ smṛtiṃ manyāmahe | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">puruṣakārānabhijña, maivam</span> |_

 

                    	**daive puruṣakāre ca dvaye siddhiḥ pratiṣṭhitā |**

 

na daiva evety abhiprāyaḥ |

 

_kiṃ ca, daivasvarūpam apy anirūpitam āyuṣmatā | yataḥ|_

 

                    	**tatra daivam abhivyaktaṃ pauruṣaṃ paurvadehikam || 1.344 ||**

 

janmāntarīyapuruṣakāra eva daivam ity ucyate, nānyad ity arthaḥ || 344 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evam api ṣāḍguṇyanirūpaṇaṃ vyartham eva | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | yadi hi sarvaṃ daivādhīnam eva syāt tadaivaṃ syāt | api tu yadā tu |_

 

                    	**kecid daivād dhaṭhāt kecit kecit puruṣakārataḥ |**

**              	siddhyanty arthā manuṣyāṇāṃ**

 

tadaitad acodyam iti śeṣaḥ |

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                                                                    	**teṣāṃ yonis tu pauruṣam || 1.345 ||**

 

teṣāṃ daivahaṭhapuruṣkārāṇāṃ pauruṣam eva yoniḥ kāraṇam ity arthaḥ | haṭho 'pi yo 'dhyavasāyātiśayaḥ vetālasādhanādikaḥ so 'pi ca puruṣakārātiśaya evety arthaḥ | ataḥ sūktaṃ "teṣāṃ yonis tu pauruṣam" iti || 345 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evam apy aparihṛtam evāsmaccodyam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">aho</span> khalv atiśayavān mātṛmato vivekaḥ | paśya |_

 

                    	**yathā hy ekena cakreṇa rathasya na gatir bhavet |**

**              	evaṃ puruṣakāreṇa vinā daivaṃ na siddhyati || 1.346 ||**

 

suṣṭhv api hi daivasaṃpannāḥ padārthasthitiṃ naivātivartante | na jātucid upanītam api bhojyaṃ vyāpāram antareṇa mukhaṃ praviśati | vyāpāro 'pi hi daivād eveti cet, na | daivasyāpi tatpūrvakatvād ity uktaṃ prāktana eva karmaṇi daivaśabda iti | tad api daivāntareṇeti cet, avyavasthaivaṃ sati syāt | bhavatu, anāditvān nirdoṣeti cet, na, nirnimittatvaprasaṅgāt | tadabhidhāne cāvasthitaṃ puruṣakārasyānapekṣatvam | dṛṣṭānuguṇyena cādṛṣṭakalpanā yuktā, na dṛṣṭbādhena | āmnāyasya caivam aprāmāṇyaprasaṅgaḥ | nimittāntarakalpane cādṛṣṭakalpanā duṣparihāryaiva syāt | ataḥ puruṣakāraprādhānyād yuktaḥ kṛtsna evāyam upadeśa iti sthitam || 346 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">yadi tu</span> mitreṇa saha tulyaphalāyāṃ yātrāyām avaṣṭabdho ripur aśakto bhūmyādi prayacchet, tadā kiṃ mitram atisaṃdhāya svakāryaṃ na kriyate uktaṃ hi manunāpi: "yathainaṃ nātisaṃdadhyur mitrodāsīnaśatravaḥ" ityādi_ (MDh 7.180)_, "vidadhyād dhitam ātmanaḥ" iti ca _(MDh 7.57)_ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">dharmetaravivekākuśala, maivam</span> |_

 

                    	**hiraṇyabhūmilābhebhyo mitralabdhir varā yataḥ |**

**              	ato yateta tatprāptau satyaṃ rakṣet samāhitaḥ || 1.347 ||**

 

samāhito lokadvayahitābhijñaḥ || 347 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

** **

**              	svāmy amātyo jano durgaṃ kośo daṇḍas tathaiva ca |**

**              	mitrāṇy etāḥ prakṛtayo rājyaṃ saptāṅgam ucyate || 1.348 ||**

 

svāmī rājā | amātyaḥ sacivaḥ | jano janapadaḥ | kośo dravyanicayaḥ | daṇḍo balaṃ hastyaśvarathapādātātmakam | mitradurge ukte | etāḥ prakṛtayaḥ saptaiva | etadapekṣayā hi rājyaṃ saptāṅgam ucyate yasmāt, tasmād yathaivātmāmātyādiprakṛtayaś ca prayatnataḥ pālanīyāḥ, tathaiva mitrāṇy apīty arthaḥ || 348 ||

 

_evaṃ yad daivapuruṣakārābhyāṃ katham api prāptuṃ śakyaṃ rājyaṃ prāktanānekavidhapuṇyasamudāyād aihikavicitraguṇasaṃpadyogāc ca, dhīmān kṛtavidyaḥ satyasaṃdhaś ca |_

 

                    	**tad avāpya nṛpo daṇḍaṃ durvṛtteṣu nipātayet |**

 

_kasmāt | yasmāt |_

 

                    	**dharmo hi daṇḍarūpeṇa brahmaṇā nirmitaḥ purā || 1.349 ||**

 

tad rājyaṃ rājā sudurlabhaṃ labdhvā nirvyājaprasādhitasamagradaṇḍapātaiś caturvargaprāptilampaṭaḥ prayatnād durvinīyamānān ālocyāvinīteṣu yathārhaṃ daṇḍaṃ pātayet | na cātimṛduhṛdayatayā hṛdvilekhaḥ kāryaḥ | dharma evāyaṃ daṇḍābhidhāno brahmāṇḍāntarvartyakhilaprāṇisaṅghopakārārthaṃ brahmaṇā vedena nirmito vihitaḥ | purety anāditvena nirvicikitsānuṣṭhānaprarocanārtham | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "tataḥ śeṣeṇa viśiṣṭadeśajāti" (GDh 11.29) ity upakramya "viṣvañco viparītā naśyanti | tān ācāryopadeśo daṇḍaś ca pālayate | tasmād rājācāryāv anindyau" (GDh 11.30–32) ityādi | āmnāyaś ca: "saha vā idam abhavat | devāś ca manuṣyāś ca te yadopakārair na śekur manuṣyān ātmīkartum atha devās tirobabhūvuḥ, tān prajāpatir abravīt | kaḥ prajāḥ pālayitā bhuvi sarve 'ntarhitāḥ stha | asaṃrakṣyamāṇāḥ prajā adharmārditās tyakṣyantītaḥ pradānam upajīvanam asmākam iti | te devāḥ prajāpatim abruvan | puruṣamūrtiṃ rājānaṃ karavāma somād rūpam ādāyādityāt tejo vikramam athendrād viṣṇor vijayaṃ vaiśravaṇāt tyāgaṃ yamāt saṃyamanam" ityādy upakramya "so 'bravīd dharmam eva me sakhyāya kurudhvaṃ tato 'haṃ prajāḥ pālayāmīti | tatas tasmai dharmaṃ dvitīyam akurvan sa eṣa dharmo nidānena yad daṇḍaḥ tasmād evaṃvid rājā daṇḍaṃ pitary api pātayet | dharmeṇainaṃ saṃskaravāmy ādhipatyāyendratvāya brahmalokāyeti | īśvaro 'haṃ tathā kartroḥ" ityādi || 349 ||

 

_yataś caivaṃrūpo daṇḍaḥ |_

 

                    	**na sa netum ataḥ śakyo lubdhenākṛtabuddhinā |**

 

_kena tarhi śakyaḥ |_

 

                    	**satyasaṃdhena śucinā susahāyena dhīmatā || 1.350 ||**

 

_kasmāt punar ayaṃ prayatnaḥ | yasmāt |_

 

                    	**yathāśāstraṃ prayuktaḥ san sadevāsuramānavam |**

**              	jagad ānandayet kṛtsnam anyathā tu krakopayet || 1.351 ||**

 

yasmād daṇḍādhīnau jagataḥ kṛtsnasyānandaprakopau, tasmād yatno daṇḍapraṇītau kārya ity abhiprāyaḥ || 351 ||

 

_yataś caitad evam, ataḥ |_

 

                    	**adharmadaṇḍanaṃ lokasvargakīrttivināśanam |**

**              	samyak tu daṇḍanaṃ rājñaḥ svargakīrttijayāvaham || 1.352 ||**

 

lokaḥ pararāṣṭraprāptiḥ svarāṣṭrasthairyaṃ ca | spaṣṭam anyat || 352 ||

 

_yasmāc ca samyag daṇḍanāt svargādiprāptiḥ, tasmāt |_

 

                    	**api bhrāta suto 'rghyo vā śvaśuro mātulo 'pi vā |**

**              	nādaṇḍyo nāma rājño 'sti dharmād vicalitaḥ svakāt || 1.353 ||**

 

_evaṃ cālocya |_

 

                    	**yo daṇḍyān daṇḍayed rājā samyag vadhyāṃś ca ghātayet |**

**              	iṣṭaṃ syāt kratubhis tena sahasraśatadakṣiṇaiḥ || 1.354 ||**

 

kratvarthahiṃsāvac corādihiṃsāpi dharmyaivety abhiprāyaḥ | sahasraśatadakṣiṇo rājasūyaḥ | kratubahutvād bahuvacanam | yad vā śatadakṣiṇā agniṣṭomādayaḥ | sahasradakṣiṇā abhijidādayaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 354 ||

 

_daṇḍyādaṇḍyavadhyāvadhyavivekakḷptyartham_ |

 

                    	**iti saṃcintya nṛpatiḥ kratutulyaphalaṃ pṛthak |**

**              	vyavahārān svayaṃ paśyet sabhyaiḥ parivṛto 'nvaham || 1.355 ||**

 

pṛthak viviktān ity arthaḥ | yad vā kratutulyaphalaṃ pṛthag iti saṃbandhaḥ | ekaikadaṇḍane kratuphalaprāptir ity arthaḥ || 355 ||

 

_evaṃ daṇḍapātanavidhir uktaḥ | adhunārthadaṇḍasyoktaṃ madhyamādhamasāhasādyapekṣayā pramāṇaṃ vaktum āha |_

 

                    	**jalaṃ sūryamarīcisthaṃ trasareṇū rajaḥ smṛtam |**

**              	te 'ṣṭau likṣā tu tās tisro rājasarṣapa ucyate || 1.356 ||**

 

sūryamarīcyantargataṃ jalam iva yad rajo dṛśyate, tad bhedabuddhyā gṛhyamāṇaṃ trasareṇusaṃjñakaṃ bhavati | trasta iva paribhramatīti trasareṇuḥ | te 'ṣṭau reṇava ekībhūtā likṣā | tāś ca tisro rājasarṣapa ucyate | evam uttaratrāpi yojyam || 356 ||

 

                    	**gauras tu te trayaḥ ṣaṭ te yavo madhyas tu te trayaḥ |**

**              	kṛṣṇalaḥ pañca te māṣas te suvarṇas tu ṣoḍaśa || 1.357 ||**

**              	palaṃ suvarṇāś catvāraḥ pañca vāpi prakīrtitāḥ |**

 

ubhayathā prayogadarśanāt | kāryaviśeṣāpekṣayā ca vyavasthā || 357 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvat suvarṇasya palaparyantaṃ pramāṇam uktam | raupyasya tu |_

 

                    	**dvikṛṣṇalo raupyamāṣo dharaṇaṃ ṣoḍaśaiva te || 1.358 ||**

**              	śatamānaṃ tu daśabhir dharaṇaiḥ palam eva tat |**

 

kṛṣṇaladvayena raupyamāṣaḥ | ṣoḍaś māṣā dharaṇam | daśa dharaṇāni śatamānam | tac ca gaṇyamānaṃ catuḥsauvarṇikaṃ palam eva palasaṃmitaṃ bhavati || 358 ||

 

_evaṃ raupyaparimāṇam uktam | suvarṇasyaiva tu |_

 

           	**niṣkaṃ suvarṇāś catvāraḥ kārṣikas tāmrikaḥ paṇaḥ || 1.359 ||**

**       	sāśītiḥ paṇasāhasrī daṇḍa uttamasāhasaḥ |**

**       	tadardhaṃ madhyamaḥ proktas tadardham adhamaḥ smṛtaḥ || 1.360 ||**

 

yat tu catuḥsauvarṇikaṃ palam uktaṃ, tasyaiva dvitīyā niṣkasaṃjñā | tāmrakarṣas tu paṇasaṃjñaḥ | aśītikṛṣṇalaḥ ṣoḍaśamāṣaḥ karṣaḥ | tad darśayati: "sāśitiḥ paṇasāhasrī daṇḍa uttamasāhasaḥ" | saiṣā paṇaśabdavācyā kṛṣṇalāśītiḥ | tāmragrahaṇam upalakṣaṇaṃ suvarṇarūpyayor api | kārṣikapaṇo daṇḍaviśeṣāpekṣayā yojyaḥ | sahasraguṇita uttamasāhaso daṇḍaḥ | yad vā sahāśītyā vartata iti sāśītiḥ | aśītyadhikasāhasra ity arthaḥ | tadardhaṃ madhyamasāhasaḥ | smṛta iti, śāstrād iyaṃ vyavasthā na pramāṇāntarād ity arthaḥ | saṃjñākaraṇaṃ svaśāstrasaṃvyavahārārtham | uttamasāhasādidaṇḍavacaneṣv eta eva yathā syuḥ || 359–360 ||

 

_atha kiṃ sarvāparādheṣūttamasāhasādyapekṣayā daṇḍaḥ prayojyaḥ | nety ucyate |_

 

                    	**vāgdaṇḍas tv atha dhigdaṇḍo dhanadaṇḍo vadhas tathā |**

**              	yojyā vyastāḥ samastā vāpy aparādhabalād ime || 1.361 ||**

 

vāgdaṇḍaḥ svarūpābhidhānamatram | dhigdaṇḍaḥ kutsanam | dhanadaṇḍa uktaḥ | vadhadaṇḍaḥ śārīraḥ | tathāśabda uccāṭanādyarthaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 361||

 

_ayaṃ cātra vyavahāranītisaṃkṣepaḥ |_

 

                    	**jñātvāparādhaṃ deśaṃ ca kālaṃ balam athāpi ca |**

**              	vayaḥ karma ca vittaṃ ca jñātvā daṇḍaṃ prakalpayet || 1.362 ||**

 

aparādhapunarvacanaṃ dṛṣṭāntārtham | yathaivāparādhaṃ jñātvā tadapekṣayā daṇḍaprakalpanaṃ, tathaiva ca deśakālādyapekṣayāpīty abhiprāyaḥ | jñātveti punarvacanaṃ nirṇīte 'pi vyavahāre dharmānusāreṇa punarvyavahāroddharaṇārtham | spaṣṭam anyat || 362 ||

 

 

                    	iti saṃbhṛtamaṇḍalaḥ sudhāmā pururuciro ramaṇaḥ pratāpaśīlaḥ |

                    	ravir iva nṛpatiḥ samaḥ prajānāṃ jagad akhilaṃ vyavahārato bibharti ||

                    	granthātirekabhītyā yan na nibaddhaṃ mayātra sad vastu |

                    	vyākhyātṛbhir viviktaṃ tal labhyaṃ saṃpradāyebhyaḥ ||

 

**iti paramabhaṭṭārakayājñavalkyapraṇīte dharmaśāstre**

**viśvarūpakṛtavivaraṇabālakrīḍāyāṃ**

**prathamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||**

 

 

 

 

**vyavahārādhyāyaḥ**

** **

**atha sāmānyanyāyaprakaraṇam |**

 

_śriyaḥ samudayaṃ prāptum icchatā vijigīṣuṇā samṛddhyai rājñā prayatnād amitrarājyany ācchidya svarājyaṃ vivardhanīyam ity uktam | tatrāpi kaṣṭatamāḥ khalv arayaḥ kāpaṭikakuyantravyavahāriṇo dasyavaḥ | tebhyo pi rāṣṭraṃ rakṣaṇiyam ity etad apy uktam | athedānīṃ taduddharaṇaprakāravivekārthaṃ vyavahāranirūpaṇaṃ prastauti |_

 

                    	**vyavahārān nṛpaḥ paśyed vidvadbhir brāhmaṇaiḥ saha |**

**              	dharmaśāstrānusāreṇa krodhalobhavivarjitaḥ || 2.1 ||**

 

<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> caitat prāg evoktam "iti saṃcintya nṛpatiḥ" (YDh 1.355) ity atra | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | guṇārthas tv ayam ārambhaḥ, na kośasaṃcicīṣayārthapradhāno bhavet | dharmaśāstrānusāreṇaiva vyavahārān nṛpaḥ paśyed ity arthaḥ | kiṃ ca vidvadbhir brāhmaṇaiḥ saha | pravaktṛtve 'pi brāhmaṇāṇāṃ nṛpasahāyopayogitaiva | draṣṭā tu nigrahānugrahasāmarthyād rājaiva | ata evoktaṃ krodhalobhavivarjita iti | samarthenāpi dharmaśāstrānusāriṇā bhāvyam | na krodhādivaśenānyathā vyavahartavyam ity arthaḥ | ekatve 'pi vyavahārasya svakīyaviśeṣāpekṣayā bahuvacanam | yathāha manuḥ: "teṣām ādyam ṛṇādānam" ityādi (MDh 8.4) | nāradaś ca: "catuṣpādaś caturvyāpī" ityādi (NSm Mā 1.8) || 1 ||

 

_yataś ca dharmaśāstraprādhānyaṃ vyavahāradṛṣṭau, ataḥ |_

 

                    	**śrutādhyayanasaṃpannāḥ kulīnāḥ satyavādinaḥ |**

**              	rājñā sabhāsadaḥ kāryā ripau mitre ca ye samāḥ || 2.2 ||**

 

nigadoktaḥ ślokaḥ || 2 ||

 

_dṛṣṭamūlatvāc ca rājñaḥ svayaṃ vyavahāradarśanasmṛter adṛṣṭārthatve 'pi ca prayojanānusārāt kāryāṇāṃ gurulaghutve samīkṣya |_

 

                    	**apaśyatā kāryavaśād vyavahārān nṛpeṇa tu |**

**              	sabhyaiḥ saha niyoktavyo brāhmaṇaḥ sarvadharmavit || 2.3 ||**

 

so 'pi rājasthānīyatvāt krodhādirahita eva syāt || 3 ||

 

_ata eva ca |_

 

                    	**rāgād dveṣād bhayād vāpi smṛtyapetādikāriṇaḥ |**

**              	sabhyāḥ pṛthak pṛthag daṇḍyā vivādād dviguṇaṃ dhanam || 2.4 ||**

 

smṛtyuktārthānyathākāriṇo rāgādibhis taddviguṇaṃ dhanam ekaikaśo daṇḍyāḥ | ādigrahaṇāt smṛtyarthaṃ cānyathāninīṣava ity abhiprāyaḥ | sarvasabhyadaṇḍād dviguṇaṃ ca rājā tatsthānīyo vā daṇḍyaḥ, tadadhīnatvān nirṇayasya | ata eva ca pṛthak pṛthag iti vīpsā | sabhyāḥ pṛthak pṛthag vivādadviguṇaṃ, taddviguṇaṃ ca rājā | tathā ca vakṣyati || 4 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">atha kiṃ</span> rājñā svapuruṣair vānviṣya kāryiṇo vyavahārayitavyāḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">na</span>, pratiṣedhāt | yathā ha manuḥ: "notpādayet svayaṃ kāryaṃ rājā nāpy asya pūruṣaḥ" iti _(MDh 8.43)_ | kathaṃ tarhi vyavahārapravṛttiḥ | ucyate |_

 

                    	**smṛtyācāravyapetena mārgeṇādharṣitaḥ paraiḥ |**

**              	āvedayati ced rājñe vyavahārapadaṃ hi tat || 2.5 ||**

 

tad eva hi vyavahārapadam, yat smṛtyācāravyapetena bāhyena mārgeṇāsaṃbaddhaiḥ khalīkṛta ity evaṃ kaścit kathayet | na tu svayaṃ kāryārambhaka ity abhiprāyaḥ | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

                    	svaniścitabalādhānas tv arthī svārthapracoditaḥ |

                    	lekhayet pūrvavādaṃ tu kṛtakāryaviniścayaḥ || iti | (NSm Mā 2.1)

smṛtyukta ācāraḥ smṛtyācāraḥ | kuladharmādyabhiprāyaṃ vaitat | parair iti guruśiṣyavādanivṛttyartham | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

                    	guruśiṣyapitāputradampatyoḥ svāmibhṛtyayoḥ |

                    	eteṣāṃ samavetānāṃ vyavahāro na vidyate ||

                    	ekasya bahubhiḥ sārdhaṃ strīṇāṃ preṣyakarais tathā ||

ityādi | kātyāyanaś ca |

                    	yaś ca rāṣṭraviruddhaś ca yaś ca rājñā vivarjitaḥ |

                    	anekapadasaṃkīrṇaḥ pūrvapakṣo na siddhyati ||

tyādi | vyavahāraḥ padanīyo nirūpaṇiyatayety arthaḥ || 5 ||

 

_evaṃ cārthibhir āvedite nirvyājaṃ pratyarthinaṃ tad evāhūya rājñārthipratyarthisabhyānumatena lekhakena |_

 

                    	**pratyarthino 'grato lekhyaṃ yathādevitam arthinā |**

**              	samāmāsatadardhāhonāmajātyādicihnitam || 2.6 ||**

 

yathāveditam ity anubandhaprayojanādiviśiṣṭāparādhajñāpanārtham | samā saṃvatsaraḥ | māsaḥ spaṣṭaḥ | tadardham ardhamāsaḥ | ādigrahaṇaṃ smṛtyantarānusāreṇa bhāṣāprapañcanirūpaṇārtham | yathāha kātyāyanaḥ |

                    	nivedya kālaṃ varṣaṃ ca māsaṃ pakṣaṃ tithiṃ tathā |

                    	lekhāpradeśaṃ viṣayaṃ sthānajātyākṛtīś ca yāḥ ||

                    	sādhyārthamānaṃ dravyaṃ ca saṃkhyā nāma tathātmanaḥ |

                    	rājñāṃ ca kramaśo nāma nivāsaṃ sādhyanāma ca ||

                    	kramāt pitṝṇāṃ nāmāni pīḍāṃ cāhartṛdāyakau |

                    	kṣamāliṅgādyādikālaṃ pakṣaṃ saṃkīrtya kalpayet || iti |

etāni ca nyāyānusāreṇālocya vyastāni samastāni vā lekhanīyāni | pūrvaṃ ca bhūmāv ālikhya pratijñāṃ śodhayitvā paścāt patrāropaṇaṃ kāryam | yathāha |

                    	adhikān śodhayed arthān nyūnāṃś ca pratipūrayet |

                    	bhūmau niveśayet tāvad yāvat pakṣaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ ||

                    	pratijñādoṣanirmuktaṃ sādhyaṃ satkāraṇānvitam |

                    	niścitaṃ lokasiddhaṃ ca pakṣaṃ pakṣavido viduḥ ||

ityādi | pratijñādoṣās tu | yathāha |

                    	apradiddhaṃ sadoṣaṃ ca nirarthaṃ niṣprayojanam |

                    	asādhyaṃ vā viruddhaṃ vā pakṣaṃ rājā vivarjayet ||

                    	nyāyaṃ me necchate kartum anyāyaṃ vā karoti ca |

                    	na lekhayati yas tv evaṃ tasya pakṣo na siddhyati ||

ityādi | nāradaś ca |

                    	bhāṣāyām uttaraṃ yāvat pratyarthī na niveśayet |

                    	arthī viśodhayet tāvad yāvad vastu vivakṣitam || iti | (NSm Mā 2.7)

nātra chalajātyādīnām avasara ity abhiprāyaḥ evaṃ pūrvavad yuktaṃ patrārūḍhaṃ śrāvayet || 6 ||

 

                    	**śrutārthasyottaraṃ lekhyaṃ pūrvāvedakasaṃnidhau |**

 

śrutaś cāsāv arthaś ca śrutārthaḥ | tasya yady anurūpam uttaraṃ bhavati, tato lekhyam | anyathā parājaya evety abhiprāyaḥ | saṃnidhāv iti sadyonirṇayārtham | etac cātyayikakāryaviṣayaṃ draṣṭavyam |

 

_yataś caivam |_

 

                    	**tato 'rthī lekhayet sadyaḥ prijñātarthasādhanm || 2.7 ||**

 

na kālaṃ hared ity arthaḥ || 7 ||

 

_kasmāt punaḥ pratijñātārthasādhanābhidhānayatnaḥ, yasmāt |_

 

                    	**tatsiddhau siddhim āpnoti viparītam ato 'nyathā |**

 

uktaṃ ca |

                    	sāras tu vyavahārāṇāṃ pratijñā samudāhṛtā |

                    	taddhānau hīyate vādī taraṃs tām uttaro bhavet || iti | (NSm Mā 1.6)

ata eva ca yat tārkikaiḥ pratijñāvacanasyānaṅgatvam uktaṃ tad api pratyuktam |

 

_yasmāt_,

 

                    	**catuṣpād vyavahāro 'yaṃ vivādeṣūpadarśitaḥ || 2.8 ||**

 

nyāyāgamābhyām iti śeṣaḥ | pratijñā uttaraṃ sādhanaṃ nirṇayaś cety evaṃ catuṣpāt | anyathā tu na syāt | tasmāt pratijākrameṇaiva vivādakriyety abhiprāyaḥ || 8 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca yadā tu mamānenāparāddham ity evam uktaḥ svam abhiyogam anistīryaiva tam eva pratyabhiyuṅkte, tadāyaṃ kramo nopapadyate | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | tenaiva ca |_

 

                    	**abhiyogam anistīrya nainaṃ pratyabhiyojayet |**

**              	na cābhiyuktam anyena noktaṃ viprakṛtiṃ nayet || 2.9 ||**

 

svābhiyogam anistīryābhiyoktāraṃ nābhiyuñjīta, anavasthāprasaṅgena vyavahārāsamāpteḥ | ata eva cānyābhiyukto 'py anabhiyojyaḥ | na ca svayam uktārthāpalāpaḥ kartavya iti || 9 ||

 

_asyāpavādaḥ |_

 

                    	**kuryāt pratyabhiyogaṃ tu kalahe sāhaeṣu ca |**

**              	ubhayoḥ pratibhūr grāhyaḥ samarthaḥ kāryanirṇaye || 2.10 ||**

 

anistīrya svābhiyogaṃ sāhasādau prayabhiyuñjīta | ayam eva tatra nirṇayaprakāra ity arthaḥ | sarvavivādeṣu ca yadā na sadya eva nirṇayaḥ syāt, tata ubhayor api kāryiṇoḥ pratibhūḥ kāryanirṇayakṣamo grāhyaḥ || 10 ||

 

_yadā tu nyāyenānyataraḥ kāryo parājitaḥ, tadā |_

 

                    	**nihnave bhāvito dadyād dhanaṃ rājñe ca tatsamam |**

**              	mithyābhiyogī dviguṇam abhiyogād dhanaṃ vahet || 2.11 ||**

 

nihnavo 'palāpaḥ tatra spaṣṭīkṛte yāvad dhaninā prārthitaṃ, tāvad deyam | rājñe ca tattulyam anyat | yadā tu mithyaivābhiyuṅkte, tadābhiyoktrā prārthitād dviguṇaṃ rājña eva dhanaṃ deyam ity arthaḥ || 11 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">kiṃ punaḥ</span> sarvatraiva sadyovyavahāranirṇītiḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | evaṃ yuktam | tathāpi tu |_

 

                    	**sāhasasteyapāruṣyago'bhiśāpātyaye striyaḥ |**

**              	vivādayet sadya eva kālo 'nyatrecchayā bhavet || 2.12 ||**

 

nirvahaṇam anirūpyaiva svabalāvaṣṭambhena sahasā prasahya yat kriyate, tat sāhasam | steyaṃ pāruṣyaṃ ca vakṣyati | govadhādyabhiśāpo go'bhiśāpaḥ | gograhaṇam udāharaṇārtham | sarvapaśūnāṃ śṛṅgiṇāṃ vābhiśāpaḥ | atyayaḥ kālapratīkṣaṇāsamarthaṃ kāryam | striyaś ca yatrābhiyujyante, tatra kālapratīkṣaṇe virodhāt sadya eva vivādayet | vivādaṃ samāpayed ity arthaḥ | anyatra tv ṛṇādānādau kālapratīkṣaṇam api kāryam | dhruvādhikaranecchayā vā bhavati | yathāha nāradaḥ |

                    	gahanatvād vivādānāṃ kṣaṇikatvāt smṛter api |

                    	ṛṇādiṣu haret kālaṃ kāmaṃ tattvabubhutsayā || iti (NSm Mā 1.38) || 12 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> anekaprakārāḥ puṃśāṃ pravṛttayaḥ | tatra yadi kaścid vyavahārānuguṇavākpravṛttyakuśalatayā satye 'py arthe mithyāvādīva lakṣyate | anyas tu kaścit kapaṭavyavahāracaturo mithyābhūte 'py arthe satyavādīva lakṣyate | tataś ca vyavahāranirūpaṇaprayāsavaiyarthyam eva | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> eva, yadi vivekāvadhṛtiprakāro na syāt | syāt tu khalūpāyaḥ |_

 

                    	**deśād deśāntaraṃ yāti sṛkvaṇī parileḍhi ca |**

**              	lalāṭaṃ svidyate cāsya mukhaṃ vaivarṇyam eti ca || 2.13 ||**

**              	pariśuṣyatskhaladvākyo viruddhaṃ bahu bhāṣate |**

**              	vākcakṣuḥ pūjayati no tathauṣṭhau nirbhujaty api || 2.14 ||**

**              	svabhāvād vikṛtiṃ gacchen manovākkāyakarmabhiḥ |**

**              	abhiyoge ca sākṣye ca sa duṣṭaḥ parikīrtitaḥ || 2.15 ||**

 

yady api vyavahāramārganipuṇatayā kutaścid vā sahāyādyavaṣṭambhāt sādhutābhāsaṃ pratyayam utpādayati, tathāpi yasyaivamādīni liṅgāni sa duṣṭaḥ parikīrtitaḥ | parikīrtitavacanaṃ dauṣṭyaniścayakhyāpanārtham | sphuṭāvagatacāturyaś caivamādibhir liṅgair adhyavaseyaḥ | anyasya tv apratibhayāpi dhūrtajanasaṃtrāsitasya vā bhavaty eva | ataś caiva vivicyaitāni liṅgāni vyavasthāpanīyānīty anavadyam | sṛkvaṇī oṣṭhasaṃdhī | "vākcakṣuḥ pūjayati no" iti chedaḥ | vācaś cakṣuṣo vā pūjāṃ na karotīty arthaḥ | vākpūjā svoktiniścayāvaṣṭambhaḥ | cakṣuṣaś ca darśanāvaṣṭambhaḥ | oṣṭhanirbhujanam anekadhauṣṭhavikāraḥ | jihvayā vā parilehanam | spaṣṭam anyat || 13–15 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">yadā</span> punar dvayor vyavahāravipratipattau svabalāvaṣṭambhenaivāntareṇāpi rājāvedanaṃ sādhayituṃ sāmarthyaṃ syāt, tadāpi kim avaśyaṃ rājña eva nivedanīyam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | evaṃ yuktam | yataḥ |_

 

                    	**saṃdigdhārthaṃ svatantro yaḥ sādhayed yaś ca niṣpatet |**

**              	na cāhūto vadet kiṃcid dhīno daṇḍyaś ca sa smṛtaḥ || 2.16 ||**

 

yathaiva yo rājñāhūto niṣpatet praṇaśyet, yo vā rājāntikaṃ gataḥ saṃbhāvitapratibhānavān api na kiṃcid vadet, sa yathā parājito daṇḍārhaś ca syād, evaṃ yo 'pi pratyarthisaṃdigdhaṃ nyāyena niścayam akṛtvaiva haṭhāt svatantraḥ sādhayet, so 'pi parājito daṇḍyaś cety abhiprāyaḥ || 16 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvad yatra sākṣiṇaḥ syuḥ, tatra tadadhīnaiva nirṇītiḥ, tadabhāve viparyaye vā deśāntaragamanādibhir liṅgaiḥ | yatra tarhi dvayor api sākṣiṇo liṅgāni vā deśāntaragamanādīni, tatra katham | ucyate |_

 

                    	**sākṣiṣūbhayataḥ satsu sākṣiṇaḥ pūrvavādinaḥ |**

**              	pūrvapakṣe 'dharībhūte bhavanty uttaravādinaḥ || 2.17 ||**

 

kva punar viṣaye dvayoḥ sākṣisaṃbhavaḥ | yatrottaravādī pratyavaskandanena vyavahāram ākṣipati | yathā kenāpy ukte mamānenāmuṣmin kāle deśe caivaṃ dravyaṃ gṛhītam iti, athāparo vadati: satyam, yady evam | ahaṃ punas tasmin kāle nirdiṣṭadeśād deśāntarastham ātmānaṃ sākṣibhiḥ sādhayāmīti | tatra dvayoḥ sākṣyabhyupagame pūrvavādina eva sākṣiṇo bhaveyuḥ, tatprādhānyād vyavahārapravṛtteḥ | yatra tv apramāṇīkṛtaḥ pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ, tatrottaravādina eva sākṣiṇaḥ syuḥ | yathā satyaṃ yathaivāyam āha | tat tu mayāsya pratiniryātitam | evaṃ ca śakṣibhiḥ sādhayāmīti || 17 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">yadā</span> tu pratyavaskandanam anena mārgeṇa punaḥ pūrvavady adharīkuryāt, tadā katham | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span> | evam auttarādharyakaraṇe saty avyavasthaiva syāt | kā tarhi gatiḥ | abhyadhikapaṇopanyāsena yadi paraṃ (?) vyavahāraparāvṛttiḥ | anyathānavasthaiva syāt | tataś ca |_

 

                    	**sapaṇaś ced vivādaḥ syāt tatra hīnaṃ tu dāpayet |**

**              	daṇḍaṃ ca svapaṇaṃ caiva dhanine dhanam eva ca || 2.18 ||**

 

daṇḍasvapaṇau rājñe deyau | svavataḥ paṇaḥ svapaṇaḥ, yo dhaninā vyavahāraṃ parāvartayituṃ paṇaḥ kṛta ity arthaḥ | dhanaṃ tu dhanina eva rājā dāpayet | caśabdo dhigdaṇḍādisamuccayārthaḥ | evaṃ tāvat sākṣisaṅkare niyama uktaḥ | lalāṭasvedādiliṅgasaṅkare katham | tatrāpy anumānamūlatvāl laiṅgakādismṛtīnāṃ samyaganumānanirūpaṇādhīna eva vyavahāranirṇayaḥ || 18 ||

 

_sarvathā tu |_

 

                    	**chalaṃ nirasya bhūtena vyavahārān nayen nṛpaḥ |**

 

vyavahāro hi nāmānṛtaprabhavo vyājaikanibandhanaḥ | tathā coktaṃ nāradena |

                    	dharmaikatānāḥ puruṣā yadāsan satyavādinaḥ |

                    	tadā na vyavahāro 'bhūn na dveṣo nāpi matsaraḥ ||

                    	naṣṭe dharme manuṣyeṣu vyavahāraḥ pravartitaḥ |

                    	draṣṭā ca vyavahārāṇāṃ rājā daṇḍadharaḥ kṛtaḥ || iti | (NSm Mā 1.1–2)

adharmaprādhānyaṃ vyavahāreṣv ity arthaḥ |

 

_yataś caitad evam, ataś ca |_

 

                    	**bhūtam apy anupanyastaṃ hīyate vyavahārataḥ || 2.19 ||**

 

vyavahāramārgeṇānyathā kriyate | tathā coktam:

                    	acoraś coratāṃ prāpto māṇḍavyo vyavahārataḥ | iti | (NSm Mā 1.36)

ataś ca prayatnato nirākṛtacchalādiḥ satyaikapravaṇo rājā vyavahāreṣu kṛtī syād ity arthaḥ || 19 ||

 

_yadi tv anekatrārthe 'bhiyuktaḥ sarvam ādau nety uktvā punaḥ kiṃcit kathaṃcit abhyupagacchet, tatra tanmātram eva kim asau dāpyaḥ | nety ucyate |_

 

                    	**nihnute likhito 'nekam ekadeśavibhāvitaḥ |**

**              	dāpyaḥ sarvān nṛpeṇārthān na grāhyas tv aniveditaḥ || 2.20 ||**

 

anekārthāpalāpakatvena likhitaḥ rājñe kathitaḥ yadi nihnute, punaś caikadeśe sa vibhāvyate, tato dāpyaḥ sarvān sadaṇḍakān arthān | yadi tu na likhitaḥ, tadaivaṃbhūto 'py adaṇḍyaḥ | yad vā "na grāhyas tv aniveditaḥ" ity asyānyā vyākhyā: dhanine rājñā sarvam arthaṃ dāpyaḥ | na tu daṇḍyaḥ | tadanabhipreto 'pīty arthaḥ || 20 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> asau tadanabhipretatve 'py aparādhitvād daṇḍya eva | evamādīny eva hi nṛpasyārthotpattisthānāni | anyathā tu kvacid eva rājño daṇḍaḥ syāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span> |_

 

                    	**smṛtivirodhe nyāyas tu balavān vyavahārataḥ |**

**              	arthaśāstrāt tu balavad dharmaśāstram iti sthitiḥ || 2.21 ||**

 

yady arthaśāstrānusāritā syāt, tataḥ syād apy evam | yadā tu dharmaśāstram eva balavat, tadā tadviruddha evārthasaṃcayo jyāyān | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evaṃ sati yatrāsatye 'pi vastuni satyatāpratibhānaṃ, tatrāpi rājño doṣaprasaṅgaḥ | yathā māṇḍavyavadhādau, smṛtyā hi samyag aparādhinām eva daṇḍavidhānāt | tatra ca nyāyato 'parādhāpādane 'pi paramārthatas tadabhāvād aparādhī naiva | na cānyo vyavahāranirṇītihetuḥ | ataḥ saṅkaṭam etat | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nātra</span> saṅkaṭam | smṛter virodhe nyāyas tu balavān | kasmād vyavahārataḥ | anyathā vyavahārapravṛttyabhāvaprasaṅga ity arthaḥ | atha vā smṛtinyāyavirodhe smṛtir eva jyāyasī, na tu nyāyaḥ, vyavahārato hi nyāyapravṛtteḥ | vividham avaharaṇaṃ vyavahāraḥ vyājabhūyiṣṭha ity arthaḥ | na cāsau śāstravirodhy apy aṅgīkartavyaḥ | yasmād arthaśāstrād darmaśāstrasyaiva balīyastvam iti sthitiḥ | anyas tv aparamārtha ity arthaḥ | iyam eva ca vyākhyā jyāyasī | yathāvastu pramāṇapravṛttiḥ, na pramāṇapravṛttyanurodhitā vastunaḥ | sthite vastuni tadanusāriṇī pramāṇāvagatir ity anavadyam | anye tv anyathemaṃ ślokaṃ varṇayanti: smṛtidvyavirodhe nyāyo balavān, vyavahāratas tu pravṛttyānuguṇyāt | yatra tv arthaśāstradharmaśāstrayor virodhaḥ tatra darmaśāstraṃ balīyaḥ | yathārthaśāstre vyavahāraprakaraṇa uktaṃ:

                    	nātatāyivadhe doṣo hantur bhavati kaścana | iti | (MDh 8.350)

punar dharmaśāstre prāyaścittaprakaraṇe:

                    	kāmato brāhmaṇavadhe niṣkṛtir na vidhīyate | iti | (MDh 11.89)

tatra dharmaśāstrabalīyastvād ātatāyivadhe doṣaprasaṅga iti | tat punaḥ prakṛtānupayogān niṣpramāṇakatvāc ca nātīva samyak || 21 ||

 

_na cāvaśyaṃ tattvābhiniveśinām api paramārthāvagatyupāyābhāva eva | yasmāt |_

 

                    	**pramāṇaṃ likhitaṃ bhuktiḥ sākṣiṇaś ceti kīrtitam |**

**              	eṣām anyatamābhāve divyānyatamam ucyate || 2.22 ||**

 

yadā hi dṛṣṭair eva likhitādibhis tattvāvagatiḥ, tadā sarvaṃ sutham eva | atha tu tāni vyastāni samastāni vā na santi, vidyamānāny api vā na paritoṣakṣamāṇi | tadā vakṣyamāṇadivyānām anyatamena tattvāvagamād avirodhaḥ || 22 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**sarveṣv eva vivādeṣu balavaty uttarā kriyā |**

**              	ādhau pratigrahe krīte pūrvā tu balavattarā || 2.23 ||**

 

sarvavivādeṣv anirṇīteṣūttarā kriyā divyalakṣaṇaiva nirṇayāvyabhicārād balīyasī | ādhyādiṣu tu pūrvā lekhyādikā | divyakriyāyās tatrāsaṃbhavāt | yato devadattena yajñadattasyāhitaṃ tatputrair api bhujyate | na ca teṣāṃ divyaprakṛtyavaṣṭambhaḥ, svānubhavābhāvāt | atha vā lekhyaviṣya evāyaṃ ślokaḥ | sarveṣv eva lekhyavivādeṣūttarottarasaṅkramaṇād uttaralekhyakriyābalīyastvaṃ parīkṣābāhulyena vyājakaraṇāpanodanāt | ādhyādiṣu tu parasaṃsthatvān mūla(?)lekhyaprādhānyena pūrvakriyaiva jyāyasīty arthaḥ || 23 ||

 

_bhuktau tu |_

 

                    	**paśyato 'bruvato bhūmer hānir viṃśativārṣikī |**

**              	pareṇa bhujyamānāyā dhanasya daśavārṣikī || 2.24 ||**

 

paśyann api yaḥ parair asaṃbaddhair bhujyamāne na kiṃcaneyatā kālenāpi brūyāt, nūnaṃ tadīyaṃ na bhaved ity abhiprāyaḥ | kālaniyamas tu vedamūlatayaiva draṣṭavyaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> etad ayuktam | yad anabhidhānamātreṇaivārthanāśaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">evaṃ</span> tarhy etad api vedād eva | upekṣayāpi dravyanāśo bhavatīty ato draṣṭavyaṃ parair bhujyamānaṃ nopekṣaṇīyam ity abhiprāyaḥ | athetarasya kiṃ svatvasaṃbandho 'sti | pūrvasya tāvad dhānir ity ācāryābhiprāyaḥ | itarasyāpi tu svatvaṃ naiva, parasvabuddhyaiva bhogapravṛtteḥ | yady evaṃ na tarhi rājñas tadā doṣaḥ | tad apy satyam | atha kiṃ nṛpasyaiva tad bhavatu svāmino hānyupadeśāt, tathāvidhasya ca rājagāmitvāt | atha vā pūrvasvāmina eva tadarpaṇīyam, tatsvatvāpāye hetvabhāvāt | smṛtis tu dṛṣṭamūlatayāpy upapadyata eva | upekṣāniṣedhamātraṃ caitat | hānivacanaṃ tu nindāmātratvenopekṣakasya vyavahārapravṛttyayogyatāmātrajñaptiphalam | tad eva cātra yuktam | anyathā śrutahānir aśrutakalpanā ca syād ity alaṃ prasaṅgena || 24 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">kim</span> upekṣayā sarvatraiva vyavahārapravṛttyayogyatā syāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> |_

 

                    	**ādhisīmopanikṣepajaḍabāladhanair vinā |**

**              	tathopanidhirājastrīśrotriyāṇāṃ dhanair api || 2.25 ||**

 

ādhyādiṣu tu bhuktir naivāpahārakāraṇam ity abhiprāyaḥ | ādhis tāvad bhogāyaiva kriyate | sīmā ca pratijāgartṛdoṣād anekadhā bhujyate | nikṣepaś ca samarpitatvāt | jaḍabālayor asāmarthyāt | upanidhiṃ vakṣyati | rājadhanam anekagāmitvāt | strīdhanaṃ cāsvātantryāt | śrotriyāṇāṃ vyāpārāntarāpekṣayā | tatheti prakārārthaḥ | sarvathā yatraiva svāmitvād ṛte 'pi bhuktiḥ saṃbhāvyate, tatraiva tatkṛtopabhogo nāpahārakāraṇam ity arthaḥ || 25 ||

 

_yataś cādhyādiṣu nimittāntarād bhuktiḥ, tataḥ|_

 

                    	**ādhyādīnāṃ hi hartāraṃ dhanine dāpayed dhanam |**

**              	daṇḍaṃ ca tatsamaṃ rājñe śaktyapekṣam athāpi vā || 2.26 ||**

 

dhanine dhanaṃ dattvānantaraṃ rājñe tatsamaṃ deyam, api vā śaktyapekṣam ity arthaḥ || 26 ||

 

_yasmāc ca bhuktimātreṇa nārthanāśaḥ, tasmāt |_

 

                    	**āgamo 'bhyadhiko bhukter vinā pūrvakramāgatāt |**

 

āgamo lekhyam | tad bhukter balīyaḥ, niścitatvād anyathāpi bhuktyupapatteḥ | pūrvakrame tu sati bhukter balīyastvaṃ lekhyāntaranirastasyāpi lekhyasya pramādataḥ sthitisaṃbhavāt | tripuruṣabhuktiḥ pūrvakramaḥ | yataś ca nāśādivyājena lekhyasyopagatādibādhitasyāpi sthitisaṃbhavaḥ |

 

_tatra |_

 

                    	**āgame 'pi balaṃ naiva bhuktiḥ stokāpi yatra no || 2.27 ||**

 

na syād yāvatyā vinā lekhyapratiṣṭhā na syād ity arthaḥ|| 27 ||

 

_yasmāc ca kramabhuktir āgamād balīyasī, tasmāt |_

 

                    	**āgamas tu kṛto yena so 'bhiyuktas tam uddharet |**

**              	na tatsutas tatsuto vā bhuktis tatra garīyasī || 2.28 ||**

 

lekhyakartuḥ putro na lekhyadoṣān apākuryāt, na hy asau pitṛval lekhyasvarūpajño yataḥ | dhanaṃ tu na tatputrasya | tasya tu yaḥ putraḥ, tasya dhanam api syāt | yasmād bhuktis tatra garīyasī lekhyād ity uktam evety abhiprāyaḥ || 28 ||

 

_lekhyakṛtputras tu kim iti dhanabhāṅ na bhavati | yasmād |_

 

**              	āgamena viśuddhena bhogo yāti praṃāṇatām |**

**              	aviśuddhāgamo bhogaḥ prāmāṇyaṃ nādhigacchati || 2.29 ||**

 

lekhyasvarūpājñatvāt[^9] taddoṣānapākaraṇamātram eva syāt | na tu pramāṇarahitaṃ svāmitvam apīty abhiprāyaḥ | prāmāṇyaṃ ca viśuddhāgamasyaiva bogasya, na tu bhuktimātrasyety arthaḥ || 29 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**yo 'bhiyuktaḥ paretaḥ syāt tasya rikthī tam uddharet |**

**              	na tatra kāraṇaṃ bhuktir āgamena vinākṛtā || 2.30 ||**

 

yadi hi lekhyadoṣāpākaraṇābhiyuktaḥ pareto mṛtaḥ syāt, tadā tadīyadhanagrāhy apākuryāt | etac ca lekhyakartṛviṣayam | itarasya dravyāpahāra eva syāt | yasmān na tatra svāmitve bhuktir āgamaśūnyā kāraṇaṃ bhavati, kṛtāpi tu vyabhicāriṇīty arthaḥ || 30 ||

 

_yadi tu duṣṭe 'pi lekhyādau tatkartā na doṣān apākuryāt, tadā kathaṃ syāt | uktaṃ tādṛśe viṣaye rājāvedanaṃ "smṛtyācāravyapetena mārgeṇa" ity atra | ata eva ca |_

** **

**              	nṛpo 'rthādhikṛtāḥ pūgāḥ śreṇayo 'tha kulāni ca |**

**              	pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ guru jñeyaṃ vyavahāravidhau nṛṇām || 2.31 ||**

 

nṛpo hi balavān vyavahāraṃ kārayituṃ samartha iti vyavahāravidhau sa eva jyāyān | itare 'pi sāmarthāpekṣayā durbalā balīyāṃsaś ca bhavanti | ataś ca kulādikrameṇaiva vyavahārāṇāṃ rājagāmitā draṣṭavyā | brāhmaṇādisamūhāḥ pūgāḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 31 ||

 

_prabhutvād eva ca rājā tadarthādhikṛto vā prāḍvivākādiḥ |_

 

                    	**balopadhivinirvṛttān vyavahārān nivartayet |**

**              	strīnaktamantarāgārabahīḥśatrukṛtāṃs tathā || 2.32 ||**

 

spaṣṭārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 32 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**mattonmattārtavyasanibālabhītaprayojitaḥ |**

**              	asaṃbandhakṛtaś caiva vyavahāro na siddhyati || 2.33 ||**

 

matto 'tiharṣitaḥ, ahaṃkṛto vā | unmatto grahagṛhītādiḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 33 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**kulāni jātayaḥ śreṇyo gaṇān janapadān api |**

**              	svadharmāc calitān rājā vinīya sthāpayet pathi || 2.34 ||**

 

kulāni kuṭumbāni | jātayo brāhmaṇādyā varṇāḥ | śreṇayaḥ kārukasamudāyaḥ | gaṇā brāhmaṇādisamūhāḥ | janapado durgāśrayo 'tra jano 'bhipretaḥ | so 'pi rājñā svadharmāc calito daṇḍya ity abhiprāyaḥ | sarvaś cetarajano vā janapadaḥ | sarvathā sarvaḥ svadharmāc calito rājñā daṇḍya ity abhiprāyaḥ || 34 ||

 

_yasmāc ca rājā vyavahāravidhāv agryo daṇḍadharaḥ, tasmāt |_

 

                    	**pranaṣṭādhigataṃ deyaṃ nṛpeṇa dhanine dhanam |**

**              	vibhāvayen na cel liṅgais tatsamaṃ daṇḍam arhati || 2.35 ||**

 

kasyacit pranaṣṭaṃ yadi rājñānyena vādhigataṃ labdhaṃ tad yadi dhaninā prārthyate, tataḥ kiṃ tat, kiyatsaṃkhyaṃ cety evaṃ pṛṣṭvāvisaṃvādakasyānviṣyārpaṇīyam | na ced evaṃ vibhāvayet tatsamaṃ daṇḍyaḥ || 35 ||

 

_yat tūsannasvāmikaṃ nidhyādikaṃ tatra kā kathā | ucyate |_

 

                    	**rājā labdhvā nidhiṃ dadyāt dvijebhyo 'rdhaṃ dvijaḥ punaḥ |**

**              	vidvān aśeṣam ādadyāt sa sarvasya prabhur yataḥ || 2.36 ||**

 

sa sarvasya prabhur ity anena pratigrahādyabhāve 'pi svatvasaṃbandho 'stīti jñāpayati || 36 ||

 

                    	**itareṇa nidhau labdhe rājā ṣaṣṭhāṃśam āharet |**

**              	aniveditavijñāto dāpyas tad daṇḍam eva ca || 2.37 ||**

 

itareṇa brāhmaṇenaivānabhirūpeṇety arthaḥ | gautamīyaṃ tv abrāhmaṇaviṣayam: "nidhyadhigamo rājadhanam" iti (GDh 10.43) | yāvān nidhyadhigamaḥ, sa sarvo rājadhanam ity arthaḥ | tathā ca "na brāhmaṇasyānabhirūpasya" ity uktvāha "abrāhmaṇo 'py ākhyātā ṣaṣṭhaṃ labetety eke" iti (GDh 10.44–45) | anākhyāya tu gṛhṇan brāhmaṇo 'pi sarvam ādāya śaktyanurūpeṇa daṇḍyaḥ syāt | vidvāṃs tu "sa sarvasya prabhuḥ" iti vacanād anākhyāyāpi gṛhṇan na doṣabhāg ity arthaḥ || 37 ||

 

_yataś ca nidhyādiṣv asvāmikeṣu rājñaḥ prabhutvaṃ, tata eva ca |_

 

                    	**deyaṃ corahṛtaṃ dravyaṃ rājñā janapadāya tu |**

 

_kasmāt | yasmāt |_

 

                    	**adadad dhi samāpnoti kilbiṣaṃ tasya yasya tat || 2.38 ||**

 

pālakatvena hi rājagāmitā nidhyādeḥ | pālakaś cet kim iti parakīyaṃ corādihṛtaṃ na prayacched ity abhiprāyaḥ | janapadagrahaṇaṃ sarvārtham | na brāhmaṇāyaivety arthaḥ | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ: "corāpahṛtaṃ tu sarvebhyo 'nviṣyārpaṇīyam alābhe svakośād vā, adadac corakilbiṣī syāt" ityādi || 38 ||

 

**iti sāmānyanyāyaprakaraṇam |**

** **

**atha ṛṇādānaprakaraṇam |**

 

_evaṃ tāvat sāmānyena nyāyasvarūpam abhidhāyedānīm ṛṇādānādivyavahārasthānakrameṇa viśeṣataḥ prastauti | tatrādyatā manvādibhir ṛṇādānasyoktā | atas tad eva tāvad ucyate |_

 

                    	**aśītibhāgo vṛddhiḥ syān māsi māsi sabandhake |**

**              	varṇakramāc chataṃ dvitricatuṣpañcakam anyathā || 2.39 ||**

 

yady apy aviśeṣeṇāśītibhāgo 'bhihitaḥ, tathāpi brāhmaṇasyaivayam | anyeṣāṃ tu pādavṛddhyā vṛddhikalpanam | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ: "pādopacayāt krameṇetareṣām" iti | anyathā tu bandhakarahite dvikatrikatvaṃ vṛddher ity abhiprāyaḥ | yac caitad vṛddhiparimāṇam uktam, ata ūrdhvaṃ na gṛhṇīyāt | na tv arvāggrahaṇe virodhaḥ || 39 ||

 

_anayaiva vṛddhyā |_

 

                    	**santatis tu paśustrīṇāṃ rasasyāṣṭaguṇā parā |**

**              	vastradhānyahiraṇyānāṃ catustridviguṇā tathā || 2.40 ||**

 

paśustrīṇāṃ vṛddhiḥ phalabhogyatvenārpitānāṃ yā prasūtiḥ sā dhanikasya syāt | tuśabdāt santatir eva, nāparā vṛddhir ity arthaḥ | paśustrīṇāṃ iti puṃspaśusantānavyavacchedārtham | atha vā paśūnāṃ strīṇāṃ ca dāsīnām iti yojyam | ikṣvādirasasyāṣṭaguṇā parā vṛddhiḥ | vastrāṇāṃ caturguṇā, dhānyānāṃ triguṇā, hiraṇyādīnāṃ dviguṇā | tac cāśītibhāgādyanusāreṇa yāvatā kālena hiraṇyaṃ dviguṇaṃ, tāvataiva dhānyādeḥ svaparimāṇayogaḥ || 40 ||

 

_cāturvarṇyātirekeṇa tu |_

 

                    	**kāntāragās tu daśakaṃ sāmudrā viṃśakaṃ śatam |**

**              	dadyur vā svakṛtāṃ vṛddhiṃ sarve sarvāsu jātiṣu || 2.41 ||**

 

kāntāragā araṇyavāsinaḥ, tadgāmino vā | sāmudrāḥ samudravyavahāriṇaḥ | te pratimāsaṃ daśakaṃ viṃśakaṃ ca śataṃ dadyuḥ | yad vā kāntāraṃ varṇāpaśadatvaṃ ye gacchanti, te kāntāragāḥ, varṇāpaśadā ity arthaḥ | saha mudrayā niyamena vartata iti samudro varṇāśramaviṣayaḥ, tam atilaṅghayanti ye, te viparītalakṣaṇayā vā sāmudrāḥ, vikarmasthā ity arthaḥ | dadyur vā svaparibhāṣītāṃ vṛddhiṃ sarve brāhmaṇādayo 'pi sarvāsv apaśadajātiṣv ity arthaḥ | āpatkalpaś cāyaṃ brāhmaṇādīnām ity etad vāśabdena dyotayati || 41 ||

 

_anayā ca vṛddhyā |_

 

                    	**prapannaṃ sādhayāno 'rthaṃ na vācyo nṛpater bhavet |**

**              	sādhyamāno nṛpaṃ gacchet dāpyo daṇḍyaś ca tad dhanam || 2.42 ||**

 

prapannaṃ nyāyena spaṣṭīkṛtaṃ yadṛcchayā sādhanāno 'rthaṃ na rājñā kiṃcid vaktavyaḥ | yadi tu sādhyamāno rājany āvedayet, tato daṇḍyo dāpyaś ca rājñaiva tad dhanaṃ, dhanikāyeti śeṣaḥ || 42 ||

 

_atha yady ekam ṛṇinaṃ yugapad dhaninaḥ prārthayeyuḥ, tadāyaṃ kramaḥ |_

 

                    	**gṛhītānukramād dadyād dhaninām adhamarṇikaḥ |**

**              	dadyāt tu brāhmaṇāyāgre nṛpāya tadanantaram || 2.43 ||**

 

grahaṇānukramād evādhamarṇikenarṇam ekajātīyebhyo deyam | jātibhede brāhmaṇādikrameṇaiva | tuśabdāt tulyajātīyatve 'pi guṇādyapekṣaṃ kramaṃ dyotayati || 43 ||

 

_vipratipannas tv ṛṇiko rājany āvedya sādyaḥ | tatra ca |_

 

**              	rājñādhamarṇiko dāpyaḥ sādhitād daśakaṃ śatam |**

**              	pañcakaṃ tu śataṃ dāpyaḥ prāptārtho hy uttamarṇikaḥ || 2.44 ||**

 

ṛṇiko rājñā sarvaṃ dhanikāyārthaṃ dāpyaḥ | svayaṃ ca tasmād evādhamarṇikād daśakaṃ śataṃ gṛhṇīyāt | dhaniko 'pi sādhitārthasaṃkhyayā pāritoṣikaṃ rājñe pañcakaṃ śataṃ dadyāt | uttamarṇiko dhanikaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 44 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvat samṛddhaṃ dāpayet | asamṛddhaṃ tu |_

 

                    	**hīnajātiṃ parikṣīṇam ṛṇārthaṃ karma kārayet |**

**              	brāhmaṇas tu parikṣīṇaḥ śanair dāpyo yathodayam || 2.45 ||**

 

spaṣṭārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 45 ||

 

_yathotpattyā ca dadataḥ|_

 

                    	**dīyamānaṃ na gṛhṇīta prayuktaṃ yaḥ svakaṃ dhanam |**

**              	madhyasthasthāpitaṃ tat syād vardhate na tataḥ param || 2.46 ||**

 

svakaṃ dhanam iti vacanād ātmanepadayogāc ca saṃnihitadhanikaviṣayam etat | anyathā tu vardhata evety abhiprāyaḥ || 46 ||

 

_ṛṇike saty ayaṃ dānakramaḥ | tadabhāve tu |_

 

                    	**rikthagrāha ṛṇaṃ dadyād yoṣidgrāhas tathaiva ca |**

**              	putro 'nanyāśritadravyaḥ putrahīnasya rikthinaḥ || 2.47 ||**

 

rikthānusāritvād ṛṇānāṃ rikthagrāhiṇa eva nirvicikitsaṃ dadyuḥ | nirdhanasya tu niyogād vinā yo 'sya bhāryāṃ saṃgṛhṇīyāt, sa dadyāt | etac cābrāhmaṇaviṣayam, tadyoṣītām evānyagāmitvasaṃbhavāt | "tathaiva ca" iti dhanagrāhivad avikalpayan yoṣīdgrāhy api dadyād ity arthaḥ | tad eva hi dravyaṃ dravyahīnasyety abhiprāyaḥ | etasmād eva cātideśād rikthābhāva eva yoṣidgrāhādayaḥ pratyetavyāḥ | "putro 'nanyāśrita dravyaḥ" iti | anyasmin nāśritaṃ dravyaṃ yasya asāv ananyāśritadravyaḥ putro dadyāt | na ced dravyam anyena gṛhītam ity arthaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> adravyasyaiva putro dadyāt | ṛṇasya dravyānusāritvād ity etat prāg eva jñāpitam | kim idaṃ punar ananyāśritadravya iti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span> | prāg apy etat padānusārād evaṃ vyākhyātam | atideśād abhyuccaya eva | atha vā bahuputrasya yady ekaḥ pitṛdhanam itarānumato gṛhṇīyāt, tadā dhanagrāhiṇa itareṣāṃ ca tulyam ṛṇabhāktvaṃ, yato 'nyair api svecchayā svāṃśotsaṃkalanaṃ kṛtam itīmām āśaṅkāṃ nirasyati: "putro 'nanyāśritadravyaḥ" iti | yenaiva putreṇa dravyam āśritaṃ, sa eva dadyāt | nānyo 'numantāpīty arthaḥ | ata eva ca jñāyate bhāgaśaḥ putrā ṛṇaṃ dadyur iti | jyeṣṭho vā bhūyo dadyād, rikthavibhāge viśeṣadarśanād ity eṣā dik | sarvathā dhanaprāptisaṃbandhānusāreṇaiva hy ṛṇasaṃgatiḥ | tathaivāputrasyāpy anye rikthabhāja evarṇabhājaḥ, ṛṇabhāktvam api pratipadyanta ity abhiprāyaḥ | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

                    	rikthahartrā ṛṇaṃ deyaṃ tadabhāve ca yoṣitaḥ |

                    	putraiś ca tadabhāve 'nyai rikthabhāgbhir yathākramam || iti | (KSm 562)

bṛhaspatiś ca: "

                    	dhanastrīhāriputrāṇāṃ pūrvābhāve yathottaram |

                    	ādhamarṇyaṃ tadabhāve kramaśo 'nyeṣām rikthabhājām || iti | (BṛSm 10.106–7)

yad vā, ananyāśritadravya ity asyānyo 'rthaḥ: pitari mṛte yasya paitṛkaṃ rikthaṃ kenāpi parinikṣiptādihetunānyasminn āśritam so 'nyāśritadravyaḥ na tadaprāpyaiva paitṛkam ṛṇaṃ dadyād ity atraiva hetuḥ | "putrahīnasya rikthinaḥ" | anye 'pi tu bhavantīti seṣaḥ | yāvad asau nyāyyam api paitṛkaṃ rikthaṃ nāpnuyāt, tāvad ṛṇaṃ kim iti dadyād ity abhiprāyaḥ | sarvāṇi caitāni smṛtyantarāt samyag vyākhyātānīty avagantavyam | yathāha kātyāyanaḥ |

                    	yāvan na paitṛkaṃ dravyaṃ vidyamānaṃ labhet sutaḥ|

                    	susamṛddho 'pi dāpyaḥ syāt tāvan naivādhamarṇikaḥ || iti (KSm 563) || 47 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvat paitṛkam ṛṇaṃ deyam | bhrātrādikṛte tu katham | tatrāpi |_

 

                    	**avibhaktaiḥ kuṭumbārthe yad ṛṇaṃ tu kṛtaṃ bhavet |**

**              	dadyus tad rikthinaḥ prete proṣite vā kuṭumbini || 2.48 ||**

 

kuṭumbe bhavaḥ kuṭumbī bhrātrādiḥ | tena kuṭumbanimittaṃ yad ṛṇaṃ kṛtaṃ, tat sarvair eva tasmin prete proṣite vā rikthabhāgbhir avibhaktair deyam | vibhaktānām api rikthabhājāṃ saṃbhavād avibhaktair ity uktam || 48 ||

 

_avibhaktatve 'pi tu |_

 

                    	**na yoṣit patiputrābhyāṃ na putreṇa kṛtaṃ pitā |**

**              	dadyād ṛte kuṭumbārthān na patiḥ strīkṛtaṃ tathā || 2.49 ||**

 

_asyāpavādaḥ |_

 

                    	**gopaśauṇḍikaśailūṣarajakavyādhayoṣitām |**

**              	ṛṇaṃ dadyāt patis tāsāṃ yasmād vṛttis tadāśrayā || 2.50 ||**

 

gopo gopālaḥ | śauṇḍikaḥ kalpālaḥ | śailūṣo naṭaḥ | rajako vastranirṇejakaḥ rañjakaś ca | vyādho lubdhakaḥ | ete strīkṛtam apy ṛṇaṃ dadyuḥ, strīpradhānatvād eteṣām | tathā ca nāradaḥ:

                    	teṣāṃ tatpratyayā vṛttiḥ kuṭumbaṃ ca tadāśrayam | iti | (NSm 1.16)

hetvabhidhānaṃ cānye 'py evaṃprakārā uktā yathā syur iti || 50 ||

 

_puruṣamātrāviśeṣeṇa tu |_

 

                    	**pratipannaṃ striyā deyaṃ patyā vā saha yat kṛtam |**

**              	svayaṃ kṛtam ṛṇaṃ vāpi nānyat strī dātum arhati || 2.51 ||**

 

dampatyor avibhaktadhanatve 'py abhyupetādivyatirekeṇa striyā na deyam ity abhiprāyaḥ | kutaḥ punaḥ strīṇāṃ svātantryeṇarṇaprasaṅgaḥ, kuto vā dānam iti | strīṇām api hi svātantryeṇa dhanaṃ vakṣyati "bhartrā prītena yad dattam" (NSm 1.24) ity atra | svaśarīropabhogārthaṃ strīṇām ṛṇaprasaṅgo 'viruddhaḥ | atraiva strīṇām ṛṇasaṃbandhaḥ || 51 ||

 

_anyatrāpi tu |_

 

                    	**pitari proṣite prete vyasanābhiplute 'pi vā |**

**              	putrapautrair ṛṇaṃ deyaṃ nihnave sākṣibhāvitam || 2.52 ||**

 

pitari mṛte proṣite vā viṃśativarṣāṇi pratīkṣya, vyasanābhibūto vā putrādibhir ṛṇaṃ deyam | apiveti ca prakārārtham | anyasminn apy evaṃprakāre vyādhyādāv asamādheyendriyavaikalye hetāv utpanna ity arthaḥ | tathā nihnave yadi ca pitā vipratipannas tadā sākṣibhāvitaṃ putrādibhir evarṇaṃ deyam | so 'pi hi prakṛtiviparyayād asāmarthyenāyogya eva | ṛṇavac cāsv avasthāsu paitṛkaṃ riktham api putrādibhir grāhyam ity avagantavyam || 52 ||

 

_asyāpavādaḥ|_
