                    	**surākāmadyūtakṛtaṃ daṇḍaśulkāvaśiṣṭakam |**

**              	vṛthādānaṃ tathaiveha putro dadyān na paitṛkam || 2.53 ||**

 

svasthapitṛkṛtam asvasthe tasmin rikthabhāgbhir deyam | na punar asvasthakṛtam apīty abhiprāyaḥ | asvāsthyaprakāraprapañcārthaś cāyaṃ ślokaḥ | daṇḍaśulkāvaśiṣṭakaṃ tu vacanād adeyam | surāṃ pītvā yan mūlyaṃ na dattaṃ, yac ca kāmasaṃyogena strīṇāṃ pratijñātaṃ, dyūtahāritaṃ daṇḍādyavaśiṣṭaṃ vṛthādānaṃ ca tathaiveha yasya phalaṃ nāmutreti niścitaṃ, tat putrādibhir adeyam | śulkaṃ pathi rājabhāvyaṃ dānam | aśāstracoditaṃ vṛthādānam | spaṣṭam anyat || 53 ||

 

_ṛṇasya pratiniryātanaprakāra uktaḥ | ko nu khalu ṛṇagrahītety etan nirūpayitum āha |_

 

                    	**bhrātṝṇām atha dampatyoḥ pituḥ putrasya caiva hi |**

**              	prātibhāvyam ṛṇaṃ sākṣyam avibhakte na tu smṛtam || 2.54 ||**

 

bhrātrādīnām avibhaktānāṃ parasparam ṛṇasākṣyaprātibhāvyāni na vidyate | tenaiva ca vibhaktāvibhaktasaṃśaye sākṣyādibhir nirṇayaḥ | dampativacanaṃ cātra vibhāgāsaṃbhāvād anyeṣām api rikthabhājām avibhaktānāṃ sākṣyādyabhāvapradarśanārtham || 54 ||

 

_kva punar viṣaye prātibhāvyam |_

 

                    	**darśane pratyaye dāne prātibhāvyaṃ vidhīyate |**

**              	ādyau tu vitathe dāpyāv itarasya sutā api || 2.55 ||**

 

apasarpaṇāśaṅkāyāṃ darśanārtham, aviśvāse viśvāsārtham, siddhārthapradānena ca prātibhavyam | vidhīyata iti vicikitsānivṛttyartham | agṛhītaṃ dadato dāpayato vā vicikitsā mā bhūt | tatra darśanapratyayapratibhuvau vitathe visaṃvādite kāryiṇi dāpyau svayaṃ, na tu tatputrāḥ | itarasya tu dānapratibhuvaḥ putrā apīty abhiprāyaḥ | apiśabdo 'nyeṣām api rikthabhājāṃ prāptyarthaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca darśanapratibhūr api pratyayārtha eva | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">naivam</span> | pratyāyitasyāpi nimittāntarād bhavaty evādarśanam | yad vā mṛte kāryiṇi dātṛtvārthaṃ darśanaprātibhāvyavacanaṃ draṣṭavyam | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ: "upasthāpya vipattāv upasthāpyasya punaḥ pratibhūr dāpyaḥ" iti (BṛSm 10.79) | etac cārthārpaṇenopaviśvāsya yatra darśanaprātibhāvyaṃ kriyate, tadviṣayam eva | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

                    	ṛṇiṣv apratikurvatsu pratyaye vā vivādite |

                    	pratibhūs tadṛṇaṃ dadyād anupasthāpayaṃs tathā || iti | (NSm 1.105)

yadopasthānaṃ saṃbhavatīti śeṣaḥ | mṛtasya copasthāpanāsaṃbhavāj jīvadadhikāra iti nāradābhiprāyaḥ | vikalpaprasaṅge viṣayavyavasthoktaiva || 55 ||

 

_pūrvaślokārtham eva spaṣṭayati |_

 

                    	**darśanapratibhūr yatra mṛtaḥ prātyayiko 'pi vā |**

**              	na tatputrā ṛṇaṃ dadyur dadyur dānāya yaḥ sthitaḥ || 2.56 ||**

 

ślokāntarārambhasāmarthyān mṛtavacanāc ca jīvataḥ putraiḥ śaktito 'nveṣaṇaṃ kāryam ity abhiprāyaḥ || 56 ||

 

_ekasyaiva tu yadā kāryiṇaḥ |_

 

                    	**bahavaḥ syur yadi svāṃśair dadyuḥ pratibhuvo dhanam |**

**              	ekacchāyāsthiteṣv eṣu dhanikasya yathāruci || 2.57 ||**

 

bahavaḥ pratibhuvo yadi syur aṃśato dhanaṃ dadyuḥ | ekacchāyāsthiteṣv eṣu dhanikasyecchayā vyastasamastatvena kṛtsnaṃ dhanaṃ dāpayet | ekacchāyākāḥ samānagrāhakatvena pratibhuvaḥ na dravyopabhoktāraḥ | etad eva caiṣv iti sarvanāmnā spaṣṭīkṛtam || 57 ||

 

_dravyānupabhoktṛtvāc ca |_

_ _

                    	**pratibhūr dāpito yatra prakāśaṃ dhanine dhanam |**

**              	dviguṇaṃ pratidātavyam ṛṇikais tasya tad dhanam || 2.58 ||**

 

prakāśavacanād yat pratibhuvo hastanirgataṃ tad eva dviguṇaṃ deyam | na tu dhanikāya yāvad deyam ity abhiprāyaḥ | hiraṇyaviṣayaś cāyaṃ ślokaḥ || 58 ||

 

_paśvādau tu |_

 

                    	**sasantiti strīpaśavyaṃ dhānyaṃ triguṇam eva tu |**

**              	vastraṃ caturguṇaṃ deyaṃ rasaś cāṣṭaguṇas tathā || 2.59 ||**

 

tathāśabdaḥ satkārādyarthaḥ | yasya yāvatī parā vṛddhir uktā, tasya tadvṛddhiyuktaṃ sasatkāraṃ pratibhuve deyam ity arthaḥ || 59 ||

 

_visrambhahetū dvāv ādhipratibhuvau | tathā coktam: "visrambhahetū dvāv atra pratibhūr ādhir eva ca" iti _(NSm 1.103)_ | tayoḥ pratibhūr vyākhyātaḥ | idānīṃ kramaprāptatvād ādhir ucyate |_

 

                    	**ādhiḥ praṇaśyed dviguṇe dhane yadi na mokṣyate |**

**              	kāle kālakṛto naśyet phalabhogyo na naśyati || 2.60 ||**

 

viśvāsārthaṃ hiraṇyādi yad ādhīyate sa ādhiḥ | sa dvividhaḥ gopyaś cāgopyaś ca | tatra gopyaḥ kadācit kālavyavasthayā kriyate "iyatā kālenāmokṣayato mamāyaṃ praṇaṅkṣyati" iti | kadācit tu saṃmugdhaḥ sa praṇaśyed dviguṇe dhane yadi na dīyate itaro 'pi kālavyavasthayā kṛtas tata eva praṇasyatīty ata āha: "phalabhogyo na naśyati" iti | phalaṃ bhujyate yasya sa phalabhogyaḥ ādhiḥ | phalaṃ vṛddhiḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 60 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**gopyādhibhogino vṛddhiḥ sopakāre 'tha bhāvite |**

**              	naṣṭo deyo vinaṣṭo vā daivarājakṛtad ṛte || 2.61 ||**

 

gopyādhibhogino vṛddhiḥ praṇasyed iti śeṣaḥ | "sopakāre 'tha" ity apiśabdārtho 'thaśabdaḥ | sopakāre 'py ādhau vṛddhir na syād ity arthaḥ | vāhadohādiyukto gavādiḥ sopakāraḥ | avikārāśaṅkayā pṛthagvacanam | bhāvita iti bhoktrābhyupagate sākṣibhir vā bhukto 'nenāyam ity evaṃ bhāvite | naṣṭa ādhir vinaṣṭo vā daivikād agnyādyupadravād rājakīyād vā vinā adhamarṇikāya deyaḥ | svarūpahānaṃ vināśaḥ | apahāras tu nāśaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 61 ||

 

_ṛṇikārpitasya |_

 

                    	**ādheḥ svīkaraṇāt siddhī rakṣyamāṇo 'py asāratām |**

**              	yātaś ced anya ādheyo dhanaṃ vā dhanine vahet || 2.62 ||**

 

samarpitasyāpi svīkaraṇenopabhogyatvasiddhiḥ syāt | yatnenāpi tu rakṣyamāṇo 'py asāratāṃ yātaś ced yadi pālyamāno 'py asārībhūtaḥ, tato 'nya ādheyaḥ syāt | yad vā asminn avasare dhanabhāg vā dhanī bhavet[^10] | dhanine vā dhanaṃ sodayaṃ deyam, ādhyantaraṃ vā kāryam ity abhiprāyaḥ || 62 ||

 

_yadā tv ādhir apuṣyamāṇa eva, sa tu bandhakamātratayā kriyate, tadā |_

** **

**              	caritrabandhakakṛtaṃ savṛddhaṃ dāpayed dhanam |**

**              	satyaṃkārakṛtaṃ dravyaṃ dviguṇaṃ pratidāpayet || 2.63 ||**

 

caritrabandhakakṛtaṃ sodayam arthaṃ dāpyaḥ | nādhityāgamātreṇa mocya ity arthaḥ | anyatrāpy evam eva viśvāsavyavahāre satyaṃkārāya ca yad dravyam arpitam, tad visaṃvadatā dviguṇaṃ pratyarpaṇīyam | satyaṃkāriṇas tu visaṃvādatas tad dhānir eva | yathāha kātyāyanaḥ |

                    	satayaṃkāravisaṃvāde dviguṇaṃ pratidāpayet |

                    	akurvatas tu taddhāniḥ satyaṃkāraprayojanam || iti (KSm 541) || 63 ||

 

_yadā tv ṛṇikaḥ sodayaṃ dravyam ādāyopasthitaḥ, tadā |_

 

                    	**upasthitasya moktavya ādhir daṇḍyo 'nyathā bhavet |**

**              	prayojake 'sati dhanaṃ kule nyasyādhim āpnuyāt || 2.64 ||**

 

sodayaṃ dravyam ādāyopasthitasyādhim anutsṛjan prayoktā daṇḍyaḥ syāt | yadā tv asaṃnihito dhanaprayoktā, tadā tasmin prayojake 'sati tatkuṭumbe samarpya dravyam ādhim āpnuyāt niḥsaṃśayaṃ gṛhṇīyād ity arthaḥ | evaṃ dhanikakule dravyaṃ samarpayitvādhir grāhyaḥ || 64 ||

 

                    	**tatkālakṛtamūlyo vā tatra tiṣṭhed avṛddhikaḥ |**

**              	vinā dhāraṇakād vāpi vikrīṇīta sasākṣikam || 2.65 ||**

 

tatkāle kṛtaṃ mūlyaṃ yasya sa tatkālakṛtamūlyaḥ | yadi mūlyād dhrāsaḥ syāt, tadā tatkālakṛtaṃ yan mūlyaṃ, tad dhanikena deyam | ity etayā paribhāṣayā vṛddhiśūnyo dhanikahaste tiṣṭhet | yadā tu dhanaṃ dviguṇībhūtam, ṛṇikaś cāsaṃnihitaḥ, tadā tatkāle śrāvayitvādhiṃ nirvikalpaṃ gṛhṇīyāt | vinaiva dhāraṇakāt sasākṣikaṃ vikrīṇītety arthaḥ || 65 ||

 

_vṛddhyarthaṃ prathamadivasād ārabhya prayoktā bhujyamāne 'pi |_

 

                    	**yadā tu dviguṇībhūtam ṛṇam ādhau tadā khalu |**

**              	mocya ādhis tadutpanne praviṣṭe dviguṇe dhane || 2.66 ||**

 

dhane praviṣṭe saty ādhir mocyaḥ | na tv arvāg eva dviguṇadravyāpradānalakṣaṇo 'sya praṇāśaḥ syād ity abhiprāyaḥ || 66 ||

 

 

**iti ṛṇādānaprakaraṇam |**

** **

**atha upanidhiprakaraṇam |**

 

_ādhyanantaraṃ viśvāsārpitatvasāmānyād upanidhir ucyate |_

 

                    	**bhājanastham anākhyāya haste 'nyasya yad arpyate |**

**              	dravyaṃ tad aupanidhikaṃ**

 

ucyata iti śeṣaḥ |

 

                                            	**pratideyaṃ tathaiva tat || 2.67 ||**

 

kvāpi sthitam anirdiṣṭasvarūpaṃ kasyacit parigrahe evam uktvā yat samarpyate: "tvayedaṃ rakṣaṇīyam" iti | hastaśabdaḥ parigrahārthaḥ | nyasya kṣiptvety arthaḥ | tad aupanidhikasaṃjñakaṃ yathā gṛhītaṃ tathaiva pratyarpaṇīyam ity arthaḥ || 67 ||

 

_yat tu dravyam upanihitam |_

 

                    	**na dāpyo 'pahṛtaṃ tat tu rājadaivikataskaraiḥ |**

**              	doṣaś cen mārgite 'datte dāpyo daṇḍaṃ ca tatsamam || 2.68 ||**

 

rājādyapahṛtam anaparādhī na dāpyaḥ | doṣaś cen mārgite prayācite adatte anarpite taskarāpahārādilakṣaṇo doṣaś ced dāpyo 'pahṛtam, tatsamaṃ ca rājñe dāpyo daṇḍam | ṛjv anyat || 68 ||

 

_svāmyananujñayaivaupanidhikaṃ dravyam |_

 

                    	**ājīvan svecchayā daṇḍyo dāpyas tac cāpi sodayam |**

**              	yācitānvāhitanyāsanikṣepeṣv apy ayaṃ vidhiḥ || 2.69 ||**

 

yācitaṃ kāryārtham āhṛtaṃ parakīyam upaskarādi | anvāhitam ādhyasāmarthye yad anyad arpitam | pratigrahaprasaṅgena vā yad alabdham eva pātrādi upakaraṇatvenāhṛtam | nyāso nirdiṣṭasvarūpaṃ dravyaṃ yad rakṣaṇārthaṃ samarpitam | nikṣepo 'nyahasta eva yad anyasmai deyatvena nikṣiptam | eteṣv api yācitādiṣv ayam evaupanidhiko vidhir draṣṭavyaḥ || 69 ||

 

**iti upanidhiprakaraṇam**

** **

**atha sākṣiprakaraṇam**

 

_sarvatra carṇādānādau vyaktihetavo likhitaṃ sākṣiṇo bhuktiś ceti | tatra bhuktiḥ sthāvarādau | anyatra tu likhitaṃ sākṣiṇaś ca | tathā ca nāradaḥ: "likhitaṃ sākṣiṇaś caiva pramāṇe vyaktikārake" _(NSm 1.103)_ iti sāmānyavivakṣayaivāha | tenārthipratyarthibhyāṃ sākṣibhir likhitena vā svapakṣasiddhiḥ kāryety ukte kiṃlakṣaṇās tu sākṣiṇo lekhyaṃ cety etad vaktavyam | tatra sākṣiṇas tāvad ucyante |_

 

                    	**tapasvino dānaśīlāḥ kulīnāḥ satyavādinaḥ |**

**              	dharmapradhānā ṛjavaḥ putravanto dhanānvitāḥ || 2.70 ||**

**              	tryavarāḥ sākṣiṇo jñeyāḥ pañcayajñakriyāratāḥ |**

**              	yathājāti yathāvarṇaṃ sarve sarvāsu vā punaḥ || 2.71 ||**

tapaḥprabhṛtayo yathopalabdhavāditve hetavaḥ | katham | yo hi niṣkāraṇaḥ paralokasādhanaikapravaṇas tapodānādipravṛtto 'tiśayitetarapuruṣaprajñaḥ, sa katham ivātmano dṛṣṭādṛṣṭaviruddhaṃ vimārgāśrayiṇaḥ parasyārthe 'nṛtaṃ brūyād ity abhiprāyaḥ | tapodānādibhir ye dharmapradhānatayā satyavādinaḥ, ye vā kulīnāḥ svakulakalaṅkabhītyā, ye vā putriṇo dhaninaś ca tadvināśabhītyā, prakṛtyā ṛjavaḥ upalabdhātiriktavacanāśaktyānanyathāvādinaḥ, te tryavarāḥ sākṣiṇo jñeyāḥ | trayo yeṣām avarās te tryavarāḥ, triprabhṛtaya ity arthaḥ | sākṣiṇo jñeyā iti pratyakṣamūlatvābhiprāyam | nipuṇataḥ pratyakṣādibhir lakṣaṇataḥ sākṣiṇo nirūpaṇīyā ity arthaḥ | pañcayajñakriyāratā iti | ānvāhikāśakyaparihārahiṃsāniṣkṛtyarthaṃ hi pañcayajñakriyāvidhānam | tad ye hy aśakyaparihārām api hiṃsām apākartuṃ pravṛttāḥ, te katham iva svābhiprāyeṇānyāyavartijanavad asadvādeṣu pravarterann ity abhiprāyaḥ | evaṃ smṛtyantarāṇy api sākṣiprapañcaviṣayāṇi vyākhyeyāni | yat tu nāradenaikādaśavidhaṃ sākṣyaṃ kṛtākṛtatvabhedenoktam (NSm 1.129), tat sauhṛdān mugdhajanavyutpattyartham | tac ca tasmād evāvagantavyam: "yathājāti" ity | manuṣyastrījātibhedābhiprāyaṃ vā jātivacanam | yathoktaṃ nāradena: "śreṇīṣu śreṇipuruṣāḥ" ityādi (NSm 1.135) | yathāvarṇaṃ ca brāhmaṇādīnāṃ ca sākṣyam | sarve vā sarvāsu jātiṣu jātiśabdābhidheyatvād varṇe 'pi strīliṅgāvirodhaḥ | punaḥśabdo 'vasarāpekṣayā | sākṣyantarābhāve punar vakṣyamāṇakāryāpekṣayā vā sarve sarveṣāṃ, yathā "sarvaḥ saṅgrahaṇe sākṣī" iti (YDh 2.74) || 70–71 ||

 

_uktanyāyavirodhe tu |_

 

                    	**strīvṛddhabālakitavamattonmattābhiśastakāḥ |**

**              	raṅgāvatāripāṣaṇḍikūṭakṛdvikalendriyāḥ || 2.72 ||**

**              	patitāptārthasaṃbandhisahāyariputaskarāḥ |**

**              	sāhasī dṛṣṭadoṣaś ca nirdhūtaś cety asākṣiṇaḥ || 2.73 ||**

 

yeṣāṃ tu dṛṣṭam adṛṣṭaṃ vā yathābhūtārthadarśane dṛṣṭārthābhidhāyitve ca kāraṇaṃ na syād, viparyaye vā syāt, te na sākṣiṇa ity arthaḥ | sarve cābhojyaprakaraṇoktā agnihīnādayaḥ sākṣyānarhā draṣṭavyāḥ | tadupalakṣaṇārthaivātra strī | yathoktam: "avīrāyāś ca yoṣitaḥ" iti (MDh 4.213) | saiva cāpy atrāpy abhipretā | savīrāyās tu tadadhiṣṭhitāyāḥ sākṣyaṃ kvacid asty eva | yathoktaṃ svayambhuvā: "strīṇāṃ sākṣyaṃ striyaḥ kuryuḥ" iti (MDh 8.68) | raṅgāvatārī mallaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat | abhojyānnānāṃ tu sākṣyānadhikāraṃ nyāyasiddham evābhipretya nāradenoktam:

                    	nārthasaṃbandhino nāptā na sahāyā na vairiṇaḥ |

                    	na dṛṣṭadoṣāḥ kartavyā na vyādhyārtā na dūṣitāḥ || (NSm 1.159)

ity uktvā, tataḥ:

                    	dāsanaikṛtikaśrāntavṛddhastrībāladhikkṛtāḥ || iti | (NSm 1.160)

evaṃ sarve 'bhojyānnā anukrāntāḥ | pramāṇāntaramūlaṃ cāsākṣitvaṃ prapañcitam | yathā |

                    	bālo 'jñānād amatyā strī pāpābhyāsāc ca kūṭakṛt |

                    	vibrūyur bāndhavāḥ snehād vairaniryātanād ariḥ || iti | (NSm 1.173)

vacanād api kvacit | yathāha |

                    	śrotriyādyā vacanataḥ stenādyā doṣadarśanāt | iti | (NSm 1.138)

sarvathānayā diśā nyāyāgamābhyāṃ sākṣyam asākṣyaṃ ca prapañcanīyam || 72–73 ||

 

_deśakālādyapekṣayā punaḥ |_

 

                    	**ubhayānumataḥ sākṣī bhavaty eko 'pi dharmavit |**

**              	sarvaḥ saṃgrahaṇe sākṣī daṇḍapāruṣyasāhase || 2.74 ||**

 

arthiprathyarthibhyām anumato 'tiśayaguṇavān eko 'pi sākṣī syāt | apiśabdād dvāv api | sākṣipunarvacanaṃ ca samakṣadarśanād eva saṃgrahaṇādau sākṣyaṃ yathā syāt | aviśeṣābhidhāne 'pi bhūtārthopalambhavacanāśakter bālādayo na syuḥ | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

                    	asākṣiṇo 'pi ye 'troktā dāsanaikṛtikādayaḥ |

                    	kāryagauravam āsādya bhaveyus te 'pi sākṣiṇaḥ ||

                    	sāhaseṣu tu sarveṣu steyasaṃgrahaṇādiṣu |

                    	vāgdaṇḍayoś ca pāruṣye na parīkṣeta sākṣiṇaḥ || (NSm 1.170–171)

ity uktvāha:

                    	eṣām api na bālaḥ syān naiko na strī na kūṭakṛt |

                    	na bāndhavo na cārātiḥ kuryus te sākṣyam anyathā || iti | (NSm 1.172)

ato bālādivarjaṃ dviprabhṛtisākṣyam aviruddham | yad vā naika iti nāyaṃ saṃkhyāniṣedhaḥ, puruṣamātrapratiṣedha evāyam | yathaivaikā strī niṣiddhā "yoṣitaṃ cāvīrām" iti, tathaiva strīrahita ekaḥ pumān anarha iti vyakhyeyam | ataś ca tryavarāṇām eva saṃgrahaṇādau sākṣyam ity avaseyam | nyāyamūlatvād eva cātyartham anumānakuśalatayāyam api nāradīyaḥ pratiṣedho 'tikrāmayitavyaḥ | tathā ca svāyambhuvam |

                    	striyāpy asaṃbhave kāryaṃ bālena sthavireṇa vā |

                    	śiṣyeṇa bandhunā vāpi dāsena bhṛtakena vā || iti | (MDh 8.70)

anumānānusāriṇī ca niścayāvagatis tatraivoktā |

                    	bālavṛddhāturāṇāṃ ca sākṣyeṣu vadatānṛtam |

                    	jānīyād asthirāṃ vācam utsiktamanasāṃ tathā || iti | (MDh 8.71)

evam anyatrāpi vyavahāraprakaraṇe nyāyāgamavivekaḥ prapañcanīyaḥ || 74 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evam api saṅkaṭe sākṣyavyavahāre yadi na kaścit sākṣyaṃ brūyāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | tenaiva cāha |_

 

**              	abruvan hi naraḥ sākṣyam ṛṇaṃ sadaśabandhakam |**

**              	rājñā sarvaṃ pradāpyaḥ ṣaṭcatvāriṃśattame 'hani || 2.75 ||**

 

yady apy arogas tripakṣeṇāpi sākṣyaṃ na brūyāt, tato rājñā sadaśabandhakam ṛṇaṃ pramathya dāpyaḥ | saha daśabandhakena sadaśabandhakam | daśāṃśābhyadhikam ity arthaḥ | ṛṇagrahaṇaṃ sarvavivādopalakṣaṇārtham || 75 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**na bravīti hi yaḥ sākṣyaṃ jānann api narādhamaḥ |**

**              	sa kūṭasākṣiṇāṃ pāpais tulyo daṇḍena caiva hi || 2.76 ||**

 

jānann apīti padaṃ niyogasyāvivakṣāṃ darśayati | tathā ca svayambhūḥ |

                    	yatrānibaddho vīkṣeta śṛṇuyād vāpi kaścana |

                    	pṛṣṭas tatrāpi tad brūyād yathādṛṣṭaṃ yathāśrutam || iti | (MDh 8.76)

yataś cānabhidhāne pratyavāyaḥ, tato jānatā tatkālaniyuktenāpi vaktavyam ity arthaḥ || 76 ||

 

_kūṭasākṣiṇo mithyāvādinaḥ | teṣāṃ yat pāpaṃ, tat prakaraṇāntareṇa darśayati |_

 

                    	**sākṣiṇaḥ śrāvayed vādiprativādisamīpagān |**

**              	ye pātakakṛtāṃ lokā mahāpātakināṃ tathā || 2.77 ||**

**              	agnidānāṃ ca ye lokā ye ca strībālaghātinām |**

**              	tān sarvān samavāpnoti yaḥ sākṣyam anṛtaṃ vadet || 2.78 ||**

 

smṛtyantarān nyāyāc ca prāṅmukhān udaṅmukhān vā prayatān pūrvāhṇe praṇihitaikāgrān arthipratyarthisabhyasamakṣaṃ tathābhūta eva prāḍvivāko 'pi hi "ye pātakakṛtāṃ lokāḥ" iti śrāvayet | spaṣṭam anyat || 77–78 ||

 

_evaṃ śrāvayitvā tatsvarūpāpekṣayā yathārhaṃ pṛcchet | dharmānabhijñas tv evaṃ pratibodhayet |_

 

                    	**yat tvayā sukṛtaṃ kiṃcij janmāntaraśataiḥ kṛtam |**

**              	tat sarvaṃ tasya jānīhi parājayasi yaṃ mṛṣā || 2.79 ||**

 

_evam ukte yathānubhavaṃ vadatām |_

 

                    	**sākṣidvaidhe prabhūtānāṃ sameṣu guṇināṃ tathā |**

**              	guṇidvaidhe tu vacanaṃ grāhyaṃ guṇavattaram || 2.80 ||**

 

_evaṃ ca parīkṣitavacanāḥ |_

 

                    	**yasyāhuḥ sākṣiṇaḥ satyāṃ pratijñāṃ sa jayī bhavet |**

**              	anyathāvādino yasya dhruvas tasya parājayaḥ || 2.81 ||**

 

pratijñām ity aviśeṣavacanāt kṛtsnapratijñātārthasatyatva eva jayo vijñeyaḥ | anyathā tu parājaya eva syāt | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

                    	deśakālavayodravyapramāṇākṛtijātiṣu |

                    	yatra vipratipattiḥ syāt sākṣyaṃ tad api cānyathā || iti | (NSm 1.212)

bahvarthapratijñāyāṃ ca |

                    	nyūnam abhyadhikaṃ cārthaṃ prabrūyur yatra sākṣiṇaḥ |

                    	tad apy anuktaṃ vijñeyam eṣa sākṣyavidhiḥ smṛtaḥ || iti | (NSm 1.213)

ataḥ kṛtsnapratijñātārthasatyatva eva dhruvo (?) jayaḥ, nyāyamūlatvāc ca vyavahārasmṛteḥ || 81 ||

 

                    	**ukte 'pi sākṣibhiḥ sākṣye yady anye guṇavattarāḥ |**

**              	dviguṇā vānyathā brūyuḥ kūṭāḥ syuḥ pūrvasākṣiṇaḥ || 2.82 ||**

 

_evaṃ ca kauṭasākṣye sākṣiṇāṃ vyavahārakartror vā kūṭavyavahārakartṛtve spaṣṭīkṛte nirvikalpaṃ rājñā |_

 

                    	**pṛthak pṛthag daṇḍanīyāḥ kūṭakṛt sākṣiṇas tathā |**

**              	vivādadviguṇaṃ dravyaṃ vivāsyo brāhmaṇo bhavet || 2.83 ||**

 

kūṭavyavahārakartā kūṭakṛd daṇḍyaḥ | ekaikaśaś ca pṛthak pṛthak sākṣī vivādadviguṇaṃ dravyaṃ dāpyaḥ | brāhmaṇas tv adadad daṇḍaṃ samagradhana eva ca rāṣṭrād vivāsyaḥ | tathā ca svāyambhuvam |

                    	na jātu brāhmaṇaṃ hanyāt sarvapāpeṣv avasthitam |

                    	rāṣṭrāt tv enaṃ bahiṣkuryāt samagradhanam akṣatam || iti | (MDh 8.380)

vadhaprasaṅge (daṇḍapradhānena ? daṇḍāpradāne) vā samagradhana eva rāṣṭrād bahiṣkāryaḥ | na tu śārīro nigraho 'nyathā vā brāhmaṇasya kārya ity arthaḥ || 83 ||

 

_uttarasākṣī tu pravatsyatā mumūrṣuṇā vā |_

 

                    	**yaḥ sākṣyaṃ śrāvito 'nyena nihnute tat tamovṛtaḥ |**

**              	sa dāpyo 'ṣṭaguṇaṃ dravyaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ tu vivāsayet || 2.84 ||**

 

ato 'vaśyaṃ vaktavyaṃ sākṣyaṃ satyaṃ ca || 84 ||

 

_asyāpavādaḥ |_

 

                    	**varṇināṃ tu vadho yatra tatra sākṣy anṛtaṃ vadet |**

**              	tatpāvanāya kartavyaś caruḥ sārasvato dvijaiḥ || 2.85 ||**

 

śūdreṇa tu dānādaya ity abhiprāyaḥ | caturṣv api bhavā brāhmaṇādayo varṇinaḥ | teṣāṃ yatra sākṣiṇi satyābhidhātari vadhaḥ syāt, tatra sākṣy anṛtaṃ vaktum arhati | sadoṣam api guṇabhūmnānṛtavacanam abhyupagamyate | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "nānṛtavacane doṣo jīvanaṃ cet adadhīnam" ity uktvāha: "na tu pāpīyaso jīvanam" iti (GDh 13.25–26) | adoṣavacanaṃ cālpadoṣābhiprāyaṃ prāyaścittavidhānasāmarthyād draṣṭavyam | etac ca nyāyaprāptam eva mandabuddhipratibodhanāya | prāyaścittavidhānāc cāvaśyakartavyatātrocyate | anyatrāpi gurulaghutve samīkṣya pāpasyāpy anuṣṭhānaṃ prāyaścittaṃ ca tadapanuttaye kāryaṃ yathā syāt | dharmāntaropayogitvāc caitat kāmakṛtam apy akāmakṛtam eva draṣṭavyam | svāyambhuve tu |

                    	vāgdaivatyaiś ca carubhir yajeraṃs te sarasvatīm |

                    	anṛtasyainasas tasya kurvāṇā niṣkṛtiṃ parām ||

                    	kūśmāṇḍair vāpi juhuyād ghṛtam agnau yathāvidhi |

                    	ud ity ṛcā vā vāruṇyā tṛcenābdaivatena vā || iti | (MDh 10.105–06)

evaṃ prāyaścittacatuṣṭayaṃ yad āmnātam, tat tannirdeśānusārāc chūdrādikrameṇa yathāvarṇaṃ kramaśo draṣṭavyam | śūdrasvarūpāpekṣayā ca caroḥ sakṛd vṛttir āvṛttir yathā syād iti carubhir ity uktam | asmād eva ca prāyaścittānṛtānujñānād rājño naiyogikaṃ vadhyānupekṣaṇam iti gamyate | sākṣiṇas tu prāyaścittopadeśamātrād rājakīyavinayānarhā ity avaseyam || 85 ||

 

**iti sākṣiprakaraṇam |**

** **

**atha likhitaprakaraṇam |**

 

_sākṣyanantaraṃ vyaktipramāṇakatvāviśeṣāl likhitam ucyate |_

 

                    	**yaḥ kaścid artho niṣṇātaḥ svarucyā tu parasparam |**

**              	lekhyaṃ vā sākṣimat kāryaṃ tasmin dhanikapūrvakam || 2.86 ||**

 

yaḥ kaścid ṛṇādhikrayapratigrahavikrayādir artho niṣṇātaḥ pariśuddhasvarūpasaṃkhyāparimāṇavṛddhyavadhyādikaḥ dhanikarṇikādīnāṃ svarucyā parasparam avasthite tasminn avyabhicarārthaṃ lekhyaṃ voktalakṣaṇasākṣiyuktaṃ bhāvisaṃdehāpanodanakṣamaṃ kāryam | tasya cāyaṃ kramaḥ | dhanikapūrvakaṃ syād ṛṇikāpekṣayā ca dhanikasya pūrvatvaṃ na kālādyapekṣayā || 86 ||

 

_tataś cāyaṃ kramaḥ |_

 

                    	**samāmāsatadardhāhovāsajātisagotrakaiḥ |**

**              	sabrahmacārikātmīyapitṛnāmnā ca cihnitam || 2.87 ||**

**              	samāpte 'rthe ṛṇī nāma svahastena niveśayet |**

**              	mataṃ me 'mukaputrasya yad atropari lekhitam || 2.88 ||**

**              	sākṣiṇaś ca svahastena pitṛnāmakapūrvakam |**

**              	atrāham amukaḥ sākṣī likheyur iti te 'samāḥ || 2.89 ||**

 

atrāham amukaḥ sākṣīty evaṃ likheyuḥ | asamāḥ traya ity arthaḥ | anye tu samā iti chedabhrāntyā dvāv ity āhuḥ | tat tu bahucavanavirodhād ayuktam | na ca caturabhiprāyaṃ tad iti yuktam | "lekhye tu paramās trayaḥ" iti vacanāt || 87–89 ||

 

                    	**alipijña ṛṇī yaḥ syāt svamataṃ lekhayet tu saḥ |**

**              	sākṣī vā sākṣiṇānyena sarvasākṣisamīpagaḥ || 2.90 ||**

 

ṛṇī sākṣī vā yo 'lipijñaḥ, sa sarvasākṣisamakṣaṃ lekhakena sākṣiṇā vānyena svamataṃ sākṣyaṃ vā lekhayet || 90 ||

 

_tataḥ |_

 

                    	**ubhayābhyarthitenedaṃ mayā tv amukasūnunā |**

**              	likhitaṃ tv amukeneti lekhakas tv antato likhet || 2.91 ||**

 

antata iti vacanaṃ prāptatvād adhikanivṛttyartham || 91 ||

 

_kiṃ punaḥ svahastāropaṇe prayojanam | ucyate |_

 

                    	**vināpi sākṣibhir lekhyaṃ svahastalikhitaṃ tu yat |**

**              	tat pramāṇaṃ smṛtaṃ sarvaṃ balopadhikṛtād ṛte || 2.92 ||**

 

ṛṇikasaṃpratipattyarthaṃ hi sākṣiṇaḥ | sa cet svahastenāpi saṃpratipadyeta, mandaṃ sākṣiprayojanaṃ manyate | etac copagatādiviṣayaṃ draṣṭavyam || 92 ||

 

_nirvyājapramāṇaśuddhaṃ ca |_

 

                    	**ṛṇaṃ lekhyagataṃ deyaṃ puruṣais tribhir eva tu |**

**              	ādhis tu bhujyate tāvad yāvat tan na pradīyate || 2.93 ||**

 

yad ṛṇaṃ lekhyagataṃ, lekhyārūḍham ity arthaḥ, tad deyaṃ puruṣais tribhir eva kartṛtatputrapaurair ity arthaḥ | tuśabdo vyavacchedārthaḥ | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

                    	kramād avyāhataṃ prāptaṃ putrair yan narṇam uddhṛtam |

                    	dadyuḥ paitāmahaṃ pautrās tac caturthān nivartate || iti | (NSm 1.4)

asyāpavādaḥ: ādhis tu bhujyate, na caturthān nivartate | kim anavadhika eva | na hi | tāvat, yāvat tad deyaṃ na pradīyate || 93 ||

 

_yadā tv ṛṇikadeśād deśāntare lekhyaṃ, pramāṇato vā bhraṣṭaṃ, tadā yaḥ prakāraḥ tam āha |_

 

                    	**deśāntarasthe durlekhye naṣṭonmṛṣṭe hṛte tathā |**

**              	chinne bhinne tathā dagdhe lekhyam anyat tu kārayet || 2.94 ||**

 

rājā, parasparaṃ vā dhanikarṇikāv ity abhiprāyaḥ | lekhyadoṣo yatra pramādāl likhyamāne saṃjātaḥ, tad durlekhyam | unmṛṣṭaṃ bhagnākṣaram | chinnaṃ mūṣikādibhiḥ | bhinnaṃ pāṭitam | tathāśabdaḥ prakārārthaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 94 ||

 

_lekhyasvarūpe ced vyabhicarāśaṅkā, ko 'tra nirṇayahetuḥ | ucyate |_

 

                    	**saṃdigdhārthaviśuddhyarthaṃ svahastalikhitaṃ tu yat |**

**              	yuktiprāptikriyācihnasaṃbandhāgamahetubhiḥ || 2.95 ||**

 

saṃdigdhaś cāsāv arthaś ceti saṃdigdharthaḥ, tadviśuddhir arthaḥ prayojanaṃ yasya lekhyasya tat tathoktam | saṃdigdhārthanirṇaye tad eva pramāṇam ity arthaḥ | tac ca svahastalikhitaṃ yadi syāt, tataḥ śuddham eva | saṃśaye tu yuktyādibhir nirṇayaḥ kāryaḥ | tasmin kāle devadattasya dravyaprayojanam āsīd, yajñadattaś ca tadā svadhanaṃ prayuktavān ityādikā yuktiḥ | samānadeśasthau tadobhāv apy abhūtām iti prāptiḥ | apratārakaś cāsau lekhakaḥ prasiddhaḥ, tadīyā lekhyā iti kriyā | cihnaṃ mudrālipiviśeṣadikam | saṃbandho balopadhyādyabhāvaḥ | āgamo lekhyalakṣaṇayogaḥ | kūṭasākṣitvādyasaṃbhavo hetuḥ | evaṃ yuktyādibhir yat parīkṣitaṃ lekhyaṃ, tat pramāṇam ity avaseyam || 95 ||

 

_evaṃ ca nyāyāgamapariniṣṭhitaprāmāṇyasya |_

 

                    	**lekhyasya pṛṣṭe 'bhilikhet praviṣṭam adhamarṇikāt |**

**              	dhanī vopagataṃ dadyāt svahastaparicihnitam || 2.96 ||**

 

yanmūlyāt kalāntarād vā dadyāt, tat tasyaiva patrasya pṛṣṭhe lekhayet | dhaniko vānyat svahastaparicihnitam ṛṇikāyopagataṃ dadyāt | anyathā dattam apy adattaṃ syāt || 96 ||

 

_niḥśeṣaṃ tu |_

 

                    	**dattvarṇaṃ pāṭayel lekhyaṃ śuddhyai vānyat tu kārayet |**

**              	sākṣimac ca bhaved yat tu dātavyaṃ tat sasākṣikam || 2.97 ||**

 

ṛṇaṃ dattvā lekhyaṃ pāṭayet | śuddhyai śuddhyarthaṃ nirapavādatvāyeti | yad vā anyat tu kārayed anyad eva vā lekhyaṃ kāryam | ṛṇikasyecchayā vikalpaḥ | lekhyavyatirekeṇāpi tu sasākṣikaṃ yad gṛhītaṃ, tat sasākṣikam eva dātavyaṃ pariśodhanīyatvāt | sarvathā lekhyavaty arthe lekhyāntarād viśuddhiḥ, sākṣimati ca sākṣyantarāt | yathaivārtho gṛhītaḥ, tathaiva pratideya ity arthaḥ || 97 ||

 

**iti likhitaprakaraṇam |**

** **

**atha divyaprakaraṇam |**

 

_likhitādyabhāve vā parituṣṭyasāmarthye sati |_

 

                    	**tulāgnyāpo viṣaṃ kośo divyānīha viśuddhaye |**

**              	mahābhiyogeṣv etāni śīrṣakasthe 'bhiyoktari || 2.98 ||**

 

mahābhiyogeṣv iti vadann amahābhiyogeṣu śapathaprāptiṃ darśayati | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

                    	satyaṃ vāhanaśastrāṇi gobījakanakāni ca |

                    	devatāpitṛpādāṃś ca dattāni sukṛtāni ca ||

                    	ity ete śapathāḥ proktā manunā svalpakāraṇe |

                    	pātake tv abhiyoge vā vidhir divyaḥ prakīrtitaḥ || iti | (NSm 20.2, 4)

mahābhiyoge mahāpātakādyabhiyoge | spaṣṭam anyat || 98 ||

 

_kim abhiyoktrāvaśyaṃ śiro vartanīyam | eṣa tāvan nyāyaḥ |_

 

                    	**rucyā vānyataraḥ kuryād itaro vartayec chiraḥ |**

**              	vināpi śīrṣakāt kuryād rājadrohe 'tha pātake || 2.99 ||**

 

icchayaivābhiyojyābhiyoktror anyataro divyaṃ kuryāt | anyataraḥ śiro vartayet | yady abhiyukto 'rtho 'nyathā syāt, tato mamedaṃ dhanaṃ sarvasvaṃ vā yad vedam aṅgaṃ śiro vā gacched ity evam avaṣṭambhena divyakriyāprayoktā śirovartīty ucyate | rājadrohamahāpātakāśaṅkāyāṃ tv aśīrṣakam api syād eva | spaṣṭam anyat || 99 ||

 

_mahāpātakādyāśaṅkābhāve tu |_

 

                    	**nāsahasraparaṃ phālaṃ na tulā na viṣaṃ tathā |**

**              	nṛpārtheṣv abhiyogeṣu vaheyuḥ śucayaḥ sadā || 2.100 ||**

 

paraśabdo 'rthavacanaḥ, yathā brāhmaṇaparam asya dravyam | brāhmaṇārtham ity arthaḥ | sahasrād arvāṅ na phālādīni syuḥ sahasrād arvāg eṣām apravṛttiḥ | nṛpārtheṣu tv alpābhiyogeṣv api vaheyuḥ kuryur ity arthaḥ | "śucayaḥ sadā" iti | ye hi nityaṃ śucayo daivād āśaṅkitāḥ ta eva kuryuḥ |  na tu saṃbhāvitāśucitvā (?) apīty arthaḥ || 100 ||

 

_evaṃ ca sati |_

 

                    	**sahasrārthe tulādīni kośam alpe 'pi kārayet |**

**              	pañcāśad dāpayec chuddham aśuddho daṇḍabhāg bhavet || 2.101 ||**

 

spaṣṭārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 101 ||

 

_kiṃ sadya eva divyakriyā | nety āha | kiṃ tarhi |_

 

                    	**sacelasnātam āhūya sūryodaya upoṣitam |**

**              	kārayet sarvadivyāni nṛpabrāhmaṇasaṃnidhau || 2.102 ||**

** **

nṛpādisaṃnidhivacanaṃ kāryagauravapratipattyartham || 102 ||

 

_na cāviśeṣeṇa sarveṣāṃ sarvadivyāni syuḥ | kiṃ tarhi |_

 

                    	**tulā strībālavṛddhārtapaṅgubrāhmaṇarogiṇām |**

**              	agnir jalaṃ vāśudrasya yavāḥ sapta viṣasya vā || 2.103 ||**

 

stryādigrahaṇaṃ kṣatriyādyartham | "agnir jalaṃ vāśūdrasya" iti | aśūdrasyāgnir jalaṃ vā syāt | vyavasthitavikalpaś cāyam | kṣatriyasyāgnir, vaiśyasya ca jalaṃ, śūdrasya tu yavāḥ sapta viṣasya vā jalaṃ vā agnir vety arthaḥ | yad vā agnir jalaṃ vāśudrasya kṣatriyādijātasyety arthaḥ | tataś ca kṣatriyādīnām agnyādiṣv icchāvikalpaḥ | smṛtyantarāt tu deśakālādivyavasthāprapañcakalpanā || 103 ||

 

_adhikṛtaś ca pāguktaniyamavān kṛtasvastyayanamaṅgalaḥ smṛtyantaroktalakṣaṇatulāṃ pratyupasthitaḥ |_

 

                    	**tulādhāraṇavidvadbhir abhiyuktas tulāśritaḥ |**

**              	pratimānasamībhūto lekhāḥ kṛtvāvatāritaḥ || 2.104 ||**

 

vakṣyamāṇaṃ karma kuryād iti śeṣaḥ | abhiyukto vyavaḥare 'bhiśastaḥ | sa tulām ārūḍhaḥ pratimānasamatvena tulādhāraṇavidvadbhir yadā lakṣitaḥ, tadāsyāsmin pradeśe idam aṅgam ity evṃa cihnārthaṃ lekhāḥ kṛtvāvatāraṇīyaḥ | tulādhāraṇavidvāṃsaḥ svarṇakārādayaḥ | pratimānam aparabhāgasthitaśikhyasthaṃ pāṃsuloṣṭapūrṇaṃ piṭakam | spaṣṭam anyat || 104 ||

 

_avatīrya codaṅmukhaḥ sthitvā |_

 

                    	**tvaṃ tule satyadhāmāsi purā devair vinirmitā |**

**              	tat satyaṃ vada kalyāṇi saṃśayān māṃ vimocaya || 2.105 ||**

**              	yady asmi pāpakṛn mātas tato māṃ tvam adho naya |**

**              	śuddhaś ced gamayordhvaṃ māṃ tulāṃ ity abhimantrayet || 2.106**

 

sa yadi tulita ūrdhvaṃ gacchet, tadā śuddhiḥ | anyathā tu viparyayaḥ | yat tu nāradīye:

                    	tulito yadi vardheta viśuddhaḥ syān na saṃśayaḥ |

                    	samo vā hīyamāno vā na viśuddho bhavet tataḥ || (NSm 20.12)

ity adhogatyā śuddhivacanaṃ, tat taduktābhimantraṇaviṣayaṃ draṣṭavyam || 105–6 ||

 

_taptāyaḥpiṇḍadhāraṇaśāstram |_

 

                    	**karau vimṛditavrīher lakṣayitvā tato nyaset |**

**              	saptāśvatthasya patrāṇi tāvat sūtreṇa veṣṭayet || 2.107 ||**

 

kṛtavrīhivimardanasya taptalohahāriṇo dāhaspaṣṭīkaraṇārthaṃ hastau kṛtavraṇapradeśau lekhākaraṇena ca lakṣayitvā saptāśvatthasya patrāṇy antardhānāya hastayor ādhāya saptakṛtvaḥ sūtreṇa veṣṭayitvā vakṣyamāṇalohapiṇḍārpaṇavipuṇaṃ lohakāraṃ gṛhītataptalohapiṇḍaṃ maṇḍalakasthitasya samīpe prāṅmukhaṃ kuryāt || 107 ||

 

_itaro 'pi prāguktaniyamavān udaṅmukho 'yaḥpiṇḍam īkṣamāṇaḥ kṛtāñjalir brūyāt |_

 

                    	**tvam eva sarabhūtānām antaścarasi pāvaka |**

**              	sākṣivat puṇyapāpebhyo brūhi satyaṃ kave mama || 2.108 ||**

 

_lohakāro 'pi |_

 

                    	**tasyety uktavato lohaṃ pañcāśat palikaṃ samam |**

**              	agnivarṇaṃ nyaset kṣipraṃ hastayor ubhayor api || 2.109 ||**

**              	sa tam ādāya saptaiva maṇḍalāni śanair vrajet |**

**              	ṣoḍaśāṅguikaṃ jñeyaṃ maṇḍalaṃ tāvadantaram || 2.110 ||**

**              	muktāgnir mṛditavrīhir adagdhaḥ śuddhim āpnuyāt |**

**              	antarā patite piṇḍe saṃdehe vā punar haret || 2.111 ||**

 

kṛtalakṣaṇau hastau darśayitvā punaś ca mṛditavrīhir apy alakṣitadāhaḥ parājayavyañjkalalāṭasvedādilakṣaṇahīnaḥ kuhakādiśaṅkāvinirmuktaḥ śuddhim āpnuyāt | dāhasaṃśayāntarāpiṇḍapatanayos tu punas trirātre saptarātre vā smṛtyantarānusārāt karaṇam avaseyam | spaṣṭam anyat || 109–11 ||

 

_prāguktaniyamavān eva nṛpabrāhmaṇādhiṣṭhitam udakaṃ gatvā tataḥ |_

 

                    	**satyena mābhirakṣasva varuṇety abhiśāpya kam |**

**              	nābhidaghnodakasthasya gṛhītvorū jalaṃ viśet || 2.112 ||**

 

"satyena mābhirakṣasya varuṇa" ity evamantenodakam abhimantrya nābhipramāṇodakasthasyātidṛḍhasya balinaḥ puruṣasyorū hastābhyāṃ gṛhītvodakaṃ praviśet | punar jalagrahaṇam ādarārtham || 112 ||

 

_madhyamena ca dhānuṣkeṇa dhanuṣā ca madhamena nimajjataḥ |_

_ _

                 	**samakālam iṣuṃ muktam ānayed yo javī naraḥ |**

**            	gate 'nyasmin nimagnāṅgaṃ paśyec cec chuddhim āpnuyāt || 2.113 ||**

 

animagnasyaiveṣutraye kṣipte madhyameṣusamīpe javiṣṭhaṃ puruṣam āsthāpya majjanasamakālam evodakasamīpād anyo javiṣṭhas tam iṣudeśaṃ pradhāvan gacchet | gate ca tasmin pūrvopasthita iṣum ādāya tathaiva pratyāgato yady udakasthitaṃ magnāṅgam adeśāntarasthaṃ ca paśyet, tataḥ śuddhim āpnuyād iti kṛtavyākhyānam evaitat || 113 ||

 

_prāguktaniyamavān eva śūdrādir nṛpabrāhmaṇasamīpasthaḥ kālavyavasthayā smṛtyantaroktaparimāṇaṃ viṣam ādāyābhimantrayet |_

 

                    	**tvaṃ viṣa brahmaṇaḥ putra satyadharmavyavasthita |**

**              	trāyasvāsmān mābhiśāpāt satyena bhava me 'mṛtam || 2.114 ||**

**              	evam uktvā viṣaṃ śārṅgaṃ bhakṣayed dhimaśailajam |**

**              	yasya vegair vinā jīrṇaṃ śuddhiṃ tasya vinirdiśet || 2.115 ||**

 

evam iti prakārārtham, mantrānadhikṛtasyānabhijñasya vāyam evārthaḥ paryāyavacanair vācyo yathā syāt | śārṅgavacanaṃ mandavīryaviṣanivṛttyartham | haimavacanaṃ kālakūṭādivyudāsārtham | spaṣṭam anyat || 115 ||

 

_prayojanālpatve rucyā vā pūrvoktaniyamavān eva nṛpabrāhmaṇasaṃnidhau gatvā |_

 

                    	**devān ugrān samabhyarcya tatsnānodakam āharet |**

**              	saṃśrāvya pāyayet tasmāj jalāt tu prasṛtitrayam || 2.116 ||**

 

devān ugrān ādityaprabhṛtīn samyag vidhānenābhimukyakaraṇāyārcayitvā tadīyaṃ snānodakam ādāyābhiyukaṃ saṃśrāvya "maivaṃ maṃsthāḥ yathānyodakapānam abhipretavaitṛṣṇyādinimittam" iti | etad dhi mithyāvādinaṃ janmāntaraśatair api dāridryakuṣṭhādyupadravaiḥ pratikurvāṇaṃ durnivāraṃ bhaviṣyati ity evam ālocya satyāvaṣṭambham antareṇa "mā kuru" ity uktvā prasṛtitrayaṃ pāyayet || 116 ||

 

_katham atra vyaktir ity ata āha |_

 

                    	**ā caturdaśamād ahno yasya no rājadaivikam |**

**              	vyasanaṃ jāyate ghoraṃ sa śuddhaḥ syān na saṃśayaḥ || 2.117 ||**

 

tātkālikaṃ lalāṭasvedādi dvisaptarātreṇa vā daivarājakaṃ yady ugraṃ vyasanaṃ notpadyate, tato niḥsaṃśayaṃ śuddhir avaseyā | etac ca sarvadivyaśeṣatayā ślokārtham avaseyam | tātkālikaṃ yadi dāhādi lalāṭasvedādi vā na syāt, yadi caturdaśarātrād arvāg daivarājakavyasanānutpādaḥ, tato niḥsaṃśayaṃ śuddhiḥ, anyathā tu viparyaya ity abhiprāyaḥ | tathā ca svāyaṃbhuvam |

                    	yam iddho na dahaty agnir āpo nonmajjayanti ca |

                    	na cārtim ṛcchati kṣipraṃ sa jñeyaḥ śapathe śuciḥ || iti | (MDh 8.115)

"na cārtim ṛcchati kṣipram" ity etat pūrveṇādāhādinā samuccīyate | caśabdasāmarthyāc ca lalāṭasvedādy api | kuhakādipratibandhenāpy adāhādisaṃbhavaḥ | ato "na cārtim ṛcchati" iti dvitīyavyañjakopādānam aviruddham |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> iyaṃ divyasmṛtir avyaktamūleva lakṣyate, yato na pratyakṣāder ayaṃ viṣayaḥ, divyābhidhānād eva | akāryatvāc ca nāgamasya | na hy anenedaṃ bhavatītyāgamasya viṣayaḥ | kathaṃ tarhi yāgāt svarga iti | svargakāmasya kartavyatopadeśād asādhanatve ca tadvyāghātād yāgādeḥ sādhanatvam avagamya yāgāt svarga ity ucyate | atrāpi tarhi prāyaścittavat saṃśodhanārtho divyopadeśaḥ syāt | satyam | yady anuṣṭhānamātropadeśaḥ syāt | iha tu taptāyaḥpiṇḍenādagdhasyāparaṃ nirdoṣatvajñāpanam uktam | tad apeśalam iva syāt |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | dve hy ete codane | steyādiśaṅkitasya abhyupagacchataḥ prāyaścittarājadaṇḍādiprasaṅgaḥ | anabhyupagame tu dhaṭādyanuṣṭhānam iti | atra cordhvagamanādau saty aduṣṭavyavahāraḥ kārya iti | ataś cārthād idam āpadyeta: ūrdhvagamanād vinā na śuddhir iti | ata evopalabhyavyañjakābhāve 'pi śapathādyanuṣṭhānamātrād evāduṣṭavyavahārasiddhiḥ | tasya tv āmuṣmiko doṣaḥ sthita eva | tathā coktam: " divyānīha viśuddhaye" (YDh 2.98) iti | ihaiva nāmutrety arthaḥ | kuhakādipratibandhe 'pi tarhi śuddhiprasaṅgaḥ | na, pratiṣedhāt | yathāha bṛhaspatiḥ |

                    	trirātraṃ pañcarātraṃ vā puruṣaiḥ svair adhiṣṭhitam |

                    	niruddhaṃ cārayet tatra kuhakāśaṅkayā nṛpaḥ || iti | (BṛSm 8.37)

ataḥ kuhakādirahita evordhvagamanādau śuddhavyavahāraḥ, kuhakādibhāvāśaṅkāyāṃ vā daivarājakavyasanānutpattau | pāramārthi(ke? kyau) tu śuddhyaśuddhī kvopayujyete | ato vedamūlatvam aviruddham | tathā cāmnyāyaś chāndogyaḥ:


    puruṣaṃ somyota hastagṛhītam ānayanty apahārṣīt steyam akārṣīt | paraśum asmai tapateti | sa yadi tasya kartā bhavati tata evātmānam anṛtaṃ kurute | so 'nṛtābhisaṃdho 'nṛtenātmānam antardhāya paraśuṃ taptaṃ pratigṛhṇāti | sa dahyate | atha hanyate | atha yady akartā bhavati tata eva satyam ātmānaṃ kurute | sa satyābhisaṃdhaḥ satyenātmānam antardhāya paraśuṃ taptaṃ pratigṛhṇāti sa na dahyate | atha mucyate | iti | (ChU 6.16.1)

evamādīny anyāny api tulādidivyaprayogamūlāny anviṣyodāharaṇīyāni | atra ca śaṅkitasya paraśugrahaṇenādagdhasya mocanam aduṣṭavyavahārakaraṇaṃ ca vidhīyate | anyat tu dāhādiprāptam anūdyate | ato 'py uktaprakāraṃ vedamūlatvam aviruddham | astu vā śravaṇānusāry eva vaidikatvam | svarūpe 'py evamādau prāmāṇyam upaniṣadvākyānām ivāviruddham eva | yathā caitad evaṃ tathā vakṣyāmaḥ | evaṃ sati vyāsādyuktetihāsadarśanānusareṇādhiṣṭhātṛtvena tulādyantargatalokapālādijagatsākṣībhūtadevatākalpanam apy aviruddham | tathā ca māntravarṇikyo devatāḥ,

                    	tvam eva sarvabhūtānām antas carasi pāvaka | (YDh 2.108)

ity uktāḥ | evaṃ svāyaṃbhuve 'pi ca devatādhiṣṭhānam eva satyadharmānusāri pradarśitam | yathāha |

                    	vatsasya hy abhiśastasya purā bhrātrā yavīyasā |

                    	nāgnir dadāha romāpi satyena jagataḥ spaśaḥ || iti | (MDh 8.116)

spaśaś caraḥ, sākṣīty arthaḥ | atha vā anumānamūltvam evāstu | nirdoṣasya doṣatayā śaṅkitasyāgnir adāhakaḥ abhrakāder iva dāhānupalambhanāt | anādikālikāvyabhicārivyavahārapravṛttyavāptānvayavyatirekaśuddhānumānaṃ vahnyabhāva iva nirdhūmatānumānam apratihatam eva | ato 'py upapannaṃ divyasmṛteḥ samūlatvam ity eṣā dik | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evaṃ sati bhāviny arthe divyāni na syuḥ, dauṣṭyatadabhāvayor asiddhatvāt | ko vānyathāha | kathaṃ tarhi bhāviny arthe kośapānādivyavahāraḥ | satyasaṃkalpaprakaṭīkaraṇamātraṃ tad vyabhicarataḥ śiṣṭavigarhaṇasiddhyartham | saṃkalpitānyathākaraṇāt tv (?) anṛtadoṣaḥ sthita evety alaṃ prasaktyā || 117 ||

 

**iti divyaprakaraṇam |**

** **

**atha dāyavibhāgaprakaraṇam |**

 

_evaṃ prāguktānekaprakārārjitasya dravyasya |_

 

                    	**vibhāgaṃ cet pitā kuryād icchayā vibhajet sutān |**

**              	jyeṣṭhaṃ vā śreṣṭhabhāgena sarve vā syuḥ samāṃśinaḥ || 2.118 ||**

 

yadā hy āśramāntaraṃ prapitsuḥ putrāṇāṃ vā guṇavatāṃ dharmapravṛttisiddhyarthaṃ kautūhalād vā svadravyeṇa putrān vibhajet saṃyojayed ity arthaḥ | tadecchayā yāvad yasmai rocate dātuṃ, tāvad eva tasmai dadyāt, na putrecchayā | na putraiḥ pitā vibhāgaṃ viśeṣaniyamaṃ vā kārayitavya ity arthaḥ | ata eva ca jyeṣṭhaṃ vā śreṣṭhabhāgenaucityād yojayed ūnaṃ vābhyadhikaṃ vā | atha vā sarvān samāṃśinaḥ kuryāt | tatra tathaiva syād, yathaiva pitur iccheti putrāśrayo vidhir anavadyaḥ || 118 ||

 

_snehaguṇādyanapekṣaṃ mādhyasthenaiva |_

 

                    	**yadi dadyāt samān aṃśān kāryāḥ patnyaḥ samāṃśikāḥ |**

**              	na dattaṃ strīdhanaṃ yāsāṃ bhartrā vā śvaśureṇa vā || 2.119 ||**

 

samāṃśadānapakṣe pramītabhartṛkāḥ putrapautrapatnyaḥ svapatnyaś ca bhartṛbhāgārhāḥ kāryāḥ, yāsāṃ bhartrā śvaśureṇa vā svayaṃ vā strīdhanaṃ na dattam | yad vā yāsāṃ strīdhanaṃ na dattaṃ, tāḥ strīdhanasamāṃśikāḥ kāryāḥ | "dvisahasraparo dāyaḥ striyāḥ" iti smṛtyantarāt tāvanmātraṃ prabhūtadhanatve 'pi deyam | svalpe 'pi samāṃśatvenaiva | anye tv anapatyānāṃ niyogābhimukhatvena samāṃśatām āhuḥ | tat tu niyogāsaṃbhavād ayuktam | saṃbhavanniyogānāṃ tu niyogāṃśatvam eva yuktam || 119 ||

 

_pitṛdravyānapekṣasyaiva svakuṭumbabharaṇādau dharmakārye ca |_

 

                    	**śaktasyānīhamānasya kiṃcid dattvā pṛthakkriyā |**

**              	ūnādhikavibhaktānāṃ dharmaḥ pitṛkṛtaḥ smṛtaḥ || 2.120 ||**

 

anīhamānasyāpi kālāntarāvirodhāya yat kiṃcit saṃmānamātraṃ kṛtvā pṛthakkaraṇaṃ kāryam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evam api yady asau brūyāt: "na mayā kṛtsno bhāgaḥ samālabdhaḥ, sa me dīyatām" iti | ato 'sty eva virodhaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nāstīti</span> brūmaḥ | kasmād | yasmād ūnādhikavibhaktānāṃ pitrā putrāṇām iti śeṣaḥ | "dharmaḥ pitṛkṛtaḥ smṛtaḥ" iti | vibhāgadharmaḥ pitrā yaḥ kṛtaḥ, sa eva smṛto vihita ity arthaḥ | tasmād avirodhaḥ || 120 ||

 

_svātantryeṇa tu |_

 

                    	**vibhajeyuḥ sutāḥ pitror ūrdhvaṃ riktham ṛṇaṃ samam |**

**              	mātur duhitaraḥ śeṣam ṛṇāt tābhya ṛte 'nvayaḥ || 2.121 ||**

 

ṛṇam apanīyāvaśiṣṭaṃ vibhajeyuḥ putrāḥ pitror ūrdhvaṃ riktham | sutagrahaṇam aurasapratipattyartham | mātā ca pitā ca pitarau | tayoḥ pitror ūrdhvaṃ mṛtayor ity arthaḥ | pitur ūrdhvaṃ ca paitṛkaṃ mātur ūrdhaṃ ca mātṛkam | rikthābhāve 'py ṛṇam aṃśāṃśato dadyuḥ | ṛṇadāne ca sāmyavacanād vibhāge 'pi sāmyam ity avagamyate | yat tu smṛtyantare,

                    	jyeṣṭhasya viṃśa uddhāraḥ sarvadravyāc ca yad varam | (MDh 9.112)

ityādivibhāgavaiṣamyam avagamyate, tad bhrātṝṇāṃ parasparānumatyā vijñeyam | anye tu guṇāpekṣaṃ vibhāgavaiṣamyavākyānāṃ viṣayaṃ varṇayanti karmārthatā ca tasya manyamānāḥ | tat tu puruṣārthatvād dravyasyāyuktam eveti gamyate | yāni tv agnihotrādyakaraṇe dravyāpaharaṇādivacanāni tāny anyāyavartipuruṣapraśāsanārthāni, na tu dravyasya kratvarthatāpratipādakāni | ato bhrātṝṇām evecchayā vibhāgavaiṣamyam | yat tv anyāyavartinā niraṃśatvaṃ gautamenoktam, tad apy "ekeṣām" (GDh 28.40) iti vacanāt paramatatvenaivānuśāsanamātraprayojanatayā vyākhyeyam ity eṣa dik | yathā ca pituḥ putrāḥ samāṃśato dhanabhāginaḥ, tathaiva mātur duhitaraḥ | kiṃ tu śeṣam ṛṇād vibhajeran | na tv adhanāyā apy ṛṇaṃ dadyuḥ | putrāṇāṃ tu mātṛsaṃbandhaḥ nāty eva | na nāsti | kiṃ tu tābhyo duhitṛbhya ṛte abhāve | anvayaḥ putrā ity arthaḥ | anye tu tābhyo duhitṛbhya ṛte tadīya evānvaya iti varṇayanti | tat tv ayuktam | "na jāmaye tān vo riktham āraik" ity mantravarṇāt | pitṛdhanābhiprāyaṃ tad iti cet, na | "yadī mātaro janayanta vahnim" iti mātṛsaṃbandhavacanāt | yadi mātaraḥ striyaṃ putraṃ ca janayanti | vahnir vahanayogyaḥ putraḥ | tatra putra eva dāyādo na stry apīty arthaḥ | asmād eva ca vahnivacanād udvāhāsamarthasya klībāder dravyābhāvasiddhiḥ | duhitṛsadbhāve 'pi tarhi putrāṇām evāstu | na, "matur duhitaraḥ" iti smṛteḥ, smṛtyantarān mantravarṇānusārāc ca duhitṛsvarūpārthataivety atas tadabhāve putragāmy eveti sthitam || 121 ||

 

_sahasthitānāṃ caikena |_

 

                    	**pitṛdravyāvināśena yad anyat svayam ārjitam |**

**              	maitram audvāhikaṃ caiva dāyādānāṃ na tad bhavet || 2.122 ||**

 

pitṛdhanānupaghātena yad anyad ārjitaṃ tathā maitram audvāhikaṃ ca, tad ārjitur eva, na dāyādāntarāṇām api syāt | mitrād avāptaṃ maitram | vivāhe labdham audvāhikam | pitṛdravyopaghātenāpi maitrādy avibhājyam eva, ārambhasāmarthyāt | anye tu maitrādikam eva pitṛdhanānupaghātārjitam avibhājyam icchanti, sāmānyaviśeṣopasaṃhṛtinyāyāt | tat tu sāmānyadravyasādhyatvād vivāhasyāyuktam eva || 122 ||

 

_maitrādivyatirekeṇa tu |_

 

                    	**sāmānyārthasamutthāne vibhāgas tu samaḥ smṛtaḥ |**

**              	anekapitṛkāṇāṃ tu pitṛto bhāgakalpanā || 2.123 ||**

 

sāmānyenārthena samutthānam ārjanaṃ prāptir yasya dravyasya tat tathoktaṃ tasmin sāmānyārthasamutthāne dravye | "vibhāgas tu" iti | avadhāraṇārthas tuśabdaḥ | asty eva vibhāga ity arthaḥ | sa caikasya śarīrādikleśātiśaye saty api sama eva smṛtaḥ vihita ity arthaḥ | kiṃ sarvadāyādānāṃ sama eva vibhāgaḥ | na | bhrātṝṇām eva samaḥ syāt | "anekapitṛkāṇāṃ tu" pitṛvyaputrādīnāṃ pitṛtaḥ pitṛvibhāgād bhāgakalpanā | arthād bhrātṝṇāṃ pūrvaṃ samo vibhāgaḥ | kṛte vibhāge 'nyatamasya putrās tadbhāgam aṃśāṃśato vibhajeyur ity arthaḥ | pitṛdvāraṃ hi pautrāṇāṃ paitāmahadravyabhāktvaṃ na pitṛvat svata evety abhiprāyaḥ || 123 ||

 

_atha kiṃ vibhāgat svatvam, uta svatve sati vibhaga iti | vibhāgāt svatvam ity āhuḥ | anyathā jātaputrasyādhānādiśrutir dravyasādhāraṇyāt svatyāgāsaṃbhavād virudhyate, icchayā vā vibhāgasmṛtir na syāt | na ca tadanujñānād anuṣṭhānam iti yuktam, jātamātrasyānujñānāśakteḥ | ityādyāśaṅkām apākartum āha |_

 

                    	**bhūr yā pitāmahopāttā nibandho dravyam eva vā |**

**              	tatra syāt sadṛśaṃ svāmyaṃ pituḥ putrasya cobhayoḥ || 2.124 ||**

 

bhūr yā pitāmahopāttā nibandho vā akṣayanidhiḥ anyad eva vā dravyaṃ, tatra pitāputrayos tulyaṃ prabhutvaṃ syāt pratyetavyaṃ nirvicikitsam evety arthaḥ | ubhayor ity avibhaktasyaiva svatvajñāpanārtham | bhūmyādeḥ pṛthagupādānam avibhājyatvāt sthāyitvād vā draṣṭavyam | yat tv anuṣṭhānavirodhādi codyam, tat svayam ārjitenāpi tatsiddher na kiṃcit | tadānīm eva vā vibhajyānuṣṭhānam astu | yā tv icchayā vibhāgasmṛtiḥ sā svayamupāttadravyavato draṣṭavyā | ataḥ svatve sati vibhāga iti siddham || 124 ||

 

_yasmāc ca svatve sati vibhāgaḥ, tasmat |_

 

                    	**vibhakte 'pi savarṇāyāḥ putro jāto vibhāgabhāk |**

**              	dṛśyād vā tadvibhāgaḥ syād āyavyayaviśodhitāt || 2.125 ||**

 

anivṛttarajaskāyāṃ mātari vibhajatāṃ vibhāgottarakālaṃ yadi putro jāyeta, tasyāpi dravyasaṃbandho 'sty eva | tasmāt svatve saty eva ity uktam | yadi hi vibhāgena svatvasaṃbandho 'bhaviṣyat, tato vibhaktajasya dravyasaṃbandho nopāpatsyata | asmin punar asty eva tasyāpi dravyasaṃbandhaḥ | ataḥ svatva iti | ato 'yaṃ ślokas tadvivekāyārabhyate: "vibhakte 'pi savarṇāyāḥ putro jāto vibhāgabhāk" | syād iti śeṣaḥ | aviśeṣe 'pi pitryavibhāgabhāg ity avaseyam | yathāha gautamaḥ: "vibhaktajaḥ pitryam" iti (GDh 28.29) | vibhaktajo 'pi ca pitur nirdhanatve bhrātṛdravyād eva dṛśyamānāt tasya vibhaktajasya vibhāgaḥ syāt | ayaṃ tu viśeṣaḥ: āyavyayavivarjitāt | yat svayam ārjitaṃ, sa āyaḥ | yat tasmād dravyam upakṣīṇaṃ, sa vyayaḥ | āyavyayaviśuddhaṃ vibhaktajena saha samaṃ vibhajanīyam ity arthaḥ || 125 ||

 

_etad eva spaṣṭayati |_

 

                    	**kramād abhyāgataṃ dravyaṃ hṛtam abhyuddhareta yaḥ |**

**              	dāyādebhyo na tad dadyād vidyayā labdham eva ca || 2.126 ||**

 

pitrādikramāgataṃ dravyaṃ vibhāgakāle vicchinnabhogaṃ vibhaktaḥ san nitaradāyādānumataḥ svaśaktyā yad abhyuddharet svīkuryāt, sa tad vibhaktajadāyādebhyaḥ punar vibhāgakāle na dadyāt | vidyayā ca yal labdham | caśabdān maitrādikaṃ ca | āyavyayaviśodhitād iti coktam eva || 126 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

**              	pitṛbhyāṃ yasya yad dattaṃ tat tasyaiva dhanaṃ bhavet |**

 

jīvatāṃ vibhaktānāṃ vibhaktajavibhāge tāvad ayaṃ vidhiḥ |

 

                    	**pitur ūrdhvaṃ vibhajatāṃ mātāpy aṃśaṃ samāpnuyāt || 2.127 ||**

 

avidyamānastrīdhanā mātāpi vibhāgaṃ putrasamam āpnuyāt | mātṛśabdaś cāyaṃ pitṛsaṃbandhāviśeṣāt tadbhāryāmātravacano draṣṭavyaḥ || 127 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**asaṃskṛtās tu saṃskāryā bhrātṛbhiḥ pūrvasaṃskṛtaiḥ |**

**              	bhaginyaś ca nijād aṃśād dattvāṃśaṃ tu turīyakam || 2.128 ||**

 

saṃskaraḥ pariṇayanam | tat pūrvasaṃskṛtair asaṃskṛtānāṃ bhrātṝṇāṃ kāryam | tādarthyena vā dravyam apanīyāvasiṣṭaṃ vibhajanīyam | asmād eva ca jñāyate: sādhāraṇadravyād vivāhanirvṛttiḥ | sopakṣayam audvāhikam ārjayitṝṇām eva dravyam iti | ataḥ sādhāraṇād eva bhrātaraḥ saṃskāryā bhaginyaś ca | yadi tv alpaṃ dravyaṃ vā na syāt, tato nijād aṃśāc caturtham aṃśaṃ bhaginyartham apanīyānyat samaṃ vibhajanīyam || 128 ||

 

_evaṃ savarṇānāṃ samo vibhāgaḥ | nānāvarṇās tu |_

 

                    	**catustridvyekabhāgīnā varṇaśo brāhmaṇātmajāḥ |**

**              	kṣatrajās tridvyekabhāgīnā vaiśyajau dvyekabhāginau || 2.129 ||**

 

brāhmaṇasya catasṛṣu brāhmaṇyādiṣu yadā putrāḥ syuḥ, tadā dravyaṃ daśadhā ṣoḍhā tredhā ca vibhajya brāhmaṇādikrameṇa catustridvyekabhāktvaṃ syāt | catvāro brāhmaṇasyāṃśāḥ, kṣatriyasya trayaḥ, vaiśyasya dvau, ekaḥ śūdrasya | evaṃ kṣatriyajātānām | trayaḥ kṣatriyasya, vaiśyasya dvau, ekaḥ śūdrasya | evaṃ vaiśyajātasya | vaiśyasya dvau, ekaḥ śūdrāputrasyeti vyavasthā | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca dvijātīnāṃ śūdrāputro nāsty eva, tadvivāhapratiṣedhāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | smṛtyarthabhrāntyā tu pravṛttāv ayaṃ vibhāgadharma ity abhiprāyaḥ || 129 ||

 

_asamāṃśabhāktve 'pi tu |_

 

                    	**anyonyāpāhṛtaṃ dravyaṃ vibhaktair yatra dṛśyate |**

**              	tat punas te samair aṃśair vibhajerann iti sthitiḥ || 2.130 ||**

 

sthitivacanaṃ nirvicikitsaṃ samavibhāgapratipattyartham || 130 ||

 

_aurasānām ayaṃ vibhāgadharmaḥ | tadabhāve tu |_

 

                    	**aputreṇa parakṣetre niyogotpāditaḥ sutaḥ |**

**              	ubhayor apy asau rikthī piṇḍadātā ca dharmataḥ || 2.131 ||**

 

<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca brāhmaṇasya niyogapratiṣedhād anārambo 'yam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kṣatriyādyarthas tarhi</span> bhaviṣyati | na ca brāhmaṇasya niyogapratiṣedhaḥ, kiṃ tarhi, brāhmaṇyāḥ | tenānyotpādito brāhmaṇasya na syāt | na tu kṣatriyādikāyāṃ brāhmaṇasyānutpādakatvam | ato 'viruddha evāyam aurasābhāve kalpaḥ || 131 ||

 

_kiṃlakṣaṇa aurasaḥ putraḥ | ucyate |_

 

                    	**auraso dharmapatnījas tatsamaḥ putrikāsutaḥ |**

**              	kṣetrajaḥ kṣetrajātas tu sagotreṇetareṇa vā || 2.132 ||**

 

savarṇā brāhmādivivāhasaṃskṛtā dharmapatnī | tasyāṃ svayam utpāditaḥ putra aurasaḥ | tatsamatvavacanaṃ kṣetrajātibhyo 'dhikatvajñāpanārtham | putrikāsvarūpaṃ smṛtyantarād avagantavyam | kṣetrajas tu kṣetre patnyāṃ sagotreṇānyena vā niyogotpāditaḥ || 132 ||

 

_niyogābhāve 'pi |_

 

                    	**gṛhe pracchanna utpanno gūḍhajas tu suto mataḥ |**

**              	kānīnaḥ kanyakājāto mātāmahasuto mataḥ || 2.133 ||**

 

imau tu mātṛjātīyau janakāparijñānād vijñeyau || 133 ||

 

_evam eva ca |_

 

                    	**akṣatāyāṃ kṣatāyāṃ vā jātaḥ paunarbhavaḥ sutaḥ |**

**              	dadyān mātā pitā vā yaṃ sa putro dattako bhavet || 2.134 ||**

 

mṛte bhartary akṣatayonyām anyasaṃskṛtāyāṃ jātaḥ paunarbhavaḥ, kṣatayonyāṃ vā | yathoktam: "anyaiś caritvā tasyaiva kuṭumbam āviśati" iti (cf. VaDh 17.19) | pitṛbhyāṃ pitrā mātrā vā | tadanujñayā datto dattakaḥ | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ: "na tu strī putraṃ dadyāt pratigṛhṇīyād vā, anyatrānujñānād bhartuḥ" iti (VaDh 15.5) | dharmeṇa mātāpitṛbhyāṃ datto dattakaḥ || 134 ||

 

                    	**krītas tu tābhyāṃ vikrītaḥ kṛtrimaḥ syāt svayaṃkṛtaḥ |**

**              	dattātmā tu svayaṃdatto garbhe vinnāḥ sahoḍhajaḥ || 2.135 ||**

 

krītas tu tābhyām adhikṛtābhyāṃ mātāpitṛbhyāṃ mūlyena vikrītaḥ kretuḥ krītākhyaḥ putraḥ | tuśabdo dattakanyāyānukarṣaṇena mātur asvātantryapratipattyarthaḥ | svayam eva tu mātāpitṛvihīnaḥ putratvenāṅgīkṛtaḥ kṛtrimaḥ | dattātmā tv evaṃlakṣaṇa eva svayaṃdattaḥ | svayam eva datta ātmā yena sa tathoktaḥ | ete ca dattakādayaḥ smṛtyantarānusārāt sadṛśā vijñeyāḥ | sahoḍhajas tu garbhe vinnaḥ, garbhasthe yasmin matur udvāhaḥ | sa ca voḍhuḥ putro mātṛjātīyaḥ pratyetavyaḥ || 135 ||

 

_mātāpitṛbhyām eva kathaṃcit |_

 

                    	**utsṛṣṭo gṛhyate yas tu so 'paviddho bhavet sutaḥ |**

 

apaviddhasaṃjñaka ity arthaḥ |

 

                    	**piṇḍado 'ṃśaharaś caiṣāṃ pūrvābhāve paraḥ paraḥ || 2.136 ||**

 

eteṣāṃ kramopadiṣṭānām aurasādīnāṃ putrāṇāṃ pūrvābhāve paraḥ paraḥ piṇḍado 'ṃśaharaś ca pratyetavyaḥ | pūrvasadbhāve tu parasyānṛśaṃsārthaṃ vṛttimātrakalpanam | tathā ca svāyambhuvam |

                    	eka evaurasaḥ putraḥ pitryasya vasunaḥ prabhuḥ |

                    	śeṣāṇām ānṛśaṃsyārthaṃ pradadyāt tu prajīvanam || iti | (MDh 9.163)

aurasavacanaṃ sarvakṣetrajādyupalakṣaṇārtham | ya evaikaḥ putratvād rikthabhāk, sa eva kṛtsnaṃ pitṛdhanaṃ gṛhṇīyāt | itareṣām ānṛśaṃsyārthaṃ prajīvanamātraṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ | yat tu kṣetrajasya saty aurase vibhāgaviśeṣāmnānam:

                    	ṣaṣṭhaṃ tu kṣetrajasyāṃśaṃ pradadyāt paitṛkād dhanāt |

                    	auraso vibhajan dāyaṃ pitryaṃ pañcamam eva vā || (MDh 9.164)

iti, punaś coktam |

                    	aurasakṣetrajau putrau pitṛrikthasya bhāginau |

                    	daśāpare tu kramaśo gotrarikthāṃśabhāginaḥ || (MDh 9.165)

iti, atra kṣetrajaḥ putrikāputra evābhipretaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> asāv aurasatulya eva | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | tenaiva coktaṃ "pitṛrikthasya bhāginau" iti | kathaṃ tarhi "ṣaṣṭhaṃ pañcamam eva vā" iti | janakapitṛdhanābhiprayam evaitat | mātāmahasya hy asāv aurasatulyatvāt kṛtsnāṃśārhaḥ | pituḥ punaḥ parārthenotpāditatvān naṣṭaḥ | tadabhiprāyam eva ca vāsiṣṭhaṃ: "tṛtīyaḥ putrikāputraḥ" iti (VaDh 17.15) | pitrā kṣetratvenaivāpatyotpādanāyānyasmai dīyate, tatas tasyāsau kṣetraja iti śakyate vaktum | janayitur api parārtham utpādakatvāt saṃskṛtatvena kṣetramātratayā strīsaṃbandha iti kṣetrajavyapadeśaḥ | tatraurasāviśiṣṭaṃ pitṛrikthabhāktvaṃ mātāmahābhiprāyam | bhāgavaiṣamyaṃ tu janakābhiprāyam ity avirodhaḥ | pañcamaṣaṣṭhāṃśayos tv aurasasyecchayā vikalpaḥ | anyatrāpy evam eva bhāgavaiṣamyakalpanā | ataḥ sthitaṃ pūrvābhāve parasya dravyasaṃbandha iti | yat punar idaṃ svāyambhuvam:

                    	aurasaḥ kṣetrajaś caiva dattaḥ kṛtrima eva ca |

                    	gūḍhotpanno 'paviddhaś ca dāyādā bāndhavāś ca ṣaṭ ||

                    	kānīnaś ca sahoḍhaś ca krītaḥ paunarbhavas tathā |

                    	svayaṃdattaś ca śaudraś ca ṣaḍ adāyādabāndhavāḥ || (MDh 9.159–160)

iti, asya ko 'rthaḥ | kṣetrajādayaḥ pañca saty aurase 'py aṃśabhājaḥ | kānīnādayas tu pūrvābhāva eva | etena vāsiṣṭhaṃ vyākhyātam | tathā ca śaṅkhaḥ: "dvau bhāgau pituḥ dvāv evaurasasya, trayaḥ kṣetrajaputrikāputrayoḥ, ekaikam itareṣām" iti | trayaḥ kṣetrajaputrikāputrayor ity ekaikasyādhyardhabhāktvam | pitṛvibhāgavacanāc ca jīvaty eva pitary ete saty aurase 'ṃśabhājaḥ | ūrdhvaṃ tv ācāryavacanāt pūrvābhāva evottarādhikāra iti vyavasthā | yat tu kramānyatvavacanaṃ tat pitur evecchāvikalpatayā draṣṭavyam | tadabhāve tv ācāryokta eva krama iti | anayā diśānyāny apy evaṃjātīyakāni vibhāgavākyāni vyākhyeyāni || 136 ||

 

_sarve caite dattakādayaḥ sajātīyā ity etat pradarśayitum āha |_

 

                    	**sajātīyeṣv ayaṃ proktas tanayeṣu mayā vidhiḥ |**

**              	jāto 'pi dāsyāṃ śūdreṇa kāmato 'ṃśaharo bhavet || 2.137 ||**

 

ayaṃ mayā vidhir ukta ity vadan smṛtyantaroktānāṃ viṣayāntare 'rthavattāṃ darśayati | tac ca vyākhyātam eva pitary uparata eveyaṃ dravyasaṃbandhapaurvāparyakalpaneti, jīvati tu smṛtyantaroktayā vibhāgavyavasthayeti | etad eva spaṣṭayati: mṛte pitari vibhāgavyavastheyam asmābhir durnirūpatvān nirūpitā | jīvati tu jāto 'pi dāsyāṃ śūdreṇa pitur icchayāṃśaharo bhaved ity anādaraṃ viśeṣanirūpaṇasya darśayati || 137 ||

 

_icchayaiva ca |_

 

                    	**mṛte pitari kuryus taṃ bhrātaras tv ardhabhāginam |**

**              	abhrātṛko haret sarvaṃ duhitṝṇām sutād ṛte || 2.138 ||**

 

ardhavacanaṃ ca nyūnāṃśapratipattyartham | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ: "kāmataś ca śūdrāvarodhajasya bhrātur aṃśaṃ saṃmānamātraṃ prete pitari dadyuḥ śuśrūṣuś cet" iti (BṛSm 26.83) | atrāpi ca śāstrātilaṅghanena pravṛttasyāyaṃ vidhiḥ dvijātīnām iva śūdrāputraḥ, na tu dāsyām avarodhavidhyanumānam ity anavadyam | abhrātṛkas tu duhitṛtatsutābhāve sarvabhāk syād rājānujñayā bṛhaspativacanād eva: "ananvayinaḥ sarvaṃ rājā haret tadanujñayā vāvarodhaja ity eke" iti | asmād eva ca dauhitrābhāvavacanād dvijātīnām api putrābhāve dauhitrā dhanabhāja iti | ata eva ca mātāmahaśrāddhaniyamopapattiḥ || 138 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvad vaiśeṣikaḥ śūdrasya vidhir uktaḥ | aviśeṣeṇaiva tu |_

 

                    	**patnī duhitaraś caiva pitarau bhrātaras tathā |**

**              	tatsutā gotrajo bandhuḥ śiṣyaḥ sabrahmacāriṇaḥ || 2.139 ||**

**              	eṣām abhāve pūrvasya dhanabhāg uttarottaraḥ |**

**              	svaryātasya hy aputrasya sarvavarṇeṣv ayaṃ vidhiḥ || 2.140 ||**

 

patnīty atra gṛhītagarbhābhipretā | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ: "atha bhrātṝṇāṃ dāyavibhāgaḥ | yāś cānapatyāḥ striyaḥ syus tāsāṃ cā putralābhāt" (VaDh 17.40–41) iti garbhiṇyo rikthārhā iti darśayati | putraśabdaś cāyam anapatyā iti vacanād garbhopalakṣaṇam eva | utpannaṃ vā stry api putrikā yathā syāt | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "strī cānapatyasya" ity uktvāha "bījaṃ vā lipseta" iti (GDh 28.21–22) | anena strīvacanaṃ garbhiṇyartham iti jñāpayati | duhitaraś ca putrikā eva | tathā ca svāyaṃbhuvaṃ putrikābhiprāyeṇaivāha |

                    	yathaivātmā tathā putraḥ putreṇa duhitā samā |

                    	tasyām ātmani tiṣṭhantyāṃ katham anyo dhanaṃ haret || iti | (MDh 9.130)

putrajanmāśaṅkāyāṃ tv apatyābhāve tadadhikāraḥ | bahuvacanaṃ putrikābahutvajñāpanārtham | caśabdaḥ samuccayenāpīcchāto dravyasaṃbandhārthaḥ | evakāraḥ sarvatrāvadhāraṇārthaḥ | mātā ca pitā ca pitarau | sahādhikārāt tu dvandvakaraṇam ekaikaprāptyartham | dvandvanirdeśe 'pi mātur eva prāthamyam | yathāha |

                    	anapatyasya putrasya mātā dāyādyam āpnuyāt |

                    	tasyām api ca vṛttāyāṃ pitur mātā hared dhanam || iti | (MDh 9.217)

sarvathā cāpatyābhāve 'naptya ity ayam evāsya viṣayaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> etad apy asti |

                    	pitā hared aputrasya rikthaṃ bhrātara eva vā | iti | (MDh 9.185)

<span style="text-decoration:underline;">mātary asatyām</span> etad draṣṭavyam | kathaṃ śaṅkhavacanam: "svaryātasya hy aputrasya bhrātṛgāmi dravyam | tadabhāve pitarau hareyātāṃ jyeṣṭhā vā patnī" iti | uktalakṣaṇapatnīduhitrabhāve sodaryabhrātrabhiprāyaṃ tat | yadi ca pitur anyā patnī syāt, tadabhāve tu pitarau, tatra pitā hared aputrasyeti vacanāt pitaiva vā pūrvo 'stu | tadanumate tu tatpatnī, ananumate tu jyeṣṭhā vā patnīti | jyeṣṭhāśabdaḥ savarṇārthaḥ | sarvā vā vāśabdād yadi savarṇāḥ syuḥ | etenaitad api vyākhyātam:

                    	bhrātṝṇām aprajaḥ preyāt kaścic cet pravrajeta vā |

                    	vibhajeran dhanaṃ tasya bhrātaraḥ strīdhanaṃ vinā || iti | (NSm 13.24)

kṣatriyādiṣu putrāṇāṃ tu pitari mātur abhāve pitur mātā hared dhanam ity asya viṣayaḥ | bhrātaras tatheti tathāśabdaḥ prakārārthaḥ sāpatnādisarvabhrātṛsaṅgrāhakaḥ | tatsutās tadanusāreṇaiva gotrajā api sapiṇḍasamānodakaikapuruṣaikarṣisaṃbandhāḥ krameṇa draṣṭavyāḥ | bandhur mātulādiḥ | ācāryo 'py arthād anukto 'pi pitṛsaṃstavād gṛhyate | śiṣya upanītaḥ | sabrahmacāry ekācāryopanītaḥ | eteṣāṃ pūrvābhāve parādhikāra iti | spaṣṭam anyat || 139–40||

 

_evaṃ tāvad varṇāśrayo vibhāgavidhir uktaḥ | adhunāśramāśraya ucyate |_

 

                    	**vānaprathayatibrahmacāriṇāṃ rikthabhāginaḥ |**

**              	krameṇācāryasacchiṣyadharmabhrātrekatīrthinaḥ || 2.141 ||**

 

brahmacārī naiṣṭhiko 'bhipretaḥ | ekācāryasaṃbaddho dharmabhrātā | ekāśramasaṃbaddha ekatīrthī | spaṣṭam anyat | naiṣṭhikavanasthayativyatiriktānāṃ tu varṇānāṃ pāriśeṣyāt prāgukto vibhāgavidhiḥ || 141 ||

 

                    	**saṃsṛṣṭinas tu saṃsṛṣṭī sodarasya ca sodaraḥ |**

**              	dadyāc cāpaharec cāṃśaṃ jātasya ca mṛtasya ca || 2.142 ||**

 

vibhaktaḥ san nimittāntarād yaḥ pitrā bhrātrā vā sahārthaṃ saṃsṛjya vasati, sa saṃsṛṣṭī | tatra yady evaṃ sahavasatāṃ pitāputrāṇāṃ pituḥ putro jāyeta, tasyāpy aṃśo deyaḥ | mṛtasya ca hartavyaḥ | sodarasya ca sodara ity etat tu mātṛto vibhagapakṣe draṣṭavyaṃ, nirdhane ca pitari vibhaktajaviṣayam | yat tu gautamīyam: "atha saṃsṛṣṭivibhāgaḥ | pretānāṃ jyeṣṭhasya" iti (GDh 28.27) | atra jyeṣṭhaḥ pitaivocyate | tasya sodaryabhrātrantarābhāve pretānāṃ putrāṇāṃ bhrātrantarāsaṃsṛṣṭānāṃ ca dhanabhāktvam | tad uktam: "pitā hared aputrasya" (MDh 9.185) iti | anye tu jyeṣṭhaśabdaṃ bhrātary āhuḥ | tat punar vicāryam | spaṣṭam anyat || 142 ||

 

_atrāpare pūrvaślokavivaraṇasthānīyam imaṃ ślokaṃ paṭhanti |_

 

                    	**anyodaryasy saṃsṛṣṭī nānyodaryo dhanaṃ haret |**

**              	asaṃsṛṣṭy api cādadyāt sodaro nānyamātṛjaḥ || 2.143 ||**

 

saṃsṛṣṭy apy anyamātṛjaḥ sodarye sati na dhanabhāk | asaṃsṛṣṭy api sodarya eva dhanabhāg ity arthaḥ || 143 ||

 

_ya eva tu dhanabhāk syāt, tenaiva bhrātaras tatsutāś caivaṃrūpāḥ |_

 

                    	**patitas tatsutaḥ klībaḥ paṅgur unmattako jaḍaḥ |**

**              	andho 'cikitsyarogī ca bhartavyās tu niraṃśakāḥ || 2.144 ||**

 

tatsutaḥ patitotpanna eva | unmatto grahagṛhītaḥ | jaḍaḥ sarvadā prajñāhīnaḥ | kuṣṭhādyasamādheyapāparogagrasto 'cikitsyarogī | caśabdaḥ smṛtyantaroktabadhirādiprāptyarthaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat | paṅgvādivacanāny agnihotrādyanadhikṛtānāṃ sarveṣām upalakṣaṇārthānīti kecit | tad asat puruṣārthatvād dravyasya, avaidyasya cānadhikṛtasyaiva dravyārhatvadarśanāt | yathāha gautamaḥ: "svayam ārjitam avaidyebhyo vaidyaḥ kāmaṃ na dadyāt" iti | "avaidyā samaṃ vibhajeran" iti ca (GDh 28.30–31) | ataḥ pratiṣedhād evaiṣām anaṃśatvaṃ, na tv anadhikṛtatvāt | janmāntarīyamahāpātakaliṅgayogād vā niraṃśatvam | pitāmahadravyasaṃbandhas tv apatitānām andhādīnām asty eveti saṃpradāyaḥ | sāmarthyenaiva tu bharaṇamātrātiriktadravyaviniyogāśakter aucityānuvādo 'yam ity avaseyam | tathā ca svāyaṃbhuvam |

                    	yeṣāṃ jyeṣṭhaḥ kaniṣṭho vā hīyetāṃśapradānataḥ |

                    	mriyetānyataro vāpi tasya bhāgo na lupyate || iti | (MDh 9.211)

anena prāptasyāṃśasya viniyogāśaktāv aucityaprāptam apahāraṃ darśayati | ata eva ca "tasya bhāgo na lupyate" iti | evaṃ ca svayam evaite niraṃśakāḥ || 144 ||

 

                    	**aurasakṣetrajās tv eṣāṃ nirdoṣā bhāgahāriṇaḥ |**

**              	sutāś caiṣāṃ prabhartavyā yāvad vai bhartṛsātkṛtāḥ || 2.145 ||**

 

aurasakṣetrajādayas tu putrāḥ paṅgvādīnām api nirdoṣāḥ santo bhāgahāriṇa eva | klībasyāpi kṣetrajādayo bhavanty eva | sutāś caiṣāṃ prabhartavyāḥ duhitaraś ca putrikāḥ paṅgvādīnāṃ tadrikthagrāhibhiḥ prakarṣeṇa grāsācchādanādinā bhartavyāḥ, yāvad ucitabhartṛbhiḥ saṃyojitāḥ, taiś ca gṛhādhipatyena satkṛtāḥ || 145 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**aputrā yoṣitaś caiṣāṃ bhartavyāḥ sādhuvṛttayaḥ |**

**              	nirvāsyā vyabhicāriṇyaḥ pratikūlās tathaiva ca || 2.146 ||**

 

avyabhicāriṇyo 'pi strīdhanādyavaṣṭambhena pratikūlāḥ svātantryavṛttayas tathaiva nirvāsyāḥ | caśabdāt strīdhanocitā evety abhiprāyaḥ || 146 ||

 

_kiṃ punaḥ strīdhanam | ucyate |_

 

                    	**pitṛmātṛsutabhrātṛdattam adhyagnyupāgatam |**

**              	ādhivedanikaṃ caiva strīdhanaṃ parikīrtitam || 2.147 ||**

 

adhyagnyupāgataṃ vivāhakāle labdham | ādhivedanikam adhivinnāyai patnyai prattam | adhivedanārthaṃ vā | caśabdāt smṛtyantroktam alaṅkārādi | etat strīdhanam ity avaseyam || 147 ||

 

_atra pravibhāgaḥ |_

 

                    	**bandhudattaṃ tathā śulkam anvādheyakam eva ca |**

**              	aprajāyām atītāyāṃ bāndhavās tad avāpnuyuḥ || 2.148 ||**

 

pitrādidattaṃ bandhudattam | ādhivedanikādi śulkam | anvādheyam anvayabhogyatayā dattam | etac cānapatyāyāṃ mṛtāyāṃ bāndhavāḥ sodaryabhrātaro gṛhṇīyuḥ | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "bhaginīśulkaṃ sodaryāṇām ūrdhvaṃ mātuḥ" iti (GDh 28.25) | asmāc cordhvam eva mātur ayam ācāryoktakalpaḥ || 148 ||

 

_śulkādivyatirekeṇa tu |_

 

                    	**aprajastrīdhanaṃ bhartur brāhmādiṣu caturṣv api |**

**              	duhitṝṇāṃ prasūtā cec cheṣeṣu pitṛgāmi tat || 2.149 ||**

 

brāhmādivivāhacatuṣṭaye yat strīdhanaṃ tad aprasūtāyāṃ bhartuḥ | prasūtā ced duhitṝṇām eva || 149 ||

 

_āsurādivivāhaprasaṅgād idam ucyate | bhartṛto dhanam ādāya tataḥ |_

 

                    	**dattvā kanyāṃ haran daṇḍyo vyayaṃ dāpyaś ca sodayam |**

**              	mṛtāyāṃ dattam ādadyāt pariśodhyobhayavyayam || 2.150 ||**

 

kanyāṃ dattvā haran rājñā daṇḍyaḥ | bhartre ca savṛddhikaṃ vyayaṃ dāpyaḥ | mṛtāyāṃ tu bhartrā yad dattaṃ tat pratyādadyāt | ātmanimittaṃ pitṛkṛtaṃ copakṣayaṃ pariśodhya || 150 ||

 

_evaṃ prāsaṅgikam uktvā prakṛtam evāha |_

 

                    	**durbhikṣe dharmakārye ca vyādhau saṃpratirodhake |**

**              	gṛhītaṃ strīdhanaṃ bhartā na striyai dātum arhati || 2.151 ||**

 

bhartṛvacanād anyo bhrātrādir durbhikṣādigṛhītam api dadyād iti gamyate | saṃpraty evādattvā mā yāsyatīty evaṃ rodhāddharaṇaṃ saṃpratirodhakam | nagaroparodha ity anye | spaṣṭam anyat || 151 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**adhivinnastriyai dadyād ādhivedanikaṃ samam |**

**              	na dattaṃ strīdhanaṃ yasyā datte tv ardhaṃ prakīrtitam || 2.152 ||**

 

yasyā upari pariṇītaṃ tasyai yat pariṇayane dravyaṃ gataṃ tatsamaṃ deyaṃ, yadi pūrvaṃ strīdhanaṃ na dattam | atha tu dattaṃ, tato 'rdhaṃ deyam | etac cādhivedananimittam antareṇādhivinnāyāṃ draṣṭavyam || 152 ||

 

_evam ayaṃ rikthavibhāgo nirūpitaḥ | yadi tu kaścid avibhakto 'ham ity evaṃ vibhāganihnavaṃ kuryāt, tatra katham ity apekṣita āha |_

 

                    	**vibhāganihnave jñātibandhusākṣyabhilekhitaiḥ |**

**              	vibhāgabhāvanādeyagṛhakṣetrakayautakaiḥ || 2.153 ||**

 

vibhāganihnave jñātyādibhir vibhāgabhāvanā kāryā | jñātir mātulādiḥ | bandhuḥ pitṛvyaputrādiḥ | ete hi prāyaśo vibhāgamadhyapātinaḥ saṃnihitāś ca bhavanti | anye vā sākṣiṇaḥ | lekhyaṃ vā yad vibhāgaprajñāpakaṃ kṛtam | yathāha bṛhaspatiḥ |

                    	kāryam ucchrāvaṇālekhyaṃ vibhaktair bhrātṛbhir mithaḥ |

                    	sākṣiṇo vāvirodhārthaṃ vibhajadbhir aninditāḥ || iti || (BṛSm 26.148)

anyatra vā sakṣyam anyo'nyam upalabhyamānaṃ vibhāgacihnam abhilikhitaṃ vā pratigrahavyavasthādyartham | tathā "ādeyagṛhakṣetrakayautakaiḥ" | ādeyaṃ dānagrahaṇam | gṛhakṣetrakayautakaṃ pṛthak kṣetragṛhādiparigraheṇāvasthitiḥ | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

                    	sākṣitvaṃ prātibhāvyaṃ ca dānaṃ grahaṇam eva ca |

                    	vibhaktā bhrātaraḥ kuryur nāvibhaktāḥ kathaṃcana || iti (NSm 13.39) || 153 ||

 

**iti dāyavibhāgaprakaraṇam |**

** **

**atha sīmāvivādaprakaraṇam |**

 

_kṣetrādīnāṃ pṛthaktvenāvasthitānāṃ saṃdehāpākaraṇam uktam | kṣetrādīnām eva tu sīmāvivāde kathaṃ syād iti | ucyate |_

 

                    	**sīmno vivāde kṣetrasya sāmantāḥ sthavirā gaṇāḥ |**

**              	gopāḥ sīmnaḥ kṛṣāṇo 'nye sarve ca vanagocarāḥ || 2.154 ||**

 

sīmno maryādāyā vivāde saṃśaye | vivādībhūtakṣetrasya sāmantāḥ sarvataḥ samīpakṣetriṇaḥ sthavirā gaṇāś ca samūhāni cāturvaidyādīni, teṣām api hi sīmājñātṛtvāt | yathāha bṛhaspatiḥ: "rājā kṣetraṃ dattvā cāturvaidyavaṇigvārikasarvagrāmīṇatanmahattarasvāmipuruṣādhiṣṭhitaṃ paricchindyāt | śāsanaṃ vā kuryāt" iti (BṛSm 19.5) | ato gaṇāḥ sīmāvivāde pramāṇam | kiṃ ca gopāḥ gopagrahaṇaṃ sarvapaśupālopalakṣaṇārtham | tathānye sīmnaḥ kṛṣāṇaḥ vṛddhahālikāḥ | sarve ca vanagocarāḥ vyādhaśākunikādayaḥ || 154 ||

 

_nṛpabrāhmaṇādhiṣṭhitāś ca |_

 

                    	**nayeyur etaiḥ sīmāntaṃ sthalāṅgāratuṣadrumaiḥ |**

**              	setuvalmīkanimnāsthicaityādyair upalakṣitam || 2.155 ||**

 

tuṣāṅgārādīni pracchannacihnāni | nimnasthaladrumādīni prakāśāni | etaiḥ sīmāntaṃ praṇayeyuḥ prakarṣeṇedaṃ sīmāntaṃ cihnaiḥ saṃpādayeyuḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 155 ||

 

                    	**sāmantā vā samagrāmāś catvāro 'ṣṭau daśātha vā |**

**              	raktasragvasanāḥ sīmāṃ nayeyuḥ kṣitidhāriṇaḥ || 2.156 ||**

 

samā apakṣapatitāḥ | samāś ca te grāmāś ca samagrāmāḥ | vāśabdaś caśabdārthe | pūrvoktāḥ kṣetrasāmantādayaḥ samagrāmāḥ sāmantāś ca | eṣāṃ madhye catvāro 'ṣṭau, atha vā daśa | atha veti smṛtyantaroktakalpārthaḥ | trayo dvāv eko veti | te ca raktasragvasanāḥ kṣitidhāriṇo bhūtvā nayeyuḥ | raktakaravīrādipuṣpamālinaḥ raktavāsasaś ca | kṣitiṃ mṛdaṃ mūrdhni kuryuḥ | aviśeṣābhidhāne 'pi caitad dvijātīnām eva | śūdrāṇāṃ tu yathāha bṛhaspatiḥ: "yadi śūdro netā syāt taṃ klaibyenālaṃkāreṇālaṃkṛtya śavabhasmanā mukhaṃ vilipyāgneyasya paśoḥ śoṇitenorasi pañcāṅgulāni kṛtvā grīvāyām antrāṇi pratimucya savyena pāṇinā sīmāloṣṭaṃ mūrdhni dhārayet" iti (BṛSm 19.6) | atra cāgneyaḥ paśuś chāgaḥ | raktakarpaṭavasanādiḥ klaibyo 'laṃkāraḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 156 ||

 

_ete ca sīmāpraṇetāraḥ |_

 

                    	**anṛte tu pṛthag daṇḍyā rājñā madhyamasāhasam |**

**              	abhāve jñānacihnānāṃ rājā sīmnaḥ pravartitā || 2.157 ||**

 

tuśabdo niścayārthaḥ | uktacihnavyabhicārāc cihnāntaradarśanād vā spaṣṭīkṛte 'nṛtavāditve rājñā madhyamasāhasaṃ pañcakārṣāpaṇaśatāny ekaikaśo daṇḍyāḥ | rājavacanaṃ tatsamakṣaṃ sīmānayaṃ yathā syāt | yadā pracchannaprakāśāni jñānacihnani na syuḥ, tadā rājā pravartitā yadṛcchayā sīmākāraka ity arthaḥ || 157 ||

 

_yo 'yaṃ kṣetrasīmāvidhir uktaḥ |_

 

                    	**ārāmāyatanagrāmanipānodyānaveśmasu |**

**              	eṣa eva vidhir jñeyo varṣāmbuprahaveṣu ca || 2.158 ||**

 

_uktamaryādakṣetrādīnāṃ ca |_

 

                    	**maryādāyāḥ prabhede ca kṣetrasya haraṇe tathā |**

**              	sīmātikramaṇe daṇḍo hy adhamottamamadhyamāḥ || 2.159 ||**

 

sāhasadaṇḍā iti śeṣaḥ | maryādābhede prathamasāhasaḥ sārdhadviśatam | kṣetraharaṇe tūttamasāhasaḥ sāśītiḥ paṇasāhasraḥ | sīmātikramaṇe madhyamaḥ || 159 ||

 

_sarvathā ca parakṣetrādyanapaharaṇaprāptāv āha |_

 

                    	**na nīṣedhyo 'lpabādhas tu setuḥ kalyāṇakārakaḥ |**

**              	parabhūmiṃ haret kūpaḥ svalpakṣetro bahūdakaḥ || 2.160 ||**

 

khāta udakapravāhasya pravṛttasya mārgāntarapravartanaṃ setuḥ | kulyety arthaḥ | kṣetramadhyena kṣetrāntaraprasecanāyānīyamāno yady alpopaghātaḥ kṛtsnasya niṣpattibāhulyāc ca kalyāṇakārakaḥ | tataḥ kṣetrasvāminā na nivāraṇīyaḥ | tathā caitad ā gopālaṃ prasiddham eva: "parabhūmiṃ haret kūpaḥ svalpakṣetro bahūdakaḥ" iti | svalpakṣetramadyena kṣetrāntaraprasecanārthaṃ nīyamānābhiḥ kulyābhiḥ parakīyām bhūmiṃ "haret kūpaḥ" iti | ataḥ pravādād idam avagacchāmaḥ setur na pratiṣedhya it | yad vāsyānyo 'rthaḥ | yasya kṣetre svalpadoṣo bahūdakaḥ khanyamānaḥ kūpaḥ syāt, tasyāsau khanyamāno rājopakārakatvena kṣetrasvāmino bhūmiṃ hared iti || 160 ||

 

_evaṃ ca sati kṣetrasvāmyananujñayāpi setupravṛttiprasaktāv āha |_

 

                    	**svāmine yo 'nivedyaiva kṣetre setuṃ prakalpayet |**

**              	utpanne svāmino bhogas tadabhāve mahīpateḥ || 2.161 ||**

 

_yat tu svāminārpitaṃ kṣetraṃ karṣako halāṅkitaṃ kṛtvā krodhādinā na kuryāt, na kārayed vā | tatra katham ity apekṣita āha |_

 

                    	**phālāhatam api kṣetraṃ yo na kuryān na kārayet |**

**              	taṃ pradāpyākṛṣṭaśadaṃ kṣetram anyena kārayet || 2.162 ||**

 

** **

**iti sīmāvivādaprakaraṇam |**

** **

**atha svāmipālavivādaprakaraṇam |**

 

_yadi tu paśupālāparādhāt svāmyaparādhād vā paśavaḥ sasyopaghātaṃ kuryuḥ, tatra katham | tatrāpi hi |_

 

                    	**māṣān aṣṭau tu mahiṣī sasyaghātasya kāriṇī |**

**              	daṇḍanīyā tadardhaṃ tu gaus tadardham ajāvikam || 163 ||**

 

kārṣāpaṇaviṃśatibhāgo māṣaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 163 ||

 

_upahatya prapalāyatām evam | yadi tu tatraivopaviśeyuḥ, tataḥ |_

 

                    	**bhakṣayitvopaviṣṭānāṃ dviguṇo 'vasatāṃ damaḥ |**

**              	samam eṣāṃ vivīte 'pi kharoṣṭraṃ mahiṣīsamam || 2.164 ||**

 

bhakṣayitvopaviṣṭānām avasatāṃ pūrvoktadviguṇo daṇḍaḥ kāryaḥ | vasatāṃ tu caturguṇaḥ smṛtiyantarāt | yac caitat kṣetropaghāte nirūpitaṃ, tad eṣāṃ mahiṣyādīnāṃ vivīte 'pi samam, tathaivety arthaḥ | vivīte ca gopracārakṣetre kharoṣṭraṃ mahiṣīsamam | evaṃ pīḍānusārād dhastyādiṣv api daṇḍakalpanā || 164 ||

 

_rājadaṇḍavac ca |_

** **

**              	yāvat sasyaṃ vinaśyet tāvat kṣetrī phalam labhet |**

**              	pālas tāḍyeta gomī tu pūrvavad daṇḍam arhati || 2.165 ||**

 

_atrāpavādaḥ |_

 

                    	**pathigrāmavivītāntakṣetre doṣo na vidyate |**

**              	akāmataḥ**

 

iti chedaḥ | grāmānte vivītānte vā yat kṣetram, tatra pramādād avatīrṇeṣu mahiṣyādiṣu nāparādhaḥ ||

 

_abhiprāyāvataraṇe tv āha |_

 

                                            	**kāmakāre coravad daṇḍam arhati || 2.166 ||**

 

pālaḥ svāmī vā | yad vobhāv api || 166 ||

 

_uktagrāmasamīpādivyatirekeṇāpi |_

** **

**              	mahokṣotsṛṣṭapaśavaḥ sūtikāgantukī ca gauḥ |**

**              	pālo yeṣāṃ ca te mocyā daivarājapariplutaḥ || 2.167 ||**

 

pālo yeṣāṃ daivarājapariplutaḥ, te mocyā iti vyavahitakalpanā | spaṣṭam anyat || 167 ||

 

_ayaṃ ca svāmipālayor anyonyaniyamaḥ |_

 

                    	**yathārpitān paśūn gopaḥ sāyaṃ pratyarpayet tathā |**

**              	pramādamṛtanaṣṭāṃś ca pradāpyaḥ kṛtavetanaḥ || 2.168 ||**

 

paricchinnavetano dattavetano vā gopaḥ prātar yathārpitān sāyaṃ pratyarpayet | arpaṇavacanāc cāsamarpitapraṇāśe nāparādhaḥ gopavacanaṃ ca paśūn ity upakramāt sarvapaśupālopalakṣaṇārtham | pramādenopekṣayā mṛtāḥ pranaṣṭā vā ye paśavaḥ, te ca pālenaiva deyāḥ || 168 ||

 

_rājany aniveditasya pūrvoktam | āvedane punaḥ |_

 

                    	**pāladoṣavināśe tu pāle daṇḍo vidhīyate |**

**              	ardhatrayodaśapaṇaḥ svāmine dhanam eva ca || 2.169 ||**

 

pāladoṣād atra vināśaḥ saṃvṛtta ity evaṃ rājany āvedite 'rdhatrayodaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ pālasya | svalpāśaṅkāyāṃ ca vidhīyate ity uktam || 169 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**grāmecchayā gopracārabhūmī rājavaśena vā |**

**              	dvijas tṛṇaidhapuṣpāṇi sarvataḥ svavad āharet || 2.170 ||**

 

spaṣṭārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 170 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**dhanuḥśataṃ parīṇāho grāmakṣetrāntaraṃ bhavet |**

**              	dve śate karpaṭasya syān nagarasya catuḥśatam || 2.171 ||**

 

grāmanagarobhayadharmayuktaṃ karpaṭam | spaṣṭam anyat || 171 ||

 

 

**iti svāmipālavivādaprakaraṇam |**

** **

**athāsvāmivikrayaprakaraṇam |**

 

_ukto dravyāṇāṃ svatvasaṃbandhaḥ | idānīm asvāmivikrayaṃ darśayati |_

 

                    	**svaṃ labhetānyavikrītaṃ kretur doṣo 'prakāśite |**

**              	hīnād raho hīnamūlye**

 

anyenāsvāminā vikrītaṃ dravyaṃ dṛṣṭvā svāmī gṛhṇīyāt | kretuś ca doṣaḥ syāt aprakāśite kraye | prakāśakraye tu mūlyamātrapraṇāśaḥ, na tu steyadoṣaḥ | kva tarhi doṣaḥ | hīnād dāsādihastād gṛhṇataḥ | tathā rahaḥ pracchannam | hīnamūlye ca steyasaṃbāvanayā gṛhīte |

 

                                                                    	**velāhīne ca taskaraḥ || 2.172 ||**

 

velāhīne ca taskaraḥ | kretā syād ity arthaḥ | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

                    	dravyam asvāmivikrītaṃ dravyasvāmī samāpnuyāt |

                    	prakāśakrayataḥ śuddhiḥ kretuḥ steyaṃ rahaḥ kṛte ||

                    	asvāmyanumatād dāsād asataś ca janād rahaḥ |

                    	hīnamūlyam avelāyāṃ krīṇaṃs taddoṣabhāg bhavet || iti (NSm 7.2–3) || 172 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**naṣṭāpahṛtam āsādya hartāraṃ grāhayen naram |**

**              	deśakālātipattau vā gṛhītvā svayam arpayet || 2.173 ||**

 

naṣṭaṃ vāpahṛtaṃ vā dravyam anyena gṛhītam āsādyopalabhya dravyagrāhiṇaṃ hartāyam iti vyapadiśya rājapuruṣair vyavahāranirṇayāya grāyayet | yadi tu rājakīyāsaṃnidhānaṃ deśakālātipattiś cāśaṅkyeta, tadā svayam eva gṛhītvā rājñe hartāram arpayet | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> etat svabhāvasiddhatvād evāvācyam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | svātantryeṇa gṛhṇataḥ stenaṃ ca dadato doṣābhāvajñāpanārtham etat | anyā vyākhyā: naṣṭāpahṛtam āsādya krītvā svāminā prārthyamāne hartāraṃ grāhayet | mūlyam arpayed ity arthaḥ | deśakālātipattau vā prakāśakrayeṇāpi gṛhītvā svayam arpayet | tathāpy adoṣa ity abhiprāyaḥ || 173 ||

 

_hartṛtayā ca rājany āveditasya |_

 

                    	**vikretur darśanāc chuddhiḥ svāmī dravyaṃ nṛpo damam |**

**              	kretā mūlyam avāpnoti tasmād yas tatra vikrayī || 2.174 ||**

 

vikretāraṃ darśayitvā kretur nirdoṣatvam | svāminaś ca tadā dravyalābhaḥ | vikrayiṇaś ca hastāt kretur mūlyaprāptiḥ | daṇḍaprāptiś ca rājña ity avaseyam || 174 ||

 

_kathaṃ punaḥ svāmyavagatiḥ | ucyate |_

 

                    	**āgamenopabhogena naṣṭaṃ bhāvyam ato 'nyathā |**

**              	pañcabandho damas tatra rājñas tenāpy abhāvite || 2.175 ||**

 

āgamena lekhyādinā prakāśam askhalitacirabhogena vā naṣṭaṃ dravyam anyahastagataṃ madīyam ity eva bhāvyam | ataḥ prakāradvayād anyathā madīyam iti vadato vivādībhūtadravyāt pañcabandho bhāgo damaḥ syāt | tac ca dravyam itareṇāpi pūrvoktaprakāradvayenātmīyam ity abhāvyaṃ rājagāmy avaseyam || 175 ||

 

_yataś caitad evam, ataḥ |_

 

                    	**hṛtaṃ pranaṣṭaṃ yo dravyaṃ parahastad avāpnuyāt |**

**              	anivedya nṛpe daṇḍyaḥ sa tu ṣaṇṇavatiṃ paṇān || 2.176 ||**

 

spaṣṭārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 176 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**śaulkikaiḥ sthānapālair vā naṣṭāpahṛtam āhṛtam |**

**              	arvāk saṃvatsarāt svāmī labheta parato nṛpaḥ || 2.177 ||**

 

arvāk saṃvatsarāt svāmī gṛhṇīyāt | parato nṛpatir gṛhṇīyāt || 177 ||

 

_pāritoṣikān rājñe |_

 

                    	**paṇān ekaśaphe dadyāc caturaḥ pañca mānuṣe |**

**              	mahiṣoṣṭragavāṃ dvau dvau pādaṃ pādam ajāvike || 2.178 ||**

 

 

**ity asvāmivikrayaprakaraṇam |**

** **

**atha dattāpradānikaprakaraṇam |**

 

_pāritoṣikadānaprasaṅgenādṛṣṭārtho 'pi dānasādhāraṇo vidhir ucyate |_

 

                    	**svakuṭumbāvirodhena deyaṃ dārasutād ṛte |**

**              	nānvaye sati sarvasvaṃ deyaṃ yac cānyasaṃśritam || 2.179 ||**

 

svaśabdo vibhaktaputrādinivṛttyarthaḥ | avirodhaś ca grāsācchādanamātrasaṃpallakṣaṇo vijñeyaḥ | dārasutagrahaṇaṃ ca sarvajñātidharmopanatādilakṣaṇārtham |nānvaye sati sarvasvaṃ pṛthak kuṭumbatayāvasthite 'pīty arthaḥ | deyaṃ yac cety atra deyaṃ pratyarpaṇīyaṃ nikṣepādi | anyasaṃśritaṃ sādhāraṇaṃ parādhīnaṃ vā svam eva | asya pāṭhāntaram "yac ca pratiśrutam" iti | deyatvenānyasmai pratiśrutam ity arthaḥ | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

                    	anvāhitaṃ yācitakam ādhiḥ sādhāraṇaṃ ca yat |

                    	nikṣepaṃ putradāraṃ ca sarvasvaṃ cānvaye sati ||

                    	āpady api ca kaṣṭāyāṃ vartamānena dehinā |

                    	adeyāny āhur ācāryā yac cānyasmai pratiśrutam || iti (NSm 4.4–5) || 179 ||

 

_adeyavyatiriktānāṃ tu deyānāṃ |_

 

                    	**pratigrahaḥ prakāśaḥ syāt sthāvarasya viśeṣataḥ |**

**              	deyaṃ pratiśrutaṃ caivaṃ dattvā nāpaharet punaḥ || 2.180 ||**

 

yat tv aprakāśyaṃ dānam iti, tad dānaviṣayam, idaṃ tu pratigrahaviṣayam ity avirodhaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 180 ||

 

**iti dattāpradānikaprakaraṇam |**

** **

**atha krītānuśayaprakaraṇam |**

 

_asvāmivikrayo nirūpitaḥ | svāmivikrayaṃ ca |_

 

                    	**daśaikapañcasaptāhamāsatryahārdhamāsikam |**

**              	bījāyovāhyaratnastrīdohyapuṃsāṃ parīkṣaṇam || 2.181 ||**

 

parīkṣākālāc cordhvaṃ krītaṃ vikrītaṃ vā syād yat tad anupahatam | yat tu tu svāyaṃbhuvam:

                    	krītvā vikrīya vā dravyaṃ yasyehānuśayo bhavet |

                    	so 'ntardaśāhāt tad dravyaṃ dadyāc copādadīta vā || (MDh 8.222)

iti, tat parīkṣya krīte draṣṭavyam | daśāhādikrameṇa bījādīnāṃ kramaśaḥ parīkṣākālāḥ| daśāho bījānāṃ godhūmādīnām | ekāhaś cāyasaḥ | ayograhaṇaṃ sarvatāmrādilakṣaṇārtham | evaṃ vāhyādiṣv api yojyam | vāhyaṃ balīvardādayaḥ | ratnāni maratakādīni | striyo dāsyādyāḥ | dohyaṃ gavādi | pumāṃso dāsādayaḥ || 181 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**agnau suvarṇam akṣīṇaṃ dvipalaṃ rajate śatam |**

**              	aṣṭau tu trapusīse ca tāmre pañca daśāyasi || 2.182 ||**

 

āvartanāyāgnau kṣiptaṃ suvarṇam akṣīṇaṃ, tāvad evety arthaḥ | rajatādau palaśatād dvipalādikaḥ kṣayaḥ | anena prakāreṇopakṣīṇaṃ suvarṇakārādayo na dāpanīyāḥ || 182 ||

 

_taulikādibhis tu vastranirmāṇāyārpite sūtre |_

 

                    	**śate daśapalā vṛddhir aurṇe kārpāsike tathā |**

**              	madhye pañcapalā hāniḥ sūkṣme tu tripalā matā || 2.183 ||**

 

palaśate daśapalāny aurṇakārpāsikayor vṛddhiḥ sthūle sūtre syāt | madhame tūktavṛddhitaḥ pañcapalahānyā vṛddhir ity arthaḥ | sūkṣme tu tripalā vṛddhiḥ | tathā ca nārado daśapalā vṛddhim uktvāha |

                    	sthūlasūtravatām eṣāṃ madhyānāṃ pañcakaṃ śatam |

                    	tripalaṃ tu susūkṣmāṇām | iti (NSm 9.14) || 183 ||

 

_asya viśeṣe 'pavādaḥ |_

 

                    	**cārmike romabaddhe ca triṃśadbhāgaḥ kṣayo mataḥ |**

**              	na kṣayo na ca vṛddhiḥ syāt kauśeye vālkale tathā || 2.184 ||**

 

carmakṛtaṃ cārmikaṃ kuruṇṭhādi | romabaddhaṃ dūṣyapaṭādi | tatra hi chedanāt triṃśadbhāgaḥ kṣayaḥ | kauśeyavālkalayos tu sāmyam eva | kauśeyaṃ trasarīmayam | spaṣṭam anyat || 184 ||

 

_vṛddhyanusāreṇaiva kṣayam ālocya rajakādibhir vastrādīnām |_

 

                    	**deśaṃ kālaṃ ca bhogaṃ ca jñātvā naṣṭe balābalam |**

**              	dravyāṇāṃ kuśalā brūyur yat tad dāpyam asaṃśayam || 2.185 ||**
