svadeśotpannaṃ paradeśotpannaṃ cirantanam alpakālikaṃ bhuktam abhuktaṃ durlabham adurlabhaṃ vety evaṃ naṣṭe dravye balābalaṃ jñātvā dravyāṇāṃ balābalajñānakuśalā yan mūlyaṃ brūyuḥ, tan nirvicāraṃ nāśayitā dadyāt | rājñā cādadad dāpyaḥ | evaṃ parīṣya krīte kretur vyabhicarato rājadaṇḍādiprasaṅgaḥ | na ca vikretā vyabhicarann api vikrītaṃ prāpnuyād iti sthitam | tathā ca svāyaṃbhuvam |

                    	pareṇa tu daśāhasya na dadyān nāpi dāpayet |

                    	ādadāno dadac caiva daṇḍyo rājñā śatāni ṣaṭ || iti (MDh 8.223) || 185 ||

 

** **

**iti krītānuśayaprakaraṇam |**

** **

**athābhyupetyāśuśrūṣāprakaraṇam |**

 

_asyāpavādārtham āha |_

 

                    	**balād dāsīkṛaś corair vikrītaś cāpi mucyate |**

**              	svāmiprāṇaprado bhāktas tattyāgān niṣkrayād api || 2.186 ||**

 

dāsyakāraṇagṛhajatvādyabhāve balād yo dāsīkṛtaḥ, corair vānyahaste dāsatvena vikrītaḥ, sa moktavyaḥ | nātra kretur doṣaprasaṅgaḥ | yasyāpi hi dāsatvakāraṇam asti, so 'pi hi svāminaṃ prāṇasaṃśayāt svaprāṇatyāganiścayāvaṣṭambhena mokṣayitvā dāsyān mucyate | yas tu bhāktaḥ bhaktadāsaḥ, sa tattyāgān niṣkrayād vā mucyate | apiśabdāt svāmiprasādādiparigrahaḥ || 186 ||

 

_evaṃ dāsyān nirmocanaprāptāv ayam apavādaḥ |_

 

                    	**pravrajyāvasito rājño dāsa āmaraṇāntikam |**

**              	varṇānām ānulomyena dāsyaṃ na pratilomataḥ || 2.187 ||**

 

pravrajya pratinivṛtto rājño dāsaḥ syāt | na cātra svāmiprāṇarakṣaṇenāpi mokṣaḥ | brāhmaṇo 'pi ca pravrajyāvasito rājño dāsaḥ syāt prātilomyenāpi | ato 'nyatra tu varṇānām ānulomyena dāsyam | yathā "mokṣito mahataś carṇāt" (NSm 5.25) ity evamādau na prātilomyena pratyetavyam | smṛtyantarāc ca dāsatvanimittāni gṛhajatvādīni dāsyanirmocanaprakārāś cānveṣyāḥ | sarvathā prātilomyena dāsyābhāva iti sthitam | yatra pāribhāṣikam ubhayor anumate dāsyam anyad vā tat tathaiva kartavyam || 187 ||

 

_yataś caitad evam, ataḥ |_

 

                    	**kṛtaśilpo 'pi nivaset kṛtaṃ kālaṃ guror gṛhe |**

**              	antevāsī guruprāptabhojanas tatphalapradaḥ || 2.188 ||**

 

śilpaśikṣaṇārthaṃ pratipannaśiṣyabhāvo 'ntevāsī | sa yadā paribhāṣya "iyantaṃ kālaṃ tvadgṛhe mayā śilpavidyāśikṣayā vastavyam" ity āste, antarāle 'pi kṛtavidyaḥ syāt, tadāpi hi kṛtaṃ pāribhāṣikaṃ kālaṃ guror gṛhe nivaset | guruṇāpi ca tasya bhojanaparidhānādikaṃ deyam | yac cāsau śilpenārjayet, tad guror evārpayed ity avaseyam || 188 ||

 

 

**ity abhyupetyāśuśrūṣāprakaraṇam |**

** **

**atha saṃvidvyatikramaprakaraṇam** |

 

 

_pāribhāṣikasya cānanyathākaraṇaprasaṅgena bhūyaḥ samayānapākaraṇārthaṃ samūhakriyām upodghātatvenāha |_

 

                    	**rājā kṛtvā pure sthānaṃ brāhmaṇān nyasya tatra tu |**

**              	traividyaṃ vṛttimad brūyāt svadharmaḥ pālyatām iti || 2.189 ||**

 

yad uktam,

                    	tatra durgāṇi kurvīta janakośātmavṛddhaye | (YDh 1.317)

iti, tad guṇavidhānāyaivāyam ārambhaḥ | rājā kṛtvā pure durge sthānaṃ sthalīṃ bhāvikālasaṃrakṣaṇārthaṃ brāhmaṇān nyasya samudāyatenāvasthāpya traividyam ṛgyajuḥsāmapāragaṃ sadācārabrāhmaṇātmakaṃ "vṛttimat kṛtvā brūyāt svadharmaḥ pālyatām iti" | vartanahetur vṛttiḥ, tad yuktaṃ vṛttimad grāmagṛhakṣetrākṣayanidhyādisthāpitam arthaṃ dattvety arthaḥ | svadharmo varṇāśramadharmasthityavyabhicāraḥ, rājñaś cānyathāpravṛttāv upadeśena sanmārgāvatāraṇam | spaṣṭam anyat || 189 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

** **

**              	nijadharmāvirodhena yas tu sāmayiko bhavet |**

**              	so 'pi yatnena saṃrakṣyo dharmo rājakṛtaś ca yaḥ || 2.190 ||**

 

śrutismṛtyukto nijadharmaḥ, tadavirodhenārthādyanuguṇaḥ, tadanuguṇo vā yo 'pi sāmayikaḥ svaparibhāṣākṛto bhaved yathoktamadhyakāhūtānāgamanadaṇḍādikaḥ, so 'pi rajñā prayatnena samyag rakṣaṇīyaḥ | kiṃ ca dharmo rājakṛtaś ca yaḥ yathaiva svaniveśitasthāne tathaiva rājāntarakṛtasthānāntareṣv api brahmaśālāniveśayātrotsavādikaḥ | tathā ca nāradhaḥ |

                    	yo dharmaḥ karma yac caiṣām upasthānavidhiś ca yaḥ |

                    	yac caiṣāṃ vṛttyupādānam anumanyeta tat tathā || iti | (NSm 10.3)

dharmo rājakṛta ity atra punar dharmavacanaṃ na rājāntarakṛtatvāt pālanīyam | kiṃ tarhi dharmānuguṇyena dharmata evety abhiprāyaḥ | tathā ca nāradhaḥ samūhadharmān upasaṃharann āha |

                    	doṣavat karaṇaṃ yat syād anāmnāyaprakalpitam |

                    	pravṛttam api tad rājā śreyaskāmo nivartayet || iti | (NSm 10.7) || 190 ||

 

_pālanavyājena |_

 

                    	**gaṇadrayaṃ hared yas tu saṃvidaṃ laṅghayec ca yaḥ |**

**              	sarvasvaharaṇaṃ kṛtvā taṃ rāṣṭrād vipravāsayet || 2.191 ||**

 

yo gaṇadravyaṃ hared, dharmāvirodhinīṃ saṃvidaṃ paribhāṣāṃ samūhakṛtāṃ (?) laṅghayet, tam apahṛtya sarvasvaṃ rāṣṭrād rājā vipravāsayet | tac cāpahṛtya samūhāyaivārpayet | na tu svayaṃ gṛhṇīyāt | kṛtveti vacanāt kartaiva rājā na grahīteti gamyate | svāyaṃbhuve 'py evamabhiprāyaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ |

                    	na jātu brāhmaṇaṃ hanyāt sarvapāpeṣv avasthitam |

                    	rāṣṭrāt tv enaṃ bahiṣkuryāt samagradhanam akṣatam || iti | (MDh 8.380)

ataḥ samūhārpaṇam anavadyam | evam anyatrāpi samūhārthaṃ daṇḍadānādi yojyam || 191 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ayaṃ bhinnābhiprāyapuruṣādhīnatvāt samūhadharmo duḥśliṣṭa eva | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span> | kāryāpekṣayaikābhiprāyatvopapatteḥ | kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**kartavyaṃ vacanaṃ sarvaiḥ samūhahitavādinaḥ |**

 

samudāyino 'nyasya vā |

 

                    	**yas tatra viparītaḥ syāt sa dāpyaḥ prathamaṃ damam || 2.192 ||**

 

rājñā samūhāyaivety arthaḥ | mahatā hi prayatnena rājñā samūhadharmaḥ pālanīyaḥ, dharmābhivṛddhyā samūhasya rājopakāritvāt || 192 ||

 

_yataś caitd evam, ataḥ |_

 

                    	**samūhakārya āyātān kṛtakāryān visarjayet |**

 

kṣipraṃ kāryāntarāṇi parihāpyāpīti śeṣaḥ |

 

                    	**sa dānamānasatkāraiḥ pūjayitvā mahīpatiḥ || 2.193 ||**

 

<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca parasvatvāpattiparyantatvād dānasya samūhināṃ ca prayekaṃ svatvāyogyatvād vyatiriktasvatvāpattikṣamasamūhalakṣaṇatvābhāvāt samūhadānam anupapannam eva | ata eva ca gaṇadravyaṃ prārthyamāmā vaktāro bhavanti: nedam adyāpy asmadīyaṃ bhavatīti | tathā cartvijām api an pariṣadaṃ pratyutsarga iṣyate | ato 'yam utsargamātre gauṇo dānavyapadeśa iti kecit | tathā ca sati tu samūhadravyaharaṇe na doṣaḥ syād, iṣyate ca, daṇḍadarśanāt | ato vaktavyam etat | tatrānye paṇḍitaṃmanyāḥ pāṣaṇḍādivad "dṛṣṭaprayojanāny eva daṇḍādivacanāni" iti varṇayanti | tathāpi ca dharmārthaḥ samūhadānādivyavahāro 'nālambana eva syāt |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">atrocyate</span> | satyaṃ samudāyināṃ svatvābhāvaḥ | samudāyasya tu svatvasaṃbandhaḥ kena vāryate | yat tu vyatiriktaḥ samudāyo nety uktam | tathaiva tat | samudāyina evaikakāryāvacchedenetaretarāpekṣāḥ samudāyatāṃ pratipadyante | śakyate caivam ekaikasyetaretarāpekṣasya svatvasaṃbandha iti vaktum | na caivaṃbhūtānāṃ dānacodanā nāsti | gavādīnām avibhaktadakṣiṇāvacanād anyatra bahūnām api dānasaṃbandha iti gamyate | brāhmaṇāya ca dānaṃ coditam | na ca sāpekṣatvena deyam iti | na ceyaṃ svatvābhimānabhrāntiḥ, bādhānupalambhāt | tatraitat syāt | sarvasamudāyyasaṃnidhāne kathaṃ dānopapattir iti | tad apy asat | grahītṝṇām itaretarāpekṣāṇām eva svatvayogāt samayasāmarthyāc cartvigyajamānānām iva śarīrendriyamanaḥsādhāraṇyāt pravasadyājamānavac ca samayabalena manaḥsāṃnidhyāc chāstracoditatvāc ca samūhasthiter ṛtvigyajamānasāmyam eva | yat tu samudāyinām anātmīyatvābhidhānam | tannairapekṣyābhiprāyam | vibhāgavidhānāc cartvijāṃ pariṣadaṃ pratyutsargo nyāyānapekṣatve 'py avyāhata eva | ye tu samudāyidānāsaṃbhavād ṛtvijāṃ dakṣiṇāvibhāgaṃ manyante teṣām "aśvo dakṣiṇā" ity evamādau dravyaikatvena vibhāgāsaṃbhavān mūlyadānāyogāc ca duḥśliṣṭataivety alam prasaṅgena || 193 ||

 

_imam eva nyayaṃ manasi kṛtvāha |_

 

                    	**samūhakāryaprahito yal labheta tad arpayet |**

**              	ekādaśaguṇaṃ dāpyo yady asau nārpayet svayam || 2.194 ||**

 

_śāstranibandhanatvāc ca samūhasthiteḥ |_

 

                    	**vedajñāḥ śucayo 'lubdhā bhaveyuḥ kāryacintakāḥ |**

 

smṛtyantarāc catuḥṣaṣṭyādisaṃkhyāyuktāḥ |

 

                    	**kartavyaṃ vacanaṃ teṣāṃ samūhahitavādinām || 2.195 ||**

 

sarvaiḥ samudāyibhir iti śeṣaḥ || 195 ||

 

_yo 'yaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ samūhavidhir uktaḥ |_

** **

**              	śreṇinaigamapāṣaṇḍigaṇānām apy ayaṃ vidhiḥ |**

**              	bhedaṃ caiṣāṃ nṛpo rakṣet pūrvavṛttiṃ ca pālayet || 2.196 ||**

 

karmakarādiśilpisamūhaḥ śreṇiḥ | sārthavāhādisamūho naigamaḥ | guggulikādisamudāyaḥ pāṣaṇḍāḥ | vaṇiksamūho gaṇaḥ | hastyārohādisamūha ity anye | pūgādilakṣaṇārtho vā gaṇaśabdaḥ | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

                    	pāṣaṇḍanaigamaśreṇipūgavrātagaṇādiṣu |

                    	saṃrakṣet samayaṃ rājā durge janapade tathā || iti | (NSm 10.2)

naigamās cātra brāhmaṇasamūhaḥ | pūgo grāmeyakādisamūhaḥ | śastrakartṛsamūho vrātaḥ | kiṃ ca bhedaś caiṣām anyonyaṃ samudāyināṃ vā rājñā rakṣaṇīyaḥ | caśabdād anyasaṅghātarājādivirodhivyavahāraś ca | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

                    	pratikūlaṃ ca yad rājñaḥ prakṛtyavasaraṃ ca yat |

                    	bādhakaṃ ca yad arthānāṃ tat tebhyo vinivartayet ||

                    	mithaḥ saṅghatakaraṇam ahite śastradhāraṇam |

                    	parasparopatāpaṃ ca tebhyo rājā nivartayet || (NSm 10.4–5)

ityādikān virodhān nṛpaḥ pratikuryāt | pūrvakalpitāṃ ca dharmāvirodhinīṃ vṛttiṃ pālayet | caśabdāt svayaṃ ca vardhayed ity abhiprāyaḥ || 196 ||

 

 

**iti saṃvidvyatikramaprakaraṇam |**

** **

**atha vetanādānaprakaraṇam |**

 

_paribhāṣāprasaṅgena svāmikarmakarayoḥ paribhāṣānusārivyavahāravyabhicāre vinayaṃ vaktum āha |_

 

                    	**gṛhītavetanaḥ karma tyajan dviguṇam āvahet |**

**              	agṛhīte samaṃ kāryaṃ bhṛtyaiḥ pālya upaskaraḥ || 2.197 ||**

 

gṛhītvā vetanaṃ karma tulyaṃ na kuryāt, tato gṛhītavetano dviguṇam āvahed dadyād ity arthaḥ | agṛhīte tu vetane samaṃ yāvat pāribhāṣikaṃ vetanaṃ dattvā karma kāryaṃ kārayitavyam | sarvakarmakaraiś cāptavetanair upaskaraḥ samarpito yaḥ karmakaraṇārthaṃ sa pālanīyaḥ | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

                    	karmopakaraṇaṃ caiṣāṃ kriyāṃ prati yad arpitam |

                    	āptabhāvena tat pālyaṃ na jihmena kathaṃcana || (NSm 6.4)

tathā |

                    	karmākurvan pratiśrutya kāryo dattvā bhṛtiṃ balāt |

                    	bhṛtiṃ gṛhītvākurvāṇo dviguṇā bhṛtim āvahet || iti (NSm 6.5) || 197 ||

 

_aparibhāṣya vetanaṃ karmaṇi kṛte yady aparibhāṣitatvavyājena svāmī na kiṃcid dātum icchet, tatra katham ity apekṣita āha |_

 

                    	**dāpyas tu daśamaṃ bhāgaṃ vāṇijyapaśusasyataḥ |**

**              	aniścitya bhṛtiṃ yas tu kārayet sa mahībhṛtā || 2.198 ||**

 

svayaṃ ca na dadyād iti śeṣaḥ | aparibhāṣya vāṇijyaṃ pāśupālyaṃ kṛṣiṃ vā yaḥ karoti tasya tadutpannopacayadaśamabhāgabhāktvam ity avaseyam || 198 ||

 

_yathā svāminā nirdiṣṭaḥ karmakaraḥ |_

 

                    	**deśaṃ kālaṃ ca yo 'tīyāt karma kuryāc ca yo 'nyathā |**

**              	tatra syāt svāminaś chando 'dhikaṃ deyaṃ kṛte 'dhike || 2.199 ||**

 

svāmyuktadeśakālādiviparyayeṇānyathā vā karmaṇi kṛte bhṛtidānaṃ prati svāminaḥ svecchā | vinayātirekāc ca karmakarair adhike karmani kṛte svāminā svecchayaivādhikaṃ deyam ity avaseyam || 199 ||

 

_asamāptakarmatyāge tu vetanahāniprāptāv apavādaḥ |_

 

                    	**yo yāvat kurute karma tāvat tasya tu vetanam |**

**              	ubhayor apy aṣāṭhyaṃ cec chāṭhye kuryād yathākṛtam || 2.200 ||**

 

yathecchayety arthaḥ | svāmy api śāṭhyenākārayan yathākṛtaṃ vetanaṃ dāpyaḥ smṛtyantarānusārāt || 200 ||

 

_śāṭhyenaiva ca |_

 

                    	**arājadaivikān naṣṭaṃ bhāṇḍaṃ dāpyas tu vāhakaḥ |**

**              	prathānavighnakartā ca pradāpyo dviguṇāṃ bhṛtim || 2.201 ||**

 

_karmakaravac ca svāmy api |_

 

**              	prakrānte saptamaṃ bhāgaṃ caturthaṃ pathi saṃtyajet |**

**              	bhṛtim ardhapate sarvāṃ pradāpyas tyājako 'pi ca || 2.202 ||**

 

prakrāntādisaptamabhāgādikrameṇa tyājakaḥ svāmy api karmakarebhyo dāpyaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 202 ||

 

 

**iti vetanādānaprakaraṇam |**

** **

**atha dyūtasamāhvayaprakaraṇam |**

 

_visaṃvādaprasaṅgenākhilavisaṃvādaikakāraṇabhūtaṃ dyūtasamāhvayavyavahāram āha |_

 

                    	**galatsabhikavṛddhis tu sabhikaḥ pañcakaṃ śatam |**

**              	gṛhṇīyād dhūrtakitavād itarād daśakaṃ śatam || 2.203 ||**

 

tuśabdo 'vadhāraṇārthaḥ | galatsabhikavṛddhir eva sabhikasya, nānyad api svaparibhāṣitamukhapaṭṭādīty abhiprāyaḥ | galitaṃ nirgalitaṃ yat sabhikahastāt parājitānāṃ devanārthaṃ dravyaṃ, yac ca dyūtopakaraṇam akṣādi tad galatsabhikaṃ dhūrtamaṇḍalādhipatir gṛhṇīyāt | kiyanti | pañcakaṃ śatam | dhūrtakitavāj jetuḥ dyūtopakaraṇanimittam | itarāt parājitāt prayuktasvadravyanimittaṃ daśakaṃ śatam ity arthaḥ || 203 ||

 

_svārthahetor eva ca rājñā |_

 

                    	**sa samyak pālito dadyād rājñe bhāgaṃ yathākṛtam |**

**              	jitam udgrāhayej jetre dadyād satyavacāḥ kṣamī || 2.204 ||**

 

yathākṛtaṃ yathāparibhāṣitaṃ yathā vā smṛtyantare nirūpitam ity arthaḥ | tad yathā bṛhaspatau |

                    	rājavṛddhiḥ sakitavāt sabhikād daśakaṃ śatam |

                    	yathāsamayaṃ vā syāt | iti | (BṛSm 27.3)

kiṃ ca jitaṃ yat kitavaiḥ, tat parājitebhyaḥ sabhika udgrāhayet | jetre ca yena jitaṃ tasmai sabhika eva satyavacano bhūtvāvisaṃvādena kṣamī cānutāpavān punar dadyād ity avaseyam || 204 ||

 

_yathākṛta eva |_

 

                    	**prāpte nṛpatibhāge tu prasiddhe dhūrtamaṇḍale |**

**              	jitaṃ sasabhike sthāne dāpayed anyathā na tu || 2.205 ||**

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**draṣṭāro vyavahārāṇāṃ sākṣiṇaś ca ta eva hi |**

**              	rājñā sacihnā nirvāsyāḥ kūṭākṣopadhidevinaḥ || 2.206 ||**

 

spaṣṭārthau ślokau | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> etad dyūtaṃ svayaṃbhuvā niṣiddham |

                    	prakāśam etat tāskaryaṃ yad devanasamāhvayam | iti | (MDh 9.222)

tathā coktam |

                    	pracchannaṃ vā prakāśaṃ vā dyūtaṃ rāṣṭre nivārayet |

iti ca | vede 'pi "akṣair mā dīvyaḥ" (RV 10.34.13) iti pratiṣedhaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | pratiṣedhātikrameṇa pravṛttau śyenādivad ayaṃ vidhir ity avirodhaḥ | mānavas tu daṇḍavidhir dharmavirodhitayā nānāmukhatvena veti || 206 ||

 

_prayojanāntarāpekṣayā tu |_

 

                    	**dyūtam ekamukhaṃ kāryaṃ taskarajñānakāraṇāt |**

**              	eṣa eva vidhir jñeyaḥ prāṇidyūte samāhvaye || 2.207 ||**

 

ekamukham ekamārgam ekasmin pradeśe rājakīyacārapuruṣādyadhiṣṭhitaṃ taskarādiprajākaṇṭakaparijñānārtham adharmarūpam api dharmāntaropāyatayā mahate 'bhyudayāya saṃpadyata iti | ataḥ kāryam evety abhiprāyaḥ | ye vākhilasvadharmatyāgenāpady api dyūtaikaniratāḥ tadviṣayatayā svāyaṃbhuve daṇḍādivacanāny avaseyāni | etena pāṣaṇḍādidharmo vyākhyātaḥ | yaś cāyam akṣādyaprāṇidevane dyūtākhye vidhir uktaḥ, samāhvayasañjake 'pi kukkuṭameṣādibhiḥ sapaṇaprāṇidyūte 'yam eva vidhir jñeyaḥ sabhikādhīnatvarājavṛddhidānādika ity abhiprāyaḥ || 207 ||

 

 

**iti dyūtasamāhvayaprakaraṇam |**

** **

**atha vākpāruṣyaprakaraṇam** |

 

_prāyeṇa dyūtaprabhavatvād vāgdaṇḍapāruṣyayor vināśakāraṇatvasāmānyād vā dyūtavyavahārānantaram ārambhaḥ | tatrāpi daṇḍapāruṣyasyāpi kāraṇabhūtatvād vākpāruṣyam eva tāvad ucyate |_

 

                    	**satyāsatyānyathāstotrair hīnāṅgendriyarogiṇām |**

**              	kṣepaṃ karoti ced daṇḍyaḥ paṇān ardhatrayodaśa || 2.208 ||**

 

hīnāṅgāḥ khañjādayaḥ | hīnendriyāḥ kāṇādayaḥ | kuṣṭhādyabhibhūtā rogiṇaḥ | teṣāṃ yady anaparādhinām eva cāpalād vidyamānendriyavaikalyādinā satyenaiva duṣṭayā vācā kṣepaṃ kuryāt, asatyenāpi he kāṇa ityakāṇam evādhikṣipet | anyathāstrotreṇa vā sātiśayastutipadaiḥ prasiddhaṃ mūkhaṃ he caturvedin ityevaṃ vadan ardhatrayodaśapaṇān rājāvedane kṛte daṇḍyaḥ | smṛtyantarāc ca tasyāpi prasādanaṃ kāryam || 208 ||

 

_rājāvedana eva ca |_

 

                    	**abhigantāsi bhaginīṃ mātaraṃ vā taveti hi |**

**              	śapantaṃ dāpayed rājā pañcaviṃśatikaṃ damam || 2.209 ||**

 

ayaṃ ca savarṇānāṃ samānaguṇānāṃ ca daṇḍakalpaḥ || 209 ||

 

_guṇavarṇavaiṣamye punaḥ |_

 

                    	**ardho 'dhameṣu dviguṇaḥ parastrīṣūttameṣu ca |**

**              	daṇḍapraṇayanaṃ kāryaṃ varṇajātyuttarādharam || 2.210 ||**

 

nirūpyeti śeṣaḥ | uktadaṇḍād ardhatrayodaśapaṇāvadhikād varṇaguṇādyadhameṣv ardhadaṇḍaḥ | dviguṇaṃ ca parastrīṣu | paraśabda utkṛṣṭārthaḥ | parair utkṛṣṭaiḥ guṇato varṇato vā pariṇītāḥ parastriyaḥ, tāsv adhikṣiptāsu | uttameṣu ca guṇavarṇādibhiḥ puruṣeṣu strīṣu vā | ardhavacanaṃ dviguṇavacanaṃ cobhayam api yathārhadaṇḍopalakṣaṇārtham ity etad darśayati | daṇḍapraṇayanaṃ kāryam iti nyūnatayādhikyena vā yathārhaṃ varṇajātyuttarādharam ālocyety abhiprāyaḥ | jātiśabdaś ca janmanimittatvād vayovacanatayā guṇalakṣaṇārtho 'vaseyaḥ || 210 ||

 

_etad evodāharaṇena spaṣṭayati |_

 

                    	**pratilomāpavādeṣu catustridviguṇā damāḥ |**

**              	varṇāntyeṣv ānulomyena tasmād evārdhahānataḥ || 2.211 ||**

 

varṇāntyāḥ śūdrāḥ | teṣāṃ pratilomāpavāde brāhmaṇādikrameṇoktadaṇḍasya caturguṇādikalpanam | evaṃ vaiśyakṣatriyānulomāntaraprabhavayor guṇādyutkarṣe 'pi yojyam | ānulomyena tu tasmād evārdhahānataḥ uktadaṇḍād ardhāpacayena | śūdrāpavāde ardhadaṇḍo vaśyasya, pādaḥ kṣatriyasya, ardhapādo brāhmaṇasya | evaṃ guṇādyānulomye 'pi yojyam || 211 ||

 

_vadhapratijñayā  tu vākpāruṣye |_

 

                    	**bāhugrīvānetrasakthivināśe vācike damaḥ |**

**              	śatyas tadardhikaḥ pādanāsākarṇakarādiṣu || 2.212 ||**

 

bāhvādicchedas te mayā kartavya ity evaṃ tathākaraṇasamarthasya bruvataḥ śatyo damaḥ kāryaḥ | śatenābhinirvṛttaḥ śatyaḥ | śataṃ daṇḍya ity arthaḥ | pādādicchedanapratijñāyāṃ tu tato 'rdhaṃ, pañcāśad ity arthaḥ | ādiśabdaś ca daṇḍapāruṣyoktadantabhaṅgādyarthaḥ | ūrvasthi sakthīty ucyate | spaṣṭam anyat || 212 ||

 

_prāguktaṃ śaktasaṃbandhitayā bāhvādicchedavākyam |_

 

                    	**aśaktas tu vadann evaṃ daṇḍanīyaḥ paṇān daśa |**

**              	tathā śaktaḥ pratibhuvaṃ dāpyaḥ kṣemāya tasya tu || 2.213 ||**

 

vaṅmātreṇāpi vadataḥ kartum aśaktasya daśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ | śaktas tu prāguktadaṇḍaṃ dāpyaḥ | trāsāpanodanāya ca samarthaṃ kṣemāya pratibhuvaṃ dāpyaḥ || 213 ||

 

_brahmahā goghno vā tvam ityevamādike kṣepe |_

 

                    	**patanīyakṛte kṣepe daṇḍyo madhyamasāhasam |**

**              	upapātakayukte tu dāpyaḥ prathamasāhasam || 2.214 ||**

 

_tathā |_

 

                    	**traividyanṛpadevānāṃ kṣepa uttamasāhasaḥ |**

**              	madhyamo jātipūgānāṃ prathamo grāmadeśayoḥ || 2.215 ||**

 

nṛpagrahaṇam ācāryapitṛśrotriyādīnām api sāmānyāl lakṣaṇārtham | pūgaśabdaś cātra gaṇamātravacanaḥ | tataś ca jātipūgānāṃ jātimatāṃ gaṇānāṃ kṣatriyādisamudāyānām ity arthaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 215 ||

 

 

**iti vākpāruṣyaprakaraṇam |**

** **

**atha daṇḍapāruṣyaprakaraṇam |**

 

_vākpāruṣyapūrvakatvād daṇḍapāruṣyasyānantaram ārambhaḥ | pāṇyādinābhighātādikaṃ daṇḍapāruṣyam | tatra nirjane 'bhihatya na mayāyam abhihata ity evaṃ mithyāvāditve dauṣṭyātiśayād vā kṣatādyātmanaḥ kṛtvā nirdoṣajanādhyārope kathaṃ syād ity apekṣita āha |_

 

                    	**asākṣikahate cihnair yuktibhiś cāgamena ca |**

**              	draṣṭavyo vyavahāras tu kūṭacihnakṛtād bhayāt || 2.216 ||**

 

asākṣike 'bhihate kṣatādibhiś cihnais tadvyabhicare vā kūṭacihnakāriduṣṭapuruṣabhayād vyavahāra eva praguktanyāyena catuṣpād yuktyāgamānusāreṇaiva vidvajjanasamakṣaṃ svayaṃ vā rājñā draṣṭavyaḥ | ayaṃ ca sarvavyavahārapadasādhāraṇaḥ ślokaḥ kāryagauravapratipattyartham ihāmnāta ity avaseyam || 216 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**yatra nokto damaḥ sarvaiḥ pramādena mahātmabhiḥ |**

**              	tatra kāryaṃ parijñāya kartavyaṃ daṇḍadhāraṇam || 2.217 ||**

 

nānabhidhānabhrāntyānadhyavasāyaḥ kāryaḥ, kiṃ tarhi uktam anuktaṃ vā dvayor guṇādibhir anubandhādibhiś ca svarūpam ālocya pīḍānusāreṇa sarvatra daṇḍamānakartavyatādhyavasānam ity abhiprāyaḥ || 217 ||

 

_etad evodāharaṇamātratayā prapañcayati |_

 

                    	**bhasmapaṅkarajaḥsparśe daṇḍo daśapaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ |**

**              	amedhyapārṣṇiniṣṭhyūtasparśane dviguṇaḥ smṛtaḥ || 2.218 ||**

 

medhyatve 'pi bhasmakardamadhūliprakṣepaṇe nirdoṣasya kṛte daśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ smṛta ity alpo 'pi smaraṇānusārād aviruddha ity avaseyam | amedhyādisparśe tu tato dviguṇaḥ viṃśatipaṇa ity arthaḥ | niṣṭhyūtagrahaṇaṃ niṣṭhyutasadṛśāmedhyasya pratipattyartham | tathā ca mūtrapurīṣādau daṇḍātirekasiddhiḥ || 218 ||

 

_yac caitad uktam |_

 

                    	**sameṣv evaṃ parastrīṣu dviguṇas tūttameṣu ca |**

**              	hīneṣv ardhadamo mohamadādibhir adaṇḍanam || 2.219 ||**

 

kṛtavyākhyānam etat || 219 ||

 

_ayaṃ cānyo viśeṣaḥ |_

 

                    	**viprapīḍākaraṃ chedyam aṅgam abrāhmaṇasya tu |**

**              	udgūrṇe prathamo daṇḍaḥ sparśane tu tadardhikaḥ || 2.220 ||**

 

udgūryānipāte prathamasāhaso daṇḍaḥ | prahārāyodgūraṇenaiva visrambheṇābrāhmaṇasya brāhmaṇaśarīrasparśane 'rdhadaṇḍaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 220 ||

 

_anutkṛṣṭaviṣayatve tu |_

 

                    	**udgūrṇe hastapāde tu daśaviṃśatikau damau |**

**              	parasparaṃ tu sarveṣāṃ śastre madhyamasāhasaḥ || 2.221 ||**

 

tuśabdaḥ pratyekam avadhāraṇārthaḥ | hasta evodgūrṇe daśakaḥ pāda eva viṃśatikaḥ | tathā ca samuccaye samuccayasiddhiḥ | evam anyatrāpi draṣṭavyam | etac ca sarvavarṇānāṃ tulyaguṇādiyoge syāt | śastrodgūraṇe tu madhyamasāhaso daṇḍaḥ || 221 ||

 

_jātyādisāmya eva tu |_

 

                    	**pādakeśāṃśukakarāluñchaneṣu paṇān daśa |**

**              	pīḍākarṣāñjanāveṣṭya pādādhyāse śataṃ damaḥ || 2.222 ||**

 

pādakeśavastrāṇām āluñchane avadhūnane sākṣepaṃ daśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ syāt | pīḍākarṣāñjanena tv āveṣṭya grīvādau pādanyāse śataṃ daṇḍyaḥ | āñjanaṃ dhyāmīkaraṇam | pīḍayā karṣaṇenāñjanaṃ pīḍākarṣāñjanam | āñjanena dhyāmīkaraṇena tv āveṣṭya vaśaṃ nītvety arthaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 222 ||

 

_sāmya eva |_

 

                    	**śoṇitena vinā kurvan duḥkhaṃ kāṣṭhādibhir naraḥ |**

**              	dvātriṃśataṃ paṇān daṇḍyo dviguṇaṃ darśane 'sṛjaḥ || 2.223 ||**

 

asṛjo lohitasyety arthaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 223 ||

 

_nikṛṣṭaviṣayatve tu |_

 

                    	**karapādadantabhaṅge chedane karṇanāsayoḥ |**

**              	madhyo daṇḍo vraṇodbhede mṛtakalpahate tathā || 2.224 ||**

 

sāmye hi śastrodgūraṇamātra eva madhyamasyoktatvān nikṛṣṭaviṣayam etad iti vyākhyeyam | ṛjv anyat || 224 ||

 

_tathā |_

 

                    	**ceṣṭābhojanavāgrodhe netrādipratibhedane |**

**              	kandharābāhusakthnāṃ ca bhaṅga uttamasāhasaḥ || 2.225 ||**

 

ceṣṭādipratirodhake 'bhighāte akṣyādīndriyādhiṣṭhānapratyekabhedane kandharādibhedane cottamasāhaso daṇḍaḥ | ceṣṭānirodho mūrchā | bhojananirodho 'tyabhighātād bhoktum aśaktiḥ | vāguccāraṇāśaktir vāgrodhaḥ | kandharā galaskandhasaṃcāriṇī sirā | spaṣṭam anyat || 225 ||

 

_sarvatraivāsmin prakaraṇe |_

 

                    	**ekaṃ ghnatāṃ bahūnāṃ tu yathoktād dviguṇā damāḥ |**

**              	kalahāpahṛtaṃ deyaṃ daṇḍaś ca dviguṇas tataḥ || 2.226 ||**

 

kalahāpahṛtād ity arthaḥ | etac cābhihatāyaiva deyaṃ rājadaṇḍavyatirekeṇety avaseyam | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

                    	daṇḍas tv abhihatāyaiva daṇḍapāruṣyakalpitaḥ |

                    	hṛte taddviguṇaṃ cānyad rājadaṇḍas tato 'dhikaḥ || iti | (BṛSm 21.14)

yat tu nāradīyam |

                    	yam eva hy ativarterann ete santaṃ janaṃ nṛṣu |

                    	sa eva vinayaṃ kuryān na tadvinayabhāṅ nṛpaḥ || iti | (NSm 15–16.14)

etac chūdraviṣayaṃ draṣṭavyam | śūdrāṇāṃ hy utkṛṣṭāparādhe rājñārthadaṇḍo na grāhyaḥ | kiṃ tarhi | anāvedya svayam evotkṛṣṭair arthadaṇḍena vinayaḥ kāryaḥ | rājñā tv āvedite vadha eva | tathā cānantaram evāha |

                    	malā hy ete manuṣyeṣu dhanam eṣāṃ malātmakam |

                    	atas tān ghātayed rājā nārthadaṇḍena daṇḍayet || iti | (NSm 15–16.15)

spaṣṭam anyat || 226 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**duḥkham utpādayet yas tu sa samutthānajaṃ vyayam |**

**              	dāpyo daṇḍaṃ ca yo yasmin kalahe samudāhṛtaḥ || 2.227 ||**

 

yo duḥkham utpādayet tena yāvat samyag asyotthānaṃ nirduḥkhatā bhavati, tāvad yo vyayaḥ sa samutthānajo vyayaḥ, sa deyaḥ | cakārād rājāvedanapravṛttyupakṣayaś ca | rājñe ca yathodāhṛto daṇḍaḥ | svayaṃ cādadad rājñā dāpyaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 227 ||

 

_idānīṃ daṇḍapāruṣyasāmānyāt sāhasavyavahāram āha |_

 

                    	**tārikaḥ sthalajaṃ śulkaṃ gṛhṇan dāpyaḥ paṇān daśa |**

**              	brāhmaṇaḥ prātiveśyānām etad evānimantraṇe || 2.228 ||**

 

tārikasya sthalanimittarājabhāvyaśulkagrahaṇe brāhmaṇyadarpāc ca yogyaprātiveśyabrāhmaṇānimantraṇe daśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ | brāhmaṇagrahaṇaṃ ca guṇārthatvāt sarvatraivarṇikārtham | darpakṛtatvāc caivamādeḥ sāhasatvam || 228 ||

 

_darpeṇaiva ca |_

 

                    	**abhighāte tathā bhede chede kuḍyāvapātane |**

**              	paṇān dāpyaḥ pañca daśa viṃśatiṃ tadvyayaṃ tathā || 2.229 ||**

 

prātiveśikagṛhāṇāṃ daurātmyāt pāṣāṇādinābhighāte kṛte pañca paṇān dāpyaḥ | tathā bhede 'bhighātasaṃtrāsāj jāte daśa paṇān dāpyaḥ | chedane tu taddvaidhībhāve kuḍyāvapātane vā viṃśatim | vyaye tu vyāpannasamādhānārthaṃ gṛhiṇe dadyāt sarvatra sāhasikatvāt || 229 ||

 

_parakīye |_

 

                    	**duḥkhotpādi gṛhe dravyaṃ kṣipan prāṇaharaṃ tathā |**

**              	ṣoḍaśādye paṇān dāpyo dvitīye madhyamaṃ damam || 2.230 ||**

 

duḥkhotpādi dravyaṃ kaṇṭakādi | prāṇaharaṃ sarpādi | spaṣṭam anyat || 230 ||

 

                    	**duḥkhe 'tha śoṇitotpāde śākhāṅgacchedane tathā |**

**              	daṇḍaḥ kṣudrapaśūnāṃ syād dvipaṇaprabhṛti kramāt || 2.231 ||**

 

dviguṇa iti śeṣaḥ | śoṇitotpādaśākhāṅgacchedaneṣūttarottaro dviguṇaḥ | śṛṅgakarṇapucchādīni śākhāḥ | cakṣurādīny aṅgāni | kṣudrapaśavaś chāgādayaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 231 ||

 

_parakīyānāṃ tu |_

 

                    	**liṅgasya chedane mṛtyau madhyamo mūlyam eva ca |**

**              	mahāpaśūnām eteṣu sthāneṣu dviguṇā damāḥ || 2.232 ||**

 

svakīye dvipaṇādimadhyamāntā yathāsthanaṃ daṇḍāḥ, parakīye tu daṇḍō mūlyaṃ ceti yojyam | mahāpaśavo gavādayaḥ | teṣāṃ prāguktaśoṇitaduḥkhotpādiṣu sthāneṣu dvipaṇādyuktadaṇḍād dviguṇā yathāsthānaṃ daṇḍāḥ kāryāḥ || 232 ||

 

_ārāmāropitānāṃ saparigrahāṇām |_

 

                    	**prarohaśākhikāśākhāskandhasarvavidāraṇe |**

**              	upajīvyadrumāṇāṃ tu viṃśatidviguṇā damāḥ || 2.233 ||**

 

upajīvyadrumā āmrādayaḥ | teṣāṃ prarohacchedane viṃśatipaṇo damaḥ | śākhikādicchedaneṣūttarottaradviguṇakalpanā | prarohaḥ pallavaḥ | alpāḥ śākhāḥ śākhikāḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 233 ||

 

_upajīvyānām eva ca |_

 

                    	**caityaśmaśānasīmāntapuṇyasthāne nṛpālaye |**

**              	jātadrumāṇāṃ dviguṇā damā vṛkṣe ca viśrute || 2.234 ||**

 

cāturthikādyapanodanasamarthaḥ pippalādivṛkṣo viśrutaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 234 ||

 

_caityādijātānām eva tu |_

 

                    	**gulmagucchakṣupalathāpratānauṣadhivīrudhām |**

**              	pūrvasmṛtād ardhadaṇḍaḥ sthāneṣūkteṣu kṛntane || 2.235 ||**

 

gulmādīnām ukteṣu caityādisthāneṣu jātānāṃ kṛntane prāguktaprarohādikrameṇaiva smṛtād ekaguṇād ardhadaṇḍāḥ kalpyāḥ | gulmaḥ guñjādi | gucchaḥ kundādi | kṣupo jātyādiviṭapaḥ | latā prasiddhā | pratānā vallarī | grāmyā oṣadhayaḥ | āraṇyā vīrudhaḥ || 235 ||

 

 

**iti daṇḍapāruṣyaprakaraṇam |**

** **

**atha sāhasaprakaraṇam |**

 

_steyam api prasahya kṛtaṃ sāhasam eva yasmād, ato nātra steyadaṇḍaḥ | kiṃ tarhi |_

 

                    	**sāmānyaprasabhadravyaharaṇāt sāhasaṃ smṛtam |**

**              	tanmūlyād dviguṇo daṇḍo nihnave tu caturguṇaḥ || 2.236 ||**

 

sāmānyaṃ dravyaṃ dvayor yad anyatareṇa prasabhaṃ prasahyānyataraṃ paribhūyāpahriyate, tat steyam apy prasahya haraṇāt sāhasam iti smṛtaṃ maharṣibhir yasmāt, tasmān na tatra steyadaṇḍaḥ | kiṃ tarhi apahṛtadravyamūlyād dviguṇaḥ sāhasikadaṇḍa ity abhiprāyaḥ | prasahyāpahṛtya nihnave kṛte mūlyāc caturguṇaḥ | sāmānyadravyaharaṇaṃ codāharaṇārtham | anyad api yat prasahya steyam anyad vā kriyate, tat sarvaṃ sāhasam eva | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

                    	sahasā kriyate karma yat kiṃcid baladarpitaiḥ |

                    	tat sāhasam iti proktaṃ saho balam ihocyate || iti (NSm 14.1) || 236 ||

 

_anyenāpi prayoktṛtayā |_

 

                    	**yaḥ sāhasaṃ kārayati sa dāpyo dviguṇaṃ damam |**

**              	yas tv evam uktvāhaṃ dātā kārayet sa caturguṇam || 2.237 ||**

 

pūrvoktād dviguṇaṃ daṇḍaṃ kārayitā dāpyaḥ | ya tv evam uktvā kārayet "kriyatām idaṃ yady atra kaścid virodho bhaviṣyati, tato 'ham eva nirvahaṇaṃ kariṣyāmi" iti sa coktadviguṇadaṇḍāc caturguṇaṃ daṇḍya ity avaseyam || 237 ||

 

_sāhasikatvād eva ca |_

 

                    	**arghyākrośātikramakṛd bhrātṛbhāryāprahāradaḥ |**

**              	saṃdiṣṭasyāpradātā ca samudragṛhabhedakṛt || 2.238 ||**

**              	sāmantakulikādīnām apakārasya kārakaḥ |**

**              	pañcāśatpaṇiko daṇḍa eṣām iti niścayaḥ || 2.239 ||**

 

spaṣṭārthau ślokau || 238–9 ||

 

_tathā |_

 

**              	svacchandavidhavāgāmī vikruṣṭe 'nabhidhāvakaḥ |**

**              	akāraṇe ca vikroṣṭā caṇḍālaś cottamān spṛśan || 2.240 ||**

**              	śūdrapravrajitānāṃ ca daive pitrye ca bhojakaḥ |**

**              	ayuktaṃ śapathaṃ kurvann ayogyo yogyakarmakṛt || 2.241 ||**

**              	vṛṣakṣudrapaśūnāṃ ca puṃstvasya pratighātakaḥ |**

**              	sādhāraṇasyāpalāpī dāsīgarbhavināśakṛt || 2.242 ||**

**              	pitāputrasvasṛbhrātṛdampatyācāryaśiṣyakāḥ |**

**              	eṣām apatitānyonyatyāgī ca śatadaṇḍabhāk || 2.243 ||**

 

etad api ślokacatuṣṭayaṃ spaṣṭārtham eva || 240–3 ||

 

_prakṣālanārtham arpitam |_

 

                    	**vasānas trīn paṇān dāpyo rajakas tu parāṃśukam |**

**              	vikrayāpakrayādhānayāciteṣu paṇān daśa || 2.244 ||**

 

parāṃśukam utkṛṣṭaṃ vastram | tatparidhāne rajakasya tripaṇo damaḥ | evaṃ madhyamādhameṣu paṇāpacayakalpanā | tathābhyāsāpekṣayā vyatirekakalpanā | vikrayādikaraṇeṣu tu svāmino mūlyaṃ, rājñe daṇḍaś cety avaseyam | bhāṇḍakenārpaṇam apakrayaḥ | ādhamanam ādhānam | spaṣṭam anyat || 244 ||

 

_evamādeyavyavahāraviṣaye tāvad daṇḍavyavasthoktā | bhrātrādikṛte tv anādeyavyavahare |_

 

                    	**pitāputravirodhādau sākṣiṇāṃ dviśato damaḥ |**

**              	sāntaraś ca tayor yaḥ syāt tasyāpy aṣṭaśato damaḥ || 2.245 ||**

 

sarvatra pitāputrādivirodhe 'nādeyavyavahāre sākṣino draṣṭāro vā ye syuḥ, sākṣivacanasya lakṣaṇārthatvāt, teṣāṃ dviśato damaḥ | yas tu pitāputrādīnāṃ sāntaraḥ viśleṣakaraḥ syāt, tasyāpy aṣṭaśatam | yad vā tayor eva pitāputrayor yaḥ sāntaraḥ syād vyājavyavahartety arthaḥ | dvayam apy etad avirodhād yuktam || 245 ||

 

_svābhipretavyavahārasiddhyartham |_

 

                    	**tulāśāsanamānānāṃ kūṭakṛn nāṇakasya ca |**

**              	ebhiś ca vyavahartā yaḥ sa dāpyo damam uttamam || 2.246 ||**

 

śāsanagrahaṇaṃ sarvalekhyalakṣaṇārtham | mānāni setikāprasthaprabhṛtīni | spaṣṭam anyat || 246 ||

 

_jānann api tu lobhādinā |_

 

                    	**akūṭaṃ kūṭakaṃ brūte kūṭaṃ yaś cāpy akūṭakam |**

**              	sa nāṇakaparīkṣī tu dāpyaḥ prathamasāhasam || 2.247 ||**

 

tuśabdaḥ suvarṇamāṇikyādāv atiriktadaṇḍajñāpanārthaḥ |

 

_ajñānād viparyayato vā |_

 

                    	**bhiṣaṅ mithyācaran dāpyas tiryakṣu prathamaṃ damam |**

**              	mānuṣe madhyamaṃ dāpya uttamaṃ rājamānuṣe || 2.248 ||**

 

paśavo varṇāpaśadāś ca tiryañcaḥ | viṭchūdrāḥ mānuṣam | kṣatriyā brāhmaṇāś ca rājamānuṣam | evaṃ mithācarato vaidyasya prathamasāhasādayo daṇḍāḥ | udāharaṇārthaṃ caitat | sarvathā cikitsyasvarūpaṃ pīḍāviśeṣaṃ ca vaidyakṛtam ālocya yathārthaṃ daṇḍakalpanety avaseyam || 248 ||

 

_varṇāparthikathayā (?) tu |_

** **

**              	abandhyaṃ yaś ca badhnāti bandhyaṃ yaś ca pramuñcati |**

**              	aprāptavyavahāraṃ ca sa dāpyo damam uttamam || 2.249 ||**

 

aprāptavyavahāro vyavahāreṇāspaṣṭīkṛtaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 249 ||

 

_akūṭenaiva kauśalāt |_

 

                    	**mānena tulayā vāpi yo 'ṃśam aṣṭakaṃ haret |**

**              	daṇḍaṃ sa dāpyo dviśataṃ vṛddhau hānau ca kalpitam || 2.250 ||**

 

etad api steyadravyasāratāpekṣayā vyavasthāpanīyam | spaṣṭam anyat || 250 ||

 

_sādṛśyādinā kretur bhramaṃ cikīrṣuḥ |_

** **

**              	bheṣajasnehalavaṇagandhadhānyagulādiṣu |**

**              	paṇyeṣu hīnaṃ kṣipataḥ paṇān dāpyas tu ṣoḍaśa || 2.251 ||**

 

hīnaṃ hīnamūlyaṃ | ṛjv anyat || 251 ||

 

_kretuḥ paṇyasvarūpājñatvam abhipretya |_

 

                    	**mṛccarmamaṇisūtrāyaḥkāṣṭhavalkalavāsasām |**

**              	ajater jātikaraṇād vikraye 'ṣṭaguṇo damaḥ || 2.252 ||**

 

mṛdādīnām ajātyaṃ jātyam iti kṛtvā vikrīṇann uktaṣoḍaśapaṇād aṣṭaguṇaṃ daṇḍyaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 252 ||

 

_yadi tu samudgakādisthaṃ darśayitvā samudgakāntaraparivartanena karpūrādisāradravyaṃ kṛtrimakaraṇena vā kaścid ādhānaṃ vikrayaṃ vā kuryāt, tasyāpi vyājavyavahāriṇaḥ |_

 

                    	**samudgaparivartaṃ ca sārabhāṇḍaṃ ca kṛtrimam |**

**              	ādhānaṃ vikrayaṃ vāpi nayato daṇḍakalpanā || 2.253 ||**

 

uktārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 253 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">kiṃ</span> svamatyaiva daṇḍakalpanā | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nety</span> āha |_

 

                    	**bhinne paṇe tu pañcāśat paṇe tu śatam ucyate |**

**              	dvipaṇe dviśato daṇḍo mūlyavṛddhau tu vṛddhimān || 2.254 ||**

 

anirdiṣṭaviṣaye tu dravye mūlyānusāriṇī daṇḍakalpanety abhiprāyaḥ || 254 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvat pratyekavyatikrame 'nuśāsanam uktam | idānīṃ kārukādīnāṃ saṃbhūyavyatikrame 'nuśāsanam āha |_

 

                    	**saṃbhūya kurvatām arghaṃ sābādhaṃ kāruśilpinām |**

**              	arghasya hānau vṛddhau vā sāhasro daṇḍa ucyate || 2.255 ||**

 

saṃbhūyaikamatyena kāruśilpināṃ sābādhaṃ pīḍākaram anyaśilpijanasya tanniṣpāditadravyasya vā kurvatāṃ kārṣāpaṇasahasraṃ daṇḍaḥ śilpārghasya hānau vṛddhau vā kartavyaḥ | ye hi bhājanādīni dravyāṇi svayam eva kṛtvā vikrīṇanti, te śilpinaḥ kāṃsyakārādayaḥ | ye tu parakīyāny eva gṛhādīni niṣpādayanti, te kāravaḥ | teṣām āgantukaśilpijanasyānavakāśārthaṃ kārayitṛjanārthitātiśayād vā arghasya hāniṃ vṛddhiṃ vā yadā kuryuḥ, tadāyaṃ daṇḍa ity avaseyam || 255 ||

 

_uktād eva hetoḥ |_

 

                    	**saṃbhūya vaṇijāṃ paṇyam anargheṇoparundhatām |**

**              	vikrīṇatāṃ vā vihito daṇḍa uttamasāhasaḥ || 2.256 ||**

 

_kena tarhy argheṇa paṇyānāṃ vikraya iti | ucyate |_

 

                    	**rājani sthāpyate yo 'rghaḥ pratyahaṃ tena vikrayaḥ |**

**              	krayo vā**

 

kārya iti śeṣaḥ |

 

_yaś cāsau rājakulādhiṣṭhitanipuṇavaṇiṅnirūpito divasārghaḥ, tena krītānāṃ punar vikrayaḥ kasmāt, yasmāc ca |_

 

                                	**vikrayo vāpi vaṇījāṃ lābhataḥ smṛtaḥ || 2.257 ||**

 

smṛta iti vacanāl lābhenāpi vikrayo dharma iti jñāyate || 257 ||

 

_lābhakalpanā tu vaṇijāṃ kiṃ yadṛcchayaiva | nety ucyate | kathaṃ tarhi |_

 

                    	**svadeśapaṇye tu śataṃ vaṇig gṛhṇīta pañcakam |**

**              	daśakaṃ pāradeśye tu yaḥ sadyaḥ krayavikrayī || 2.258 ||**

 

yo yasya paṇyasya sadyaḥ krayavikrayī, sa tasya daśakaṃ pañcakaṃ vā gṛhṇīyād ity arthaḥ || 258 ||

 

_rājñā tu kiṃ yadṛcchayaivārghaḥ sthāpyaḥ | nety āha |_

 

                    	**paṇyasyopari saṃsthāpya vyayaṃ paṇyasamudbhavam |**

**              	argho 'nugrahakṛt kāryaḥ kretur vikretur eva ca || 2.259 ||**

 

 

 

**iti sāhasaprakaraṇam |**

** **

**atha vikrīyāsaṃpradānaprakaraṇam** |

 

 

_krayavikrayaprasaṅgād vikrīyāsaṃpradānam idānīm āha |_

 

**              	gṛhītamūlyaṃ yaḥ paṇyaṃ kretur naiva prayacchati |**

**              	sodayaṃ tasya dāpyo 'sau diglābhaṃ vā diśāṃ gate || 2.260 ||**

 

yadi dattvānyathā mūlyaṃ kretā paṇyaṃ na gṛhṇīyāt, tadā kretur eva doṣaḥ | anyathā tu vikretur evety abhiprāyaḥ || 260 ||

 

_gṛhitamūlye tu |_

 

                    	**rājadaivopaghātena paṇye doṣam upāgate |**

**              	hānir vikretur evāsau yācitasyāprayacchataḥ || 2.261 ||**

 

"mamedaṃ paṇyam arpaya" ity evaṃ yācitasyāpy anarpayato yas tatrāpacayaḥ, sa vikretur evety uktam | yadi tu rājakṛtād vyāsedhād daivikād vā parjanyādidoṣāt paṇyaṃ doṣavat syāt, tatra yā mūlyahāniḥ, sā vikretur evety avaseyam || 261 ||

 

_kretrā tūtsaṅkalitam eva hi |_

 

**              	anyahaste tu vikrītaṃ duṣṭaṃ vāduṣṭavad yadi |**

**              	vikrīyate damas tatra tanmūlyād dviguṇo bhavet || 2.262 ||**

 

yas tv anyatra kretrā tūtsaṅkalitam eva vikrītam api punar vikrīṇīyād, aduṣṭam iti vā kṛtvā duṣṭam api, tasya dravyamūlyād dviguṇo daṇḍaḥ | kretuś ca dravyamūlyaṃ vā pratyarpaṇīyam | spaṣṭam anyat || 262 ||

 

_idānīṃ krayavikrayānuśayasya viṣayaṃ pradarśayati |_

 

                    	**kṣayaṃ vṛddhiṃ ca vaṇijā paṇyānāṃ tu vijānatā |**

**              	krītvā nānuśayaḥ kāryaḥ kurvan ṣaḍbhāgadaṇḍabhāk || 2.263 ||**

 

candragatyādivaśena paṇyānām arghahānir vṛddhir vā bhavati | tac caivaṃ vijānatā vaṇijā kṣayaṃ vṛddhiṃ vā nirūpyāvirodhe sati krītvā vikrīya vā nānuśayaḥ kāryaḥ | kurvato vā paṇyamūlyaṣaḍbhāgo rājadaṇḍaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 263 ||

 

 

**iti vikrīyāsaṃpradānaprakaraṇam |**

** **

**atha saṃbhūyasamutthānaprakaraṇam** |

 

_vāṇijyaprasaṅgāt saṃbhūyotthānam āha |_

 

                    	**samavāyena vaṇijāṃ lābhārthaṃ karma kurvatām |**

**              	lābhālābhau yathādravaṃ yathā vā saṃvidākṛtā || 2.264 ||**

 

sarvaṃ lābham ekīkṛtya yathādravyaṃ vibhāgaḥ kāryaḥ | lābhasya mūlyānusāritvāt karmāpekṣayā vā yathā saṃvit paribhāṣā anyonyam ākṛtā maryādā kṛtety arthaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 264 ||

 

_evaṃ kṛtasamayānāṃ vyavahārāpetaṃ svācchandyāt |_

 

                    	**pratiṣiddham anādiṣṭaṃ pramādād yac ca nāśitam |**

**              	sa tad dadyād viplavāc ca rakṣitā daśamāṃśabhāk || 2.265 ||**

 

pratiṣiddham anādiṣṭam anyair vaṇigbhir ananuṣṭhitam iti śeṣaḥ | kiṃ ca pramādād yac ca nāśitaṃ, sa tad dadyāt | asyānapekṣayaiva | viplavāt tu rakṣitā daśamāṃśabhāg rakṣitadravyād rakṣitā lābhād daśamāṃśaṃ prāpnuyād ity artham || 265 ||

 

_idānīṃ rājabhāvyam nirūpayati |_

 

                    	**arghaprakṣepaṇāc chulkaṃ viṃśadbhāgaṃ nṛpo haret |**

**              	vyāsiddhaṃ rājayogyaṃ ca vikrītaṃ rājagāmi tat || 2.266 ||**

 

yo 'rgho rājñā prakṣiptaḥ sthāpitaḥ, tata evārghasyāpanād vikrītānāṃ viṃśatibhāgo rājabhāvyaḥ śuklaḥ kretṛvikretṛbhyām ubhābhyām anyonyam icchayānyatareṇa vā deyaḥ | yac ca rājñā vyāsiddhaṃ rājayogyaṃ ca hastyādidravyaṃ rājany anāvedyānākhyāya vikrītaṃ tad rājagāmy eva sarvam ity avaseyam || 266 ||

 

_rājabhāvyaśulkanimittaṃ ca paṇyadravyādeḥ  |_

 

                    	**mithyā vadan parīmāṇaṃ śulkasthānād apākraman |**

**              	dāpyas tv aṣṭaguṇaṃ yaś ca sa vyājakrayavikrayī || 2.267 ||**

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">atha kiṃ</span> saṃbhūya vyavaharatām anyataravipattau tadīyaṃ dravyam anyair vaṇigbhir grahītavyam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nety</span> ucyate | kiṃ tarhi |_

 

                    	**deśāntaragate prete dravyaṃ dāyādabāndhavāḥ|**

**              	jñātayo vā hareyus tad āgatais tair vinā nṛpaḥ || 2.268 ||**

 

deśāntaragate prete āyavyayaviśuddhaṃ tadīyam aṃśaṃ yathāvibhajamānaṃ rikthino 'nye gṛhṇīyuḥ, tadabhāve tu rājā gṛhṇīyāt | kim arthaṃ punar idam ucyate, ṛṇadāne hi pratiṣedhāt | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "prātibhāvyavaṇikśulkamadyadyūtadaṇḍā na putrān adhyāvaheyuḥ" iti (GDh 12.41) | ṛṇavac ca dhanasaṃbandho 'pīti tadabhāktvam eva yuktam ity āśaṅkānivṛttyartham etat | spaṣṭam anyat || 268 ||

 

_saṃbhūya ca pravṛttānāṃ svāmikarmakarādīnām anyonyam ayaṃ vidhiḥ |_

 

                    	**jihmaṃ tyajeyur nirlābham aśakto 'nyena kārayet |**

**              	anena vidhinā khyātam ṛtvikkarṣakakarmiṇām || 2.269 ||**

 

anyonyaṃ svāmikarmakarasāmājikādayo jihmaṃ kuṭilaṃ vyabhicāriṇaṃ tyajeyuḥ, tathā lābhaśūnyam | pravṛttas tu svayam aśakto 'py anyenāvirodhinā svakāryaṃ sāmājikaṃ kārayet | yo 'yaṃ saṃbhūyotthāne vidhir uktaḥ, anenaiva vidhinā nirūpitam ṛtvigādyanuṣṭhānam api draṣṭavyam | smṛtyantarāt tu vaiśeṣikartvigādyanuṣṭhānaprapañco 'nveṣṭavyaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 269 ||

 

 

**iti saṃbhūyasamutthānaprakraṇam |**

** **

**atha steyaprakaraṇam |**

 

_yadi punaḥ pratyekaṃ pratigrahādinā saṃbhūyārtvijyādinā vā kṛcchrārjitaṃ dravyaṃ kaścid apahṛtya gacchet sa kathaṃ jñātavyaḥ | jñātasya vā kiṃ tasya kartavyam ity apekṣite stenasvarūpanirūpaṇāyāha |_

 

                    	**grāhakair gṛhyate coro loptreṇātha padena vā |**

**              	pūrvakarmāparādhād vā tathaivāśuddhavāsakaḥ || 2.270 ||**

 

apahṛtadravyasvāmibhiś coratvapratipādanena grāhakair gṛhyate coraḥ | atha vā loptreṇa apahṛtadravyeṇa, apaharaṇadeśād vā nipuṇair unnīyamānena padena, yad vā pūrvakarmaṇā saṃbhāvitacauryāparādhāt, tathānyair api smṛtyantaroktacoratvapratipādakair vakṣyamāṇair aśuddhavāsakādibhiḥ | aśuddho vāso yasyāsāv aśuddhavāsakaḥ kutastyo 'yam ity avijñāyamāno lubdhaveśyādigṛhanivāsī || 270 ||

 

_loptrādivac ca |_

 

                    	**anye 'pi śaṅkayā grāhyā jātināmādinihnavaiḥ |**

**              	dyūtastrīpānasaktāś ca śuṣkabhinnamukhasvarāḥ || 2.271 ||**

**              	paradravyagṛhāṇā ca pṛcchakā gūḍhacāriṇaḥ |**

**              	nirāyā vyayavantaś ca vinaṣṭadravyavikrayāḥ || 2.272 ||**

 

pramāṇāntarmūlatvād asyāḥ smṛtes tadanusāreṇaiva vivicya vyākhyā kāryā | padārthās tu nigadoktā eva || 271–272 ||

 

_uktanyāyānusāreṇa ca |_

 

                    	**gṛhītaḥ śaṅkayā caurye nātmānaṃ ced viśodhayet |**

**              	dāpayitvā hṛtaṃ dravyaṃ coradaṇḍena daṇḍayet || 2.273 ||**

 

smṛtyantarānusāreṇa yathārhaṃ daṇḍakalpanā || 273 ||

 

_loptrādibhiś caurye spaṣṭīkṛte |_

 

                    	**coraṃ pradāpyāpahṛtaṃ ghātayed vividhair vadhaiḥ |**

 

smṛtyantaroktadaṇḍaiḥ śārīraiś ca netrādyuddhāraṇalakṣaṇaiḥ prāṇaharaṇaśūlāropaṇādibhiś cety abhiprāyaḥ |

 

_evam abrāhmaṇam | brāhmaṇaṃ tu kathaṃ kuryāt |_

 

                    	**sacihnaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ kṛtvā svarāṣṭrād vipravāsayet || 2.274 ||**

 

sacihnaṃ śvapadādyaṅkitam | spaṣṭam anyat || 274 ||

 

_prayatnenānviṣyamāṇaghātakacorādyanupalabdhau tu katham iti |_

 

**              	ghātitāpahṛte doṣo grāmabhartur anirgate |**

 

padādau prayātacihna iti śeṣaḥ |

 

                    	**vivītabhartus tu pathi**

 

vivītādyupakaṇṭha iti śeṣaḥ | tuśabdo 'nyasyāpi samarthasya yathāsaṃnidhānaṃ doṣavattvajñāpanārthaḥ |

 

                                            	**     	coroddhartur avītake || 2.275 ||**

 

pūrvoktādyabhāve coroddhartur eva doṣaḥ | sarvathā cāpahṛtaṃ dravyaṃ prayatnenānviṣya rājñā labdhavyam ity abhiprāyaḥ | yad vā apahṛte dravye ghātite ca sadravyake core dravyānupalabdhau kasya doṣa ity apekṣite grāmabhartur anirgata ityādi samānam || 275 ||

 

_asaṃnihite tu grāmabhartari |_

 

                    	**svasīmni dadyād grāmas tu padaṃ vā yatra gacchati |**

**              	pañcagrāmī bahiḥ kṛṣṭād daśagrāmy api vā tathā || 2.276 ||**

 

svaśabdo dhanajñātyarthaḥ | yatra dvipadacatuṣpadādyanavarataṃ saṃcarati, sā svasīmā | spaṣṭam anyat || 276 ||

 

_corādiviśeṣe tu vadhaprakāram āha |_

 

                    	**vandigrāhāṃs tathā vājikuñjarāṇāṃ ca hāriṇaḥ |**

**              	prasahyaghātinaś caiva śūlam āropayen narān || 2.277 ||**

 

tathāśabdaḥ prakārārthaḥ | naravacanam abrāhmaṇārtham | spaṣṭam anyat || 277 ||

 

_dravyādiviśeṣāpekṣayā tu |_

** **

**              	utkṣepakagranthibhedau karasaṃdaṃśahīnakau |**

**              	kāryau dvitīye 'parādhe karapādaikahīnakau || 2.278 ||**

 

utkṣepakaḥ paṭākṣepakaḥ | granthibhedako granthibhettā | tāv ubhāv api karasaṃdaṃśahīnau prathame 'parādhe kāryau | karasaṃdaṃśo 'ṅgulayaḥ, taddhīnau yad vā karasaṃpuṭaḥ karasaṃdaṃśaḥ, taddhīnau | anyatarahastacchedanam ity arthaḥ | dvitīye 'parādhe tv eko hastaḥ pādaś ca | spaṣṭam anyat || 278||

 

_yaś cāyam uktaḥ śārīro daṇḍaḥ, yaś ca smṛtyantarokto dhanadaṇḍaḥ, tatra sarvatra sādhāraṇo 'yaṃ nyāyabījasaṃkṣepaḥ |_

 

                    	**kṣudramadhyamahādravyaharaṇe sārato damaḥ |**

**              	deśakālavayaḥśakti saṃcintyaṃ daṇḍakarmaṇi || 2.279 ||**

 

anyatrāpīti śeṣaḥ || 279 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**bhaktāvakāśāgnyudakamantropakaraṇavyayān |**

**              	dattvā corasya hantur vā jānato daṇḍa uttamaḥ || 2.280 ||**

 

coro 'yaṃ sāhasiko vā prasahya hantīty evaṃ jānataś corasāhasikayor bhaktādidānaṃ kurvato daṇḍa uttamasāhasaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 280 ||

 

_strīṣv aduṣṭāsu corayitum |_

 

                    	**śastrāvapāte garbhasya pātane cottamo damaḥ |**

**              	uttamo vādhamo vāpi puruṣaḥ strīpramāpaṇe || 2.281 ||**

 

brāhmaṇastrīśastrāvapatane garbhasya cāviśeṣeṇa vyāpattāv uttamo daṇḍaḥ kāryaḥ, vadha ity arthaḥ | uttamo vā brāhmaṇaḥ, adhamo vā śūdrādiḥ, apiśabdān madhyamo 'pi kṣatriyādiḥ puruṣaḥ strīpramāpaṇe vadhya evety abhiprāyaḥ | tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ |

                    	garbhasya pātane steno brāhmaṇyāṃ śastrapātane |

                    	aduṣṭāṃ yoṣitaṃ hatvā hantavyo brāhmaṇo 'pi hi || iti (KSm 806) || 281 ||

 

_steyavyatirekeṇāpi tu |_

 

                    	**viṣapradāṃ striyaṃ caiva puruṣaghnīm agarbhiṇīm |**

**              	setubhedakarīṃ cāpsu śilāṃ baddhvā praveśayet || 2.282 ||**

 

auṣadhādivyājena viṣapradāṃ striyam | caśabdāt puruṣaṃ ca | evakāro 'nyatra strīvadhābhāvajñāpanārthaḥ | vadhābhāve 'pi viṣādimṛtyunimittaprayoktrī hantavyety arthaḥ | puruṣaghnīṃ sāhasikaparapuruṣaprasaṅgātiśayāt puruṣamāraṇanimittabhūtām | jñātyādibhayāc ca garbhaṃ pātayitvāgarbhiṇy aham iti yā vadati (?), tām agarbhiṇīm āhuḥ | tathā ca smṛtyantaram |

                    	yā pātayitvā svaṃ garbhaṃ brūyād aham agarbhiṇī |

                    	tām apsu prakṣiped rājā jāraiś ca naramāriṇīm || iti |

setuḥ kulyāsaṃkramaḥ, maryādā vā | spaṣṭam anyat || 282 ||

 

_bhartrādīnāṃ tu viṣapradānādau vadhaprakāram āha |_

 

                    	**viṣāgnidāṃ patigurunijāpatyapramāpaṇīm |**

**              	vikarṇakaranāsoṣṭhīṃ kṛtvā gobhiḥ pramāpayet || 2.283 ||**

 

guruḥ śvaśurādiḥ | nijā bhrātrādayaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 283 ||

 

_viṣāgnidānena ca vadhasiddhāv ayaṃ māraṇavidhiḥ, bhartrādīnāṃ tv idānīṃ sāmānyenāvijñātakartṛkavadhaniṣpattāv anveṣaṇaprakāram āha |_

 

                    	**avijñātahatasyāśu kalahaṃ sutabāndhavāḥ |**

**              	praṣṭavyā yoṣito vāsya parapuṃsi ratāḥ pṛthak || 2.284 ||**

 

hantur avijñāne 'nantaram eva śīghraṃ hatasya putrāḥ svajanāś ca praṣṭavyāḥ kalahaṃ kena sahāsya kalaho bhūtapūrvaḥ | sākṣāraḥ ka enaṃ pratītyarthaḥ | yoṣitaś cāsya bhāryāḥ kiṃ kvāpi parapuruṣe saktā iti | evaṃ pṛthak pṛthag jñātayaḥ praṣṭavyāḥ | tatprātiveśyādau vā yāḥ parapuṃsi ratā yoṣitaḥ pṛthak ekaikaśaḥ praṣṭavyāḥ | tadīyabhāryā eva vā sapatnyaḥ parapuruṣaprasaktim anyonyaṃ praṣṭavyāḥ | pramāṇāntaramūlatvād asyārthasya tadanusāryanveṣaṇaṃ kāryam || 284 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**strīvṛttidravyakāmo vā kena vāyaṃ gataḥ saha |**

**              	mṛtyudeśasamāsannaṃ pṛcched vāpi janaṃ śanaiḥ || 2.285 ||**

 

stryādikāmo vāsya kīdṛśa ity evaṃ ca putrādayaḥ praṣṭavyāḥ | kim asya kvacit parastrīprasaṅga āsīt | kā vāsya vṛttiḥ | kiṃ vāsya dravyam abhipretaṃ, śarīralagnaṃ vā | kena vā sahāyaṃ gṛhān nirgataḥ | kena vāsya maitram | anekavidhatvād duṣṭajanacetasāṃ sarvam evamādi praṣṭavyam | yatra vāsau vyāpātitaḥ, taṃ deśam āsanno gopālādijanaḥ śanaiḥ praṣṭavyaḥ | ko 'tra tadānīṃ bhavadbhir dṛṣṭa ityevam anumānakuśalatayā ghātako 'nveṣṭavyaḥ | ghātakaś cātrodāharaṇārthaḥ | sarveṣām eva tv akāryakāriṇām evam anveṣaṇaprakāra ity avaseyam || 285 ||

 

_anviṣya ghātakās tathā vakṣyamāṇāś ca |_

 

                    	**kṣetraveśmagrāmavanavivītādeś ca dāhakāḥ |**

**              	rājapatnyabhigāmī ca dagdhavyās tu kaṭāgninā || 2.286 ||**

 

caśabdaḥ śrotriyādistryarthaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 286 ||

 

 

**iti steyaprakaraṇam |**

** **

**atha strīsaṃgrahaṇaprakaraṇam |**

 

_rājapatnyabhigamanaprasaṅgāt paraparigṛhītastrīmātrāśrayaṃ saṅgrahaṇavidhim āha |_

 

**              	pumān saṃgrahaṇe grāhyaḥ keśākeśi parastriyāḥ |**

**              	sādyair vā kāmajaiś cihnaiḥ pratipattau dvayos tathā || 2.287 ||**

 

puṃgrahaṇaṃ puṃso damātirekārtham | keśākeśigrahaṇaṃ yantrārūḍhagrahaṇārtham | sādyair vā kāmajair nakhadantakṣatādibhir cihnaiḥ, dvayor eva vā saṃpratipattau || 287 ||

 

_anumānakauśalāt prayakṣopalambhanād vā spaṣṭīkṛte saṃgrahaṇe |_

 

                    	**sajātāv uttamo daṇḍa ānulomye tu madhyamaḥ |**

**              	prātilomye vadhaḥ puṃsāṃ strīṇāṃ nāsādikṛntanam || 2.288 ||**

 

ānulomyādiviśeṣe smṛtyantrānusārād dhanadaṇḍavadhadaṇḍayor yathārhaṃ vyavasthā kalpanīyā | udāharaṇārthaṃ caitad ācāryeṇoktam ity avaseyam | ṛjv anyat || 288 ||

 

_anyatarānicchāyāṃ tu pumān yoṣid vā |_

 

                    	**nīvīstanaprāvaraṇanābhikeśāvamarśanam |**

**              	adeśakālasaṃbhāṣāṃ sahāvasthānam eva ca || 2.289 ||**

                    	**strī niṣiddhā śataṃ daṇḍyā kurvatī dviśataṃ pumān |**

**              	aniṣedhe tayor daṇḍo yathā saṃgrahaṇe tathā || 2.290 ||**

 

nīvyādisparśanādeśakālasaṃbhāṣaṇasahāvasthānādi puṃśā nivāritā strī kurvatī śatam daṇḍyā | striyā nivāritaḥ pumān dviśataṃ daṇḍyaḥ | dvayor api tv anyonyam icchayā saṃgrahaṇokta eva daṇḍaḥ | nīvī raśanāparivartikādeśaḥ | rahovivakṣayā saṃbhāṣaṇam adeśakālasaṃbhāṣaṇam | spaṣṭam anyat || 289–90 ||

 

_saṃgrahaṇaprāyatvāt kanyāharaṇam api prasaṅgād āha |_

 

                    	**alaṃkṛtāṃ haran kanyām uttamaṃ tv anyathādhamam |**

**              	daṇḍaṃ dadyāt savarṇas tu prātilomye vadhaḥ smṛtaḥ || 2.291 ||**

 

alaṃkṛtopakḷptavivāhā | spaṣṭam anyat || 291 ||

 

_kanyāsv eva |_

 

                    	**sakāmāsv anulomāsu na doṣas tv anyathādhamaḥ |**

**              	dūṣaṇe tu karaccheda uttamāyāṃ vadhas tathā || 2.292 ||**

 

icchantīṣu kanyāsu savarṇāsv anulomāsu vā pradūṣyāpahṛtāsu na doṣaḥ, gāndharvavivāhaviṣayatvāt | yas tv analaṃkṛtāpaharaṇe 'dhamo daṇḍaḥ, so 'nyathā niṣkāmāsv ity arthaḥ | dūṣaṇe tu kanyābhigamane karacchedaḥ, anicchāyām eva | anyathā tv aṅgulivicchedaḥ smṛtyantarānusārāt | prātilomyena tu kanyādūṣaṇe vadha eva | tathāśabdaḥ smṛtyantaroktaśūlārohaṇādiprakārārthaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 292 ||

 

_dūṣayitur daṇḍa uktaḥ | dūṣyā tu kanyā |_

 

                 	**śataṃ strī dūṣaṇe dāpyā dve tu mithyābhiśaṃsitā |**

**            	paśūn gacchan śataṃ dāpyo hīnastrīṃ gāṃ ca madhyamam || 2.293 ||**

 

strītvenopagamya dūṣitā kanyā strīty uktā | sā dūṣaṇe kṛte sataṃ daṇḍyā | yadi tv aduṣṭām eva dūṣiteyam iti brūyāt, tato mithābhiśaṃsitā dve śate daṇḍyaḥ | govyatiriktāśvādipaśugamane śataṃ daṇḍyaḥ | hīnāṃ tv anulomāṃ striyaṃ gāṃ ca gacchato madhyamo daṇḍaḥ | hīnastrīvacanaṃ gavādiṣv api strīvad daṇḍadānadṛṣṭāntatvena | anyathā tu prāg evoktatvāt punaruktataiva syāt | tasmāt paśvādiṣv api strīṣv iva gantur daṇḍādikalpanaṃ parigrahaviśeṣāśrayaṃ yojyam || 293 ||

 

_parigrahānusāreṇaiva ca |_

 

                    	**avaruddhāsu dāsīṣu bhujiṣyāsu tathaiva ca |**

**              	gamyāsv api pumān dāpyaḥ pañcāśatpaṇikaṃ damam || 2.294 ||**

 

bhujiṣyā karmakāriṇyo dāsyaḥ | tāsv api svāmikarmaparihāpaṇenākramy gacchato daṇḍaḥ | gamyāsv api śūdrādīnām uparatabhartṛkāsu bhrātṛbhāryāsu puṣpāñjalyādyanupanītāsu | puṃvacanam avaruddhādistrīṇām ardhadaṇḍyatvajñāpanārtham || 294 ||

 

_adattvaiva śulkam |_

 

                    	**prasahya dāsyabhigame daṇḍo daśapaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ |**

**              	bahūnāṃ yady akāmāsau dvirdvādaśapaṇaḥ pṛthak || 2.295 ||**

 

akāmābhigamane bahūnām ekasyām eva dāsyāṃ pratyekaṃ caturviṃśatipaṇo daṇḍaḥ || 295 ||

 

_aviśeṣeṇaiva tu |_

 

                    	**ayonau gacchato yoṣāṃ puruṣaṃ cābhimehataḥ |**

**              	dvirdvādaśapaṇo daṇḍas tathā pravrajitāgame || 2.296 ||**

 

āsyapādādau puruṣasya śiśnaprakṣepaṇaṃ puruṣamehanam | vyabhicāriṇītvād jñātibhis tyaktā strī pravrajitā | spaṣṭam anyat || 296 ||

 

_kāmatas tu traivarṇikānām |_

 

                    	**antyābhigamane tv aṅkyaḥ kabandhena pravāsayet |**

**              	śūdras tathāṅkhya eva syād antyasyāryāgame vadhaḥ || 2.297 ||**

 

antyaśabdo 'yaṃ śūdrān nikṛṣṭāpaśadavacanaḥ | tām antyām apaśadastriyaṃ gacchaṃs traivarṇikaḥ kabandhenāṅkayitvā svarāṣṭrād bahiṣkāryaḥ | śūdras tathāṅkya eva syāt, na bahiṣkāryaḥ | prāyaścittaṃ tv akurvataḥ kāmato vābhyāsād etad draṣṭavyam | tataś ca śūdrasyāpravāsanaṃ dāsatvajñāpanārtham | dāsīkṛtya ca prāyaścittaṃ kārayitavyam | antyasya tv apaśadasya śūdrādyāryastryabhigame vadha eva | anayā diśā saṃgrahaṇasvarūpaparijñānopāyadaṇḍaprapañcaḥ kāryaḥ || 297 ||

 

 

**iti strīsaṃgrahaṇaprakaraṇam |**

** **

**atha prakīrṇakaprakaraṇam |**

 

_yat pūrvaprakaraṇeṣv anuktaṃ tat pūrvanirṇītavyavahāraparipūraṇāyedānīm āha |_

 

                    	**nyūnam abhyadhikaṃ vāpi likhed yo rājaśāsanam |**

**              	pāradārikacorau vā muñcato daṇḍa uttamaḥ || 2.298 ||**

 

śāsanavacanaṃ sarvalekhyalakṣaṇārtham | lekhayitā lekhako vā nyūnātiriktādilekhyadoṣakartā, rakṣaṇārpitaṃ pāradārikādikaṃ moktukāma uttamasāhasaṃ daṇḍyaḥ || 298 ||

 

_yo rājaprasādādyavaṣṭambhāt prasahya sāhasikatvena |_

 

        	**abhakṣyair dūṣayan vipraṃ daṇḍya uttamasāhasam |**

**     	kṣatriyaṃ madhyamaṃ vaiśyaṃ prathamaṃ śūdram ardhikam || 2.299 ||**

 

upapatanīyābhakṣyair laśunādibhir ayaṃ daṇḍo 'vaseyaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 299 ||

 

_pracchannatāskaryayogāt tu |_

 

                    	**kūṭasvarṇavyavahārī vimāṃsasya ca vikrayī |**

**              	tryaṅgahīnās tu kartavyā dāpyāś cottamasāhasam || 2.300 ||**

 

dhūpitarañcitādi kūṭasvarṇam | śvasṛgālādiprabhavaṃ vimāṃsam | tadviśeṣāpekṣayaiva dhanadaṇḍaḥ | tryaṅgahīnatvaṃ ca vyastasamastatayā yojyam | dvau hastāv ekaś ca pādas tryaṅgāni | spaṣṭam anyat || 300 ||

 

_akāmatas tu pravṛttatvāt |_

 

                    	**catuṣpādakṛte doṣo nāpehīti prabhāṣataḥ |**

**              	kāṣṭhaloṣṭeṣupāṣāṇabāhuyuddhakṛte tathā || 2.301 ||**

 

"duṣṭo 'yaṃ balīvardādiḥ, apasarpaṇāya tvaryatām" ityevaṃvādinaḥ svāminaś catuṣpādakṛte 'parādhe na doṣaḥ | evam eva cāsyāsāv arthaḥ | kāṣṭhādi kṣipator bāhuyuddhena vā saṃrabdhayoḥ | tathāśabdād anabhikruṣṭe sadoṣataiveti gamyate || 301 ||

 

_anabhipretatvād eva ca |_

 

                    	**chinnanāsyena yānena tathā bhagnayugena ca |**

**              	paścāc caivāpasaratā hiṃsite svāmy adoṣabhāk || 2.302 ||**

 

nastādirahitabalīvardādiyuktaṃ chinnanāsyam | tathāśabdaḥ prakārārthaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 302 ||

 

_hiṃsataḥ parigṛhītasya balīvardādeḥ |_

 

                    	**śakto 'py amokṣayan svāmī śṛṅgiṇo daṃṣṭriṇas tathā |**

**              	prathamaṃ sāhasaṃ dāpyo vikruṣṭe dviguṇaṃ tathā || 2.303 ||**

 

tathāśabdo 'parādhaviśeṣānusāreṇa daṇḍaviśeṣakalpanāpratipattyarthaḥ | prasiddham anyat || 303 ||

 

_lobhādinā pracchannaṃ yadi tu |_

 

                    	**coraṃ corety ati vadan dāpyaḥ pañcaśataṃ damam |**

**              	upajīvya dhanaṃ muñcaṃs tad evāṣṭaguṇīkṛtam || 2.304 ||**

 

coram atikramyācoram evānyaṃ coreti vadataḥ pañcaśato damaḥ | dravyam upajīvya muñcatas tad evopabhuktaṃ dravyam aṣṭaguṇaṃ daṇḍaṃ cety uktam | ṛjv anyat || 304 ||

 

_prasahyakāritayā tu |_

 

                    	**rājño 'niṣṭapravaktāraṃ tasyaivākrośakaṃ tathā |**

**              	tanmantrasya ca bhettāraṃ chittvā jihvāṃ pravāsayet || 2.305 ||**

 

_sāhasikatayaiva tu |_

** **

**              	mṛtāṅgalagnavikretur guros tāḍayitus tathā |**

**              	rājaśayyāsanāroḍhur daṇḍo madhyamasāhasaḥ || 2.306 ||**

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**dvinetrabhedino rājadviṣṭādeśakṛtas tathā |**

**              	vipratvena ca śūdrasya jīvato 'ṣṭaśato damaḥ || 2.307 ||**

 

dvinetragrahaṇaṃ kṛtsnendriyalakṣaṇārtham | etac ca paśuviṣayaṃ draṣṭavyam | rājā dviṣṭo yasya sa rājadviṣṭaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 307 ||

 

_yaś cāyaṃ vyavahāramārga uktaḥ, tatra sarvasminn evāyaṃ rājāśrayaḥ sādhāraṇo vidhiḥ |_

 

**                    	durdṛṣṭaṃ tu punar dṛṣṭvā vyavahāraṃ nṛpeṇa tu |**

**              	sabhyāḥ sajayino daṇḍyā vivādadviguṇaṃ pṛthak || 2.308 ||**

 

prāg asyoktatvāt punarārambho rājñaḥ svayaṃ draṣṭṛtvena prayatnātirekārthaḥ || 308 ||

 

_yathā vijito daṇḍyo mithyābhidhānāt, tathaiva |_

 

                    	**yo manyetājito 'smīti nyāyenāpi parājitaḥ|**

**              	tam āgataṃ punar jitvā dāpayed dviguṇaṃ damam || 2.309 ||**

 

spaṣṭārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 309 ||

 

_ṛṇādānādyakhilavyavahārasaṃbandhitayā yathāsthānaṃ yuktyāgamānusāreṇa prāpto 'pi hi |_

 

                    	**rājñā nyāyena yo daṇḍo 'gṛhīto varuṇāya tam |**

**              	nivedya dadyād viprebhyaḥ svayaṃ triṃśadguṇīkṛtam || 2.310 ||**

 

rājñā nyāyena prāpto 'pi hi yo daṇḍaḥ snehādinā kathaṃcid agṛhītaḥ, taṃ svayam eva triṃśadguṇīkṛtya, udakasaṃnidhau varuṇāya nivedya varuṇam uddiśyety arthaḥ | tato viprebhyaḥ prāguktadānavidhyanusāreṇa (deyam? dadyāt) | codanāmūlatvāc cāsyāḥ smṛter akaraṇe 'nyathākaraṇe vā pratyāvaya ityevaṃ vyākhyeyam | anyāyena vā yo daṇḍo rājñā gṛhītaḥ, taṃ svayam evānyenāśakyo 'pi kārayituṃ triṃśadguṇaṃ varuṇāya nivedya viprebhyo dadyād iti | yad vā nyāyenaiva rājñā yo daṇḍo gṛhītaḥ, tam eva sāmarthyāt svayam eva triṃśadguṇīkṛtaṃ viprebhyo dadyād it | sarvaṃ caitat śrutismṛtyanusārān nyāyyam evety avaseyam iti || 310 ||

 

                    	prathamodayānurakto nikhilam alaṃ maṇḍalaṃ nijaṃ kṛtvā |

                    	pālayati satatam urvīm atibalavān eṣa nṛpasavitā ||

                    	iti nirastanijavyasanaklamaḥ kṛtavipakṣacaritraviparyayaḥ |

                    	nṛpatir āśu samuddhṛtakaṇṭako harir iveṣṭatamāyatanaṃ sriyaḥ ||

 

**iti paramabhaṭṭārakayājñavalkyapraṇīte dharmaśāstre**

**viśvarūpakṛtavivaraṇabālakrīḍāyāṃ**

**dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ ||**

** **

 

 



 

 

**prāyaścittādhyāya**

 

**athāśaucaprakaraṇam |**

 

 

_śriyām avyabhicaritanirvyājaprāptihetutayā kaṇṭakoddharaṇaṃ rājadharmatvenānekadhā vyavahāraprakaraṇe viprakīrṇatayoktam | sarvavarṇānāṃ cāśramadvayasādhāraṇo dharma uktaḥ | athedānīm āśramāntaraṃ prasaktam apy utkṛṣya pūrvāśramaśeṣabhūtāṃ pretaśuddhim eva tāvat prastauti | kasmāt punaḥ prasaktam apy āśramāntarābhidhānam utkṛṣyate | varṇamātrasaṃbandhitayāpy ucyamānā pretakriyā tadvyatirekeṇaiva yathā syāt, pratipattyantaraṃ ca taccharīrasyāraṇyanayanādi | yathoktam: "etad vai paramaṃ tapo yat pretam araṇyaṃ nayanti" iti _(BāU 5.11.1)_ | tad adhunā vayo'vasthāviśeṣeṇaiva tāvat pretakriyām āha |_

 

**              	ūnadvivarṣaṃ nikhanen na kuryād udakaṃ tataḥ |**

**              	ā śmaśānād anuvrajya itaro jñātibhir mṛtaḥ || 3.1 ||**

 

ūnadvivārṣiko mṛtaḥ khātvā garte nikhātavyaḥ | na dāhādyudakakriyā kāryā | yataś codakakriyānivṛttis tata eva jñātibhir nānugantavya ity arthaḥ | itaras tūrdhvaṃ varṣadvayād ā śmaśānād anugantavyaḥ | dāhādyudakariyā tasya kāryety arthaḥ | yat tu svāyaṃbhuvam,

                    	ūnadvivārṣikaṃ pretaṃ nidadhyur bāndhavā bahiḥ |

                    	alaṃkṛtya śucau bhūmāv sthisaṃcayanād ṛte ||

                    	nāsa kāryo 'gnisaṃskāro nāpi kāryodakakriyā |

(nivṛttis tata eva jñatibhiḥ ?)

                    	araṇye kāṣṭhavat tyaktvā kṣapeyus tryaham eva tu || iti | (MDh 5.68)

tad āśaucakālaviśeṣavidhānārtham | etadanusārāc ca nidadhyur iti nikhananam eva tatrābhipretam | yat punas tatraivoktam,

                    	nātrivarṣasya kartavyā bāndhavair udakakriyā |

                    	jātadantasya vā kuryur nāmni vāpi kṛte sati || (MDh 5.70)

iti, tad etad vaikalpikatvena kṛtanāmakadehadāhādividhānaparatayaivāvaseyam | pāraskarīyaṃ tu "dvivarṣe prete mātāpitror evāśaucam" (PārG 3.10.2) iti, tad anugamanāṅgatvād aṅgasparśābhiprāyaṃ draṣṭavyam | yat tu svāyambhuve,

                    	nṛṇām akṛtacaulānām aśuddhir naiśikī smṛtā | (MDh 5.67)

iti, tad ūrdhvaṃ nāmakaraṇāt prāk saṃvatsarād vijñeyam | paratas tu kṛtacaulasyākṛtacaulasya vā trirātram eva prāg upanayanāt | tathā coktam |

                    	nirvṛttacaulakānāṃ tu trirātrāc chuddhir iṣyate | iti | (MDh 5.67)

vākyadvayārambhas tu vyavasthayā dāhavikalpārthaḥ | nāmakaraṇāc cordhvaṃ varṣadvayaṃ dāhavikalpaḥ | paratas tu naiyamiko dāhaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 1||

 

_yasya ca dāhādhikāraḥ |_

 

**              	yamasūktaṃ tathā gāthā japadbhir laukikāgninā |**

**              	sa dagdhavya upetaś ced āhitāgnyāvṛtārthavat || 3.2 ||**

 

yamadevatyaṃ sūktaṃ, tathā yamadevatyā gāthā ekaśo brāhmaṇapaṭhitāḥ, tadubhayaṃ japadbhir jñātibhiḥ | sa dāhādhikṛtaḥ | itaro laukikāgninā dagdhavyaḥ | upetaḥ upanītaḥ | sa cāhitāgnisaṃbaddhetikartavyatayā | arthavad anarthaluptatayā | yathāsambhavaṃ dagdhavyaḥ | smṛtyantarāt tu mantranivṛttiḥ | śālāgninā ca vidyamānatve dāhaḥ || 2 ||

 

_evaṃ ca yathādhikāraṃ dagdhvā tataḥ |_

 

                    	**saptamād daśamād vāpi jñātayo 'bhyavayanty apaḥ |**

**              	apa naḥ śośucad agham anena pitṛdiṅmukhāḥ || 3.3 ||**

 

ā saptamāt puruṣāt sapiṇḍatayā pratibaddhā ā daśamād vā samānodakatvena jñātayaḥ snānādyudakakriyānimittam apo 'vatīrya "apa naḥ śośucad agham" (RV 1.97) ity anena dakṣiṇāmukhāḥ snānaṃ kuryuḥ | abhyavayantīti codgharṣaṇādipratiṣedhena sakṛd āplavanamātrārtham | tathā ca śaṅkhaḥ: "dakṣiṇāmukhā apo 'vatīrya sakṛd āplutya nodgharṣaṇaṃ kuryuḥ" iti | yat tv anyatra "janmanāmnor avedane" iti (MDh 5.60) samānodakavidhitvenoktam, tad daśapuruṣavacanānusāreṇaucityānuvādamātratayāvaseyam || 3 ||

 

_samānodakatvābhāve 'pi hi yathā jñātīnām |_

 

**              	evaṃ mātāmahācāryaprattānāṃ codakakriyā |**

**              	kāmodakaṃ sakhiprattāsvasrīyaśvaśurartvijām || 3.4 ||**

 

mātāmahādīnām apy evam evodakakriyā kāryety arthaḥ | apariṇītādattāś ca kumāryaḥ prattāḥ, bhrātrādipatnyo vā | sakhyādīnāṃ tu kāmodakam iti | icchayā tūdakaṃ kāryam ity arthaḥ | prattāśabdaś cātra svavāsinīvacanaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 4 ||

 

_ye cāmī jñātaya udakakriyārtham apo 'avatīrṇāḥ, te snātvā smṛtyantarānusārāc ca saṃyuktādyabhyanujñātāḥ |_

 

**              	sakṛt prasiñcanty udakaṃ nāmagotreṇa vāgyatāḥ |**

 

spaṣṭārtham etat |

 

_sapiṇḍatve 'pi ca |_

 

**              	na brahmacāriṇaḥ kuryur udakaṃ patitā na ca || 3.5 ||**

 

brahmacāripatitaśabdau ca smṛtyantarānusārād vanasthādipāṣaṇḍādilakṣaṇatvena yathāyogaṃ draṣṭavyau || 5 ||

 

_kartṛtvenāpavādam uktvedānīṃ nimittatvenāpavādam āha |_

 

**              	pāṣaṇḍam āśritā stenā bhartṛghnyaḥ kāmagās tathā |**

**              	surāpya ātmatyāginyo nāśaucodakabhājanāḥ || 3.6 ||**

 

tathāśabdaḥ smṛtyantaroktavṛthāsaṃkarajātādyarthaḥ | pāṣaṇḍādīnāṃ nimittatvenāśaucabhāktvapratiṣedhād brahmacāryādīnāṃ kartṛtāmātreṇaiva pratiṣedho 'vaseyaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 6 ||

 

_ye tva adhikṛtā jñātayaḥ |_

 

**              	kṛtodakān samuttīrṇān mṛduśādvalasaṃsthitān |**

**              	snātān apavadeyus tān itihāsaiḥ purātanaiḥ || 3.7 ||**

 

kṛtodakān punaḥ snātān anye lokayātrikā yathoktadeśasaṃsthitān duḥkhopaśamanārtham apavadeyus tān abhimanyuvadhādibhir itihāsaiḥ purāvṛttaiś cetaramanuṣyasaṃbaddhaiḥ || 7 ||

 

_etam evāpavādaṃ prapañcayati |_

 

**              	mānuṣye kadalīstambhaniḥsāre sāramārgaṇam |**

**              	karoti yaḥ sa saṃmūḍho jalabudbudasaṃnibhe || 3.8 ||**

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

**              	pañcadhā saṃbhṛtaḥ kāyo yadi pañcatvam āgataḥ |**

**              	karmabhiḥ svaśarīrotthais tatra kā paridevanā || 3.9 ||**

 

_paśya |_

 

**              	gantrī vasumatī nāśam udadhir daivatāni ca |**

**              	phenaprakhyaḥ kathaṃ nāśaṃ martyaloko na yāsyati || 3.10 ||**

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

**              	śleṣmāśru bāndhavair muktaṃ preto bhuṅkte yato 'vaśaḥ |**

**              	ato na roditavyaṃ syāt kriyāḥ kāryāś ca śaktitaḥ || 3.11 ||**

 

pretam uddiśya svacodanānusāreṇeti śeṣaḥ || 11 ||

 

_anayā diśā lokayātrikair apavadanāyokte sādhv evaibhir uktam |_

 

**              	iti saṃcintya gaccheyur gṛhān bālapurogamāḥ |**

_ _

_bālān agrataḥ kṛtvā yatra pretas tadgṛhadvāraṃ yāvad gatvā tataḥ |_

_ _

**              	vidaśya nimbapatrāṇi niyatā dvāri veśmanaḥ || 3.12 ||**

 

vidaśya dantair avakhaṇḍyety arthaḥ || 12 ||

 

_abhyavahārābhāve 'pi ca |_

 

**              	ācamyāthāgnim udakaṃ gomayaṃ gaurasarṣapān |**

**              	praviśeyuḥ samālabhya kṛtvāśmani padaṃ śanaiḥ || 3.13 ||**

 

yathākaniṣṭham eveti śeṣaḥ | agnyādīnāṃ ca maṅgalārthatvāt saṃśabdāc ca samuccitānām evālambhanam | spaṣṭam anyat || 13 ||

 

_smṛtyantarāc ca gṛhaṃ praviśyāghaprastare tryaham anaśnanta evāsīran | tadaśaktau tu |_

 

**              	krītalabdhāśino bhūmau śayīraṃs te pṛthak pṛhak |**

_ _

_kiṃ ca |_

_ _

**              	pitṛyajñāvṛtā deyaṃ pretāyānnaṃ dinatrayam || 3.14 ||**

 

trirātrāvadhitvena krītvā saṃvyavahārādinā vā labdhvāśnīyuḥ | ekaśaś ca brahmcāriṇo bhūmau śayīran svapeyuḥ | putrādīnāṃ ca yathādhikāraṃ pratyāsattyanusārād etenaiva pitṛyajñoktāvanejanādītikartavyatayā śrāddham akṛtvaiva pretāyānnaṃ deyam | pretam evoddiśya "pretātra snāhi" (PārG 3.10.28) ity anena mantreṇa || 14 ||

 

**              	jalam ekāham ākāśe sthāpyaṃ kṣīraṃ ca mṛnmaye |**

 

pātra iti śeṣaḥ |

 

_saty api cāśaucanimitte 'nadhikāre sarvajñātibhiḥ |_

 

**              	vaitānikāśrayāḥ kāryāḥ kriyāś ca śrutidarśanāt || 3.15 ||**

 

spaṣṭārtham etat || 15 ||

 

yac coktam "ācamyāthāgnim udakam" (YDh 3.13) iti, etat |

 

**              	praveśanādhikaṃ karma pretasaṃsparśanām api |**

**              	icchatāṃ**

 

samānam itaraiḥ | icchatām iti chedaḥ |

 

**                       	     	tatkṣaṇac chuddhiḥ pareṣāṃ snānasaṃyamāt || 3.16 ||**

 

pareṣāṃ pretavāhakavyatiriktānugantṝṇām asamānodakānām | vakṣyamāṇasnānasaṃyamanāgnisparśanādes tatkṣaṇāt sadya eva śuddhir ity arthaḥ | kaṭadhāraṇānicchāyāṃ tu pretavāhakānāṃ pāraskaroktaṃ "pretaspṛśo grāmaṃ na praviśeyur ā nakṣatradarśanād rātrau ced ādityasya" iti (PārG 3.10.35–36) | dṛṣṭasnehakāraṇābhāve tu pretavāhakānāṃ sadyaḥ śaucam parāśaroktam |

                    	anāthaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ pretaṃ ye vahanti dvijātayaḥ |

                    	pade pade yajñaphalam ānupūrvyāl labhanti te ||

                    	na caiṣām aśubhaṃ kiṃcit pāpaṃ vā śubhakarmiṇām |

                    	jalāvagāhanāt teṣāṃ sadyaḥ śaucaṃ vidhīyate || iti (PSm 3.39–40) || 16 ||

 

_snehādināpi tu |_

 

                    	**ācāryopādhyāyapitṝn nirhṛtyāpi vratī vratī |**

**              	sa kaṭānnaṃ ca nāśnīyān na ca taiḥ saha saṃvaset || 3.17 ||**

 

ācāryam upādhyāyaṃ mātāpitarau vā nirhṛtyāpi pretadharmeṇa vratī brahmacārī vraty eva vratān na hīyata ity arthaḥ | ayaṃ tv asya viśeṣaḥ: kaṭānnaṃ nāśnīyāt taiś ca sapiṇḍādibhiḥ saha na saṃvaset | etasmād evānyatra vratahānir iti gamyate | ācāryādisapiṇḍais tu saha kaṭadhāraṇādi na kuryāt, tatkaraṇe vratalopa evety abhiprāyaḥ || 17 ||

 

_udakakriyādhikṛtānām api sapiṇḍasamānodakānāṃ yathāyogam |_

 

**              	daśarātraṃ trirātraṃ vā śāvam āśaucam ucyate |**

**              	ūnadvivarṣam ubhayoḥ sūtakaṃ mātur eva hi || 3.18 ||**

 

daśarātraṃ sapiṇḍānāṃ trirātraṃ samānodakānām | vāśabdaś cobhayatra smṛtyantaroktacaturahapakṣiṇyādikalpānusāreṇa yathāyogaṃ vikalpārthaḥ śavanimitto 'śucibhāvaḥ śāvam āśaucam | tataś ca prāg eva saṃskārān maraṇaprabhṛti daśarātram iti kecit | tad ucyata iti vadann ācāryo nirākaroti | kṛtodakānām apavadanānantaram anyair lokayātrikaiḥ śāvam āśaucaṃ prati sapiṇḍādibhiḥ pṛṣṭair daśarātrādikalpena kriyatām ity evam ucyata ity abhiprāyaḥ | tataś ca saṃskārādy eva syāt | tadabhāve tu smṛtyantarān maraṇādy eveti vyavasthā | anucyamānam api tu ūnadvivārṣikam ubhayoḥ sapiṇḍasamānodakayos tulyakalpam eva | syād iti śeṣaḥ | sūtakaṃ tu mukhyavṛttyā mātur eva yasmāt tasmāt tadanusāreṇaiva garbhasraṃsanādau garbhamāsatulyarātrādikalpas tadarthatayaiva yojya ity abhiprāyaḥ | yad vā ayam aṅgasparśāvadhividhānārthaḥ ślokaḥ | śūdrādikrameṇa brāhmaṇāntānām ātmīyāśaucakalpatṛtīyāṃśatvena daśarātrādināṅgasparśaḥ | tataś ca daśarātraṃ śūdrasya brāhmaṇasya trirātram | vāśabdāt pañcarātraṃ catūrātraṃ vaiśyarājanyayoḥ śavavad aṅgasparśābhāvenāśaucam ucyate | ūnadvivārṣikaṃ cobhayor mātāpitror evāśaucatribhāgatvenātmīyāśaucakalpatṛtīyāṃśatvena daśarātrādināṅgasparśābhāvaḥ | sūtakaṃ tu mātur eva | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ |

                    	nāśaucaṃ sūtake puṃsaḥ saṃsargaṃ cen na gacchati |

                    	rajas tatrāśucikaraṃ tac ca puṃsi na vidyate || iti (VaDh 4.23) || 18 ||

 

_idānīm āśaucakālaparimāṇam āha |_

 

**              	brāhmaṇasya daśāhaṃ tu bhavati pretasūtakam |**

**              	kṣatrasya dvādaśāhāni viśāṃ pañcadaśaiva vā || 3.19 ||**

**              	triṃśad dināni śūdrasya pretasūtakam ucyate |**

**              	antarā janmamaraṇe śeṣāhobhir viśudhyati || 3.20 ||**

 

"brāhamaṇasya daśāhaṃ tu" ity adhikanivṛttyarthas tuśabdaḥ | pretaṃ ca sūtakaṃ ca pretasūtakaṃ, pretatvanimittaṃ janmanimittaṃ ca daśarātrāvadhi brāhmaṇasyāśaucaṃ bhavatīty arthaḥ | "viśāṃ pañcadaśaiva vā" iti vāśabdaḥ smṛtyantarokāvadhyantaravikalpārthatayā sarvatrāviśeṣeṇa draṣṭavyaḥ | śūdrasaṃbandhitayā ca punaḥ pretasūtakavacanam aśūdrāṇāṃ varṇāpaśadānāṃ nivṛttyartham | janmamaraṇayoś ca samānajātīyatvena punar antarā janmamaraṇe pūrvāśaucakālaśeṣeṇaiva śuddhiḥ | tathā ca smṛtyantaram: "janmamaraṇayos tulyopanipātaś ced ā trirātraśeṣaṇāt pūrveṇaiva śuddhiḥ, nyūne trirātrapūraṇaṃ, purodayād antye trirātram udite tu yathoktam" iti | spaṣṭam anyat || 19, 20 ||

 

_kiṃ cānayat |_

 

**              	garbhasrāve māsatulyā niśāḥ śuddhes tu kāraṇam |**

**              	proṣite kālaśeṣaḥ syāt pūrṇe dattvodakaṃ śuciḥ || 3.21 ||**

 

garbhasrāve māsasaṃkhyātāhorātrāṇi cāśaucam | etac ca mātṛviṣayam eva | sapiṇḍānāṃ tu trirātram eva, vasiṣṭhavacanāt: "garbhapatane sapiṇḍānāṃ trirātram āśaucam" iti (VaDh 4.34) | proṣite jñāte jñānaprabhṛtyavaśiṣṭakālam āśaucaṃ syāt | pūrṇe tu daśarātrādāv āśaucakāle dattvodakam udakadānasaṃbhandhivihitatrirātreṇaiva śuciḥ syāt | yad vā smṛtyantarānusārāt pūrṇe saṃvatsare dattvodakaṃ sadyaḥ śaucam iti yojyam || 21 ||

 

_aviśeṣeṇaiva tu sarvavarṇānām |_

 

**              	ahas tv adattakanyāsu bāleṣu ca viśodhanam |**

**              	gurvantevāsyanūcānamātulaśrotriyeṣu ca || 3.22 ||**

 

ahaḥśabdo 'horātravacanaḥ, anantaraśloke tad ahar iti tanmātrārthaṃ punar vacanāt | ahas tv adattakanyāsv ity adbhir vācā ca yad dānam, tadapekṣayāvaseyam | tuśabdaḥ kalpanāntarārthaḥ prattādiviṣayatvena | antevāsī śilpaśiṣyaḥ | tatsaṃnidhiyogāc ca tadgurāv eva guruśabdaḥ | anūcānaḥ anuvaktaivopādhyāyaḥ | mātulo mātuḥ sodaryaḥ śrotriyaś cānupasaṃpannaḥ, anāśritaprātiveśyādir ity arthaḥ | mukhyagurvādīnāṃ tu smṛtyantaroktaṃ draṣṭavyam || 22 ||

 

_sarvavarṇāvaiśeṣikatvenaiva ca |_

 

**              	anauraseṣu putreṣu bhāryāsv anyagatāsu ca |**

**              	nivāsarājani tathā tad ahaḥ śuddhikāraṇam || 3.23 ||**

 

anaurasavacanaṃ bījakṣetrasaṃbandhavyatirekaparatvād dattakādiviṣayaṃ draṣṭavyam | bhāryātvenānyasaṃbaddhāsu | āgatāsu avaruddhāsv iti yāvat | nivāsahetubhūte nyāyavṛtte kṣatriye rājani | tathāśabdād evamādyuktaprakāraniścayaḥ | eṣāṃ vipattau tad evāhaḥ śuddhikāraṇaṃ, nāhorātram ity arthaḥ || 23 ||

 

_sapiṇḍatayaiva prāptasya yathoktāśaucakalpasyāpavādārtham āha |_

 

**              	gonṛpabrahmahatānām anvakṣaṃ cātmaghātinām |**

**              	prāyānāśakaśastrāgniviṣādyair icchatāṃ svayam || 3.24 ||**

 

gavādibhir anicchatām api vyāpāditānām anvakṣam āśaucaṃ syāt | akṣam indriyaṃ tadupalabdhivṛttyā, yāvad darśanam ity arthaḥ | tataś cādarśanāc chuddhiḥ | aśuddhivacanāc ca darśanam apy akartavyam eveti jñāpayati | prāyādibhiś ca svayam icchatām ātmavyāpādane 'nvakṣam eva | svayam iti vacanaṃ brāhmaṇādyarthanivṛttyartham | prāyo mahāpathagamanam | āmnāyaś cecchayaiva jñaptyartham ātmavyāpādanābhyupagamaṃ darśayati: "yady u mā mārayiṣyati yajñaṃ vikṛṣṭam anu vikrakṣya" ityādi (ŚB 11.8.4.2) || 24 ||

 

_kāryāntaroparodhāc ca |_

 

**              	mahīpatīnāṃ nāśaucaṃ hatānāṃ vidyutā tathā |**

**              	gobrāhmaṇārthe saṃgrāme yasya necchati bhūmipaḥ || 3.25 ||**

 

mahīpatīnāṃ rājñāṃ pālanārtham āśaucābhāvaḥ | tadarthaṃ yasyāśaucābhāvam icchati rājā prāḍvivākādeḥ, tasyāpy āśaucābhāvaḥ | vidyudādihatānāṃ tu nirdoṣatve 'pi vacanāt, gobrāhmaṇādyarthe tv abhyudayātirekād evety avagantavyam || 25 ||

 

_anugantṝṇāṃ tv idānīm āha |_

 

**              	brāḥmaṇenānugantavyo na śūdro hi mṛtaḥ kvacit |**

 

kvacid ity āpady apy ananugamārtham |

 

_yas tv anugantavyo jñātir ajñātir vā sajātīyaḥ, tam api |_

 

**              	anugamyāmbhasi snātvā spṛṣṭvāgniṃ ghṛtabhuk śuciḥ || 3.26 ||**

 

ambhovacanaṃ bahiḥ snānakriyārtham | spaṣṭam anyat || 26 ||

 

_sapiṇḍatve 'pi ca |_

 

**              	ṛtvijāṃ dīkṣitānāṃ ca yājñe karmaṇi kurvatām |**

**              	satrivratibrahmacāridātṛbrahmavidāṃ tathā || 3.27 ||**

**              	dāne vivāhe yajñe ca saṃgrāme deśaviplave |**

**              	āpady api ca kaṣṭāyāṃ sadyaḥśaucaṃ vidhīyate || 3.28 ||**

 

ṛtvigdīkṣitavacanaṃ varaṇadīkṣāmātrapravṛttyaiva prāg eva yajñārambhād āśaucanivṛttyartham | "yājñe karmaṇi kurvatām" iti anṛtvijām api camasādhavaryvādīnāṃ parigrahārtham | satrī prasiddhaḥ | ādiṣṭaprāyaścittī vratī | brahmacārī upakurvāṇako naiṣṭhikaś ca | dātā satatapravṛttahiraṇyādidānaḥ | brahmavit tādarthyādhikārāt parivrājakaḥ, tadupāsanaikaniṣṭho vā | tathāśabdo vanasthādyarthaḥ | dānādau ca tatsaṃbandhabrāhmaṇābhimukhyakaraṇādyaṅgena prastute rāṣṭrabhaṅgādau ca deśaviplave anyasyāṃ vā nirvyājakaṣṭāyām āpadi | "sadyaḥśaucaṃ vidhīyate" iti vicikitsānivṛttyartham || 27–28 ||

 

_evaṃ śāvāśaucam abhidhāyedānīṃ sūtakāśrayaṃ viśeṣāpavādam āha |_

 

**              	pitros tu sūtakaṃ mātus tad asṛgdarśanād dhruvam |**

**              	tad ahar na praduṣyeta pūrveṣāṃ janmakāraṇāt || 3.29 ||**

 

mātāpitror bījaśoṇitasaṃbandhād aṅgasparśāyogyatvakaraṃ sūtakaṃ, na punaḥ sapiṇḍānām api, tadasaṃbhavāt | evaṃ cen mātur eva, tadasṛgdarśanāt | dhruvaṃ niścitam ity arthaḥ | tathā ca svāyambhuvam |

                    	sarveṣāṃ śāvam āśaucaṃ mātāpitros tu sūtakam |

                    	sūtakaṃ mātur eva syād upaspṛśya pitā śuciḥ || iti | (MDh 5.62)

śāvaśabdo 'ṅgasparśābhāvapratipattyarthaḥ | yad api cānayat sapiṇḍasāmānyaṃ dānādyanadhikāralakṣaṇam āśaucaṃ tadapekṣayāpi yasminn ahani putro jātas tadahar na praduṣyeta | kim artham | pūrveṣāṃ pitrādīnāṃ pitṝṇāṃ janmakāraṇāt | janmani śrāddhakāraṇād ity arthaḥ | praśabdāc ca bhoktṝṇām apy adoṣa iti gamyate || 29 ||

 

_ayaṃ tu sāmānyena puruṣamātradharmaḥ |_

 

**              	udakyāśaucibhiḥ snāyāt saṃspṛṣṭas tair upaspṛśet |**

**              	abliṅgābhir japec caiva sāvitrīṃ manasā sakṛt || 3.30 ||**

 

udakyā rajasvalā, āśaucino 'ṅgasparśānarhāḥ, taiḥ spṛṣṭaḥ snāyāt | kāmatas tu saṃgamya taiḥ spṛṣṭo 'bliṅgābhiḥ "āpo hi ṣṭhā" ityādibhiḥ snātvopaspṛśet | ācāmed ity arthaḥ | ācamya sāvitrīṃ manasā sakṛj japtvā śudhyatīty avaseyam |

        	idaṃ tv atra cintyam | anekadhā virodhinām āśaucavākyānāṃ kathaṃ viṣayakalpaneti | tad yathā: svayambhuvā "daśāhaṃ śāvam āśaucam" (MDh 5.59) ity atra catvāraḥ kalpāḥ pradarśitāḥ | daśāhaḥ, tathā "ā vā sañcayanād asthnām" (MDh 5.59) ity anena caturahaḥ, "tryaham ekāham eva vā" (MDh 5.59) ity anena tryahaikāhau | tathā parāśareṇa |

                    	brāhmaṇasya trirātraṃ tu śāvam āśaucam ucyate |

                    	kṣatriyasya daśāhāni vaiśyasaikādaśaiva tu || iti |

gautamenāpi: "śāvam āśaucaṃ daśarātram anṛtvigdīkṣitabrahmacāriṇāṃ sapiṇḍānām" ity upakramya, "ekādaśarātraṃ kṣatriyasya dvādaśarātraṃ vaiśyasya" (GDh 14.1–3) ity uktam | vasiṣṭhenāpy uktam: "brāhmaṇo daśarātreṇa pañcadaśarātreṇa kṣatriyo vaiśyo viṃśatirātreṇa" iti (VaDh 4.27–29) | śūdrasya tu māsa eva sarvatroktaḥ | tatra kecic chlokāntarārambhasāmarthyād vṛttasvādhyāyādyapekṣayā viṣayavyavasthāṃ varṇayanti |

                    	ekāhāc chudhyate vipro yo 'gnivedasamanvitaḥ | (PSm 3.5)

ityādi | tat tu nātīva samyak | yadi hi vṛttādyapekṣayaikāhādy ucyeta, tadā

                    	ubhayatra daśāhāni kulasyānnaṃ na bhujyate |

                    	dānaṃ pratigraho yajñaḥ svādhyāyaś ca nivartate ||

ityādy anupapannam eva syāt | gautamo 'pi ca dīkitādiparyudāsena daśarātraṃ vidadhad vṛttādimatām evaitad iti jñāpayati | evaṃ sarvasmṛtyantareṣu svādhyāyādyanadhikāra evāśaucam, taddhīnasya ca svabhāvasiddho 'nadhikāra iti kim āśaucaṃ kariṣyati | tathā dakṣeṇa sadyaḥśaucādidaśapakṣaṃ sūtakaṃ prakramyoktam |

                    	vyādhitasya kadaryasya ṛṇagrastasya sarvadā |

                    	kriyāhīnasya mūrkhasya strījitasya viśeṣataḥ ||

                    	vyasanāsaktacittasya parādhīnasya nityaśaḥ |

                    	śraddhātyāgavihīnasya bhasmāntaṃ sūtakaṃ bhavet || iti |

evaṃjātīyakānāṃ svabhāvasiddhānām ā maraṇād anapāyyevāśaucam, nāśaucavidhiviṣayabhāktvam eṣām ity abhiprāyaḥ |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">kathaṃ tarhy</span> ayaṃ ślokaḥ: "ekāhāc chudhyate vipraḥ" iti (PSm 3.5) | nindārthavādatvena bhasmāntasūtakavacanavad etad api vṛttādipraśaṃsāmātrārthaṃ prakramānusārāt smṛtyantarād nyāyavirodhāc ca draṣṭavyam | na hi vedarahitasyāgnisaṃyogo 'sti | stutyarthatāyāṃ tv avirodhaḥ | evaṃ pārāśaryam api |

                    	nāmadhārakaviprāṇāṃ daśāhaṃ sūtakaṃ bhavet | (PSm 3.6)

ityādi yojyam | anye tu,

                    	dantajāte 'nujāte ca kṛtacaule ca saṃsthite | (MDh 5.58)

ity etacchlokānusāreṇa vayo'vasthāpekṣayā vyavasthām āhuḥ | jātā dantā yasya sa dantajātaḥ, tam anu paścād yo jātaḥ so 'nujātaḥ nāmakaraṇād ūrdhvaṃ (syāt?) prāg dantajananāt | parato nyūnatrivarṣo dantajātaḥ | paratas tu prāg upanayanāt kṛtacaulaḥ | caśabdāc ca kṛtopanayanaḥ | teṣu kṛtopanayanādiṣu saṃsthiteṣu daśāhādikalpavyavastheti | tad etat kṛtacaule trirātravidhānād itaratrāpi ca yathāyogaṃ vacanāntarārambhasāmarthyād ayuktam eva | svabuddhyanusārinyaś caitāḥ kalpanāḥ | na caitac codanālakṣaṇatve yuktam | kas tarhi prakāraḥ |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | sapiṇḍoddeśenaiva hi catvāro 'pi kalpāḥ | sapiṇḍatāpi hi catuṣprakāraiva | yathoktam: "piṇḍanivṛttiḥ saptame pañcame vā" iti (GDh 14.13) | vṛtte vartamāne ceti cobhaythā sūtrārthayojanād etad āpadyete: pañcame ṣaṣṭhe vā saptame 'ṣṭame vā puruṣe piṇḍanivṛttir iti | ata evoktam |

                    	sapiṇḍatā tu puruṣe saptame vinivartate | iti | (MDh 5.60)

saptame vigate 'ṣṭame nivartata eva, na parataḥ pravartata ity arthaḥ | tad evaṃ catuṣprakārāṃ sapiṇḍatām ālocya, yathāsaṃnikarṣaṃ daśāhādikalpayojanā | tataś ca samānodakānāṃ catuṣprakārāṇāṃ tryahapakṣiṇyekāhasadyaḥśaucādikalpavyavasthāpy upapannā bhavati | piṇḍanivṛttikalpanāyām eva tu kathaṃ vyavastheti ced, uktam "piṇḍakaraṇe prathamaḥ pitṝṇāṃ pretaḥ syāt putravāṃś cet" ityupakramya, "nivartate caturthe" iti (PārG 3.10.50–51) | ataḥ pramītapitṛkasya pañcame piṇḍanivṛttiḥ, evaṃ jīvapitṛkasya ṣaṣṭhe, jīvapitāmahasya saptame, jīvaprapitāmahasyāṣṭama iti vyavasthā | sahanivasatāṃ ca pitṛnimittam eva putrāṇām āśaucam | pṛthaṅnivāse tu pratyātmikam | tathā ca parāśaro nivāsabhedābhiprāyeṇaivāha |

                    	saṃparkeṣu nivṛttānāṃ na pretaṃ naiva sūtakam | iti ||

evaṃ sarvavarṇāṇāṃ sapiṇḍasamānodakatvenāśaucakalpavyavasthā yojyā | brāhmaṇādijanmānusāreṇa vākyavyavasthā | "vaiśyavac chaucakalpaḥ syāt" (MDh 5.140) ity etadanusārāc ca śūdrasyāpy anekakalpaprasaṅge pūrvavad yojyam | "nyāyavartinām" (MDh 5.140) iti vacanād dvijātyāśritaśūdraviṣaya evāyam, itarasya tv aṣṭapauruṣy eva sapiṇḍatā | māsa evāsyaikaḥ śuddhiprakāraḥ | kṣatriyādīnāṃ tu brāhmaṇādijātaviṣayatayā ca brāhmaṇādīnāṃ tripuruṣam eva sapiṇḍatā | tathā ca śaṅkhaḥ: "piṇḍas tv āvartate triṣu" iti | āśaucakalpaś ca pratyātmika eva "ekapiṇḍāḥ pṛthakśaucāḥ" iti vacanāt | evaṃ ca pitṛvyatatputrādiviṣayaṃ svaputrādiviṣayatayā tu sahanivāsināṃ pitṛtulyam evāśaucam | tathā coktam |

                    	mṛte sūte tu dāsānāṃ putrāṇāṃ cānulominām |

                    	svāmitulyaṃ bhavec chaucam ṛte svāmini yautakam | iti |

pituḥ punaḥ |

                    	varṇāṇām ānulomyena strīṇām eko yadā patiḥ |

                    	daśāhaṣaṭtryahaikāhāḥ sūtake mṛtake tathā || iti |
