anayā diśā sarveṣām āśaucakalpānāṃ viṣayakalpanā | yadi tv avaśyaṃ vṛttādyapekṣayāpi viṣayakalpanā, tato varam aśvastanatrai(ya)hikādivṛttiviśeṣāpekṣayaiva, dṛṣṭārthatvāt | yat tu gautamīyam "rājñāṃ ca kāryavirodhāt" (GDh 14.45) ityādisadyaḥśaucābhidhānaṃ tad dhetvabhidhānāt pravṛttabrahmayajñānāṃ tanmātra eva draṣṭavyam | adhyāpanapravṛtter vāśvastanikādivad eva svādhyāye | evaṃ satrivratiprabhṛtīnām api tanmātratayaivāśaucanivṛttir avagantavyety eṣā dik | sūtakam apy evam evātideśānusārād yojyam | anye tu daśāhamātrātideśaṃ sūtakaṃ manyante | tat punar aśābdatvād akiṃcit | yat tu mātur ekāhādiprasaṅgāt samācārāt smṛtyantaroktadaśarātrasamālambhanādivirodhāc ca daśāhātideśa iti, tan mātāpitroḥ sapiṇḍatāvadhiviśeṣāśrayacaturahādyaprasaṅgāt phalguprāyam eva syāt | ataḥ śāvāśaucavad atrāpy atideśānusāriṇy eva vyavasthākalpanety anavadyam | yat tu "sūtakaṃ mātur eva syāt" iti, tad aṅgasparśapratiṣedhārtham iti vyākhyātam eva | yat tu,

                    	nirasya tu pumāñ chuklam upaspṛśyaiva śudhyati |

                    	baijikād abhisaṃbandhād anurundhyād aghaṃ tryaham || (MDh 5.63)

iti, tac chūdraviṣayam avaruddhadāsīsaṃbandhena niyogasaṃbandhena vā draṣṭavyam | avaruddhadāsīviṣayatvena tu nirasya śuklaṃ putrajanmādāv upaspṛśya sadya eva śuciḥ | niyogapakṣeṇa tu "baijikād abhisaṃbandhāt tryaham" ity eṣā dik | kanyāviṣayaṃ tu vākyatrayaṃ viṣayavyavasthayaiva paṭhyata ity avirodhaḥ | tad yathā |

                    	aprauḍhāyāṃ tu kanyāyāṃ sadhyaḥśaucaṃ vidhīyate |

ityetadvākyānusārād akṛtacūḍāviṣayaṃ draṣṭavyam | "ahas tv adattakanyāsu" (YDh 3.22) ityetat kṛtacūḍāyām adattāyām | dattāyāṃ tu mānavaṃ, yebhyo dattā teṣāṃ trirātram evāstu yair dattā teṣāṃ caikāhādinā,

                    	yathoktenaiva kalpena śuddhyanti tu sanābhayaḥ | (MDh 5.72)

iti vacanāt | anye tu "yathoktenaiva kalpena" iti daśarātraṃ varṇayanti | yat tu svaśāstrānusāreṇa kliṣṭakalpanayā pratīyamānam api nyāyasamācārasmṛtyantarānusārād ayuktam eva | proṣitapretavākyāni tu trirātrapakṣiṇyekāhasadhyaḥśaucaviṣayāṇi sapiṇḍatāvidhiviśeṣānusāreṇaiva vyākhyeyāni | mātulādiviṣayatvena tu,

                    	viśudhyati trirātreṇa mātur āptāṃś ca bāndhavān | (MDh 5.101)

iti vacanān nirharaṇakartur eva trirātram, anyasya tu pakṣiṇy eva | ekāhas tu sāpatnādiviṣaya eva | sapiṇḍasamānodakavyatirekeṇa ca sarvatra kṣapaṇamātram anujjvalaveṣatālakṣaṇam āśaucasādṛśyād āśaucavacanaṃ draṣṭavyam, na tu yajñādyadhikāranivṛttiḥ,

                    	sabrahmacāriṇy ekāham atīte kṣapaṇaṃ smṛtam | (MDh 5.71)

iti prakramāt samācārāc ca | evaṃ sarvathā sarvavākyānāṃ vyavasthāsiddhir iti alaṃ prasaṅgena || 30 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvad vispaṣṭavijānanimittakaṃ sarvatra sarvathā cāśaucavidhim uktvā svabhāvopahatasyedānīṃ nisargajāvidyopaplavād ātmana indriyāṇāṃ śarīrasya tadupakaraṇasya vā samyak saṃśuddhikāraṇaṃ sāmānyenaivāha |_

 

                    	**kālo 'gniḥ karma mṛd vāyur mano jñānaṃ tapo jalam |**

**              	paścāttāpo nirāhāraḥ sarve 'mī śuddhihetavaḥ || 3.31 ||**

 

agnir iti tejasa udāharaṇam | mṛt pṛthivyāḥ | jalavāyvos tu svarūpeṇaivopādānam | etāni pṛthivyādīni catvāri mahābhūtāni etadātmakasya bāhyasyopakaraṇasya vyastasamastātmanā yathāyogaṃ śuddhisādhanāni, kālakarmaṇos tu bāhyasyābhyantarasya cātmana indryagrāmasya ca, mana indriyāntarāṇāṃ, manasas tu vakṣyati, avaśiṣṭāni jñānādīny ātmanaḥ | evaṃ yathāyogam aviśeṣeṇa vā sarvatra sarve 'mī śuddhihetava ity avaseyam | sarveṣāṃ svadeśadeśāntarābhihitasvaviṣayaśuddhisādhanānāṃ saṃkṣepeṇa punar vacanārthatayā vāyam upasaṃhārārtho 'nuvādaḥ || 31 ||

 

_etad eva spaṣṭayituṃ viṣayavyavasthayā prapañcayati |_

 

**              	akāryakāriṇāṃ dānaṃ vego nadyās tu śuddhikṛt |**

**              	śodhyasya mṛc ca toyaṃ ca saṃnyāso vai dvijanmanām || 3.32 ||**

**              	tapo vedavidāṃ kṣāntir viduṣāṃ varṣmaṇo jalam |**

 

varṣma śarīram | tathā ca svāyaṃbhuvaḥ: "mṛdbhir adbhiś ca gātrāṇi" iti (cf. MDh 5.109) || 32 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

**              	japaḥ pracchannapāpānāṃ manasaḥ satyam ucyate || 3.33 ||**

**              	bhūtātmanas tapovidye buddher jñānaṃ viśodhanam |**

**              	kṣetrajñasyeśvarajñānād viśuddhiḥ paramā matā || 3.34 ||**

 

trayaḥ ślokāḥ spaṣṭārthā vakṣyamāṇopaniṣatkāṇḍaprāyaścittakāṇḍayoḥ sūtrabhūtā draṣṭavyāḥ || 33–34 ||

 

**ity āśaucaprakaraṇam |**

 

 

**athāpaddharmaprakaraṇam |**

 

_"akāryakāriṇāṃ dānāc chuddhiḥ" _(YDh 3.32)_ ity asya vivekārtham āha |_

 

**              	kṣātreṇa karmaṇā jīved viṣāṃ vāpy āpadi dvijaḥ |**

**              	nistīryārthaṃ tam utsṛjya pāvyātmānaṃ nyaset pathi || 3.35 ||**

 

kṣātreṇa prajāpālanādikarmaṇā brāhmaṇavaiśyayoḥ vaiśyakarmaṇā vā pūrvayoḥ, akāryabhūtenāpi svavṛttyasaṃbhavalakṣaṇāyām āpadi jīvanaṃ dharmyam eva | dvijavacanāc ca kṣatriyavaiśyadharmān vācayatvena varṇatrayasādhāraṇyaṃ vyākhyātam | tathā ca nāradaḥ |

                    	utkṛṣṭaṃ cāpakṛṣṭaṃ ca tayoḥ karma na vidyate |

                    	madhame karmaṇī hitvā sarvasādhāraṇe hi te || iti | (NSm 1.54)

akāryatvāc cāpatkalpatvam | tena tām āpadaṃ nistīrya utsṛjya cāvaśiṣṭaṃ dravyaṃ dānena vidhivat pāvayitvā ātmānaṃ svavṛttilakṣaṇa eva pathi sthāpayet, na tasyām eva kṣatriyādivṛttau ratiṃ kuryād ity abhiprāyaḥ || 35 ||

 

_āpadgato 'pi ca |_

 

                    	**phalopalakṣaumasomamanuṣyāpūpavīrudhaḥ |**

**              	tilaudanarasakṣārān dadhi kṣīraṃ ghṛtaṃ jalam || 3.36 ||**

**              	śastrāsavaṃ madhūcchiṣṭaṃ madhu lākṣātha barhiṣaḥ |**

**              	mṛccarmapuṣpakutapakeśatakraviṣairakān || 3.37 ||**

**              	kauśeyanīlīlavaṇamāṃsaikaśaphahetavaḥ |**

**              	śākārdrauṣadhipiṇyākatūlagandhāṃs tathaiva ca || 3.38 ||**

**              	vaiśyavṛttyāpi saṃjīvan vikrīṇīta na karhicit |**

**              	dharmārthaṃ vikrayaṃ neyās tilā dhānyena tatsamāḥ || 3.39 ||**

 

vaiśyavṛttyāpi hi brāhmaṇakṣatriyayor āpadi jīvatoḥ phalādīni ślokatrayapaṭhitāny avikreyāṇi | tatpratiṣedhād vaiśyasyaitāny aniṣiddhānīti gamyate | phalāny āmrādīni | upalāḥ pāśāṇaśilādayaḥ padmarāgādayaś ca | kṣaumam atasīmayaṃ goṇyādi | somādīni prasiddhāni | vīrudha āraṇyā oṣadhayaḥ | apūpā maṇḍakāḥ | tilādīni spaṣṭāni | jalam ādhārastham uddhṛtaṃ vā | mūlyena tu yad udakāharaṇaṃ sasyaprasecanāya vapram āpādyārpaṇaṃ tadudakavikrayatvena kriyāntarārthatvān nāśaṅkanīyam | śastrāṇi khaḍgādīni | āsavaḥ kharjūrādirasaḥ | rasatvena ca niṣiddhasya punarvacanaṃ śabdāntarābhidheyatvāt prāyaścittaviśeṣārtham evety etad eva ca yuktataram arthānusāritvāt pratiṣedhasya | madhu madyam | ucchiṣṭaṃ prasiddham | madhu mākṣikaṃ mādanaṃ vā madhūcchiṣṭam ucyate | athaśabdo 'bhidheyānyatvapratipattyarthaḥ | barhiṣa iti tu ṣaṣṭhyantanirdeśo vyatyayapratipattyarthaḥ | tataś ca tṛṇamātravacano 'pi barhiḥśabdaḥ saṃskṛtatvānusāreṇāśeṣasrugādiyajñasādhanapratiṣedharthaḥ | mṛdādīni prasiddhāni | jalavyākhyānavac ca yojanā | arthāntaratvāc ca bhūmer na doṣaḥ | prakṛtivikārayoś cātra yāvaduktopādānam eva, kṣīratakrayoḥ pṛthagvacanāt | viṣairakā viṣam udakaṃ tatprabhavā matsyādayaḥ | kauśeyaṃ trasarīmayam | nīlī gulikā vastrādyanupraviṣṭā kevalā vā | lavaṇamāṃsādīni prasiddhāni | ekaśaphā ekakhurā aśvādayaḥ | hetavo vadhasādhanāni viṣādīni | śākānām anyatra vikrayopadeśād iha nālikādīny abhakṣyāṇi pratyetavyāni | ārdrauṣadhayas tv alūnāḥ kṣitisthāḥ, paraśastrādyupahatās tu na pratiṣidhyante | piṇyākaḥ khaliḥ | tūlaṃ śalmalyādiprabhavam | gandhāḥ karpūrādayaḥ | tathāśabdaḥ smṛtyantaroktaśāṇādyarthaḥ | tilās tv avaiśyavṛttisthenāpi dharmārthaṃ svakṛṣyādyutpannā vikreyāḥ, dhānyāntaraparivartanena vā vaiśyasyāpi ca | anyathā tilavikraye pratyavāyaḥ | tathā coktam |

                    	bhojanābhyañjanād dānād yo 'nyatra kurute tilaiḥ |

                    	kṛmībhūtaḥ sa viṣṭhāyāṃ pitṛbhiḥ saha majjati || iti | (MDh 10.91)

kāmaṃ vā svayaṃ kṛṣyotpādyaṃ tilān vikrīṇīyād iti vaiśyasya || 36–39 ||

 

_api ca |_

 

**              	lavaṇaṃ tanayā lākṣā patanīyāni vikraye |**

**              	payo dadhi ca madyaṃ ca hīnavarṇakarāṇi tu || 3.40 ||**

 

kathaṃ tarhi śunaḥśephādivikraḥ | śruteḥ pratiṣiddhatvād eva pitrādinindādvāreṇa śunaḥśephasya prasaṃsārtham | yad vā sarvathāpy āpadi svaprāṇaparirakṣaṇārtham ity arthaḥ || 40 ||

 

_tad eva spaṣṭayati |_

 

                    	**āpadgataḥ saṃpragṛhṇan bhuñjāno vā yatas tataḥ |**

**              	na lipyetainasā vipro jvalanārkasamo hi saḥ || 3.41 ||**

 

yathaiva jvalanaś caṇḍālādigṛheṣv api vartamāno 'rko vā sarvatra sāmyena vartamāno nirdoṣaḥ, evaṃ brāhmaṇo 'pi japādibhir āpadgataḥ pratilabhya śarīram ārjitaduritakṣapaṇasamartha ity ādityavad eva yadṛcchāpracāritvam aviruddham || 41 ||

 

_yataś caitad evam ataḥ |_

 

                    	**kṛṣiḥ śilpaṃ bhṛtir vidyā kusīdaṃ śakaṭaṃ giriḥ |**

**              	sevānūpo nṛpo bhaikṣam āpattau jīvanāni tu || 3.42 ||**

 

kṛṣyādīni yathāsaṃbhavam āpado nistaraṇahetutvenaikādaśa jīvanāni | etāni codāharaṇārthatvena, sarvathā tu na tad asti yad āpady akartavyam ity abhiprāyaḥ | kṛṣiḥ prasiddhā | śilpaṃ citrakarmādi | bhṛtir māsādivṛttyā parakīyakarmakaraṇam | vidyā mūlyenādhyāpanam | kusīdaṃ prāyogyam | śakaṭaṃ mūlyena śakaṭavāhanam | giriḥ parvataḥ tadīyatṛṇakāṣṭhādivikrayaḥ tadupajīvanam | sevā prasiddhā | anūpo nadyādikacchaḥ tadutpannaśākādivikrayaḥ tadupajīvanam | nṛpo rājā tatpratigrahānujīvanam | bhaikṣaṃ kṛtākṛtānnādibhedena dviprakāram || 42 ||

 

_dustaratvād eva cāpadām |_

 

                    	**bubhukṣitas tryahaṃ sthitvā dhanam abrāhmaṇād dharet |**

**              	pratigṛhya tad ākhyeyam abhiyuktena dharmataḥ || 3.43 ||**

 

svarūpaparimāṇādyavipratipattyety arthaḥ || 43 ||

 

_evaṃ ca rājābhiyuktasyāvipratipannatvena |_

 

                    	**tasya vṛttaṃ kulaṃ śīlaṃ śrutam adhyayanaṃ sutān |**

**              	jñātvā rājā kuṭumbāt svād dharmyāṃ vṛttiṃ prakalpayet || 3.44 ||**

 

tasya vṛttādīni vyastasamastatayā nirūpya guṇānusāreṇaiva rājā svāt svakīyād dhanabhāṇḍāgārād apy anyāni paribhāvya kāryāntarāṇi dharmyāṃ vṛttiṃ dharmāvirodhinīṃ yathā vṛttānusāreṇa dṛṣṭādṛṣṭārthāt svakarmaṇo na hīyate tathābūtāṃ śāśvatīṃ vṛttiṃ prakalpayed iti || 44 ||

** **

**ity āpaddharmaprakaraṇam |**

** **

**atha vānaprasthadharmaprakaraṇam |**

 

evaṃ tāvad āśramadvayam abhihitam | idānīṃ gṛhasthāśramam upabhujya valīpalitavato vidyamānasantānasya viṣayaviraktasya ca kramaprāptas tṛtīyo vānaprathāśrama ucyate | pūrvaṃ tu vedānuvacanātmakād brahmacaryād anantaraṃ "yam icchet tam āvaset" (VaDh 7.3) ity evaṃ nyāyāgamānusāreṇa vyutthānapakṣo 'bhihitaḥ | tatra samuccayapakṣas tv idānīm ucyate |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca yuktaṃ yad vairāgyātiśayād dārāharaṇādyanapekṣasya vyutthāyāśramāntarāṅgīkaraṇam | kṛtadārasya tu kāmākṛṣṭacetaso yāvajjīvaśrutyavaruddhasya tadvirodhitayā cāpramāṇībhūtasmṛtyarthānusāriṇī duḥśliṣṭaivāśramāntarapratipattiḥ | atha punar vairāgyayogād evety ucyate |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">tad asat</span> | pratipattikāla eva hi śāstrārtho nirūpyate, na tv anuṣṭhīyamānaprayogamadhye 'pi |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca yathaiva kāmino 'dhikṛtasyāpavṛttakāmasya prayogamadhye 'py anadhikārād vyutthānam | evam atrāpi syāt | api ca jīvato 'pi prayogaparyanta evādhikāraḥ | tatra paurṇamāsyantare pūrvaprārabdhaprayogaparyavasānāt prayogāntare ca vairāgyātiśayād adhikārānavagateḥ |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span> | yuktaṃ hi kāminaḥ phalaṃ prati sādhanabhūta eva dhātvarthe 'dhikārāvagamād vītāyāṃ ca phalecchāyāṃ tadvyāvṛtteḥ jīvataḥ punar na vidhyarthād anyatra yāgādeḥ sādhanatvaṃ, na ca niyojyatvavyāvṛttiḥ jīvanānapāyāt, prayuktadāratvāc ca na tadgato 'pi viśeṣaḥ pūrvavad atra kaścic chakyate vaktum | prayogabhedābhedau tv adhikārahetvanapāyād akiṃcitkarāv eva | atra śrutivirodhāt krameṇāyukta eva vanasthāśramaḥ | ata eva ca gautamena "aikāśramyaṃ tv ācāryāḥ pratyakṣavidhānād gārhasthyasya" (GDh 3.36) ity uktam | tatrānye puruṣamedhānte vanasthādyāśramam āhuḥ, pratyakṣacodanānusārāt | tathā hi: "athātmany agnīn samāropya" iti prakṛtya, "anavekṣamāṇo 'raṇyaṃ gacchet" ityādi | tad apy aviśeṣeṇaiva vanasthādismṛtyārambhād anupayogiprāyam eva | jarāmaryavacanaṃ tu liṅgād, nyāyāntarāpekṣavacanavidhyanumānaṃ pratyakṣavidhivirodhāt | ato vaktavyam etat | atrābhidhīyate: kāmādibhiḥ prayuktadārāṇāṃ yāvajjīvaśrutir ity etat prāg apy uktam eva | apagatakāmatve ca tadaprayuktā naivāgnihotrādibhir dārāḥ prayoktuṃ śakyāḥ | tadabhāvāc ca kṛtadāreṣu caritārthatayā yāvajjīvaśrutyanadhikṛtānāṃ kim ity āśramāntaraṃ na syāt |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> cotpattiṃ vidhayo na prayuñjate | utpannasya tu dārādeḥ svotpattihetvapāye 'pi svarūpānapāyāt tadapekṣatve 'py adhikāracodanānām avirodha eva | na hi kāmāpāye dārāṇām atathātvam, anyathānekapatnīkasyaikapatnīviṣayakāmāpagamād apatnīkatvaprasaṅgāt smṛtivirodho 'pi syāt |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">naiva</span> vayam utpattinimittatvena kāmāpāyād apatnī(ka)tvaṃ brūmaḥ | kiṃ tarhi | svīkṛtaṃ hi strī dravyam | svīkaraṇahetur vivāhasaṃskāraḥ | svīkaraṇaṃ ca dravyāṇāṃ yāvatkāryaṃ yāvatsvarūpaṃ vā svīkartrabhiprāyānusāreṇa | tatra yady atyantakāmākṛṣṭacetanas tadādāv eva yāvajjīvacodanām ālocya svarūpāśrayatvenaivātyantāyodvāhakarmaṇā svīkuryāt, īṣatkāmākṛṣṭacetanas tu yāvadartham, ā valīpalitasaṃbhavāt santānārthatayā vā putrotpatter eva svīkaraṇadvāratvād uktāvadhyantataiva | dārābhāvāc cākṛtadārasyeva yāvajjīvaśrutir aniyoktry eva | atas tadvirodho 'py anāśaṅkanīyaḥ | svīkaraṇāvadhivyavasthāyāṃ tu jīvanaśruteḥ kṛtadārādhikāratvād evaudāsīnyam ity aviruddhā krameṇāpi catuḥsamuccayasmṛtiḥ | evaṃ ca jarāmaryavacanam apy apekṣitāvadhisamarpakatvāt smṛtimūlatvena sālambanaṃ bhavati, anyathā tu nirālambanatvād anarthakam eva syāt | gautamīyam api yāvajjīvapakṣāṅgīkaraṇenaiva "aikāśramyaṃ tv ācāryāḥ" (GDh 3.36) iti vyākhyeyam | pratyakṣeṇaiva kāmenātmasātkṛtadārān prati tathaiva vidhānād gārhasthyasyety abhiprāyaḥ | evaṃ cāvadhiparyavasānād dārābhāva eva | ataś cāsmin pakṣe putrādiṣu tatpālakatvenādhikṛteṣu svabhāryāṅgīkaraṇapravartiketi viṣayabhedena vikalpasaṃbhavād aviśeṣeṇaiva hi yāvajjīvaśrutiḥ | puruṣamedhayājinaś cecchāyāraṇyagamanopadeśād ubhayoś ca pratyakṣatvād viṣayavyavasthāśrayaṇam aviruddham | sapatnīkasya tu vaikhānasatvaṃ yāyāvarādikalpavac chrutyaviruddham eva | ataś cāsmin pakṣe sāgnikasyaivāraṇyāśrayaṇaṃ, na śrāmaṇakānusāreṇāgnyādhānam | yāvajjīvapakṣāṅgīkaraṇe tu jarādisaṃyogād bhāryāmaraṇe vāpavṛttakāmasya ca tadasaṃbhave kiṃ vanasthādhikāro 'stīti, utsannābhilāṣasya tāvad dārādyāharaṇahetvabhāvād asty eva, itarasya tu vicāryam |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">apara āha</span>: udvāhakāla eva hi yenaiva nirūpitaṃ mayāśramāntaram apy āstheyam iti tasya tadavadhika evaṃ hi dārasaṃyoga iti tadanusārī ca jīvanādhikāro 'pi tadaivāpamṛjyate | yena tv ādāv evāmaraṇāntaḥ patnīsaṃyogo 'vadhṛtaḥ, tadanusāreṇa cāmaraṇād evāgnihotrādyadhikāraḥ | tasyotsannābhilāṣitve 'pi ca saṃkalpānapagamāj jīvanaśrutyavaruddhasya kutas tadāśrayāntarapratipattir iti | tathā ca smaranti |

                    	punar dārakriyāṃ kuryāt punar ādhānam eva ca | iti | (MDh 5.168)

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">tad etad vicāryam</span> | sarvathāśramasamuccayo 'stīti naḥ pakṣaḥ, sa caivam apy upapannaḥ, pūrvokta eva tu jyāyān iti saṃpradāyaḥ | "punar dārakriyām" ity etat tv apravṛttāśramāntaraviṣayam evety eṣā dik ||

 

_ubhayathāpi ca vanasthāśramapravṛttim avyāhatāṃ manyamānaḥ prastauti |_

 

**              	sutavinyastapatnīkas tayā vānugato vane |**

**              	vānaprastho brahmacārī sāgniḥ saupāsanaḥ kṣamī || 3.45 ||**

 

syād iti śeṣaḥ | "tapo vedavidāṃ śuddhisādhanaṃ kṣāntir viduṣām" (YDh 3.33) iti tad idānīṃ prapañcayati | vānapratha iti viśeṣāśramiṇo nāmadheyam | sa kadācit pūrvoktanyāyānusāreṇa sahaiva patnyā vanaṃ gacched, vinyasya vā sutādiṣu patnīm | yadā ca sapatnīkas tadā tayānugato 'pi vane vasan brahmacāry eva syād iti abhiprāyaḥ | pakṣāntare tu sāmarthyaprāptatvād avācyam evaitat | sāgnir iti vaitānikābhiprāyam | saupāsana āvasathyayuktaḥ | gatārtham anyat || 45 ||

 

_ayaṃ cāsya viśeṣaḥ |_

 

**              	aphālakṛṣṭenāgnīṃś ca pitṝn devātithīṃs tathā |**

**              	bhṛtyāṃś ca tarpayec chaśvac chmaśrulomabhṛd ātmavān || 3.46 ||**

 

sāgnikagamanapakṣe 'gnihotrādisādhanatvenāphālakṛṣṭavidhānam | pakṣāntare tu vaikhānasaśāstroktasyaivamādeḥ pradarśanārtha upanyāsaḥ | tathāśabdaś ca pakṣadvaye 'pi tacchāstrānusāreṇa dīkṣādiviśeṣaprakāraparigrahārthaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 46 ||

 

_atithipūjādyartham eva ca |_

 

**              	ahno māsasya ṣaṇṇāṃ vā tathā saṃvatsarasya vā |**

**              	arthasya nicayaṃ kuryāt kṛtam āśvayuje tyajet || 3.47 ||**

 

tathāśabdaḥ saṃvatsarād arvāg aniyamārtham || 47 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

**              	dāntas triṣavaṇasnāyī nivṛttaś ca pratigrahāt |**

 

apratyākhyeyatayā vihitād apīty abhiprāyaḥ ||

 

_sarvadaiva ca |_

 

**              	svādhyāyavān dānaśīlaḥ sarvasattvahite rataḥ || 3.48 ||**

 

_ātmabharaṇāya tu |_

 

**              	dantolūkhalikaḥ kālapakvāśī vāśmakuṭṭakaḥ |**

**              	śrautasmārtaṃ phalasnehaiḥ karma kuryāt kriyās tathā || 3.49 ||**

** **

dantair evolūkhalārthaṃ saṃpādayitā dantolūkhalikaḥ | satuṣānnabhoja ity arthaḥ | aśmakuṭṭako vā syād aśmanā saṃskṛtya vituṣaṃ bhakṣayitety arthaḥ | śaktyapekṣayā caivamādayaḥ sarva eva vikalpā yojyāḥ | kālapakvāśitāvacanam agnipakvārtham | nityatvenaivāpratiṣiddhākṣādiphalasnehais tv ājyasādhyaṃ śrautasmārtādikaṃ karma kuryāt | kriyāś ca vanasthaśāstravihitāḥ | tathā taduktaprakāreṇaivety arthaḥ || 49 ||

 

_svaśaktyanusariṇaiva ca |_

 

**              	cāndrāyaṇair nayet kālaṃ kṛcchrair vā vartayet sadā |**

**              	pakṣe gate vāpy aśnīyāt māse vāhani vā gate || 3.50 ||**

 

punar gata ity vacanam uktakālavyatirekeṇāpi yathāsāmarthyaṃ vikalpārtham | spaṣṭam anyat || 50 ||

 

_nityaṃ cāpramāditvena |_

 

**              	śucir bhūmau svaped rātrau divasaṃ prapadair nayet |**

**              	sthānāsanavihārair vā yogābhyāsena vā punaḥ || 3.51 ||**

 

rātrāv iti divānivṛttyartham | prapadair iti agrocchritapāda ity arthaḥ | sthānādīni spaṣṭāni | yogābhyāso vakṣyamāṇaḥ | punar iti prapadādibhiḥ | punaḥ punar viśramyety arthaḥ || 51 ||

 

_yathāsāmarthyaṃ ca |_

 

**              	grīṣme pañcāgnimadhyastho varṣāsu sthaṇḍileśayaḥ |**

**              	ārdravāsāś ca hemante śaktyā vāpi tapaś caret || 3.52 ||**

 

sthaṇḍilavacanam āvaraṇanivṛttyartham | ṛjv anyat || 52 ||

 

_sarvaprakārasya vanasthasyāyam evāśramasarvasvabhūtaḥ paramo dharmaḥ |_

 

**              	yaḥ kaṇṭakair vitudati candanair yaś ca limpati |**

**              	akruddho 'parituṣṭaś ca samas tasya ca tasya ca || 3.53 ||**

 

vitudati vividhaṃ kaṇṭakādibhir vyathayatīty arthaḥ | evam uktaprakāreṇaiva vanasthāśramaṃ pālayet || 53 ||

 

**              	agnīn vāpy ātmasāt kṛtvā vṛkṣāvāsī mitāśanaḥ |**

**              	vānaprasthagṛheṣv eva yātrārthaṃ bhaikṣam ācaret || 3.54 ||**

 

sapatnīkasya ca patnīmaraṇe patnyā evātmārdhabhūtāyā agnibhir yo dāhaḥ tad evātmasamāropaṇam anyasya tu pravṛttāśramasyāśaktau vā vairāgyātiśaye vāyaṃ vidhiḥ | anenaiva vādita eva pravṛttir ity avaseyam || 54 ||

 

_vānaprasthāntarābhāve tu |_

 

**              	grāmād āhṛtya vā grāsān aṣṭau bhuñjīta vāgyataḥ|**

 

āhṛtyeti bhikṣākālavyatirekeṇa grāmapreśanivṛttyartham | vāgyata iti grāmajanair asaṃbhāṣaṇārtham | bhojane tu vāgyamanasya prāptatvād avācyam ||

 

_vairāgyātiśaye jñānātiśaye vā |_

 

**              	vāyvaśanaḥ prāgudīcīṃ gacched vāvarṣmasaṃkṣayāt || 3.55 ||**

 

vāyvaśano niraśana ity arthaḥ | ā varṣmasaṃkṣayād iti | varṣma śarīram ā śarīrasaṃkṣayād ity arthaḥ | āśramasaṃbandhiphalaviśeṣānupadeśād duṣkaratvāc cāyam āśramo naiyamika ity avagamyate | yogābhyāsopadeśāc cāpavargasādhanatvāt kaivalyaprāptisādhanam | tathā cāmnyāyaḥ: "sarva ete puṇyalokā bhavanti brahmasaṃstho 'mṛtatvam eti" (ChU 2.23.1) iti || 55 ||

 

**iti vānaprasthadharmaprakaraṇam |**

** **

**atha yatidharmaprakaraṇam |**

 

_evaṃ yathoktavidhyarthānuṣṭhānāt pratiṣiddhārthopekṣaṇāc cotpannavairāgyatayā saṃjātasamyagvijñānaḥ paraṃ brahmāpipāyeṣuḥ nirastākhilasāṃsārikasukhāsvādābhilāṣaḥ svarucivaikalpikatvena |_

 

**              	gṛhād vanād vā kṛtveṣṭiṃ sarvavedasadakṣiṇām |**

**              	prājāptyāṃ tadante tān agnīn āropya cātmani || 3.56 ||**

**              	adhītavedo japakṛt putravān annado 'agnimān |**

**              	śaktyā ca yajñakṛn mokṣe manaḥ kuryāt tu nānyathā || 3.57 ||**

 

prājāpayteṣṭisvarūpaṃ samāropaṇaprakāraś ca saṃnyāsavidhānaśāstrād evāvaseyam | mokṣe manaḥ kuryāt caturtham āśramam āśrayed ity arthaḥ | tuśabdo 'dhītavedādikrameṇaivety avadhāraṇārthaḥ | nānyatheti tu sāmarthyaprāptatvāt praśaṃsārtho nityānuvādaḥ | tathā ca svāyaṃbhuvam |

                    	anadhītya dvijo vedān anutpādya tathātmajān |

                    	aniṣṭvā caiva yajñaiś ca mokṣam icchan vrajaty adhaḥ || iti | (MDh 6.37)

<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> anadhītavedasya kāmaṃ mā bhūt pārivrājyaṃ, putrādyabhāve tu ko virodhaḥ | uktam etad: "rāgiṇāṃ eva gārhasthyam" iti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">tad yadi</span> kṛtadāro 'pi putrādyutpattāv aprayatyaiva pārivrājam āśrayet tataś codanārthātikramān "mokṣam icchan vrajaty adhaḥ" iti yuktam eva | vītarāgaviṣayatayā tu "yam icchet tam āvaset" (VaDh 7.3) ity uktam eva | spaṣṭam anyat || 56–57 ||

 

                    	**sarvabhūtahitaḥ śāntas tridaṇḍī sakamaṇḍaluḥ |**

**              	ekārāmaḥ parivrajya bhaikṣārthaṃ grāmam āśrayet || 3.58 ||**

 

sarvebhyo 'pakāribhyo 'pi bhūtebhyo 'nabhidroheṇa hitaḥ sarvabhūtahitaḥ | yad vā ātmābhedadarśanena sarvabhūtaḥ sarvātmabhāvāc cānabhidrogdhā bhavaty eva | hitaḥ śānta iti viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatvaṃ, bhavaty aśānto vyabhicārādinā hitaḥ sāṃkhyādiyogānusāreṇāhito 'pi śāntaḥ tadvyavacchedārthaṃ hitaḥ śānta iti | yad vā hito hiṃsānārambhakaḥ śānto 'nugrahānārambhakaḥ | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "hiṃsānugrahayor anārambhī" iti (GDh 3.24–25) | tridaṇḍī manovākkāyadaṇḍābhiprāyeṇa "vāgdaṇḍo'tha manodaṇḍaḥ" ityādi (MDh 12.10) | tridaṇḍasaṃyogenaiva kamaṇḍalvādisaṃbandha iti gamyate | eka evāramate yas tv ātmaratitvena, sa ekārāmaḥ | evaṃ grāmād ucchinnābhilāṣaḥ parivrajyāraṇyanityo bhūtvā bhikṣārtham eva grāmam āśrayet, nānyadā grāme muhūrtam ātiṣṭhed ity abhiprāyaḥ || 58 ||

 

                    	**apramattaś cared bhaikṣaṃ sāyāhne 'nupalakṣitaḥ |**

**              	rahite bhikṣukair grāme yātrāmātram alolupaḥ || 3.59 ||**

 

stryādisaṃdarśanād atyantajitendriyatve 'pi pramādī mā bhūd ity apramattaś caret | bhaikṣaṃ bhikṣāṇāṃ samūho bhaikṣam | tataś caikānnanivṛttiḥ | sāyāhno 'parāhṇaḥ, tasmin | anupalakṣitaḥ bhikṣālābhanimittena pāṇḍityādinātmānam aprakhyāpayann ity arthaḥ | aparāhṇe 'pi ca yadā sarvabhikṣukair grāmo rahitas tadā | yātrāmātraṃ śarīradhāraṇamātrārtham | alolupaḥ alampaṭaḥ | yad vā dvividhaparivrājakābhiprāyaṃ bhikṣāṭanadvaividhyam atrocyate | tatra apramattaś cared ity anenaikānnapratiṣedhena tridaṇḍādyupalakṣitasya bhaikṣopaseśaḥ | itareṇa tridaṇḍādyanupalakṣitasya jñānabhikṣor yātrāmātram ekānnopadeśaḥ | tenaiva ca rahite sopalakṣaṇabhikṣukair grāma iti kālāntaropadeṣaḥ | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "bhikṣārthī grāmam iyāj jaghanyam anivṛttaṃ caret" (GDh 3.14–15) ity ekānnābhiprāyeṇaivāha | anyathā tu bhaikṣārtīty evāvakṣyat | jaghanyam iti ca bhikṣukāntarāpekṣayaiva kālavacanam | yat tu saṃvartoktam,

                    	aṣṭau bhikṣāḥ samādāya prakṣālya niśi vāgyataḥ |

iti, tat sopalakṣaṇaviṣayam | itarasya tv ekabhikṣaṇam eva | tathā ca śrutiḥ: "athānyaḥ parivrāḍ ekaśāṭīparihito muṇḍa udarapātry araṇyanityo bhikṣārthī" iti | anenaitad eva spaṣṭīkroti || 59 ||

 

_yathāyogaṃ vyavasthayā tu |_

 

                    	**yatipātrāṇi mṛdveṇudārvalābumayāni ca |**

**              	salilaṃ śuddhir eteṣāṃ govālaiś cāvagharṣaṇam || 3.60 ||**

 

mṛnmayādīni yatipātrāṇi bhikṣārthaṃ bhojanārthaṃ ca | caśabdaḥ patrapuṭādyarthaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 60 ||

 

_evaṃ ca nityam utpannavairāgyaḥ pūrvoktakrameṇa vā pārivrājyam āsthāya tataḥ |_

 

                    	**saṃnirudhyendriyagrāmaṃ rāgadveṣau prahāya ca |**

**              	bhayaṃ hitvā ca būtānām amṛtībhavati dvijaḥ || 3.61 ||**

 

parabrahmaprāptir amṛtībhāvaḥ | dvijagrahaṇaṃ brāhmaṇārtham, teṣām eva saṃnyāsopadeśāt | ṛjv anyat || 61 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**kartavyāśayaśuddhis tu bhikṣukeṇa viśeṣataḥ |**

**              	jñānotpattinimittatvāt svātantryakaraṇāya ca || 3.62 ||**

 

āśayaḥ śarīraṃ tacchuddhiḥ pavanajayādinā kartavyā jñānabhikṣuṇāpi, viśeṣatas tv itareṇa bhikṣukeṇa | sopalakṣaṇaparivrājakeneti yāvat | jñānotpattinimittatvād viśuddhāśayasyaiva hi jñānotpattir ity abhiprāyaḥ | svātantryakaraṇāya ca parakāyapraveśādisiddhyartham || 62 ||

 

_atha kim āśayaśuddhyādinā svātantryakaraṇam evātra paramārthaḥ | nety ucyate | svātantryasyāhiraṇyagarbhalokamātrajayahetoḥ kṣayiṣṇutayā ca saṃsārahetutvād duḥkharūpataiva | ato niratiśayānandāvāptyarthaṃ svātantryakaraṇamātraparitoṣiṇā na bhavitavyam | kiṃ tarhi |_

 

                    	**avekṣyo garbhavāsaś ca karmajā gatayas tathā |**

**              	ādhayo vyādhayaś caiva jarā rūpaviparyayaḥ || 3.63 ||**

**              	bhavo jātisahasreṣu priyāpriyaviparyayaḥ |**

**              	dhyānayogena saṃdṛśyaḥ sūkṣma ātmātmani sthitaḥ || 3.64 ||**

 

garbhavāsādayo hy āhiraṇyagarbhavyāpinaḥ kleśāḥ, tāṃś cāvekṣya tatsvarūpālocanād virakto vyutthāya dhyānayogena vakṣyamāṇaprakāreṇa sūkṣmaḥ paramātmā vijñānātmany evāvyatirekeṇāvasthitaḥ samyag draṣṭavyaḥ | sarvam eva hi karmakāṇḍam asāratayā mantavyam ity abhiprāyaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 63–64 ||

 

_yataś caitad evam, ataḥ |_

 

**              	nāśramaḥ kāraṇaṃ dharme kriyamāṇo bhaved dhi saḥ |**

 

karmapakṣāntargater āśramaparigraho 'py asāra ity abhiprāyaḥ |

 

**              	ato yad ātmano 'pathyaṃ parasya na tad ācaret || 3.65 ||**

 

parasya prakṛṣṭasyādvaitasya paramātmano yad apathyaṃ saṃsārakāraṇaṃ karmādi na tad ācaret | dhyānayogenaiva tu nityaṃ paramātmano nididhyāsanaṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evaṃ sati yadṛcchāpracāritaiva prāpnoti, karmaṇo 'naṅgīkaraṇāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span> | paralokārthatayā hi karmaṇo 'naṅgīkaraṇaṃ, kriyamāṇaṃ hi karma paralokārambhakaṃ mā bhūd iti vihitasyānanuṣṭhānam | niṣiddhaṃ punar anuṣṭīyamānam eva paralokārambhakam iti tatparijihīrṣayā niṣiddheṣu yathāniṣedham eva vartitavyam || 65 ||

 

_evaṃ cet karmasaṃnyāsinām api pratiṣiddhārthavarjam aviruddhaṃ manyamāna āha |_

 

                    	**satyam asteyam akrodho hrīḥ śaucaṃ dhīr dhṛtir damaḥ |**

**              	saṃyatendriyatā vidyā dharmaḥ sārva udāhṛtaḥ || 3.66 ||**

 

vidhisvarūpatve 'pi ca satyādīnām anṛtavarjanādirūpatayā pratiṣiddhapakṣīyatvam evety avirodhaḥ | hrīr lajjā | varjanīyatayā ca tadupanyāsaḥ punar ājananābhiprāyeṇa vā kartavyatāyām apy avirodhaḥ | mahaty eveyaṃ viduṣo lajjā yat pāratantryeṇa garbhavāsādikleśavaj janmasaṃgatiḥ | śaucaṃ tu trividham apy apavargānuguṇyāt kartavyatayaivopadiśyate | dhīḥ prajñā | dhṛtir dhāraṇā | damo dvandvasahiṣṇutā | saṃyatendriyatā spaṣṭaiva, rūpādiprapañcoparatidhyānaṃ vā | vidyā brahmaṇaḥ sākṣātkaraṇam | sarvaṃ caitat satyādi tadaṅgatayopadiśyamānaṃ karmasaṃnyāsinām apy aviruddham ity abhipretyāha: ayaṃ satyādiko "dharmaḥ sārva udāhṛtaḥ" iti | sarveṣām ayaṃ sārvaḥ | udāhṛta ity udāharaṇārtham etat | anyad api bhikṣāṭanādi sarvaviṣayam aviruddham ity avaseyam | ataś ca paramahaṃsānām api na kāmacāratety abhiprāyaḥ | ataḥ sūktaḥ sopalakṣaṇādibhedena parivrājakāśramaḥ |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">atra kecid</span> imaṃ pārivrājyaprakārabhedam abhyasūyanta sopalakṣaṇam eva pārivrājyaṃ manyante | tathā coktaṃ dakṣeṇa |

                    	yastaital lakṣaṇaṃ nāsti prāyaścittī na cāśramī | iti |

vasiṣṭhenāpi: "parivrājakaḥ sarvabhūtābhayadakṣiṇāṃ dattvā pratiṣṭheta" (VaDh 10.1) ity upakramya taddharmakalāpam abhidhāyopasaṃhṛtam: "yajñopavīty udakamaṇḍaluhastaḥ śucir brāhmaṇo vṛṣalānnavarjī na hīyate brahmalokāt" iti (VaDh 10.31) | tridaṇḍasaṃyogenaiva kamaṇḍalvādisaṃgatir ity uktam eva | ato 'nupalakṣaṇaḥ parivrāḍ iti durbhaṇam | bhikṣāṭanaślokas tv anyathaiva vyākhyātaḥ | prasiddhasvāyaṃbhuvādiśāstravyatiriktāni tu smṛtyantarāṇy aspaṣṭamūlatvād evaitadvirodhe 'nādṛtyāny eva | kiṃ cehāpi śaucasya sarvadharmatvam, yajñopavītaṃ ca śaucāṅgam, atas tenāpi sarvārthenaiva bhāvyam | evaṃ cet kathaṃ tadabhāvaḥ parivrājakasyāśaṅkyeta | ato 'py ayuktataiva | samācāravirodhaś ca sthita evety eṣā dik |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">atrābhidhīyate</span> | apavargārthaṃ hi pārivrājyaṃ jñānaikasādhanam | na tatra karmaṇā prayojanam ity uktam eva | yat tu vācanikatvena tridaṇḍādidhāraṇam, tad apy ādyapārivrājyaviṣayam eva | itarasya tv āśramaniyamānaṅgīkaraṇaṃ karmapakṣīyatvena | uktaṃ ca: "nāśramaḥ kāraṇaṃ dharme" iti | yat tu vāsiṣṭham: "yajñopavīty udakamaṇḍaluhastaḥ" (VaDh 10.1) iti, tad apy akarmasaṃnyāsiviṣayam eva | katham avagamyate: "muṇḍo 'mamo 'parigrahaḥ" (VaDh 10.6) ity upakramya tataḥ kalpāntaratvena, "brāhmaṇakule vā yal labheta tad bhuñjīta" (VaDh 10.24) iti viśeṣānukramaṇād, āditaś ca "muṇḍo 'mamo 'parigrahaḥ" (VaDh 10.6) ity anena karmasaṃnyasinām akhilayajñopavītādiparigrahapratiṣedhāt | ata eva cetarārthaṃ punar yajñopavītādipratiprasavaḥ | anyathā tv avirodhitayaiva prāptatvāt tadvacanam asamañjasaṃ syāt | na cāviśeṣeṇa pratiprasava ity āśaṅkanīyaṃ, kramabhedenopanyāsāt | anyathā hi "ekaśāṭīparihito 'jinena vā" (VaDh 10.9–10) iti vāsaḥpratiprasavānantaram etad apy uktam abhaviṣyat | prakārabhede tv avirodhaḥ | vāśabdasya ca vyavasthayaivopapannatvād anyāyyavikalpanā na syāt | smṛtyantare tu vispaṣṭaiva vyavasthāśramāṇām:


    athānyaḥ parivrāḍ ekaśāṭīparihito muṇḍa udarapātry araṇyanityo 'śaktau bhikṣārthī grāmaṃ praviśet susāyaṃ pradakṣiṇenāvicikitsan sārvavarṇikaṃ bhikṣācaraṇam abhiśastapatitavarjam ayajñopavītī śaucaniṣṭhaḥ kāmam ekaṃ vaiṇavaṃ daṇḍam ādadīta |

ityādi | āmnyāyaś ca: "vyutthāyātha bhikṣācaryaṃ caranti" (BāU 3.5.1) iti samastaiṣaṇāpratiṣedhena karmavyutthānaṃ darśayati | tathā ca: " bālyaṃ pāṇḍityaṃ ca nirvidyātha muniḥ" ity uktvā "tato vyutthāya maunaṃ cāmaunaṃ ca nirvidyeta" (BāU 3.5.1) ity amaunam āśramāntaravihitaṃ tadvihitaṃ maunaṃ ubhayam apy apāsya jñānaikaniṣṭho 'nantaram atha brāhmaṇaḥ paramahaṃsaḥ syād ity abhiprāyaḥ | tathā cāśramānavakḷptiṃ darśayati: "sa brāhmaṇaḥ kena syād yena syāt tenedṛśa eva bhavati" iti (BāU 3.5.1) | nātrāśramaniyamavyapadeśaḥ, karmapakṣīyatvād āśramavidhānasya | anyathā ca virodhād asamañjasataiva syāt | ataḥ sūktam "nāśramaḥ kāraṇaṃ dharme" ityādi | yat tu śaucāṅgatayā yajñopavītaprāptir iti, tad vidyamānopavītaviṣayatayaivāvaseyam, tadabhāve 'pi stryādīnāṃ śaucāvighātāt | yathā copavītādyaprāptis tathoktam eva | ataś caivamādayo 'pi nindārthavādā vidyamānaviṣayatayaiva draṣṭavyāḥ |

                    	vinā yajñopavītena muktakakṣyaśikho 'pi vā |

                    	akṛtvā pādaśaucaṃ ca nācānto 'pi viśudhyati || iti |

anyathā viśikhasya brahmacāriṇo 'py aśuddhiprasaṅgaḥ | tasmād vidyamānānām evopavītādīnāṃ śaucāṅgatvād anavadyam | anayā diśā sarvavākyāni yojanīyāni | smṛtyantarebhyaś ca viṣṇvādibhyo viśeṣataś caturvidhaḥ pārivrājyaprakārabhedo 'bhyupagantavyaḥ | evaṃ tāvan mokṣārthatvena pārivrājyam uktam |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">idam idānīṃ cintyate</span>: kutaḥ punar ātmano baddhasya mokṣopadeśo 'yam | yadi tāvat svābhāviko bandhaḥ, tatas taducchedānupapatter duśliṣṭaiva | atha hetvantarāt, tad api śuddhatvād brahmaṇo 'nupapannam eva | kiṃ ca yadi śuddhasyāpy āgantuko bandhahetuḥ syāt, tato mokṣaprayatnānarthakyam eva syād, muktasyāpi tatsaṃbhavāt |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyaṃ</span>, yadi hetvabhyupagamaḥ syāt | tattvāgrahaṇātmakatvenāvidyotthatvāt prapañcasyaivamādicodyānavakāśa eva | na cātmano vyatiriktaṃ vastvantaraṃ pramāṇāvagamyaṃ, yad bandhahetutayocyeta | ātmanaiva tv ātmano 'nupapanna eva bandhādivyavahāraḥ | bhavati tv ajñānād ekasminn apy agrahaṇanimittaś candra iva dvitvapratibhāsaḥ | tattvena brahmaṇo nānyad vastvantaram astīti brahmavidāṃ sthitiḥ | kathaṃ tarhi vijñānātmanāṃ nānevopalabdhiḥ, ajñānanimittaiva sety uktam || 66 ||

 

_imam evārthaṃ yogīndraḥ prapañcayann āha |_

 

                    	**niścaranti yathā lohapiṇḍāt taptāt sphuliṅgakāḥ |**

**              	sakāśād ātmanaḥ sarva ātmāno 'pi tathaiva hi || 3.67 ||**

 

<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evaṃ paramātmopādānatvaṃ vijñānātmanām uktam svābhāvikatvena | yathaivāgnivārṇāt taptāl lohapiṇḍād viṣphuliṅgāḥ svabhāvād eva nimittāntarānapekṣā niścaranti, evaṃ paramātmanaḥ sakāśād vijñānātmāno 'pīty asyārthaḥ |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span>, upādānapakṣasya pratyuktatvāt | kas tarhy asyārthaḥ | abhinnasyāpi brahmaṇo 'yam avidyotthaḥ prapañca iti | yathānityenābinnasyāpi tad agrahaṇāt piṇḍād viṣphuliṅgatayā bheda upādānopādeyatvaṃ ca pratibhāsate, evam evābhinnasyāpi paramātmano vijñānātmāno 'bhinnās tadupādānāś ca tattvāgrahaṇāt pratibhāsanta ity anavadyam | evam api yathā dvaitāśrayā dharmādharmādivyavasthopapadyate karmakāṇḍāvirodhitvaṃ ca, tathopariṣṭād vakṣyāmaḥ || 67 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvad avicchinno 'vidyayā vijñānātmānekaduḥkhahetau saṃsāre yathā parivartate, tathā prapañcayati |_

 

                    	**tatrātmā hi svayaṃ kiṃcit karma kiṃcit svabhāvataḥ |**

**              	karoti kiṃcid abhyāsād dharmādharmabhavātmakam || 3.68 ||**

 

tatra asmin dvaitaprapañce 'vasthito vijñānātmā svayam eva kiṃcit karma karoti yathā vihitānuṣṭhānaṃ, kiṃcit svabhāvato jātamātra eva stanapānādi, kiṃcid abhyāsād vyutthāyāraṇyavāsādi  | dharmādharmabhavātmakaṃ stanapānādi dharmādharmavyatiriktaṃ bhavātmakam | atha vā dharmādharmābhyāṃ nimittabhūtābhyāṃ saṃsārabījatvena bhavātmakam iti yojyam | dharmādharmayor apy vidyāntargatatvād bhrāntyaiva saṃsārabījatvaṃ niḥsaṅgatvād brahmaṇo 'vaseyam | kathaṃ punar niḥsaṅgaṃ brahmety avagacchāmaḥ, ajātatvād brahmaṇaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> jāyata evātmā | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">na hi</span>, prāg api janmano vidyamānatvāt || 68 ||

 

_kathaṃ tarhi jātavyapadeśaḥ kathaṃ vā prāg janmano bhāvaḥ | ucyate |_

 

                    	**nimittam akṣaraṃ kartā boddhā brahma guṇī vaśī |**

**              	ajaḥ śarīragrahaṇāt sa jāta iti kīrtyate || 3.69 ||**

 

kim idaṃ śarīragrahaṇād iti, śarīratayā vyatirekāvagamād ity arthaḥ | vyatirekāvagamanimittatvena cākṣaratve 'pi brahmaṇaḥ kartṛtvādyupapattiḥ, bhoddhṛtayā ca samyagjñānotpattyā paraprāptyā brahmatvaṃ, viparyayāc ca rāgadveṣādibhir guṇair vaśīkṛtasyāpy anucchinna eva janmasaṃbandhaḥ | tataś cājñānataḥ śarīragrahaṇāj jāta ity upapannam || 69 ||

 

_idānīm ajñānātirekāc charīragrahaṇaṃ prapañcayati |_

 

**              	sargādau sa yathākāśaṃ vāyuṃ jyotir jalaṃ mahīm |**

**              	sṛjaty ekottaraguṇāṃs tathādatte 'bhavann api || 3.70 ||**

 

yathaiva hi bhagavān prajāpatir mahāpralayottarakālam ādisarge prajāḥ sisṛkṣur mahābhūtāny ākāśādīni pṛthivyantāni śabdasparśarūparasagandhair ekadvitricatuṣpañcaguṇayuktāni jagannirvṛttyarthaṃ sṛjati, evam evāyaṃ pratijanmadharmādyanugṛhītaḥ svayam evādatte | abhavann api anutpadyamāno 'pi śarīranirvṛttyartham ity arthaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca mahāpralayasarjane naiva piṇḍitair iṣyete sraṣṭur anupasthānādidoṣaprasaṅgād iti vadadbhiḥ | pāramārthikatve saty evamādicodyaprasaṅgo 'pi syāt | ajñānalakṣaṇe tu prapañcavilāse 'nupapatticodyaṃ cācodyam eva | yadi ca svarūpe 'py āgamaḥ pramāṇaṃ, tadānanyaparāgamapratipanne 'rthe pramāṇāntaravirodhābhidhānam ayuktam eva | yad vā paramatanirāsāyaivāyaṃ ślokaḥ | yathaiva hi sraṣṭāram icchatāṃ sargādau prajāpatir ākāśādīni śarīravyavahārasiddhyartham utpādayati, evam evāsaty api sraṣṭari svayam evāvidyānibandhanaprapañcānusāreṇābhavann apy ajāyamāno janmavyapadeśāya ādatte gṛhṇātīty arthaḥ || 70 ||

 

_yathā cājñānanibandhana eva śarīraprapañco na vastunibandhanaḥ, tathā prapañcayati |_

 

                    	**āhutyāpyayyate sūryas tasmād vṛṣṭir athauṣadhiḥ |**

**              	tad annaṃ rasarūpeṇa śukaltvam upagacchati || 3.71 ||**

 

svādhikāranivṛttyartham eva hi hūyamānayānuṣaṅgikaphalatvena āhutyāpyāyyate sūryaḥ | tad uktaṃ jābālipraśne śrutāv api: "vettha yatheti vyomāhutyā" iti prakṛtya, "tasminn etasminn agnau devā reto juhvati tasyā āhuteḥ puruṣaḥ saṃbhavati" iti (ChU 5.3.1–9) || 71 ||

 

_nityānām eva cārthānāṃ kāryatayābhidhānāt prapañcamātram evaitad iti spaṣṭayati |_

 

                    	**strīpuṃsayoḥ saṃprayoge viśuddhe śuklaśoṇite |**

**              	pañca dhātūn svayaṃṣaṣṭhān ādatte yugapat prabhuḥ || 3.72 ||**

 

śuklaśoṇitaviśuddhir bhiṣakchāstrāt pūtigandhādivyudāsenāvaseyā | dhātuśabdo 'yam ākāśādimahābhūtavacanaḥ | tān pañca | svayaṃṣaṣṭhān ādatte | svayaṃṣaṣṭhān iti yathaiva hy atyantāvyatiriktasyaivātmano vyatirikavad upādānavyapadeśo bhrāntinibandhanaḥ, tathaivākāśādīnām apīty avaseyam || 72 ||

 

_asyaiva dārḍhyārthaṃ bhūyaḥ prapañcam āha |_

 

                    	**indriyāṇi manaḥ prāṇo jñānam āyuḥ sukhaṃ dhṛtiḥ |**

**              	dhāraṇāpreraṇe duḥkham icchāhaṃkāram eva ca || 3.73 ||**

**              	prayatnākṛtirūpāṇi svaradveṣau bhavābhavau |**

**              	tasyedam ātmajaṃ sarvam anāder ādim icchataḥ || 3.74 ||**

 

indriyādi sarvam evaitat tasyaivākalaṅkasya brahmaṇo 'nāder ādim icchato vyāmohātirekād ātmano 'vyatireky api vyatiriktavad ābhāsata ity arthaḥ | vijñānātmatām āpannasyāpi cātmīyadharmādharmānusāreṇātmajam evaitad vaicitryaṃ sukhaduḥkhādilakṣaṇam ity avaseyaṃ, yathendriyāṇi kasyacid avikalāni kasyacit tu viparyaya ity evaṃ sarvatra yojyam | indriyāṇi cakṣurādīni hastādīni ca | ubhayātmakatvāt tu manaso bhedenābhidhānam | prāṇādi prasiddham | sukhatve 'pi ca dhṛtes tatkāraṇatvopacārāt pṛthagvacanam | dhāraṇāpreraṇe śarīrasyārthāntarāṇāṃ vā | duḥkhaṃ prasiddham | icchāhaṃkārayoḥ samāsābhidhānaṃ tulyahetutvāt | prayatnaḥ svābhāvikī karmaviśeṣapravṛttiḥ | ākṛtirūpe prasiddhe | samāsakaraṇaṃ svābhāvikatvenaikarūpyāt | svaraḥ śabdaḥ tadgrahaṇaṃ ca sarvaviṣayāṇām upalakṣaṇārtham | bhavaḥ saṃsāraḥ abhavo mokṣaḥ | api ca yathādvaitavyavahārasya pāramārthikatvam apavargānuguṇyaṃ ca tathopariṣṭād vakṣyāmaḥ | vyāmohanibandhanatvāt tu tatpravṛtteḥ sarvatra prapañcābhidhānam aviruddham || 73–77 ||

 

_avidyāvacchinnasya ca brahmaṇaḥ śarīrasaṃbandhaṃ tatsvarūpaṃ ca prapañcayati |_

 

                    	**prathame māsi saṃkledabhūto dhātuvimūrcchitaḥ |**

**              	māsy arbudaṃ dvitīye tu tṛtīye 'ṅgendriyair yutaḥ || 3.75 ||**

 

niṣiktaṃ retaḥ prathame māsi saṃklinnam aghanībhūtaṃ yasya śarīriṇaḥ sa saṃkledabhūtaḥ | dhātavo mahābhūtāni viśeṣātmanābhivyaktāni vimūrcchitāni yasya saḥ dhātuvimūrcchitaḥ | evaṃ ca kalalādikrameṇārbudāvasthāṃ dvitīye prāpya tṛtīye pravibhaktāṅgendriyādhiṣṭhāno bhavati || 75 ||

 

_idānīm aṅgendriyayogaṃ vivecayati |_

 

                    	**ākāśāl lāghavaṃ saukṣmyaṃ śabdaṃ śrotraṃ tathā balam |**

**              	vāyos tu preraṇaṃ ceṣṭāṃ**[^11]** vyūhanaṃ raukṣyam eva ca || 3.76 ||**

**              	agnes tu darśanaṃ paktim auṣṇyaṃ rūpaprakāśanam |**

**              	rasebhyo rasanaṃ śaityaṃ snehakledanamārdavam || 3.77 ||**

**              	bhūmer gandhaṃ tathā ghrāṇaṃ gauravaṃ mūrtim eva ca |**

**              	ātmā gṛhṇāty ataḥ sarvaṃ tṛtīye spandate tataḥ || 3.78 ||**

 

ākāśādibhyo mahābhūtebhyo 'dṛṣṭānusārāl lāghavādīn guṇān śabdādīṃś ca viṣayān śrotrādīnīndriyāṇi ātmā saṃsāraṃ prapitsur ata evāvidyāprapañcānusārād gṛhṇāti | tasmād dvaitavyavahārāntaḥpātī karmānubaddhaḥ spandata ityādi yojyam | pramāṇāntaramūlatvāc cāsyārthasyāparatvāc ca smṛter indriyādīnāṃ bhautikatvāhaṃkāritvādivivekābhiniveśo na kāryaḥ | adhiṣṭhānāni cākāśādibhyaḥ | indriyaśaktayas tu jñānānupātitād ātmaviṣayatayaivāvaseyāḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 76–78 ||

 

_bhiṣakchāstrānusāreṇaiva ca |_

 

**              	dauhṛdasyāpradānena garbho doṣam avāpnuyāt |**

**              	vairūpyaṃ maraṇaṃ vāpi tasmāt kāryaṃ priyaṃ striyāḥ || 3.79 ||**

 

dauhṛdo bhojanādiviśeṣābhilāṣaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat | pramāṇāntarānusāriṇo 'py atrābhidhānam akriyāyāṃ doṣatvajñāpanārtham || 79 ||

 

_evaṃ tṛtīye 'ṅgendriyayuktasya kramaśaḥ |_

 

                    	**sthairyaṃ caturthe tv aṅgānāṃ pañcame śoṇitodbhavaḥ |**

**              	ṣaṣṭe balasya varṇasya nakharomṇāṃ ca saṃbhavaḥ || 3.80 ||**

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**manasā cetasā yukto nāḍisnāyusirātataḥ |**

**              	saptame cāṣṭame caiva tvacāvān smṛtimān api || 3.81 ||**

 

caśabdāt ṣaṣṭhe ca manaādisaṃyogo 'dṛṣṭavaśād bhavaty evety avagantavyam || 81 ||

 

_paripūrnendriyasyāpi tu yasmāt |_

 

**              	punar garbhaṃ punar dhātrīm ojas tasya pradhāvati |**

**              	aṣṭame māsy ato garbho jātaḥ prāṇair vimucyate || 3.82 ||**

 

yasya hi jantor anyasyāṃ dhātryāṃ mātari garbho niṣpannaḥ tasyaivāṣṭame māsi prasavaḥ syāt | tasya caujaḥ prāṇaḥ pūrvasmād garbhāt punar anyaṃ garbhaṃ pūrvāyāś ca dhātryā mātuḥ punar anyāṃ dhātrīṃ mātaraṃ pradhāvati saṃcarati yasmāt, tasmād aṣṭame māsi jātaḥ prāṇair vimucyate na jīvatīty arthaḥ || 82 ||

 

_nirvyūḍhe tv aṣṭame māsi kalyāṇataḥ |_

 

                    	**navame daśame māsi prabalaiḥ sūtimārutaiḥ |**

**              	niḥsāryate bāṇa iva yantracchidreṇa sajvaraḥ || 3.83 ||**

 

pramāṇāntaramūlatvān navamādigrahaṇaṃ māsāntarāṇān apy upalakṣaṇārtham | prabalaiḥ sūtimārutair iti parādhinatayā janmapradarśanaṃ lajjākaratvena vairāgyātiśayārtham | tathaiva spaṣṭayati yantracchidreṇa sajvara iti | evam uttaratrāpy asthisaṃkhyādyupavarṇanādau vyākhyeyam || 83 ||

 

_idam evāvidyāvilasitaṃ bhūyaḥ prapañcayati |_

 

**              	tasya ṣoḍhā śarīraṃ tat ṣaṭ tvaco dhārayanti hi |**

**              	ṣaḍaṅgāni tathāsthnāṃ ca saṣaṣṭiṃ vai śatatrayam || 3.84 ||**

 

māsmin śarīrake kāmopakaraṇatvāropeṇālīkamaṇḍanādiparipoṣaṇaṃ kṛthāḥ | naivaitad yathopalabhyamānaṃ vyāmohahetusamudāyātmakaṃ, kiṃ tarhi, tasyāvibhaktasya brahmaṇaḥ saṃsāragrahaṇāyāvacchedakam | ṣoḍhā ṣaṭprakāram avasthitaṃ pṛthivyādīny adṛṣṭaṃ cety evaṃ ṣoḍhā ṣaḍvikārabhūtaṃ ca pūyaśoṇitādiṣaṭtvacaḥ pracchādya dhārayanti yasmāt, tasmād atrāgraho na kārya iti hiśabdasyārthaḥ | kiṃ ca | ṣaḍaṅgāni śiro bāhū śarīrakāṇḍam ūrū ceti | tathāśabdaḥ prakārārthaḥ, tathābhūtaṃ kuṇapātmakam iti yāvat | ṛjv anyat || 84 ||

 

_idānīṃ ṣaṣṭyadhikaṃ śatatrayam asthnām upapādayati |_

 

                    	**sthālaiḥ saha catuḥṣaṣṭir dantā vai viṃśati nakhāḥ |**

**              	pāṇipādaśalākāś ca tāsāṃ sthānacatuṣṭayam || 3.85 ||**

 

sthālāni dantabandhanāny asthīni dvatriṃśad dantāś ca evaṃ catuḥṣaṣṭiḥ | nakhaviṃśatyā pāṇipādaśalākāviṃśatyā saha pāṇyādisthānacatuṣṭayena cāṣṭottaraśatam | pāṇyādiśalākā aṅgulīmūlāny asthīni tāni yasmin pratiṣṭhitāni tat sthanam | spaṣṭam anyat || 85 ||

 

_tathā |_

 


                            	**ṣaṣṭy aṅgulīnāṃ dve pārṣṇyor gulpheṣu tu catuṣṭayam |**


        **              	catvāry aratnyor asthīni jaṅghayor tāvad eva tu || 3.86 ||**

 

catvārīty arthaḥ | pāṇyoḥ pṛthagvacanād atrāratniśabdas tadvyatirekeṇa draṣṭavyaḥ | evaṃ pūrvaiḥ sahāśītiśataṃ dve ca || 86 ||

 

                    	**dve dve jānukapāloruphalakāṃsasamudbhave |**

**              	akṣaḥ sthālūṣake śroṇiphalake caiva nirdiśet || 3.87 ||**

 

ekaikasmin jānuni kapāladvayaṃ tathaikasminn ūrau phalakādvayam aṃsayor ekaikam akṣādīni caiva nirdiśet | dve dve ity etāni saṃkalitāni ṣoḍaśa pūrvaiḥ saha dvyūnaṃ śatadvayam | akṣaḥ kaṭyasthi | sthālūṣake tadbandhane | spaṣṭam anyat || 87 ||

 

                    	**bhagāsthy ekaṃ tathā pṛṣṭe catvāriṃśac ca pañca ca |**

**              	grīvā pañcadaśāsthīni jatrv aikyaṃ hi tathā hanuḥ || 3.88 ||**

 

etayā triṣaṣṭyā sahaikaṣaṣṭyadhikaṃ śatadvayam | bāhvaṃsayoḥ sandhir jatruḥ | prasiddham anyat || 88 ||

 

                    	**tanmūle dve lalāṭāsthi gaṇḍanāsāghanāsthikā |**

**              	pārśvakāḥ sthālakaiḥ sārdham arbudaiś ca dvisaptatiḥ || 3.89 ||**

 

tanmūle dve lalāṭasthy ekaṃ gaṇḍanāsāpratibandhakam evāsthi gaṇḍanāsāghanāstikety uktam | etāni catvāri dvisaptatyā saha ṣaṭsaptatiḥ || 89 ||

 

                    	**dvau śaṅkhakau kapālāni catvāri śirasas tathā |**

**              	uraḥ saptadaśāsthīni puruṣasyāsthisaṃgrahaḥ || 3.90 ||**

 

pūrvasaṃkalane yad uktam "saṣaṣṭiṃ vai śatatram" iti, tat pūrṇaṃ bhavati || 90 ||

 

_eṣām eva pṛthivyādyākāśāntānāṃ śarīrārambhakāṇāṃ mahābhūtānāṃ guṇāḥ |_

 

**              	gandharūpasparśaśabdās tu viṣayāḥ smṛtāḥ |**

 

_eṣām eva ca grāhakāṇi |_

 

**              	nāsikā locane jihvā tvak śrotraṃ cendriyāṇi tu || 3.91 ||**

 

śārīraprakramād buddhīndriyādhiṣṭhāneṣv ayam aupacārikas tacchabdaḥ śrotraśabdaś ca karṇavacanaḥ tuśabdasāmarthyāt | ṛjv anyat || 91 ||

 

_imāni tu |_

 

**              	hastau pāyur upasthaṃ ca mukhaṃ pādau ca pañcamam |**

**              	karmendriyāṇi jānīyān manaś caivobhayātmakam || 3.92 ||**

 

mukhagrahaṇaṃ tālvādivāgadhiṣṭhanābhiprāyam | pañcamavacanaṃ pāṇyādāv abhedajñāpanārtham | prasiddham anyat || 92 ||

 

_kiṃ ca _|

 

                    	**nābhir ojo gudaṃ śuklaṃ śoṇitaṃ śaṅkhakau tathā |**

**              	mūrdhā ca hṛdayaṃ kaṇṭhaḥ prāṇasyāyatanāni tu || 3.93 ||**

 

jīvanahetoḥ prāṇasyāyuṣo nābhyādīny āyatanāni | āśayaśuddhāv eṣāṃ parijñānopayogitā | evam uttaratrāpi yojyam | pravṛttarudhirādyārambho 'nnarasa ojaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 83 ||

 

_koṣṭhasaṃbandhitayā _|

 

                    	**vapā vapāvahananaṃ nābhiḥ kloma yakṛt plihā |**

**              	kṣudrāntraṃ vṛkakau vastiḥ purīṣādhānam eva ca || 3.94 ||**

**              	āmāśayo 'tha hṛdayaṃ shūlāntraṃ guda eva ca |**

**              	udaraṃ ca gudaḥ koṣṭhyo vistāro 'yam udāhṛtaḥ || 3.95 ||**

 

vapāvahananaṃ vapāntrabandhanam | klomayakṛdādīni tv abhidhānakośān māṃsavikrayibhyo bhiṣakcchāstrād vāvagantavyāni | yathāha |

                    	uśanti tilakaṃ kloma tālakhaṇḍaṃ yakṛt tathā | iti |

tathā |

                    	pakvāśayād adho nāber ūrdhvaṃ cāmāśayaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

ityādi || 94–95 ||

 

_avibhakte 'py avayavaśo vibhajyamāne |_

 

                    	**kanīnike 'kṣiṇī kūṭe śaṣkulī karṇaputrakau |**

**              	gaṇḍau śaṅkhau bhruvau dantāveṣṭāv oṣṭhau kakundarau || 3.96 ||**

**              	vaṅkṣaṇau vṛṣaṇau vṛkkau śleṣmasaṃghātike stanau |**

**              	upajihvikā sphijau bāhū jaṅghe corū sapiṇḍake || 3.97 ||**

**              	tālūdaraṃ vastiśīrṣaṃ cibukaṃ galagaṇḍikā |**

**              	avaṭuś caivam etāni sthānāny atra śarīrake || 3.98 ||**

 

kanīnike akṣitārake | avaśiṣṭe tv akṣiṇī | tacchādane carmaṇī kūṭe | karṇaśaṣkulī spaṣṭe | tacchidre karṇaputrakau | dantāveṣṭau dantānām āveṣṭanāni | kakundarau nitambakūpakau | ūrusaṃdhir vaṅkṣaṇaḥ | vṛṣaṇayor upari vṛkkau | jihvāmūle upajihvikā | abhito gudaṃ māṃsapiṇḍau sphijau | gudasyāntar mūtrādānaṃ vastiḥ | prasiddham anyat || 96–98 ||

 

_asminn eva śarīrake |_

 

                    	**akṣivartmacatuṣkaṃ ca paddhastahṛdayāni ca |**

**              	navacchidrāṇi tāny eva prāṇasyāyatanāni ca || 3.99 ||**

 

vartmacatuṣkam avabodhakam indriyacatuṣṭayaṃ śrotraghrāṇarasasparśānīty arthaḥ | etāny akṣyādīni pañca buddhīndriyāṇi | pāṇipādau karmendriyārthau | caśabdo 'vaśiṣṭānāṃ grāhakaḥ | hṛdayaṃ manaḥ | yāny etāny ekādaśendriyāṇi tāny eva pāṇyādivarjaṃ nava chidrāṇi ca | etāni prāṇasya prādhānyenāyatanāni | śirasi sapta pāyur upasthaṃ cety evaṃ nava cchidrāṇi || 99 ||

 

_kiṃ ca _|

 

                    	**sirāśatāni saptaiva nava snāyuśatāni ca |**

**              	dhamanīnāṃ śate dve tu pañca peśīśatāni ca || 3.100 ||**

 

rudhirasrāvicchidrāṇi sirā | snāyu prasiddham | vāyugrāhiṇyaḥ sirā eva dhamanyaḥ, yāsāṃ pūraṇe sthūlatā recane kṛśatā | medovāhinyaḥ sirā eva peśyaḥ | bhiṣakchāstropayogitvena sthūlaparimāṇam etat || 100 ||

 

_vāyuvijayārthaṃ tu sūkṣmaparimāṇālocanāyedānīm āha |_

 

                    	**ekonatriṃśataṃ lakṣās tathā navaśatāni ca |**

**              	ṣaṭpañcāśac ca nirdiṣṭāḥ sirā dhamanisaṃjñakāḥ || 3.101 ||**

 

nigadoktaḥ ślokaḥ || 101 ||

 

_yogaśāstrābhiprāyacaturaiḥ śarīratattvabubhutsubhiḥ |_

 

**              	trayo lakṣās tu vijñeyāḥ keśaśmaśru manīṣibhiḥ |**

 

romabhedasaṃkhyayeti śeṣaḥ |

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

**              	aṣṭottaraṃ marmaśataṃ dve tu saṃdhīśate tathā || 3.102 ||**

 

vijñeye ity anuṣaṅgaḥ | tathāśabdaḥ śātrāntaroktakeśādiparimāṇavikalpadyotanārthaḥ sarvasmin saṃkhyāprakaraṇe vyakhyeyaḥ || 102 ||

 

_śāstrāntaroktaparimāṇavaikalpikatvenaiva ca |_

 

**              	romṇāṃ koṭyas tu pañcāśat tathā koṭicatuṣṭayam |**

**              	saptaṣaṣṭis tathā lakṣāḥ sārdhāḥ svedāyanaiḥ saha || 3.103 ||**

 

<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> etat keśasaṃkhyādiparimāṇaṃ bādhakānupalambhamātreṇa yadṛcchayābhidhānāt parasparavyāghātāc ca dūrtanikhātapṛthivīmadhyalakṣaṇārthakīlāditulyam ivopalakṣyate | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam evam</span>, śarīranindāparatvāt smṛteḥ | atiśayapuṇyakāribhiś ca purāṇair brahmavidbhir anvayavyatirekābhyām api saṃbhāvyamānatvād adoṣaḥ || 103 ||

 

_etad eva spaṣṭayati |_

 

**              	vāyavīyair vigaṇyante vibhaktāḥ paramāṇavaḥ |**

**              	yady anye ko nu vedaiṣāṃ bhāvānāṃ caiva saṃsthitim || 3.104 ||**

 

sanatkumārādayo vāyuśiṣyā vāyavīyāḥ, tais tāvad ye 'smābhir uktāḥ saṃkhyāviśeṣās te vigaṇyante | yadi tv etebhyo 'pi paramāṇavaḥ paramasūkṣmā anye saṃkhyāviśeṣā bhavanti, bhavantu, na doṣo yasmāt, tasmāt ko nu vedaiṣāṃ paramārthataḥ parimāṇam | śraddhāmātreṇa yathāvagamaṃ kiṃcid abhidhīyata ity abhiprāyaḥ | kiṃ ca bhāvānāṃ ca prāṇinām anekaprakārāṃ vicitrāṃ saṃsthitiṃ ko nu vedeti yojyam || 104 ||

 

_āgamānusāreṇaiva ca |_

 

                    	**rasasya nava vijñeyā jalasyāñjalayo daśa |**

**              	sapta caiva purīṣasya raktasyāṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ || 3.105 ||**

 

svasthasya caitan niṣpannasya dhātuparimāṇaṃ vijñeyam | yat tu kaiścid dhetvanusārād uktam "aniyataṃ mūtrapurīṣam" iti, tad ihāpariniṣpannajātamātraviṣayatvād acodyam || 105 ||

 

_añjalinaiva ca |_

 

                    	**ṣaṭ śleṣmā pañca pittaṃ tu catvāro mūtram eva ca |**

**              	vasā trayo dvau tu medo majjaikārdhaṃ ca mastake || 3.106 ||**

 

eko 'ñjalir majjā mastake cārdham, evam adhyardo 'ñjaliḥ || 106 ||

 

                    	**śleṣmaujasas tāvad eva retasas tāvad eva tu |**

**              	ity etad asthiraṃ varṣma yasya mokṣāya kṛty asau || 3.107 ||**

 

ojo vyākhyātam | tad eva śleṣmaṇaḥ kāraṇabhūtaṃ śleṣmaujaḥ, tasya (tāva?)d evādhyardho 'ñjalir ity arthaḥ | evaṃ retaso 'dhyardha eva | evaṃ yad vyākhyātam asthiram anityaṃ vināśi mahāghoraṃ durlakṣyaṃ saṃsāranimittaṃ varṣma śarīraṃ yasya kṣetriṇaḥ puṇyakṛtaḥ saṃjātavairāgyasyocchinnābhilāṣasya mokṣārthaṃ caturthāśramapratipattyarthaṃ syāt, kṛty asau kṛtakṛtya ity arthaḥ || 107 ||

 

_kaḥ punar atra mokṣaprakāro yeneha punarjanma na syāt, ucyate |_

 

                    	**dvisaptatisahasrāṇi hṛdayād abhiniḥsṛtāḥ |**

**              	hitā nāma hi tā nāḍyas tāsāṃ madhye śaśiprabham || 3.108 ||**

**              	maṇḍalaṃ tasya madhyastha ātmā dīpa ivācalaḥ |**

**              	madhye yas taṃ viditvā tu punar ājāyate na tu || 3.109 ||**

 

saṃsārāpanodanakṣamatvād dhitā ity anvarthasaṃjñaiveyam ity avagantavyam | hiśabdo hetvarthaḥ | yasmāt prāṇātmanaḥ saṃcaraṇārthatvenotkarṣanimittam, tasmād dhitā nāmeti | tāsāṃ madhye śaśiprabhaṃ maṇḍalaṃ hṛdayāntarvarti dhyānaikagamyaṃ yat, tasya madhyastha ātmā dīpa ivetyādinā dṛṣṭāntena spaṣṭīkṛtaḥ | yo 'yaṃ madhye hṛnmaṇḍalasyopalabhyas taṃ viditvā tu saṃsāracakre na punar ājāyate mucyata evety arthaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> cātmanaḥ sarvagatatvān niyatadeśābhidhānam ayuktam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span> | upalabdhimārgopadeśo 'yaṃ, nātmanaḥ svarūpopadeśaḥ | ata eva ca punar viśeṣābhidhānaṃ "madhye yas taṃ viditvā" iti | pradīpadṛṣṭāntas tv ananyaprakāśyatvād vyāpitvāc ca | yathaiva hy avibhaktasyāpi pradīpatejasaḥ pracitataratvenaikatropalambhād ihaivāyam iti vyavacchedābhidhānam, tathaivātmavyavacchedābhimāno 'pīty abhiprāyaḥ || 108–9 ||

 

_asyaiva tu samyag vivekārtham |_

 

**              	jñeyam āraṇyakam ahaṃ yad ādityād avāptavān |**

**              	yogaśāstraṃ ca matproktaṃ jñeyaṃ yogam abhīpsatā || 3.110 ||**

 

"ahaṃ yad ādityād" ityādinā bṛhadāraṇyakam iti jñāpayati | āraṇyakajñānopadeśāc ca vedād evāyam artho 'vagantavyaḥ nānyata ity avagamyate | vedād api cācāryato brahmacaryādhigatād ity "aham ādityād" ityādinā dyotitam | na caivaṃ sati smṛtyānarthakyam | kiṃ tarhi, vedārthopakaraṇatayā | yogasiddhim ābhimukhyena kartum icchatā "yogaśāstram api matproktaṃ jñeyam" evety abhiprāyaḥ | matproktaṃ vedārthānuguṇam, na tu tadviparītaṃ buddhādyuktam ity abhiprāyaḥ | tatha cōktaṃ svayambhuvā |

                    	ārṣāṃ dharma(pra)vacanaṃ vedaśāstrāvirodhinā |

                    	yas tarkeṇānusaṃdhatte sa dharmaṃ veda netaraḥ || iti | (MDh 12.106)

ṛṣayo brahmavidas teṣām idam ity ārṣaṃ brahmasvarūpapratipattyartham | spaṣṭam anyat || 110 ||

 

_tad idānīṃ vedānuguṇadhyānaprakāraṃ prapañcayati |_

 

                    	**ananyaviṣayaṃ kṛtvā manobuddhismṛtīndriyam |**

**              	dhyeya ātmā sthito yo 'sau hṛdaye dīpavat prabhuḥ || 3.111 ||**

 

nāsmād anyo vidyata ity ananya ātmā tadviṣayaṃ manobuddhismṛtīndriyaṃ kṛtvā anyaviṣayatāyā vyāvartyety arthaḥ | kva punaḥ śarīradeśe vartamānasya manobuddhyāder ananyaviṣayatā syāt, tad āha: "hṛdaye" iti | yadā hi bāhyaviṣayoparameṇendriyapravṛttayo hṛdi niyamyante, tadā mano 'pi tadanuvidhānāt svadeśavarty api svaviṣayāt sukhāder apavṛttam akalpakaṃ bhavati | tadadhīnatvāc ca smṛtibuddhyor ātmany avasthānātmano buddhismṛtīndriyasyātmaviṣayatvasiddhiḥ | ato hṛdaye saṃniruddhendriyagrāmam ātmaviṣayatayā pradīpavad abhinno 'pi bhedāvabhāsī vyāpitayā prabhur avyayaḥ paramātmā dhyeya ityādi yojyam || 111 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> etat durvāratvād indriyagrāmasya duḥśakam ivopalakṣyate | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyaṃ</span> duḥśakam, na tv aśakyam eva | yataḥ paśya |_

 

                    	**yathāvadhānena pumān sāma gāyaty avidhy ayam |**

**              	sāvadhānas tathābhyāsāt paraṃ brahmādhigacchati || 3.112 ||**

 

kim atrāśakyam, dṛṣṭaṃ hi praṇihitamanasāṃ sāmagānām ṛkto vivekena durlakṣyām api rathantarādigītim ṛgantarāropitām idam atra sāmety evam avibhāvyaṃ yamavinaṣṭaṃ sāmagānaṃ yathaiva ca pumān eva prasaktabāhyaviṣayamanā apy avidhy ayaṃ sāvadhānaḥ sāma gāyati, evam eva dhyānābhyāsāt param api brahmādhigacchaty eva | ato 'tra yatnavatā bhāvyaṃ nāśakyam evaitad iti parābhaṅgaḥ kāryaḥ | tathā coktam:

                    	utsekaṃ jaladher dṛṣṭvā tṛṇāgreṇaikabindunā |

                    	aśakyam iti mantavyaṃ na kiṃcit kṛtabuddhinā || iti || 112 ||

 

_ata eva cendriyanirodhakatvena parabrahmaprāptihetor yogasyopāyabhūtaṃ gānam iti manyamānā gītivedavido nāradādayaḥ smaranti |_

 

**              	aparāntakam ullopyaṃ madrakaṃ prakarīṃ tathā |**

**              	auveṇakaṃ sarobindum uttaraṃ gītikāni tu || 3.113 ||**

**              	ṛggāthā pāṇikā dakṣavihitā brahmagītikā |**

**              	geyam etat tadabhyāsakāraṇāc coktasaṃjñakam || 3.114 ||**

 

imāny aparāntakādīni prāyeṇa vastumātrāpādabhāgātmakāni svaviṣayaviśiṣṭāni sapta gītikāni gānaśāstrād evāvaseyāni | tad yathā |

                    	atha vastūni ṣaṭ sapta pañca vāpy aparāntakam |

ityādi | tathā |

                    	ādāv ullopyakasyātha mātrābhiḥ patanair yutā |

iti evamādi mahat tantraṃ granthagauravaprasaṅgād atra na prapañcyate | tathā vastumātrāpādabhāgādiviveko 'pi tat eva mṛgyaḥ | yathā: "svayaṃ vastuṣaṇmātrāḥ" ityādi | ṛggāthā ity atrāpi ca viśiṣṭā eva hy ṛco divyavīṇayā brahmanā gītāḥ | tathā gāthā kāśyapaprajāpatigītā | pāṇikā dakṣavihitā dakṣaprajāpatigītety arthaḥ | brahmastutyarthā gītikā brahmagītikā | sarvam etac coktasaṃjñakaṃ nāradādyuktalakṣaṇaṃ yogamārgopayogitvād geyam | anyaparatvāc copadeśaya nātyabhiniveśaḥ kāryaḥ | yad vā nāradādismaraṇād ihāpi ca prasaṅgābhidhānād vedamūlatvam evānumeyam ity anavadyam || 113–4 ||

 

_bhūyaś ca nāradādyabhiprāyeṇaivāha |_

 

                    	**vīṇāvādanatattvajñaḥ śrutijātiviśāradaḥ |**

**              	tālajñaś cāprayāsena yogamārgaṃ nigacchati || 3.115 ||**

 

śrutir dhvanyātmikā dvāviṃśatiprakārā svaraparimāṇaniyāmikā vijñeyā | jātis tv aṣṭādaśaprakārā ṣaḍjādyā | tālaḥ kālapātātmako mānaviśeṣaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 115 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

**              	gītijño yadi yogena nāpnoti paramaṃ padam |**

 

_tathāpi tu |_

 

**              	rudrasyānucaro bhūtvā tenaiva saha modate || 3.116 ||**

 

anena ca gānādhidevatā rudra ity etad jñāpitam || 106 ||

 

_prāsaṅgikam abhidhāyedānīm idam evātmatattvam atisauhṛdāt kṛtsnaṃ jīvalokam anujighṛkṣur ācāryaḥ spaṣṭayituṃ śāstrārambhaprayojakān eva munīn praṣṭṛtvenopanyasyati sma |_

 

**              	anādir ātmā kathitas tasyādiś ca śarīrakam |**

**              	ātmanaś ca jagat sarvaṃ jagataś cātmasaṃbhavaḥ || 3.117 ||**

 

"nimittam akṣaraṃ kartā" (YDh 3.69) ityādau kathita eveti śeṣaḥ || 117 ||

 

_evaṃ cānupapanne jagataś cātmanaś ca kāryakāraṇabhāve sati |_

 

                    	**katham etad vimuhyāmaḥ sadevāsuramānavam |**

**              	jagad utpannam ātmā ca kathaṃ nv asmin vadasya naḥ || 3.118 ||**

 

kathaṃ nu khalv ayaṃ viruddhaḥ kāryakāraṇabhāvaḥ | asmin virodhe parihārāya naḥ asmākaṃ vadasva kathayety arthaḥ || 118 ||

 

_idānīṃ yogīndras teṣām uttaram āha |_

 

**              	mohajālam apāsyedaṃ puruṣo dṛśyate hi yaḥ|**

**              	sahasrakarapannetraḥ sūravarcāḥ sahasraśaḥ || 3.119 ||**

**              	sa ātmā caiva yajñaś ca viśvarūpaḥ prajāpatiḥ |**

**              	virāṭ ca somarūpeṇa yajñatvam upagacchati || 3.120 ||**

 

grantharūpatayā praśnottarābhidhānaṃ kṛtavyākhyānam eva | māsmin vyāmohaṃ kṛthāḥ | kutārkikoktālīkakucodyānusārimohajālam apanīyākhilaprapañcarūpātirikto vakṣyamāṇayuktyanugrahāt pratyakṣeṇaiva pratyagātmany aparokṣarūpatayā nirastadvitayapratibhāsaḥ puruṣo yo dṛśyate anubhūyate | kathaṃlakṣanaḥ, sahasrakarapannetra ityādilakṣaṇaḥ | sa evātmā yajñaś ca, yajñaśabdaś ca tatkāraṇapṛthivyādimahābhūtavacanaḥ, pṛthivyādīny api sa evety arthaḥ | kathaṃ punaḥ sa evātmā yajñaś ca, yato viśvarūpaḥ prajāpatiś ca saḥ | sarvāṇi bhūtāny asyaivāvibhaktasyātmano rūpāṇi yasmāt, tasmād viśvarūpaḥ | ata eva coktaṃ sahasrakaracaraṇa ityādi | sahasraśabdaś ca bahvartho na saṃkhyārthaḥ, anantajātirūpasaṃbandhenābhinno 'pi ghaṭākāśādivad bhidyamānaḥ sahasraśo dṛśyate | sūryavarcāḥ svayaṃprakāśa ity arthaḥ | svayaṃ ca bhedena prajāsarjanāt prajāpatiḥ virāṭ ca | annaṃ sa eva bhūtvā somādirūpeṇa yajñatvaṃ yajñasādhanatvam upagacchati prāpnotīty arthaḥ || 119–20 ||

 

_tataś ca |_

 

                    	**yo dravyadevatātyāgasaṃbhūto rasa uttamaḥ |**

**              	devān sa saṃtarpya raso yajamānaṃ phalena tu || 3.121 ||**

**              	saṃyojya vāyunā somaṃ nīyate raśmibhis tataḥ |**

**              	ṛgyajuḥsāmavihitaṃ sauraṃ dhāmopanīyate || 3.122 ||**

 

yo 'yam āhutyātmako dravyadevatātyāgasaṃbhūto yājñaḥ somādidravyasya darśanānuvidhāyī sādhāraṇātmako jagatkāraṇabhūtaḥ sūkṣma uttamā rasaḥ sa devān samyak tarpayitvā viśeṣātmanā ca yajamānaṃ phalenānuṣṭhitaniyogatayā saṃyojya tataḥ sādhāraṇātmanā "samiṣṭayajuṣā svāhā vātedhā" ityevaṃ vidyādarśanād vāte prakṣiptaḥ sa vātena somaṃ somamaṇḍalaṃ nīyate | tataś ca saurair eva raśmibhir darśanānugrahād ṛgādimantrārthavādādipratipāditaṃ sauraṃ sthānam upanīyata ityādi | tad etad ṛcāpy uktam: "yam akṣitam akṣitayaḥ pibanti" (TS 2.4.14.1) ityādi || 121–22 ||

 

_yaś cāsau yājño rasaḥ sauraṃ dhāma prāpto jagatkāraṇatvena saṃbhṛtaḥ |_

 

**              	tanmaṇḍalam asau sūryaḥ sṛjaty amṛtam uttamam |**

**              	yajjanma sarvabhūtānām aśanānaśanātmanām || 3.123 ||**

 

(yo 'sau yājño rasaḥ ?) tanmaṇḍalam asau paramātmā sūryaḥ | tad uktam: "sūrya ātmā jagatas tasthuṣaś ca" (RV 1.115.1) iti | asau sūryas tad uttamam amṛtam udakaṃ jagatkāraṇabhūtaṃ sṛjati muñcatīty arthaḥ | tad evodakaṃ viśinaṣṭi: "yajjanma sarvabhūtānām" ityādi | "aśanānaśanātmanām" sthāṇujaṅgamānām ity arthaḥ || 123 ||

 

_yo 'sāv udakabhāvena yājño rasa iha prāptaḥ phalabhūto virāṭtvam annarūpatām āpannaḥ |_

 

                    	**tasmād annāt punar yajñaḥ punar annaṃ punaḥ kratuḥ |**

**              	evam etad anādyantaṃ cakraṃ saṃparivartate || 3.124 ||**

 

tasmād annāt pūrveṇaiva mārgeṇa punaḥ sādhāraṇātmā yajño niṣpadyate tasmāc ca yajñāt tenaiva vāyvādinā mārgeṇa punar virāṭ cānnam, tato 'pi cānnāt tathaiva punaḥ kratur yajñaḥ tataś ca punar apy annam ity evam etad anādinidhanaṃ viśvarūpasya brahmaṇaḥ saṃsārabījaṃ cakrakramāt parivartate | tataś cānyonyakāryakāraṇatve 'py avirodhaḥ || 124 ||

 

_idaṃ cānādinidhanaṃ cakraṃ parivartamānam ālocyāsmābhir uktaḥ |_

 

                    	**anādir ātmā saṃbhūtir vidyate nāntarātmanaḥ |**

**              	samavāyī tu puruṣo mohecchādveṣakarmajaḥ || 3.125 ||**

 

yady anādir ātmā kathaṃ jāyate mriyata iti vyavahārāḥ, uktam: "śarīragrahaṇāt sa jāta iti kīrtyate" iti (YDh 3.69) | paramārthatas tv anādir ātmā nāsyāntarā saṃbhūtir janma ity abhiprāyaḥ | śarīragrahaṇam evākalaṃkasya brahmaṇaḥ kasmād iti cet, naivākṣarasya paramātmanaḥ śarīrasaṃbandhaḥ, śarīrāsaṃsṛṣṭa eva hi saḥ | ayaṃ tv anya eva tato 'vicchinnaḥ śarīrasamavāyī puruṣaḥ avidyāvyāmohād icchādveṣābhyāṃ sādhāraṇaviśeṣātmakatvena ca karmaṇā saṃsṛṣṭo janmavyapadeśabhāg ity avaseyam || 125 ||

 

_ataś cāyaṃ parāvarātmako mūrtāmūrtarūpaḥ sa eva paramātmā |_

 

                    	**sahasrātmā mayo yo va ādideva udāhṛtaḥ |**

**              	mukhabāhūrupajjātās tasya varṇā yathākramam || 3.126 ||**

 

mukhenādhyayanabhojanādikāryasaṃyogāc chraiṣṭhyena ca prāthamyād brāhmaṇasya mukhajatvam evaṃ rakṣaṇādibāhukāryasaṃbandhād bāhujatvam ityādi brahmaṇaḥ pāramārthikamukhādyabhāvāt prapañcanīyam || 126 ||

 

_evam eva pratiṣṭhādipadādikāryayogāt |_

 

                    	**pṛthivī pādatas tasya śiraso dyaur ajāyata |**

**              	nastaḥ prāṇā diśaḥ śrotrāt tvaco vāyur mukhāc chikhī || 3.127 ||**

 

_mānasena darśanena cābhivyaṅgyatvāt |_

 

                    	**manasaś candramā jātaś cakṣuṣaś ca divākaraḥ |**

**              	jaghanād antarikṣaṃ ca jagac ca sacarācaram || 3.128 ||**

 

jaghanaśabdao nābhyādyarthaḥ | sacarācaraṃ jagat tasmād eva brahmaṇo jātam ityādi yojyam | ṛjv anyat || 128 ||

 

_evaṃ paramātmasvarūpe 'bhihite munayaś codayanti |_

 

                    	**yady evaṃ sa kathaṃ brahman pāpayoniṣu jāyate |**

**              	īśvaraḥ sa kathaṃ bhāvair aniṣṭaiḥ saṃprayujyate || 3.129 ||**

**              	karaṇair anvitasyāpi pūrvajñānaṃ kathaṃ ca na |**

**              	vetti sarvagatāṃ kasmāt sarvago 'pi na vedanām || 3.130 ||**

 

yady evam anādinidhano 'kṣaraḥ paramātmā, tato brahman pṛcchāmo bhavantaṃ kathaṃ pāpayoniṣu parādhīnavaj janma pratipadyate | atha mataṃ rāgādyaniṣṭasaṃprayogād iti tad api paryanuyogabhāg eva īśvaro 'py aparādhīnaḥ sa kathaṃ bhāvair aniṣṭaiḥ saṃprayujyata iti | athāyam abhiprāyaḥ saṃsāryātmatayā pūrvajñānanirodhād iti | tad apy asat | kathaṃ tasyākalaṃkasya saṃsāryātmatā, kathaṃ ca tadātmakatve 'pi śaktirūpair dṛṣṭyādyair anapāyibhiḥ karaṇair anvitasyāpi pūrvajñānaṃ nāsti | saṃsāryātmatayā vicchedād eveti cet, ajñatvaprasaṅgaṃ eva syāt | sarvagataparamātmasvarūpānapāyād jñānotpattir iti cet, evaṃ sati sarvago 'pi san sa devaḥ kasmāt sarvaśarīrāntargatāṃ vedanāṃ sukhādisaṃvidaṃ na vetti na jānātīty arthaḥ || 130 ||

 

_evaṃ munibhiḥ paricodite bhagavatottaram ucyate |_

 

                    	**antyapakṣisthāvaratāṃ manovākkāyakarmajaiḥ |**

**              	doṣaiḥ prayāti jīvo 'yaṃ bhavan jātiśateṣu ca || 3.131 ||**

 

yad uktaṃ pāpayoniṣu kathaṃ jāyata iti tatredam uttaraṃ manovākkāyakarmajair doṣair antyapakṣisthāvaratāṃ jātibhedeṣu ca śataśo bhavann utpadyamāno yātīti | etad eva tu prathamataraṃ vācyam āsīt, kathaṃ brahmaṇaḥ saṃsāryātmataiveti | tat tu sādhāraṇaviśeṣātmakatvenārambhakasya yajñādicakrasyānādinidhanatvābhidhānenaiva parihṛtaprāyatvāt kūpapatitasyevoddhāraṇaprakārārthinaḥ patanaprakārānveṣaṇavad anupayogitvān na parāmṛśyate || 131 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**anantā hi yathā bhāvāḥ śarīreṣu śarīriṇām |**

**              	rūpāṇy ap tathaiveha sarvayoniṣu dehinām || 3.132 ||**

 

vākkāyakarmaṇo 'pi hi kāraṇabhūtā mānasā eva bhāvāḥ | tathā cāmnāyo 'pi: "atha khalu kratumayo 'yaṃ puruṣaḥ" iti (ŚB 10.6.3.1) | te cānantāḥ śarīriṇā saṃsāryātmanāṃ śarīreṣu vartamānānāṃ yathaiva ca kāraṇabhūtā anantā bhāvāḥ, tathaiva ca kāryabhūtāni rūpāṇy apīha vartamānānāṃ dehinām api | ataś ca paramātmasvarūpavad anantamānasabhāvasaṃbandhāt saṃsāryātmanām apy anāditvasiddhiḥ || 132 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">yadi</span> karmato yonyantarasaṃbandhaḥ yasyāṃ tarhi tiryagādiyonāv anadhikāraḥ tato yonyantarsaṃbandho na prāpnoti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | yady aihikaphalāny eva vaidikāni karmāṇi syuḥ, tataḥ syād apy (?) evam | yadā tu khalu |_

 

                    	**vipākaḥ karmaṇāṃ pretya keṣāṃcid iha jāyate |**

**              	iha cāmutra caikeṣāṃ**

 

tadaitad acodyam iti śeṣaḥ |

 

_kiṃ ca naiva hi tatra karmaphalotpāde 'dhikārajñānasyopayogaḥ | kiṃ tarhi |_

 

                                                                    	**bhāvas tatra prayojakaḥ || 3.133 ||**

 

bhāvamātreṇāparijñātam api karma phalam utpādayaty evety abhiprāyaḥ | pretya vipākaḥ svargādiphalānām, ihaiva vṛṣṭyādeḥ, aniyataḥ paśvādīnām | ṛjv anyat || 133 ||

 

_tad idānīṃ karmajaṃ kāryakāraṇabhāvaṃ prapañcayati |_

 

                    	**paradravyāṇy abhidhyāyaṃs tathāniṣṭāni cintayan |**

**              	vitathābhiniveśī ca jāyate 'ntyāsu yoniṣu || 3.134 ||**

 

paradravyābhidhyānādibhir mānasair doṣair antyāsu caṇḍālādiyoniṣu jāyata ity mantavyam || 124 ||

 

_sa vāgdoṣais tu |_

 

                    	**puruṣo 'nṛtavādī ca piśunaś caiva mānavaḥ |**

**              	asaṃbandhapralāpī ca mṛgapakṣiṣu jāyate || 3.135 ||**

 

punar mānava iti puruṣavacanāt puruṣamātrāśrayam etd iti jñapayati | mṛgapakṣivacanaṃ cāśeṣatiryagjātilakṣaṇārtham | ṛjv anyat || 135 ||

 

_kāyikais tu karmadoṣaiḥ |_

 

                    	**adattādānanirataḥ paradāropasevakaḥ |**

**              	hiṃsakaś cāvidhānena sthāvateṣūpajāyate || 3.136 ||**

 

_sattvaguṇātiśayayogāt punaḥ |_

 

                    	**ātmajñaḥ śaucavān dāntas tapasvī niyatendriyaḥ |**

**              	dharmakṛd vedavid yāti**[^12]** sāttviko devayoniṣu || 3.137 ||**

 

ātmajñaḥ śaucādiniṣṭho vedavic ca yaḥ sa sāttviko devayoniṣu yāti karmaṇā devatvaṃ prāpnotīty arthaḥ || 137 ||

 

_atiśayarajaḥsaṃbandhāt tu |_

 

                    	**asatkāryarato 'dhīra ārambhī viṣayī ca yaḥ |**

**              	sa rājaso manuṣyeṣu mṛto janma prapadyate || 3.138 ||**

 

sacchabdo nityavacanaḥ | nityaṃ yat kāryam agnihotrādi tat sat kāryam | tato 'nyad asat kāryaṃ kāmyaṃ | tatpradhānaḥ adhīraś cañcalacittaḥ ārambhī sāṃdṛṣṭikārambhapradhānaḥ bhogādikāmaviṣayāsaktaś ca yaḥ sa rājaso manuṣyajātyāśrayaphalopabhoktṛtvān manuṣyeṣu jāyate mṛto martyaḥ amṛtatvalakṣaṇadevatvānarha ity arthaḥ || 138 ||

 

_apuṇyabhūyastvāt tu svabhāvata eva |_

 

                    	**nidrāluḥ krūtakṛl lubdho nāstiko yācakas tathā |**

**              	pramādavān bhinnavṛtto bhavet tiryakṣu tāmasaḥ || 3.139 ||**

 

yad ekaikatra sātvikādau svayaṃbhuvā traividhyam uktaṃ tad ihodāharaṇārthatayopanyāsān na prapañcitam || 139 ||

 

_evaṃ ca manobhāvamūlatvāt saṃsārasthiter mānasair eva |_

 

                    	**rajasā tamasā caiva samāviṣṭo bhramann iha |**

**              	bhāvair aniṣṭaiḥ saṃyuktaḥ saṃsāraṃ pratipadyate || 3.140 ||**

 

sattvālpatayā rajastamobhyāṃ samāviṣṭaḥ parādhīnatvād ihaiva saṃsāre bhraman bhūyaḥ saṃsāram evāniṣṭair mānasair bhāvaiḥ saṃyuktaḥ pratipadyate na vimucyata ity arthaḥ || 140 ||

 

_rajastamobhyām abhibhūtasattvaś ca sarvajñatve 'pi vijñānātmatayā vicchedāt |_

 

                    	**malino hi yathādarśo rūpālokasya na kṣamaḥ |**

**              	tathāvipakvakaraṇa ātmā jñānasya na kṣamaḥ || 3.141 ||**

 

saty api hy ālokasāmarthye malopaghātād yathaivādarśo rūpālokanāsamarthaḥ, tathaiva rajastamopaghātād apakvo 'paṭukaraṇo vijñānātmā samyag jñānasyāsamarthaḥ | ato yad uktaṃ kathaṃ karaṇavato 'pi pūrvajñānābhāva iti tat parihṛtam || 141 ||

 

_ataś cānucchinnakaraṇaśaktāv api |_

 

                    	**kaṭūrvārau yathāpakve madhuraḥ san raso 'pi na |**

**              	prāpyate**

iti chedaḥ |

                                	**ātmany api tathā nāpakvakaraṇe jñatā || 3.142 ||**

 

urvāruś cidbhiṭasadṛśaṃ phalam | spaṣṭam anyat || 142 ||

 

_yad uktaṃ "vetti sarvagatāṃ kasmāt sarvago 'pi na vedanām" _(YDh 3.130)_ iti, tat parihartum āha |_

 

                    	**sarvāśrayāṃ nije dehe dehī vindati vedanām |**

**              	yogī yuktas tu sarveṣāṃ yo nāvāpnoti vedanām || 3.143 ||**

 

bhogāyatanatvān nija eva dehe yasmād vijñānotpādaḥ tasmāt sarvagato 'pi sarvāśrayāḥ saṃvido na vibhāvayati | yadā tu yogī pariniṣpannayogajñānaḥ syāt tadā yuktaḥ samādhistho nija eva dehe 'vasthitaḥ sparśayogasāmarthyāt sarvāśrayāṃ dehāntaravartinīm api vijānātmāntareṇa bhedapratyayam apanīyātmavyavasthito vedanāṃ saṃvidaṃ vetti upalabhata ity arthaḥ | tuśabdasya cotkṛṣya nañā saṃbandhaḥ "na tv avāpnoti vedanām" iti | etad uktaṃ bhavati: upalabhata eva na tv avāpnoti vijñānaphalaṃ sukhādi nopabhuṅkte ity arthaḥ | kathaṃ punar jñātṛtvenābhinnasyāpi sukhādyabhoktṛtvam, karmasādhyatvāt phalopabhogasya bhedānupātinaś ca karmaṇo vijñānātmāśrayatvād ity avirodhaḥ || 143 ||

 

_kathaṃ punar ekasyaiva vibhaktāvibhaktatvaṃ tathaiva yuktyāgamābhyām upalambhanāt | tathā hi |_

 

                    	**ākāśam ekaṃ hi yathā ghaṭādiṣu pṛthag bhavet |**

**              	tathātmaiko hy anekaś ca jalādhāreṣv ivāṃśumān || 3.144 ||**

 

yathaiva hy ekatve 'py ākāśaṃ ghaṭādibhir avacchinnaviśeṣam ekatāpratyayaṃ bhidāṃ ca bibharti na ca bhedānupātidharmasaṃkaraḥ, tathā brahmaṇo 'pīty avaseyam | tathā cāha |

                    	yathaikasmin ghaṭākāśe rajodhūmādibhir yute |

                    	na sarve saṃprayujyante sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ tathātmanaḥ || iti | (MāṇUK 3.5)

tathānyair api |

                    	dhūmapūrṇaghaṭānāṃ ca yasyaikasyaiva recanam |

                    	utpāṭya kriyate tatra jāyate vyoma nirmalam || iti || 144 ||

 

_yadi tarhi savitur ivābhinnasyāpi jalādhārādivad brahmaṇo bhedāvabhāsaḥ na tarhi bhedaḥ pramāṇavān vyāmohanibandhanatvād ityādikām āśaṅkāṃ nirākaroti |_

 

**              	brahma khānilatejāṃsi jalaṃ bhūś ceti dhātavaḥ |**

 

paramārthasatyā eveti śeṣaḥ | yad uktam,

                    	pañca dhātūn svayaṃṣaṣṭān ādatte yugapat prabhuḥ | (YDh 3.72 )

ity atra yathaite pañca dhātavaḥ paramārthasatyāḥ |

 

                    	**ime lokā eṣa cātmā tasmāc ca sacarācaram || 3.145 ||**

 

lokaśabdaḥ śarīravacanaḥ lokā śarīrāṇīty arthaḥ | tasmāc cātmano 'nanyatayaiva ghaṭādyākāśavat sacarācaraṃ bhedavyavahārānupāti jagad ity arthaḥ | kathaṃ punar abhinna evātmātmanaḥ śarīrādi kuryāt, uktaṃ bhāvaviśeṣānugrahād iti || 145 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**mṛddaṇḍacakrasaṃyogāt kumbhakāro yathā ghaṭam |**

**              	karoti tṛṇamṛtkāṣṭhair gṛhaṃ vā gṛhakārakaḥ || 3.146 ||**

**              	hemamātram upādāya rūpaṃ vā hemakārakaḥ |**

**              	nijalālāsamāyogāt kośaṃ vā kośakārakaḥ || 3.147 ||**

**              	karaṇāny evam ādāy tāsu tāsv iha yoniṣu |**

 

kāryagamyatvāt sāmagrīniyamasya taddarśanānusāriṇy eva kalpanety abhiprāyaḥ | yathā ca ghaṭagṛhādau sāmagrīvaicitryopalambhaḥ, kośakārādes tu kośādisarjanaṃ lālādikaraṇavataḥ tatsṛṣṭau tv ātmana eva kartṛtvakaraṇatve evaṃ brahmaṇo 'pi mahābhūtādijanyakarmādikaraṇavataḥ śarīrādisarjanaṃ karaṇādisṛṣṭau tv ātmana eva kartṛtvakaraṇatve || 146–7 ||

 

_tad darśayati,_

 

                    	**sṛjaty ātmānam ātmaiva saṃbhūya karaṇāni ca || 3.148 ||**

 

iti | saṃbhūya karaṇāni ca svayaṃ kartṛkaraṇabhūta ity arthaḥ |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> cānyonyavyāhata evāyaṃ cetanācetanatvenaikabahutvānusārī parāvararūpaḥ paramārthānveṣaṇenātmapratyayaḥ | tathā hi, yadi tāvad yuktyāgamānusarād advayaṃ brahma, tato bhedavyavahāro jalapātreṣv iva savitur upādhito bhrāntinibandhanatayaiva syāt | atha bhedavyavahārasatyatā kutas tarhy ātmano vyatirekiṇaḥ śarīrasaṃbandhaḥ | na ca mahābhūtavyatirekeṇātmanaḥ svarūpaṃ paśyāmaḥ caitanyasya madaśaktivad bhūtasamudāyadharmatayāpy upapatteḥ | api ca mahābhūtāny api vijñānavādinaṃ prati sādhyāny eva jñānākāratayā nīlādyavabodhasaṃbhavāt | ato vaktavyam etat |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">atrābhidhīyate</span> | pratīyate hi bāhyo 'rthaḥ katham asāv apahnūyate na jñānākāratayaiva tadupapattiḥ asaṃvitprasaṅgāt, na hy ātmanaivātmasaṃvitsaṃbhavaḥ | kiṃ ca grāhyagrāhakapratyayas tāvad bhedahetutāyām anapekṣaḥ | kalpyaṃ tv ekatvam āropyādvyākāratvam | na copalabdhivirodhinyaḥ kalpanāḥ saṃbhavanti | na ca svapnādivaitathyena jāgratpratyayavaitathyaṃ jāgratsvapnādibhidaivānyasiddheḥ, pramuṣitasmaraṇābhimānatve 'pi ca smārtatvena bāhyālambanatvam | athocyeta kathaṃ vyatirikto 'rthaḥ saṃvidaṃ janayet janane vā sarvārthasaṃvidavabodho vā syād iti | tad api hīndriyārthasaṃbandhānusārāt jñānotpādanasyācodyam eva | na ca sato 'pi brāhmasya kṣaṇikatvaṃ pratyabhijñānenaikatādhyavasānāt antarā ca vināśahetvanupalambāt sāmagryadhīnatvāc ca kāryotpādasya sthāsnutāyām api kramayaugapdyādinā tadasaṃbavādicodyānavakāśa evety eṣā dik | evaṃ ced yathopalambham arthasthiter mahābhūtāni tāvat satyāny eva | yat tu tatsatyatve tatsaṃghadharmatayā madaśaktivad vijñānotpattau nairātmyaprasaṅga iti tad api bāhyārthānubhūtivad ātmano 'py anubhavata eva siddher akiṃcit || 148 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**mahābhūtāni satyāni yathātmāpi tathaiva hi |**

**              	ko 'nyathaikena netreṇa dṛṣṭam anyena paśyati || 3.149 ||**

 

yathaiva hy anubhūyamānatvān mahābhūtāni pṛthivyādīni satyāni evam evānubhavitṛtvād ātmāpi satya evety abhiprāyaḥ | anyathā hi bhūtadarmatve jñānasyānubhavitāram antareṇa ekenākṣṇā dṛṣṭaṃ punas tad evedaṃ pūrvadṛṣṭam ity anyenākṣṇā kaḥ paśyet ko 'nusaṃdadhyād ity abhiprāyaḥ || 149 ||

 

_etad eva bhūyaḥ spaṣṭayati |_

 

                    	**vācaṃ vā ko vijānāti punaḥ saṃśrutya saṃśrutām |**

**              	atītārthasmṛtiḥ kasya ko vā svapnasya kārakaḥ || 3.150 ||**

 

prapañcārtham etat || 150 ||

 

_api cānubhavata evātmatattvāvagamaḥ kim atra yuktyā prayojanam | yo hy ayaṃ rajastamobhyām upaplutacetāḥ |_

 

                    	**jātirūpavayovṛttavidyādibhir ahaṃkṛtaḥ |**

**              	saktaḥ śabdādiviṣaye karmaṇā manasā girā || 3.151 ||**

 

sa evāparokṣasvasaṃvit nātmety abhiprāyaḥ || 151 ||

 

_kiṃ ca yas tāvad yogasaṃsiddhaḥ sa nirvikalpam aparokṣam advayaṃ brahmāvabudhyata eva | itaro 'pi kutārkikacodyābhimānī yaḥ |_

 

                    	**sa saṃdigdhamatiḥ karmaphalam asti na veti vā |**

**              	saṃplutaḥ siddham ātmānam asiddho 'pi hi manyate || 3.152 ||**

 

yo 'sau kutārkikamānī saṃdigdhamatis tamasā saṃpluto 'vaṣṭabdhaḥ so 'pi yadaivam atipāṇḍityād vikalpayati karmaphalam asti na veti tadā siddhaṃ niścitaṃ śarīravyatiriktam ātmānaṃ manyata eva | asiddho 'pi yogadarśanānapekṣo 'pīty arthaḥ | yat tv idam uktaṃ kathaṃ mahābhūtasatyatve vyatiriktasyātmanaḥ śarīratayā nibandha iti tan mahābhūtānām apy ātmasvarūpatvenāvyatirekitvād acodyam eva | yathānubhavānusāreṇa vijñānātmasatyatvāc codyam eveti cet | na, nimittāntarasya saṃbhavāt || 152 ||

 

_tathā hi |_

 

                    	**mama dārasutāmātyā aham eṣām iti sthitaḥ |**

**              	hitāhiteṣu bhāveṣu viparītamatiḥ sadā || 3.153 ||**

**              	jñe 'jñe ca prakṛtau caiva vikāre cāviśeṣavān |**

**              	anāśakāgnipraveśajalaprapatanodyamī || 3.154 ||**

**              	evaṃvṛtto 'vinītātmā vitathābhiniveśavān |**

**              	karmaṇā dveṣamohābhyām icchayā caiva badhyate || 3.155 ||**

 

evaṃ ślokadvayoktavṛtto 'līkakutārkikacodyābhiniveśavān avinītaḥ sādhāraṇaviśeṣātmakena karmaṇā mānasābhyāṃ ca dveṣamohābhyāṃ bhogātiviṣayecchayā ca vyatirikto 'pi badhyata ity abhiprāyaḥ | mama dāraputrādayo 'haṃ caiṣām ity anyonyam upakāryopakārakatayā yo 'vasthitaḥ hitāhiteṣau cādṛṣṭārthasāṃdṛṣṭikārtheṣu ca bhāveṣu yo viparītabuddhiḥ sāṃdṛṣṭika eva hitābhimānī ahitābhimānī cetaratra tathā jñe ca jñātari vedārthavidi ajñe ca kutārkikādau prakṛtau cātmani vikāre ca rajastamolakṣaṇe viśeṣānabhijñaḥ ataś ca dharmabuddhyabhimānād anāśakādāv udyukto yaḥ evaṃvṛttaḥ, sa badhyate iti vyākyātam etat || 153–155 ||

 

_evaṃ ca mahāghoraṃ saṃsāram āpannasyāyaṃ tanumocanaprakāropadeśaḥ |_

 

                    	**ācāryopāsanaṃ vedaśāstrasyārthavivekitā |**

**              	tatkarmaṇām anuṣṭhānaṃ saṅgaḥ sadbhir giraḥ śubhāḥ || 3.156 ||**

**              	stryālokālambhavigamaḥ sarvabhūtātmadarśanam |**

**              	tyāgaḥ parigrahāṇāṃ ca jīrṇakāṣāyadhāraṇam || 3.157 ||**

**              	viṣayendriyasaṃrodhas tandryālasyavisarjanam |**

**              	śarīraparisaṃkhyānaṃ pravṛttiṣv aghadarśanam || 3.158 ||**

**              	nīrajastamasaḥ sattvaśuddhir nispṛhatā śamaḥ |**

**              	etair upāyair saṃśuddhaḥ sattvayogy amṛtī bhavet || 3.159 ||**

 

ācāryopāsanādibhir etair adhyardhaślokatrayoktair upāyaiḥ samyak śuddhaḥ sāttviko yogaṃ prāpya kaivalyajñānād amṛtī bhaved brahmatvaṃ prāpnuyād ity arthaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 156–9 ||

 

_yogāt kaivalyam uktam | sa eva tu yogaḥ kathaṃ syād ity ucyate |_

 

                    	**tattvasmṛter upasthānāt sattvayogāt parikṣayāt |**

**              	karmaṇāṃ saṃnikarṣāc ca satāṃ yogaḥ pravartate || 3.160 ||**

 

tattvāni pṛthivyādīni teṣām āgamānuvidhānenātmābhedadarśanaṃ tattvasmṛtiḥ tasyās tattvasmṛter upasthānād udbhavāt nīrajastaskatvena ca sattvayogād janmāntarakṛtānāṃ ca dhyānādinā parikṣayāt karmaṇāṃ saṃnikarṣāc ca saṃbandhāt satāṃ sādhūnāṃ yogaḥ parānandaprāptilakṣaṇaḥ pravartata iti vyākhyeyam || 160 ||

 

_yady api ca kathaṃcid yuktasyāpi pramādāt paraprāptir na syāt, tathāpy ānuṣaṅgikaphalatayaiva tāvat |_

 

                    	**śarīrasaṃkṣaye yasya manaḥ sattvastham īśvaram |**

**              	aviplutasmṛtiḥ samyak sa jātismaratām iyāt || 3.161 ||**

 

śarīrasaṃkṣaye utkrāntikāle yasya mano viṣayānāsaktaṃ sattvastham īśvaram aparādhīnaṃ rāgādyanabhibhūtam, sa samyag avinaṣṭasmṛtiḥ pretya jātismaratām iyāt jātismaratāṃ prāpnuyāt | tataś ca punar api yogasaṃbandhād amṛtī bhavaty evety abhiprāyaḥ || 161 ||

 

_kiṃ ca svayaṃkṛtair eva śubhāśubhaiḥ karmabhir yujyamānaḥ |_

 

                    	**yathā hi bharato varṇair vartayaty ātmanas tanum |**

**              	nānārūpāṇi kurvāṇas tathātmā karmajas tanum || 3.162 ||**

 

upasaṃhārārthaḥ ślokaḥ | bharato naṭaḥ | sa yathā svāṃ tanuṃ bhūmikāviśeṣānusāreṇa varṇair vartayati, evaṃ karmajo 'pi vijñānātmā nānāvidhāni śubhāsubhāni karmāṇi kurvan vicitrāsu yoniṣu saṃbhūtiṃ nirvartayatīty arthaḥ || 162 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca jātismaratve 'py avikalāṅgasyaiva dharmādyanuṣṭhānasāmarthyāt tatraiva tāvad upāyo vaktavyaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | nātropāyābhidhānam upayujyate, svābhāvikatvād avikalāṅgatāyā | tathā hi |_

 

                    	**kālakarmātmabījānāṃ doṣair mātus tathaiva ca |**

**              	garbhasya vaikṛtaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ nāṅgahānaṃ hi janmataḥ || 3.163 ||**

 

kāladoṣaḥ pratiṣiddharātryupagamādikaḥ | garbhādhānādikarmaṇi vaiguṇyam akriyā vā karmadoṣaḥ | aniṣṭastryantarābhidhyānādikas tv ātmadoṣaḥ | alpatvādiko bījadoṣaḥ | parapuruṣābhidhyānaṃ mātṛdoṣaḥ | evamādibhir doṣair garbhavikriyāvairūpyaṃ, na tu janmataḥ svabhāvato 'ṅgahānam ity abhiprāyaḥ || 163 ||

 

_yat tv idam uktaṃ katham akṣarasya brahmaṇaḥ saṃsārāpattir iti, atrocyate |_

 

                    	**ahaṃkāreṇa manasā gatyā karmaphalena ca |**

**              	śarīreṇa ca nātmāyaṃ muktapūrvaḥ kadācana || 3.164 ||**

 

anya eva hy asau nityam avasthitaḥ paramānandarūpaḥ paramātmā | ayaṃ tv anya eva | tadavibhāge 'py anāditayaivāvacchinno vijñānātmāhaṅkārādibhiḥ śarīreṇa ca na viyuktaḥ | tasyaiva cāyaṃ parabrahmābhedaprāptyartho bhagavata āmnāyasya prayatnaḥ || 164 ||
