_asyaiva ca paraprāptyupadeśamārgasya yadi paraṃ rogitayā vighātaḥ, tatrāpy etad ucyate |_

 

**              	dātā satyaḥ kṣamī prājñaḥ śubhakarmā jitendriyaḥ |**

**              	tapasvī yogaśīlaś ca na rogaiḥ paribhūyate || 3.165 ||**

 

nigadoktaḥ ślokaḥ || 165 ||

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca sādhāraṇaviśeṣātmakasya karmaṇo 'nādinidhanatvād yathaivānādiḥ śarīrasaṃbandhaḥ, tathaivānanto 'pi | tataś cānirmokṣaprasaṅgāt tatpratipādanaprayāsānarthakyam eva syāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> |_

 

                    	**vartyādhārasnehayogād yathā dīpasya saṃsthitiḥ |**

**              	vikriyāpi ca dṛṣṭaivam akāle prāṇasaṃkṣayaḥ || 3.166 ||**

 

ārambhakānāditayā hy ārabhyasyānāditaiva syān na tv anantatayānantatāpi | na hy avaśyaṃ kāraṇavināśād eva kāryavināśaḥ, tatsadbhāve 'py anyato nāśadarśanāt | tathā ca vartyādhārasnehayogāt tadārabhyasya pradīpāder yāvatkāraṇaṃ ca saṃsthitir dṛṣṭā nimittāntarād api vātādyabhighātād vikriyā | evam ātmano 'pi karmakāryaśarīrasaṃbandhinas tadanucchede 'py anyatas tattvāvabodhāder akāle prāṇasaṃkṣayaḥ sūkṣmāvacchedakaliṅgādisaṃkṣaya ity arthaḥ | sāṃsārikatve 'pi caivam eva tīvraphalakarmādisaṃnipātāt puruṣasya śarīrasaṃkṣayo yojyaḥ || 166 ||

 

_tad idānīṃ prāṇasaṃkṣayahetubhūtaṃ tattvāgamopāyaṃ prapañcayati |_

 

                    	**anantā raśmayas tasya dīpavad yaḥ sthito hṛdi |**

**              	sitāsitāḥ kadrunīlāḥ kapilāpītarohitāḥ || 3.167 ||**

 

yo 'sau pūrvavyākhyāto dīpavad hṛdi nididhyāsyatayāvasthitas tasya prāptyupāyās tadavabhāsakatayā anantā raśmayo nāḍyaḥ sitādivarṇāḥ | sitā cātra śuklā niṣkalaṃkā paraprāptir abhipretā | tadupāyatayā ca nāḍyāṃ tācchabdyam | evaṃ kadrvādiṣv api yojyam | sitaikaiva | anyāḥ sarvā asitāḥ | tatprapañcaḥ kadrunīlā ityādikaḥ | yathāviprakarṣaṃ yojyam | kadruśabdaḥ kutsitagatyartho nīlādiviśeṣaṇo na varṇavacanaḥ | kutsitagatyarthā nīlāḥ kadrunīlāḥ kadrupiṅgalā iti ca yojyam | āpītā haritāḥ | tathā cāmnāyaḥ: "tasmin śuklam uta nīlam āhuḥ piṅgalaṃ haritaṃ lohitaṃ ca" ityādi (BāU 4.4.9) || 167 ||

 

_paraprāptyupāyabhūtaś ca suṣumnākhyo hṛdayād ūrdhvam ṛjur mūrdhānam abhiprasthitaḥ śuklo raśmiḥ |_

 

                    	**ūrdhvam ekaḥ sthitas teṣāṃ yo bhittvā sūryamaṇḍalam |**

**              	brahmalokam atikramya tena yāti parāṃ gatim || 3.168 ||**

 

_kāmyopāsanayogād brahmārpaṇanyāyena vā yaḥ karmaṇy avasthitaḥ |_

 

                    	**yad asyānyad raśmiśatam ūrdhvam eva vyavasthitam |**

**              	tena devanikāyānāṃ sa dhāmāni prapadyate || 3.169 ||**

 

vasvādayo devanikāyāḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 169 ||

 

_yas tu kāmātmako rājasaḥ khalu karmānusāreṇaiva |_

 

                    	**ye 'nekarūpāś cādhastād raśamayo 'sya mṛduprabhāḥ |**

**              	iha karmopabhogārthās taiś ca saṃcarate 'vaśaḥ || 3.170 ||**

 

kṛtavyākhyānaḥ ślokaḥ || 170 ||

 

_evaṃ caitat parāvaraṃ brahmaṇaḥ svarūpam ālocya sarvasyātmādhigamavyatiriktasya prayāsasya niṣprayojanatvād yathākathaṃcit svaśaktyanusāreṇātmānaṃ jñātum, he munayaḥ, prayatnaḥ kriyatām ity evaṃ yogīndro vaktum āha |_

 

                    	**vedaiḥ śāstraiḥ savijñānair janmanāmaraṇena ca |**

**              	ādhyā gatyā tathāgatyā satyena hy anṛtena ca || 3.171 ||**

**              	śreyasā sukhaduḥkhābhyāṃ karmabhiś ca śubhāśubhaiḥ |**

**              	nimittaśakunajñānair grahasaṃyogajaiḥ phalaiḥ || 3.172 ||**

**              	tārānakṣatrasaṃcāraiḥ jalajaiḥ svapnajair api |**

**              	ākāśapavanajyotirjalabhūtimirais tathā || 3.173 ||**

**              	manvantarair yugaprāptyā mantrauṣadhibalair api |**

**              	vittātmānaṃ vidyamānaṃ kāraṇaṃ jagataḥ sadā || 3.174 ||**

 

sarvaprakāraṃ vedādibhir mantrauṣadhibalāntair yathāsāmarthyam ātmānaṃ vitta vettuṃ prayatnino bhavatha | yathāśakti ātmajñānāya prayatnaḥ kriyatām ity abhiprāyaḥ | vedādyupāyāsaṃbhave 'pi janmamaraṇādibhir api nimittaśakunijñānādibhir api mantrauṣadhibalair api, na tv asaṃbhāvyopāyatayātmajñānāya śaithilyaṃ kāryam, avaśyaṃ cātmajñānaṃ kāryam ity evaṃparatvād ārambhasya | na mantrauṣadhyādāv atyabhiniveśaḥ karyaḥ | vedais tattvajñānopayabhūtaiḥ, śastraiḥ vyākaraṇādibhiḥ śāstraiḥ, savijñānaiḥ vividhetihāsādijñānasahitaiḥ | janmanā ihāvadhāraṇāśaktāv anyenāpi janmanety arthaḥ | āmaraṇena ca yāvajjīvam atyabhiyogenety arthaḥ | caśabdo janmāntaraśatair apy aparābhaṅgapradarśanārthaḥ | ādhyā mahatyāpi manaḥpīḍayā | gatyā deśāntaragamanena | agatyā ekāvasthānatayā | tathāśabdaś caivaṃbhūtaprakārāntarārthaḥ | satyenaikātmyadarśanena | anṛtena caturbhujādikalpitopāsanāprakāreṇa | śreyasā pārivrājyena | sukhaduḥkhābhyāṃ karmabhiś ca śubhāśubair iti caśabdena sukhādīnāṃ samuccayād gārhasthyenety arthaḥ | sukhaṃ gandhamālyādisevanam, asukhaṃ yamaniyamāvasthitiḥ, śubhaṃ karmāgnihotrādi, aśubhaṃ karma sarvasvārādi vihitatve 'pi maraṇasaṃbandhād aśubhatvam, asāmarthye ca jñānakṣamaśarīrāntotpādakatvāt prakṛtopayogitvam | nimittādijñānaiś ca abhyudayakālam upalakṣyānirvedena punaḥ punaḥ pravṛttyarthaṃ nimittaṃ dakṣiṇākṣispandanādi udagayanādi ca | śakunajñānaṃ vāyasarutādijñānam | grahasaṃyogaś candrabalādiḥ | tārānakṣatrasaṃcāraḥ krūragrahair janmanakṣatrādyapīḍanam | jalajāni tīrthayātrādīni | svapnajānīṣṭasvapnadarśanāni | apiśabdaḥ pūrvavad upāyatvasaṃbhāvanārthaḥ | ākāśadibhiś ca paramārthataḥ purāṇadarśanānusāreṇotpannair jāyamānais timiraiś ca tadanusāreṇaivādityarūpātmatattvāvarodhakaiḥ tathaiva taduktaprakāreṇaivāpanīyamānaiḥ | taddarśanād eva ca manvantarayugādiprāptyā kālacakrajñānenāpi | prajñāsthairyahetubhir mantrauṣadhibalair vittātmānam | kathaṃlakṣaṇaṃ, vidyamānaṃ sadā vidyamānaṃ kālatrayaparāmarśaśūnyam ity arthaḥ | kāraṇaṃ jagata ity uktārtham etat | na cāyam atiparokṣaḥ kevalāgamikatvamātreṇa śraddheya ātmalakṣaṇo 'rthaḥ, kiṃ tarhi, pramāṇāntaram atroktam eva "mahābhūtāni satyāni yathātmāpi tathaiva" (YDh 3.149) ity atra || 171–4 ||

 

_bhūyaś copasaṃhārārthaṃ sauhṛdāt tad eva spaṣṭayati |_

 

                    	**ahaṃkāraḥ smṛtir medhā dveṣo buddhiḥ sukhaṃ dhṛtiḥ |**

**              	indriyāntarasaṃcāra icchā dāraṇajīvite || 3.175 ||**

**              	svapnesargaś ca bhāvānāṃ preraṇaṃ manaso 'gatiḥ |**

**              	nimeṣaś cetanā yatna ādānaṃ pāñcabhautikam || 3.176 ||**

**              	yata etāni cihnāni dṛśyante paramātmanaḥ |**

**              	tasmād asti paro dehād dehī sarvaga īśvaraḥ || 3.177 ||**

 

medhā prajñātiśayaḥ | dhṛtir dhāraṇā | indriyāntaragṛhītasya parāmarśaḥ indriyāntarasaṃcāraḥ | icchayā yad dhāraṇaṃ śarīrasya tatparityāgaḥ tad icchādhāraṇam | svapne 'nekavidho vidyamānabhūtasargaḥ svapnesargaḥ | tathā cāmnāyo 'pi: "na tatra rathāḥ" ity upakramya, "atha rathān rathayogān pathaḥ sṛjate" ityādi (BāU 4.3.10) | preraṇaṃ tu manaso jāgadavasthāyām api | agatir manasaḥ suṣuptāvasthāyām | nimeṣaḥ sarvakāyikaceṣṭopalakṣaṇam | cetanā antarvartinī | prayatnaḥ sarvaprakāraḥ | ādānaṃ grahaṇaṃ trividhakarmānusāreṇa | pāñcabhautikaṃ pṛthivyādipañcabhūtaviṣayam | yataś caitāni bhūtadharmavailakṣaṇyena paramātmanaś cihnabhūtāny upalabhyante, tasmād asti dehād dehavartinaḥ kṣetrajñād vyatirikto 'nyo dehī kṣetrajñaḥ sarvagataḥ paraḥ paramātmā īśvaraḥ karmaṇā grahītum aśakyaḥ ānando 'jaro 'mṛta ity arthaḥ | atra ca jāgratsvapnasuṣuptāvasthānupāyitvaṃ mahābhūtādyādānopapattiś cāvyatirekābhiprāyeṇa paramātmaliṅgam | avaśiṣṭāni tu vijñānātmasādhāraṇāny api brahmaṇaḥ parāvarātmakatvasiddhyarthaṃ prasaṅgad upanyastānīty avagantavyam | spaṣṭam anyat || 175–7 ||

 

_idānīṃ kṣetrajñapatyor vivekaṃ parāvaratvaṃ ca brahmaṇaḥ kṣetrajñābhidhānānugamadvāreṇa spaṣṭīkaroti |_

 

                    	**buddhīndriyāṇi sārthāni manaḥ karmendriyāṇi ca |**

**              	ahaṃkāraś ca buddhiś ca pṛthivyādīni caiva ha || 3.178 ||**

 

buddhīndriyāṇi cakṣurādīni | eṣām arthā rūpādayaḥ | ahaṃkāraḥ pratyagātmany avamarśo 'nyakāraṇāsaṃsṛṣṭo buddhinimittakaḥ | buddhir anubhavahetuphalākriyā | caśabdād avyaktaṃ pradhānākhyam, tac ca na sāṃkhyābhimataṃ sattvādiguṇasāmyāvasthātmakam, kiṃ tarhi jagatkāraṇabhūtaṃ sādhāraṇātmakam | tad uktam: "yo dravyadevatātyāgasaṃbhūto rasaḥ" (YDh 3.121) ity atra | sattvādīnāṃ tv ātmaguṇatvam eva | spaṣṭam anyat || 178 ||

 

_etac caturviṃśatitattvātmakaṃ yat kṣetram |_

 

                    	**avyakta ātmā kṣetrajñaḥ kṣetrasyāsya nigadyate |**

**              	īśvaraḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ sann asan sad asac ca saḥ || 3.179 ||**

 

asya caturviṃśatitattvātmakasya vettādhiṣṭhātṛtvena phalabhoktṛtayā ceśvaro 'vyakte ca karmaṇy avasthitaḥ karmāvabaddho yaḥ kṣetrajña ity evaṃ brahmavidbhiḥ sa nigadyate | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

                    	etad yo vetti taṃ prāhuḥ kṣetrajña iti tadvidaḥ | iti | (BhG 13.1)

yad vā ātmaviśeṣaṇatvenāvyakta ity etad yojanīyam | avyakto rūpādyasaṃsṛṣṭa ity arthaḥ | sarvabhāvānāṃ tu kṣetrakṣetrajñātmakānāṃ ya īśvarḥ sa paramātmā ity evam anayor bhedaḥ | bhūtaśabdo bhāvamātratayā kṣetrajñavacano 'pi | yaś cāyaṃ paramātmā san asan sad asac ca, saḥ san kṣetrajñatyā asan paramātmarūpatayā sadasad ity evaṃ vyapadeśāt | paramārthatas tu yat sad asac ca yat tat sarvaṃ sa eva sadasadātmakaḥ, tathaivopalambhāt | tathā cāmnāyaḥ: "dve vāva brahmaṇo rūpe mūrtaṃ cāmūrtaṃ ca" (BāU 2.3.1) iti || 179 ||

 

_idānīṃ kṣetrajñotpattikramaṃ darśayati |_

 

**              	buddher utpattir avyaktāt tato 'haṃkārasaṃbhavaḥ |**

**              	tasmāt khādīni jāyante ekottaraguṇāni tu || 3.180 ||**

 

suṣuptāvasthāyām eva tāvat sarvavijñānamahāpralaye saty avyaktād upabhoganimittāt karmaṇaḥ sakāśād buddher utpattiḥ | tataś ca prabodhāt pratygātmany avabodhād ahaṃkārasaṃbhavaḥ | tathaiva bāhyaviṣayaprasaṅgād ākāśādīny ekottaraguṇāny ekadvitricatuṣpañcaguṇānīty arthaḥ | tadgrāhakatvaprayuktāni ca tadvikārāpattyā tadātmakānīndriyāṇi manaś cādāv eva svaviṣayānusārāt sadasadātmakam ity eṣā prakriyā sṛṣṭipralayopavarṇanādau sarvatra purāṇādiṣv api yojyā || 180 ||

 

_yāni ca khādiny atrākāśapavanajyotirjalapṛthivyantāni ekottaraguṇatvena mahābhūtāny uktāni |_

 

                    	**śabdaḥ sparśaś ca rūpaṃ ca raso gandhaś ca tadguṇāḥ |**

 

uttaratra caśabdaḥ pūrvaguṇasamuccayārthaḥ rasaś cety atrāpi chandonurodhād anucyamāno 'pi draṣṭavyaḥ |

 

_sṛṣṭau ca |_

 

                    	**yo yasminn āśritas teṣāṃ sa tatraiva pralīyate || 3.181 ||**

 

bhūteṣu ca guṇānāṃ pralayāt paramātmano nirguṇatvasiddhiḥ || 181 ||

 

_idānīṃ pūrvoktam arthaṃ kārtsnyenopasaṃharati |_

 

**              	yathātmānaṃ sṛjaty ātmā tathā vaḥ kathitaṃ mayā |**

**              	vipākas triprakārāṇāṃ karmaṇām īśvaro 'pi san || 3.182 ||**

 

uktanigadārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 182 ||

 

_trirūpakarmavipākātmakam avyaktam adṛṣṭaṃ pradhānākhyaṃ saṃsārapravṛttibījaṃ na punar tantrāntarābhiprāyeṇa sattvādiguṇasāmyalakṣaṇaṃ, yato na sattvādayaḥ prakṛtiguṇāḥ | kiṃ tarhi |_

 

**              	sattvaṃ rajas tamaś caiva guṇās tasyaiva kīrtitāḥ |**

 

ātmano na prakṛter ity arthaḥ |

 

_yady evaṃ kathaṃ tarhi bandhamuktyādivyavasthā | ucyate |_

 

**              	rajastamobhyām āviṣṭaś cakravad bhrāmyte hi saḥ || 3.183 ||**

 

taducchedāt tu sattvaguṇayogāt svarūpāvasthiter mucyata evety abhiprāyaḥ || 183 ||

 

_idānīṃ parāvarabrahmopasaṃhartum āha |_

 

**              	anādimān ādimāṃś ca ya eṣa puruṣaḥ paraḥ |**

**              	liṅgendriyair upagrāhyaḥ savikāra udāhṛtaḥ || 3.184 ||**

 

mahadādibhir vikāraiḥ kṣetralakṣaṇamahadādisaṃbandhād ādimān kṣetrajñaḥ, yaś cānadir akalaṃkaḥ paramātmā ubhayarūpatvāl liṅgendriyopagrāhyatayā udāhṛtaḥ, sa eṣa bhagavān ubhayaprakāraḥ sadasadātmanā viśvarūpaḥ paramātmaivety avagantavyam | nātra vyāmohaḥ kārya ity abhiprāyaḥ | liṅgādīny ahaṃkārādīny ātmaviṣayatvena, indriyāṇi cakṣurādīni prakṛtiviṣayatvenety evaṃ yojanā || 184 ||

 

_yaś cāyaṃ kṣetrajñatayā pravibhaktaḥ tasyendriyopalabdhabāhyaliṅgasaṃsūcitam utkarṣāpakarṣahetumārgam āha |_

 

                    	**pitṛyāṇo 'javīthyāś ca yad agastyasya cāntaram |**

**              	tenāgnihotriṇo yānti prajākāmā divaṃ prati || 3.185 ||**

 

"yad asyānyad raśmiśatam" (YDh 3.169) ityādyanantaraṃ mārgābhidhānam, tasyaivedam upalakṣaṇatvena bāhyamārga(m?) ucyate: yad etad ajavīthyagastyayor antaraṃ sa pitṛyāṇaḥ panthāḥ | tenāgnihotriṇaḥ prajākāmāḥ karmamātraniṣṭhāḥ saṃvatsaropāsakā yānti | evaṃ mārgāntare 'pi yojyam | purāṇe hi bhagavataḥ savitur bahvyo vīthyo divi paddhatayaḥ śrūyante | tatrāgastyasyānantarā ajavīthī | spaṣṭam anyat || 185 ||

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

                    	**ye 'pi dānaparāḥ samyag aṣṭābhiś ca guṇair yutāḥ |**

**              	te 'pi tenaiva gacchanti satyavrataparāyaṇāḥ || 3.186 ||**

 

dayā sarvabhūteṣu kṣāntir anasūyetyādayo 'ṣṭāv ātmaguṇāḥ | prasiddam anyat || 186 ||

 

_yaś cānena mārgeṇa dyurlokaḥ, tatra |_

 

**              	aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi munayo gṛhamedhinaḥ |**

**              	punar āvartino bījabhūtā dharmapravartakāḥ || 3.187 ||**

 

tiṣṭhantīti śeṣaḥ | tasyāṃ hi janasthānasaṃjñāyāṃ divi gṛhamedhino gṛhasthāḥ karmaṇāgnihotrādinā lokajitaḥ saṃsārabījabhūtāḥ pralīyamānadharmoddhārapravartakāḥ aṣṭāśītisahasrās tatparimāṇā agnihotrādinā tatra yānti | punar dharmapravartanāyehābhimukhyena vartanta ity evaṃ tatpravartakāḥ punarāvartina iti vyākhyēyam || 187 ||

 

_devayānenāpy evam eva mārgeṇa |_

 

**              	saptarṣināgavīthyos tu devalokaṃ samāśritāḥ |**

**              	tāvanta eva munayaḥ sarvārambhavivarjitāḥ || 3.188 ||**

 

ayam api pūrvavat || 188 ||

 

_saptarṣināgavīthyor antarālena ca yo 'yaṃ lokaḥ |_

** **

**              	tapasā brahmacaryeṇa saṅgatyāgena medhayā |**

**              	yātās tatrāvatiṣṭhanti yāvad ābhūtasaṃplavam || 3.189 ||**

 

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca kāryārthatvād vedasya pramāṇāntarasya cābhāvān nirmūlakam ivedaṃ mārgādinirūpaṇaṃ lakṣyate, | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span>, yadi kāryārthatayaiva vedasya prāmāṇyaṃ syāt | svarūpe 'pi tu prāmāṇyam iṣyata eva |_

 

                    	**yato vedāḥ purāṇaṃ ca vidyopaniṣadas tathā |**

**              	ślokāḥ sūtrāṇi bhāṣyāṇi yat kiṃcid vāṅmayaṃ kvacit || 3.190 ||**

**              	vedānuvacanaṃ yajño brahmacaryaṃ tapo damaḥ |**

**              	śraddhopavasasātatyam ātmano jñānahetavaḥ || 3.191 ||**

 

yadi hi karmānuṣṭhānamātranimittatayā kriyaiva vedārthaḥ syāt, tataḥ svarūpaparatā na syāt | yadā tu niyogasiddhir eva vākyārthaḥ, tadā niyojyatvāvagama eva tatsiddhiḥ | pratipannātmasvarūpasyaiva nirvartitaniyogatā syāt | tataś cātmasvarūpāvagatir eva vedārtha iti svarūpa evāvasitaṃ vedasya prāmāṇyam | kiṃ ca kāryatayā vyutpatteḥ kārye prāmāṇyam uktam | na ca parārthasya kārytvopapattiḥ | ko hi parārthaṃ buddhipūrvakārī kuryāt | ataḥ svārtha eva kāryaṃ, na cānyo 'taḥ kaścid ātmano 'rtho 'nyatra svarūpajñānād iti tad eva kāryam avaśiṣyate | ataś ca pārmārthikaṃ tatraiva bhagavato vedasya prāmāṇyam | tathā coktam: "codanā hi bhūtaṃ bhavantaṃ bhaviṣyantam ityādyevaṃjātīyakam arthaṃ śaknoty avagamayitum" iti (TV on PMS 1.1.2, p. 15) | evaṃjātīyakam ātmasvarūpam ity arthaḥ | tathā cendriyāntarapratiṣedhas tadviṣayatayaivopadyate "nānyat kiṃca nedriyam" iti (TV on PMS 1.1.2, p. 15) | anyathā hi vidhyarthe tatprāptyabhāvād ākasmika eva pratiṣedhaḥ syāt | ato brahmasvarūpa evāmyāyasya prāmāṇyaṃ syāt | tad eva ca pāramārthikaṃ vidhyarthasatattvam | yat tu agnihotrādikāryāvabodhanaṃ, tad avāntaravākyārthatayā tadapekṣitāvidyāvyudāsaparatvena tadupāyatayaiva pramāṇāntarāviṣayatayā kāryavyapadeśabhāg ity avaseyam | evaṃ cen mārgādisvarūpapratipādane 'py aviruddhaṃ kāryavyapadeśitvam ity eṣā dik | tad darśayati: "yato vedāḥ purāṇaṃ ca" ityevamādayaḥ sarva evātmano jñānahetavaḥ, śabdapravṛttes tatparatayaiva vyutpattyavadhāraṇāt | tataḥ svarūpe 'py avyāhataṃ prāmāṇyaṃ vedasya | ataś ca mārgādismṛter apy anavadyaṃ vedamūlatvam ity abhiprāyaḥ | "purāṇaṃ ca" iti, itihāsārthaś caśabdaḥ | vidyā mīmāṃsādikā | upaniṣadāṃ pṛthagvacanaṃ vedabhāgāntarasya tādarthyapradarśanārtham | tathā ślokāḥ upaniṣatsūtrasthānīyā mantrā eva | "tad apy ete ślokāḥ: aṇuḥ panthā vitataḥ purāṇaḥ" ityādikāḥ (BāU 4.4.8) | upaniṣatsūtratāpratipattyartham eva teṣāṃ pṛthagvacanam | tadvivaraṇārthāny eva cārthavādādivākyāni bhāṣyāṇi | prādhānyāc cāyam upaniṣadām atiprapañcaḥ | kiṃ ca "yat kiṃcid vāṅmayaṃ kvacid" iti | loke hy apy ātmaparatayaiva śabdavyutpattir ity arthaḥ | evaṃ ca vedānuvacanādis tādarthyenaiva cāturāśramyaprayāsaḥ | tathāmnāyaḥ: "tam etaṃ vedānuvacanena brāhmaṇā vividiṣanti" ityādi (BāU 4.4.22) | gurūktasyānupāṭho vedānuvacanam | ādyaṃ brahmacaryam | yajñā iti gārhasthyopalakṣaṇam | brahmacaryaṃ naiṣṭhikatvam | tapo dama iti vānaprasthatvam | śraddopavāsasātatyam iti pārivrājyam, "aṣṭau grāsā muner bhaktam" (ĀpDh 2.9.13) iti vacanāt | laghvaśanārtho vāyam upavāsaśabdaḥ | vyākhyātam anyat || 190–1 ||

 

_yataś caitad evam ataḥ |_

 

**              	sa hy āśramair nididhyāsyaḥ samastair evam eva tu |**

 

sarvārambhāṇāṃ tatparatvād ity abhiprāyaḥ |

 

_kiṃ ca |_

 

**              	draṣṭavyas tv atha mantavyaḥ śrotavyaś ca dvijātibhiḥ || 3.192 ||**

 

dvijātivacanaṃ dvitīyasyopanayanajanmanas tādarthyapradarśanārtham | draṣṭavyaḥ

pratyakṣādinā | śrotavya āgamāt | mantavyas tarkeṇa | kramabhedaś chando'nurodhāt | nididhyāsyaḥ sākṣātkartuṃ yogamārgeṇa || 192 ||

 

_pūrvokamārgadvayānusāriṇaś ca |_

 

                    	**ya evam enaṃ vidanti ye cāraṇyakam āśritāḥ |**

**              	upāsate dvijāḥ satyaṃ śraddhayā parayā yutāḥ || 3.193 ||**

 

araṇyam evāraṇyakam | evaṃ vidantīti prakramānusārād iha hiraṇyagarbhādyavāntaraṃ brahmasvarūpam | spaṣṭam anyat || 193 ||

 

_ye caivaṃ viduḥ |_

 

                    	**kramāt te saṃbhavanty arcir ahaḥ śuklaṃ tathottaram |**

**              	ayanaṃ devalokaṃ ca savitāraṃ savaidyutam || 3.194 ||**

**              	tatas tān puruṣo 'bhyetya mānaso brahmalaukikān |**

**              	karoti punar āvṛttis teṣām iha na vidyate || 3.195 ||**

 

arcirādimārgo 'yaṃ paramātmaviṣayo yathopāsanāsāmarthyaṃ krameṇānekavidhalokajayahetuḥ paurāṇikaiḥ prapañcitaḥ | vaidyuta indro mānasād abhidhyānāt saṃstutaḥ | ayam evāntarātmā mānasaḥ puruṣaḥ | anāgamanaṃ cātra tadbhāvāpattiḥ | iha brahmāṇḍāntarvartini vikāre punarāvṛttyabhāvaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 194–5 ||

 

_ajavīthimārgāvasthityā ca |_

 

                    	**yajñena tapasā dānair ye hi svargajito narāḥ |**

**              	dhūmaṃ niśāṃ kṛṣṇapakṣaṃ dakṣiṇāyanam eva ca || 3.196 ||**

**              	pitṛlokaṃ candramasaṃ nabho vāyuṃ jalaṃ mahīm |**

**              	kramāt te saṃbhavantīha punar evaṃ vrajanti ca || 3.197 ||**

 

dhūmādikrameṇa candrāntayānantaroktanyāyena gatiṃ prāpya punar ākāśādikrameṇa pṛthivīṃ prāpnuvanti | tataś ca punar evotkṛṣyamāṇāś cakravat kramāt saṃsārabījabhāvaṃ pratipadyante ity avaseyam | ṛjv anyat || 196–7 ||

 

_rajastamobhyām atipariplavād apuṇyopahatacetāḥ |_

 

                    	**etad yo na vijānāti mārgadvayam ātmanaḥ |**

**              	dandaśūkaḥ pataṅgo vā bhavet kīṭo 'tha vā kṛmiḥ || 3.198 ||**

 

tasyāpi ca kṣīṇāśubhasya kathaṃcit puṇyodayād yajñādyupayogitāṃ prāpya punar utkarṣasiddhiḥ | dandaśūko daṃśanaśīlaḥ sarpādiḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 198 ||

 

_idānīm atisauhṛdāt paramātmaprāptyupāyabhūtaṃ yogamārgasaṃpradāyam āha |_

 

                    	**ūrusthottānacaraṇaḥ savye nyasyetaraṃ karam |**

**              	uttānaṃ kiṃcid unnamya mukhaṃ viṣṭabhya corasā || 3.199 ||**

**              	nimīlitākṣaḥ sattvastho dantair dantān asaṃspṛśan |**

**              	tālusthācalajihvaś ca saṃvṛtāsyaḥ suniścalaḥ || 3.200 ||**

**              	saṃnirudhyendriyagrāmaṃ nātinīcocchritāsanaḥ |**

**              	dviguṇaṃ triguṇaṃ vāpi prāṇāyāmam upakramet || 3.201 ||**

 

yogaśāstrāntarānusārāt prāṇāyāmo recakādilakṣaṇo 'vaseyaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat | ete ca padmāsanādayo manaḥsamādhānahetutvenārthaprāptā eva yogāṅgatayā niyamyante | ataś cānyathāpy ekāgratā na virudhyata iti kecit | tathā ca dakṣeṇoktam: "na ca padmāsanodyogaḥ" ityādi | tat tu niyāmakatvāc chāstrasyāyuktam eva | dakṣavacanaṃ tv indriyajayapraśaṃsārthatvād aviruddham || 199–201 ||

 

_prāṇāyāmaiś cātmānaṃ saṃśodhya |_

 

                    	**tato dhyeyaḥ sthito yo 'sau hṛdaye dīpavat prabhuḥ |**

**              	dhārayet tatra cātmānaṃ dhāraṇāṃ dhārayan budhaḥ || 3.202 ||**

 

yo 'sau hṛdaye dīpavad ananyaprakāśyaḥ sarvasya prakāśakatvenāvasthitaḥ paramātmoparatabāhyaprapañcaḥ, sa eva dhyeyaḥ | hṛdaye cāvasthito darśanaśravaṇamananādibhir nididhyāsyatayā yas tatrāvasthitas tadviṣayatvenāpastabhedhāṃ dhāraṇāṃ prasaṃkhyānādikāṃ dhārayann ubhayātmakasyāpi brahmaṇaḥ kaivalyātmakatayaiva tatrātmānaṃ dhārayed budhaḥ pratipannobhayātmakāntaryāmirūpabrahmasvarūpaḥ paraṃ brahmoparatadhyātṛdhyeyātmasvarūpātmanātmānaṃ tatra dhārayaṃs taṃ cātmany akalaṃkam abhayam apunarāvṛttam aparokṣam ānandam apāstākhilavyapadeśaṃ paśyed ityādi prapañcanīyam || 202 ||

 

_pratipannāntaryāmisvarūpasya yogasiddhasya parabrahmaṇo nididhyāsanam uktam, tasyaiva tv adhikāriṇo lakṣaṇaṃ vācyam ity ata āha |_

 

                    	**antardhānaṃ smṛtiḥ kāntir dṛṣṭiḥ śrotrajñatā tathā |**

**              	nijaṃ śarīram utsṛjya parakāyapraveśanam || 3.203 ||**

**              	arthānāṃ chandataḥ sṛṣṭir yogasiddhes tu lakṣaṇam |**

**              	siddhe yoge tyajan deham amṛtatvāya kalpate || 3.204 ||**

 

antardhānaṃ parair anupalabhyatvam | smṛtiḥ samādhyavagatasyāvismaraṇam, nityaṃ tathaivāvyavadhānena pratipattir ity arthaḥ | kāntir aśanāyādyapagamaḥ | dṛṣṭir bhaviṣyadādāv avyāghātaḥ | śrotragrāhyatvāc chrotraṃ śabdaḥ, tadarthajñatvaṃ śrotrajñatā | tathāśabdād vedānusaṃdhānānapekṣatvenety arthaḥ | nijaṃ ca vaiśeṣikam asādhāraṇakarmārabhyaṃ śarīraṃ nijatayaivāsādhāraṇapratyayagrāhyatvenotsṛjya sadasadātmakatvena prāguktaviśvarūpātmakaparakāyapraveśanam ekatvāpattiḥ | yat punaḥ śarīratayaiva parakāyapraveśanam, tan mantravidyāsv apy astīti nātropayujyate ity evam eva vyākhyeyam | arthānāṃ mahadahaṃkārādīnāṃ chandataḥ icchātaḥ sṛṣṭir visarjanam utpādanaṃ vā | spaṣṭam anyat | evaṃ cāntaryāmyātmanā siddhe yoge tyajaṃs tathā parāvarabhāvātmakadhyeyadhyātṛvyapadeśabhāktvena dehaṃ paraṃ brahmarūpatayā amṛtatvāyāpunarāvṛttaye kalpate ghaṭata ity arthaḥ || 203–4 ||

 

_evam etatprāptiparyantaṃ pārivrājyam uktaṃ viśuddhasatattvānāṃ tattvavidām | yas tv atra manovākkāyikānām anyatamadoṣeṇāsamarthaḥ, taṃ pratīmam anyaṃ pārivrājaprakārabhedam āha |_

 

              	**atha vāpy abhyasan vedaṃ nyastakarmā sute vasan |**

**              	ayācitāśī mitabhuk parāṃ siddhim avāpnuyāt || 3.205 ||**

 

granthārtharūpatayā japānuvacanādinā vedam abhyasan parityaktāgnihotrādyanuṣṭhāno 'nupalakṣitaliṅgaviśeṣo bhaikṣeṇaiva varteta | atha vā tadaśaktāv ayācitāśī aṣṭagrāsādinā mitabhuk putragṛhādau vaset | evam api parāṃ siddhiṃ prāptyupāyalakṣaṇāṃ (?) brahmatvaṃ prāpnuyād iti || 205 ||

 

_yady api pārivrājyam adhikṛtyāyaṃ muktyupadeśaḥ, tathāpy āśramasyātantrataiva, yadṛcchayā pracāramātravyudāsahetutvād apavargasya ca jñānaikasādhyatvāt | yatas caitad evam ataḥ |_

 

**              	nyāyārjitadhanas tattvajñānaniṣṭho 'tithipriyaḥ |**

**              	śrāddhakṛt satyavādī ca gṛhastho 'pi vimucyate || 3.206 ||**

 

śrāddhaśabdaḥ samastagṛhasthadharmopalakṣaṇārthaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 206

 

 

**iti yatidharmaprakaraṇam |**

** **

**atha prāyaścittadharmaprakaraṇam |**

 

_evaṃ pratyātmikān sarvāśramāṇāṃ sādhāraṇāṃś ca dharmān abhidhāyedānīṃ naimittikān doṣanirghātārthān prāyaścittātmakān dharmān upadidikṣuḥ pratiṣedhātikramahetukaṃ doṣam evādau prapañcayitum āha |_

 

                    	**mahāpātakajān ghorān narakān prāpya garhitān |**

**              	karmakṣayāt prajāyante mahāpatakinas tv iha || 3.207 ||**

 

mahāpātakam upapātakaṃ vā kṛtvā prāyaścittam akṛtvā ye mriyante, te tannimittaprabhavān ghorān yamalokasaṃbandhinas tāmisrādīn ekaviṃśatinarakān atiśayena garhitān ekadvitrisāmastyādinānubhūya tīvrakarmaphalopabhogena kṣīṇe punas tadavaśiṣṭopabhogāyeha vakṣyamāṇaprakāreṇa mahāpātakino jāyante iti vyākhyeyam | yadi tu kṛtsnakarmakṣayād eveti vyākhyāyeta, tato mahāpātakinas tv ihety asaṃbaddhaṃ syāt | ataḥ karmakṣayād ity evaṃ vyākhyeyam || 207 ||

 

_tatra narakān vakṣyati | yathā tv iha jāyante tathā prapañcayati |_

 

**              	śvasūkaramṛgoṣṭrāṇām brahmahā yāti yoniṣu |**

**              	kharapulkasavenānāṃ surāpo nātra saṃśayaḥ || 3.208 ||**

**              	kṛmikīṭapataṅgatvaṃ svarṇahārī samāpnuyāt |**

**              	tṛṇagulmalatātvaṃ ca kramaśo gurutalpagaḥ || 3.209 ||**

 

śvādayaḥ prasiddhāḥ | sūkaraś cātra grāmyaḥ śvasaṃnidhānāt | mṛgaśabdo 'pi prakramānusārāt sṛgālādiṣu draṣṭavyaḥ | udāharaṇārthatvāc copanyāsasya nātrātīva smṛtyantaraiḥ saha viṣayavibhāgāya yatitavyam | mahāpātakajān ghorān narakān prāpyeti copakramāt kāmakṛtamahāpātakādiviṣayo 'yaṃ prapañco veditavyaḥ | ghoragarhitakarmajanyatayā kāraṇānurūpyeṇa kāryasaṃbandhaviśeṣasyārthavattvāt | itarathā tu narakaśabdād eva tatsiddher niṣprayojanatvaṃ syāt | tataś ca smṛtyantareṣv apy evam eva vyākhyeyam | tathā cāmnāyaḥ: "saha tata eva prāk pravavrāja" ity upakramya "itthaṃ vā ime 'muṣmin loke sacante tān vayam iha pratisacāmahe" (ŚB 11.6.1.3) iti kāmakṛta eva yātanāṃ darśayati | tathā ca vyāsaḥ:

                    	kāmakārakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ narakeṣūpabhujyate |

                    	ihaiva prāpnuyuḥ kleśān akāmakṛtapātakāḥ || iti |

ato yady api smṛtyantareṣu akāmakṛte 'pi kiṃcid yātanātiśayavacanaṃ syāt, tathāpy atyantavarjanārthaṃ nindāparatvena vyākhyeyam | "kharapulkasavenānāṃ surāpo nātra saṃśayaḥ" ity asaṃśayavacanaṃ nindārthavādāśaṅkānivṛttyartham | kharaśabdaś ca gardabhādisadṛśatiryagyonyupalakṣaṇārthaḥ | pulkasaḥ kṣatriyāyāṃ śūdrāj jātaḥ | veno naṭaḥ | kṛmikīṭāditvaṃ ca svarṇahārī samāpnuyāt | saṃśabdo 'tiśayaduḥkhapratipattyarthaḥ | tṛṇādikāṃś cānekavidhān sthāvabhāvān gurutalpagaḥ prāpnuyāt | kramaśa iti vadann ekenaiva nimittenānekavidhānekajanmaprāpyaṃ kleśasaṃbandhaṃ darśayati | spaṣṭam anyat || 208–9 ||

 

_evaṃ kramaśas tiryagyonitvam anubhūya tataś cāturvarṇyaviṣaye jāyante | tatrāpi tu |_

 

                    	**brahmahā kṣayarogī syāt surāpaḥ śyāvadantakaḥ |**

**              	hemahārī tu kunakho duścarmā gurutalpagaḥ || 3.210 ||**

 

kṣayo rājayakṣmā | śyāvadantādayaḥ spaṣṭāḥ | dauścarmyaṃ ca strīṇām api yathāsaṃbhavaṃ draṣṭavyam | akāmakṛte 'pi pāpe yaḥ prāyaścittaṃ samarthaḥ san na kuryāt, tasyāpy etā narakayātanāḥ svakarmānurūpyeṇa draṣṭavyāḥ | kṣayarogādīni ca liṅgāny aśaktyāpy akṛtaprāyaścittānāṃ bhavanty eva | tathā ca |

                    	iha duścaritaiḥ kecit kecit pūrvakṛtais tathā |

                    	prāpnuvanti durātmāno narā rūpaviparyayam || iti | (MDh 11.48)

iha duścaritair iti vacanād ihāpi janmani duścaritaiḥ prāyaścittaiḥ pūrvajanmakṛtaiś cācaritaprāyaścittaiḥ tathāśabdān narakādyupabhogānte kathaṃcin nimittāntarād akṛtaprāyaścittāḥ santo durācārātmāno virūpakaśarīrāḥ santaḥ svābhāvikaśukladantādiviparyayaṃ śyāvadantādikaṃ prāpnuvantīty arthaḥ || 210 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvac caturṇāṃ mahāpātakinām uktam, tatsaṃparke tu |_

 

**              	yo yena saṃpibaty eṣāṃ sa talliṅgo 'bhijāyate |**

 

yeṣāṃ patitānāṃ yo yena saṃpibati sa tadīyenaiva kṣayarogādinā liṅgena vyastasamastatayā saṃsargānurūpyeṇa jāyata ity arthaḥ | abhiśabdāc ca tadabhijanatvena kṣayarogādiyuktayor eva pitroḥ tadanurūpaliṅgo jāyata iti draṣṭavyam | yadi tu sa talliṅge 'bhijāyate iti pāṭhas tadā svayam anevaṃliṅgatve 'pi yo yalliṅge kule jāyate sa tathābhūtapatitasaṃsṛṣṭa ity avagantavyam | ataś ca tair api prāyaścittaṃ kartavyam evety uttaratrāpi yojyam |

 

_mahāpātakavyatirekeṇāpi rūpaviparyayā bhavanty evety etat prapañcayituṃ cauryaviṣaye tāvad darśayitum āha |_

 

**              	annahartāmayāvī syān mūko vāgapahārakaḥ || 3.211 ||**

**              	dhānyamiśry atiriktāṅgaḥ piśunaḥ pūtināsikaḥ |**

**              	tailahṛt tailapāyī syāt pūtivaktras tu sūcakaḥ || 3.212 ||**

 

āmayāvitvaṃ tu mandāgnitā | vāgapahārakaḥ yo garādi dattvā kuvaidyatayā vā mithyopacāreṇa vācam apaharati | adhītya vāpalāpaḥ anabhyanujñātādhyayanaṃ ca vāgapahāra ity anye | tat tu brahmasteyam ucyate na vāgapaharaṇam | yathāha manuḥ |

                    	brahma yas tv ananujñātam adhīyānād avāpnuyāt |

                    	sa brahmasteyasaṃyukto narakaṃ pratipadyate || iti | (MDh 2.116)

vikrayādyarthaṃ dhānyasyānyamiśrī dhānyamiśrī | piśunaḥ paraguṇāpahārī | pūtināsikaḥ kuthitanāsikaḥ | tailahṛt tailamātrasya hartā | tailapāyī kīṭaviśeṣaḥ | pūtivaktraḥ kuthitamukhaḥ | sūcakaḥ parasyārthalābhādiprasaṅge tadvināśāya vāgdoṣodbhāvakaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 211–2 ||

 

_tathā |_

 

                    	**parasya yoṣitaṃ hṛtvā brahmasvam apahṛtya ca |**

**              	araṇye nirjale deśe jāyate brahmarākṣasaḥ || 3.213 ||**

 

parasyotkṛṣṭasya jātito guṇato vā yoṣitaṃ strītvenopabhogyāṃ brahmasvaṃ ca brāhmaṇadravyaṃ jñātiṃ vāpahṛtya brahmarākṣaso bhavatīti vyākhyeyam | brahmaṇā vedātmakenāgnikalpenāntar bahiś ca dahyamāno 'tyantayātanāśarīro brahmarākṣasaḥ | vedādhyāyina evaitad brahmarākṣasatvaṃ sāmarthyād draṣṭavyam | ataś ca śrutādhyayanasaṃpannenāpi parasyotkṛṣṭasya bhāryā nopagantavyā | tathā cāmnāyaḥ: "tasmād evaṃvic chrotriyasya jāyayopahāsaṃ necched uta hy evaṃvit parābhavati" (BāU 6.4.12) iti | tathā "sa vā eṣa nirindriyo nirvīryaḥ kṣīṇasamastasukṛtaś ca mriyate tasya kim anyad īdṛśād brahmarākṣasatvād bhavet" iti | ataḥ sūktam araṇye nirudake brahmarākṣaso jāyata iti || 213 ||

 

**              	hīnajātau prajāyante ratnānām apahārakāḥ |**

**              	patraṃ śākaṃ śikhī hṛtvā gandhāṃś cucchundarī śubhān || 3.214 ||**

 

mānave tu:

                    	maṇimuktāpravālāni hṛtvā lobhena mānavāḥ |

                    	vividhāni ca ratnāni jāyante hemakartṛṣu || (MDh 12.61)

iti svarṇakāritvaṃ darśitam | iha tu hīnajātāv iti | tad manuvacanasyāntyalakṣaṇārthatvād aviruddham, svarṇakārajāter vātyantanikṛṣṭatvapratipattyartham | spaṣṭam anyat || 214 ||

 

                    	**mūṣiko dhānyahārī syād yānam uṣṭraḥ phalaṃ kapiḥ |**

**              	ajaḥ paśuṃ payaḥ kāko gṛhakāra upaskaram || 3.215 ||**

 

yānaṃ gantryādi | phalam āmrādikam | paśavo 'śvādayaḥ | payo dugdham | gṛhakāro mṛttikāsūkarikaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 215 ||

 

                    	**madhu daṃśaḥ palaṃ gṛdhro gāṃ godhāgniṃ bakas tathā |**

**              	śvitrī vastraṃ śvā rasaṃ tu cīrī lavaṇam eva ca || 3.216 ||**

 

madhu mākṣikaṃ madyaṃ vā | palaṃ māṃsam | gām iti cātra strī pratyetavyā, paśugrahaṇenaiva gomātrasyoktatvāt | tathāśabdo 'tra saṃskṛtaupāsanādiprakārabhedenāgniharaṇe 'nekavidhabakādijātipratipattyarthaḥ | tathottaratrāpi vastragataraktādiprakārabhedānurūpyeṇa śvitrasya raktaśuklādibhedapratipattyarthaḥ | śvā prasiddhaḥ | arasam iti vā, tulyatvāt saṃhitāyāḥ | nīrasaṃ paryuṣitādi hṛtvā śvayoniṃ prāpnuyāt | tuśabdo 'vadhāraṇārthaḥ | ādarārthaṃ caitat | yatra paryuṣitādiharaṇe 'pi śvā bhavati tatrābhyadhikaharaṇe na vidmaḥ kiṃ bhaviṣyatīti pradarśayitum | cīrī nāma nidāghakāle 'tavīṣu vāsyate kīṭaviśeṣaḥ || 216 ||

 

_idānīm upasaṃharati |_

 

**              	pradarśanārtham etat tu mayoktaṃ steyakarmaṇi |**

**              	dravyaprakārā hi yathā tathaiva prāṇijātayaḥ || 3.217 ||**

 

steyakarmaṇīty upalakṣaṇārtham | sarvatra vadhakarmaṇy abhakṣyakarmaṇi paradārābhigamanakarmaṇi ca svakarmānurūpyeṇa tiryagyoniṣu mānuṣye cānekavidhavairūpyavyādhidāridryabandhuviyogādir vadhabandhanādikleśaś ca prapañcanīyaḥ | etad eva prapañcayati | hriyamāṇadravyaprakārā hanyamānaprāṇiprakārā abhigamyamānaparadārādiprakārāś ca yathānekavidhāḥ, tathaiva tadupabhogāyānekavidhaprāṇijātayo 'pi | ataḥ svakarmānurūpyeṇa pratiṣiddhasevanād vihitānanuṣṭhānād anyatrāpi parivittyādau nimitte prāyaścittākaraṇāt tāsu tāsu duḥkhopabhogabahulāsu yoniṣu utpādakleśādiprāptiḥ prapañcanīyā || 217 ||

 

_etad eva spaṣṭayati |_

 

**              	yathākarma niṣevyaivaṃ tiryaktvaṃ kālaparyayāt |**

**              	jāyante lakṣaṇabhraṣṭā daridrāḥ puruṣādhamāḥ || 3.218 ||**

 

pāpakarmaṇo viśeṣānurūpyeṇa narakāṃs tiryagyonitvaṃ cānubhūya tataḥ kālaparyāyāt satpuruṣocitalakṣaṇarahitā daridrāḥ puruṣādhamāś ca jāyante, na teṣām utkarṣaḥ saṃbhavatīty abhiprāyaḥ | ato 'vaśyaṃ tair ihāpi janmani prāyaścittaṃ caritavyam | tathā ca vasiṣṭhenoktam: "kunakhī kṛcchraṃ dvādaśarātraṃ caritvātmānam uddharet" iti (VaDh 20.6) | ato 'nevaṃliṅgair api daridraiḥ puruṣādhamaiś ca prāyaścittaṃ kartavyam evety abhiprāyaḥ | yataś ca kaunakhyādilakṣaṇayogitvam api tiryagyonigrahaṇād eva gṛhītam, tataś ca kālaparyayāt tad apy anubhūya tair lakṣaṇaiḥ kaunakhyādibhir bhraṣṭāḥ santo daridrāḥ puruṣādhamāś ca jāyante | tataś ca prāyaścittaṃ kartavyam evety abhiprāyaḥ || 218 ||

 

_ye punaḥ kṛtvāpi pāpāni tadanurūpaprāyaścittāni samyag anutiṣṭhanti, teṣām apuṇyānuvṛttir manāg api yato nāsti |_

 

                    	**tato niṣkalmaṣībhūtāḥ kule mahati bhoginaḥ |**

**              	jāyante lakṣaṇopetā dhanadhānyasamanvitāḥ || 3.219 ||**

 

spaṣṭārthaḥ ślokaḥ | anye tu tata evāśubhakarmopabhogān niṣkalmaṣībhūtā iti vyācakṣate | tat tu mandaprayojanaṃ viparītārthaṃ ceti nādartavyam || 219 ||

 

_idānīṃ yasmin nimitte prāyaścittaṃ kartavyaṃ, tad darśayati |_

 

                    	**vihitasyānanuṣṭhānān ninditasya ca sevanāt |**

**              	anigrahāc cendriyāṇāṃ naraḥ patanam ṛcchati || 3.220 ||**

 

vihitasya smārtasya saṃdhyopāsanāṣṭakādeḥ śrautasya cāgnihotrāder ananuṣṭhānāt | ninditasya ca arthataḥ prāptau satyāṃ pratiṣiddhasya sevanāt | ata eva ca pratiṣiddhasyeti vaktavye ninditasyety uktam | anyathā hi śabdaprāptasyāpi ṣoḍaśīgrahaṇāder niṣiddhasya sevanāt patanaprasaṅgaḥ syāt | indriyāṇāṃ cānigrahāt prāyaścittākaraṇād ity arthaḥ | naragrahaṇaṃ sārvavarṇikatvapradarśanārtham | patanam ṛcchatīti ca patanaṃ prāyaścittārhatvam evābhipretaṃ na tu dvijātikarmabhyaḥ, tasya mahāpātakaviṣayatvāt | tathā ca mānave "prāyaścittīyate naraḥ" (MDh 11.44) iti prāyaścittārhatvam evoktam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca prāyaścittākaraṇam api vihitānanuṣṭhānam eva | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span> | doṣanirghātārthaṃ hi prāyaścittam, na tv agnotrādivan naimittikamātram | atas tadakaraṇād doṣanirghāta eva na syād na tv abhyadhikadoṣatvam | asminn anigrahāc cendriyāṇām iti vacane sati na kevalaṃ doṣanirghāto na bhavati, atiriktaṃ ca patanakāraṇam āpadyate | ataś ca tathāvidhasya gurutaro daṇḍaḥ prāyaścittaṃ ca gurutaraṃ yathā syād ity evamarthaḥ prayatnaḥ | mānave 'pi ca |

                    	akurvan vihitaṃ karma ninditaṃ ca samācaran |

                    	prasajaṃś cendriyārtheṣu prāyaścittiyate naraḥ || (MDh 11.44)

iti prāyaścittākaraṇam evendriyārthaprasajanaṃ vyākhyeyam | yadi tv avihitāpratiṣiddhaviṣayābhiprāyeṇātiprasaṅganivṛttyarthaṃ prasajaṃś cendriyārtheṣu ity ucyeta, tataḥ:

                    	dharmam arthaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca yathāśakti na hāpayet | (MDh 4.21)

ity anena virodhaḥ syāt, "kāmātmatā na praśastā" (MDh 2.2) ity anenaivātiprasaṅgasya nivāritatvāt | ataḥ pūrvaiva vyākhyā jyāyasī | spaṣṭam anyat || 220 ||

 

_yasmāc ca vihitasyānanuṣṭhānān ninditasya ca sevanāt prāyaścittākaraṇena cendriyāṇām anigrahāc ca gurutaraprāyacittārhatvena puruṣasya patanaprasaṅgaḥ |_

 

                    	**tasmāt teneha kartavyam prāyaścittaṃ viśuddhaye |**

**              	evam asyāntarātmā ca lokaś caiva prasīdati || 3.221 ||**

 

yasmin nimitte sati prāyaścittākaraṇāt patanaprasaṅgaḥ, tasmāt tena nimittavatā puruṣeṇa yathādhikāraṃ rahasyaṃ vā vakṣyamāṇena rahasyaprāyaścittamārgeṇa prakāśaṃ vā prakāśaprāyaścittaprakāreṇa prāyaścittam ātmaviśuddhyarthaṃ lokavyavahāraprasiddhyarthaṃ cāvaśyaṃ kartavyam | ihety ānantaryārtham | ihaiva, nimittānantarakāla ity arthaḥ | evaṃ ca sati asya pāpakṛto 'ntarātmā rahasyaprāyaścittakaraṇāl lokaś ca prakāśaprāyaścittānuṣṭhānāt prasīdati prasanno vyavahāraviṣaye bhavatīty arthaḥ || 221 ||

 

_itaś ca prāyaścittaṃ niyogataḥ kartavyam | yataḥ |_

 

**              	prāyaścittair apaity eno yad ajñānakṛtaṃ bhavet |**

**              	kāmato vyavahāryas tu vacanād iha jāyate || 3.222 ||**

 

prāyaścittair viśeṣavihitaiḥ prakāśarahasyātmakair niḥśeṣaṃ pāpaṃ yasmād abuddhipūrvakṛtaṃ buddhipūrvakṛtaṃ vāpagacchati, tasmāt prāyaścittāny avaśyakartavyānīti ślokasya samastasyārthaḥ |

 

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca kāmakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ naiva prāyaścittair apagacchati | yadi nāma vacanasāmarthyād[^13] ihānapagate 'pi saṃvyavahāryatvaṃ bhavati, bhavatu | ata evoktam: "kāmato vyavahāryas tu vacanād iha jāyate" iti | asmiṃl loke saṃvyavahāryatvaṃ bhavati, na tu pāpam apaitīty abhiprāyaḥ | tathā cāha manuḥ |

                    	iyaṃ viśuddhir uditā pramāpyākāmato dvijam |

                    	kāmato brāhmaṇavadhe niṣkṛtir na vidhīyate || iti | (MDh 11.89)

iti, tathā:

                    	akāmataḥ kṛte pāpe prāyaścittaṃ vidhīyate | (MDh 11.45)

iti svābhiprāyeṇoktam | tathā ślokottarārdhena paramatopanyāsaḥ kṛtaḥ |

                    	kāmakārakṛte 'py āhur eke śrutidarśanāt || iti | (MDh 11.45)

anyaparair vaidikair arthavādair vyāmohitāḥ kecit kāmakārakṛte 'pi prāyaścittam āhuḥ, na tu tan mamābhipretam iti bhagavato 'bhiprāyaḥ | tathā ca smṛtyantareṣv apy evaṃvidhāny eva vacanāni vāsiṣṭhādiṣu: "anabhisaṃdhikṛte prāyaścittam aparādhe" (VaDh 20.1) ityevamādīni | ataḥ svamatiparikalpitam idaṃ kāmakārakṛte 'pi prāyaścittāt pāpāpagama iti | kathaṃ tarhy ayaṃ ślokaḥ:

                    	enasvibhir anirṇiktair nārthaṃ kiṃcit samācaret | iti | (MDh 11.189)

asyāpy ayam evārthaḥ: yāvat prāyaścittaṃ na kurvanty enasvinaḥ, tāvat taiḥ saha na kaścid vyavahāraḥ kāryaḥ | ata eva coktam:

                    	kṛtanirṇejanāṃś caitān na jugupseta karhicit | iti | (MDh 11.189)

etad uktaṃ bhavati: yady api kāmakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ prāyaścittair nāpagacchati, tathāpy enān kṛtaprāyaścittān vyavahāraviṣaye na manāg api jugupseteti | anyathā hy anirṇiktair nācared ity ukte sāmarthyāt kṛtanirṇejanaiḥ sahācaraṇaṃ prāpnoty eva | tatra kṛtanirṇejanāṃś cainān ity etad anārabhyam eva syāt | tasmāt kāmakṛte saṃvyahāryatvamātraṃ na pāpāpagamaḥ | kiṃ ca yaḥ pratiṣedhaṃ dṛṣṭvā tadatikrameṇa pravartate, sa narakādyupabhogam aṅgīkṛtyaiva pravartate | tataś ca taṃ prati prāyaścittaṃ pāpakṣapaṇārthatvenānapekṣitatvād adṛṣṭārthaṃ syāt | ato vyākhyeyam etat kāmato vyavahāryas tv iti |

 

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">atrocyate</span> | prāyaścittaṃ tāvad doṣavati nimitte vidhīyamānaṃ phalāntarānupapatter doṣanirghātārtham eva pratīyate | tatra nimittagataḥ śrūyamaṇo 'pi viśeṣo "yasyobhayaṃ havir ārtim ārcchet" (cf. ŚabB on PMS 6.4.31) itivad avivakṣitaḥ | tenobhayatrāviśeṣeṇaiva brahmahatyādau prāyaścittopadeśaḥ | yat tu,

                    	kāmato brāhmaṇavadhe niṣkṛtir na vidhīyate | (MDh 11.89)

iti, tan nindārthaṃ maraṇāntikaprāyaścittārthaṃ vā na tu prāyaścittanivṛttyarthaṃ, pūrvārdhenaiva siddhatvāt, tathā saty ānarthakyaprasaṅgaḥ syāt | ata eva ca kāmakṛte 'pi jivaprāyaścittasiddhyarthaṃ kāmato vyavahāryas tv ity atroktam |

 

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> atra vyavahāryatvam iha loke vacanāt syād ity uktam, pāpaṃ tv ajñānakṛtam evāpaiti netarad apīti |

 

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">naitad</span> yuktam, śrutivirodhāt | yathoktam: "indro yatīn sālāvṛkebhyaḥ prāyacchat tam aślīlā vāg abhyāvadat sa prajāpatim upādhāvat tasmād etad upahavyaṃ prāyacchad" ity upakramya, "abhiśasyamanaṃ yājayet" ity uktam (PB 18.9–10) | ataś copakramasāmarthyāt kāmakṛta evaitad vijñāyate | tathā "etena hendro daivāpaḥ śaunako janamejayaṃ pārīkṣitaṃ yājayāñcakāra" ity upakramya, "sarvāṃ ha vai pāpakṛtyāṃ tat sarvāṃ brahmahatyām apahanti yo 'śvamedhena yajate" iti (ŚB 13.5.4.1) | sarvagrahaṇāt kāmakṛta evāśvamedho vijñāyate | ataḥ pāpāpanuttaye prāyaścittaṃ kartavyaṃ na saṃvyavahāryatvasiddhyartham | tathā cānantaram evoktam: "pārīkṣitā yajamānā aśvamedhaiḥ parāvaram ajahuḥ karma pāpakaṃ puṇyāh puṇyena karmaṇā" (ŚB 13.5.4.3) iti pāpāpanodanatvaṃ darśayati | puṇyāḥ puṇyena karmaṇety apuṇyamūlocchitim eva spaṣṭayati | ataḥ pratyakṣaśrutyānuguṇyenaiva smṛtivyākhyānaṃ yuktam | tathā ca manuḥ |

                    	akāmataḥ kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ vedābhyāsena śudhyati |

ity uktvā,

                    	kāmatas tu kṛtaṃ mohāt prāyaścittaiḥ pṛthagvidhaiḥ | iti | (MDh 11.46)

mohaś cātrāvaliptatayā śrutismṛtyor anādaro 'bhipreto na tūnmādādilakṣaṇaḥ, tathāvidhasyonmattādeḥ kāmaṛtākāmakṛtayor aviśeṣāt | yo hi pratyakṣādiviṣaye samyagvartamānaḥ śāstrārthaṃ ca jānann api nāstikyenātiśayasāṃdṛṣṭikaviṣayābhilāṣeṇa codito mohāc chāstram asamañjasaṃ manyate, tasya tatkāmato mohāt kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ prāyaścittaiḥ pṛthagvidhair atyantagurubhir apagacchatīty abhiprāyaḥ | tataś ca kāmakṛtabrahmahatyādau maraṇāntikair eva prāyaścittair apanodanaprasaktāv ācāryeṇoktam: kāmato 'pi pāpaṃ kṛtvā pratyakṣaśrutivacanād[^14] ihaiva janmany aśvamedhādibhiḥ pāpaṃ nirṇijya vyavahāryatvaṃ jāyata iti | kiṃ ca: yadi prāyaścittāt saṃvyavahārtvamātram eva syād na doṣanirghātaḥ, tato yena sakṛt kṛtaṃ prāyaścittaṃ, sa punaḥ kṛtvāpi brahmahatyām asaṃvyavahāryo na syāt | yadi prāyaścittaṃ doṣāpaghātārthaṃ bhavet, tataḥ kṛtaprāyaścittasyāpi punar doṣotpattes tannirghātāya prāyaścittaṃ prasajyeta | yadā tu kṛtaprāyaścittataiva saṃvyavahāryatve hetuḥ, tadā sakṛtkṛte 'pi kṛtapāyaścittatāyā yāvajjīvam anapagamāt kim ity asaṃvyavahāryaḥ syāt |

 

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">athocyeta</span> | apāpāpanodakatve 'pi prāyaścittasya naimittikatvāt punar api nimittotpāde sati prasajyata iti |

 

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">tad ayuktam</span> | naivedaṃ "bhinne juhoti" (TV 4.2.3) itivad brahmahatyādau nimitte naimittikaṃ prāyaścittam | kiṃ tarhi | asaṃvyavahāryatve 'pi sati saṃvyavahāryatvārtham | tatra ca yady ayaṃ vacanārthaḥ: yo brahmahatyādi kuryāt, tam akṛtaprāyaścittaṃ na saṃpibed iti | tato yena sakṛt kṛtaṃ tasyāmaraṇaṃ kṛtaprāyaścittatvam asty eveti nāsaṃvyavhāryatvaṃ syāt | atha yadā yadā brahmahatyā bhavati, tadā tadā prāyaścitte kṛte saṃvyavahārtvam iti | tathā sati kālārthaḥ saṃyogaḥ syāt | tataś ca yadi kathaṃcid dhananānantaraṃ na kṛtaṃ tataḥ kālasyāpagatatvād uditasaṃdhyopāsanādivan na kaścid upakāraḥ syāt | yadi ca naimittikaṃ prāyaścittaṃ na doṣanirghātārtham, tataś ca yāvanti prāyaścittāny upādiśyante sarvāṇi tāny aviśeṣāt kartavyāni syuḥ, vikalpasya viṣayavibhāgasya cābhāvāt | doṣanirghātārthatve hi sarvaprāyaścittānāṃ samānakāryatvād yukto vikalpaḥ | viṣayavibhāgakalpanā ca yuktā | tasyākāmakṛtanaimittikatve tu prayojanāntarābhāvād asaty ekasmin kāryavikalpo niṣpramāṇakaḥ syāt | yatrāpi caśabdokta eva vāśabdāt vikalpaḥ, yathā:

                    	haviṣyabhug vānusaret pratisrotaḥ sarasvatīm | (MDh 11.77)

ityādau, tatrāpi yaḥ kaścid aniyamenaikaḥ kalpaḥ syāt | na cātra gurutarakalpasyānarthakyaprasaṅgād yuktā, tasyākāmakṛte doṣanirghātārthatvena tadviśeṣārthatvasiddheḥ |

 

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">athocyeta</span> | patitasyānadhikṛtasya dvijātikarmasv adhikārasañjananārthāni prāyaścittanīty asty evaikakāryatvaṃ teṣām, ataś cātrāpy upapadyata eva viṣayakalpaneti |

 

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">tad apy ayuktam</span>, pūrvoktadoṣaprasaṅgād eva | kiṃ cādhikārārthatve 'pi kartur ayogyatvavyāvṛttiṃ yogyatāṃ vā prāyaścittaṃ kuryāt | tatrāyogyatvaṃ tāvad brahmahatyādinimittam | tac ca tajjanitadoṣavattayā kartṛtvamātreṇa vā syāt | yadi ca vadhakartṛtvamātraṃ tat kriyānantaram eva pralīnam iti na tadvyāvṛttyā projanam asti | atha tūttarakāle 'apy asti, tat prāyascittasahasreṇāpy aśakyam apanetum | atha tu doṣavattātmakam ayogyatvaṃ, tataḥ tadupākaraṇadvāreṇa śaktyā yogyatā kartum iti doṣanirghātārtham eva prāyaścittaṃ syāt | atha prāyaścittenānyad apūrvaṃ yogyatvaṃ janyate na tu doṣavattātmakam ayogyatvam apanīyat ity ucyeta | tathā saty anvārambhaṇiyāvat sakṛd eva karaṇaṃ syāt, karmāṅgatā ca prāyaścittānāṃ prasajyeta, atrāpi kratūpakārakatvaṃ tādarthyaṃ ca pramāṇaśūnyaṃ kalpyaṃ syāt | yadi ca kāmakṛte 'dhikāramātrārthatocyeta, tato maraṇāntikaṃ prāyaścittam akāmakṛta eva syād, jīvaprāyaścittany eva kāmakṛte syuḥ, mṛtasyādhikārāsaṃbhavāt, saṃvyavahāryatvaṃ hi jīvata evāpekṣitaṃ yataḥ | tatraivamādīni vacanāny asaṃbandhāni syuḥ | yathāpastambena "asyāsmin loke pratyāpattir vidyate kalmaṣaṃ tu nirhaṇyate" (ĀpDh 1.24.25) | tathā,

                    	matipūrvam anirdeśyaṃ prāṇāntikam iti sthitiḥ | (MDh 11.146)

ity ajñātaviṣaye ca viṣayopadeśaḥ | yathā "surāyāś cājñāne taptakṛcchraḥ" iti vāsiṣṭham (VaDh 20.19) | tathā,

                    	ajñānād vāruṇīṃ pītvā saṃskāreṇaiva śudhyati | iti | (MDh 11.146)

evaṃ sarvasmṛtiṣv evaṃjātīyakānām asāmañjasyaṃ syāt | rahasye ca prāyaścittaṃ na syāt |

 

        	ata evam ayaṃ yājñavalkīyaśloko vyākhyātavyaḥ: yathaiva prāyaścittavacanād ajñāte 'pi pratiṣiddhakarmaṇi pāpaṃ bhavati | tac ca prāyaścittair apaiti | evam eva kāmato 'pi kṛte pāpe na maraṇāntikam eva prāyaścittam, api tu "tarati sarvaṃ pāpmanam" (VaDh 22.6) ityādivacanād ihaiva saṃvyavahāryo niṣkalmaṣo jāyate ity alaṃ prasaṅgena || 222 ||

 

_etad evānantaraślokena spaṣṭayati |_

 

                    	**prāyaścittam akurvāṇāḥ pāpeṣu niratā narāḥ |**

**              	apaścāttāpinaḥ kaṣṭān narakān yānti dāruṇān || 3.223 ||**

 

ye hi kāmataḥ pravartante, pravṛttikāle nitarāṃ pāpeṣu ratiṃ badhnanti, te pāpeṣu ratāḥ santo yady apaścāttāpinaḥ syuḥ, tataḥ prāyaścittāny akurvāṇāḥ kaṣṭān duḥsahān narakān pratipadyante | kaṣṭavacanāt siddhe 'pi punar dāruṇān ity atiśayanindārtham | ye tv akāmāt kathaṃcit pāpaṃ kuryuḥ, te niyogataḥ paścāttāpino bhavanty eva | na ca teṣāṃ pāpaniratatvam | te yady api prāyaścittaṃ na kuryuḥ, tathāpy asminn eva manuṣyaloke yātanāṃ prāpnuyur asminn eva janmani janmāntare vā, na tu yamalokasaṃbandhiṣu tāmisrādiṣv ity etat purastād apy uktam eva | tathā ca mantravarṇaḥ: "no jihmāyanto narakaṃ patāma" iti | jihmāyantaḥ kauṭilyena pravṛttāḥ, kāmakārapravṛttā iti yāvat | ataś cākāmakṛte naiva narakaprāptiḥ | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

                    	kāmakārakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ narakeṣūpabhujyate |

                    	ihaiva prāpnuyuḥ kleśān akāmakṛtapātakāḥ || iti |

ataś ca doṣanirghātārthatvāt prāyaścittasya, tadakaraṇe kaṣṭataranarakaprāptir upapannā || 223 ||

 

_tān idānīṃ narakān darśayati |_

 

                    	**tāmisraṃ lohaśaṅkuś ca mahānirayaśalmalī |**

**              	rauravaṃ kuḍmalaṃ pūtimṛttikaṃ kālasūtrakam || 3.224 ||**

**              	saṃghātaṃ lohitodaṃ ca saviṣaṃ saṃpratāpanam |**

**              	mahānarakakākolaṃ saṃjīvananadīpatham || 3.225 ||**

**              	avīcim andhatāmisraṃ kumbhīpākaṃ tathaiva ca |**

**              	asipatravanaṃ caiva tapanaṃ caikaviṃśakam || 3.226 ||**

 

atra dvābhyāṃ ślokābhyāṃ ṣoḍaś narakāḥ, tṛtīyena pañca | evam ekaviṃśatiḥ | tāmisro 'tyarthaṃ tamobahulaḥ | lohamayāḥ śaṅkavo yasmin anavarataṃ sarvagātreṣu nikhanyante, sa lokaśaṅkhuḥ | mahatā rayeṇa vegena nitarāṃ yatrājasraṃ kṣepaṇaṃ, sa mahānirayaḥ | tāmramayā agnivarṇāḥ śalmalidrumāḥ kaṇṭakino yatra pariṣvajyante, sa śalmaliḥ | yatrāsthīni bhittvā ruruvat taptāni lohaśṛṅgāṇy uttiṣṭhanti, sa rauravaḥ | kuḍmalam ity avikasitam ucyate | tad yathā padmādyavikasitaṃ piṇḍībhūtam āste, tadvad yatra sarvāṅgāni saṃpīḍya kuḍmalīkriyante, (sa) kuḍmalo nāma narakaḥ | pāṭhāntaraṃ ca: rauravaṃ kaśmalam iti, keśamalaprāyaḥ | pūtimṛttikaḥ spaṣṭaḥ | kṛṣṇasūtre protā yatrāntarikṣasthā (?) dhāryante, tac ca sūtraṃ nityaṃ cālyate, sa kālasūtrakaḥ | yathaiva dvau sumalinau saṃhatya taṇḍulādyavaghātaṃ kurutaḥ, evaṃ yatra saṃhanyante, sa saṃghātaḥ | sarveṣūdakakāryeṣu lohitaṃ yatra, sa lohitatodaḥ | saviṣāḥ phaṇino 'navarataṃ yatra bhakṣayanti, sa saviṣaḥ | prakarṣeṇāntar bahiś ca tāpanāt saṃpratāpanam | pāṭhāntaraṃ tu: ṛbīsaṃ saṃpratāpanam iti | tatrāntarudare nityaṃ garbhasthitāpacyante yasmin, sa ṛbīsaḥ | yam apekṣyānye narakāḥ kālasūtrādayo laghavaḥ, sa mahānarakaḥ | lohatuṇḍaiḥ kākolūkair aharniśaṃ tudyante yatra, sa kākolaḥ | saṃjīvya saṃjīvyānekavidhaiḥ prakārair yatra pramāpyante, sa saṃjīvanaḥ | vaitaraṇī nāma nadī pūyaprāyodakā, sā panthā yasya narakasya, sa nadīpathaḥ | adhomukhā gartāyām aṅgārapūrṇāyāṃ nikhātā dāvāgninā yatropajvālyante, so 'vīciḥ | andhasarpāḥ santas tāmisrāyām iva śakaṭaiḥ saṃcūrṇyante yatra, so 'ndhatāmisraḥ | kumbhīpākaḥ spaṣṭaḥ | khaḍgadhārāvat tīkṣṇāni patrāṇi yasmin tālavane, tasmin kṛṣyante yatra, so 'sipatravanaḥ | pracaṇḍaḥ savitaiva yatra tapati, na tv anyāni mahābhūtāni santi, sa tapanaḥ || 224–6 ||

 

_evam etān ekaviṃśatinarakān svakarmānurūpyeṇa |_

 

                    	**mahāpātakajair ghorair upapātakajais tathā |**

**              	anvitā yānty acaritaprāyaścittā narādhamāḥ || 3.227 ||**

 

ghoragrahaṇaṃ kāmakārapratipattyartham | kāmakṛtamahāpātakopapātakajanitaiḥ pāpair anvitā yuktāḥ santo ye prāyaścittaṃ nācaranti nāstikyātiśayāt, ta evaitān narakān yānti, na tv akāmakṛtapāpā apīty abhiprāyaḥ | mahāpātakopapātakatatsamātideśikavyatirekeṇātra kāmakṛte 'pi naiva narakaprāptiḥ, tiryaktvam eva tatra | yathāha manuḥ |

                    	yad vā tad vā paradravyam apahṛtya balān naraḥ |

                    	avaśyaṃ yāti tiryaktvaṃ jagdhvā caivāhutaṃ haviḥ || iti | (MDh 12.68)

balāt kāmakārād ity arthaḥ || 227 ||

 

_ke punas te mahāpātakina ity ata āha |_

 

                    	**brahmahā madyapaḥ stenas tathaiva gurutalpagaḥ |**

**              	ete mahāpātakino yaś caitaiḥ saṃpibet samām || 3.228 ||**

 

yo brāhmaṇaṃ svātantryeṇa prayojakatvena vā hanti ghātayati vā, sa brahmahā | madyaśabdaś ca paiṣṭyāṃ draṣṭavyaḥ | stenaś ca brāhmaṇasuvarṇastenaḥ | gurutalpagas tv ācāryasya pitur vā bhāryāṃ ya upagacchati, sa vijñeyaḥ | taiś ca vyastaiḥ samastair vā saṃpibet saṃgatya bhojanapānādy ācaret | kiyantaṃ kālam ity ata āha: samāṃ saṃvatsaram ity arthaḥ | tathā cāmnāyaḥ |

                    	steno hiraṇyasya surāṃ pibaṃś ca guros talpam āvasan brahmahā ca |

                    	ete patanti catvāraḥ pañcamaś cācaraṃs taiḥ || iti | (ChU 5.10.9)

hiraṇyaśabdaś ca viśeṣaṇāntarād ṛte suvarṇa eva prayujyate | sthitam etac chāndogye: "hiraṇyam iti jātarūpaṃ pratīyāt sarvatra" iti śrutiprasthānam evāṅgīkṛtya sūtrakārair uktam | tathā ca carakāḥ: "āgneyo vai brāhmaṇaḥ āgneyaṃ hiraṇyaṃ tasmād agnaye brāhmaṇasya hiraṇyaṃ dadyād yathāgnaya evāgnī(dhre ? dhe) hiraṇyaṃ deyam" iti prakṛtya, "na suvarṇaṃ brāhmaṇebhyo 'pahartavyaṃ mahad vā ena enam ārchati yo brāhmaṇebhyo 'pahṛtyāvarundhate" iti | ato brāhmaṇasuvarṇaharaṇaṃ steyam atrābhipretam | tathā ca vasiṣṭha ete eva śrutismṛtī upasaṃhṛtya mahāpātakādhikāre "brāhmaṇasuvarṇaharaṇaṃ ca" ity uktavān (VaDh 1.20) | "surāṃ pibaṃś ca" ity atrāpi paiṣṭy evābhipretā | tasyām eva mukhyaḥ surāśabdaḥ, gaulīprabhṛtiṣu tu madyasāmānyād gauṇaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca "vijñeyā trividhā surā" (MDh 11.94) iti sarvāsāṃ mukhyatvam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span> | na hy anekārthatvam asati pratibandhe nyāyyam | kathaṃ nirṇaya iti cet | paiṣṭyām eva hi vede prayogadarśanād vājapeye sautrāmaṇyāṃ ca surāgraheṣu | tathā agnīṣomīyabrāhmaṇe carakāṇām "atha yan malyam āsīt tat paścāt samadohat surā vai malyaṃ yan nāmānṛtaṃ pāpmā tamaḥ surā" ity evaṃ surāśabdaḥ paiṣṭyām eva prayuktaḥ | tatraiva copasaṃhāre "tasmād brāhmaṇaḥ surāṃ na pibet" ity uktam | ataḥ paiṣṭīpāna eva mahāpātakaṃ nānyatreti sthitam | guros talpam āvased ity atrāpi pitary ācārye vā guruśabdaḥ, pitary eva vā,

                    	niṣekādīni karmāṇi yaḥ karoti yathāvidhi |

                    	saṃbhāvayati cānnena sa vipro gurur ucyate || (MDh 2.142)

iti manuvacanāt | pitṛtvopacārāc cācārye gauṇatvam eva yuktam | yathoktam |

                    	tatrāsya mātā sāvitrī pitā tv ācārya ucyate | iti | (MDh 2.170)

evam anyatrāpi śabdārthavivekaḥ kāryaḥ | tathā cācāryānyāṃ vasiṣṭhena gurutalpātideśaḥ kṛtaḥ: "ācāryaputraśiṣyabhāryāsu caivam" iti (VaDh 20.15) | yat tu nāradenoktam:

                    	mātā mātṛṣvasā śvaśrūr mātulānī pitṛṣvasā |

                    	pitṛvyasakhiśiṣyastrī bhaginī tatsakhī snuṣā ||

                    	duhitācāryabhāryā ca sagotrā śaraṇāgatā |

                    	rājñī pravrajitā dhātrī sādhvī varṇottamā ca yā ||

                    	āsām anyatamāṃ gatvā gurutalpaga ucyate |

                    	śiśnasyotkartanāt tasya nānyo daṇḍo vidhīyate || (NSm 12. 72–74 )

iti, tat tu nyāyavirodhān manuvirodhāc ca daṇḍasāmyapratipattyarthaṃ na śabdaniyamāyety avagantavyam | yat tu ihaiva pitṛṣvasāṃ mātulānīm ityādi, tat svāvasare vakṣyāmaḥ | "brahmahā caite patanti catvāraḥ" (ChU 5.10.9) ity atra ātatāyisaṃgrāmavyatirekeṇa yo brāhmaṇam anyenāprayuktaḥ svātantryeṇa hanyād anyaṃ vā dravyadānādinā vaśīkṛtya ghātayati, sa pratyetavyaḥ | kuta etat | "ātatāyinaṃ hatvā nāsya prāṇān ācchettuḥ kilbiṣm āhuḥ" (VaDh 3.15) iti vacanāt | tathā |

                    	svādhyāyinaṃ kule jātaṃ yo hanyād ātatāyinam |

                    	na tena bhrūṇahā bhavati manyus taṃ manyum ṛcchati || iti | (VaDh 3.18)

tathā |

                    	guruṃ vā bālavṛddhau vā brāhmaṇaṃ vā bahuśrutam |

                    	ātatāyinam āyāntaṃ hanyād evāvicārayan || iti | (MDh 8.350)

ātatāyinam āyāntam iti vacanāt saṃgrāmābhyanujñāpy atraiva śloke | "api vedāntagaṃ raṇe" "jighāṃsantaṃ jighāṃsīyāt" (VaDh 3.17) ity evaṃ saṃgrāmādhikāre sarvatra smṛtiṣv anujñāvacanāni santi | yas tu dhanakrītaḥ paraprayukto hanyāt, tasya svāmigāmitvāt kriyāphalānām ṛtvijām iva brahmahatyājanyaphalasaṃbandho nāsty eva | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca "brāhmaṇo na hantavyaḥ" ity āmnāyavacanād dhanādikrītasyāpi brahmahatyāsty eva | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">śyenādivad</span> etad draṣṭavyam | yathaiva śyenādijanye vadhe nartvijāṃ doṣaḥ, tathātrāpi | yathāgnīṣomīyavadhe "na hiṃsyāt sarvā bhūtāni" iti ṛtvijāṃ pratiṣedho na bhavati, tathātrāpi | anye tu kutaścid āgamayyemaṃ ślokaṃ paṭhanti |

                    	rāgād dveṣāt pramādād vā svataḥ parata eva vā |

                    	yo hanyad brāhmaṇaṃ kaścit sa sarvo brahmahā bhavet || iti |

tat tv avijñātamūlatvād vicāryam | yady api ca syāt, tathāpy ātideśikatvān mahāpātakaṃ tāvan na bhavati | yathā, "sṛṣṭaś ced brāhmaṇavadhe hatvāpi rājanyavaiśyau cejānau" ityādi (cf. MDh 11.88) | tathā ca lokayātrikāḥ paṭhanti: "anyāyena gṛhītasvaś ca" ityādi | "tam āhur brahmaghātakam" ity aghātakam api vacanasāmarthyād ghātakam ity āhuḥ, evaṃ dhanakrītāder api syāt | ato ya eva svayam ananyaprayuktaḥ śastrādinā parikrayādibhir vā hantāraṃ svīkṛtya brāhmāṇaṃ hanti ghātayati vā, tasyaiva brahmahāśabdenātra grahaṇam | brāhmaṇasuvarṇastenādayaś catvāra iti pāṭhāt siddhe 'pi punaḥśrutiḥ pātakasaṃyojakādinivṛttyarthā | tad etad ācāryeṇāpy uktam: "ete mahāpātakinaḥ" iti | "pañcamaś cācaraṃs taiḥ" (ChU 5.10.9) ity atrāpi tair eva caturbhiḥ sahācaraṇe mahāpatakitvaṃ na tu tatsaṃsargino 'pi | pañcama iti cāsyaiva dārḍhyārtham uktam || 228 ||

 

_idānīṃ mahāpātakasamāni |_

 

                    	**gurūṇām atyadhikṣepo vedanindā suhṛdvadhaḥ |**

**              	brahmahatyāsamaṃ hy etad adhītasya ca nāśanam || 3.229 ||**

 

atra ca bahuvacanād ācāryādayo 'pi sarve guravaḥ pratyetavyāḥ | teṣāṃ "mahāpātakitvaṃ yuṣmākam asti" ity evaṃprakāro 'tiśayenādhikṣepo 'atyadhikṣepaḥ | tatra ca guruviśeṣāpekṣayā adhikṣepaviśeṣāpekṣayā ca prāyaścittakalpanā | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> agurāv api "brāhmaṇābhiśaṃsane doṣas tāvān | dvir anenasi" (GDh 21.17–18) ity asty eva pātakasamatvam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | prāyaścittāntaraṃ tu tatra | yathāha vasiṣṭhaḥ: "brāhmaṇam anṛtenābhiśasya patanīyenopapatanīyena vā māsam abbhakṣaḥ śuddhavatīr āvartayet" iti (VaDh 23.39) | atra tu brahmahatyāprāyaścittam eva yathā syād ity ārambhaḥ | mahāpātakavyatirikte tv adhikṣepe tadanurūpam eva prāyaścittaṃ veditavyam | vedanindā ca hetuśāstrāvaṣṭambhena śrutismṛtyor bādhitāntaḥkaraṇatayānuṣṭhānaparyantatvenānādaraḥ | tathā cāha manuḥ |

                    	yo 'vamanyeta te tūbhe hetuśāstrāśrayād dvijaḥ |

                    	sa sādhubhir bahiṣkāryo nāstiko vedanindakaḥ || iti | (MDh 2.11)

suhṛdvadhas tv abrāhmaṇaviṣayaḥ, tasya tatsamatvavacanāt | adhītanāśanaṃ tu pitrādyadhītāṃ śākhāṃ neyaṃ śobhaneti kṛtvā tatparityāgaḥ | anye tv adhītavismaraṇam evācakṣate | tat tv atiprasaṅgān nātīya yuktam | manunā tu surāpānasamatvena,

                    	brahmojjho vedanindā ca kauṭasākṣyaṃ suhṛdvadhaḥ |

                    	garhitānādyayor jagdhiḥ surāpānasamāni ṣaṭ || (MDh 11.56)

ity uktam | ataś ca prāyaścittavikalpaḥ | anyatrāpy anekapāṭhe saty evam eva vyākhyeyam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> vedavirodhavan manuvirodho 'pi smṛtyantarāṇāṃ bādhanāya yuktaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span>, yadi virodhaḥ syāt | iha tu mahāpātakatvāviśeṣād brahmahatyātideśamadhye suhṛdvadhasya surāpānasamamadhyapaṭhitasya punaḥ pāṭhād avirodha eva | vispaṣṭataraṃ tv etad upariṣṭād vakṣyāmaḥ || 229 ||

 

                    	**niṣiddhabhakṣaṇaṃ jaihmyam utkarṣe ca vaco 'nṛtam |**

**              	rajasvalāmukhāsvādaḥ surāpānasamāni tu || 3.230 ||**

 

niṣiddhasya laśunāder nāstikyātiśayān niṣedhaṃ jānata eva kāmakāreṇa bhakṣaṇam | yathāha manuḥ |

                    	chatrākaṃ viḍvarāhaṃ ca laśunaṃ grāmakukkuṭam |

                    	palaṇḍuṃ gṛñjanaṃ caiva matyā jagdhvā pated dvijaḥ || (MDh 5.19)

iti viśeṣābhidhānāt | aviśeṣābhidhāne 'pi caitāny eva gṛhyante, asmād eva manuvacanāt | jaihmyaṃ tu kauṭilyam ucyate | tad api yadi kaścit surāpānādipravṛttaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ nivāraṇasamartho 'pi kauṭilyenopekṣate, sa evātra pratyetavyaḥ | yathāha gautamaḥ: "durbalahiṃsāyāṃ ca vimocane śaktaś cet" iti (GDh 21.19) | hiṃsāvacanaṃ tatropalakṣaṇatvenaiva draṣṭavyaṃ sarvatraiva tu śaktasyopekṣaṇe pātakātideśārtham | jātibhraṃśakaramadhye ca jaihmyaṃ manunoktam (MDh 11.67) | tad etad upariṣṭād vakṣyāmaḥ | "utkarṣe ca vaco 'nṛtam" iti | etac ca manunā brahmahatyāsamatvenoktam (MDh 11.55) | tatraivaṃ vivekaḥ | brahmahatyāprasaṅge yad anṛtaṃ tasya tatsamatvam, surāpānaprasaṅge yad anṛtaṃ tasya surāpānasamatvam, yathā kaścit pakṣapātādinā brahmahaṇam eva svapakṣotkarṣārthaṃ nāyam evaṃvidha iti brūyād viparītaṃ vā | evam anyatrāpi yojyam | rajasvalā cātra surāpī vyākhyeyā nodakyā, tasyā upagamane 'py alpadoṣatvād, upagamanāṅgatvāc ca mukhāsvādasya | prakramānuguṇyāc caitad evaṃ yuktam || 230 ||

 

                    	**aśvaratnamanuṣyastrībhūdhenuharaṇaṃ tathā |**

**              	nikṣepasya ca sarvaṃ hi suvarṇasteyasaṃmitam || 3.231 ||**

 

aśvo 'tra yajñasādhanabhūtaḥ prādhānyena vā saṃgrāmasādhanabhūtaḥ pratyetavyaḥ | dhenur api yajñāṅgabhūtaiva | traivarṇikāś ca manuṣyāḥ | strī ca brāhmaṇaparigṛhītaiva | bhūmir api brāhmaṇasātkṛtaiva, nikṣepaś ca | tathāśabdo rajatādyarthaḥ | tathā ca manuḥ |

                    	nikṣepasyāpaharaṇaṃ narāśvarajatasya ca |

                    	bhūmivastramaṇīnāṃ ca rukmasteyasamaṃ smṛtam || iti | (MDh 11.57)

pūrvatra steyavacanaṃ suvarṇaviṣayam eveti jñāpitam | ataś ca nikṣepaḥ suvarṇavyatirekeṇeti vyākhyeyam || 231 ||

 

                    	**sakhibhāryākumārīṣu svayoniṣv antyajāsu ca |**

**              	sagotrāsu sutastrīṣu gurutalpasamaṃ viduḥ || 3.232 ||**

 

antyaḥ śūdraḥ tena pūrvavarṇeṣu triṣu jātā antyajāḥ svayoniṣv iti ca mātṛpitṛsaṃbandhāḥ pitṛṣvasrīyādayo gṛhyante | sutastriyaś cāsavarṇāḥ, snuṣābhaginyor uttaratrāmnānāt | spaṣṭam anyat | mānave 'pi ca "retaḥsekaḥ svayonyāsu" (MDh 11.58) ity atra cakaradvayasāmarthyād sagotropādānaṃ vyākhyeyam || 232 ||

 

_prāyaścittātirekārthaṃ tu bhedenāha |_

 

                    	**pitṛśvasāṃ mātulānīṃ snuṣāṃ mātṛṣvasām api |**

**              	mātuḥ sapatnīṃ bhaginīm ācāryatanayāṃ tathā || 3.233 ||**

**              	ācāryapatnīṃ svasutāṃ gacchaṃs tu gurutalpagaḥ |**

**              	chittvā liṅgaṃ vadhas tasya sakāmāyāś ca yoṣitaḥ || 3.234 ||**

 

atra evaśabdārthe tuśabdasyotkṛṣya yojanā gacchan gurutalpaga eveti | etad uktaṃ bhavati: yuktaṃ sakhibhāryādiṣu samatvavacanaṃ pitṛṣvasrādiṣu gurutalpaga eva, yathābhyarhite mantrāṇi kim ayaṃ rājasama ity ucyate dhruvam ayaṃ rājaiveti | evaṃ ca vadatā piṛṣvasrādiṣu gurutalpānyūnatvaṃ tatsamātirekaś ca darśito bhavati | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye tu</span> mukhyam eva gurutalpaṃ vyācakṣate | (tad ayuktaṃ ?) tat tv iha mātur anupādānād (ayuktam) | smṛtyantare ca "brahmahasurāpagurutalpaga" ity uktvā, "mātṛpitṛyonisaṃbandhāga" (GDh 21.1) ity uktam, "snuṣāyāṃ gavi ca tatsamo 'vakara ity eke" iti ca (GDh 23.12–13) | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">tad asamañjasaṃ syād</span>, ataḥ pūrvaiva vyākhyā jyāyasī | mātuḥ sapatnīti cāsavarṇābhipretā itarāsu tu gurutalpasamatvaṃ mukhyam eva yataḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 233–4 ||

 

_idānīm upapātakāny ucyante |_

 

                    	**govadho vrātyatā stainyam ṛṇānāṃ cānapakriyā  |**

**              	anāhitāgnitāpaṇyavikrayaḥ parivindanam || 3.235 ||**

**              	bhṛtād adhyayanādānaṃ bhṛtakādhyāpanaṃ tathā |**

**              	pāradāryaṃ pārivittyaṃ vārdhuṣyaṃ lavaṇakriyā || 3.236 ||**

**              	strīśūdraviṭkṣatravadho ninditārghopajīvanam |**

**              	nāstikyaṃ vratalopaś ca sutānāṃ caiva vikrayaḥ || 3.237 ||**

**              	dhānyarūpyapaśusteyam ayājyānāṃ ca yājanam |**

**              	pitṛmātṛsuhṛttyāgas taṭākārāmavikrayaḥ || 3.238 ||**

**              	kanyāyā dūṣaṇaṃ caiva parivindakayājanam |**

**              	kanyāpradānaṃ tasyaiva kauṭilyaṃ brahmalopanam || 3.239 ||**

**              	ātmārthe ca kriyārambho madyapastrīniṣevaṇam |**

**              	svādhyāyāgnisutatyāgo bāndhavatyāga eva ca || 3.240 ||**

**              	indhanārthaṃ drumacchedaḥ strīhiṃsrauṣadhijīvanam |**

**              	hiṃsrayantravidhānaṃ ca vyasanāny ātmavikrayaḥ || 3.241 ||**

**              	asacchāstrādhigamanam ākareṣv adhikāritā |**

**              	bhāryāvikrayaṇaṃ caiṣām ekaikam upapātakam || 3.242 ||**

 

ete 'ṣṭau ślokā nigadoktāḥ | ekaikagrahaṇaṃ dvitrādyanuṣṭhāne prāyaścittagauravārtham | upapātakasaṃjñāpy evamarthaiva, upacayenopetya vā sevyamānaṃ pātakam eva syād iti | ata eva gautamena pātakamadhye ninditakarmābhyāso darśitaḥ (GDh 21) | evam etair aṣṭābhiḥ ślokair ekapañcāśadupapātakāny uktāni | anyāny api ca sūryābhyuditaḥ sūryābhinirmukta ityādīny atraiva tathāśabdādigṛhītatvena draṣṭavyāni | atha vā prāyaścittasāmyārtha eṣām iha pāṭho na tūpapātakasaṃjñāniyatyarthaḥ | tathā śaṅkhenāṣṭādaśaivopapātakāny uktāni | yathāha: "ata ūrdhvam upapatanīyāni | kanyādūṣī somavikrayī vṛṣalīpatiḥ kaumāradāratyāgy asurāmadyapāyī goghnaḥ śūdravadhī guroḥ pratihantā nāstikaḥ kṛtaghnaḥ kūṭavyavahārī vṛttighno mithābhiśaṃsī hiraṇyastenaḥ patitasaṃvyavahārī mitradhruk śaraṇāgataghātī pratikūlavṛttir ity etāny aṣādaśaivopapātakāni" iti | evaṃ sumantuḥ: "strīrajatagostainyaṃ goś ca gamanaṃ nāśakaṃ bhūmyanṛtaṃ kṣatriyavaiśyagoghnatā parivittitāvakīrṇitā pratirūpakavṛttiś cety upapātakāni" iti | śātātape tv aṣṭāv evopapātakāny uktāni: "athopapātakāny agnyutsādī" ityādīni | vāsiṣṭhe tu "sūryābhyuditaḥ sūryābhinirmuktaḥ" (VaDh 1.18) ity upakramya, upapātakinām enasvina ity evaṃ saṃjñā kṛtā, tanmadhye niḥsaṃdigdhopapātakināṃ parivittyādīnām anukramaṇāt | ato yathānirdiṣṭānām eva prāyaścittasāmyārtham iyaṃ saṃjñety evam eva vyākhyeyam | atra ca pāradāryasteyastrīvadhādīni mahāpātakatatsamātirekeṇa vyākhyeyātni || 235–42 ||

 

_idānīṃ yathānirdeśaṃ brahmahatyādīnāṃ prāyaścittāny āha |_

 

**              	śiraḥkapāladhvajavān bhaikṣāśī karma vedayan |**

**              	brahmahā dvādaśa samā mitabhuk śuddhim āpnuyāt || 3.243 ||**

 

śiraḥsaṃlagnam eva kapālaṃ dhvajaś cihnaṃ yasya sa evamuktaḥ | kapālagrahaṇaṃ cākhaṇḍaśirovāraṇārtham | spaṣṭam anyat | etac ca sārvavarṇikaṃ prāyaścittam | smṛtyantare tu kvacit sāmarthyān niyamaḥ | yathāha śaṅkah: "brahmahā pariṣadānumataḥ khaṭvāṅgī gardabhājinī mṛnmayapātrapatitaśiṣṭānnabhojī svakarma vikhyāpayaṃś cared baikṣam ekakālāhāraḥ śūnyāgāranadīparvataguhāvṛkṣamūlaniketanaḥ | sa evaṃ dvādaśe varṣe śuddhim āpnoti, antarā vā brāhmaṇaṃ maraṇān mocayitvā gavāṃ vā dvādaśānāṃ paritrāṇāt, sadya eva vāśvamedhāvabhṛthe snātvā pūto bhavati" ity upakramya, sarvāṇi prāyaścittany abhidhāya, punas tadante gosahasrapradānam uktvā, punar uktam:

                    	prāyaścittam upāsīno vāgyatas trir upaspṛśet |

                    	ekavāsārdravāsāś ca laghvāśī sthaṇḍileśayaḥ ||

                    	sthānaṃ vīrāsanaṃ maunaṃ mauñjī daṇḍakamaṇḍalū |

                    	bhaikṣacaryāgnikāryaṃ ca kūśmāṇḍībhiḥ sadā ghṛtam || iti |

na hy atraivarṇikasya kūśmāṇḍībhir agnikāryam upapadyate | atas traivarṇikasyaivaitat | kvacic copadeśād eva viśeṣaḥ | yathāha śātātapaḥ: "brāhmaṇo brāhmaṇaṃ hatvā tasya śiraḥkapālam ādāya" iti | atra kapālaniyamamātram eva viśeṣaḥ | evaṃ yatra sāmarthyāc chabdato vā kartṛlābhaḥ tan niyatakartṛkam | yatra tv aviśeṣābhidhānam, yathātraiva, tat sārvavarṇikam | evam anyatrāpi yojyam | na caikam evaitat sarvasmṛtisiddhaṃ dvādaśavārṣikaṃ vratam ity āśaṅkanīyaṃ, pratismṛti prayogabedasya "vaktāro dharmaśāstrāṇām" (YDh 1.4–5) ity atra śloke 'bhihitatvāt | ata eva ca yadi śaṅkhoktaṃ dvādaśavārṣikam ārabdham, tato 'ntarā brāhmaṇaṃ maraṇān mocayitvā gavāṃ vā dvādaśānāṃ paritrāṇāc chuddhiḥ | anyatra tu niyogataḥ parisamāpanam eva | aśvamedhāvabhṛthas tu śāṅkhe 'pi kalpāntaratayaiva vyākhyeyaḥ, śrutau nairapekṣyopadeśāt | evaṃ hi śrūyate:


                            	sa yadā rājānam unnetonnayati, athainasvina upatiṣṭhante 'ta upabruvate itthaṃ brāhmaṇam avadhiṣam itthaṃ guror jāyām abhyagām iti | niruktam eno yathā yathā tān ṛtvijo rājā ca brūyur aśvamedhāvabhṛthapūtā bhavatheti | te 'po 'bhyavayanti | yathāhis tvaco nirmucyate, evaṃ sarvasmāt pāpmano nirmucyante | tān na jugupseyuḥ | sa yāvantam aśvemedheneṣṭvā lokaṃ jayati, tris tāvantaṃ jayati | yasyaivaṃ viduṣa evam enasvino 'vabhṛtham abhyavayanti |

iti jābāliśrutiḥ | iyam eva hi kātyāyanenāpi nibaddhā: "utkrānte yajamāne pāpakṛto 'bhyavayanty acaritvā vratāny aśvamedhāvabhṛthākhyāsta" iti | ato nāsya smārtaprāyaścittārthatā ghaṭate | na hi smṛtiśeṣatvena śrutiḥ śakyā kalpayitum | yadi tu prakrāntadvādaśavārṣikasyaitat syāt, tataḥ śrutāv eva tadanuvādena vidhīyeta | na caivaṃ śrutir asti | api ca, yadi śrutau dvādaśavārṣikānuvādaḥ syāt, tato 'nyataḥ prāptyabhāvāt tad eva tāvad vidheyaṃ syāt | na hi tathā śravaṇe sati smṛter mūlāntarakalpanopapadyate yataḥ | tatrāśvamedhāvabhṛthasnānam aṅgatvena parisamāptyarthaṃ vā vidhīyeta | na ca nityasyānityaparisamāptir yuktā | yadi tu naimittikī parisamāptir ucyeta, tathā sati yadi kathaṃcin na snāyāt, tato dvādaśavārṣike kṛte 'pi na śudhyati | atha tu naimittikaṃ tadaṅgaṃ snānam ity ucyeta, tathā saty avabhṛthe snātvāpi dvādaśavārṣikaśeṣaṃ parisamāpanīyam eva syāt | ato 'śvamedhāvabhṛthasya svātantryakalpanaiva nyāyyā | ata eva ca vāsiṣṭhe bhrūṇahatyāprakaraṇam ullaṅghyānyatroktam: "athāparaṃ bhrūṇahatyāyā dvādaśarātram abbhakṣo dvādaśarātram upavased aśvamedhāvabhṛthaṃ vā gacchet" iti (VaDh 23.37) | laghutvād asyānyaśeṣatvāśaṅkāpi kasyacit syāt | ata eva śaṅkhenāpi: "sadya evāśvamedhāvabhṛthe snātvā pūto bhavati" iti sadya evety avadhāraṇād dvādaśābdākaraṇāc cāsya svātantryam eva darśitam | etac ca śaṅkhoktaṃ kṣatriyavaiśyayor evādhītavedayor anagnikayoś cākāmato guṇavadbrāhmaṇavadhe draṣṭavyam, kāmato hy etad eva gosahasradānopacitam | śūdrasāpy etad dānasahitaṃ mantravarjaṃ vākāmakṛta eva | kāmakṛte tu śūdrasya maraṇāntikam eva | pratilomānāṃ tv akāmato 'pi maraṇāntikam eva | kuta etat | śaṅkhavacanād eva: "ata ūrdhvaṃ patanīyāni" iti prakṛtya, "niṣkṛtis teṣāṃ vihitā sadbhir akāmakṛte" ity uktam | kṣatriyavaiśyayoś caitat | anyatra svalpetikartavyatāyuktaṃ brāhmaṇasyopadiṣṭaṃ yataḥ "brāhmaṇo brāhmaṇaṃ ghātayitvā tasya śiraḥkapālam ādāya tīrthāny anucared ātmanaḥ pāpaṃ saṃkīrtayan dvādaśe varśe śuddhim āpnoti, athāśvamedhaṃ paśyati tasya darśanād eva śuddhim āpnoti" iti [śātātapaḥ] | tac ca svaśabdopādānād brāhmaṇasyaiva | na caitat kāmakṛtaviṣayaṃ brāhmaṇasyāpīti vaktuṃ śakyam, akāmakṛta iti vacanāt | ataḥ kṣatriyavaiśyayor evaitad iti yuktam | śūdrasya tv asāmarthyān naitad yuktam | anagnikayor iti kuto labdham, kevalasya puṃso 'vidhānāt, patnyadhīnatvāc cāgnisādhyānāṃ karmaṇām, tasyāś ca patanakāraṇābhāvāt | yatraivobhayoḥ patanam, tatraiva vaitānikasaṃbaddhāni prāyaścittāni | anyatarapatane tu śarīramātrasādhyair evādhikāraḥ | na cātra kiṃcid aupāsanādisaṃbaddhaṃ karmāsti | yat tu kūśmāṇḍībhir agnikāryam, tat samidādhānaṃ brahmacārisaṃbandhivat pratyetavyam | tac ca laukika evāgau yuktam | gardabhājinopadeśāc cātrāvakīrṇipaśur api yadi prāpnoti, so 'pi laukika evāgnau yuktaḥ | ato 'nagikasyaivaitad iti sthitam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evam api yadi nāmāgner atropayogo na syāt, na tv anagnikasyaiva prāyaścittam iti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">stayam</span> | yady atrāpy agnisaṃbandhaṃ prāyaścittāntaraṃ na syāt | tad api tu śrūyata eva | tad yathā: "yajeta vāśvamedhena" (MDh 11.74) ityādi mānavam | tatrāśvamedho rāṣṭrādhipater eva, "tasmād rāṣṭry aśvamedhena yajeta" iti śruteḥ | svarjidādayas trayāṇām api varṇānām iṣṭaprathamayajñānāṃ bhavanti | na ca teṣām anyat prāyaścittam asti, sāpekṣatvena viṣamaśiṣṭavikalpāsaṃbhavāt | tadanadhikṛtānām evānyat prāyaścittaṃ yuktam, tasyānanyaviṣayatvād iṣṭaprathamayajñasya | ananyaviṣayatvād aniṣṭaprathamayajñasyāpy āhitāgner agniṣṭoma eva prāyaścittam | gautamenāśvamedhāvabhṛtham uktvā, "anyayajñe 'py agniṣṭudantaś cet" ity uktam (GDh 22.9–10) | na cāgniṣṭudantaḥ kaścit kratur asti, satrāhīnayoḥ prāyaśo 'tirātrāntatvāt | yatrāpi kvacid atirātrāntatā nāsti, tatrāpy agniṣṭudantatā nāsty eva | ato 'yam agniṣṭucchabdo 'nvagniṣṭomastotravacano draṣṭavyaḥ | tadantaś cāgniṣṭoma eva bhavati | yasya cānyaprayuktasyāpy avabhṛte snātvā śuddhir bhavati, tatra svayaṃpravṛtter daṇḍāpūpanyāyena siddher agniṣṭomasyāsty eva vidhānam | kāṭhake 'py aśvamedhavad agniṣṭomasyāpi "bhrūṇahatyāyā vā eṣo 'timucyate, yo 'gniṣṭomasaṃsthaṃ yajate" ity āhitāgner agniṣṭoma evāniṣṭaprathamayajñasya | itarasya tu svarjidādayo draṣṭavyāḥ | yasya tv aupāsanamātram, tasyānyat prāyaścittaṃ śāṅkha evoktam | tatra prāyaścittam akāmāvāptau | kāmakṛte 'py eke:


                            	patito hy ātmānam uddharet | saṃvatsaraṃ taptakṛcchram ācaret | kṛtavāpanaḥ śucir apo 'bhyaveyāt trir ekārdravāsāḥ kāṣṭhamaunī vīrāsanam āsīta rātrau, divā tiṣṭhed yukto 'gnikāryaparaḥ sāvitrīṃ savanānugāṃ japet, svayaṃ vratam abhyupagamya kuśacīraphalakavāsā mauñjī mekhalī darbhapavitrapāṇir haviṣyaṃ śrapec caruṃ bhaikṣam aduṣṭaṃ vā yātrikam aśnīyād dvādaśarātraṃ copavāso brāhmaṇatarpaṇaṃ gavāhnikam ity evaṃ vyavahāryo 'nyathā patitaḥ śiṣṭair asaṃbhāṣyaḥ | iti

yady api caitad "na vikrīṇīyād avikreyāṇi" iti prakṛtya, "tilamadhugulaghṛtatailetyādinīlīparyantavikrayāt sadyaḥ patati" ity uktvoktam, tathāpy etan na tadviṣaytvena prāyaścittaṃ yuktam, "patito hy ātmānam uddharet" iti śruteḥ | na caiṣā pūrvatropayujyate, prakṛtatvenaiva siddhatvāt, prāyaścittasya cātigurutvena mahāpātakocitatvāt | ataḥ śruteḥ sāmarthāc ca prakaraṇasya bādhitatvān mahāpātakaprāyaścittam eveti vyākhyātṛsaṃpradāyāvicchedāt siddham | tathā ca sumantunā:


                            	rāgadveṣād alabhymāne prāyaścitte japahavanādhyayanabrahmacaryaparo bhaikṣāśī daṇḍī mekhalī triṣavaṇy adhaḥśāyī svayam eva mahad aśubhaṃ punāti | na brāhmaṇasya patanam icchanty ācāryāḥ, kilbiṣy upagataḥ pātavya ity āṅgirase | iti |

brāhmaṇagrahaṇaṃ cātra pradarśanārtham | yatra ca svayam abhyupagamya saṃvatsarāc chuddir iṣyate, tatrāvaśyaṃ tato 'dhikaṃ pariṣadā na dātavyam | tathā cānenaivoktam: "brahmahasurāpagurutalpagasuvarṇasteyināṃ mahāpātakināṃ vakṣyāmaḥ prāyaścittam" iti |


                            	brahmahā saṃvatsaraṃ kṛcchraṃ cared adhaḥśāyī svakarmācakṣāṇo bhaikṣāhāro divyanadīpulinaśāyī sadgrāmāśramagauṣṭhaparvataprasravaṇataponavavihārī syāt | saṃvatsare pūrṇe hiraṇyamaṇigovṛṣānnatilabhūmisarpīṃṣi brāhmaṇebhyo dattvā pūto bhavaty aśvamedhāvabhṛtasnānena vā sadyaḥ | iti |

"ato 'rdham ardhaṃ kṣatriyavaiśyavadhe vyākhyātam" iti japahavanasvādhyāyaparatādi pūrvoktaṃ ca samuccīyate | kṛcchraśabdaś cāyaṃ taptakṛcchre draṣṭavyaḥ | tad etan nāsaty aupāsane bhavati, "karma smārtaṃ vivāhāgnau" (YDh 1.96) iti niyamāt |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> etad apy apatnīkasya patane naiva yuktam, "jāyāpatyor na vibhāgo vidyate | pāṇigrahaṇād dhi sahatvaṃ karmaṇas taddravyaphaleṣu ca" (ĀpDh 2.14.16–18) iti smaraṇāt | na ca patnyāḥ patanaṃ,

                    	ā śuddheḥ saṃpratīkṣyo hi mahāpātakadūṣitaḥ | (YDh 1.76)

ity uktatvāt |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> evam, vaitānike patnyā vinā karmānuṣṭhānāsaṃbhavāt | smārtāni tu kṛtāvasathyasyaiva kaivalyasaṃbandhīny api karmāṇy aupāsane bhavanti | yathā brahmayajñasaṃbandhīni prāyaścittāni | na hi brahmayajñe sapatnīkasyādhikāra iti śakyaṃ vaktum | na ca tadgate 'py apacāre mahāvyāhṛtihomādyadhikāraḥ | evam upākarmaṇy api | yathā ca tatra, tathaupāsane yuktatvād dhomānāṃ kevalasyāpi patane pravṛttir avyāhataivety alaṃ prasaṅgena |

        	ataḥ sthitam etat kṣatriyavaiśyayor anagnikayor adhītavedayoś ca guṇavadbrāhmaṇavadhe śaṅkhotaṃ dvādaśavārṣikam iti | śūdrasya ca brāhmaṇamātravadhe āpastambena dvādaśavārṣikam uktam | śūdrāpekṣayā ca kṣatriyavaiśyayor alpaṃ prāyaścittam ity etad darśayiṣyāmaḥ | ata idaṃ guṇavadbrāhmaṇavadha ity uktam | kākakṛte tu gosahasradānasahitam | kuta etat | śaṅkhavacanād eva: "caturṣu varṇeṣu pramāpya dvādaśa saṃvatsarān ṣaṭ trīn saṃvatsaraṃ ca vratam ādiśet, teṣām ante gosahasraṃ tatho 'rdhaṃ tasyārdhaṃ tadardhaṃ ca dadyāt, sarveṣām ānupūrvyeṇa" iti | śūdrasya caitat prāyaścittaṃ sāmarthyāt vijñeyam | na hy utkṛṣṭavarṇānām apakṛṣṭavadha etat saṃbhavati | evaṃ hy uktam: "sarveṣām anyonyāpakṛṣṭavadhe cāndrāyaṇam" iti | ataḥ śūdrasyaiva vittavata idaṃ prāyaścittam | niḥsvasya tv āpastamboktam, vaiśyasya vā samastaṃ coktam | tataś ca kṣatriyavaiśyayoḥ kāmakṛta etat syāt, śaṅkhavacanād eva, yathāpakṛṣṭaṃ ca yad akāmakṛte kāmakṛte tad yathotkṛṣṭam iti, ataḥ kāmakṛte gosahasrasahitam ity eṣā dik |

        	āpastamboktaṃ tu śūdraviṣayam:


                            	pūrvayor varṇayor vedādhyāyinaṃ hatvā savanagataṃ vābhiśastaḥ | brāhmaṇamātraṃ ca | garbhaṃ ca tasyāvijñātam | ātreyīṃ ca striyam | tasya nirveśaḥ | araṇye kuṭiṃ kṛtvā vāgyataḥ śavaśirodhvajo 'rdhaśāṇīpakṣam adhonābhy upari jānvor ācchādya | tasya panthā antarā vartmanī | dṛṣṭvāryam atikrāmet | khaṇḍena lohitena śarāveṇa grāmaṃ pratiṣṭheta | tato 'bhiśastāya bhikṣām iti karmācakṣāṇaḥ saptāgārāṇi caret | sā vṛttiḥ | alabdhopavāsaḥ | gāś ca rakṣet | tāsāṃ niṣkramaṇapraveśane dvitīyo grāme 'rthaḥ | dvādaśa varṣāṇi caritvā siddhaḥ sadbhiḥ saṃprayogaḥ | ājīpathe vā brāhmaṇagavyupajigīṣamāṇas triḥ pratirāddho 'vajitya vā muktaḥ | āśvamedhikaṃ vāvabhṛtham upetya mucyate | dharmārthasaṃnipāte arthagrāhiṇa etad eva | iti | (ĀpDh 1.24.6–23)

atra ca pūrvayor varṇayor iti śūdrāpekṣayā kṣatriyavaiśyāv uktau, brāhmaṇamātraṃ ceti vacanād na brāhmaṇakṣatriyau pūrvavarṇāv iti ghaṭate | tenaitac chūdrasyeti draṣṭavyam | na cātra japahomādi kiṃcic chrutam, yena traivarṇikaviṣayatvam āśaṅkyeta | anenaivānyatrāpi jātikṛtā guṇakṛtā ca vyavasthā vyākhyeyā | dvādaśasu ca smṛtiṣu dvādaśa vāriṣikāṇi paṭhyante | tāny evaṃ vivektavyāni | tatra mānavaṃ yājñavalkīyaṃ ca sarvavarṇānām | tatra ca brāhmaṇasya kāmakṛte guṇavadbrāhmaṇavadhe, kṣatriyavaiśyayor akāmakṛte nirguṇavadhe, śūdrasya tv akamakṛte brāhmaṇamātravadhe, evaṃ vaiśyasyāpi kṣatriyāpekṣayā sarvatra ca gurutaraṃ prāyaścittaṃ prayojyam || 243 ||

 

_brahmahatyāyām evedam anyat prāyaścittam |_

 

**              	lomabhyaḥ svāheti hi vā lomaprabhṛti vai tanum |**

**              	majjāntaṃ juhuyād vāpi mantrair ebhir yathākramam || 3.244 ||**

 

hiśabdavaiśabdau pādapūraṇārthau | vāśabdaś cājyāpekṣayā lomādidravyavikalpārthaḥ | tanuḥ śarīram | tad lomaprabhṛti lomāni tvacaṃ ca lohitaṃ medo māṃsaṃ snāyv asthi majjānam ity evamantam | lomabhyaḥ svāhety etair yajurvedapaṭhitair āśvamedhikair dvirabhyastair mantrair juhuyāt | ājyaṃ vā dvirabhyastaiḥ pratyekaṃ ṣoḍaśabhir juhuyāt | vāpīty ayaṃ tu dvitīyo vāśabdaḥ pūrṇaprāyaścittāpekṣayā vikalpārthaḥ | sa naikakartrapekṣayā | brahmahatyāyām ekasyām eva yathādhikāraṃ kartṛbhir dvādaśavārṣikam idaṃ vā kartavyam ity arthaḥ | tataś caitat sāmarthyād adhītavedasyāgnimataś ca syāt | lomaprabhṛtīnāṃ cātra caturthyā māntravarṇikaṃ devatātvam | tataś ca ya eva lomatvagādīnām adhyātmādhidaivādhiyajñavit, tasyaivādhikāraḥ | tadadhigamaviśeṣāpekṣayā ca dravyavikalpavyavasthā vyākhyeyā | na cātra śarīradāhaḥ, vacanābhāvāt | lomādīnāṃ kārtsnyena hotum aśakyatvād avaśyam ekasmād evāṅgulyāder avayavād dhotavyāḥ | tena naitan maraṇāntikam iti vyākhyeyam | vāsiṣṭhe 'py evam eva: "bhrūṇahāgnim upasamādhāya juhuyāt, 'lomāni mṛtyor juhomi, lomabhir mṛtyuṃ vāsaye prathamām" ity ārabhya, "majjānaṃ mṛtyoḥ" ityevamantam (VaDh 20.25–26) | tatrāpi homamātram eva, śarīraprakṣepasyānupadeśāt | ye tv alpatvāt prāyaścittasya, smṛtyantare ca,

                    	prāsyed ātmānam agnau vā samiddhe trir avākśirāḥ | (MDh 11.73)

iti śarīratyāgadarśanād, atrāpi śarīratyāgaṃ varṇayanti, te saṃhitādhyayane kim ity ā maraṇād āvṛttir na kurvanti: "triḥ saṃhitām adhītyāto niyataṃ bhuktvā punas triḥ" iti | evaṃ sarveṣāṃ jīvaprāyaścittānām alpatvād yathāsaṃbhavaṃ maraṇāntikaiḥ saha tulyatāsiddhyarthaṃ kalpanā prasajyeta | atha kathaṃcit teṣu viṣayakalpanā, tato 'trāpi tad eva yuktam, na tv aśruta evāgnau śarīraprakṣepaḥ | ataś ca vāsiṣṭhe 'pi homa eveti sthitam | yad api "bhrūṇahāgnim upasamādhāya juhuyāt" (VaDh 20.25) iti homavacanād eva prāptasyāgneḥ punarvacanam, tad api na laukikāgniprāptyartham, adṛṣṭakalpanāprasaṅgāt | bhrūṇahatayā (??) vā kasyacin mandabuddheḥ saṃskṛtāgnivināśāśaṅkā mā bhūd ity evaṃ vyākhyeyam, na tu vacanaprāptasyāgneḥ saṃskṛtasya jñāpakamātreṇa tyāgakalpanety eṣā dik | spaṣṭataraṃ tu viṣayakalpanāṃ prāyaścittaprakaraṇasyānte vakṣyāmaḥ || 244 ||

 

_tathedam anyad vaikalpikam |_

 

**              	brāhmaṇasya paritrāṇād gavāṃ dvādaśakasya vā |**

**              	tathāśvamedhāvabhṛtasnānād vā śuddhim āpnuyāt || 3.245 ||**

 

brāhmaṇagrahaṇaṃ cātra guṇavati draṣṭavyaṃ na jātimātre, samāsākaraṇāt | samāse hi liṅgānabhivyakter jātimātrapratipattiḥ syāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evam api puṃsa ity eva labhyate, na tu guṇavata ity api | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam evam</span> | kiṃ tv evaṃ sati strītvanivṛttyarthatvāt parisaṃkhyā syāt | liṅgavac caikatvasyāpi vivakṣitatvād brāhmaṇadvayaparitrāṇe vaiguṇyaṃ prasajyeta | athātantraṃ liṅgaṃ tatsahacaritādhyayanādiguṇaprāptyarthaṃ bhavet | tato na kaścid doṣaḥ | tena guṇavato brāhmaṇasya paritrāṇād ity eva yuktam | pariśabdāc ca sarvataḥ svaprāṇaparityāgenāpīty arthaḥ | gavāṃ dvādaśakasya vety atrāpi guṇavato brāhmaṇasya svabhūtānām ity adhikārāl labyate | tathāśabdaḥ prakārārthaḥ | yathā "śiraḥkapālī" ityādinā śuddhim avāpnuyāt, tathā gobrāhmaṇaparitrāṇād apy anyānapekṣād evety arthaḥ | tathā ca manunā:

                    	kṛtavāpano vā nivased grāmānte govraje 'pi vā |

                    	āśrame vṛkṣamūle vā gobrāhmaṇahite rataḥ || (MDh 11.78)

ity uktvoktam:

                    	brāhmaṇārthe gavārthe vā sadyaḥ prāṇān parityajan |

                    	mucyate brahmahatyāyā goptā gobrāhmaṇasya ca || iti | (MDh 11.79)

tena jñāyate prāyaścittāntaram idaṃ na tu prakrāntadvādaśavārṣikasya | tadviṣayatvena "gobrāhmaṇahite rataḥ" ity anenaiva siddhatvāc chlokāntarārambo niṣprayojanaḥ syāt | na cānena prakāreṇa hite rataḥ syād ityevamarthaḥ ślokāntarārambha iti yuktam, vāśabdavaiyarthyāt, "goptā gobrāhmaṇasya vā" iti ca punarabhidhānāt | ataḥ svatantram evedaṃ prāyaścittāntaraṃ bhagavato 'bhipretam | ata eva ca niḥsaṃdighenāśvamedhāvabhṛthasnānenāsya vaikalpikatvam ācāryeṇoktam:

                    	tathāśvamedhāvabhṛtahsnānād vā śuddhim āpnuyāt | iti |

yathā cāśvamedhāvabhṛthasyānyatrānupraveśo na saṃbhavati, tathā pradarśitam eva | śaṅkhotasya ca "antarā vā brāhmaṇān maraṇān mokṣayitvā" iti tad uktadvādaśavārṣikaviṣayaṃ na sārvatrikam ity etad vyākhyatam eva || 245 ||

 

_tathedam anyat vaikalpikam |_

 

                    	**dīrghatīvrāmayagrastaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ gām athāpi vā |**

**              	dṛṣṭvā pathi nirātaṅkaṃ kṛtvā vā brahmahā śuciḥ || 3.246 ||**
