āmayo rogaḥ | tena dīrgheṇa cirakālaprarūḍhatayātyarthaṃ kṛcchrasādhyena tīvreṇa ca rājayakṣmamahākuṣṭhādinā grastam ekāntato bhuktam | brāhmaṇam ity atrāpi puṃlliṅganirdeśo 'dhyayanādiguṇapratipattyartha eva, na strītvanivṛttyarthaḥ | athaśabdasyotkṛṣya vāśabdena saha yojanā: atha voktaviśeṣaṇāṃ gām apīti | apiśabdaś caikasaṃkhyāpekṣayā saṃbhāvanārthaḥ: brāhmaṇajātīyaṃ nirguṇam api, tathaikam api, kim uta guṇavanto bhūyāṃso vety abhiprāyaḥ | pathi dṛṣṭvety abhisaṃdhinivṛttyartham | nirātaṅkaṃ niḥśeṣarogacchedān nirbhayaṃ vyapagatākūtaṃ svasthaṃ kṛtvā | vāśabdād ā maraṇād vā sarvātmanā sarvasvenāpi svaprāṇoparodhenāpi śuśrūṣitvā | brahmahā śuciḥ syād iti prakṛtatve 'pi brahmahā śucir iti punar vacanaṃ sarvādhikārapratipattyartham, sarvatrāmatipūrve kāmakṛte ca traivarṇikānām idaṃ paricaryamāṇabrāhmaṇaguṇāpekṣayā bhūyastvāpekṣayā paricārakaśaktigunāpekṣayā ca yojyam | śūdrasyāpy amatipūrva etad bhavaty eva paritrāṇaṃ tadātvaviṣayam | yathā pradīpte veśmany antar brāhmaṇaṃ godvādaśakaṃ vā niḥsaraṇāsamarthaṃ svamaraṇam aṅgīkṛtya praviśyātivāhayed yaḥ, sa tatparitrāṇād maraṇād vā śudhyatīti | atra tu ā nirātaṅkabhāvād ā maraṇād vā paricaryeti punarārambhaḥ || 246 ||

 

_tathedam anyad vaikalpikaṃ brahmahatyāyām eva |_

 

                    	**ānīya viprasarvasvaṃ hṛtaṃ ghātita eva vā |**

**              	tannimittaṃ kṣataḥ śastrair jīvann api viśudhyati || 3.247 ||**

 

sarvasvavacanaṃ bahutvopalakṣaṇārtham, bhūyaso hy apahṛtasya pratyānayanaṃ duṣkaraṃ yataḥ | sarvasvaṃ tu kadācit ghaṭamātram api bhavati | tac cālpenāpi prayāsena śakyam āhartum | tatra ghātitavacanaṃ nātīva samañjasaṃ syāt | ghātita eveti caivakāreṇa yatra hṛtapratyāharaṇe maraṇam evaucityāt prāpnoti tat sarvasvam iti spaṣṭayati | tataś ca tadāharaṇanimittaṃ yathāśaktyāghātito 'pi punaḥ punar utthāya vyāyacchann anekaśaḥ śastraiḥ kṣato yadi jīvati, tathāpy anāhṛte 'pi dravye viśudhyaty eva | etac cākṣatriyasyāharaṇasaṃbhāvanāyuktasya ca prāyaścittam | kṣatriyasya tv etan nityatvād anupadeśyam eva | yasyāpy udāharaṇasaṃbhāvanāsti, tasyāpy ānīyety etan nātīva samañjasam | tena saṃbhāvitasyākṣatriyasya ceti sthitam | śastragrahaṇaṃ ca pratipakṣasya durjayatvaṃ pradarśayitum | tenāśastrair api pāṣāṇādibhir niśceṣṭīkṛtaḥ kṣatam antareṇāpi śudhyatīty avaseyam || 247 ||

 

_tathedam aparaṃ prāyaścittadvayam |_

 

                    	**araṇye niyato japtvā triṣkṛtvo vedasaṃhitāṃ |**

**              	śudhyeta vā mitāśītvā pratisrotaḥ sarasvatīm || 3.248 ||**

 

grāmān niṣkramyāraṇye sthitvā nitarāṃ yataḥ tadarthānusaṃdhānaikaniṣṭhaḥ trirāvṛttyā vedasaṃhitāṃ, mantrabrāhmaṇam ity arthaḥ | saṃhitāgrahaṇaṃ cāramaṇathāneṣv evāramaṇaniyamārtham | padakramādīnāṃ tu puruṣakṛtatvād eva vyāvṛtter na tannivṛttyarthaṃ saṃhitāvacanam | trir ity etāvatā ca siddhe triṣkṛtva ity uktaṃ kṛtvasujviṣayāvṛttisiddhyartham[^15] (?) | tena pañcakṛtvaḥ ṣaṭkṛtvaḥ ity evamādy apy atrānubandhaguṇāpakṣayā yojyam | mānave 'pi |

                    	japed vā niyatāhāras trir vai vedasya saṃhitām | iti | (MDh 11.77)

vedasya trir iti saṃbandhād ekasya trir japtvā tato vedāntarasya trir ity evaṃ yojyam, asmād eva kṛtvasucprayogāt | vaiśabdena ca prasiddhārthadyotakenaitad eva dyotitam: smṛtyantarasaṃpradāyāpekṣaḥ ślokārtho grāhya iti | etac ca vidvadviṣayatvād vedārthajñasyaiva prāyaścittaṃ tadviśeṣāpekṣayā yojyam | anye tv araṇya eva yo niyataḥ sa japtvā triṣkṛtvo vedasaṃhitāṃ śudhyatīty evaṃ vanasthasyaivaitad iti vyācakṣate | tat tv araṇyasya mānave 'nupadeśād aviśeṣābhidhāne 'pi ca tatsiddher nāvaśyam aṅgīkartavyam | "śudhyeta vā mitāśītvā": mitāśī ca yathāśramocitam "aṣṭau grāsā muner bhaktam" (ĀpDh 2.9.13) ityevamādi, na pathi śrānto 'pi gotṛptyā vartetety arthaḥ | mitāśī itvā gatvety arthaḥ | śroto 'bhimukhaḥ someśvarād ārabhyāplakṣam | mānave tu "haviṣyabhug vā" (MDh 11.77) ity uktam | tac ca yatibrahmacāriṇor yathoktalakṣaṇaṃ bhaikṣam eva | itarayos tu svadharmānusāreṇaupāsanaśrāmaṇakāgnisaṃskṛtavrīhiyavaśyāmākanīvārādi pratyetavyam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca patitasyāśramavyavasthā naivāsti, patitatvād eva, "dvijātikarmabhyo hāniḥ patanam" (GDh 21.4) iti gautamavacanāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam evam</span>, prāk prāyaścittapravṛtteḥ | prāyaścittapravṛttau tu yathāvarṇaṃ yathāśramaṃ ca prāyaścittāvirodhena vartitavyam | yadi tu patitatvenāśramavyavasthāpagamaḥ syāt, tataḥ patitasyāhavanīyādyagnivināśād agniṣṭudādicodanā duḥśliṣṭā eva syuḥ | tena saty api patane gṛhasthatvasyānapagamād agīnām avināśaḥ | ataś cānyatarapatane sūtakādāv ivānyatareṇāgnayo dhāryāḥ | śuddhyanantarakāle ca karmapravṛttiḥ | ubhayapatane tv aparityajyaivāgnīṃs tatpālanam ubhābhyāṃ kartavyam | prāyaścittaṃ ca tatsaṃbandhāparityāgena japahomādilakṣaṇaṃ pratyetavyam | tena sarasvatīprāyaścittam api haviṣyabhojananiyamād yathāśramaṃ svadharmānusāreṇa vyākhyeyam | anagnikasya tu snātakasyāpi bhikṣāhāratvam "bhaikṣāhāro vā sarasvatīṃ pratisrotasam" iti hārītavacanād, ity eṣā dik || 248 ||

 

_tad etad aparaṃ kṣatriyasyaiva prāyaścittam |_

 

**              	saṃgrāme vā hato lakṣabhūtaḥ śuddhim avāpnuyāt |**

 

kiṃ maraṇāntikam evedaṃ prāyaścittam, pravṛttis tāvat kṛtamaraṇaniścayasyaiva |

 

_tathā pravṛttas tu saḥ |_

 

                    	**mṛtakalpaḥ prahārārto jīvann api na śudhyati || 3.249 ||**

 

saṃgrāmavacanaṃ kṣatriyādhikārapratipattyartham | lakṣabhūta ātmano rakṣām akurvan saṃnahanādirahitaḥ parakīyaśastrāṇy akavacayan sāṃgrāmikavidhinā rājārthe gavārthe brāhmaṇārthe vābhimukho ghātitaḥ | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ: "rājārthe brāhmaṇārthe gavārthe vā saṃgrāme 'bhimukha ātmānaṃ ghātayet" iti (VaDh 20.27) | asvāmī ca rājā pratyetavyaḥ | śuddhim āpnuyād iti saṃśayavyudāsārtho liṅprayogaḥ | tathā cāha manuḥ |

                    	lakṣaṃ śastrabhṛtāṃ vā syād viduṣām icchayātmanaḥ | (MDh 11.73)

viduṣāṃ śastravidāṃ saṃgrāmanipuṇānām | ātmana icchayā na svāmyādeḥ | śaravedhyakam ivātmānam agopāyan yuddhābhimukho bhavet | nātra saṃśayaḥ kārya ity atrāpi saṃśayavyāvṛttyartha eva liṅprayogaḥ |

                    	prāsyed ātmānam agnau vā samiddhe trir avākśirāḥ | (MDh 11.73)

ity etad api brāhmaṇavyatirekeṇaiva | steyādhikāre "brāhmaṇas tapasaiva ca" (MDh 11.100) iti brāhmaṇas tapasaiva pāpam apanayed, na maraṇāntikeneti | etac ca steyādhikāroktam api viśeṣavacanād ṛte sarvaviṣayaṃ draṣṭavyam | tathā cāpastambena "gurutalpagaḥ sūrmīṃ jvalantīṃ praviśyātmānaṃ dahet" ity upakramya, "mithyaitad iti hārīto yo hy ātmānaṃ paraṃ vābhihanyate 'bhiśasta eva saḥ" ity anena vidhinā "ottamād ucchvāsāc caret" (ĀpDh 1.28.16–18) ity abrāhmaṇābhiprāyeṇaiva darśitam | ācāryeṇa tv agnipraveśo noktaḥ, pratyakṣaśruticoditatvāt | evaṃ hi kāṭhake śrūyate: "anāśakena karśito 'gnim ārohet trir avākśirāḥ" iti | ata evāśvamedhasvarjidādīnām apy atrānupadeśaḥ | mānave tu śrautasmārtānām ekīkṛtyopanyāsaḥ samānārthatayaiva smārtānāṃ bādhāśaṅkānivṛttyarthaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">evaṃ tarhi</span> bādha eva smārtānāṃ yukta iti vyartho bhagavataḥ prayatnaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyaṃ</span>, yady ekaviṣayatā syāt | ata eva viṣayabhedena vyākhyātam | itarathā hi vāśabdād ekanimittasaṃbandhāc ca yadṛcchāvikalpa eva syāt | yan nāmāviśeṣeṇaiva prāpnoti, tatraiva kalpāntarānarthakyād viṣayavyavasthā | yathā darśitam: "yo 'śvamedhena yajate, ya u cainam evaṃ veda" iti (cf. Śab on PMS 1.2.4) | na hy anadhītyāśvamedhena yaṣṭuṃ kaścic chaknuyāt | ata eva, "arke cen madhu vindeta kim arthaṃ parvataṃ vrajet" iti, "tenaiva pathā madhvarthinaḥ parvataṃ gaccheyuḥ" iti ca śābare (Śab on PMS 1.2.4) darśitam | na cātrālpatvamahattve vidyete | kasyacid dhi kleśāsahiṣṇoḥ sāttvikasya dvādaśavārṣikāmaraṇam eva sukaram | anyasya tu kleśasahiṣṇoḥ sattvahīnasyetarat | evam udāratṛṣṇāparāpekṣayā maraṇasarvasvadānayos tulyatā | vidvanmūrkhayoś ca saṃhitādhyayanamaraṇadvādaśavārṣikādiṣv evam eva | na ca yasyāviśiṣṭaṃ trayodaśasv api sāmarthyaṃ, tam evaikaṃ puruṣam aṅgīkṛtya mānava ārambhaḥ | tathā sati samaviklpa eva syāt | ato viṣayavyavasthayaiva śrautasmārtānāṃ parasparavyākhyānam upadeśabalenaivānusartavyaṃ na tv anyānarthakyena ity eṣā dik || 249 ||

 

_vittavatas traivarṇikasyedam anyat prāyaścittaṃ pūrvokavaikalpikatvena |_

 

                    	**pātre dhanaṃ vā paryāptaṃ dattvā śuddhiṃ nigacchati |**

**              	ādātuś ca viśuddhyartham iṣṭir vaiśvānarī smṛtā || 3.250 ||**

 

pātre vidyāvṛttatapaḥsaṃpannāya svājanyavidviṣṭābhisaṃdhirahitaṃ dhanaṃ gobhūtilahiraṇyādi paryāptaṃ tadīyebhyo nityatayā prāptebhyaḥ śrautasmārtakarmabhyo yad bhavati, tad dattvā śuddhiṃ nitarāṃ gacchati | sarvaprāyaścittānām idam evābhyarhitam ity abhiprāyaḥ | mānave tu dānaprakārāpekṣaḥ prapañco na deyaviśeṣāpekṣaḥ | deyaṃ tv etāvad eva | tatra kadācit sarvasvam etan mamety evaṃ niḥśeṣam arpayet | yadi tu nityānuṣṭhānasaṃpradānasaṃbandhi kārtsnyenālocyātiriktam api dātuḥ svaṃ syāt, tato yāvajjīvanasaṃbandhivihitaśrautasmārtānuṣṭhānāya yat paryāptaṃ, tāvad eva dadyāt | kadācit tāvanmātreṇa dravyeṇa pūrayitvā saparicchadaṃ gṛhaṃ vā dadyād iti | atra dātur icchāvikalpaḥ, na dravyaparimāṇe kaścid bhedaḥ | etac ca kāmakṛte guṇavadbrāhmaṇavadhe draṣṭavyaṃ, pātre dātavyam iti vacanāt | na hy alpena prayāsenaivaṃbhūto brāhmaṇaḥ śakyo grāhayitum | yo hi samyag granthato 'rthataś cānupūrvyeṇa nyāyānusārataś ca vedaṃ kārtsnyena vetti, prāyaścittopadeśāt sāgniḥ svakarmānuṣṭhānanirataḥ sa katham iva pratigṛhṇīyāt | kiṃ vā tādṛśe pātre etāvad dravyaṃ dattvā pāpān nāpagacchet | ato gurutara eva prāyaścittaṃ yuktam | tac ca darśitam | tasya cādātuḥ pratigṛhṇānasya viśuddhyarthaṃ vaiśvānaro dvādaśakapālaḥ puroḍāśaḥ | caśabdād dātuś cāhitāgner eva mahādhanasya tāvanmātradhanasyaiveti sthitam | śrautatve 'pi ceṣṭer "iṣṭir vaiśvānarī smṛtā" iti smṛtatvavacanaṃ mānave 'nuktatvād apasmṛtitvāśaṅkānivṛttyartham | saty api tatrāvacane manunaivāyam artha smṛta ity avagantavyam ity abhiprāyaḥ | tatrāsyānabhidhānaṃ dātur aniyamo yathā syād ity evamartham | tenānāhitāgner api sarvasvaṃ vā vedavida ity etat prāyaścittam asty evety eṣā dik |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> caitāni prakrāntadvādaśavārṣikasyaivāśaktau parisamāptyarthānīti yuktam | tathā ca manunā: "brahmahā dvādaśābdaṇi" ity upakramya, "lakṣaṃ śastrabhṛtāṃ vā syāt" ityādi "japed vā niyatāhāraḥ" ity evamantam uktvā (MDh 11.72–77), punar dvādaśavārṣikasaṃbandhitayaivoktam:

                    	kṛtavāpano vā nivased grāmānte govraje 'pi vā |

                    	āśrame vṛkṣamūle vā gobrāhmaṇahite rataḥ ||

                    	brāhmaṇārthe gavārthe vā sadyaḥ prāṇān parityajan |

                    	mucyate brahmahatyāyā goptā gobrāhmaṇasya vā ||

                    	tryavaraṃ pratirāddho vā sarvasvam avajitya vā |

                    	viprasya tannimitte vā prāṇālābhe vimucyate || (MDh 11.78–80)

ity evaṃ brāhmaṇārthaprāṇatyāgādinā dvādaśavārṣikasya parisamāptim uktvopasaṃhṛtam:

                    	evaṃ dṛḍhavrato nityaṃ brahmacārī samāhitaḥ |

                    	samāpte dvādaśe varṣe brahmahatyāṃ vyapohati || iti | (MDh 11.81)

evam upakramopasaṃhārābhyām ekam evedaṃ prāyaścittaṃ sopaskaram avagamyate | tathā cottaratra:

                    	hatvā garbham avijñātam etad eva vrataṃ caret | iti | (MDh 11.87)

etad eva prakṛtaṃ dvādaśavārṣikam iti sāmañjasyaṃ syād, itarathā caitad eveti na jñāyate kasyāyaṃ nirdeśa iti | ānantaryād vāśvamedhāvabhṛthasyaiva syāt | tatra tasyāsaṃbavaḥ kādācitkatvāt prāyaścittasya ca nityatvenāpekṣitatvāt | ataḥ pūrvaparisamāptāv eva viṣayavyavasthayā "lakṣaṃ śastrabhṛtām" (MDh 11.73) ityādīni draṣṭavyāni, na svātantryeṇa | na ca maraṇāntikaṃ prāyaścittaṃ yuktam, kāryavirodhāt | śuddhyarthaṃ hi tad iṣyate, jīvataś ca śudddhyā kāryaṃ yataḥ | na ca jīvaprāyaścittasyetareṇa vikalpo ghaṭate, vaiṣamyāt | svecchayā cetarasaṃbhave maraṇāntikam adhyavasyata ātmaghātadoṣo 'pi prasajyeta | ata evāpastambena: "gurutalpagaḥ sūrmīṃ jvalantīṃ praviśyātmānaṃ dahet" ity upakramya, "mithyaitad iti hārītaḥ" iti, "yo hy ātmānaṃ paraṃ vābhihanyate abhiśasta eva saḥ" iti (ĀpDh 1.28.15–17) | ato 'pi maraṇāntikam ayuktam | yatra ca savanasthavipravadhādau dviguṇaṃ vratam ucyate, tatra dvir maraṇāsaṃbhavāt tadanupapattir eva syāt | ata ekaprāyaścittakalpanaiva yukteti | na tv idam atīva nyāyyam | yat tāvad upakramopasaṃhārabalam ālocyaikatvam uktam, tac chrautair āśvamedhādibhir vyavadhānād ayuktam eva | na hi dvādaśasaṃvatsaroddeśenāśvamedhasvarjidādivacanāny avakalpante | avaśyaṃ hy eṣāṃ pratyakṣaśrutimūlatvaṃ vācyam | smṛtau caitāni tu | kramānupapattes tatra ca dvādaśavārṣikaṃ brahmahatyoddeśena prakṛtya ya etat samāpayituṃ na śaknuyāt, sa etenāśvamedhādinā yajetety evaṃ kratavo vidhātavyāḥ, phalādyarthatayā vā kratūn prakṛtya dvādaśavārṣikāśaktāv api yajetety evam | ubhayathāpi cāyuktam, dampatyor adhikārāt, kevalasya ca pravṛttatvāt | na ca bhartur aśaktyā patny api pravartatām iti yuktam, patnīśabdasya svāmivacanatvād aṅgini dvādaśavārṣike tasyā anadhikārāt | tatra yadi vā saha patane dvādaśavārṣikam, yadi vā kratūnāṃ tatrānanupraveśaḥ, vidhānād dvādaśavārṣikasya jayāhomeneva kṛṣyādīnām āhavanīyādisaṃyuktaiḥ karmabhir saṃbandhāt tādarthyakalpanānupapattiḥ | ato 'vaśyaṃ kratūnāṃ svātantryam eva vaktavyam | tathā cāmnāya: "sarvāṃ brahmahatyām apahanti, yo 'śvamedhena yajate | agniṣṭutābhiśasyamānaṃ yājayet | bhrūṇahatyāyā vā eṣo 'timucyate, yo 'bhijitā yajeta" iti (cf. ŚB 13.5.4.1; GDh 19.10) | etāni ca pratyakṣāṇy atikramya nānupalabdhavākyāntarakalpanāyāṃ pramāṇam asti | ato 'śvamedhādicodanās tāvat pūrvaprakramānapekṣā eva | tābhir vyavahitāḥ sarvasvadānādayas tadvyavahitena dvādaśābdena na saṃbandhaṃ labhante | smṛtyantareṣu tu "agnau saktir brahmaghnas trir avacchātasya, lakṣaṃ vā syāj janye śastrabhṛtāṃ, khaṭvaṅgakapālapāṇir vā" (GDh 22.2–4) iti ca prakramālocanayā maraṇāśaktāv eva dvādaśavārṣikaṃ lakṣyate | vāsiṣṭhe 'pi: "brahmahāgnim upasamādhāya" iti prakṛtya, "rājārthe brāhmaṇārthe vābhimukha ātmānaṃ ghātayet trirañjito[^16] vā pratirāddhaḥ pūto bhavatīti vijñāyate" ity uktvoktaṃ dvādaśavārṣikam: "dvādaśavarṣāṇy ātmanā vratam ādiśya na grāme nāraṇye vaset khaṭvāṅgakapālapāṇiḥ" iti (VaDh 20.25–28) | atrāpi ca prakramānusārāt pūrvānadhikṛtasyaiva dvādaśābdikam ity avagamyate | anyāsu tu dvādaśābdikasyānupadeśa eva | vāsiṣṭhe ca "vijñāyate" iti, tryavaraṃ "pratirāddhaḥ" ity asya pratyakṣaśrutivihitatvena dvādaśābdānanupraveśaḥ spaṣṭīkṛta eva | ataḥ svātantryeṇaiva viṣayavyavasthayā sarvāṇi vyākhyeyāni vyākhyātāni ca | yas tūpasaṃhāraḥ, sa pūrvoktāpekṣayā yojyo na tu tadpakṣeyā pūrvoktam | uktasya hy upasaṃhāraḥ, nopasaṃhārād uktatā | tena "kṛtavāpano vā nivaset" (MDh 11.78) ityevamādeḥ pūrvoktasamastaprāyaścittaśeṣatvam | sarvatra cāyam aviruddha eva niyamakalāpaḥ | pratyuta dvādaśābdika eva "araṇye kuṭiṃ kṛtvā" (ĀpDh 1.24 11) ity anena virodhād asyānanupraveśaḥ | na ca vikalpaḥ saṃbhavati, tatkalpanāyāṃ dvādaśābdānanupraveśo 'yuktaḥ | yau tv anantarau ślokau, tābhyāṃ prāyaścittāntaratvena gobrāhmaṇārthe prāṇatyāgādīny upadiśyante na tu prakrāntadvādaśābdikasya, pramāṇābhāvād, vāsiṣṭhe ca "trirañjito vā" ity atra "vijñāyate" ity anena śrautatvasya darśitatvāt | yas tāvad upasaṃhāraḥ "evaṃ dṛḍhavrato nityam" (MDh 11.81) iti, ayam api sarvaśeṣa eva | evam uktena prakāreṇāmunā prāyaścittena mayātmanā niyamena śodhanīya ity evaṃrūpaṃ dvādaśābdaśastrabhṛllakṣabhāvāgnipraveśakratvanuṣṭhānādi yad vratam, tatra dvādaśābdādau samāpte vrate brahmahatyāṃ vyapohatīty evaṃ yojyaḥ | tathā ca paramopasaṃhāraḥ samañjaso bhavati:

                    	ato 'nyatamam āsthāya vidhiṃ vipraḥ suyantritaḥ |

                    	brahmahatyākṛtaṃ pāpaṃ vyapohetātmavattayā || iti | (MDh 11.86)

anyathaikatvād "anyatamam āsthāya" ity asaṃbaddham eva syāt | na cānyatamam agnipraśādikaṃ dvādaśābdasamāptividhim āsthāyeti yuktam, tathā sati guṇatvāt prādhānyena nirdeśo na syāt | na ca tatsamāptyarthatā saṃbhavatīty uktam eva | yad apy anantaram:

                    	hatvā garbham avijñātam etad eva vrataṃ caret | (MDh 11.87)

iti, atrānantaryād eva "anyatamam āsthāya vidhiṃ" (MDh 11.86), "brahmahatyāvrataṃ caret" (YDh 3.254) ityādi yojyaṃ na tu dvādaśavārṣikam, vyavadhānena sarvanāmaparāmarśāsaṃbhavāt |

                    	turīyo brahmahatyāyāḥ kṣatriyasya vadhe smṛtaḥ |

                    	vaiśye 'ṣṭamo 'ṃśo vṛttasthe śūdre jñeyas tu ṣoṣaśaḥ ||

                    	akāmatas tu rājanyaṃ vinipātya dvijottamaḥ |

                    	ṛṣabhaikasahasrā gā dadyāc chuddyartham ātmanaḥ ||

ity uktvoktam:

                    	tryabdaṃ cared vā niyato jaṭilo brahmahavratam |

                    	vasan dūratare grāmād vṛkṣamūlaniketanaḥ || iti | (MDh 11.126–28)

tac ca turīyavacanād eva siddhe saty asaṃbaddhaṃ syāt | yadi turīyavacanāt sarvasvacaturthabhāgadānam api prāpnoti, tato mahādhanasyākāmakṛte gosahasradānopedeśaḥ, traivārṣikaṃ vā vratam ādiśyeta | itarathā hi pūrvaślokāt kāmakṛte 'pi traivārṣikasyāpi prāptatvād akāmakṛte tadvacanam asamañjasaṃ syāt | ato yathoktaiva vyākhyā yuktā | yat tu kāryavirodhān maraṇāntikam ayuktam iti, tad api "bhaikṣaṃ cātmaviśuddhyartham" (cf. MDh 11.73) ity ātmaviśuddhyarthaṃ prāyaścittaṃ na śarīraśuddhyartham | ātmadravyam eva prāyaścittena saṃskriyate | tac ca maraṇāntike itaratra cāviśiṣṭam | yat tu vaiṣamyād vikalpo maraṇāntikasyetareṇāyukta iti, tat puruṣāṇāṃ buddhivaicitryād akāraṇam evety uktam | yat tu svecchayā prāyaścittāntare saṃbhavati maraṇam adhyavasyata ātmaghātakatvaprasaṅga iti, tat paśvekādaśinyām apy ekena paśunā saha vikalpenopadiṣṭāyām anekaprāṇivadhe doṣotpattiḥ prasajyeta | surāyāś cāgnivarṇair udakagomūtrādibhiḥ saha vaikalpikatve svecchayopādāne doṣaḥ syāt | dvādaśābdasamāptyarthatve 'pi cāyaṃ tulyo doṣaḥ | viṣayavibhāgakalpanā cobhayatra tulyaiva | āpastambavacanaṃ tu brāhmaṇasya maraṇāntikanivṛttyarthaṃ prakārāntareṇa vā maraṇāntasyopadeśārtham "ottamād ucchvāsāt" iti (ĀpDh 1.24.24) | anyathā maraṇāntasyopadeśānām aprāmāṇyam eva syāt | gurutalpāvasare ca nipuṇataraṃ vakṣyāmaḥ | yat tu dviguṇaṃ vratam iti dvirmaraṇānupapattiḥ, tatra sāmarthyāj jīvaprāyaścittānāṃ prayogāvṛttikalpanā na tu dvādaśābdikamātrasaṃbandhitā ity alaṃ prasaṅgena || 250 ||

 

_idānīm ātideśikāny āha |_

 

**              	yāgasthakṣatriyaviḍghāte cared brahmahaṇo vratam |**

**              	garbhahā ca yathāvarṇaṃ tathāreyīniṣūdakaḥ || 3.251 ||**

 

yāgavacanaṃ prayogamadhya eva doṣa ity evamartham | yāgaśabdaś cāyaṃ somayāga eva draṣṭavyaḥ, "savanagatau ca rājanyavaiśyau" (VaDh 20.34) iti smṛtyantarāt | tathā cāmnāyaḥ: "tasmād āhur na savanagataṃ hanyād enasvī haiva savanakṛteti" (ŚB 3.2.1.40) jyotiṣṭomaprakaraṇe caitad dīkṣito 'yaṃ brāhmaṇa ity āvedanaśeṣatvena | ataś cāvedanottarakālaṃ doṣa iti kecit | ṛtvigvaraṇaprabhṛty eva tu yuktam, savanagata ity atra bhūtārthasyāvivakṣitatvāt, kratupravṛttir eva vivakṣyate yataḥ | itarathā tu nirvṛttayāgasyaiva syāt | yat tu "āvedanena hi brāhmaṇo jāyate, yo yajñāj jāyate" iti, arthavādamātraṃ tat | mānave tu "rājanyavaiśyau cejānau" (MDh 11.87) iti kartṛtvamātravivakṣayaiva, na kṛtayāgatvavivakṣayety evaṃ yojyam | atha vā savanakṛcchruter ījānāv iti manuvacanād iṣṭavator eva doṣaḥ | iha sthavacanāc ca prayogamadhye 'pīti vyākhyeyam | "brahmahaṇo vratam" (MDh 11.101) ca dvādaśābdikādiparyāptadhanadānāntaṃ pūrvavad viṣayavyavasthayā yojyam | garbhahantā ca yad yasya varṇasya vadhe prāyaścittam, tad eva tadīyagarbhavadhe kuryāt | tathātreyīṃ[^17] hatvā tadvarṇavihitaṃ kuryāt | ātreyī ca rajodarśanād ārabhyāṣoḍaśāny ahāny ucyante | tasyāś ca saṃnihite bhartari prāk saṃprayogād etad draṣṭavyam, vāsiṣṭhe "atra hy eṣyad apatyaṃ bhavati" (VaDh 20.36) iti śrutyupanyāsāt | anye tu "tathātreyīniṣūdakaḥ" ity atra "cared brahmahaṇo vratam" (MDh 11.101) ity etad yojayanti, na tv anantaraṃ yathāvarṇam iti, ātreyīṃ cātrigorāṃ varṇayanti | tad api yuktam eva | tathā cāmnāyaḥ: "tato 'triḥ saṃbabhūva" ity uktvā, "tasmād apy ātreyyā yoṣitainasvinam āhuḥ" (ŚB 1.4.5.13) | tenobhe samyag vyākhyāte[^18] eva | spaṣṭam anyat || 251 ||

 

_idaṃ cānyad ātideśikam eva |_

 

                    	**cared vratam ahatvāpi ghātārthaṃ cet samāgataḥ |**

**              	dviguṇaṃ savanasthe tu brāhmaṇe vratam ācaret || 3.252 ||**

 

avaśyam asmābhir asau brāhmaṇo hantavyaḥ ity evaṃ ghātārthaṃ bahūnāṃ samāgatānāṃ niṣpanne ca brāhmaṇavadhe yenāpy asau na ghātitaḥ, so 'pi pūrvoktaviṣayavyavasthākalpitaṃ vrataṃ cared eva | prahṛte ca saty etad draṣṭavyam | aprahṛte tu:

                    	bahūnāṃ samavetānāṃ brāhmaṇādivadhaṃ prati |

                    	yasya prahārād vyāpattiḥ sa duṣyen netaras tathā ||

iti hārītopadeśāt | tathāśabdāc ca tadvat patito bhavati, na tu na duṣyatīty gamyate | savanasthe dviguṇam ity atrāpi na prāyaścittābhyāsaḥ | kiṃ tarhi, gurutaraṃ tatra prāyaścittam | tataś ca yathāpastambenoktam "etenaiva vidhinā ā uttamād ucchvāsāc caret" (ĀpDh 1.24.24) ityevamādi draṣṭavyam | prāyaścittadvayaṃ vā: "sarvasvaṃ dattvā dvādaśābdikaṃ vā kṛtvā tato maraṇāntikam" ityādinā prakāreṇa | itarathā tu dvir vratam ādiśed ity evāvakṣyad, na tu dviguṇam iti | savanasthe ca yajamāna evedaṃ nartvijīti | tatrāpi tu doṣātireko 'sty eva | prāyaścittaṃ tu tatra tadanurūpaṃ kalpyam | anye tu anyathemaṃ ślokaṃ varṇayanti:

                    	cared vratam ahatvāpi ghātārthaṃ cet samāgataḥ |

samyag buddhipūrvaṃ vadhaprayojanaṃ vastu kṛtveti yāvat | yena kṛtenātiśayena brāhmaṇasya svayam eva vadhe pravṛttir bhavati, tat krodhotpādanaṃ dravyaharaṇādi | yady api brāhmaṇo mriyatām ity anayā buddhyā na kṛtaṃ, tathāpi tasmin dravyāpaharaṇādau kāmataḥ kṛte yadi nimittāntarānapekṣiṇī brāhmaṇasya prāṇavipattiḥ syāt, tadā vrataṃ brahmahatyāsaṃbandhi yat, tad ahatvāpi cared iti | etad eva mānave 'py uktam:

                    	uktvā caivānṛtaṃ sākṣye pratirabhya guruṃ tathā |

                    	apahṛtya ca nikṣepaṃ kṛtvā ca strīsuhṛdvadham || iti | (MDh 11.88)

yatrānṛte sākṣye brāhmaṇasya svato 'nyato va prāṇavipattiḥ, tathāpi tathāvidham anṛtam uktvā tatprakāreṇaivābhiśāpādinā guruṃ pratirabhya prakopayitvā saṃyojya vā brahmahatyāvrataṃ cared eva | gurau cābrāhmaṇe 'py etad draṣṭavyam | nikṣepaṃ ca maraṇahetubhūtaṃ brāhmaṇasyāpahṛtya, striyaṃ vā brāhmaṇasya, maraṇahetubhūtām abrāhmaṇīm api hatvā, suhṛdaṃ cābrāhmaṇam apy evaṃbhūtaṃ hatvā, brahmahatyāvrataṃ kārtsnyena cared ity abhiprāyaḥ | tathāśabdaś cātra prakārārthaḥ | anyad apy evaṃprakāraṃ maraṇakāraṇaṃ brāhmaṇasyotpādyety evam arthaḥ | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "durbalahiṃsāyāṃ cāpi mocane śaktaś cet" (GDh 21.19) ity evamartham evāha | etac ca kṣatriyādiṣv api yojyam | savanasthe caitad eva dviguṇam ity eṣā dik || 252 ||

 

_idānīṃ surāṃ praty āha |_

 

                    	**surāmbughṛtagomūtrapayasām agnisaṃnibham |**

**              	surāpo 'nyatamaṃ pītvā maraṇāc chuddhim ṛcchati || 3.253 ||**

 

surāṃ pānīyaṃ gavyaṃ vā ghṛtaṃ payo vā gavyam agnisaṃnibhaṃ dahanakṣamaṃ pītvā tenaiva nirdagdhaḥ surāpo maraṇāc chuddiṃ gacchatīti ślokārthaḥ | atra ca paiṣṭyām eva surāśabda ity etad ity etad "brahmahā madyapaḥ stenaḥ" (YDh 3.228) ity atroktam eva | trayāṇāṃ ca varṇāṇāṃ matipūrve surāpāna evaitat prāyaścittam, brāhmaṇyāś ca | kṣatriyavaiśyayoṣitāṃ punar naitat prāyaścittam:

                    	surāṃ pītvā dvijo mohād agnivarṇāṃ surāṃ pibet | (MDh 11.90)

iti dvijasyaiva prāyaścittopadeśāt, strīṇāṃ cādvijatvāt | kathaṃ tarhi brāhmaṇyāḥ:

                    	patilokaṃ na sā yāti brāhmaṇī yā surāṃ pibet | (YDh 3.256)

iti, ārambhasāmarthyāt | gautame ca: "surāpasya brāhmaṇasyoṣṇām āsiñceyuḥ surām āsye mṛtaḥ śudhyet" (GDh 23.1) ity atra stryartham eva brāhmaṇagrahaṇaṃ kṛtam | anyathā tu dvijasyety evāvakṣyat | na ca kṣatriyavaiśyavyāvṛttyarthaṃ tad iti yuktam, mānave dvijavacanāt | nopasaṃhārārthaṃ, pratiṣedhaśloke trayāṇāṃ pṛthagupādānāt:

                    	surā vai malam annānāṃ pāpmā ca malam ucyate |

                    	tasmād brāhmaṇarājanyau vaiśyaś ca na surāṃ pibet || iti | (MDh 11.93)

tena gautamīye brāhmaṇasyeti prāyaścittasya brāhmaṇajātimātrasaṃbandhārtham | na ca puṃlliṅganirdeśāt puṃso brāhmaṇasyeti yuktam, upādānānarthakyaprasaṅgād ity uktam | ata eva mānave pṛthak pratiṣedhaślokārambhaḥ | anyathā tu brahmahatyāyām iva prāyaścittopadeśād eva siddher anarthakaḥ syāt | tenātra surāpa ity aviśeṣābhidhāne 'pi smṛtyantarānusārād evaṃ vyākhyeyam | gaulamādhvyos tu brāhmaṇasaṃbandhitayaiva pratiṣedhād dvijasaṃbandhitvāc ca prāyaścittasya nedaṃ prāyaścittam, surāsaṃbandhena copadeśāt "surāṃ pītvā dvijo mohāt" iti | itarayoś cāsurātvāt | ato gaulīmādhvyoḥ kāmataḥ pāne vāsiṣṭham: "madyapāne tv asurāyāḥ surāyāś cājñāne kṛcchrātikṛcchrau ghṛtaprāśaḥ punaḥ saṃskāraś ca" iti (VaDh 20.19) | evam anyāny api surāpānavākyāni yojyāni || 253 ||

 

_evaṃ kāmakṛte tv abhyāse maraṇāntikaṃ prāyaścittam uktam | adhunā kāmakṛta evānabhyāse prāyaścittam āha |_

 

                    	**vālavāsā jaṭī vāpi cared brahmahaṇavratm |**

**              	piṇyākaṃ vā kaṇān vāpi bhakṣayīta samāṃ niśi || 3.254 ||**

 

brahmahatyāvrataṃ samāṃ cared ity evaṃ yojyam | na ca prāyaścittadvayopadeśabhrāntiḥ kartavyā, mānavaikavākyatvāt:

                    	kaṇān vā bhakṣayed abdaṃ piṇyākaṃ vā sakṛn niśi |

                    	surāpānāpanuttyarthaṃ vālavāsā dhvajī jaṭī || iti | (MDh 11.92)

                    	surāṃ pītvā dvijo mohād agnivarṇāṃ surāṃ pibet | (MDh 11.90)

ity etasmāt prakṛte 'pi punaḥ surāpānāpanuttyartham iti sakṛtpānāyaiva bhagavatoktam | ataḥ kāmakṛta eva sakṛt surāpāne etad iti sthitam | śāṅkhe 'pi: "surāpo 'gnitaptam aspṛṣyam udakaṃ pibet sa tena nirdagdhakāyaḥ śuddhim āpnoti" iti kāmakṛtābhyastapānavivakṣayābhidhāya, tata āha: "atha vā vālacīravāsāḥ surāpaḥ khaṭvāṅgī gurutalpagaś ca brahmahatyāvratam eva careyātām, tau tāvatā kālena śuddhim āpnutaḥ" ity etad eva sāṃvatsarikam uktam, na tu dvādaśābdikam | tatra "tāvatā kālena" ity etad avaktavyam eva syāt | ato yat pūrvaṃ "patito hy ātmānam uddharet, saṃvatsaraṃ taptakṛcchram ācaret" (cf. on YDh 3.243) ityādi brahmahatyāvihitam, tad evācared ity abhiprāyaḥ | evaṃ manunā sahaikavākyatā sidhyati | anyathā tu tadvirodhāt praijñātārthavirodhaḥ syāt | yad uktam:

                    	samīkṣya nipuṇaṃ dharmam ṛṣibhyo manubhāṣitam |

                    	āmnāyāt samyag uddhṛtya śaṅkhaś ca likhitas tathā || iti |

sāṃvarte 'py etad evoktam:

                    	vatsaraṃ vā kaṇān aśnan sarvānnarasavarjitaḥ | iti |

atra viśeṣo "vālavāsā jaṭī kaṇapiṇyākayor anyatarad rātrau sakṛd aśnan" iti | āpastamboktaṃ tu: "surāṃ pītvā steyaṃ kṛtvā gurutalpaṃ ca gatvā brahmahatyām akṛtvā caturthakālaṃ mitabhojinas trir apo 'bhyavayantas tribhir varṣaiḥ śudhyante" (ĀpDh 1.25.10) iti | etac ca samucchitaviṣayam | anyathā brahmahatyām akṛtvā ity etad avacanīyaṃ syāt | atas tritayam apy abuddhipūrvaṃ kathaṃcit kṛtvāpastamboktam | yady apy āṅgirase vajrākhyaṃ vrataṃ prakṛtyoktam:

                    	mahāpātakasaṃyuktā varṣaiḥ śudhyanti te tribhiḥ |

iti, tad brahmahatyāviṣayam eva dvādaśābdikavaikalpikaṃ viduṣāṃ brāhmaṇānām eva draṣṭavyam | surāpāne tu:

                    	kālasya tu yathoktasya brāhmaṇā eva kāraṇam |

iti tatraiva yad uktaṃ tad draṣṭavyam | "brāhmaṇā eva kāraṇam" iti vadan smṛtyantarādhīnaḥ kālaniyama ity etad eva jñāpayati | evam anyāny api smṛtyantaroktāni surāpānaprāyaścittāni yojyāni || 254 ||

 

_evaṃ matipūrve 'bhyāse maraṇāntam anabhyāse ca saṃvatsaraṃ brahmahatyāvrataṃ kaṇādibhojanayuktam uktvā, athedānīm amatipūrve vaktum āha |_

 

                    	**ajñānāt tu surāṃ pītvā reto viṇmūtram eva vā |**

**              	punaḥ saṃskāram arhanti trayo varṇā na saṃśayaḥ || 3.255 ||**

 

ajñānād iti | pratiṣedhājñānaṃ yadi syāt | tathā retoviṇmūtreṣv api | tatas trayo varṇāḥ saṃskāram upanayanaṃ kṛtopanayanāḥ santo 'pi punar apy arhanti | na cātra svalpam idaṃ prāyaścittam, ato 'nyad api kiṃcit kalpyam ity etad "na saṃśayaḥ" ity anena spaṣṭīkṛtam | yas tu pratiṣedhaṃ jānāti, sureyam iti jñātvā pibati, tasyāpy anabhyāse vāsiṣṭham (VaDh 20.19) | evaṃ mūtrādiṣv api yojyam | prāgupanayanāt tv ajñātasurāpāne tenaivopanayanasaṃskāreṇa śuddhiḥ | tathāha manuḥ |

                    	ajñānād vāruṇīṃ pītvā saṃskāreṇaiva śudhyati | iti | (MDh 11.146)

atra punaḥśabdābhāvād ādya eva saṃskāro 'bhipretaḥ | tathā cānyatra punaḥśabdaḥ kṛtaḥ |

                    	ajñānāt prāśya viṇmūtraṃ surāsaṃspṛṣṭam eva ca |

                    	punaḥsaṃskāram arhanti trayo varṇā dvijātayaḥ || iti | (MDh 11.150)

dvijātivacanāt punaḥśabdāc ca kṛtopanayanānām evaitaj jñāyate | ataś ca "saṃskāreṇaiva śudhyati" ity etad ādyasaṃskāraviṣayaṃ draṣṭavyam | gautamīyāt tu pratiṣedhāt "madyaṃ nityaṃ brāhmaṇaḥ" (GDh 2.20) iti prāg apy upanayanād doṣo 'sti, na tu tatra prāyaścittāntaram, "saṃskāreṇaiva śudhyati" iti vacanāt | ataś caitad api ślokārdham anupanītasyaiveti kecit:

                    	matipūrvam anirdeśyaṃ prāṇāntikam iti sthitiḥ | iti | (MDh 11.146)

ayam asyārthaḥ | yady anupanītaḥ sann ajñānād akāmato vāruṇīṃ paiṣṭīṃ surāṃ pibet, tataḥ saṃskāreṇaiva śudhyatīti, matipūrvaṃ tv anirdeśyaṃ pītvā prāṇāntikaṃ tasyāpi prāyaścittam iti sthitiḥ iti, nātra prāyaścittāntaram ālocyam ity abhiprāyaḥ | anirdeśyam ity etat pānaviśeṣaṇam, tāvad anekaśaḥ kāmakāreṇa pibati yāvan nirdeṣṭuṃ na śakyate, katikṛtvaḥ kiyatparimāṇāṃ veti yāvat | anye 'py etad aviśeṣeṇaiva varṇayanti: nānupanitasyaiveti, tat tu "surāṃ pītvā dvijo mohāt" (MDh 11.90) ity anenaiva siddhatvān nātīvopayujyata iti pūrvavyākhyaiva yuktā | surāsaṃspṛṣṭapāśane copanītasya saṃskāropadeśāḍ daṇḍāpūpikayā siddher nātīva tadviṣayatā syāt | ato 'pi yathoktaiva viṣayakalpanā ity eṣā dik || 255 ||

 

_brahmaṇyā apy etad eva surāpāne prāyaścittaṃ saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtaviṣayatvena yathārhaṃ kalpyam ity etat pratipādayituṃ nindārthavādopanyāsenāha |_

 

                    	**patilokaṃ na sā yāti brāhmaṇī yā surāṃ pibet |**

**              	ihaiva sā śunī gṛdhrī sūkarī vopajāyate || 3.256 ||**

 

pativratātvenārjitam api patilokaṃ na sā gacchati, yā brāhmaṇī surāṃ pibet | surāśabdaś cāyaṃ madyamātropalakṣaṇārtho na mukhyasurāpratipattyarthaḥ, arthavādagatatvāt | yadi hi vidhāyakavākyagataḥ syāt, tato mukhyārtha eva gṛhyeta | arthavāde tu madyamātraṃ nindituṃ surāśabdenocyate | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> cābuddhipūrvaprabhavatvād vedasyārthavādatvena vyākhyānaṃ yuktam, pauruṣeyeṣu punarvacaneṣv arthavādatvam abuddhipūrvakāritām evāvahati | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyaṃ</span>, yady arthavādamātravivakṣayaiva prayujyeta | smṛtikārās tu na prarocanāmātraparyavasāyitvenārthavādān prayuñjate, kiṃ tarhi, kāryaviśeṣapratipattyartham eva | ata eva prāyaścittavidhānārtha evāyaṃ śloka iti vyākhyātam | lakṣaṇavyākhyānasiddhyartham arthavādaprakāreṇopanyāsaḥ | ataś ca patilokaṃ na sā yātīti vacanād bhartur nirdoṣatvam iti gamyate | yat tu smṛtyantaram:

                    	pataty ardhaṃ śarīrasya bhāryā yasya surāṃ pibet |

                    	patitārdhaśarīrasya niṣkṛtir na vidhīyate || (VaDh 21.15)

iti, tad bhāryāśabdaśravaṇād aparityajataḥ patitasaṃprayogād draṣṭavyam | iha tu bhartrā parityaktā satī yā pibati, sā patilokaṃ na yātīti vyākhyeyam | sā hi ghorān narakān anubhūya punar apīhaiva loke śunī gṛdhrī grāmasūkarī cety evaṃvidhāsu tiryagyoniṣv ā pralayāt punaḥ punar utpādyate notkṛṣyate ity abhiprāyaḥ | evaṃ brāhmaṇyā matipūrve 'nyatra vā sakṛdabhyāse surāpāne madyapāne ca brāhmaṇavat prāyaścittakalpanā | kṣatriyavaiśyayos tu mukhyasurāpāne sumantunoktam: "surāpasya prāyaścittaṃ ṣaṇmāsaṃ vṛtasamudraukaḥsnānaṃ sāvitryā daśasahasrasaṃpātaḥ śirasy ante sāntapanaṃ sarvakṛcchreṇa śuddho bhavati" | asyārthaḥ: surāṃ yaḥ pītavān prakarṣeṇa matipūrvaṃ ca sa surāpaḥ | asādhāraṇye hi samāso bhavati | atas tatsiddhyarthaṃ buddhipūrve 'bhyāse cety uktam | tasya surāpasya prāyaścittaṃ ṣaṇmāsam | "vṛtasamudraukaḥsnānam" oko nivāsaḥ samudra oko nivāso yāsāṃ nadīnāṃ tāḥ samudraukasaḥ, samudragāminya ity arthaḥ | vṛtāś ca samudraukasaś ca vṛtasamudaukasaḥ, tāsu snānaṃ vṛtasamudraukasaḥsnānam | vṛtāś ca kaṭādibhiḥ pariveṣṭitāḥ | samudragāminyāṃ kaṭādipariśrite gupte snānam ity arthaḥ | ṣaṇmāsasya cānte daśabhir gāyatryāḥ sahasraiḥ śirasi udakamokṣaḥ sāntapanaṃ ca | ekasminn ahani pañcagavyaṃ pītvopavāsaḥ, anyasminn apītvety etat | nātra mahāsāntapanam, ṣaṇmāsam api kṛcchreṇa prājāpatyena taptakṛcchreṇa vāvasthānam | etac ca yady apy aviśeṣeṇoktam, tathāpi kṣatriyavaiśyayoṣitām eva draṣṭavyam | kutas tat,

                    	prāyaścittārdham arhanti striyo vyādhita eva ca | (ViDh 54.33)

iti smṛtyantarāt | kṛcchrābdaṃ ca dvijānāṃ vihitaṃ tadardhaṃ caitat | ataḥ puṃsām asaṃbhavāt strīṇām evaṃvidhānāṃ ca bālavṛddhāturāṇāṃ ca | evaṃ ca pariśritasnānasya stryādisaṃbandhād aucityaṃ samarthitaṃ syāt | atrāpi ca brāhmaṇyāḥ puruṣavat prāyaścittopadeśād itarayor ity eṣā dik | sakṛtpāne tu matipūrve kṛcchraṃ cāndrāyaṇaṃ ca | amatyā kṛcchram eva | yathāha manuḥ |

                    	etad eva vrataṃ kuryād yoṣitsu patitāsv api |

                    	vastrānnam āsāṃ deyaṃ tu vaseyuś ca gṛhāntike || iti | (MDh 11.188)

anyasyātrānantarasya vratasyānupadeśāt patitaparityāgoddhāraślokavyavahitam api strīsaṃbandhitayaiva vihitaṃ vratam "etad eva vrataṃ kuryāt" ity anena nirdiśyate | tatra coktam:

                    	sā cet punaḥ praduṣyeta sadṛśenopamantritā |

                    	kṛcchraṃ cāndrāyaṇaṃ caiva tad asyāḥ pāvanaṃ smṛtam || iti | (MDh 11.177)

atra caśabdaivaśabdābhyāṃ vyastasamastatayā prayogo vijñāyata iti viṣayavyavasthayā vyākhyātam iti | evam anyāny api surāpaprāyaścittāni vyākhyeyāni | kecit tu strīṇāṃ madyapāne naiva doṣa iti varṇayanti:

                    	yakṣarakṣaḥpiśācānnaṃ madyaṃ māṃsaṃ surāsavam |

                    	tad brāhmaṇena nāttavyaṃ devānām aśnatā haviḥ || (MDh 11.95)

iti pratiṣedhe puṃyuktasaṃyogaśravaṇāt | tat tu jātimātravivakṣayaiva na liṅgavivakṣārtham, brāhmaṇasyāvidheyatvād brāhmaṇajātyupalakṣitasya pānānuvādena pratiṣedho vidhīyate | na ca lakṣyamāṇasya viśeṣaṇaṃ vivakṣyata iti nyāyavidaḥ | anye tu brāhmaṇaśabdam apy upalakṣaṇaṃ manyamānāḥ śudrasyāpi pānapratiṣedhaṃ varṇayanti, hetuvan nigadānām aviśeṣāt |

                    	amedhye vā paten matto vaidikaṃ vāpy udāharet | iti | (MDh 11.96)

śūdrasyāpy etat kila saṃbhavaty eva | api ca tasyaiva vaidikodāharaṇe doṣaḥ svasthāvasthāyām | atas tasyaiva mattasya satas tatprasaṅgo mā bhūd iti sutarāṃ hetuḥ samañjaso bhavatīti | atrāpy upalakṣaṇatve hetur vaktavyaḥ | surāśabdasyāpy annamātropalakṣaṇatvaṃ kim iti na syāt, tasyāpy atyaśanād viṣūcikādinā bhavaty evāyaṃ hetur "amedhye vā paten mattaḥ" iti | ato yat kiṃcid eva | uttaraśloke ca:

                    	yasya kāyagataṃ brahma madyenotplāvyate sakṛt |

                    	tasya vyapaiti brāhmaṇyaṃ śūdratvaṃ ca nigacchati || (MDh 11.97)

iti yad uktam, tac chūdrasya nopapadyata iti kṛtvā vicāraṇīyam | "devānām aśnatā haviḥ" ity etat tu kṣatriyavaiśyayor api vaitānikāgnisaṃskṛtabhakṣaṇapratiṣedād anupapannam | kim uta dravyasya | atha pākayajñasaṃbandhena kṣatriyavaiśyayoḥ śūdrasyāpi pākayajñīyaṃ yad devānāṃ havis tad aśnatā ity ucyeta, tathā sati vyāvartyābhāvād anarthakam eva syāt | ato yat kiṃcid eva | tathānye madyaśabdaṃ madayoganimittaṃ vyācakṣate | tataś ca saṃdhānānantaram anutpannāyāṃ madaśaktau paścād vāpagatāyāṃ brāhmaṇasyāpy adoṣa eveti | tathā ca kila kvacid evam ācaranti | yatra tu nācaryate, tatra madyabhāṇḍasthitam iti kṛtvā (MDh 11.147) | tat tu madanīye 'pi kodravaudanādāv aprayogād viśiṣṭasāmagrījanyatayaiva parigrāhyaṃ madasyotpādakaṃ kiṇvādisāmagryupalakṣitam | saṃdhānadvāreṇaiva madyaśabdasya prayogo laukikānām | lokaś ca śabdārthādhigamahetur iti nātīva kleśanīyam | yathaivāryāvartanivāsiśiṣṭavyavahārasthitiḥ, tathaiva smṛtyartho 'nusartavyo na tadviparyayeṇa | viśeṣas tu mahāpātakādhikāre ity alaṃ prasaṅgena || 256 ||

 

_idānīṃ kramaprāptaṃ suvarṇasteyaprāyaścittaṃ vaktum āha |_

 

                    	**brāhmaṇ	asvarṇahārī tu rājñe musalam arpayet |**

**              	svakarma khyāpayaṃs tena hato mukto 'pi vā śuciḥ || 3.257 ||**

 

brāhmaṇasātkṛtaṃ svarṇam apaharati yaḥ sa ātmano viśuddhyarthaṃ rājāntikaṃ svayam eva musalaṃ gṛhītvā gacchet | tataś ca svakarma yathāvṛttaṃ niḥśeṣaṃ nirvyājaṃ ca khyāpayitvā tan musalaṃ rājñe samarpayet: "anena mā bhavān śāstum arhati" iti | tato rājñā tena musalena hataḥ śudhyet | yadi vā kathaṃcin maraṇāntikaprāyaścittānarho 'yam iti kṛtvā kṛpayā vā na hanyāt, tathāpi rājñā mukto visarjito daṇḍena vā muktaḥ śucir eva syāt, naiva prāyaścittāntaraṃ kuryād ity abhiprāyaḥ | tuśabdāc ca suvarṇaharaṇamātram eva kṛtvaitat | yena tv apahṛtyopayuktam, na ca pratiniryātayituṃ kṣamaḥ, tasyaitan naiva śuddhisādhanam ity abhiprāyaḥ | śrautaṃ tu tasyāpi bhavaty eva | yathāha vasiṣṭhaḥ: "brāhmaṇasuvarṇaharaṇe prakīrya keśān rājānam abhidhavet, steno 'smi bhoḥ śāstu mā bhavān iti | tasmai rājaudumbaraṃ śastraṃ dadyāt | tenātmānaṃ ghātayed maraṇāt pūto bhavatīti vijñāyate | niṣkālako vā ghṛtāktaḥ karīṣāgninā pādāt prabhṛty ātmānaṃ dāhayed maraṇāt pūto bhavatīti vijñāyate" iti (VaDh 20.41–42) | atra vijñāyata iti śrutyupanyāsād etadvyatirekeṇa smṛter viṣayakalpanā nyāyyā | tatra tuśabdābhāvād upayogaparyanta eva haraṇa iti gamyate | "brāhmaṇasuvarṇahārī tu" iti tuśabdasāmarthyāt pratiniryātanaśaktasyaiva haraṇe saty etad ity avagamyate, rājābhigamanecchātaḥ sarvavarṇānām | rājñā tv abrāhmaṇānām eva vadhaḥ kāryaḥ, brāhmaṇas tu daṇḍena moktavya iti kecit | tat tv ayuktam, brāhmaṇoddeśenaivāsyoktatvāt | tathā cāha manuḥ |

                    	suvarṇasteyakṛd vipro rājānam abhigamya tu |

                    	svakarma khyāpayan brūyān mā bhavān anuśāstv iti ||

                    	tato musalam ādāya svayaṃ hanyāt tu taṃ nṛpaḥ |

                    	vadhena śudhyati steno brāhmaṇas tapasaiva vā || iti | (MDh 11.99–100)

na cātra vipragraṇasyānyārthatvaṃ śakyate vaktum, ānarthakyaprasaṅgād, antareṇāpi vipragrahaṇaṃ stenamātrasya labdhatvāt | na ca rājābhigamanamātraṃ viprasyoktaṃ vadhas tv anyaviṣaya iti yuktam,

                    	tato musalam ādāya hanyāt tu taṃ nṛpaḥ |

ity atra śāstv iti vacanāt tam eva prakṛtaṃ vipram iti gamyate | yat tu brāhmaṇas tapasaiva vety evakārasāmarthyād brāhmaṇasya tapa eva, anyasya tu vadhas tapo veti varṇayanti, tad apy anyasyātrāprakṛtatvān niryuktakam eva syāt | evakāras tu tapaso vadhena sahātulyārthatvāt kalpāntaraprasaṅganivṛttyarthaḥ, tapasaiva vā kevalena śudhyati, vadhena vā rājāntikagamanadvāreṇeti | tataś cecchan brāhamaṇo rājānam upagacchet, tena hato mukto vā śudhyet, yad vā rājāntikam gatvaiva tapaḥ kuryāt | tac ca tapaḥ saṃvartoktam |

                    	svatantras tu sa saṃtāpya suvarṇasteyajaṃ malam |

                    	cīravāsā dvijo 'raṇye cared brahmahaṇavratam || iti |

araṇyavāsāc ca liṅgād dvādaśavārṣikam eva syād | yad vā sarvabrahmahatyāvratātideśa evāyam | tathā copasaṃhāre "etair vrataiḥ" (MDh 11.102) iti bahuvacanam upapannaṃ bhavati | anyathā tu dvivacanam eva syāt | dvijagrahaṇāc copanītasyaivaitat | anupanītasya tv adoṣa evety abhiprāyaḥ | yat tu kṣatriyādīnāṃ prāyaścittāntarānupadeśād vipragrahaṇam upalakṣaṇam iti vyācakṣate | te "brāhmaṇo na hantavyaḥ" "surā na peyā" ity evamādiṣv api brāhmaṇādiśabdān hanyamānamātropalakṣaṇārthān yan na varṇayanti, tat kim apy āścaryam | rājānam abhigamyeti atra vā rājaśabdam anuśāsakamātralakṣaṇayācāryādyarthaṃ kim iti na vyācakṣate | ye tu brāhmaṇavadho rājño na yukta iti kṣatriyādīnām evaṃjātīyakam iti bruvate, te nūnaṃ codanāvyāpāranirapekṣā eva svayaṃ dharmādharmau jānantīty apratisamādheyā evety alaṃ prasaṅgena || 257 ||

 

_idānīm atraiva prāyaścittāntaram āha |_

 

                    	**anākhyāya nṛpe śuddhyai surāpavratam ācaret |**

**              	ātmatulyaṃ suvarṇaṃ vā dadyād vā vipratuṣṭikṛt || 3.258 ||**

 

anivedyaiva rājñe surāpavratena śudhyed iti | atra,

                    	vālavāsā jaṭī vāpi cared brahmahaṇo vratam |

                    	piṇyākaṃ vā kaṇān vāpi bhakṣayīta samāṃ niśi || (YDh 3.254)

ity etat surāpavrataṃ vijñeyam | tataś ca tadvad eva matipūrve svalpasuvarṇaharaṇa eva syāt | svalpaṃ cārvāk suvarṇāt, suvarṇaśabdasya dravye  tatparimāṇe cāviśeṣāt | na cānekārthagrahaṇe 'pi doṣaḥ, suvarṇagata eva parimāṇe darśanāt | ataś ca parimāṇavacana evātra grāhyaḥ, arthato dravyāvagatiḥ | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

                    	suvarṇasyāpaharaṇe māṣakenāpi pātakam |

                    	niṣkaṃ pādaṃ tu harato na vidmaḥ kim bhaviṣyati || iti |

tathā:

                    	suvarṇam ekaṃ gām ekāṃ bhūmer apy ekam aṅgulam |

                    	apahṛtya dvijāgrebhyo (nāsthirā ? nacirād) vadhyate dhruvam ||

iti prāksuvarṇād alpadoṣatāṃ darśayati | tathā:

                    	deyasya parimāṇena pātrasya ca yathottaram |

                    	dāne 'paharaṇe ca syāt phalaṃ madhyādhamottamam || iti |

ato 'pi hriyamāṇadravyaviśeṣāpekṣayā parigrahaviśeṣāpekṣayā ca prāyaścittakalpanā yujyata eva | tataś ca suvarṇād ūrdhvaṃ dravyaparmāṇāpekṣayā brahmahatyāprāyaścittānāṃ viṣayakalpanā | suvarṇaśatam apaharato brāhmaṇasya rājāntikagamanam | tatra ca rājñā musalena hataḥ,

                    	yadi jīvati sa stenas tataḥ pāpāt pramucyate |

iti saṃvartavacanāc chudhyet | yadi tu rājāntikaṃ na gacchet, tadā ātmatulyam ātmanā samatulitaṃ suvarṇaṃ brāhmaṇāya dadyāt | atha vā tāvataḥ suvarṇasyānyat prativastu grāmādikaṃ viprasya tuṣṭikaraṃ dadyāt | kṣatriyādīnāṃ tu suvarṇaśatātirekeṇa haraṇe vāsiṣṭham eva prāyaścittadvayaṃ vikalpena syāt | āpastamboktam api:

           	steyaṃ kṛtvā surāṃ pītvā gurutalpaṃ ca gatvā brahmahatyām akṛtvā |

           	caturthakālaṃ mitabhojinaḥ syur apo 'bhyaveyuḥ savanānukalpam |

           	sthānāsanābhyāṃ viharanta ete tribhir varṣais tad apahanti pāpam || iti | (ĀpDh 1.25.10)

tat prāk suvarṇād amatipūrve 'paharaṇe gurutalpe cāmatipūrve sakṛdgate surāyāś cāmatipūrva evābhyavahārasaṃyogamātre yugapat kathaṃcid abhinirvṛtte ity etad vyākhyātam eva | āṅgirasoktam api brahmahatyāprāyaścittaiḥ saha viṣayavyavasthayā yojyam:

                    	mahāpātakasaṃyuktā varṣaiḥ śudhyanti te tribhiḥ | iti |

guṇavatas tu hartuḥ suvarṇād arvāṅ matipūrve sumantuvihitam: "suvarṇasteyī māsaṃ sāvitryāṣṭasahasram ājyāhutīnāṃ juhuyāt | sarvakṛcchreṇa ca pūto bhavati" iti | evam anyad api | yadi steyaprāyaścittaṃ smṛtyantare syāt, tato 'nenaiva mārgeṇa yojyam | suvarṇasteye ca guṇavadbrāhmaṇasaṃbandhiny eva mahāpātakaṃ syāt | tasyaiva dravyaṃ praty anaupacārikaṃ svāmitvam | itarasya tu saṃvyavahāramātreṇaupacārikam, prabhutvamātrāpekṣayā svaśabdo yataḥ | atha kasmān nirguṇānām api svatvaṃ na bhavati, śāstragamyatvāt svatvasaṃbandhasya | yadi hi parigrahaṇamātreṇa prabhutvamātreṇa vā syāt, tataḥ sarvasya syāt | tathā ca sati cauryeṇāpi tatsaṃbhavād apaharaṇam eva na syāt | śāstragamyatve vā nirguṇasya kim iti neṣyate, pratigrahādīnām evārjanopāyatvena niyamān nirguṇasya ca tadasaṃbhavāt | yathoktam:

                    	vidyātapobhyāṃ hīnena na tu grāhyaṃ pratigrahaḥ | iti | (YDh 1.200)

evaṃ yājanādhyāpanayor api | yathāha kātyāyanaḥ |

                    	avidvān yājako vā syāt pravaktā cānavasthitaḥ |

                    	tāv ubhau coradaṇḍena vinīya sthāpeyet pathi || iti | (KSm 828)

evam anyāny apy anekaśaḥ pratigrahādyanadhikāraṃ pratipādayanti | tataś ca tadabhāvāt svatvābhāva eva | siloñchādivṛttayas tu yāyāvarāṇām eva | kṛṣivāṇijyakusīdādīni tv adhikṛtasyaivārjitavataḥ pratigrahādīnām anvācayatvenaiva vyākhyātāni | evaṃ pitṛpitāmahādyārjitam api prāk samāvartanāt pitrādyabhāve rājñā pālanīyam | paratas tu guṇavataḥ pratipannakarmādhikārasyaiva tat tasya bhavati | yasya tv anyaḥ kaścid guṇavān dāyādo 'sti tad guṇavadbrāhmaṇadravyam eva | ata eva ca nāradenāpi traividhyaṃ dhanasyoktam:

                    	śuklaṃ ca śabalaṃ caiva kṛṣṇaṃ ca trividhaṃ dhanam |

                    	śuklaṃ nyāyārjitaṃ dharmyam itarad vyāvahārikam || iti | (cf. NSm 1.40)

mānave 'pi:

                    	dhanaṃ yad yāgaśīlānāṃ devasvaṃ tad vidur budhāḥ |

                    	ayajvanāṃ tu yad vittam asurasvaṃ tad ucyate || iti | (MDh 11.20)

na tāvad devānāṃ tat svaṃ, tathā sati yāga eva na syāt | na hi devasvaṃ yajamānaḥ śaknuyāt tyaktum | ato yathāvidhaṃ devān uddiśya tyajyate, tathāvidhaṃ devasvam | ato yāgaśīlānām eva dravye svatvaṃ mukhyam, gauṇam itareṣām ity etad evānena darśitam | tataś cāyajvanāṃ yad vittaṃ parigrahamātreṇa sāṃvyavahārikaṃ kāmabhogamātraupayikaṃ tad asurasvam, tatra teṣāṃ svatvaṃ nāstīty abhiprāyaḥ | tathā ca mantravarṇaḥ: "kiṃ te kṛṇvanti kīkaṭeṣu gāvaḥ" ity apariharaṇīyam evaitad iti jñāpayati | ato nirguṇabrāhmaṇānām aupacārikatvāt svatvasya na tadapaharaṇe mahāpātakayogaḥ | prāyaścittaṃ tu tatrāpi parigrahītṛsaṃbandhopayogādyapekṣayāpaharaṇaprayojanāpekṣayāpahartṛguṇāpekṣayā ca kalpanīyam | tac ca bhūyaso 'paharaṇe dyūtādiprayojane ca śaṅkhoktam: "hiraṇyastenaḥ patitasaṃvyavahārī mitradhruk śaraṇāgataghātī pratirūpakavṛttir ity ete jalaśayanaṃ pañcatāpam abhrāvakāśaṃ cānutiṣṭheyur grīṣmavarṣāhemanteṣu" iti etad eva | tāny aniyatakālatvāt saṃvatsaraṃ dvau trīn vā yathārhaṃ kalpanīyam | yadi tu guṇavān apahartā alpaṃ cāpahṛtaṃ pramādāt tu guṇavato 'py asadupayogaḥ, tataḥ śaṅkhoktam eva pūrvasyaivānantaropadiṣṭam: "māsaṃ vā gomūtrayāvakaṃ pibeyur evaṃ śudhyehuḥ" iti | evaṃvidhāny anyāny api nirguṇabrāhmaṇasuvarṇaviṣayatayā yathārhaṃ yojyāni | daṇḍas tu yo rājapuruṣair balād ānīyate | yathoktaṃ daṇḍaprakaraṇe:

                    	rājā stenena gantavyo muktakeśena dhīmatā |

                    	ācakṣāṇena tat pāpam evaṃkarmāsmi śāstu mām ||

                    	skandhenādāya musalaṃ laguḍaṃ vāpi khādiram |

                    	śaktiṃ vobhayatas tīkṣṇām āyasaṃ daṇḍam eva vā ||

                    	śāsanād vā vimokṣād vā stenaḥ steyād vimucyate |

                    	aśāsitvā tu taṃ rājā stenasyāpnoti kilbiṣam || iti | (MDh 8.314–6)

etac ca rājapuruṣair eva nīyamānasya draṣṭavyaṃ na tu svayaṃ prāyaścittārtham āgatasya, tatra hi tato musalam ādāyeti vadhasyaiva niyatatvāt | iha tv aparādhāpekṣayā śāsanaṃ vā vividhair vāgdaṇḍādibhir vadhaparyantair mocanaṃ vā kathaṃcin niraparādhasyaivāvimṛśyānītasya | ata eva "śāsanād vā vimokṣād vā" ity uktam | prāyaścittārthaṃ tu pariṣadā vimṛśyānumatasya kuto vimocanāśaṅkā | ataś ca yājñavalkye 'pi "hato mukto 'pi vā śuciḥ" (YDh 3.257) ity etat saṃvartaikavākyatayā rājñā hato yadi jīvati, tato daṇḍam agṛhītvaiva rājñā mukto viśudhyatīty evaṃ vyakhyeyam | tathā ca mānave rājño daṇḍaprakaraṇe 'pi doṣa uktaḥ: "śāsanād vā vimokṣād vā" iti | etad uktaṃ bhavati: vimokṣād api steno doṣān mucyate | kiṃ tv aśāstivā yadi rājotsṛjet, tatas tasya yat kilbiṣaṃ tad āpnotīty arthaḥ | kena | śāsanārhaḥ śāsyaḥ | tatra ca brāhmaṇasya na śarīradaṇḍaḥ | kiṃ tu prāyaścittārthaṃ caitad eva | nātra vadhadaṇḍo 'pi:

                    	na jātu brāhmaṇaṃ hanyāt sarvapāpeṣv avasthitam | (MDh 8.380)

iti pratiṣedhāt | pāpa eva yo 'vasthitaḥ prāyaścittārthaṃ rājābhigamanaṃ necchati, na balād ānītya taṃ hanyād ity arthaḥ | na śārīro brahmaṇadaṇḍa iti daṇḍasyaiva pratiṣedho na tu prāyaścittārthatayāgatasyety eṣā dik || 258 ||

 

_idānīṃ gurutalpaprāyaścittāny āha |_

 

                    	**tapte 'yaḥśayane sārdham āyasyā yoṣitā svapet |**

**              	gṛhītvotkṛtya vṛṣaṇau nairṛtyāṃ cotsṛjet tanum || 3.259 ||**

**              	prājāpatyaṃ caret kṛcchraṃ samāṃ vā gurutalpagaḥ |**

**              	cāndrāyaṇaṃ vā trīn māsān abhyasan vedasaṃhitām || 3.260 ||**

 

atra pūrvaśloke gurutalpagrahaṇaṃ na kṛtam, mahāpātakoddeśādhikāra evoktatvāt, "pitṛṣvasāṃ mātulānīm" ity upakramya, "chittvā liṅgaṃ vadhas tasya sakāmāyāś ca yoṣitaḥ" (YDh 3.233–4) iti | na ca rājñas tad upadiśyate, prakaraṇavirodhāt | ataḥ chittvā liṅgaṃ savṛṣaṇaṃ vadha evātmanas tasya prāyaścittaṃ nānyad iti tasyārthaḥ | ataś ca yadi sakāma etāḥ striyo 'bhyāsena vā gacchet, tata etat prāyaścittam, sakāmāyāś ca yoṣito 'py anicchantam evaṃvidhaṃ gacchantyā abhyāsena vā niṣkāmāyā api | caśabdasāmarthād etad eva prāyaścittam | tenātra prāyaścittāntaropadeśārtham uttaraśloka eva gurutalpagrahaṇaṃ kṛtam | pūrvaśloke pūrvoktaliṅgacchedanasaṃbandhād eva jñāyata eveti punar noktam | ataś ca pūrvopadiṣṭasyaiva liṅgotkartanasya vadhasya ca prakāranirdeśa iha kṛtaḥ | evaṃ ca sati yady akāmāṃ pitṛṣvasrādīnāṃ kāṃcid balāt pramathya pratārayitvā vābhyāsena gacchet, tataḥ pūrvaṃ tapte 'yaḥśayane sārdham āyasyā yoṣitā svaped ity etad draṣṭavyam | dvayos tulyāyāṃ pravṛttāv uttaram "sakāmāyāś ca yoṣitaḥ" iti smaraṇāt | aviśeṣeṇa vobhayam astu | sarvathā kāmakṛte 'bhyāse caitat prāyaścittadvayaṃ veditavyam | tapte 'gnivarṇe lohaphalake tanmadhye vā agnivarṇayābhigamyamānayā yoṣitpratirūpayā saiveyam iti snehenānurakta ivāliṅgya svaped ity arthaḥ | yoṣidgrahaṇaṃ ca pradarśanārtham | ataś ca yoṣitāpi pumān evaṃvidha evāliṅganīyaḥ | yad vā gṛhītotkṛttavṛṣaṇaḥ san nairṛtyāṃ diśi tanuṃ śarīram utsṛjet, maraṇāc chudyatīty arthaḥ | svayam utkṛtya kṣurādinā śastreṇa hastābhyāṃ vṛṣaṇau gṛhītvā pratyagdakṣiṇāṃ diśaṃ gacched akuṭilena ca mārgeṇa | yady antare kūpādi bhavati tato na parihṛtya gantavyam | yadi tu kenacid vṛkṣādināntare pratihanyeta, tatas tatraiva ā maraṇād āsīta | vṛṣaṇagrahaṇaṃ copalakṣaṇam atra | ataś ca savṛṣaṇasyaiva liṅgasyoddhāraḥ | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ: " gurutalpagaḥ savṛṣaṇaṃ śiśnam utkṛtyāñjalāv ādhāya dakṣiṇāmukho gacchet | yatraiva pratihanyāt tatraiva tiṣṭhed ā pralayāt" iti (VaDh 20.13) | tathā: "niṣkālako vā ghṛtāktas taptāṃ sūrmiṃ pariṣvajed maraṇāt pūto bhavatīti vijñāyate" iti (VaDh 20.14) | niṣkālakaḥ kālānapekṣaḥ, sadyo maraṇam icchann iti yāvat | śarīragataṃ vā kālaṃ keśalomādyapanītaṃ yasmāt sa niṣkālakaḥ, kālaśabdasya kṛṣṇaparyāyatvāt | pūrvaṃ tu yuktataram | sūrmī cātra pratikṛtir āyasī, pariṣavjed iti liṅgāt | ṛjv anyat | dakṣiṇādigvacanaṃ copalakṣaṇārthaṃ vikalpārthaṃ vā | spaṣṭam anyat | śāṅkhe 'py evam eva | kṣureṇa tu śiśnotkartanam iti viśeṣaḥ | yathāha: "gurutalpagas taptam āyasaṃ śayanam upasaṃviśet, kṣureṇa vā śiśnaṃ savṛṣaṇam utkṛtyāñjalāv ādhāya nairṛtīṃ diśam anavekṣamāṇo vrajed ā śarīrapātāt pūto bhavati" iti | evam "mātulānīpitṛṣvasāsnuṣābhaginīduhitṛgamaneṣv ācāryaduhitari ca" iti | atra caśabdād ācāryabhāryāyāṃ ceti gamyate | gamaneṣv iti bahuvacanād abhyāse kāmataś cety etal labhyate | bhedena ca mātulānīduhitrādyabhidhānād mukhyagurutalpo 'nyatra jananyāḥ kāmakṛte sakṛdgamane jananyāṃ tv akāmata evaitad iti jñāyate | mukhyatvaṃ ca pitṛsavarṇāsv eva pitṛbhāryāsu, pitur evānaupacārikaṃ gurutvaṃ yataḥ | tathā cācāryabhāryāyām ātideśikaṃ darśitam | vāsiṣṭhe ca "ācāryaputraśiṣyabhāryāsu caivam" (VaDh 20.15) iti spaṣṭa evātideśaḥ | ataś ca sūktā viṣayakalpanā | jananyāṃ punar ajñānād api sakṛdgamana evaitat syāt | yathāha saṃvartaḥ:

                    	mātaraṃ yo 'bhigacchet tu sutāṃ vā puruṣādhamaḥ |

                    	bhaginīṃ vā nijāṃ mūḍho niṣkṛtir nāsya vidyate || iti |

jīvaprāyaścittābhiprāyeṇa coktam, gurutalpaprāyaścittasyānyathā nirviṣayatvaprasaṅgāt | yathā tenaivoktam:

                    	gurutalpagas tu śayane tapte svapyād ayomaye |

                    	anvagūheta vā dīptāṃ striyaṃ kṛṣṇāyasīkṛtām || iti |

tathā ca hārītaḥ:

                    	pitṛbhāryāṃ tu vijñāya yo 'bhigacchati mānavaḥ |

                    	jananīṃ vāpy abhijñāya nāmṛtaḥ śuddhim āpnuyāt || iti |

evaṃ smṛtyantarāṇy api vyākhyeyāni | samānārthatvāt tu nodāhriyante | yadi tv ajñānato jananīvyatirekeṇa savarṇāsu pitṛbhāryāsu sakṛd gamanaṃ syāt, tadā

                    	prājāpatyaṃ caret kṛcchraṃ samāṃ vā gurutalpagaḥ | (YDh 3.260)

ity etat | samāṃ samvatsaram ity arthaḥ | cared iti khaṭvāṅgādiprāptyartham | yathāha manuḥ:

                    	khaṭvāṅgī cīravāsā vā śmaśrulo nirjane vane |

                    	prājāpatyaṃ caret kṛcchram abdam ekaṃ samāhitaḥ || iti | (MDh 11.105)

asavarṇāsu tu sakṛd avijñātagamane:

                    	cāndrāyaṇaṃ vā trīn māsān abhyased vedasaṃhitām | iti | (MDh 11.106)

etac ca vedādhyayana eva syāt, sāmarthāt | yas tu vedābhyāsāsamarthaḥ, sa catvāri cāndrāyaṇāni kuryāt "trīṇi catvāri vā punaḥ" iti | punaḥśadāc cāmatipūrve punargamane saty etad eva punaḥ punaḥ kuryād ity abhiprāyaḥ | tataś cākāmata upagamanasaṃkhyayāsyaiva vratasyābhyāsaḥ | kāmataś ca sakṛd gamane sāṃvatsarikam | abhyāse ca maraṇāntikam eva |

                    	yathākathaṃcit piṇḍānāṃ catvāriṃśac chatadvayam | (MDh 11.220)

ity etac cāndrāyaṇam, na yavamadhyādi, māsān iti māsagrahaṇasāmarthyād vāśabdadvayāc ca | smṛtyantaropasaṃhārād iyaṃ viṣayakalpanā | yāvac ca guroḥ parigrārhāḥ, tāvat gurutalpaprāyaścittānām avasaraḥ | yadā tu vyabhicāriṇyaḥ, tadā pāradāryaprāyaścittam eva syāt | tac ca cāndrāyaṇaṃ goghnaprāyaścittaṃ vety uttaratra vakṣyaty eva | vyabhicāritve 'pi yadi guruṇā na parityaktā, tathāpy asty eva gurutalpateti kecit | tat punar yadi guruṇā vā vyabhicāritvaṃ na jñātam, tannimittaṃ vā prāyaścittaṃ kārayitum ārabdham, tadaitad evaṃ syāt | yadā tu gurur apy anarhām evāṅgīkuryāt, tadānyad eva sāmānyavihitaṃ guror aparityāgakāranānurūpyeṇa kalpyam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecit</span> tu parityaktāsu pāradāryaprāyaścittaṃ naivecchanti, saṃbandhinimittatvād dāraśabdasya | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">tathā ca sati</span> vidhavāsv api pāradāryaṃ na syāt | na ca vyabhicārādibhis tasyāpagamo yuktaḥ, saṃskāranimittatvād dāraśabdasya, tasya ca patane 'py anapagamāt | ata eva patitā yoṣitaḥ kṛtaprāyaścittāḥ punar na saṃskriyante | anyathā tu patanena saṃskārasyāpagamāt kṛtaprāyaścittā apy adārāḥ syuḥ | ato vyabhicāriṇīṣv apy asty eva pāradāryam | prāyaścittāntaraṃ tu svairiṇītvanimittaṃ viśeṣavihitatvāt tāsu bhavaty eva | yathāha śaṅkhaḥ: "svairiṇyāṃ vṛṣalyām avakīrṇaḥ sacelaḥ snātvodakumbhaṃ dadyāt brāhmaṇāya | vaiśyāyāṃ caturthakālāhāro brāhmaṇān bhojayet | kṣatriyāyāṃ trirātropoṣito yavāḍhakaṃ dadyāt | brāhmaṇyāṃ ṣaḍaham upoṣya ghṛtapātraṃ dadyāt | prakīrṇāsv evam | asvatantrāsv anyathā" iti | etac cāyonisaṃbandhācāryādisamastagurvasaṃbandhāsu gurvīsakhyādivyatiriktāsv avarṇottamāsu cākāmato gamane veditavyam | kāmatas tūpapātakaprāyaścittam eva | tac ca gautamīyam "dve paradāre trīṇi śrotriyasya" (GDh 22.29–30) ity etat pratyetavyam | aparityaktāsu tu vyabhicāriṇīṣv akāmato vāsiṣṭham: "brāhmaṇaś ced aprekṣāpūrvakaṃ brāhmaṇadārān abhigacched, nivṛttadharmkarmaṇaḥ kṛcchro 'nivṛttadharmakarmaṇo 'tikṛcchraḥ" (VaDh 21.16) ity etat syāt | kāmatas tu cāndrāyaṇaṃ goghnaprāyaścittaṃ vā | tatra yadi vyabhicāritvam aparijñāyāparityāgaḥ, tadā cāndrāyaṇam | yadi tu prāyaścittaṃ kārayitum ārabdhā tadā goghnaprāyaścittam, "enasi gurūṇi gurūṇi laghūni laghūni" (GDh 19.19) iti vacanāt | avyabhicāriṇīṣu tv akāmato 'tiśayena guṇavatāṃ brāhmaṇādīnāṃ savarṇāsu guṇavatīṣu ca gamane śaṅkhoktam: "aprakīrṇāsu tv anyathā vaiśyāyām avakīrṇaḥ saṃvatsaraṃ triṣavaṇam anutiṣṭhet | kṣatriyāyāṃ dve brāhmaṇyāṃ trīṇi trīṇi vaiśyāvac ca śūdrāyām" iti | śūdrāyāṃ ca brāhmaṇajātāyām utkṛṣṭabhāryāyāṃ caitat syāt | kāmatas tv abhyāsena ca gamane gurutalpaprāyaścittam | yathā nāradena daṇḍaprakaraṇe 'bhihitam:

                    	mātā mātṛśvasā śvaśrūr mātulānī pitṛśvasā |

                    	pitṛvyasakhiśiṣyastrī bhaginī tatsakhī snuṣā ||

                    	duhitācāryabhāryā ca sagotrā śaraṇāgatā |

                    	rājñī pravrajitā dhātrī sādhvī varṇottamā ca yā |

                    	āsām anyatamāṃ gatvā gurutalpaga ucyate || iti | (NSm 12.72–74)

tena sādhvyāṃ gurutalpagavacanāt tadīyaprāyaścittaprasaṅgaḥ | mātṛpitṛsaṃbandhāyāṃ yathāsaṃnikarṣaṃ prāyaścittagurutvam | tac ca pitṛsaṃbandhi gurutvam aṣṭamāt puruṣād ārabhya mātṛsaṃbandhi ca ṣaṣṭād vivāhavad āśaucakalpavac ca vivektavyam | tathā tatsakhīṣv api saṃnikṛṣṭaviprakṛṣṭatvena prāyaścittaviśeṣakalpanā | jananīvyatiriktapitṛbhāryāṇāṃ tu bhrātaro mātulāḥ tadbhaginyaś ca mātṛṣvasāraḥ | tathā bhaginīsapatnyaś ca bhaginyaḥ, tadapatyaṃ ca bhāgineyaḥ | ataś ca tatrāpi nijamātulānyādyapekṣayā kiṃcin nyūnaṃ pṛyaścittaṃ syāt | tathā ca sumantuḥ: "pitṛpatnyaḥ sarvā mātaras tadbhrātaro mātulās tad bhaginyaś ca mātṛṣvasāraḥ, tathā bhaginīsapatnyaś ca bhaginyas tad apatyaṃ ca bhāgineyaḥ | ato 'nyathā saṃkarakārakāṇi kṛtvā yāpyāḥ patitāś ca bhavanti" ity ātideśikam eva vyapadeśaṃ darśayati | ataś ca prāyaścittālpatvasiddhiḥ | evam anyeṣām apy etadviṣayāṇāṃ prāyaścittānāṃ vivekah kāryaḥ | viśeṣavihitānāṃ tu kāmakārādivyavasthayaiva viṣayakalpanā | yathā tāvan mānave:

                    	paitṛṣvaseyīṃ bhaginīṃ svasrīyāṃ mātur eva ca |

                    	mātuś ca bhrātur āptasya gatvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret || iti | (MDh 11.171)

tathā saṃvarte:

                    	guror duhitaraṃ gatvā svasāraṃ mātur eva ca |

                    	tasyā duhitaraṃ caiva carec cāndrāyaṇaṃ vratam ||

                    	mātulānīṃ tathā śvaśrūṃ sutāṃ vai mātulasya ca |

                    	etā gatvā striyo mohāt parākeṇa viśudhyati ||

                    	pitṛvyadāragamane bhrātṛbhāryāgame tathā |

                    	gurutalpavrataṃ kuryān niṣkṛtir nānyathā bhavet ||

                    	kumārīgamane caiva vratam etad vinirdiśet |

                    	sakhibhāryāṃ samāruhya snuṣāṃ mātṛśvasuḥ sutām |

                    	ahorātroṣito bhūtvā taptakṛcchradvayaṃ caret || iti |

tathā sumantunā sāmānyenaivoktam: "agamyāgamanastrīvadhacaṇḍālasaṃparkeṣu kṛcchratrayaṃ caret" iti | viśeṣeṇa coktam: "mātṛpitṛṣvasṛsnuṣābhaginībhāgineyīgocaṇḍālīgamaneṣu taptakṛcchratrayaṃ sāntapanaṃ ca tiryagyonigamane prāṇayāmaḥ" iti | tathā gautame "sakhisayonisagotrāśiṣyabhāryāsu snuṣāyāṃ gavi ca talpasamaḥ, avakara ity eke" (GDh 23.12–13) ity uktam | avakaro 'vakīrṇiprāyaścittam | evaṃ smṛtyantareṣv api prāyaścittāni viśeṣataḥ sāmānyataś caivaṃprakārāṇy eva paṭhyante, samānārthatvāt tu na likhyante | tad etat sarvaṃ kāmakṛtādivyavasthāyāṃ yathāyathaṃ yojyam | sarvatra cānāmnātaprāyaścitte gautamīye "kṛcchrātikṛcchrau cāndrāyaṇam iti sarvaprāyaścittam" (GDh 19.20) ity etad vyastasamastatayā yojyaṃ, sarvaprāyaścittavacanāt | itiśabdasya ca prakārārthatvāt pāpaviśeṣāpekṣayā tasyaivāvṛttiḥ kalpanīyā ity eṣā dik |

 

        	strīṇām apy evam eva prāyaścittakalpanā | yac chūdrasya brāhmaṇīnāṃ gamane, tad eva brāhamaṇyāḥ śūdragamane syāt | evaṃ kṣatriyādiṣv api | yonisaṃbandhagamane 'py evam eva | tathā cāha manuḥ:

                    	vipraduṣṭāṃ striyaṃ bhartā nirundhyād ekaveśmani |

                    	yat puṃsaḥ paradāreṣu tac caināṃ cārayed vratam || iti | (MDh 11.176)

kṛtaprāyaścittā yadi bhūyaḥ pravarteta, tato yat puruṣasya pāradāryaprāyaścittaṃ, tat kārayitvā punar anubandhādyapekṣayā kṛcchram, tac ca kevalaṃ cāndrāyaṇottaraṃ vā | yathāha manuḥ:

                    	sā cet punaḥ praduṣyeta sadṛśenopamantritā |

                    	kṛcchraṃ cāndrāyaṇaṃ caiva tad asyāḥ pāvanaṃ smṛtam || iti | (MDh 11.177)

etac ca yasyāsau rakṣaṇīyā sa yadi saṃgrahītum icchati tataḥ prāyaścittam ekagṛha eva niruddhāṃ kārayet, yadi tu na saṃgṛhṇīyāt tato vipraduṣṭāṃ parityajato na doṣaḥ ity etad bhartṛgrahaṇāl labhyate | anyathā tu "nirundhyād ekaveśmani" ity etāvataiva siddhatvād bhartṛgrahaṇam anarthakam eva syād, anyasyaivaṃvidhaprayatnāsaṃbhavāt | na cāyaṃ rājña upadeśaḥ, anyatra daṇḍaprakaraṇe 'bhihitatvāt | tato bhartṛgrahaṇād yadi bhartum icchati, tata etat kārayed iti gamyate | vāsiṣṭhāni tu prāyaścittādikāroktāny api sāmarthyād rājña evopadiśyante: "śūdraś ced brāhmaṇīm abhighacced, vīraṇair veṣṭayitvā śūdram agnau prāsyed, brāhmaṇyāḥ śirasi vapanaṃ kārayitvā" ityādīni (VaDh 21.1) | yadi tu svayam eva striyaḥ prāyaścittaṃ kuryuḥ, tato "manasā bhartur aticāre trirātraṃ yāvakaṃ kṣīraudanaṃ vā bhuñjānādhaḥ śayīta | ūrdhvaṃ trirātrād apsu nimagnāyāḥ sāvitryāṣṭaśatena śirobhir juhuyāt pūtā bhavatīty vijñāyate | vāksaṃbandha etad eva māsaṃ caritvordhvaṃ māsād apsu nimagnāyāś caturbhir sāvitryāṣṭaśataiḥ śirobhir juhuyāt pūtā bhavatīti vijñāyate | vyavāye tu saṃvatsaraṃ ghṛtapaṭaṃ dhārayet gomayagarte kuśaprastare vā bhuñjānādhaḥ śayīta | ūrdhvaṃ saṃvatsarād apsu nimagnāyāḥ sāvitryāṣṭasahasreṇa śirobhir juhuyāt pūtā bhavatīti vijñāyate" iti (VaDh 21.6–8) | etac ca traivarṇikayoṣitāṃ traivarṇikaviṣayaṃ sarvatrāviśeṣeṇaiva syād, viśeṣānupadeśād eva, śūdragamane cotttaratra prāyaścittavacanāt |

                    	brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviṣāṃ striyaḥ śūdreṇa saṃgatāḥ |

                    	aprajātā viśudhyanti prāyaścittena netarāḥ || (VaDh 21.12)

ity uktvā, prāyaścittaṃ yad aprajātānāṃ śūdragamane, tad darśitam:

                    	pratilomaṃ careyus tāḥ kṛcchraṃ cāndrāyaṇottaram || iti | (VaDh 21.13)

atra ca traivarṇikastrīṇām aviśeṣopadeśāt pūrvatrāpy aviśeṣa eveti jñāyate | kartavyatāniścaye cānyenāpratāritāyāḥ svayam eva dṛḍhe manasy avasthite mānasaṃ, vācikam apy evam eva, vyavāye caivaṃvidha evaitat syāt | śūdraprasaṅge ca etat kṛtvā "pratilomaṃ careyuḥ" ity etat syāt, abhigamanasaṃkhyayā ca prāg garbhotpatteḥ | garbhe tu gurutalpaprāyaścittam evety eṣā dik | akāmatas tu pratāritāyā hṛdayena savyalīkena yadi kathaṃcid vyabhicāraḥ syāt, tataḥ saṃvartoktāni prāyaścittāni pratyetavyāni | yathāha:

                    	brāhmaṇī brāhmaṇaṃ gatvā kṛcchram eva samācaret |

                    	evaṃ śuddhiḥ samākhyātā saṃvartavacanaṃ yathā ||

                    	yadi tu brāhmaṇī gacchet kṣatriyaṃ vaiśyam eva vā |

                    	gomūtrayāvakāhārā daśarātreṇa śudhyati ||

                    	brāhmaṇyāḥ śūdrasaṃparke kathaṃcit samupāgate |

                    	cāndrāyaṇena śuddhiḥ syāt tad asyāḥ pāvanaṃ param || iti |

atra paraṃ kṛcchrāt cāndrāyaṇaṃ pāvanam ity evaṃ vyākhyeyam | spaṣṭam anyat || 260 ||

 

              	**rajakavyādhaśailūṣaveṇucarmopajīvinaḥ |**

**          		brāhmaṇy etān yadā gacchet kṛcchraṃ cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret || 3.261 ||**[^19]

 

vyādho lubdhakaḥ | śailūṣo naṭaḥ | atrāpi kṛcchraṃ cāndrāyaṇaṃ, kṛcchraṃ cāndrāyaṇe, kṛcchraṃ cāndrāyaṇāni | spaṣṭam anyat || 261 ||

 

                    	**śvapākaṃ pulkasaṃ mlecchaṃ caṇḍālaṃ patitaṃ tathā |**

**              	etāṃs tu brāhmaṇī gatvā carec cāndrāyaṇatrayam || 3.262 ||**

 

śvapāko marukuntikaḥ | pulkaso meyaḥ | mlecchāḥ pulindāḥ tārjikādayaḥ | atrāpi tathāśabdaḥ pūrvaślokoktaprakāraprāptyarthaḥ | tataś ca kṛcchrapūrvāṇy etāni pratyetavyāni, ekaikagamane ca sarvatra bahuvacanasyāvivakṣitatvāt | yadi tu kathaṃcid balāt pramathyātiśayaduḥkhārtā bhujyate, tato hārītoktaṃ draṣṭavyam:

                    	balāt pramathya bhuktā yā gṛhyamāṇena cetasā |

                    	prājāpatyena śudhyeta caṇḍālapatiteṣv api ||

yadi tu bhartāyaṃ madīya evety evaṃ manyamānā sakāmaivopabhuktā syāt, tato yadā vijñānaṃ, tadā,

                    	striyaḥ pavitram atulaṃ naitā duṣyanti karhicit |

                    	māsi māsi rajo hy āsāṃ duṣkṛtāny apakarṣati ||

ity evamādīnām arthavattā | yadi tu paścāt kathaṃcit sāmānyataḥ parapuruṣeṇāhaṃ bhuktety etāvad evāvagacchet, tato vāsiṣṭham:

                    	balātkāropabhuktā vā corahastagatāpi vā |

                    	svayaṃ vipratipannā vā yadi vā vipravāditā |

                    	na tyājyādūṣitā nārī nāsyās tyāgo vidhīyate || (VaDh 28.2–3)

ity uktvoktam:

                    	puṣpakālam upāsīta ṛtukālena śudhyati || (VaDh 28.3)

ayam asyārthaḥ: yadi tu svayam eva nāyaṃ mama bhartā bhrāntyaivāyaṃ mayā tadbuddhyā gṛhīta ity evaṃ pūrvasmāt tathātvāvagamād vipratipannā, atha vānyena kenacin nāyaṃ tvadīyo bhartety evaṃ tadbuddher vipravāditā, balātkāreṇa vā kenacit savarṇenopabhuktā, pararāṣṭropaplavādau vā kathaṃcic corahastagatā hīnavarṇopabhuktāpy atyājyā syāt | kasmād, yatas tena prakāreṇa sādūṣitaiva | nārītvaṃ hi yā pratipadyate, sā dūṣyate | yā tv anārītvena tiryagvidhinā bhujyate, na tasyās tyāgo 'bhyāsena vāpy upabhuktāyāḥ vidhīyate, saṃgrāhyaivāsāv ity abhiprāyaḥ | vidhīyata iti vacanād arthalakṣaṇas tyāgo bhartur icchayā na pratiṣidhyate, svecchayā parigraho 'py aduṣṭaḥ ity abhiprāyaḥ | idaṃ tu tasyāḥ prāyaścittam: "puṣpakālam upāsīta" ityādi | puṣpaśabdena ṛtukāla ucyate | pūrvoktena yāvakakṣīraudanādi gomayagarte bhuñjānā adhaḥśāyinī ghṛtapaṭaṃ dhārayanty āsīta yāvat puṣpakālam | tatas taduktayaiva vratacaryayā trirātrānte snātāpy āsīta yāvat ṣoḍaśa rātrayaḥ | evam ṛtukālena śudhyatīti | etad eva ca purastāt pradarśitam | "tasyā uktaṃ prāyaścittaṃ rahasyeṣu" iti hārītoktena kṛcchreṇa sahāsya vikalpaḥ | pratilomavyabhicāre 'py evaṃvidhasyaivābhyāsakalpanā ity alaṃ prasaṅgena | puruṣasyāpi svabhāryābuddhyaivābhigamane eṣaiva prakriyā yojyā | ata eva ca gautamenokam: "na strīṣv agurutalpaṃ patatīty eke" iti (GDh 21.8) | gurutalpe tu svabhāryābuddhyāpi patanam evety abhiprāyaḥ | yac ca manunoktam:

                    	yat puṃsaḥ paradāreṣu tac caināṃ cārayed vratam | (MDh 11.176)

iti, tatra caśabdād yac ca strīṇāṃ parapuruṣe 'bhihitaṃ tat puṃsa ity evaṃ vyākhyeyam | tataś ca hārītoktaṃ kṛcchraṃ tenaiva prakāreṇa puṃso 'pi bhavaty evety eṣā dik || 262 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvac caturṇāṃ gurutalpaparyantānāṃ mahāpātakānāṃ prāyaścittāny abhidhāyedānīṃ tatsaṃsargiṇaḥ prāyaścittāvasare 'rthāntaropadeśadvāreṇa prāyaścittam āha |_

 

                    	**ebhis tu saṃpibed yo vai vatsarāt so 'pi tatsamaḥ |**

**              	kanyāṃ samudvahed eṣāṃ sopavāsām akiṃcanām || 3.263 ||**

 

mahāpātakoddeśe "yaś caitaiḥ saṃpibet samām" (YDh 3.228) iti mahāpātakitvam uktam | idaṃ tu prāyaścittārthaṃ tatsamatvavacanam | ya ete brahmahaprabhṛtaya uktāḥ pātakinaḥ ebhir yaḥ saṃvatsaraṃ saṃpibet sahabhojanādy ācaret, so 'pi saṃvatsarāt tatsamaḥ, tadaviśiṣṭaprāyaścittārha ity abhiprāyaḥ | samaśabdaś cātra tad evāsya prāyaścittaṃ samam anyūnāna(ti?)riktaṃ pūrvoktayaiva viṣayavyavasthayā yathā syād ity evamarthaḥ | ataś ca samaśabdād īṣannyūnatvaṃ nāśaṅkanīyam | tathā ca mānave:

                    	yo yena patitenaiṣāṃ saṃsargaṃ yāti mānavaḥ |

                    	sa tasyaiva vrataṃ kuryāt tatsaṃsargaviśuddhaye || (MDh 11.181)

iti prāyaścittasāmyam evoktam | vatsarād iti pañcamyantaṃ parata ity adhyāhṛtya yojyam, saṃvatsarāt paratas tadīyaprāyaścittārha ity arthaḥ | prāk tv anyad eva prāyaścittaṃ darśayiṣyāmaḥ | asyāpavādaḥ: kanyām akṣatayonikāṃ samyaṅ nirviciktsam udvahet | ayaṃ tu viśeṣaḥ: "sopavāsām akiṃcanām" | upavāsaśabdo 'tra prāyaścittopalakṣaṇārtha iti kecit | upavāsamātram eva prāyaścittam iti yuktataram, upalakṣaṇatve hetvabhāvāt | akiṃcanatvaṃ ca puṣpamālāmātram api tadīyaṃ na grāhyam ity abhiprāyam | tathā ca hārītaḥ: "patitasya tu kumārīṃ vivastrām āplāvyāhorātropoṣitāṃ prātaḥ śuklenāhatena vāsasācchādya 'nāham eteṣāṃ na mamaite' iti trir uccair abhidhāya tīrthe svagṛhe vodvahet" iti | yat tu manunoktam:

                    	saṃvatsareṇa patati patitena samācaran |

                    	yājanādhyāpanād yaunān na tu yānāśanāsanāt || iti | (MDh 11.180)

yājanādhyāpanādinā nimittena yāni yānāśanāsanādīni, na taiḥ saṃvatsareṇa patati | kiṃ tarhi, arvāg eva saṃvatsarāt | yani tu lokasaṃvyavahāreṇa yānādīni, taiḥ saṃvatsareṇety abhiprāyaḥ | yājanādhyāpanayoś caikavadbhāvo yaunāpekṣayā nyūnatvārthaḥ | yājanādhyāpanād dhetoḥ patitena samācarann ity evaṃ padānāṃ yojanā | tataś ca yājanādhyāpanayor api patanam eveti gamyate | yatra ca yājanādi kārayiṣyāmīty evaṃ tannimitte yānāsanādāv api prāg eva saṃvatsarāt patanam, tatra tadācaraṇe sadya evety etat sāmarthyasiddham evety abhiprāyaḥ | tataś ca yadi prakārāntareṇa yonisaṃbandho bhavati, tataḥ patanam | yathoktena tu prakāreṇa sopavāsām akiṃcanāṃ codvahato nirdoṣatvam ity anavadyam | yad api gautamena patitātyāginaḥ patitatvam uktam (GDh 21.2), tad api yaunādidvārakam eva, anyatra "taiś cābdaṃ samācaran" (GDh 21.3) ity ārambhāt | ato yājanādinā ye patitena saha vyavaharanti, te "patitātyāginaḥ" (GDh 21.1) | ye tv aucityāt prasaktam api yājanādy apatitasyaiva patito 'yam iti kṛtvā na kurvanti, te tv "apatitatyāginaḥ" (GDh 21.1) | ye tu grāhyavacanatvena saṃbhāvitāḥ krodhādinā saṃdehamātre 'pi pariṣadi niyuktāḥ santo niḥsaṃdigdhaṃ patitatvaṃ samarthavāditayā samarthayanti, te "pātakasaṃyojakāḥ" (GDh 21.2) | taiś ca mukhyapatitair iva saṃvatsaraṃ ya ācaret, so 'pi saṃsargapatitaḥ, "taiś cābdaṃ samācaran" (GDh 21.3) iti vacanāt | ye tu saṃvatsaraṃ vyavaharantaḥ patitā bhavanti, tatsaṃparke 'nyeṣāṃ patanaṃ nāsti | tad uktam: "pañcamaś cācaraṃs taiḥ" (āmnāya under 3.228) iti, pañcamagrahaṇasyādhikanivṛttyarthatvād ity eṣā dik | atra ca vasiṣṭhoktam: "patitasaṃprayoge tu brāhmeṇa yaunena vā yās tebhyaḥ sakāśān mātrā upalabdhās tāsāṃ tyāgas taiś ca na saṃvased udīcīṃ diśam upaniṣkramyānaśnan saṃhitādhyayanam adhīyānaḥ pūto bhavatīti vijñāyate" iti (VaDh 20.45–46) | "tebhyaḥ sakāśāt" iti vacanād yās tv apatitebhyas tadīyebhyo jñātisakhiprabhṛtibhyas tenaiva hetunopalabdhās tāsām atyāga eva | mātrāgrahaṇaṃ ca tāmbūlāder api tadīyasya tyāgo yathā syād ity evamartham | upalabdhā iti cāsaṃcetitāsv adoṣārthaṃ, saṃcetitānāṃ ca svarūpanāśe 'pi tattulayasyānyasya tyāgārtham | taiś ca na saṃvased iti prāyaścittārambhād eva siddhatvād ekagrāmavāsanivṛttyartham antikavāsanivṛttyarthaṃ vā | spaṣṭam anyat | śaṅkhenāpy uktam: "patitasaṃvyavahāriṇo jalaśayanaṃ pañcatāpam abhrāvakāśaṃ cānutiṣṭheyur grīṣmavarṣāhemanteṣu māsaṃ vā gomūtrayāvakaṃ pibeyur evaṃ śudhyanti" iti | tathā mahāpātakamadhye "taiś ca saha saṃprayogaś ca sa pañcamaḥ pātakaḥ" ity uktam, na ca tatra prāyaścittam uktam | ato yat sāmānyenoktam "patito hy ātmānam uddharet saṃvatsaraṃ taptakṛcchram ācaret" ityādi brahmahtyāprakaraṇe vyākhyātam, tad eva saṃprayogiṇo 'bhipretam iti gamyate | tathā saṃvarte 'pi caturṇāṃ mahāpātakānāṃ prāyaścittāny uktvoktam:

                    	ebhiḥ saṃparkam āyāti yaḥ kaścit pāpamohitaḥ |

                    	ṣaṇmāsam abdam ekaṃ vā pūrvoktānāṃ vrataṃ caret || iti |

atra caibhiḥ ṣaṇmāsam abdam ekaṃ vā ya saṃparkam āyāti, sa pūrvoktānāṃ vrataṃ cared iti kecid yojayanti | tathā saty abdagrahaṇāt siddhe saty ekaṃ vety avaktavyaṃ syāt | ataḥ prāyaścittakālopadeśo 'yaṃ na saṃparkakālasya | tenāyaṃ ślokārthaḥ: ya ebhir brahmahaprabhṛtibhiḥ smṛtyantarānusāreṇa "saṃvatsareṇa patati" (MDh 11.180) ityādinā saṃparkam ābhimukhyena yāti, sa eṣāṃ pūrvoktānāṃ yad vrataṃ dvādaśābdādy uktaṃ tad eva ṣaṇmāsam ekaṃ vābdaṃ cared iti | vāśabdāc ca dvau vā trīn vā ity etad api gamyata eva | tathā ṣaṇmāsaṃ trīn vā māsān iti | evaṃ sumantunāpi suvarṇasteyasyoktvā "suvarṇasteyī māsaṃ sāvitryāṣṭasāhasram ājyāhutīr juhuyāt sarvakṛcchreṇa ca pūto bhavati" iti, tata uktam: "yaś caitaiḥ saha yaunamukhyabrāhmāṇāṃ saṃbandhānām anyatamena saṃparkaṃ kuryāt, tasyāpy etad eva prāyaścittaṃ vidadhyāt" iti | ānantaryāc caitad eva steyasaṃbaddham iti gamyate, na tu yena saṃparkas tadīyam evety evaṃ yojanopapadyate | śātātape tu: "patitasaṃvyavahārī taptakṛcchreṇa śudhyati" ity evam | smṛtyantareṣu tu patitasaṃparkaprāyaścittāni mānavenaikārthāny eva:

                    	yo yena patitenaiṣāṃ saṃparkaṃ yāti mānavaḥ |

                    	sa tasyaiva vrataṃ kuryāt tatsaṃsargaviśuddhaye || iti | (MDh 11.181)

sarvathātrāyaṃ siddhāntaḥ: patitasaṃprayoge kāmakṛte yājanādhyāpanādau "yo yena patitena" ity etaduktayaiva viṣayavyavasthayā syāt | tatrāpi ca saṃparke maraṇāntikaṃ naiva bhavati, "tatsaṃsargaviśuddhaye" ity ārambhāt | anyathā tv ayam antyaḥ ślokapādo 'narthaka eva syāt | ataḥ patitasaṃparkaṃ viśodhayitum apatitaiḥ saha saṃparkasiddhyarthaṃ tasyaiva yaj jīvaprāyaścittaṃ tat kuryād iti | maraṇāntikārheṇāpi saṃparke gurutaraṃ kalpyaṃ na maraṇāntikaṃ dvādaśābdaṃ vā, "ṣaṇmāsam abdam ekaṃ vā" iti saṃvartavacanāt | nāpy asya dvādaśābdaṃ yuktam, maraṇāntikena tulyakalpatvāt | na ca dvādaśābdārheṇāpi saṃparke svayaṃ tadanarhasya tad yuktam | na ca yathāvidho 'nubandho hantuḥ, tathāvidhaḥ saṃsarge saṃbhavati | hantā hi vidyāvṛttatapaḥsaṃpannaṃ savanagataṃ ca brāhmaṇaṃ tasyaiva mahāsatīṃ yoṣitam apahartuṃ kāmato hanyāt | na ca tena saha saṃsarge tathāvidho 'nubandhaḥ saṃbhavati | ataḥ saṃsargahetvapekṣayaiva tasya prāyaścittaṃ kalpyam, na ca tatkalpanāyāṃ kalpāntarasyānupraveśaḥ, yena pūrvoktā kalpanā syāt | tato yāny etāni smṛtyantareṣu saṃsargoddeśena viśeṣavihitāni, tair eva saha sāmānyopadiṣṭānāṃ viṣayakalpanā yuktā | na ca taiḥ saha dvādaśābdikaṃ maraṇāntikaṃ vā śakyaṃ kalpayitum | ato 'pi yāny eva sarasvatīgamanasaṃhitājapasaṃvatsarakaṇapiṇyākabhakṣaṇatulyāni, tāny eva kāmakṛte saṃsarge ghoratarānubandhe ca sarasvatyādyarhasaṃparke ca viśeṣavihitāni pūrvam udāhṛtāni pratyetavyāni | parasparaṃ tu viṣayakalpanā jñātaivety alaṃ prasaṅgena | caṇḍālasaṃparkaprāyaścittāny apy anenaiva mārgeṇa vyakhyeyāni | tatrāpi,

                    	caṇḍālāntyastriyo gatvā bhuktvā ca pratigṛhya ca |

                    	pataty ajñānato vipro jñānāt sāmyaṃ tu gacchati || (MDh 11.175)

iti mānave patitatvavacanāt patitaprāyaścittāni sarvāṇi prasajyante | "jñānāt sāmyaṃ tu gacchati" iti ca prāyaścittābhāva evaivaṃvidhasya kāmato vyavaharata ity evamarthaḥ | ataś ca patitasaṃparkād gurutaras tatsaṃparka iti jñāyate, na tv abhāva eva prāyaścittasyety abhiprāyaḥ | tenātra dvādaśābdikaṃ maraṇāntikaṃ ca prāpnoty eva | saṃparkakālasya cānabhidhānāt pūrvaprakṛta eva kālo 'trāpi draṣṭavyaḥ:

                    	saṃvatsareṇa patati patitena samācaran | (MDh 11.180)

iti, sparśādhikāre ca:

                    	divākīrtym udakyāṃ ca patitaṃ sūtikāṃ tathā | (MDh 5.85)

ity ekaprakaraṇapāṭhāt | ataḥ saṃvatsarāt parataḥ kāmasaṃsarge maraṇāntikam, arvāk prāyaścittāntarāṇi mahāpātakaprakaraṇoktāni viṣayavyavasthayā yojyāni | tathā smṛtyantareṣv api caṇḍālasaṃkare, yathā vāsiṣṭhe: "gurvīsakhyādigamane kṛcchābdapādaṃ caret" ity uktvoktam: "etad eva caṇḍālapatitānnabhojaneṣu" iti (VaDh 20.16–17) | atra ca kṛcchragaṇanayā sapta sārdhāni kṛcchrāṇi | tenaitat saptarātraṃ bhuktvā kuryāt | kuta etat:

                    	bhuktvāto 'nyatamasyānnam amatyā kṣapaṇaṃ tryaham |

                    	matyā bhuktvā caret kṛcchraṃ reto viṇmūtram eva vā || (MDh 4.222)

iti manuvacanāt, tanmadhye ca patitasyoktatvāt:

                    	abhiśastasya ṣaṇḍasya puṃścalyā ḍāṃbikasya ca | iti | (MDh 4.211)

yadi tu abhiśasto 'ntareṇāpi patanaṃ mahāpātakābhiśasto gṛhyate, tathāpi daṇḍāpūpikayā mahāpātakināṃ bhedenānabhidhānenaivābhojyatvasiddheḥ sakṛdbhojane matyā kṛcchram | tataś cāvṛttiviṣayatvād vāsiṣṭam: "kṛcchābdapādaṃ caret" (VaDh 10.16) ity etat saptāhaviṣayam iti sthitam | caṇḍālabhojanaṃ tu yady api patitabhojanāviśeṣeṇa paṭhyate, tathāpi lokopacārān mānavāc ca jñāpakād gurutaram eva | ataś cākāmataś caṇḍālānnabhojane kṛcchraṃ, kāmatas tu sakṛdbhojane 'pi patanam eva, "jñānāt sāmyaṃ tu gacchati" (MDh 11.175) iti manuvacanāt | ajñānatas tu saṃvatsareṇa patanam | prāk tu saṃvatsarāt patitasaṃparkavad viṣayakalpanā | yatra tv ajñātaś caṇḍālādiḥ kasyacid gṛhe 'vatiṣṭhate, tena ca sahānye vyavaharanti na tu sākṣāt tena caṇḍālādinā, teṣāṃ prāk saṃvatsarād ūrdhaṃ ca ṣaṇmāsāt saṃvartoktam:

                    	caṇḍālasaṃkare vipraḥ śvapāke pulkase 'pi vā |

                    	gomūtrayāvakāhāro māsenaikena śudhyati || iti |

atra saṃkaramātram uktam, na tu sākṣātsaṃbandhe | tathā ca kāśyapaḥ: "caṇḍālaśvapākapulkasādisaṃkare saṃvyavadhāne ṣaṇmāsān gomūtrayāvakāḥ pañcāhakālaṃ pātavyāḥ | evaṃ pratimāsavṛddhyā vṛddhir ā parivṛtteḥ sūryasya | iti | sūryaparivṛttiś ca ṣaṇmāsena bhavati | ataḥ prāk ṣaṇmāsād ity ayam asyārthaḥ | vipragrahaṇāt tu brāhmaṇasyaivaitat | itareṣāṃ tu kṛcchratrayam | tac ca prājāpatyaṃ syāt | yathāha sumantuḥ: "agamyāgamane strīvadhacaṇḍālasaṃkare ca kṛcchratrayaṃ caret" iti | sākṣāt tu yasya gṛhe sthitaḥ, tasya parāśaroktam:

                    	avijñātas tu caṇḍālo nivased yasya veśmani |

                    	vijñānenopasannasya viprāḥ kurvanty anugraham ||

                    	ṛṣivaktracyutān dharmān paṭhanto dharmapāṭhakāḥ |

                    	patantam uddhareyus taṃ dharmaśāstraviśāradāḥ ||

                    	dadhikṣīraghṛtair yuktaṃ kṛcchraṃ gomūtrayāvakam |

                    	bhuñjīta sahito bhṛtyais trisaṃdhyam avagāhayan ||

                    	dadhnādau triyahaṃ pūrvaṃ sarpiṣā ca tataḥ param |

                    	kṣīreṇa triyahaṃ bhojyam ekaikena punas tathā ||

                    	tiṣṭhed dināni yāvanti tāvanty evaṃ samācaret |

                    	bhāvaduṣṭaṃ na bhuñjīta prakṛtyā gorasaplutam ||

                    	tripalaṃ tu dadhi kṣīraṃ palamātraṃ tu sarpiṣaḥ |

                    	aśaktāv upavāsena phalamūlāśanena vā ||

                    	ākareṣu bhavec chuddhis taijasānām aśeṣataḥ |

                    	jalaśaucena vastrāṇāṃ mṛnmayāni parityajet ||

                    	kusuṃbhaṃ gulakārpāsaṃ lavaṇaṃ tailasarpiṣī |

                    	dvāre kurvīta dhānyāni dadyād veśmani pāvakam ||

                    	sa pūtaḥ sahito bhṛtyaiḥ kuryād brāhmaṇabhojanam |

                    	viṃśad gāvo vṛṣaṃ caikaṃ brāhmaṇebhyo nivedayet |

                    	evaṃ sa śuddhim āpnoti parāśaramataṃ yathā || iti | (PSm 6.34–41)

kṛcchram iti gomūtrayāvakaviśeṣaṇam | tataś ca yathā kṛcchro durabhyavahāryo bhavati, tathā kevale gomūtre kartavyaḥ | sa yathoktaparimāṇair dadhyādibhir upasikto bhoktavyaḥ | saṃparkānurūpyeṇa ca bhṛtyānāṃ gṛhapateś ca kālaniyamaḥ | dvādaśarātrāc ca prāg vijñāne saty etat prāyaścittam | paratas tv etad evāhaḥsaṃkhyayābhyasitavyam | dakṣiṇā tv etāvaty eva | saṃvatsarāt tu parato brahmahatyāyām eva syāt | varṣatrayāt tu parato maraṇāntikam eva | anyeṣāṃ tu tatsaṃsargiṇāṃ saṃvatsarād ūrdhvaṃ patitasaṃparkavad viṣayakalpanety alam atiprasaṅgena | caṇḍālaparigṛhītodakapāne tu kṣullakaṃ sāntapanam,

                    	gomūtraṃ gomayaṃ kṣīraṃ dadhi sarpiḥ kuśodakam |

                    	ekarātropavāsaś ca śvapākam api śodhayet ||

iti vacanāt |

                    	caṇḍālāvarjite cānne spṛṣṭvā cainaṃ viśeṣataḥ |

                    	bhuktvā kṛcchram avijñāte jñātvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret ||

ity atrivacanaṃ spaṣṭārtham eva | yathā:

                    	caṇḍālaparigṛhītā apaḥ kiṃcit pibed yadi |

                    	ahorātroṣitaḥ snātvā pañcagavyena śudhyati ||

                    	caṇḍālena ca saṃspṛṣṭaṃ pibet kiṃcid akāmataḥ |

                    	atra sāntapanaṃ kṛcchraṃ carec chuddhyartham ātmanaḥ ||

                    	antāvasāyinām annam aśnīyād yas tu kāmataḥ |

                    	sa tu cāndrāyaṇaṃ kuryāt taptakṛcchram athāpi vā ||

ity āṅgirasāḥ ślokāḥ | tatra caṇḍālena ca sākṣāt yat spṛṣṭaṃ tat tadīyaṃ cājñānāt kathaṃcit pibati yas tasya mahāsāntapanam | yas tv akāmata eva tatparigṛhītakūpādau, tasya kṣullakasāntapanam | yas tu jñātvā tadīyam evānnaṃ svayaṃ saṃskṛtya bhuṅkte, tasya cāndrāyaṇam | yas tv ācamanārhāṇāṃ pratilomānāṃ kāmataḥ pakvānnaṃ bhuṅkte, tasya taptakṛcchram | yas tv akāmatas tasya prājāpatyam:

                    	bhuktvā tu pratilomānāṃ sūtādīnām akāmataḥ |

                    	prājāpatyaṃ caret kṛcchraṃ trirātraṃ tv āhṛtāśanaḥ ||

ity atrivacanāt | mānave 'pi ca |

                    	bhuktvāto 'nyatamasyānnam amatyā kṣapaṇaṃ tryaham | (MDh 4.222)

iti tadīyaṃ pakvānnam āhṛtam eva bhuktvā pratyetavyam | tadīyagṛhabhojane tu yājñavalkyoktaṃ caturaham ity eṣā dik |

        	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye</span> tu "bhuktvāto 'nyatamasyānnam" ity evamādīny arthavādatvena vyācakṣate, prāyaścittaprakaraṇa eva yat paṭhyate tad eva prāyaścittārthaṃ bhavati, aprakraṇe tv arthavādataiva yukteti vadantaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">tathā sati</span> śatapathe madhyamakāṇḍe prāyaścittaprakaraṇe pauroḍāśike kāṇḍe 'bhihitam: "skannam abhimṛśati bhūpataye svāhā" (ŚB 1.3.3.17) ityādi, tasyāpy arthavādatvaṃ syāt | na ca smṛtāv arthavādānāṃ tanmātraparyavasānaṃ yuktam ity uktam eva | na cātra kiṃcid arthavādasārūpyam asya syāt | ato 'rthavādo nāma vākyaprakāro 'sti, tam apy ahaṃ jānāmīty etāvān evābhiprāya ity upekṣaṇīyam || 263 ||

 

_evaṃ pañcānām api mahāpātakānāṃ prāyaścittam uktam | idānīṃ jātita utkṛṣṭānāṃ jātito 'pakṛṣṭānāṃ vadhe prāyaścittam āha |_

 

                    	**cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret sarvān apakṛṣṭān nihatya tu |**

**              	śūdro 'dhikārahīno 'pi kālenānena śudhyati || 3.264 ||**

 

brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyādīn, kṣatriyo vaiśyādīn, vaiśyo rathakārādīn, śūdraś ca pratilomādīn ātmano nikṛṣṭān nihatya cāndrāyaṇaṃ kuryāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca śūdrasya japagrāsānumantraṇānadhikāra eva | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam evam</span> | kiṃ tu "adhikārahīno 'pi śūdraḥ kālenānena śudhyati" | māsaṃ mayūrāṇḍakapramāṇān ekopacayādinā grāsān aśnan mantrarahito viśudhyatīty abhiprāyaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye</span> tu kṣatriyādivadhe prāyaścittāntarasya vakṣyamāṇatvāt pratilomavadha evaitat prāyaścittam iti vyacakṣate | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">tathā sati</span> "sarvān apakṛṣṭān" ity atra sarvaśabdo 'narthakaḥ syāt | tathā hi śaṅkhaḥ: "sarveṣām anyonyāpakṛṣṭavadhe cāndrāyaṇam" ity aviśeṣeṇaivāha | aviśeṣābhidhāne 'pi ca kṣatriyavadha eva brāhmaṇasya cāndrāyaṇam | vaiśyavadhe tu nyūnam anyat kalpyam | anyonyāpakṛṣṭavadha iti vacanāc cāndrāyaṇaprakārāpekṣayā vyavasthā kalpyā | yat tu kṣatriyādīnāṃ vaiśeṣikam, tan nikṛṣṭasyaiva hantur utkṛṣṭavadhe vijñeyam | tatraiva ca viśeṣaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ || 264 ||
