_yadi tv apakṛṣṭe 'pi kṣatriyādau deśāntaragate vyāpādite svayaṃ kṣatriyo 'yam ity evaṃ jānann api dveṣād brāhmaṇo 'yam anena vyāpādita ity evaṃ mithyaiva kaścid abhiśaṃset, tasyāpi kiṃ doṣaḥ prāyaścittaṃ vā bhaved uta neti, tathā yathāvasthitam apy avijñātaṃ loke brāhmaṇādivadham anyad vā pāpaṃ yo 'bhiśasya khyāpayati, tasyāpi kim ity ata āha |_

 

                    	**mithyābhiśaṃsino doṣo dviḥ samo bhūtavādinaḥ |**

**              	mithyābhiśastapāpaṃ ca samādatte mṛṣā vadan || 3.265 ||**

 

yas tāvan mithyaivābhiśaṃset tasya dvirdoṣaḥ, dviguṇam ity arthaḥ | yas tu bhūtam evārtham aprakhyātam abhiśasya prakhyāpayati, tasyābhiśasyamānena tulyadoṣatvam | kasmāt punar mithyābhiśaṃsino dviguṇadoṣatvam, yasmād abhiśaṃsanāt pātakasaṃyojakatayā patitatvopadeśāt tulyatvaṃ tāvad asty eva | anyac ca: yat tasya mithyābhiśastasya pāpaṃ, tac cāsau samyag ādatte mṛṣā nirdoṣasyaiva doṣavattāṃ vadan | tasmād yato na tāvat tasya doṣo 'sti, ato yaś cādhyāropitaḥ, yaś cādhyāropakatvena prāptaḥ, tau dvāv api tasyaiva doṣāv ity upapannam | dviguṇadoṣatvaṃ tāvat pūrvoktenaiva prakāreṇa siddham | kiṃ ca anyad api yat kiṃcit tena pāpaṃ kṛtam, tad apy asāv eva mithyābhiśaṃsanād ādatte | tataś cābhiśastaḥ pūrvakṛtād api pāpān mucyate ity abhiprāyaḥ | yuktaṃ caitat, duḥkhopabhogasya pāpakṣayahetutvāt | yat tv abhiśastasya prāyaścittāvadhānam, tad uttaratra vakṣyāmaḥ || 265 ||

 

_evaṃ mahāpātakaprāyaścittāni saprapañcam abhidhāyedānīm uddeśakramāpekṣayaivopapātakaprāyaścittānām avasaraḥ | tatra prāthamyād govadhasyāha |_

 

                    	**pañcagavyaṃ piban goghno māsam āsīta saṃyataḥ |**

**              	goṣṭheśayo go'nugāmī gopradānena śudhyati || 3.266 ||**

 

pañcagavyaṃ cātra bhojanārtham | tataś ca gomūtrādīni pañcāpi tulyapramāṇāny ekatrāloḍya pratyahaṃ sakṛd bhoktavyāni | saṃyamaś cātra cāndrāyaṇetikartavyatāvasthāna(ṃ?) smṛtyantaroktaṃ vā gocarmadhāraṇagomūtrasnānādi | saṃyamavacanād iha tu vaktavyam evam | goghno māsaṃ pañcagavyam aśnan goṣṭha eva gor upasaṃnidhau śayanaṃ rātrau kurvan divā ca go'nugāmī yathā ca gāvaḥ svecchayā sukhena gacchanti tathā gacchantīnāṃ paricārakatvenānugāmī syād ity arthaḥ | tato 'nte gopradānaṃ kṛtvā śuddhaḥ syāt | liṅgasya cānabhivyaktatvād ṛṣabhadhenudānaṃ ca yathāliṅgaṃ yojyam || 266 ||

 

_tathedam anyad govadha eva |_

 

                    	**kṛcchraṃ caivātikṛcchraṃ ca cared vāpi samāhitaḥ |**

**              	dadyāt trirātraṃ vopoṣya ṛṣabhaikādaśās tu gāḥ || 3.267 ||**

 

atra "kṛcchraṃ caiva" ity evakārād apiśabdāc caikaikam api prāyaścittam iti gamyate | ataś caitāni prāyaścittāni trīṇi kṛcchram atikṛcchram ubhayaṃ ca | samāhitaśabdaś ca pūrvavat smṛtyantaroktadharmaprāptyarthaḥ | tathedam anyat: trirātropoṣito daśa gā ekādaśam ca ṛṣabhaṃ dadyāt | evam etāni pañca goghnaprāyaścittāni ślokadvayoktāni viṣayavyavasthayā yojyāni | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecit</span> trīṇy evaitānīti vyācakṣate, kṛcchrātikṛcchrayoḥ samuccitayor eva prāyaścittatvāt | tathā sati trīṇy api samānatvād icchayaiva vikalpyante | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye</span> tu pañcagavyaṃ piban māsaṃ kṛcchraṃ caivātikṛcchraṃ ca cared ity ekam evecchanti | apiśabdāc ca api vā pūrvānapekṣaṃ kṛcchraṃ caivātikṛchraṃ cety evaṃ yojayanti, smṛtyantarānusārāt | tathā ca hārīto mānavaṃ traimāsikam abhidhāyāha |

                    	pañcagavyena vā māsaṃ sthitvā kṛcchradvayaṃ caret | iti |

aviśeṣābhidhāne 'pi caitadanusārād eva dvitīyam atikṛcchraṃ pratyetavyam || 267 ||

 

_etad evopapātakāntareṣv api prāyaścittāntaraiḥ saha vaikalpikatvenātidiśati |_

 

**                    	upapātakaśuddhiḥ syād evaṃ cāndrāyaṇena vā |**

**              	payasā vāpi māsena parākeṇāpi vā punaḥ || 3.268 ||**

 

sarvasyaivopapātakamadhyapaṭhitasyāyājyayājanapāradāryāder upapātakasyaivaṃ pūrvaślokadvayoktair goghnaprāyaścittaiḥ śuddhiḥ syāt | yad vā cāndrāyaṇena | yad vā māsaṃ payovratatvena | yad vā parākeṇa | parāko dvādaśarātropavāsaḥ | punaḥśabdāc ca vyastasamastatayā prayogo 'bhyāsena ca | smṛtyantarānusārāc ca vyavasthā kalpanīyā | atra ca smṛtyantareṣv anekaprakārāṇi goghnaprāyaścittāni paṭhyante | tathopapātakāntareṣv api | vaiśeṣikāṇi ca bahuṣu bahūni paṭhyante | teṣām api tu prasaṅganirūpaṇā yuktaiva kartum | yathā tāvan mānave:

                    	etair vratair apoheyur mahāpātakino  malān |

                    	upapātakinas tv evam ebhir nānāvidhair vrataiḥ ||

ity uktvoktam:

                    	upapātakasaṃyukto goghno māsaṃ yavāṃ pibet |

                    	kṛtavāpano vased goṣṭhe carmaṇā tena saṃvṛtaḥ ||

                    	caturthakālam aśnīyād akṣāralavaṇaṃ mitam |

                    	gomūtreṇācaran snānaṃ dvau māsau niyatendriyaḥ ||

                    	divānugacchet tā gās tu tiṣṭhann ūrdhvaṃ rajaḥ pibet |

                    	śuśrūṣitvā namaskṛtvā rātrau vīrāsanī vaset ||

                    	tiṣṭhantīṣu ca tiṣṭheta vrajantīṣv apy anuvrajet |

                    	āsīnāsu tathāsīta niyato vītamatsaraḥ ||

                    	āturām abhiṣaktāṃ ca coravyāghrādibhir bhayaiḥ |

                    	patitāṃ paṅkalagnāṃ ca sarvaprāṇair vimokṣayet ||

                    	uṣṇe varṣati śīte vā mārute vāti vā bhṛṣam |

                    	na kurvītātmanas trāṇaṃ gor akṛtvā tu śaktitaḥ ||

                    	ātmano yadi vānyeṣāṃ kṣetre gehe 'tha vā khale |

                    	bhakṣayantīṃ na kathayet pibantaṃ caiva vatsakam ||

                    	anena vidhinā yas tu goghno gā anugacchati |

                    	sa gohatyākṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tribhir māsair vyapohati ||

kecit tu "tribhir varṣaiḥ" iti paṭhanti |

                    	ṛṣabhaikadaśā gās tu dadyāt sucaritavrataḥ |

                    	avidyamāne sarvasvaṃ vedavidbhyo nivedayet ||

                    	etad eva vrataṃ kuryur upapātakino dvijāḥ |

                    	avakīrṇivarjaṃ suddhyarthaṃ cāndrāyaṇam athāpi vā || iti | (MDh 11.107–117)

āṅgirasenāpy evam evoktam |

                    	upapātakasaṃyukto goghno bhuñjīta yāvakam |

                    	akṣāralavaṇaṃ rūkṣaṃ ṣaṣṭhe kāle 'sya bhojanam ||

                    	kṛtavāpano vased goṣṭhe carmaṇā tena saṃvṛtaḥ |

                    	dvau māsau snānam apy asya gomūtreṇa vidhīyate ||

                    	pānaśaucakriyākāryam adbhiḥ kurvīta kevalam |

                    	vratavad dhārayed daṇḍam amantrāṃ caiva mekhalām ||

                    	gāś caivānuvrajen nityaṃ rajas tāsāṃ pibet sadā |

                    	gomatīṃ ca japed vidyām oṃkāraṃ vedam eva ca ||

anyat tu sarvaṃ mānavenāviśiṣṭam | ayaṃ tu viśeṣaḥ:

                    	anena vidhinā yas tu goghno gā anugacchati |

                    	sa gohatyākṛtaṃ dvābhyāṃ māsābhyāṃ vai vyapohati || iti |

tathā "dakṣināyām avidyamānāyāṃ tadvarṇaṃ talliṅgaṃ vopapādayet" iti | saṃvartas tu |

                    	goghnaḥ kurvīta saṃsthānaṃ goṣṭhe gor upasaṃnidhau |

                    	tatraiva śayanaṃ cāsya māsārdhaṃ kṣitiśāyinaḥ ||

                    	saktuyāvakabhaikṣāṇi payo dadhi ca saṃyataḥ |

                    	etāni kramaśo 'śnīyān naras tatpāpamokṣakaḥ ||

                    	śudhyate so 'rdhamāsena nakharomavivarjitaḥ |

                    	snānaṃ triṣavaṇaṃ kuryāt saṃyato vītamatsaraḥ ||

                    	gāyatrīṃ ca japen nityaṃ pavitrāṇi ca sarvaśaḥ |

                    	pūrṇe caivārdhamāse tu sa viprān bhojayet tataḥ ||

                    	bhuktavatsu tu vipreṣu gā dadyāc chaktito dvijaḥ | iti |

tathā kaśyapena govadham evādhikṛtyoktam: "prāyaścittam akāmāvāptau, kāmakṛte 'py eke" | dogdhryādīnāṃ prāyaścittaṃ dogdhrīdhamanadānena | tadāmayāśaṅkāyāṃ ca ghaṇṭābharaṇabhūṣaṇayojane vā pānatailauṣadhabheṣajakriyābhir viniyogair vyāpannānāṃ prāyaścittam: "brāhmaṇebhyo nivedayitvā saśikhaṃ vapanaṃ kṛtvā prājāpatyaṃ kṛcchram ācaret | cīrṇānte (?) dhenuṃ tiladhenuṃ dadyāt" iti kāśyapaḥ | athānyo varṇaḥ: "tena carmaṇā prāvṛto māsaṃ goṣṭhe vaset | triṣavaṇasnāyī nityaṃ pañcagavyāhāraḥ ṣaṣṭhānnakālaṃ payobhakṣī vā gacchantiṣv anugacchet tāsu stabdhāsu nopaviśet | nātiplavaṃ gacchet | na viṣameṇāvatārayet, nālpodake nālpayavase vā | ante brāhmaṇatarpaṇaṃ kuryāt | dhenuṃ tiladhenuṃ vā dadyāt" iti kāśyapaḥ | tathā śāṅkhe 'pi: "goghnaḥ pañcagavyāhāraḥ pañcaviṃśatirātraṃ tiṣṭhet | saśikhaṃ vapanaṃ kṛtvā gocarmaṇā prāvṛto gā anugacchet | goṣṭhe vaset | gopradānaṃ ca kuryāt" iti | vāsiṣṭhe tu: "gāṃ ced dhanyāt, tasyāś carmaṇārdreṇa prāvṛtaḥ ṣaṇmāsaṃ kṛcchraṃ taptakṛcchraṃ vānutiṣṭhet | tayor vidhiḥ" (VaDh 18–19) iti tatsvarūpam uktvā, "ṛṣabhavehatau ca dadyātām" (VaDh 22) ity uktam | paiṭhīnasināpi: "goghno yavāgūṃ prasṛtitaṇḍulaśṛtāṃ māsaṃ buñjāno gobhyaḥ priyaṃ kurvāṇaḥ śudhyet" iti | sumantus tu: "goghnasya goṣṭhe śayanaṃ dvādaśarātraṃ pañcagavyabhojanaṃ gavām anugamanaṃ ca" iti | tathā yamo 'pi |

                    	pādapāśanibandhād vā atiyoktrātivāhanāt |

                    	nadīkāntārasantāraśvabhrabhṛgvadripātanāt ||

                    	evaṃ gaur mriyate yatra tatra śuddhir vidhīyate |

                    	saśikhaṃ vapanaṃ kṛtvā maunī kaupīnavastradhṛk ||

                    	gomūtrayāvakaṃ māsam aśnan gobhiḥ samaṃ vrajet | iti |

tathātraivāparam |

                    	upapātakasaṃyukto goghno bhuñjīta yāvakam | (cf. MDh 11.108)

ity āṅgirasenaivāviśiṣṭaṃ granthato 'rthataś ca | ayaṃ tu viśeṣaḥ |

                    	gāyatryā daśasāhasraṃ japyaṃ kurvīta cāhnikam |

                    	gomatīṃ ca japed vidyām |

ityādi ca | tathā |

                    	gosahasraṃ śataṃ vāpi dadyāt sucaritavrataḥ |

                    	avidyamāne sarvasvaṃ vedavidbhyo nivedayet || iti | (cf. MDh 11.116)

gautame ca "gāṃ ca vaiśyavat" (GDh 22.18) ity atideśaḥ kṛtaḥ | vaiśyavadhe ca "prākṛtaṃ traivārṣikaṃ brahmacaryam ṛṣabhaikādaśāś ca gā dadyāt" (GDh 22.15) ity evam | bṛhaspatinā tu |

                    	dvādaśāhena goghātī tasmāt pāpāt pramucyate |

                    	kṣīrāhāro bhavet tatra kṣīradadhyaśano 'pi vā ||

tathedam anyat |

                    	gāyatryā daśasāhasraṃ japed vā yāvakāśanaḥ |

                    	nirmuṇḍaṃ vapanaṃ kṛtvā maunī kaupīnavastradhṛk ||

                    	gavāṃ madhye vased goṣṭhe divā tābhiḥ samaṃ vrajet |

                    	cīrṇānte tu dvijātibhyo dadyād gāṃ hemam eva ca ||

tathedaṃ tatraivānyat: "dvādaśarātraṃ pañcagavyāhāraḥ ṣaḍrātraṃ vā yāvakāhāro goṣṭhe vaset | deśakālaśarīraśaktyanurūpaṃ vā bhavet | śmaśrunakhādyapanayanaṃ kṛtvā brāhmaṇān praṇipatyānujñāto 'nte gāṃ vṛṣaṃ vā tadvadhe dadyāt | brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā śudhyed ity āha bṛhaspatiḥ" iti | śātātape tu: "trīn kṛcchrān prājāpatyādīn ācared gomatīṃ ca japet" iti | pārāśare tu:

                    	gavāṃ bandhanayoktreṣu bhaven mṛtyur akāmataḥ |

                    	akāmataḥ kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ brāhmaṇebhyo nivedayet || (PSm 8.1)

ity upakramya,

                    	saśikhaṃ vapanaṃ kṛtvā trisaṃdhyam avagāhanam |

                    	gavām madhye vased rātrau gobhiḥ samaṃ vrajet || (PSm 8.31)

ityādigo'nugamanaprakāram uktvā, prājāpatyaṃ kṛccharam uktam: "tataś cīrṇānte brāhmaṇabhojanam anaḍutsahitadhenudānaṃ ca" iti | evaṃ smṛtyantareṣv apy evaṃvidhāny eva govadhaprāyaścittāni | atra ca svayaṃbhuvā:

                    	upapātikinas tv evam ebhir nānāvidhair vrataiḥ | (MDh 11.107)

ity uktvoktam: "upapātakasaṃyukto goghnaḥ" ityādi (MDh 11.108) | tena jñāyate asty upapātakavyatirekeṇāpi goghnatvam | anyathā tu viśeṣaṇānarthakyam eva syāt | tac ca dvividham: kiṃcidupapātakasaṃyogād atiriktaṃ pātakāntaḥpāti, kiṃcic copapātakād nyūnam | tatra yad "upapātakasaṃyukto goghnaḥ" ity evam upakramya paṭhyate yathāṅgirase, tasya mānavena vaikalpikatvam | yat tu mānavād gurutaram asaṃyuktaṃ ca yathā gautamīyam, yathā yāmye:

                    	gosahasraṃ śataṃ vāpi dadyāt sucaritavrataḥ |

iti, tatra ca "upapātakasaṃyukto goghnaḥ" ity evaṃrūpatvād upakramasya etad mānavenāviśiṣṭhatvād vaikalpikatvena vyākhyeyam | anyat tu sahasradakṣiṇātmakaṃ pātakocitatvād gautamīyavaikalpikatvena | śatadānam api tasminn eva viṣaye 'nubandhādyapekṣayā yojyam | yāni tu nyūnāni śaṅkhayājñavalkyapracetaḥprabhṛtiṣu, tāny upapātakasaṃyuktatvenānupadeśād alpatvāc ca prāg upapātakād draṣṭavyāni | tatra ca kratvarthānāṃ gavāṃ vadhe mānavād abhyadhikānāṃ viṣayaḥ | itaratra tu vadhāyaiva pravṛttasya yo vadhaḥ, sa upapātakasaṃyogaḥ | yas tv anyārthaṃ pravṛttasya bhavati, sa yady upapātakamadhye paṭhyate, tathāpi nyūna eva, "upapātakasaṃyukto goghnaḥ" iti viśeṣaṇasāmarthyāt | na cātra parigrahālocanayā viṣayavyavasthā yuktā, tasya vadhaṃ praty anupayogāt | yat tu brāhmaṇasaṃsthagoharaṇe daṇḍabhūyastvam uktam:

                    	goṣu brāhmaṇasaṃsthāsu sthurikāyāś ca bhedane |

                    	pasūnāṃ haraṇe caiva daṇḍaḥ kāryo 'rdhapādikaḥ ||

iti, tat tasminn eva steyaprakaraṇe yuktam | tatra hi yadīyaṃ yac ca dravyaṃ hriyate, tatsvarūpāpekṣayaiva daṇḍaviśeṣanirūpaṇāt | iha tu yady apy ātmīyā hanyate, tathāpi tāvad evābhyadhikaṃ vā prāyaścittaṃ syāt | ato 'tra kasyeyaṃ gaur ity etan nopayujyate | tataś ca hīnasātkṛtāyā uttamasātkṛtāyāś ca vadhe hantṛgatānubandhāpekṣayaiva viṣayakalpanā | vacanāt tu kratvarthahiṃsāyāṃ doṣātirekāvagatiḥ, yathāha śaṅkhaḥ:

                    	mārutāḥ paśavo yājñāḥ daivīś ca maruto diśaḥ |

                    	vaiśyahatyāvrataṃ kuryād atas teṣāṃ pramāpaṇe || iti |

yady api cātra paśumātra uktam, tathāpi gautamīyād "gāṃ ca vaiśyavat" (GDh 22.18) iti vacanād goviṣayam evaitad iti draṣṭavyam | anyatrāpi ca mahatāṃ prāyaścittānām eṣaiva prakriyā yojyā | yathā svāyambhuve:

                    	mārjāranakulau hatvā cāṣaṃ maṇḍūkam eva ca |

                    	śvagodholūkakākāṃś ca śūdrahatyāvrataṃ caret || iti | (MDh 11.131)

kratvarthānām evaiṣāṃ vadha etac chūdrahatyāprāyaścittaṃ syāt | evaṃ smṛtyantareṣv api | yathā gautame: "maṇḍūkanakulakākabimbadaharamūṣikāśvahiṃsāsu ca" iti (GDh 22.19) | atrāpi śūdrahatyāvratam eva caśabdenopadiṣṭam | bimbaḥ kṛkalāsaḥ | daharamūṣikā cucchundarikā | mānavāt tu gurutaram etat | mānave 'py uktam:

                    	etad eva vrataṃ kṛtsnaṃ ṣaṇmāsāñ chudrahā caret |

                    	ṛṣabhaikādaśā vāpi dadyād viprāya gāḥ sitāḥ || iti | (MDh 11.130)

gautame tu: "śūdravadhe saṃvatsaraṃ prākṛtaṃ brahmacaryam ṛṣabhaikādaśā gāś ca dadyāt" iti (GDh 22.16) | atrāpi mānavaṃ brāhmaṇasya kratvarthaśūdravadhe ca | gautamīyaṃ tv abrāhmaṇaviṣayam | evam anyatrāpi kratvarthapuruṣārthāpekṣayā hantṛgatānubandhāpekṣayā ca hiṃsāprāyaścittānāṃ viṣayakalpanā karyā | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecit</span> tu samuccitānāṃ maṇḍūkādīnāṃ vadha etad iti varṇayanti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">tat tu</span> "hiṃsāsu ca" (GDh 22.19) iti bahuvacanān nyāyvirodhāc cāyuktam | ataḥ kratvarthaviṣayatayāiva vyākhyeyam | tatra ca kratvarthām agnihotrādisādhanabhūtāṃ gāṃ hatvākāmato vāsiṣṭham, kāmatas tu gautamīyam | somayāgāṅgabhūtānāṃ somakrayaṇyādāv akāmato gautamīyaṃ, kāmatas tu yāmyaṃ gosahasradānam iti | evam anyāny apy evaṃprakārāṇi vyākhyeyāni | puruṣārthāyās tu kāmato vadhe mānavam, akāmatas tv ātatāyitvena vā yājñavalkīyam | akāmena cāndhakārādau gaur ity evam ajānato mṛgavyādyadhikṛtasyāsty eva vadhaprasaṅgaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ātatāyivadhe naiva doṣo yuktaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span>, paśūnāṃ tv abuddhipūrvatvāt pravṛtter na mānuṣais tulyakalpatvaṃ yuktam | tathā ca sumantuḥ: "nātatāyivadhe prāyaścittam anyatra gobrāhmaṇebhyaḥ" iti | atas tadvadhe 'pi prāyaścittam asty eva, ātmatrāṇaparatvāt tv akāmata eva tatra vadha iti prāyaścittālpatvaṃ yuktam | yāni tu viśeṣeṇaiva paṭhyante, yathā:

                    	gavāṃ bandhanayoktreṣu bhaven mṛtyur akāmataḥ | (PSm 8.1)

iti pārāśare, tāni śrutita eva vyavasthitāni | na cāsmin viṣaya upapātakatvam | ato yat sāmānyenocyate:

                    	prāyaścittīyatāṃ prāpya daivāt pūrvakṛtena vā |

                    	na saṃsargaṃ vrajet sadbhiḥ prāyaścitte 'kṛte dvijaḥ || (MDh 11.47)

iti, tat pātakopapātakaviṣayatvād evaṃvidhe govadhe na syāt, yatraivopapātakatvaṃ tatraiva bhavati, na tu bandhanyojanādau, vyavahārocchedaprasaṅgāt | ato yadi saṃgopanādyarthaṃ bandhane kṛṣyādyarthaṃ vā yojane tatkṛto vadhaḥ syāt, tataḥ pārāśaryaṃ vijñeyam | yat tu:

                    	sāyaṃ saṃyojanārthāya na duṣyed rodhabandhayoḥ | (PSm 9.1)

iti, tad rodhabandhāv eva nirdoṣau na tu tannimitto vadho 'pi | tathā cānyatroktam:

                    	auṣadhaṃ sneham āhāraṃ dadyād gobrāhmaṇasya tu |

                    	tannimittaṃ vipanne 'pi puṇyam eva na pātakam ||

iti, anyatrāsty eva doṣa iti gamyate | anye tu saṃvarta evemaṃ ślokaṃ paṭhanti:

                    	niruddhānāṃ gṛhe vāpi vane vā śvāpadādibhiḥ |

                    	vidyutsarpāgnibhir vāpi maraṇe nāsti pātakam ||

iti, tat punar vicāryam | yat tu saṃvarta eva:

                    	ekaś ced bahubhiḥ kaścid daivād vyāpādito bhavet |

                    	pādaṃ pādaṃ hi hatyāyāś careyus te pṛthak pṛthak ||

iti, tad govadhaprakaraṇe 'pi śrutaṃ brāhmaṇādihiṃsāsv api draṣṭavyam, kaścid ity aviśeṣopadeśāt | ayaṃ cāsya viṣayaḥ: durbalahiṃsāyāṃ bahavo yadi mocanasamarthāḥ pratyekaṃ saṃbhūya vā syuḥ, tatra yady anyonyāpekṣayā vimocanaṃ na kṛtaṃ kathaṃcid daivayogāt, tatraikasya yat prāyaścittaṃ prāpnoti, tasya pādenaikaikaḥ śudhyatīty abhiprāyaḥ | pārāśaryoktaṃ ca sarvavarṇānām aviśeṣeṇaiva syāt, aviśeṣopadeśād eva | saṃvartoktaṃ tu yadi kathaṃcid gāṃ maraṇāyāgatāṃ vadhād anyena na śaknoti parihartum, tataś traivarṇikasya draṣṭavyam: "goghnasyāpi pravakṣyāmi niṣkṛtim" iti | apiśabdo 'tra rahitatvaṃ vadhasya jñāpayati | ato japopadeśād evaṃbhūte sākṣād vadhe draṣṭavyam | āṅgirasaṃ tu mānavena vaikalpikam | tad api japopadeśāt traivarṇikānām eva kāmakṛte vadhe draṣṭavyam | kāśyapīyaṃ tu dogdhryādisaṃyogenaiva coditatvāt sujñānam eva | dogdhrī ādir yeṣāṃ te dogdhryādayaḥ | tatra dogdhuṃ yantritāyāṃ vyāpattau tadartha eva ca dhamane | yā gaur mṛtavatsādikā, tasyā dhamanaṃ kriyate | tad gojīvināṃ prasiddham | evaṃ ghaṇṭābharaṇādi vikrayāṅgatayā yat kriyate, snehauṣadhadānādy api vikrayādyarthatayaiva śīghrapoṣaṇavivakṣayā yat kriyate, tat pratyetavyam | etad api sārvavārṇikam eva | dvitīyaṃ tu kāśyapoktaṃ śūdrasyaiva sāṃvartenaikaviṣayaṃ draṣṭavyam | pañcagavyāhāratve ca pratyahaṃ bhojanam | payobhakṣitve tu ṣaṣṭānnakālatā | samānam anyat | śaṅkhoktam apy asminn eva viṣaye śaktyapekṣayā yojyam | paiṭhīnasīyaṃ tv asminn eva viṣaye 'nugamanāsamarthasya stryāder draṣṭavyam | sumantuvihitaṃ tu yadi gṛhakṣetrakhalādāv upadravaṃ kurvatī gaur abhihanyamānā śvabhrādau kathaṃcid patati, tadviṣayaṃ stryādīnām eva | samarthānāṃ cāsminn eva viṣaye yāmyam:

                    	pādapāśanibandhād vā atiyoktrātivāhanāt |

ity upakramya yad vihitim:

                    	gomūtrayāvakaṃ māsam aśnan gobhiḥ samaṃ vrajet |

ity etad vijñeyam | yat tu tatraiva:

                    	upapātakasaṃyukto goghno bhuñjīta yāvakam |

ityādi, tad āṅgirasena tulyakalpam | yat tu tatraiva:

                    	gosahasraṃ śataṃ vāpi dadyāt sucaritavrataḥ |

iti, tad gautamīyavaikalpikatvena kratvarthagovadhaviṣayaṃ vyākhyātam eva | bārhiṣpatyaṃ tu "dvādaśāhena goghātī" ity etat pārāśaryeṇa vaikalpikaṃ traivarṇikānām eva | lakṣajapas tu brāhmaṇānām eva,

                    	japyenaiva tu saṃsidhyed brāhmaṇo nātra saṃśayaḥ | (MDh 2.87)

iti vacanāt | yat tu tatraiva "dvādaśarātraṃ pañcagavyāhāraḥ" iti, tat saumantavena vaikalpikam | yat tu tatraiva "ṣaḍrātraṃ yāvakāhāraḥ" iti, tat tasminneva viṣaye bālavṛddhādyapekṣayā yojyam | śātātapoktaṃ tu saṃvartokavaikalpikatvenānubandhaviśeṣāpekṣayā yojyam | evaṃ yogīśvaroktānām api parasparato viṣayakalpanā | sarvatraiva ca prāyaścittaprakaraṇe,

                    	jātiśaktiguṇāpekṣaṃ sakṛd buddhikṛtaṃ tathā |

                    	anubandhaṃ parijñāya prāyaścittaṃ prakalpayet ||

ity etad eva saṃkṣepasūtram | tathā:

                    	anuktaniṣkṛtīnāṃ tu pāpānām apanuttaye |

                    	śaktiṃ cāvekṣya pāpaṃ ca prāyaścittaṃ prakalpayet || iti | (MDh 11.209)

tathā:

                    	te yāṃ vedavido brūyus trayo 'py enaḥsu niṣkṛtim |

                    	sā teṣāṃ pāvanāya syāt pavitraṃ viduṣāṃ hi vāk || iti | (MDh 11.85)

evaṃ sarvatrāpi yojyam | ayājyayājanādāv upapātakavarge goghnaprāyaścittātideśād viśeṣavihitaiḥ saha viṣayakalpanā kāryā | viśeṣavihitaṃ caikaṃ tāvat svāyaṃbhuve:

                    	etad eva vrataṃ kuryur upapātakino dvijāḥ |

                    	avakīrṇivarjaṃ śuddhyarthaṃ cāndrāyaṇam athāpi vā || iti | (MDh 11.117)

athaśabdāpiśabdābhyāṃ ca smṛtyantarokānām upakṣepaḥ | tatra cāndrāyaṇaṃ goghnaprāyaścittena vaikalpikam, dvijagrahaṇāt tadviṣayam eva | yad api yogīndroktam:

                    	upapātakaśuddhiḥ syād evaṃ cāndrāyaṇena vā | (YDh 3.268)

iti, "evam" iti goghnaprāyaścittānāṃ pūrvaślokavihitānām atideśaḥ | cāndrāyaṇaṃ ca,

                    	yathākathaṃcit piṇḍānāṃ catvāriṃśac chatadvayam | (YDh 3.322)

ity etat pratyetavyam | tenaitat sārvavarṇikaṃ sarvopapatakeṣu draṣṭavyam | śaktyapekṣayaiva ca "payasā vāpi māsena" ity etad api vikalpenaiva | "parākeṇāpi vā punaḥ" ity atra cāpiśabdāt punaḥśabdāc ca "jātiśaktiguṇāpekṣam" ity etacchlokānusāreṇa punar apīty evaṃ yojyam | tathā cāndrāyaṇena payasā vāpīty evaṃ vyastasamastatayānubandhānusāreṇa kalpanety eṣā dik | yatra copapātake viśeṣavihitam asti, tatra tad api viṣayavyavasthayā syān na tu viśeṣavihitatvāt sāmānyasyānaṅgīkaraṇam, upapātakamadhyapāṭhasyānarthakyaprasaṅgāt, yathā vrātyatāyām upanayanakālātikrame prāk ṣoṣaśād varṣāt pāraskaroktam "kālātikrame niyatavad" iti (PārG 2.5.41) | niyatavad iti cāvijñāne pratimahāvyāhṛtitisṛbhir homaḥ, sarvābhiś caturthaṃ sarvaprāyaścittaṃ cety etad vyācakṣate | tac caitad ādyaupanāyanikakālātikrame prāyaścittam | upanīyamānasya tu

                    	triṣṭubhaṃ brāhmaṇo 'tīya prājāpatyaṃ samācaret |

                    	aśaktau pādaśaḥ kuryāt tataḥ saṃskāram arhati ||

iti hārītavacanāt, kṛtaprāyaścittasyaivopanayanam iti gamyate | paratas tu ṣoḍaśād varṣān mānavam:

                    	yeṣāṃ dvijānāṃ sāvitrī nānūcyeta yathāvidhi |

                    	tāṃś cārayitvā trīn kṛcchrān yathāvidhy upanāyayet || iti | (MDh 11.191)

etad ā dvāviṃśater varṣād anupanītasya brāhmaṇasya, "pūrvaḥ pūrva uttarottarakālātikamaṇe patati" iti śaṅkhavacanāt | gautamānusāreṇa sarveṣām ayam eva kālaḥ, "dvyadhikāyā vaiśyasya" (GDh 1.14) ity uktatvāt, "ata ūrdhvaṃ patitasāvitrīkā bhavanti"  (VaDh 11.74) iti vacanāt | tataḥ paraṃ ca vāsiṣṭham: "uddālakavrataṃ cared dvau māsau yāvakena vartayed māsaṃ payasā ardhamāsam āmikṣayā aṣṭarātraṃ ghṛtena ṣaḍrātram ayācitena trirātram abbhakṣo 'horātram upavased aśvamedhāvabhṛtaṃ vā gacchet" iti (VaDh 11.76–78) | yadi tv ādyād upanayanakālād ārabhyāṣṭācatvāriṃśadvarṣāṇi nopanītas tato 'sya vrātyastomaḥ, "yo vratakālam asaṃskṛto 'tikrāmet, sa ādyena yajeta" iti vrātyastomopadeśāt | ye tūpanītāḥ santo 'nadhītya vedam anyat kim api kṛtavantaḥ, na ca saṃdhyopāsanādi tyaktam, adhītya vā yaiḥ saṃdhyopāsanādyācaraṇe śaithilyaṃ kṛtam, te 'pi trīṇi kṛcchrāṇi yatnena kṛtvā vedaṃ paṭheyuḥ, ācāreṣu ca prayatnino bhaveyuḥ | yathāha manuḥ:

                    	prāyaścittaṃ cikīrṣanti vikarmasthās tu ye dvijāḥ |

                    	brahmaṇā ca parityaktās teṣām apy etad ādiśet || iti | (MDh 11.192)

goghnaprāyaścittasya coddālakavratavaikalpikatvam, cāndrāyaṇasya tu kṛcchratryeṇeti | evam anyāny api smṛtyantarāṇi vyākhyeyāni | steyādiṣv apy ayam eva mārgaḥ | granthavyākhyāyāṃ ca nipuṇato vakṣyāmaḥ | prakṛtam idānīm ucyate || 268 ||

 

_strīśudraviṭkṣatravadhasyopapātakamadhyapāṭhāt sāmānyena prāyaścittam uktam eva "upapātakaśuddhiḥ syād evaṃ cāndrāyaṇena vā" ityādinā _(YDh 3.268)_ | idānīṃ tu teṣām eva vaiśeṣikaṃ vaktum āha |_

 

                    	**ṛṣabhaikasahasrā gā dadyāt kṣatravadhe pumān |**

**              	brahmahatyāvrataṃ vāpi vatsaratritayaṃ caret || 3.269 ||**

**              	vaiśyahābdaṃ cared etad dadyād vaikaśataṃ gavām |**

**              	ṣaṇmāsāñ chūdrahā vāpi dadyād vā dhenavo daśa || 3.270 ||**

 

ṛṣabha eko 'dhiko yāsāṃ sahasrasya tā ṛṣabhaikasahasrāḥ | spaṣṭam anyat | pumān iti ca śūdrasyaivaitat kṣatriyādivadhe prāyaścittam ity evam artham akāmataś ca | yathāha manuḥ |

                    	akāmatas tu rājanyaṃ vinipātya dvijottamaḥ |

                    	ṛṣabaikasahasrā gā dadyāc chuddhyartham ātmanaḥ || iti | (MDh 11.127)

vṛttasthavadhe caitat, "pramāpya vaiśyaṃ vṛttastham" (MDh 11.129) iti jñāpakāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> etad brāhmaṇasyaiva, dvijottama iti vacanāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nāyaṃ</span> dvijottama iti samānādhikaraṇaḥ, kiṃ tarhi, dvija uttamo yasyety evaṃ bahuvrīhiḥ pratyetavyaḥ | kuta etat, apakṛṣṭavadhe cāndrāyaṇopadeśāt | tathā ca dvayor eva ślokayor dvijottamagrahaṇaṃ kṛtam:

                    	etad eva cared abdaṃ prāyaścittaṃ dvijottamaḥ |

                    	pramāpya vaiśyaṃ vṛttasthaṃ dadyād vaikaśataṃ gavām || iti | (MDh 11.129)

tṛtīye tu,

                    	etad evaṃ vrataṃ kṛtsnaṃ ṣaṇmāsāñ chūdrahā caret | (MDh 11.130)

ity atra naivaitad asti, anupayogāt | pūrvatra tu dvija uttamo yasya śūdrasya, kṣatriyavaiśyau vā | sa yadi nikṛṣṭaḥ sann utkṛṣṭaṃ hanyāt, tadaiva tat kuryād ity evamarthaṃ tad vacanam | iha tu sajātīyasya hantus tad vacanam evety abhipretyāvacanaṃ yuktaṃ syāt | itarathā tv ādāv evoktam adhikārād uttaratrāpi labhyata eveti punar na vācyam, sarvatra vā vācyam | ato yogīśvarīyāt punarvacanād iha coktanyāyānusārāc chūdrābhiprāyeṇaivaitad iti yuktam | ataś copapātakamadhypāṭho 'py utkṛṣṭāpekṣayārthavān syāt | itarathā tu tulyavad upapātakamadhye saṃkīrtanam abuddhipūrvam iva syāt | evaṃ ca yac chaṅkhenoktam: "sarveṣām anyonyāpakṛṣṭavadhe cāndrāyaṇam" iti, tad api samañjasaṃ syāt | yadi tv avaśyaṃ dvijottamavacanād brāhmaṇasyaivaitad ity evaṃ samarthanīyam, tato vṛttasthavacanāt karmaprayogamadhyagatayor ity evaṃ vyākhyeyam, somayāgavyatirikteṣṭipaśvādiviṣayatvena ca savanasaṃbandhena brahmahatyātideśāt | karmagatavyatirekeṇa tūpapātakaprāyaścittam eva | tatrāpy akāmataś cāndrāyaṇam, kāmatas tu goghnaprāyaścittam | anubandhādyapekṣayā ca japādibhiḥ pratipūraṇam | apakṛṣṭānāṃ tv akāmata etat | kāmatas tu:

                    	turīyo brahmahatyāyāḥ kṣatriyasya vadhe smṛtaḥ |

                    	vaiśye 'ṣṭamo 'ṃśo vṛttasthe śūdre jñeyas tu ṣoḍaśaḥ || iti | (MDh 11.126)

avṛttasthe tu saṃvartoktam:

                    	pramāpya kṣatriyaṃ mohāt tribhiḥ kṛcchrair viśudhyati |

                    	prājāpatyātikṛcchrābhyāṃ taptakṛcchreṇa ca kramāt ||

                    	kṛcchrātikṛcchrau kurvīta sa naro vaiśyaghātakaḥ |

                    	śūdraṃ hatvā tu kurvīta kṛcchraṃ sāntapanaṃ tathā || iti |

somavyatiriktakratugate tv akāmato nikṛṣṭasya sajātīyasya vā hantuḥ gautamīyam: "rājanyavadhe ṣaḍvārṣikaṃ prākṛtaṃ brahmacaryam ṛṣabhaikasahasrāś ca gā dadyāt | vaiśyavadhe traivārṣikam ṛṣabhaikaśatāś ca gā dadyāt | śūdravadhe tu saṃvatsaram ṛṣabhaikādaśāś ca gā dadyāt" (GDh 22.14–16) iti | kāmatas tu vāsiṣṭham: "evaṃ rājanyaṃ hatvāṣṭau varṣāṇi caret ṣaḍ vaiśyaṃ trīṇi śūdram" iti (VaDh 20.31–33) | savanasthavadhe tu śūdrasyāpastamboktaṃ brahmahatyāprāyaścittam (ĀpDh 1.24.6–23) | sarvatra ca jātyutkarṣāpakarṣāv ālocya viśeṣaḥ kalpanīyaḥ | uktaṃ ca: "jātiśaktiguṇāpekṣam" iti | śaṅkhoktam api gautamīyenaikārtham anubandhānusareṇa yojyam: "caturṣu varṇeṣu pramāpya dvādaśa saṃvatsarān ṣaṭ trīn ekaṃ tadante gosahasraṃ tato 'rdhaṃ tasyārdham tadardham ca dadyāt" iti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecit</span> tu gautamīyaṃ brāhmaṇasaṃbandhenaiva manyante | pūrvasūtrāc ca "garbhe cāvijñāte brāhmaṇasya" (GDh 22.13) ity ato 'vacchidya brāhmaṇasyety uttarasūtreṇa yojayanti | brāhmaṇasya rājanyavadhe ṣaḍvārṣikam iti | tataś caitadanusārād eva mānave 'pi dvijottamavacanaṃ vispaṣṭam eva brāhmaṇavivakṣayopapannaṃ syāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">tat tv idaṃ</span> nātīva yuktam | evaṃ hi pratyutāniṣṭam āpadyeta, brāhmaṇavadha eva rājanyakartṛke ṣaḍvārṣikavrataprasaṅgāt | na ca brāhmaṇasyety etat kartṛviśeṣaṇam "ubhyaprāptau karmaṇi" (Pāṇ 2.3.66) iti niyamāt | tataś ca brāhmaṇasya karmatvāpatter aniṣṭaprasaṅgaḥ | ata evāsahāyaprabhṛtibhir "garbhe cāvijñāte brāhmaṇasya" ity eva vyākhyātam | ato yathoktaiva viṣayakalpanā | tathā cāmnāyaḥ: "tasmād yady api rājā paramatāṃ gacchati" ity upakramya "vadha enaṃ hinasti svāṃ yonim ṛcchati sa pāpīyān bhavati yathā śreyāṃsaṃ hiṃsitvā" (BāU 1.4.11) iti nikṛṣṭena śreyaso vadhaṃ siddhavad dṛṣṭāntatvena doṣavattayā darśayati | tathā ca vākpāruṣye svāyaṃbhuvam:

                    	śataṃ brāhmaṇam ākruśya kṣatriyo daṇḍam arhati |

                    	vaiśyo 'dhyardhaṃ śate dve vā śūdras tu vadham arhati || (MDh 8.267)

ity anena nikṛṣṭānāṃ yathotkarṣaṃ doṣātirekam āha | tathā:

                    	pañcāśad brāhmaṇo daṇḍyaḥ kṣatriyasyābhiśaṃsane |

                    	vaiśyasya cārdhapañcāśac chūdre dvādaśako damaḥ || (MDh 8.268)

iti yathāpakarṣam apakarṣaḥ | tathā:

                    	ekajātir dvijātiṃ tu vācā dāruṇayā vadan |

                    	jihvāyāḥ prāpnuyāc chedaṃ jaghanyaprabhavo hi saḥ || (MDh 8.270)

iti hetuvannigadenāpakṛṣṭānām utkṛṣṭahiṃsāṃ gurvīm āha | evam anyāny api daṇḍapāruṣyādiṣu vacanāny anusaraṇīyāni || 270 ||

 

_idānīm upapātakamadhyapāṭhāt strīvadhasya taduktaprāyaścittaprāptau satyāṃ kvacid apavādam āha |_

 

                    	**durvṛttabrāhmaṇakṣatraviṭchūdrastrīpamāpaṇe |**

**              	dṛtiṃ dhanur bastam aviṃ kramād dadyād viśuddhaye || 3.271 ||**

 

durvṛttāṃ brāhmaṇādisaṃbandhinīṃ striyaṃ hatvā kramaśo dṛtyādīni deyāni | dṛtir udakoddhāraṇārthaḥ kuruṇṭhaḥ | basto yuvā chāgaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat | durvṛttastrīpramāpaṇaṃ ca rājña eva vihitam | yathāha manuḥ saṃgraṇādhikāre:

                    	bhartāraṃ laṅghayed yā tu jñātistrīguṇadarpitā |

                    	tāṃ śvabhiḥ khādayed rājā saṃsthāne bahusaṃsthite || iti | (MDh 8.371)

gautame tu prāyaścittādhikāra evoktam: "śvabhiḥ khādayed rājā nihīnavarṇagamane striyaṃ prakāśaṃ pumāṃsaṃ ghātayet" iti (GDh 23.14–15) | ato rājña evaitat prāyaścittaṃ netarasya | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> rājño vihitānuṣṭhānāt prāyaścittam ayuktam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">yuktaṃ</span> ca, yathaiva sākṣiṇām anṛtābhidhāne:

                    	vāgdevatyaiś ca carubhir yajeraṃs te sarasvatīm | (MDh 8.105)

ity atra | etasmād eva prāyaścittābhidhānāj jñāyate strīvadhasyātyantikam akartavyatā | tathā cāmnāyo 'pi: "na ca vai striyaṃ ghnanti" iti | ata eva svāyaṃbhuve:

                    	bālaghnāṃś ca kṛtaghnāṃś ca viśuddhān api dharmataḥ |

                    	śaraṇāgatahantṝṃś ca strīhantṝṃs ca na saṃpibet || iti | (MDh 11.191)

ataś ca kāmakṛte strīvadhe prāyaścittābhava eva | akāmatas tu kathaṃcid daivād āpanne strīsvarūpāpekṣayā kratvarthadyapekṣayā hantṛgatānubandhāpekṣayā ca prāyaścittāni yojyāni | kecit tu bhartur avyavasthitastrīvadhe dṛtyādidānaṃ manyante | anye tu sārvatrikam eva | tat punar vicāryam || 271 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvad vyabhicāriṇyāṃ dṛtyādidānam uktvā idānīm avyabhicāriṇyām āha |_

 

                    	**apraduṣṭāṃ striyaṃ hatvā śūdrahatyāvrataṃ caret |**

**              	asthanvatāṃ sahasraṃ ca tathānasthimatām anaḥ || 3.272 ||**

 

apraduṣṭām avyabhicāriṇīṃ striyam akāmataḥ kathaṃcit dhatvā śūdrahatyāvrataṃ caret | vratacaraṇopadeśaś ca "dadyād dhenavo daśa" (YDh 3.270) ity asya vyāvṛttyartho vyākhyeyaḥ | etac cāpaśadastrīviṣayam eva:

                    	nikṛṣṭajāṃ tu nirjñātām utkṛṣṭāyāṃ ca mātari |

                    	aduṣṭāṃ yoṣitaṃ hatvā ṣaṇmāsān etad ācaret ||

iti bṛhaspativacanāt | etacchabdena ca tatra pūrvaślokāc chūdrahatyāvrataṃ sāṃvatsarikam uktam | itarāsu tu vāsiṣṭham: "anātreyīṃ rājanyahiṃsāyāṃ rājanyāṃ vaiśahiṃsāyāṃ vaiśyāṃ śūdrīhiṃsāyāṃ śūdrāṃ hatvā saṃvatsaram" iti (VaDh 20.37–40) | gautamīyam api śūdrāyām anātreyyām evātyantaguṇavatyāṃ vadhe draṣṭavyam "anātreyyāṃ caivam" (GDh 22.17) iti, vāsiṣṭḥānusārāt | yat tu mānavam: "kṛtvā ca strīsuhṛdvadham" (MDh 11.88) iti, tad āṅgirasavacanāt,

                    	āhitāgner dvijāgryasya hatvā patnīm aninditām |

                    	brahmahatyāvrataṃ kuryād ātreyīghnas tathaiva ca ||

ity etadviṣayam eva | śātātapoktaṃ tu yājñavalkīyena vaikalpikam | "strīghātī ṣaṇmāsān kṛcchram ācaret" iti śaṅkhoktasya gautamīyena samānaviṣayatvam | "strīṇāṃ vadhe śūdrahatyāvratam ādiśet" iti guṇātiśayāpekṣayā yojyam | pravṛttāsu tv aniṣpanne vyabhicāre 'nubandhaviśeṣāpekṣayopapātakaprāyaścittāni yojyāni | smṛtyantarāṇy apy anenaiva mārgeṇa vyākhyeyāni, yathā strīvadhe kṛcchratrayaṃ sumantunoktam | yathā cāṅgirase:

                    	anāhitāgnipatnīnāṃ tathā viṭkṣatrayoṣitām |

                    	goghātakavrataṃ kuryāc chūdrāṇāṃ caiva nityaśaḥ || iti |

saṃvarte tu:

                    	striyaṃ pramāpayed yas tu taptakṛcchraṃ samācaret | iti |

evam anyāny api mānasavācikādivyabhicārālocanayā yojyāni | evaṃ ślokapūrvārdhena,

                    	apraduṣṭāṃ striyaṃ hatvā śūdrahatyāvrataṃ caret |

ity uktvottarārdhena,

                    	asthanvatāṃ sahasraṃ ca tathānasthimatām anaḥ |

ity etad eva śūdrahatyāvratam uktam | yeṣāṃ sāsthikānāṃ prāṇināṃ vaiśeṣikaṃ noktam, teṣāṃ sahasraṃ hatvā ṣāṇmāsikaṃ śūdrahatyāvrataṃ kāryam | yāni cānasthikāni pipīlikādīni, teṣāṃ ca yāvanty anasā śakyante voḍhuṃ dvābhyāṃ balīvardābhyāṃ madhyamābhyām, tāvatparimāṇe syāt | "anasthnām anaḍudbhāre" (GDh 22.21) iti gautamasmaraṇād anogata evānaḍudbhāro gṛhyate, "pūrṇe cānasy anasthnām" (MDh 11.140) iti manuvacanāt | etac ca yāny ahiṃsakāni santi vyāpadyante anādiṣṭaviśeṣaṇāni ca, tadviṣayaṃ draṣṭavyam,

                    	yo 'hiṃsakāni bhūtāni hinasty ātmasukhecchayā |

                    	sa jīvaṃś ca mṛtaś caiva na kvacit sukham edhate || (MDh 5.45)

iti manuvacanāt | yāni tu hiṃsāsvabhāvāni yūkamaśakajalūkādīni, teṣāṃ yathāsāmarthyam apanīyamānānāṃ yadi vadho 'pi syāt tathāpy adoṣa eva | kāmatas tu yūkādiṣv apy asty eva doṣaḥ | tathā yāny apy asthimanty ādiṣṭaprāyaścittāni ca, nityopadravakāriṇaś ca sarpamūṣikaprabhṛtayaḥ, tadapanayanārthaṃ ca mārjārādisaṃgrahādiprakāreṇa vadho nirdoṣa eva | yāni ca saṃmārjanopalepanadhānyasaṃskārādinā hanyante, yāni cendhnādyanupraviṣṭāni maṇikādiṣu ca, tatrāpy adoṣa eva, vadhe karmasādhanatvena śarīradhāraṇāṅgatvena ca pravṛtteḥ | yeṣāṃ kāmabhogamātranibandhanaiva pravṛttis teṣāṃ tatrāpy asty eva doṣaḥ | tad etat "pañcasūnā gṛhasthasya" (MDh 3.68) ity atra svayaṃbhuvā pradarśitam | sahasragrahaṇam anograhaṇaṃ cātra bhūyastvopalakṣaṇārthaṃ na niyamārtham, arvāg ūrdhvaṃ ca prāyaścittāntarānupadeśād, hanyamānānāṃ ca samuccyopādāne hetvabhāvād ity eṣā dik || 272 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvat sāmānyenoktvādhunā keṣāṃcid vaiśeṣikāṇy āha |_

 

                    	**mārjāragodhānakulamaṇḍūkaśvapatatriṇaḥ |**

**              	hatvā tryahaṃ pibet kṣīraṃ kṛcchraṃ vā pādikaṃ caret || 3.273 ||**

 

svāyaṃbhuve tu kākolūkacāṣāṇām eva viśeṣopadeśaḥ (MDh 11.131) | so 'pi ca kratvarthaviṣayatayā pakṣimātropalakṣaṇārtho vyākhyeyaḥ, athāpi niyamārthaḥ | tathā kartvarthavadha eveti vyākhyātam etat | iha tv akratvartha eva trirātraṃ payobhakṣatā pādakṛcchraṃ veti vyākhyeyam | mānave 'pi ca:

                    	mārjāranakulau hatvā cāṣaṃ maṇḍūkam eva ca |

                    	śvagodholūkakākāṃś ca śūdrahatyāvrataṃ caret || (MDh 11.131)

ity uktvānantaram evoktam:

                    	payaḥ pibet trirātraṃ vā yojanaṃ vādhvano vrajet |

                    	upaspṛśet sravantyāṃ vā sūktaṃ vābdaivataṃ japet || iti | (MDh 11.132)

na caiṣāṃ śūdrahatyāvratena vaikalpikatvaṃ yuktam | ato yathoktaiva viṣayakalpanā | atrāpi ca snānādhvagamane kṣatriyavaiśyayoḥ, japas tu brāhmaṇasyaiva, "japyenaiva saṃsidhyed brāhmaṇaḥ" (MDh 2.87) iti vacanāt | payaḥpānapādakṛcchre tu śūdrasya | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

                    	anādiṣṭavratādeśe śūdraṃ tapasi yojayet |

                    	rājanyavaiśyau saṃskāre brāhmaṇaṃ japakarmaṇi || iti |

tathā:

                    	yajñārthaprāṇihiṃsāyāṃ kṣudrajantuvadheṣv api |

                    	pāpakṛtyāṃ vadanty ugrāṃ yajñād dhi jagataḥ sthitiḥ || iti |

evaṃ smṛtyantarāṇy api vyākhyeyāni | yathāhāṅgirāḥ:

                    	gaje vyāghre ca turage khaḍge kṛṣṇamṛge vṛke |

                    	siṃhe śuni varāhe ca mayūre pakṣiṇām api ||

                    	cāṣe bhāse ca śīghre ca ṭiṭṭibhe khañjarīṭake |

                    	yathā śūdre tathā vadhyā bhagavān aṅgirābravīt || iti |

kecit tu "yathā gavi tathā" ity evaṃ paṭhanti | sṛgālo 'pi mayūra ucyate,

                    	mayur mayūro gomāyuḥ sṛgālaś ceti śabditaḥ |

iti nāmaratnamālāvacanāt | tenoktaṃ "mayūre pakṣiṇām api" iti | apiśabdāt sṛgālo 'pīty arthaḥ | śīghraḥ śyenaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat | yāni tv ato 'tyalpatarāṇi tāny akratvarthānāṃ prāṇinām akāmavadhe vyākyeyāni | yathā pārāśare:

                    	haṃsaṃ sasārasaṃ krauñcaṃ cakravākaṃ sakukkuṭam |

                    	hatvā meṣamayūraṃ ca śudhyate naktabhojanāt ||

tathā:

                    	cāṣam bhāsaṃ kapotaṃ vā śārikāṃ tittiriṃ tathā |

                    	antarjale ubhe saṃdhye prāṇāyāmena śudhyati || (PSm 6.4)

tathā:

                    	gṛdhraṃ śyenaṃ śvāviḍaṃ ca kapotolūkaghātane |

                    	apakvāśī dinaṃ tiṣṭhed vilāle mārutāśanaḥ || (PSm 6.5)

                    	hatvā nakulamaṇḍūkasarpājagaraḍuṇḍubhān |

                    	kṛsaraṃ bhojayed vipraṃ lohadaṇḍaś ca dakṣiṇā || (PSm 6.9) iti |

tathā smṛtyantareṣv 'py uccāvacāny udāhṛtyānenaiva mārgeṇa yojyāni | yathā vāsiṣṭhe: "śvamārjāranakuladaharamūṣikān hatvā kṛcchraṃ dvādaśarātraṃ caret | kiṃcic ca dadyāt" iti (VaDh 21.24) | etat kratvarthahiṃsāyām eva kāmataḥ, itaratra vā gurutarānubandhe yojyam || 273 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvad mārjārādīnāṃ prāyaścittam uktam | idānīm anyeṣāṃ kratvarthānām eva vadhe āha |_

 

                    	**gaje nīlā vṛṣāḥ pañca śuke vatso dvihāyanaḥ |**

**              	kharājameṣeṣu vṛṣo deyaḥ krauñce trihāyanaḥ || 3.274 ||**

 

mānavenābhinnārthatvāt tatra ca prādhānyena kratvarthahiṃsāyā evādhikṛtatvāt "nipātya vaiśyaṃ vṛttastham" (MDh 11.129) iti vṛttasthaśabdasya yajñasthavacanatvād etad api tadviṣayatayaiva vyākhyeyam | spaṣṭam anyat || 274 ||

 

                    	**hatvā śyenakapikravyājjalasthalaśikhaṇḍinaḥ |**

**              	bhāsaṃ ca hatvā dadyād gām akravyādeṣu vatsikām || 3.275 ||**

 

kravyaṃ māṃsam ucyate | tad bhakṣayanti ye te kravyādāḥ | te ca kecij jale bakādayaḥ, kecit sthale gṛdhādayaḥ | śikhaṇḍī mayūraḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 275 ||

 

                    	**urageṣv āyaso daṇḍaḥ paṇḍake trapumāṣakaḥ |**

**              	kole ghṛtaghaṭo deya uṣṭre guñjā haye 'ṃśukam || 3.276 ||**

 

urageṣv iti bahuvacanaṃ ḍuṇḍubhādīnām api grahaṇārtham | paṇḍakaḥ ṣaṇḍaḥ | kolaḥ sūkaraḥ | guñjā kṛṣṇalaḥ | hayo ghoṭaḥ | aṃśukaṃ vastram | sarvatra prāyaścittaprakaraṇe vacanād vinā na parigrahakṛtaḥ kaścid viśeṣa ity etad govadha eva vyākhyātam | kecit tu paṇḍakam uragādhikārād gonasam āhuḥ | tatrāpi hi smaranti palālabhāram (MDh 11.133) || 276 ||

 

                    	**tittirau tu tiladroṇaṃ gajādīnām aśaknuvan |**

**              	dānaṃ dātuṃ caret kṛcchram ekaikasya viśuddhaye || 3.277 ||**

 

tittiriprakāreṣu sarveṣu kapiñjalakṛkaralāvakādiṣu tiladroṇa ekaikasya vadhe deyaḥ: "gaje nīlā vṛṣāḥ pañca" ity etasmād arabhya tittiriparyantānāṃ vadhe yathoktadānāśaktau prājāpatyaṃ pratyekaṃ caret | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecit</span> tv ata eva jñāpakāt sarvatra hiṃsāprakaraṇe dānasya prāthamakalpikatvaṃ manyante | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">tat tv ayuktam</span>, trapumāṣakārthe vṛṣapañcakārthe cāviśeṣeṇa kṛcchradarśanāt | na ca tat samuccitānām, ekaikasyeti vīpsopādānavaiyarthyāt | ataḥ śāstrasyāmīmāṃsyatvād gajādiṣv eva dānaprādhānyam, anyatra tu tapasa eveti sthitam | tathā cāha manuḥ:

                    	mahāpātakinaś caiva śeṣāś cākāryakāriṇaḥ |

                    	tapasaiva sutaptena mucyante kilbiṣāt tataḥ || iti | (MDh 11.239)

evakāraś ca prāthamakalpikatvaṃ sarvapāpeṣu tapasaḥ spaṣṭayati | tathā:

                    	dānena vadhanirṇekaṃ sarpādīnām aśaknuvan |

                    	ekaikaśaś caret kṛcchraṃ prājāpatyaṃ viśuddhaye || iti | (MDh 11.139)

atrāpi sarpādīnām eva dānāśaktau tapaḥ kāryam, anyatra tu tapasa evāśaktau dānam iti | sarvatra ca prāyaścittaprakaraṇe yasya tu dānaṃ coditaṃ tad anaupacārikaṃ draṣṭavyam || 277 ||

 

_sarvatraiva tv anuktaniṣkṛtyartham |_

 

                    	**kiṃcit sāsthivadhe deyaṃ prāṇāyāmas tv anasthike |**

**              	vṛkṣagulmalatāvīrucchedane japyam ṛkchatam || 3.278 ||**

 

kiṃcid ity aviśeṣābhidhānād atyantanikṛṣṭaṃ bhikṣāmātradānaṃ pratyetavyam | anubandhāpekṣayā cātirekakalpanā | spaṣṭam anyat || 278 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvat kartṛtvena kārayitṛtvena vā yatra pāpaprasaṅgaḥ, tatra prāyaścittany uktāni | adhunā atrānyakartṛke 'pi vyāpāre karmādibhāvam āpannasya pāpotpattiḥ prāyaścittaṃ ca, tad vaktum āha |_

 

                    	**puṃścalīvānarakharair daṣṭaś caiva śvavāyasaiḥ |**

**              	prāṇāyāmāñ jale kṛtvā ghṛtaṃ prāśya viśudhyati || 3.279 ||**

 

puṃścalī gaṇikā, viplutā yoṣid ity anye | vānarādayaḥ prasiddhāḥ | caśabdān nakhādivilikhitasyāpy etad eva prāyaścittam | evakārāc caikaikaśaḥ samuccite 'pīti gamyate | prāṇāyāmān iti bahuvacanaṃ śarīrapradeśāpekṣayā triprabhṛtiśataparyanteṣv aviśeṣeṇa vyākhyeyam | tathā ca śaṅkhaḥ: "naravāyasakharavānaraśvapuṃścalībhir daṣṭaḥ samudragāṃ nadīṃ gatvā prāṇāyāmaśataṃ kṛtvā ghṛtaprāśanena śudhyati" iti | atra cānādiṣṭaprāyaścittānāṃ śarīrapradeśāpekṣayaiva viṣayakalpanā | sarvatraiva ca yatra samantrakaṃ prāyaścittam āmnātam, tatra strīśudrayor api tad evāmantrakaṃ pratyetavyam || 279 ||

 

                    	**phalapuṣpānnarasajasattvaghāte ghṛtāśanaḥ |**

**              	syād oṣadhivṛthācchede kṣīrāśī go'nugo dinam || 3.280 ||**

 

badaraudumbarādiphaleṣu kṛmimaśakādīni sattvāni, tathā puṣpeṣu anne cāme pakve vā kāñcikādiṣu raseṣv anyeṣv apy evaṃprakāreṣu | ghṛtāśī ghṛtenaivaikarātravṛttiḥ | evaṃ vrīhyādyoṣadhīnāṃ vṛthācchedane ca kṣīravrato gavām ekadinam anugamanaṃ kuryāt || 280 ||

 

_suptasya jāgrato vā yad retaḥ skandet, tatra śaucam akṛtvaiva |_

 

                    	**yan me 'dya reta ity ābhyāṃ skannaṃ reto 'bhimantrya vā |**

**              	stanāntaraṃ bhruvor vāpi tenānāmikayā spṛśet || 3.281 ||**

 

vāśabdaḥ sparśanānumantraṇayor vikalpārthaḥ | "yan me 'dya retaḥ pṛthivīm askāt" "punar mām aitv indriyam" (BāU 6.4.5) ity etābhyāṃ śatapathādhītābhyām anumantrya tenānāmikayā kaniṣṭhāmadhyayor antareṇa stanau bhruvau vinimārjayet, na cānyac chaucaṃ kartavyam | atra ca śloke spaṣṭānabhidhānaṃ chandonurodhāt | yat tu smṛtyantare śaucopadeśaḥ, sa mantrānadhikṛtasyānabhijñasya vā pratyetavyaḥ || 281 ||

 

                    	**mayi teja iti chāyāṃ svāṃ dṛṣṭvāmbugatāṃ japet |**

**              	gāyatrīm aśucau dṛṣṭe cāpale 'thānṛte 'pi ca || 3.282 ||**

 

"mayi tejaḥ" (BāU 6.4.6) ity etad yajuḥ śatapathāmnātaṃ brāhmaṇasvareṇaiva japyam | spaṣṭam anyat || 282 ||

 

_upapātakimadhye 'vakīrṇino 'pi pāṭhāt prāyaścittāntaraṃ vaktum āha |_

 

                    	**avakīrṇī bhaved gatvā brahmacārī tu yoṣitam |**

**              	gardabhaṃ paśum ālabhya nairṛtaṃ sa viśudhyati || 3.283 ||**

 

upakurvāṇo naiṣṭhiko vā brahmacārī stryabhigamanād avakīrṇīty ucyate | sa ca nirṛtiṃ gardabheneṣṭvā smṛtyantaroktaṃ ca taccarmaṇā prāvṛto vrataṃ caritvā viśudhyati | "gardabhaṃ paśum ālabhya" ity etat kṛtsnaprayoganirvṛttyabhiprāyeṇaiva vyākhyeyam || 283 ||

 

_brahmacāry eva |_

 

                    	**bhaikṣāgnikārye tyaktvā tu saptarātram anāturaḥ |**

**              	kāmāvakīrṇa ity evaṃ hutvājyenāhutidvayam || 3.284 ||**

**              	upasthānaṃ tataḥ kuryāt saṃ mā siñcety anena tu |**

 

"kāmāvakīrṇo 'smi" "kāmabhidrugdho 'smi" (PārG 3.12.9) ity ābhyām ājyāhutidvayaṃ pākayajñavidhānena hutvā "saṃ mā siñcantu marutaḥ" (TĀ 2.18.1) ity etayā taittirīyakāmnātayarcā sūryam upasthāya śudhyati | arvāk tu saptarātrāt,

                    	saṃdhyāṃ yadi ca nopāste samidho vāpi nāhitāḥ |

                    	gāyatrīm āparaṃ kālaṃ japann eno vyapohati ||

ity evamādi smṛtyantaroktaṃ draṣṭavyam | idaṃ tu brahmacārivanasthaparivrājakānām aviśeṣeṇaiva prāyaścittam || 284–5b ||

 

                    	**madhumāṃsāśane kāryaḥ kṛcchraḥ śeṣavratāni ca || 3.285 ||**

 

yathāha manuḥ:

                    	vratacārī tu yo 'śnīyān madhu māṃsaṃ kathaṃcana |

                    	sa kṛtvā prākṛtaṃ kṛcchraṃ vrataśeṣaṃ samāpayet || iti | (MDh 11.158)

vrataśeṣaṃ tu prāyaścittakālātirekeṇa samāpanīyam | prākṛtaṃ kṛcchraṃ prājāpatyam eva | spaṣṭam anyat || 285cd ||

 

_guruś ca yadi svakāryeṇa brahmacāriṇaṃ kvacit preṣayet, tasya ca pravāsocitaṃ maraṇam syāt, tataḥ |_

 

                    	**kṛcchratrayaṃ guruḥ kuryān mriyeta prahito yadi |**

 

etac cānyasminn api vetanādyapekṣiṇy ājñākare draṣṭavyam ||

 

_śiṣyas tu śaktaḥ sann ājñātikramam anyad vā upaghātakāntarārambhi |_

 

                    	**pratikūlaṃ guroḥ kṛtvā taṃ prasādya viśudhyati || 3.286 ||**

 

smṛtyantarāc ca sacelaṃ snātveti | gurugrahaṇaṃ cātra sarvamānyoplakṣaṇatvena vyākhyeyam || 286 ||

 

_evaṃ tarhi preṣitavyāpattivad bheṣajādidāne 'pi vyāpattau doṣaḥ syād ity āśaṅkām apākartum āha |_

 

                    	**auṣadhānnapradānādyair bhiṣagyogādyupakramaiḥ |**

**              	kriyamāṇopakāre tu mṛte vipre na pātakam |**

**              	vipāke govṛṣādīnāṃ bhaiṣajyāgnikriyāsu ca || 3.287 ||**

 

sarvāṅgayantritasyāturasya bhiṣagbhir vaidyair ye chedanadāhādiyogā anekadhā kriyante, te bhiṣagyogāḥ | bhāvaśuddhyā kriyaṃāṇopakāre brāhmaṇe mṛte vaidyaparicārakacikitsākārayitṝṇāṃ snehādibhiś ca prabhūtasnigdhādyannadātṝṇāṃ ca nirdoṣatvam | tathā govṛṣādīnāṃ bhaiṣajyāgnidāhādinimittake vipāke saṃjāte tannimittake vā mṛtyau nirdoṣatvam | vipragograhaṇaṃ copalakṣaṇārtham || 287 ||

 

_bhaiṣajyānnapradānādiprabhave 'pi mṛtyau yadi dauṣṭyāt pāṇḍityābhimānād vā doṣavattām āropya brahmahā goghno vāyam ity evam |_

 

                    	**mahāpāpopapāpābhyāṃ yo 'bhiśaṃsen mṛṣā param |**

**              	abbhakṣo māsam āsīta sa jāpī niyatendriyaḥ || 3.288 ||**

 

paragrahaṇaṃ yadi kaścic chubhālutayātmānaṃ doṣavattayābhiśasya pariṣadi nivedayet, na tasya doṣa iti jñāpanārtham | jape cāviśeṣite 'pi śuddhavaty eva | yathāha vasiṣṭhaḥ: "brāhmaṇam anṛtenābhiśasya patanīyenopapatanīyena vā māsam abbhakṣaḥ śuddhavatīr āvartayet" iti (VaDh 23.39) | atra cāviśeṣābhidhāne 'pi nimittavaiṣamyān mahāpatanīyābhiśaṃsane yathoktam | upapatanīye tu niyatendriyo japann āsīteti vyākhyeyam | spaṣṭam anyat || 288 ||

 

_abhiśaṃsakasyoktam | yas tv asāv abhiśastaḥ, saḥ |_

 

                    	**abhiśasto mṛṣā kṛcchraṃ cared āgneyam eva vā |**

**              	nirvapeta puroḍāśaṃ vāyavyaṃ paśum eva vā || 3.289 ||**

 

puroḍāśapaśvor āhitāgniviṣayatvaṃ nimittānurūpyeṇa vyākhyeyam | kṛcchraṃ tv anyeṣām | idaṃ cābhiśastasya gehadāhādiṣv iva naimittikam, na tu doṣanirghātārtham, doṣe pramāṇābhāvāt | janmāntarīyadoṣānumānakalpanā tu śarīropādānād evāgnihotrādiṣv apy aviśiṣṭā | yat tu vāsiṣṭham: "etenābhiśasto vyākhyātaḥ" (VaDh 23.37) iti, tad yatra kaścit kaṃcid uddiśyānyāyena gṛhītasvaḥ svayaṃ prāṇāṃs tyajati, tadviṣayaṃ vyākhyeyam, na hi tatrānṛtābhiśasta iti viśeṣaṇopādānaṃ yataḥ | idaṃ tu "abhiśasto mṛṣā kṛcchram" iti viśeṣitatvād yathoktaiva vyavasthā || 289 ||

 

                    	**aniyukto bhrātṛjāyāṃ gacchaṃś cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret |**

**              	trirātrānte ghṛtaṃ prāśya gatvodakyāṃ viśudhyati || 3.290 ||**

 

niyuktād yo 'nyaḥ so 'niyuktaḥ | na cānyaḥ kaścit tathāvidho 'sti | ato niyogakālād ṛtukālalakṣaṇād anyadā sa evāniyuktaḥ pratyetavyaḥ | bhrātṛjāyā ca brāhmaṇasyāpi kṣatriyā bhavaty eva | anyasyāṃ tu sodaryabhrātṛjāyāyāṃ gurutalpaprāyaścittam eva | udakyāṃ tu trirātrānte caturthe 'hani gatvā ghṛtaprāśanam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye</span> tūdakyāgamane trirātropoṣitas trirātrānte ghṛtaṃ prāśya viśudhyatīty evaṃ vyācakṣate | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">tat tv ayuktam</span>, rajasvalāgamane sāntapanasya manunoktatvād (MDh 11.173) ihāpi rajasvalāmukhāsvādopalakṣitasyābhigamanasyaiva surāpānasāmyopadeśāt | ato yathoktaiva vyākhyā jyāyasī || 290 ||

 

_idānīṃ śūdrād anyasmād vā pāpakāriṇaḥ pratigrahe prāyaścittam āha |_

 

                    	**goṣṭhe vasan brahmacārī māsam ekaṃ payovrataḥ |**

**              	gāyatrījāpanirato mucyate 'satpratigrahāt || 3.291 ||**

 

asataḥ śūdrāder apratigrāhyasya vābhiśastāder yaḥ pratigraḥ so 'satpratigrahaḥ | gāyatrījāpaniratatvaṃ cānvahaṃ trisāhasro japaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat | tathā ca mānavam:

                    	japtvā tu trīṇi sāvitryāḥ sahasrāṇi samāhitaḥ |

                    	māsaṃ goṣṭhe payaḥ pītvā mucyate 'satpratigrahāt || iti | (MDh 11 194)

pratyahaṃ ca trisāhasro japaḥ payovratatvaṃ ceti || 291 ||

 

_idānīṃ vrātyayājakasyābhicarataś ca prāyaścittam āha |_

 

**              	trīn kṛcchrān ācared vrātyayājako 'bhicarann api |**

**              	vedaplāvī yavāśy abdaṃ tyaktvā ca śaraṇāgatam || 3.292 ||**

 

viśyudhyatīti śeṣaḥ | apiśabdād yaś cābhicarato yājakaḥ | yavānnabhojanaṃ yavāśitā | spaṣṭam anyat || 292 ||

 

                    	**prāṇāyāmāṃś caret snātvā kharayānoṣṭrayānagaḥ |**

**              	nagnaḥ snātvā ca suptvā ca gatvā caiva divā striyam || 3.293 |**

 

kharair yuktaṃ yānaṃ kharayānam, tathaivoṣṭrair yuktam uṣṭrayānam | prāṇāyāmās trayaḥ | anubandhābhyāsādyapekṣayā tadabhyāsakalpanā | spaṣṭam anyat || 293 ||

 

                    	**guruṃ tvaṃkṛtya huṃkṛtya vipraṃ nirjitya vādataḥ || 3.294 ||**

**              	hatvāvabadhya vā kṣipraṃ prasādyopavased dinam |**

 

guruṃ pitrādikaṃ mānyaṃ tvam ity evaṃprakāraṃ mānarahitam ābhāṣya, brāhmaṇaṃ vā niraprādhinaṃ huṃkārādinā nirbhartsya vā, vivāde vā laukike vinirjitya krodhātiśayād vā paribhavamātrakaraṇāya hastādinā hatvā avabadhya vā vastrādyākarṣaṇādinā, kṣipraṃ prasādya naktaṃ bhuñjīta upavased vā | anubandhādyapekṣayā tv abhojanābhyāsaḥ || 294 ||

 

_yadi tu vadhabuddhyaiva krodhād brāhmaṇāya daṇḍodyamanādi kuryāt, tataḥ |_

 

                    	**vipradaṇḍodyame kṛcchras tv atikṛcchro nipātane || 3.295 ||**

**              	kṛcchrātikṛcchro 'sṛkpāte kṛcchro 'bhyantaraśoṇite |**

 

"kṛcchrātikṛcchraḥ payasā divasān ekaviṃśatim" (YDh 3.323) iti vakṣyamāṇaḥ | yad vā kṛcchrasahito 'tikṛcchraḥ kṛcchrātikṛcchraḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 295 ||

 

_sarvatraiva prāyaścittaprakaraṇe 'dhikāryapekṣayaiva |_

 

                    	**deśaṃ kālaṃ vayaḥ śaktiṃ pāpaṃ cāvekṣya yatnataḥ |**

**              	prāyaścittaṃ prakalpyaṃ syād yatra coktā na niṣkṛtiḥ || 3.296 ||**

 

sarvathādhikṛtasāmarthyādyapekṣayā gurūṇāṃ laghūnāṃ ca prāyaścittānāṃ viṣayakalpanam, na tu prakārāntareṇety abhiprāyaḥ | yatra ca nindārthavādādinā lokavyavahāraprātilomyena vā doṣavattā jñātā, na ca prāyaścittaṃ viśeṣataḥ kiṃcid āmnātam, tatra smṛtyantropadiṣṭānāṃ japādīnām evādhikṛtasāmarthyānuguṇyena prāyaścittakalpanā | spaṣṭam anyat || 296 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvad uktaniṣkṛtīnām anuktaniṣkṛtīnāṃ ca prāyaścittāvagamaprakāra uktaḥ | yadi tu kaścin nāstikyān na prāyaścittaṃ kuryāt, sa ca paribhāṣya bhūyobhūyaḥ parityājya eva | tasya ca tathāvidhasya nāstikyātiśayād durātmanaḥ patitasyodakacchedam anena prakāreṇa kartum |_

 

                    	**dāsīghaṭam apāṃ pūrṇaṃ ninayeran svabāndhavāḥ |**

**              	patitasya bahiṣkuryuḥ sarvakāryeṣu caiva tam || 3.297 ||**

 

dāsīgṛhāt tadīyānām evāpāṃ pūrṇaṃ ghaṭam ānīya bahir grāmād dakṣiṇāṃ diśaṃ niṣkramya sarvajñātiguruśiṣyartviksamakṣaṃ sapiṇḍasamānodakāḥ padā viparyasyānavekṣamāṇā gṛhān etya ekarātraṃ kṣapayeyuḥ | sarvakāryeṣu ca dṛṣṭādṛṣṭanibandhaneṣu taṃ bahiṣkuryuḥ | tathā cāha manuḥ:

                    	patitasyodakaṃ chedyaṃ sapiṇḍair bāndhavair bahiḥ |

                    	nindite 'hani sāyāhne śiṣyartviggurusaṃnidhau || (MDh 11.182)

ityādi || 297 ||

 

_yad vā tyakto 'sau paścāttāpāt prāyaścittaṃ karoti, tatas tadā tasmin |_

 

                    	**caritavrata āyāte ninayeran navaṃ ghaṭam |**

**              	jugupseyur na cāpy enaṃ saṃpibeyuś ca sarvaśaḥ || 3.298 ||**

 

spaṣṭārthaḥ ślokaḥ | tathā ca manuḥ:

                    	caritavrata āyāte pūrṇaṃ kumbham apāṃ navam |

                    	tenaiva sārdhaṃ prāsyeyuḥ snātvā puṇye jalāśaye || (MDh 11.186)

ityādi || 298 ||

 

_yaś caiṣa ghaṭāpavarjanādiko vidhir uktaḥ patitānām |_

 

                    	**eṣa eva vidhiḥ strīṇāṃ patitānāṃ prakīrtitaḥ |**

**              	vāso gṛhāntike deya annaṃ vāsaḥ sarakṣaṇam || 3.299 ||**

 

strīṇāṃ patitānāṃ prāyaścittam akurvatīnāṃ eṣa eva ghaṭāpavarjanavidhiḥ prakarṣeṇa manvādibhiḥ kīrtito vihitaḥ | ayaṃ tu viśeṣaḥ: yadā tāḥ prāyaścittānuṣṭhāne pravartante, tadā tāsāṃ svagṛhasamīpe nivāsa āvasatho deyaḥ, annaṃ ca bhojanaṃ prāyaścittānuguṇyena deyam, vāsaś ca parivānaṃ saha rakṣaṇena iti | tathā ca svāyaṃbhuvam:

                    	eṣa eva vidhiḥ kāryo yoṣitsu patitāsv api |

                    	vastrānnam āsāṃ deyaṃ tu vaseyuś ca gṛhāntike || iti | (MDh 11.188)

viśeṣapatanīyeṣu parityāga evety evamarthaḥ pūrvatrāmnātasyāpi punaḥ pāṭhaḥ || 299 ||

 

                    	**nīcābhigamanaṃ garbhapātanaṃ bhartṛhiṃsanam |**

**              	viśeṣapatanīyāni strīṇām etāny api dhruvam || 3.300 ||**

 

apiśabdaḥ strīṇām apīty evaṃ yojyam, na mṛduhṛdayatā kāryā kathaṃ striyaḥ parityajyanta iti | etāni hi strīṇām api dhruvaṃ niścitaṃ viśeṣapatanīyāni parityāgakāraṇānīty abhiprāyaḥ || 300 ||

 

_yathaiva ca nīcābhigamanādiṣu strīṇām ātyantikaḥ parityāgaḥ, tathaiva ca |_

 

                    	**śaraṇāgatabālastrīhiṃsakān saṃpiben na tu |**

**              	cīrṇavratān api sataḥ kṛtaghnasahitān imān || 3.301 ||**

 

na caitan nindārthaṃ vacanam, asaṃvyavahāryā eva śaraṇāgatādihantāraś cīrṇaprāyaścittā apīty evamarthatvād upadeśasya | prāyaścittopadeśāt tu janmāntare nirdoṣā evety avaseyam || 301 ||

 

_na kevalaṃ śaraṇāgatahantrādayo 'saṃvyavahāryāḥ, anye 'pi | yeṣāṃ ghaṭāpavarjanaṃ kṛtaṃ te 'pi hi kṛtaprāyaścittāḥ punar nave ghaṭe 'psu prakṣipte 'pi gobhir asatkṛtā saṃvyavahāryā ity etad darśayitum āha |_

 

                    	**ghaṭe 'pavarjite jñātimadhyasthaḥ prathamaṃ gavām |**

**              	pradadyād yavasam gobhiḥ satkṛtasya sahakriyā || 3.302 ||**

 

kāryeti śeṣaḥ | gobhir yavasabhakṣaṇaṃ gosatkāraḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 302 ||

 

_evaṃ tāvat prakhyātapāpānāṃ prāyaścittāny abhidhāyādhunā rahasyaprāyaścittāni prastotum āha |_

 

                    	**vikhyātadoṣaḥ kurvīta parṣadānumataṃ vratam |**

**              	anabhikhyātadoṣas tu rahasyaṃ vratam ācaret || 3.303 ||**

 

tathā cāha manuḥ:

                    	etair dvijātayaḥ śodhyā vratair āviṣkṛtainasaḥ |

                    	anāviṣkṛtapāpās tu mantrair homaiś ca śodhanaiḥ || iti | (MDh 11.226)

dvijātayo 'py āviṣkṛtainasaḥ pariṣadā prāyaścittārthaṃ kṛtopasadanāḥ śodhyāḥ | ye tv anāviṣkṛtainaso dvijātayaḥ śrutismṛtyarthatattvajñāś ca, te pariṣady anivedyaiva vakṣyamāṇair aghamarṣaṇādimantrajapaiḥ śākalādibhiś ca homaiḥ śodhanārtham upadiṣṭaiḥ svayam evātmānaṃ śodhayeur ity abhiprāyaḥ | aviduṣām advijātīnāṃ cānaviṣkṛtainasām apy uparitanaḥ ślokārambho mānava eva:

                    	khyāpanenānutāpena tapasādhyayanena ca |

                    	pāpakṛn mucyate pāpāt tathā dānena cāpadi || iti | (MDh 11.227)

rahasyaṃ vrataṃ pārśvasthair apy aviditaṃ dharmavyājādinā kartavyam | yat tu smṛtyantaram:

                    	dharmavyājena yo mohāt prāyaścittaṃ samācaret |

                    	na tasya tena śuddhiḥ syād enasvī cādhikaṃ bhavet ||

iti, tad āviṣkṛtapāpaviṣayaṃ draṣṭavyam | na cātraitac codyam: kim ity anāviṣkṛtainasām alpaṃ prāyaścittam iti | amīmāṃsyatvāc chāstrasya | vidvattayaiva ca tasyainasā saṃbandhābhāvāt | tathā ca "vedābhāsarataṃ kṣāntam" (YDh 3.313) ityādi vakṣyaty eva | ātmaśuddhipradhānatvāc ca pravṛtter yuktam eva prāyaścittālpatvam | rahasyaprakāraś ca lokataḥ | vidvān avidvatsaṃnidhau prakāśam api pāpaṃ kṛtvā svayam eva vetti, itare tv anena pāpaṃ kṛtam ity evaṃ na jānanti, tat prakāśakṛtam api rahasyam eva | evaṃ deśakālādinimittenāpy aprijñānena rahasyatā yojyā || 303 ||

 

_evaṃ rahasyaprāyaścittānāṃ viṣayam uktvādhunā tāny upadiśati |_

 

                    	**trirāropoṣito japtvā brahmahā tv aghamarṣaṇam |**

**              	antarjale viśudhyeta dattvā gāṃ ca payasvinīm || 3.304 ||**

 

trirātam upoṣyāntarjale nimagno 'ghamarṣaṇaṃ japtvā gāṃ ca payasvinīṃ brāhmaṇāya dattvā viśudhyatīty evaṃ yojanā | anye tu trirātropoṣito 'ntarjale 'ghamarṣaṇaṃ japtvā viśudhyeta, gāṃ ca payasvinīṃ dattvā viśudhyeta, ity evaṃ prāyaścittadvayaṃ varṇayanti | tathā ca sati pūrvaṃ caturṇām apy āśramāṇāṃ prāyaścittam, uttaraṃ tu dānādhikṛtānām eveti mahāviṣayatāpi śāstrasyābhyuccayāya syāt | tathā ca svayaṃbhuvā dānarahitam eva trirātropoṣitasyāghamarṣaṇaṃ japyam uktam:

                    	tryahaṃ tūpavased yuktas trir ahno 'bhyavayann apaḥ |

                    	mucyate pātakaiḥ sarvair japtvā trir aghamarṣaṇam || iti | (MDh 11.259)

ato bedakalpanāpi yuktaiva || 304 ||

 

_sāgnikasya tu brāhmaṇavadhe pūrvavaikalpikatvena prāyaścittāntaram āha |_

 

                    	**lomabhyaḥ svāheti hi vā divasaṃ mārutāśanaḥ|**

**              	jale suptvābhijuhuyāc catvāriṃśad ghṛtāhutīḥ || 3.305 ||**

 

divasaṃ mārutāśana ity udakapānapratiṣedhārtham | anyatrāpy evaṃ vyākhyeyam | jale suptveti rātim udake tiṣṭhed ity arthaḥ | tataḥ pākayajñavidhānenaupāsane lomabhyaḥ svāhetyādibhiḥ (VS 39.10) śukriyādhitaiś catvāriṃśad ājyāhurīr juhuyāt || 305 ||

 

_surāpasvarṇahārinos tu |_

 

                    	**trirāropoṣito hutvā kūśmāṇḍībhir ghṛtaṃ śuciḥ |**

**              	surāpaḥ svarṇahārī tu rudrajāpo jale sthitaḥ || 3.306 ||**

 

kūśmāṇḍībhiḥ "yad devā devaheḍanam" (TB 2.4.4.8) ity evamādhyābhis taitttirīyāmnātābhis trirātropoṣitaḥ surāpaḥ pūrvavad ghṛtaṃ hutvā śuciḥ syāt | svarṇahārī tu trirātropoṣita eva nābhimātre jale tiṣṭhan rudraṃ (VS 16.1) japañ śucir iti yojyam | tathā ca bhāradvājaḥ:

                    	nābhidadhnodakasthas tu rudraṃ dhyāyan samāhitaḥ |

                    	triratropoṣito japtvā svarṇahārī viśudhyati || iti || 306 ||

 

_trirātropoṣita eva pūrvavat |_

 

                    	**sahasraśīṣā(di)jāpāc chudhyeta gurutalpagaḥ |**

**              	gaur deyā karmaṇaś cānte pṛthag ebhiḥ payasvinī || 3.307 ||**

 

"sahasraśīrṣā puruṣḥ" (RV 10.90) itīmam ṣoḍaśarcaṃ japtvā gurutalpagaḥ śudhyet | ebhiś ca "lomabhyaḥ svāhā" (VS 30.10) ity ārabhya puruṣasūktajapāntakarmādhikṛtair homakarmaṇo japakarmaṇaś cānte brāhmaṇāya payasviṇī gaur deyā pṛthak caikaikapātakoddeśena | homādyanadhikṛtair api triratram upoṣya gaur deyā | sarvatra ca rahasyaprakaraṇe na kāmakṛtādyapekṣayā viṣayavyavasthā kalpanīyā | svarucivaikalpikatvenaiva tu vyavasthā sāmarthyakṛtā vā, yathā homacodanāsv agnimatām | prakāśaprāyaścittānāṃ tu viṣayavyavasthā pradarśitaiva | rahasyeṣu tv ātmatuṣṭir eva jñānāgnidagdhakalmaṣasya śuddhikāraṇam | tathā ca rahasyeṣv eva svayaṃbhuvābhihitam:

                    	yasmin karmaṇy asya kṛte manasaḥ syād alāghavam |

                    	tasmiṃs tāvat tapaḥ kuryād yāvat tuṣṭikaraṃ bhavet || iti | (MDh 11.233)

ātmatuṣṭir eva gurulaghutvopādāne vyavasthāhetutvam uktam | itaratra tu pariṣacchāstropadiṣṭhaṃ gurulaghutvādyālocyopadiśet, na tu tatrātmatuṣṭer vyavasthāhetutvam || 307 ||

 

_evaṃ caturṇāṃ mahāpātakānām uktam | tatsaṃsarge tu |_

 

                    	**prāṇāyāmaśataṃ kuryāt sarvapāpāpanuttaye |**

**              	upapātakajātānām anirdiṣṭasya caiva hi || 3.308 ||**

 

sarvapāpāpanuttaya ity aviśeṣābhidhāne 'pi prakramānusārāt sarvair mahāpātakibhir yat saṃsarganimittaṃ pāpam, tadapanuttaye ity evaṃ vyākhyeyam | na kevalaṃ saṃsargajānāṃ sarvapāpānām, upapātakajātānām apy etad eva prāyaścittam | anirdiṣṭaprāyaścittāntarāṇām apy etad eveti yojyam || 308 ||

 

                    	**oṃkārābhiṣutaṃ somasalilaṃ pāvanaṃ pibet |**

**              	kṛtopavasanaṃ retoviṇmūtraprāśane dvijaḥ || 3.309 ||**

 

ahorātram upoṣyāparedur oṃkāreṇa somam abhiṣutya pāvanena tīrthodakena tatas tad oṃkārābhijñātaṃ somasalilaṃ pāvanaṃ pibed iti yojyam | spaṣṭam anyat | dvijagrahaṇaṃ brāhmaṇartham, itarayoḥ somapānapratiṣedhāt | advijāter vā rahasyaprāyaścittānadhikārajñāpanārtham || 309 ||

 

_yat tu kartrā svayam apy asaṃcetitaṃ, tac chāstrīyaśrautasmārtanityakarmānuṣṭhātṝṇāṃ naiva doṣārambhakaṃ bhavatīty evaṃ prapañcayitum āha |_

 

                    	**niśāyāṃ vā divā vāpi yad ajñānakṛtaṃ tv agham |**

**              	triṣkālasaṃdhyākaraṇāt tat sarvaṃ vipraṇaśyati || 3.310 ||**

 

kṛtavyākhyānaḥ ślokaḥ || 310 ||

 

                    	**śukriyāraṇyakajapo gāyatryāś ca sahasraśaḥ |**

**              	sarvapāpaharaḥ prokto rudraikādaśinī tathā || 3.311 ||**

 

ādiṣṭaprāyaścittāntarāṇām anādiṣṭaprāyaścittānāṃ sarveṣāṃ mahāpātakādīnāṃ rahasyānāṃ śukriyo japa āraṇyako vā sakṛtkṛta eva prāyaścittam | gāyatryās tu sahasrakṛtvaḥ | rudrādhyāyasya caikādaśakṛtvaḥ | āraṇyakaṃ brāhmaṇam | śukriyā mantrāḥ || 311 ||

 

_sarvatra ca rahasye prāyaścitte kṛte 'pi |_

 

                    	**yatra yatra ca saṃkīrṇam ātmānaṃ manyate dvijaḥ |**

**              	tatra tatra tilair homaḥ sāvitryā japa eva vā || 3.312 ||**

 

kārya iti śeṣaḥ | dvijagrahaṇam uktārtham || 312 ||

 

_rahasyāni vā prakāśāni vā yāny avijñātāni tāni |_

 

                    	**vedābhyāsarataṃ kṣāntaṃ pañcayajñakriyāratam |**

**              	na spṛśantīha pāpāni mahāpātakajāny api || 3.313 ||**

 

spaṣṭārthaḥ slokaḥ || 313 ||

 

_yaś caivaṃ vedābhyāsarataḥ, sa rahasye prakāśe vā kathaṃcid akāmakṛte |_

 

                    	**vāyubhakṣo divā tiṣṭhan rātriṃ nītvāpsu sūryadṛk |**

**              	japtvā sahasraṃ gāyatryāḥ śudhyed brahmavadhād ṛte || 3.314 ||**

 

yat tu viduṣaḥ prāyaścittabhūyastvam, tat kāmakṛtaprakāśaviṣayaṃ draṣṭavyam | vāyubhakṣavacanam udakapānapratiṣedhārtham | tiṣṭhan rātriṃ nītveti ca yojyam | spaṣṭam anyat || 314 ||

 

_rahasyādyadhikṛtānāṃ sarvaprāyaścittān vācayatvena |_

 

                    	**brahmacaryaṃ dayā kṣāntir dhyānaṃ satyam akalkatā |**

**              	ahiṃsāsteyam adroho damaś caite yamāḥ smṛtāḥ || 3.315 ||**

 

prakāśaprāyaścittādhikṛtānām apy avirodhād ete yamāḥ pratyetavyāḥ || 315 ||

 

_pūrvavad eva |_

 

                    	**snānamaunopavāsejyāsvādhyāyopasthanigrahāḥ**

**              	niyamā guruśuśrūṣā śaucākrodhapradātṛtāḥ || 3.316 ||**

 

brahmacaryaṃ yathāśāstraṃ maithunaprasaṅgaḥ | upasthanigrahaḥ stryanabhilāṣa iti vivekaḥ | pradātṛtā tu prakarṣeṇa dānaśīlatā | spaṣṭam anyat || 316 ||

 

_adhunā sarvapāpakṣapaṇārthāny abhyudayasādhanāni ca yāni sāntapanādīni tapāṃsi tatra tatra ca prāyaścittārtham upadiṣṭāni, teṣāṃ svarūpaṃ vaktum āha |_

 

                    	**pañcagavyaṃ tu gokṣīraṃ dadhi mūtraṃ śakṛd ghṛtam |**

**              	pītvā paredyūpavaset kṛcchraṃ sāntapanaṃ caran || 3.317 ||**

 

pañcagavyavacanam atrānuktakuśodakānvitaṃ ca yathā syād ity evamartham | gokṣīram iti tv aciradugdhopādānārtham | bhojanāya caitat prāśanam, nādṛṣṭāya | kṛcchram iti kṛcchradharmaprāptyartham | tathā ca hārītaḥ: "dhāroṣṇaṃ tu gavyaṃ payo dadhiśakṛnmūtraghṛtāni ca mantrapūtāny ekakālaṃ bhuktvā paredyur upavaset sa sānpatanaḥ" iti || 317 ||

 

_etair eva kṣīrādibhiḥ |_

 

                    	**pṛthak sāntapanadravyaiḥ ṣaḍahaḥ sopavāsakaḥ |**

**              	saptāhena tu kṛcchro 'yaṃ mahāsāntapanaḥ smṛtaḥ || 3.318 ||**

 

pṛthak sāntapanadravyaiḥ kṣīrādibhiḥ kuśodakāntaiḥ ṣaḍahāny ekakālaṃ bhojanaṃ kāryam | kuśodakaṃ ca kuśakvāthitam udakaṃ sarvatra pratyetavyam | spaṣṭam anyat || 318 ||

 

                    	**parṇodumbararājīvabilvapatrakuśodakaiḥ |**

**              	pratyekaṃ pratyahābhyastaiḥ parṇakṛcchra udāhṛtaḥ || 3.319 ||**

 

parṇaḥ palāśaḥ | rājīvaṃ padminī | spaṣṭam anyat | palāśādipatrakvathitenodakena pañcarātraṃ vartitavyam ity arthaḥ | yady api ca parṇakṛcchrasya kvacid viniyogo noktaḥ, tathāpy anādeśe pāpagurutvāpekṣayā pratyetavyaḥ | abhyudayasādhanatvaṃ tu vakṣyaty eva || 319 ||

 

                    	**taptakṣīraghṛtāmbūnām ekaikaṃ pratyahaṃ pibet |**

**              	ekarātropavāsaś ca taptakṛcchra udāhṛtaḥ || 3.320 ||**

 

smṛtyantare tu: "payo ghṛtam udakaṃ vāyuṃ pratyahaṃ taptāni, sa kṛcchaḥ" (GDh 23.2) ity uktam | tatra vyākhyātāro vāyor apy uṣṇasya pānaṃ varṇayanti | tat punar vicāryam | iha tūpavāsavacanād vāyūpādānaṃ tatropavāsapratipattyartham, na taptānīty anena saṃbandhayitum iti vyākhyeyam || 320 ||

 

                    	**ekabhaktena naktena tathaivāyācitena ca |**

**              	upavāsena caikena pādakṛcchraḥ prakīrtitaḥ || 3.321 ||**

 

prājāpatyasya cāyaṃ tṛtīye bhāge pādakṛcchraśabdaḥ prayuktaḥ | parṇakṛcchrādiṣv apy ayam evānusartavyaḥ | spaṣṭam anyat || 321 ||

 

                    	**yathākathaṃcit triguṇaḥ prājāpatyo 'yam ucyate |**

**              	ayam evātikṛcchraḥ syāt pāṇipūrānnabhojinaḥ || 3.322 ||**

 

yathākathaṃcid ity ekabhaktādikramasyāvivakṣārtham | etad api parṇakṛcchrādiṣv apy uktaṃ draṣṭavyam | eṣv eva prājāpatyārtheṣu bhojanakāleṣu pāṇipūrānnabhojinaḥ kartur ayam evātikṛcchrasaṃjñaḥ pratyetavyaḥ | pāṇiḥ pūryate yāvān annena tat pāṇipūrānnam, tad bhuṅkte yaḥ sa pāṇipūrānnabhojī | bhojanādhikārāc ca bhojanārthaṃ yāvat sakṛd ādīyate, tāvat pratyetavyam | tathā cāha manuḥ: "ekaikaṃ grāsam āśnīyāt" (MDh 11.213) iti || 322 ||

 

                    	**kṛcchātikṛcchraḥ payasā divasān ekaviṃśatim |**

**              	dvādaśāhopavāsena parākaḥ parikīrtitaḥ || 3.323 ||**

 

ekaviṃśatirātraṃ payovratatā kṛchrātikṛcchraḥ | dvādaśarātram abhojanaṃ parākaḥ | atra ca pādādibhāgābhāvaḥ || 323 ||

 

                    	**piṇyākācāmatakrāmbusaktūnāṃ prativāsaram |**

**              	ekaikam upavāsaś ca kṛcchraḥ saumyo 'yam ucyate || 3.324 ||**

 

piṇyākaḥ khalaḥ | ācāma odanāsrāvaṇam, maṇḍa iti yāvat | takraṃ mathitam | ambusaktava udakasaktavaḥ | eṣām ekaikena pratyaham | pañcame 'hany upavāsa ity eṣa saumyo nāma kṛcchraḥ | somasyātrārṣam iti saumyaḥ | evaṃ prājāpatyādiṣv apy ārṣeyanimittaivākhyā pratyetavyā || 324 ||

 

_ya ete piṇyākādayaḥ |_

 

                    	**eṣāṃ trirātram abhyāsād ekaikasya yathākramam |**

**              	tulāpuruṣa ity eṣa jñeyaḥ pañcadaśāhnikaḥ || 3.325 ||**

 

tulāpuruṣasaṃjñā mahāpātakādibhiḥ pāpair yuktaḥ puruṣo 'nena tapasā tulitaḥ pāpebhyo 'dhikatayā dharma evāvatiṣṭhate ity evamarthā | spaṣṭam anyat || 325 ||

 

                    	**tithivṛddhyācaret piṇḍāñ śukle śikhyaṇḍasaṃmitān |**

**              	ekaikaṃ hrāsayet piṇḍān kṛṣṇe cāndrāyaṇaṃ caran || 3.326 ||**

 

tithivṛddhyeti | śuklapakṣādau pratipatprabhṛti grāsopacayena pūrṇamāsā[^20] yāvad ācared aśnīyād ity arthaḥ | tataḥ pratipady api pañcadaśaiva grāsān bhuktvā dvitīyāprabhṛty ekaikaṃ grāsaṃ kṛṣṇapakṣe hrāsayet | etad yavamadhyaṃ cāndrāyaṇam | spaṣṭam anyati || 326 ||

 

                    	**yathākathaṃcit piṇḍānāṃ catvāriṃśac chatadvayam |**

**              	māsenaivopabhuñjīta cāndrāyaṇam athāparam || 3.327 ||**

 

yathākathaṃcid iti "pipīlikāmadhyatayā aṣṭagrāsena śiśucāndrāyaṇaprakāreṇa vā" iti smṛtyantarokacāndrāyṇaprakāropasaṃgrahaṇārtham | "catvāriṃśac chatadvayam" iti yavamadhyeṣu pratipady api pañcadaśagrāsaprāptyartham, "cāndrāyaṇam athāparam" iti | vāśabdādhyāhāreṇa atha vānya evāyaṃ cāndrāyaṇaprakāropadeśa ity arthaḥ || 327 ||

 

_yāny etāni sāntapanādīni kṛcchrāṇy uktāni, eṣām ekaikam |_

 

                    	**kuryāt triṣavaṇasnāyī kṛcchraṃ cāndrāyaṇaṃ tathā |**

**              	pavitrāṇi japet piṇḍaṃ gāyatryā cābhimantrayet || 3.328 ||**

 

nigadoktaḥ ślokaḥ || 328 ||

 

                    	**anādiṣṭeṣu pāpeṣu śuddhiś cāndrāyaṇena tu |**

**              	dharmārthaṃ yaś cared etac candrasyaiti salokatām || 3.329 ||**

 

yāni pariṣadā nādiśyante, tāny anādiṣṭāni, rahasyānīty arthaḥ | prāyaścittāntaraṃ vā yeṣv anādiṣṭaṃ tāny anādiṣṭāni | yas tu nirdoṣa eva dharmārthaṃ cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret, sa candrasya salokatām eti | (yathā?) candramaṇḍale svargopabhogaṃ prāpnotīty arthaḥ || 329 ||

 

_yas tv anabhisaṃdhāya phalam ātmasaṃskārārthaṃ kuryāt |_

 

                    	**kṛcchrakṛd dharmakāmas tu mahatīṃ śriyam aśnute |**

**              	yathāguru kratuphalaṃ prāpnoti ca na saṃśayaḥ || 3.330 ||**

 

kṛcchraśabdo 'tra cāndrāyaṇasyāpi grāhakaḥ | kṛcchrakṛc cāndrāyaṇakṛd vā dharmakāmaś coditānuṣṭānamātrārthī na phalam itcchatīty arthaḥ | mahatī śrīr devayānena mārgeṇaindra upabhogaḥ | yathāgurv iti | alpena sāntapanādinālpasya kratoḥ, tathā guruṇā parākacāndrāyaṇādinā gurutarasya krator yat phalam, tat prāpnotīty arthaḥ || 330 ||

 

_ya ete "yasmin deśe mṛgaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ" _(YDh 1.2)_ ity ārabhya "yathāguru kratuphalaṃ prāpnoti ca na saṃśayaḥ" _(YDh 3.330)_ ity evamantā yājñavalkyenopadiṣṭāḥ |_

 

                    	**śrutvaitān ṛṣayo dharmān yājñavalkyena bhāṣitān |**

**              	idam ūcur mahātmāno yogīndram amitaujasam || 3.331 ||**

                    	**ya idaṃ dhārayiṣyanti dharmaśāstram atandritāḥ |**

**              	iha loke yaśaḥ prāpya te yāsyanti triviṣṭapam || 3.332 ||**

_kiṃ ca |_

                    	**vidyārthī cāpnuyād vidyāṃ dhanakāmo dhanāni ca |**

**              	āyuṣkāmas tathaivāyuḥ śrīkāmo mahatīṃ śriyam || 3.333 ||**

_tathā _|

                    	**ślokatrayam api hy asmād yaḥ śrāddhe śrāvayiṣyati |**

**              	pitṝṇāṃ tatra tṛptiḥ syād ānantyāya na saṃśayaḥ || 3.334 ||**

_kiṃ ca |_

                    	**brāhmaṇaḥ pātratāṃ yāti kṣatriyo vijayī bhavet |**

**              	vaiśyaś ca dhānyadhanavān asya śāstrasya dhāraṇāt || 3.335 ||**

 

granthato 'rthataś ceti śeṣaḥ || 335 ||

 

_idaṃ cānyat |_

 

                    	**ya idaṃ śrāvayed viprān dvijaḥ parvasu saṃyataḥ |**

**              	aśvamedhaphalaṃ tasya tad bhavān anumanyatām || 3.336 ||**

 

spaṣṭārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 336 ||

 

_yad etan munibhiḥ prārthitam |_

 

                    	**śrutvaitad yājñavalkyas tu prītātmā munibhāṣitam |**

**              	eva astv iti hovāca namaskṛtvā svayaṃbhuve || 3.337 ||**

 

idam idaṃ cāstv iti munibhiḥ prārthitopanyāso munīnāṃ dharmopadeśe kṛte paritoṣajñāpanārthatayāsya dharmaśāstrasyāvicikitsaṃ prāmāṇyapratipattyartham, yājñavalkyasya caivam evāstv iti prītātmanaḥ prativacanaṃ samyag ebhir maduktaṃ dharmaśāstram avadhṛtaṃ bhaviṣyati asmād dharmaśāstrād varṇinām āśramiṇāṃ naiḥśreyasam ity upadeśasāphalyapratipattyartham, brāhmaṇāś ca pariṣaddharmeṇāvasthitā yad brūyur idam evam astv iti, tat tathaiva syād iti brāhmaṇavacanasya darmapramāṇatāpratipattyartham, gurusaṃnidhau ca na śiṣyaiḥ svātantryeṇa dharmāvadhāraṇaṃ gurvananumataiḥ kāryam ity evaṃ sadācāraparipālanārtham | "namaskṛtvā svayaṃbhuve" iti | manave namaskṛvety arthaḥ | etac cācāraparipālanārtham | na hy āgamike 'rthe gurum anabhipūjya svātantryeṇa kiṃcid vaktavyam ity abhiprāyaḥ | mānavaś cāyaṃ sarvo 'rthaḥ smārta ity etad api tannamaskāreṇaiva spaṣṭīkṛtam | tataś ca vedavirodhavan manuvirodhe 'pi smṛtyantarāṇām aprāmāṇyam | smṛtyantarānusāreṇaiva mānave 'pi saṃdigdhārthanirṇayaḥ, mānavīya evārthaḥ smṛtyantare 'pi yasmāt | ataḥ sūktam: "namaskṛtvā svayaṃbhuve" iti || 337 ||

 

 

                    	labdhvā rahasyāni sudurlabhāni yajūṃṣi śuklāni vivasvato yaḥ |

                    	svarvāpavargāv akarot prakāśau jayaty asau brahmavid ekahaṃsaḥ ||

                    	prajñāparādhād iha yad duruktaṃ noktaṃ ca tat sarvam anākulimnā |

                    	kṛpālubhiḥ samyag amatsareṇa vivecanīyaṃ svamatiprabhāvāt ||

 

**iti paramabhaṭṭārakayogīndrapraṇīte dharmaśāstre**

**viśvarūpakṛtavivaraṇabālakrīḍāyāṃ**

**tṛtīyo 'dhyāyaḥ ||**

** **

**samāptaś cāyaṃ granthaḥ |**

**śubhaṃ bhūyāt |**

 

 


## Footnotes

[^1]:
     The subcommentary _Vacanamālā_ provides the first line of this verse: kaścic chiṣṭo 'tikāruṇyāt sarvadharmāgamārthavit |

[^2]:
     See AitB 5.32 (25.7). The reading here should be _ṛkto _in place of _ukto._

[^3]:
     Here the printed edition is blurred and the reading is not quite certain.

[^4]:
     Editor's note: apasīmantonnayanā sīmantonnayanavyatiriktāḥ.

[^5]:
     In the Munshiram Manoharlal reprint of 1982 this word has been changed to what appears to be: avagaktavāṃ.

[^6]:
     Ascribed to Bhṛgu in the _Vacanamālā: _snānāni pañca puṇyāni kīrtitāni manīṣibhiḥ | āgneyaṃ vāruṇaṃ brāhmaṃ vāyavyaṃ divyam eva ca ||

[^7]:
     The edition reads _apūrvam_, which I think is a typo.

[^8]:
     The two pādas in this sentence probably constitute the second half of verse ascribed to Vasiṣṭha give above.

[^9]:
     Ganapati Sastri's edition places here (na?), assuming that there should be a negative here. But we already have the negative in -anapākaraṇa-; the son, because he does not know the details of the document cannot eliminate its defects.

[^10]:
     The Vulgate has this reading for pāda-d: dhanabhāg vā dhanī bhavet.

[^11]:
     The printed edition reads "tv eṣāṃ", but, as I have noted in my edition of the YDh, this is probably a typo. The Malayalam manuscripts I used in the edition and on which the Viśva edition is based have "ceṣṭāṃ".

[^12]:
     Even though the printed text of Viśva reads: _vedavidyābhiḥ sāttviko_, the commentary itself clearly shows the reading _yāti_: _vedavic ca yaḥ sa sātviko devayoniṣu yāti_. The reading of the edition is probably a typo.

[^13]:
     Edition reads "sāmarthād" but I think it is a typo.

[^14]:
     The edition reads: kṛtvāpratyakṣaśrutivacanād, that is, "apratyakṣaśruti". I think this reading is doubtful, and the sandhi here is probably a typo.

[^15]:
     The edition is faulty here: _kṛtvasujviṣayā ttisiddhyartham_. Clearly an _akṣara_ is missing between the two compounds. The statement _kṛtvasuc_ refers to Pāṇini 5.4.17: _saṅkhyāyāḥ kriyābhyāvr̥ttigaṇane kr̥tvasuc_._ _It appears likely that here the reference is to _āvṛtti _of the Pāṇini's rule. I think Madhav Deshpande for his help in resolving this problem.

[^16]:
     The editions of VaDh read: "ajito".

[^17]:
     The edition here reads "tathāreyā", which is probably a typo.

[^18]:
     The edition here reads "vyākhyāne", which is probably a typo.

[^19]:
     Verses 261 and 262 are omitted in the critical edition. I note there that these two verses are probably part of the commentary rather than verses within the root text.

[^20]:
     The edition reads "pāṇamāsā"; probably a typo.
